 vimala kalā āśraya abhinava sṛṣṭi mahā jananī bharita tanuḥ ca pañcamukha gupta ruciḥ janakaḥ tad ubhaya yāmala sphurita bhāva visarga mayam hṛdayam anuttara amṛta kulam mama sa sphuratāt  naumi cit pratibhām devīm parām bhairava yoginīm mātṛmān aprameya aṃśa śūla ambuja kṛta āspadām naumi devīm śarīra sthām nṛtyataḥ  bhairava akṛte prāvṛṣ megha ghana vyoma vidyut lekhā vilāsinīm dīpta jyotiḥ chaṭā pluṣṭa bheda bandha trayam sphurat  stād jñāna śūlam sat pakṣa vipakṣa utkartana kṣamam svātantrya śaktiḥ krama saṃsisṛkṣā krama ātma tā ca iti vibhoḥ vibhūtiḥ tad eva devī trayam antarāstām anuttaram me prathayat svarūpam tad devatā vibhava bhāvi mahā marīci cakra īśvarāyita nija sthitiḥ eka eva devī sutaḥ  gaṇapatiḥ sphurat indu kāntiḥ samyak samucchalayatān mama saṃvid abdhim rāga aruṇām granthi bila avakīrṇa yaḥ  jālam ātāna vitāna vṛtti kalombhitam bāhya pathe cakāra stān me sa mad chandavibhuḥ prasannaḥ traiyambaka abhihita santati tāmra parṇī sanmauktika prakara kānti viśeṣa bhājaḥ pūrve jayanti guravaḥ  guru śāstra sindhu kallola keli kalana amala karṇa dhārāḥ jayati guruḥ eka eva śrī śrīkaṇṭhaḥ  bhuvi prathitaḥ tad apara mūrtiḥ bhagavān maheśvaraḥ  bhūtirājaḥ ca śrī somānanda bodha śrīmat utpala viniḥsṛtāḥ jayanti saṃvid āmoda sandarbhā diś prasarpiṇaḥ tad āsvāda bhara āveśa bṛṃhitām mati ṣaṭpadīm guroḥ lakṣmaṇaguptasya nāda saṃmohinīm numaḥ yaḥ pūrṇa ānanda viśrānta sarva śāstra artha pāragaḥ sa śrī cukhulakaḥ  diśi ādiṣṭam me guruḥ uttamaḥ jayatāt jagat uddhṛti kṣamaḥ  sau bhagavatyā saha śaṃbhu nātha ekaḥ yad udīrita śāsana aṃśubhiḥ me prakaṭaḥ  yam gahanaḥ  pi śāstra mārgaḥ santi paddhatayaḥ citrāḥ srotaḥ bhedeṣu bhūyasā anuttara ṣaṣ ardha artha krame tu ekā api na īkṣyate iti aham bahuśas  sadbhiḥ śiṣya sabrahmacāribhiḥ arthitaḥ  racaye spaṣṭām pūrṇa arthā prakriyām imām śrī bhaṭṭanātha caraṇa abja yugāt tathā śrī bhaṭṭārikā aṃghri yugalāt guru santatiḥ yā bodha anya pāśa viṣa nud tad upāsana uttha bodha ujjvalaḥ  bhinavagupta idam karoti na tad asti iha yad na śrī  mālinīvijaya uttare devadevena nirdiṣṭam sva śabdena atha liṅgataḥ daśa aṣṭādaśa vasu aṣṭa bhinnam yad śāsanam vibhoḥ tad sāram trika śāstram hi tad sāram mālinīmatam atas  tra antargatam sarva saṃpradāya ujjhitaiḥ budhaiḥ adṛṣṭa prakaṭīkurmaḥ  gurunā atha ājñayā vayam abhinavaguptasya kṛtiḥ sā iyam yasya uditā gurubhiḥ ākhyā trinayana caraṇa saroruha cintana labdha prasiddhiḥ iti śrī śambhu nātha bhāskara caraṇa nipāta prabhā apagata saṃkocam abhinavagupta hṛd ambujam etad vicinuta maheśa pūjana hetoḥ ādi vākyam iha tāvat samasteṣu śāstreṣu parigīyate ajñānam saṃsṛteḥ hetuḥ jñānam mokṣa eka kāraṇam malam ajñānam icchanti saṃsāra aṅkura kāraṇam iti proktam tathā va śrī malinīvijaya uttare viśeṣaṇena buddhi sthe saṃsāra uttara kālike saṃbhāvanām nirasya etad abhāve mokṣam abravīt  ajñānam iti na jñāna abhāvaḥ ca atiprasaṅgataḥ sa hi loṣṭa ādike pyasti na ca tasya asti saṃsṛtiḥ atas  jñeyasya tattvasya sāmasti ena aprathā ātmakam jñānam eva tad ajñānam śivasūtreṣu bhāṣitam caitanyam ātmā jñānam ca bandha iti atra sūtrayoḥ saṃśleṣa itara yoga āśyāmayam arthaḥ pradarśitaḥ caitanyam iti bhāva antaḥ śabdaḥ svātantrya mātrakam anākṣi pra viśeṣam sadāha sūtre purātane dvitīyena tu sūtreṇa kriyām vā karaṇam ca vā bruvatā tasya cit mātra rūpasya dvaitam ucyate dvaitaprathā tad ajñānam tuccha tvāt bandha ucyate tatas  eva samucchedyam iti āvṛttyā nirūpitam svatantra ātmā atiriktaḥ tu tucchaḥ tucchaḥ pi kaścana na mokṣaḥ  nāma tad na asya pṛthak nāma api gṛhyate yad tu jñeyasa tattvasya pūrṇa pūrṇa prathā ātmakam tad uttarottaram jñānam tad tad saṃsāra śānti dam rāga ādi akaluṣaḥ  smi antar śūnyaḥ  ham kartṛ tā ujjhitaḥ ittham samāsa vyāsābhyām jñānam muñcati tāvataḥ tasmāt muktaḥ  pyavacchedāt avaccheda antara sthiteḥ amukta eva muktaḥ tu sarva avaccheda varjitaḥ yad tu jñeyasa tattvasya jñānam sarva ātmanā ujjhitam avacchedaiḥ na tad kutra api ajñānam satya mukti dam jñāna ajñāna svarūpam yad uktam pratyekam api adaḥ dvidhā pauruṣa bauddhatva bhidā uktam śiva śāsane tatra puṃsaḥ yad ajñānam mala ākhyam tad jam apyaya sva pūrṇa cit kriyā rūpa śiva tā āvaraṇa ātmakam saṃkoci dṛkkriyā rūpam tad paśoḥ avikalpitam tad ajñānam na budghi aṃśaḥ  dhyavasāya ādi abhāvataḥ aham ittham idam vedmi iti evam adhyavasāyinī ṣaṣ kañcukā bila aṇu uttha pratibimbanataḥ  yadā dhīḥ jāyate tadā tādṛś jñānam ajñāna śabditam bauddham tasya ca tad pauṃsnam poṣaṇīyam ca poṣṭṛ ca kṣīṇe tu paśu saṃskāre puṃsaḥ prāpta para sthiteḥ vikasvaram tad vijñānam pauruṣam nirvikalpakam vikasvara avikalpa ātma jñān aucityena yāvasā tad bauddham yasya tad pauṃsnam prāgvat poṣyam ca poṣṭṛ ca tatra dīkṣā ādinā pauṃsnam ajñānam dhvaṃsi yadi api tathā api tad śarīra ante tad jñānam vyajyate sphuṭam bauddha jñānena tu yadā bauddham ajñāna jṛmbhitam vilīyate tadā jīvanmuktiḥ kara tale sthitā dīkṣā api bauddha vijñāna pūrvā satyam vimocikā tena tatra api bauddhasya jñānasya asti pradhāna tā jñāna ajñāna āgatam ca etad dvi tvam svāyambhuve rurau mataṅga ādau kṛtam śrīmat kheṭapāla ādi daiśikaiḥ tathāvidha avasāya ātma bauddha vijñāna sampade śāstram eva pradhānam yad jñeya tattva pradarśakam dīkṣayā galite pyantara jñāne pauruṣa ātmani dhī gatasya anivṛtta tvāt vikalpaḥ  pi hi saṃbhaveta deha sadbhāva paryantam ātma bhāvaḥ  yatas  dhiyi dehānte pi na mokṣaḥ syāt pauruṣa ajñāna hānitaḥ bauddha ajñāna nivṛttau tu vikalpa unmūlanāt dhruvam tadā eva mokṣa iti uktam dhātrā śrīmat niśāṭane vikalpa yukta citaḥ tu piṇḍa pātāt śivam brajet  itaraḥ tu tadā eva iti śāstrasya atra pradhānataḥ jñeyasya hi param tattvam yaḥ prakāśa ātmakaḥ śivaḥ na hi aprakāśa rūpasya prākāśyam vastu tāpi vā avastu tā api bhāvānām camatkāra eka gocarā yad kuḍya sadṛśī na iyam dhīra vastu etad iti api prakāśaḥ  nāma yaḥ ca ayam sarvatra eva prakāśate anapahnavanīya tvāt  kim tasmin māna kalpanaiḥ pramāṇāni api vastūnām jīvitam yāni tanvate teṣām api paraḥ  jīvaḥ sa eva parameśvaraḥ sarva apahnava hevāka dharmā api evam hi vartate jñānam ātma artham iti etad na iti mām prati bhāsate apahnutau sādhane vā vastūnām ādyam īdṛśam yad tatra ke pramāṇānām upapatti upayogite [ missing] kāmike tatas  eva uktam hetuvāda vivarjitam tasya deva atidevasya para apekṣā na vidyate parasya tad apekṣa tvāt svatantraḥ  yamatas  sthitaḥ anapekṣasya vaśinaḥ deśa kāla ākṛti kramāḥ niyatā na iti sa vibhuḥ nityaḥ  viśva ākṛtiḥ śivaḥ vibhu tvāt sarva gaḥ nitya bhāvāt ādi anta varjitaḥ viśva ākṛti tvāt cit acit tad vaicitrya avabhāsakaḥ tatas  sya bahu rūpa tvam uktam dīkṣā uttara ādike bhuvanam vigrahaḥ  jyotiḥ kham śabdaḥ  mantra eva ca bindu nāda ādi saṃbhinnaḥ ṣaḍvidhaḥ śiva ucyate yaḥ  yad ātmaka tā niṣṭhaḥ tad bhāvam sa prapadyate vyoma ādi śabda vijñānāt paraḥ  mokṣaḥ  na saṃśayaḥ viśva ākṛti tve devasya tad etad ca upalakṣaṇam anavacchinna tā ārūḍhau  avaccheda laye sya ca uktam ca kāmike devaḥ sarva ākṛtiḥ nirākṛtiḥ jala darpaṇavat tena sarvam vyāptam carācaram na ca asya vimuta ādyaḥ  yam dharmaḥ  nyonyam vibhidyate eka eva asya dharmaḥ  sau sarva ākṣepeṇa vartate tena svātantrya śaktyā eva yukta iti āñjasaḥ vidhiḥ bahu śakti tvam api asya tad śaktyā eva aviyukta tā śaktiḥ ca nāma bhāvasya svam rūpam mātṛ kalpitam tena advayaḥ sa eva api śaktimat parikalpane mātṛklṛpte hi devasya tatra tatra vapuṣi alam kaḥ  bhedaḥ  vastu tas  vahneḥ dagdhṛ paktṛ tvayoḥ iva na vāsau parama arthena na kiṃcid bhāsanāt ṛte na hi asti kiṃcid tad śakti tadvat bhedaḥ  pi vāstavaḥ sva śakti udreka janakam tādātmyāt vastunaḥ  hi yad  śaktiḥ tad api devī evam bhānti api anya svarūpiṇī śivaḥ ca alupta vibhavaḥ tathā sṛṣṭaḥ  vabhāsate sva saṃvid mātṛm akure svātantryāt bhāvanā ādiṣu tasmāt yena mukhena eṣa bhāti anaṃśaḥ  pi tad tathā śaktiḥ iti eṣa vastu eva śakti tadvat kramaḥ sphuṭaḥ śrīmat kiraṇa śāstre ca tad praśna uttara pūrvakam anubhāvaḥ  vikalpaḥ  pi mānasaḥ  na manaḥ śive avijñāya śivam dīkṣā katham iti atra ca uttaram kṣudhā ādi anubhavaḥ  na eva vikalpaḥ  na hi mānasaḥ rasa ādi anadhyakṣa tve pi rūpāt eva yathā tarum vikalpaḥ  vetti tadvat tu nādabindu ādinā śivam bahu śakti tvam asya uktam śivasya yadatas  mahān kalā tattva pura arṇa aṇu pada ādiḥ bheda vistaraḥ sṛṣṭi sthiti tirodhāna saṃhāra anugraha ādi ca turyam iti api devasya bahu śaktitva jṛmbhitam jāgrat svapna suṣupta anya tad atītāni yāni api tāni api amuṣya nāthasya svātantrya laharī bharaḥ mahā mantra īśa mantra īśa mantrāḥ śiva purogamāḥ akalau sakalaḥ ca iti śivasya eva vibhūtayaḥ tattva grāmasya sarvasya dharmaḥ syāt anapāyavān ātmā eva hi svabhāva ātmā iti uktam śrī triśiraḥ mate hṛdistham sarva deha stham svabhāva stham su sūkṣmakam sāmūhyam ca eva tattvānām grāma śabdena kīrtitam ātmā eva dharma iti uktaḥ śiva amṛta pariplutaḥ prakāśa avasthitam jñānam bhāva abhāva ādi madhyatas  sva sthāne vartanam jñeyam draṣṭṛ tvam vigata āvṛti vivikta vastu kathita śuddha vijñāna nirmalaḥ grāma dharma vṛttiḥ uktaḥ tasya sarvam prasiddhyati ūrdhva  tyaktvā adhas  viśet sa rāma sthaḥ  madhyadeśa gaḥ gatiḥ sthānam svapna jāgrat unmeṣaṇa nimeṣaṇe dhāvanam plavanam ca eva āyāsaḥ śakti vedanam buddhi bhedāḥ tathā bhāvāḥ saṃjñāḥ karmāṇi anekaśas  eṣa rāmaḥ  vyāpakaḥ  tra śivaḥ parama kāraṇam kalmaṣa kṣīṇa manasā smṛti mātra nirodhanāt dhyāyate paramam dhyeyam gama āgama pade sthitam param śivam tu vrajati bhairava ākhyam japāt api tad svarūpam japaḥ proktaḥ  bhāva abhāva pada cyutaḥ tad atra api tadīyena svātantryeṇa upakalpitaḥ dūra āsanna ādikaḥ  bhedaḥ cit svātantrya vyapekṣayā evam svātantrya pūrṇa tvāt ati durghaṭa kārī ayam kena nāma na rūpeṇa bhāsate parameśvaraḥ nirāvaraṇam ābhāti bhāti ābṛta nija ātmakaḥ āvṛta anāvṛtaḥ  bhāti bahudhā bheda saṃgamāt  iti śakti trayam nāthe svātantrya apara nāmakam icchā ādibhiḥ abhikhyābhiḥ gurubhiḥ prakaṭīkṛtam devaḥ  hi anvartha śāstra uktaiḥ śabdaiḥ samupadiśyate mahābhairava devaḥ  yam patiḥ yaḥ paramaḥ śivaḥ viśvam bibharti pūraṇa dhāraṇa yogena tena ca śriyate sa vimarśa tayā rava rūpataḥ ca saṃsāra bhīru hita kṛt ca saṃsāra bhīti janitāt ravāt parāmarśataḥ  pi hṛdi jātaḥ prakaṭībhūtam bhava bhaya vimarśanam śaktipātatas  yena nakṣatra preraka kāla tattva saṃśoṣa kāriṇaḥ  ye ca kāla grāsa samādhāna rasika manaḥsu teṣu ca prakaṭaḥ saṃkoci pa śujana bhiye yāsām ravaṇam sva karaṇa devīnām antar bahis caturvidha khecarī ādika gaṇasya api tasya svāmī saṃsāra vṛtti vighaṭana mahā bhīmaḥ bhairava iti gurubhiḥ imaiḥ anvarthaiḥ saṃstutaḥ śāstre heya upādeya kathā virahe sva ānanda ghana tayā ucchalanam krīḍā sarva utkarṣeṇa vartana icchā tathā svatantra tvam vyavaharaṇam abhinne pi sva ātmani bhedena saṃjalpaḥ nikhila avabhāsanāt ca dyotanam asya stutiḥ yatas  sakalam tad pravaṇam ātma lābhāt prabhṛti samaste pi kartavye bodha ātmakaḥ samasta kriyāmayaḥ  dṛkkriyā guṇaḥ ca gatiḥ iti nirvacanaiḥ śiva tanu śāstre gurubhiḥ smṛtaḥ  devaḥ śāsana rodhana pālana pācana yogāt sa sarvam upakurute c tena patiḥ śreyaḥ maya eva śivaḥ  na aśivam kim api tatra īdṛś rūpam kiyat api rudra upendra ādiṣu sphuret yena tena avaccheda nude parama mahat pada viśeṣaṇam upāttam iti yad jñeya sa tattvam darśyate tad śiva ājñayā mayā sva saṃvid sat tarka pati śāstra trika kramāt tasya śaktaya eva etāḥ tisraḥ  bhānti para ādikāḥ sṛṣṭau sthitau laye turye tena etā dvādaśa uditāḥ tāvān pūrṇa svabhāvaḥ  sau paramaḥ śiva ucyate tena atra upāsakāḥ sākṣāt tatra eva pariniṣṭhitāḥ tāsām api ca bheda aṃśa nyūna ādhikya ādi yojanam tad svātantrya balāt eva śāstreṣu paribhāṣitam eka vīraḥ  yāmalaḥ  tha tri śaktiḥ catur ātmakaḥ pañcamūrtiḥ ṣaṣ ātmā ayam saptakaḥ  ṣṭaka bhūṣitaḥ nava ātmā daśa diś chaktiḥ ekādaśa kalā ātmakaḥ dvādaśa ara mahā cakra nāyakaḥ  bhairavaḥ tu iti evam yāvat sahasrāre niḥsaṃkhyāre pi vā prabhuḥ viśva cakre maheśānaḥ  viśva śaktiḥ vijṛmbhate teṣām api ca cakrāṇā sva varga anugama ātmanā aikyena cakra gaḥ bhedaḥ tatra tatra nirūpitaḥ catuṣṣaṣ dvis dvi gaṇanā yogāt traiśirase mate ṣaṭcakra īśvara tā nāthasya uktā citra nija ākṛteḥ nāmāni cakra devīnām tatra kṛtya vibhedataḥ saumya raudra ākṛti dhyāna yogīni anvartha kalpanāt  ekasya saṃvid nāthasya hi āntarī pratibhā tanuḥ saumyam vā anyat mitam saṃvid ūrmi cakram upāsyate asya syāt puṣṭiḥ iti eṣā saṃvid devī tathā uditāt  dhyānāt saṃjalpa saṃmiśrāt  vyāpārāt ca api bāhyatas  sphuṭībhūtā satī bhāti tasya tādṛś phala pradā puṣṭiḥ śuṣkasya sarasībhāvaḥ  jalam atas  sitam anugamya tatas  dhyānam tad pradhānam pratanyate ye ca svabhāvataḥ  varṇā rasa niḥṣyandinaḥ  yathā dantī oṣṭhya danti aprāyāḥ te kaiścid varṇaiḥ kṛtāḥ saha tam bīja bhāvam āgatya saṃvidam sphuṭayanti tām puṣṭim kuru rasena enam āpyāyaya tarām iti saṃjalpaḥ  pi vikalpa ātmā kim tām eva na pūrayet  amṛtā iyam idam kṣīram idam sarpiḥ bala āvaham tena asya bījam puṣṇīyām iti ena am pūrayet kriyām tasmāt viśveśvaraḥ  bodha bhairavaḥ samupāsyate avaccheda anavacchidbhyām bhoga mokṣa arthibhiḥ janaiḥ ye pyanya devatā bhaktā iti atas  guruḥ ādiśat  ye bodhāt vyatiriktam hi kiṃcid yājya tayā viduḥ te pi vedyam viviñcānā bodha abhedena manvate tena avicchinna tāmarśa rūpāhantā prathā ātmanaḥ svayan prathasya na vidhiḥ sṛṣṭi ātmā asya ca pūrva gaḥ vedyā hi devatā sṛṣṭiḥ śakteḥ hetoḥ samutthitā ahaṃrūpā tu saṃvittiḥ nityā sva prathana ātmikā vidhiḥ niyogaḥ tri aṃśā ca bhāvanā codanā ātmikā tad eka siddhā indra ādyā vidhi pūrvā hi devatāḥ ahaṃbodhaḥ tu na tathā te tu saṃvedya rūpa tām unmagnām eva paśyantaḥ tam vidantaḥ  pi naḥ viduḥ tad uktam na viduḥ mām tu tattvena atas calanti te calanam tu vyavacchinna rūpa tā āpattiḥ eva yā devān deva yajaḥ  yānti ityādi tena nyarūpyata nimajjya vedya tām ye tu tatra saṃvid mayīm sthitim viduḥ te hi anavacchinnam tad bhaktā api yānti mām sarvatra atra hi ahaṃśabdaḥ  bodha mātra eka vācakaḥ sa bhoktṛ prabhu śabdābhyām yājyayaṣṭṭatayā uditaḥ yājamānī saṃvid eva yājyā na anyā iti coditam na tu ākṛtiḥ kutaḥ pyanyā devatā na hi sa ucitā vidhiḥ ca na uktaḥ kaḥ  pyatra mantra ādi vṛtti dhāma vā saḥ  yama ātmānam āvṛtya sthitaḥ  jaḍa padam gataḥ āvṛta anāvṛta ātmā tu deva ādi sthāvara anta gaḥ jaḍājaḍasya api etasya dvairūpyasya asti citra tā tasya svatantra bhāvaḥ  hi kim kim yad na vicintayet  tad uktam triśiraḥśāstre saṃbuddha iti vetti yaḥ c jñeya bhāvaḥ  hi cit dharmaḥ tad chāyā ācchādayet na tām c tena ajaḍasya bhāgasya pudgala aṇu ādi saṃjñinaḥ anāvaraṇa bhāga aṃśe vaicitryam bahudhā sthitam saṃvid rūpe na bhedaḥ  sti vāstavaḥ  yadi api dhruve tathā api āvṛti nirhāsa tāratamyāt sa lakṣyate tad vistareṇa vakṣyāmaḥ śaktipāta vinirṇaye samāpya para tām sthaulya prasaṃge carcayiṣyate atas  kaṃcid pramātāram prati prathayate vibhuḥ pūrṇam eva nijam rūpam kaṃcid aṃśa aṃśikā kramāt viśva bhāva eka bhāva ātma svarūpa prathanam hi yad  aṇūnām tad param jñānam tad anyat aparam bahu tad ca sākṣāt upāyena tad upāya ādinā api ca prathamānam vicitrābhiḥ bhaṃgībhiḥ iha bhidyate tatra api sva para dvāra dvāri tvāt sarva śoṃśaśas  vyavadhāna avi avadhinā bhūyān bhedaḥ pravartate jñānasya ca abhyupāyaḥ  yaḥ  na tad ajñānam ucyate jñānam eva tu tad sūkṣmam param tu icchā ātmakam matam upāya upeya bhāvaḥ tu jñānasya sthaulya viśramaḥ eṣā eva ca kriyāśaktiḥ bandha mokṣa eka kāraṇam tatra ādye sva parāmarśe nirvikalpa eka dhāmani yad sphuret prakaṭam sākṣāt tad icchā ākhyam prakīrtitam yathā visphurita dṛśām anusandhim vinā api alam bhāti bhāvaḥ sphuṭaḥ tadvat keṣām api śiva ātma tā bhūyaḥ bhūyaḥ vikalpa aṃśa niścaya krama carcanāt yad parāmarśam abhyeti jñāna upāyam tu tad viduḥ yad tu tad kalpanāklṛpta bahis bhūta artha sādhanam kriyā upāyam tad āmnātam bhedaḥ  na atra apavarga gaḥ yatas  na anyā kriyā nāma jñānam eva hi tad tathā rūḍheḥ yoga antatām prāptam iti śrī gamaśāsane yogaḥ  na anyaḥ kriyā na anyā tattva ārūḍhā hi yā matiḥ sva citta vāsanā śāntau sā kriyā iti abhidhīyate sva citte vāsanāḥ karma mala māyā prasūtayaḥ tāsām śānti nimittam yā matiḥ saṃvid svabhāvikā sā deha ārambhi bāhya stha tattva brātā adhiśāyinī kriyā sā eva ca yogaḥ syāt tattvānām cit layīkṛtau loke pi kila gacchāmi iti evam antar  sphura eva yā sā deham deśam akṣān  ca api āviśantī gati kriyā tasmāt kriyā api yā nāma jñānam eva hi sā tatas  jñānam eva vimokṣāya yuktam ca etad udāhṛtam mokṣaḥ  hi nāma na eva anyaḥ svarūpa prathanam hi saḥ svarūpam ca ātmanaḥ saṃvid na anyat tatra tu yāḥ punar  kriyā ādikāḥ śaktayaḥ tāḥ saṃvid rūpa adhikā na hi asaṃvid rūpa tā yogāt dharmiṇaḥ ca anirūpaṇāt parameśvara śāstre hi na ca kāṇāda dṛṣṭivat  śaktīnām dharma rūpāṇām āśrayaḥ kaḥ  pi kathyate tatas ca dṛkkriyā icchā ādyā bhinnāḥ ced śaktayaḥ tathā ekaḥ śiva iti iyam vāc vastu śūnyā eva jāyate tasmāt saṃvid tvam eva etad svātantryam yad tad api alam vivicyamānam bahvīṣu paryavasyati śaktiṣu yatas ca ātma prathā mokṣaḥ tad na iha āśaṅkyam īdṛśam na avaśyam kāraṇāt kārya tad jñāni api na mucyate yatas  jñānena mokṣasya yā hetu phala tā uditā na sā mukhyā tatas  na ayam prasaṃga iti niścitam evam jñāna svabhāvā eva kriyā sthūla tvam ātmani yatas  vahati tena asyām citra tā dṛśyatām kila kriyā upāye bhyupāyānām grāhya bāhya vibhedinām bheda upabheda vaividhyāt niḥsaṃkhya tvam avāntarāt anena ca etad pradhvastam yad kecana śaśaṅkire upāya bhedāt mokṣe pi bhedaḥ syāt iti sūrayaḥ mala tad śakti vidhvaṃsa tiras bhū cyuti madhyataḥ hetu bhede pi naḥ bhinnā ghaṭa dhvaṃsa ādi vṛttivat  tad etad trividha tvam hi śāstre śrī pūrva nāmani ādeśi parameśitrā samāveśa vinirṇaye akiṃcid cintakasya eva guruṇā pratibodhataḥ utpadyate ya āveśaḥ śāmbhavaḥ  sā vidīritaḥ uccāra rahitam vastu cetasā eva vicintayan yam samāveśam āpnoti śāktaḥ saḥ  trābhidhīyate uccāra karaṇa dhyāna varṇa sthāna prakalpanaiḥ yaḥ  bhavet sa samāveśaḥ samyak āṇava ucyate akiṃcid cintakasya iti vikalpa anupayogi tā tayā ca jhaṭiti jñeya samāpattiḥ nirūpyate sā katham bhavati iti āha guruṇā ati garīyasā jñeya abhimukha bodhena drāk prarūḍhatva śālinā tṛtīya arthe tasi vyākhyā vā vaiyadhikaraṇyataḥ āveśaḥ ca asvatantrasya sva tad rūpa nimajjanāt  para tad rūpa tā śambhoḥ ādyāt śakti avibhāginaḥ tena ayam atra vākya arthaḥ  vijñeyam pronmiṣat svayam vinā api niścayena drāk  mātṛ darpaṇa bimbitam mātāram adharīkurvat  svām vibhūtim pradarśayat  āste hṛdaya nairmalya atiśaye tāratamyataḥ jñeyam dvidhā ca cit mātram jaḍam ca ādyam ca kalpitam itarat tu tathā satyam tad vibhāgaḥ  yam i īdṛśaḥ jaḍena yaḥ samāveśaḥ sa praticchandaka ākṛtiḥ caitanyena samāveśaḥ tādātmyam na aparam kila tena avikalpā saṃvittiḥ bhāvanā ādi anapekṣiṇī śiva tādātmyam āpannā samāveśaḥ  tra śāṃbhavaḥ tad prasādāt punar  paścāt bhāvinaḥ  tra viniścayāḥ santu tādātmyam āpannā na tu teṣām upāya tā vikalpa apekṣayā mānam avikalpam iti bruvan pratyukta eva siddham hi vikalpena anugamyate gṛhītam iti su spaṣṭā niścayasya yatas  prathā gṛhṇāmi iti avikalpa aikya balāt tu pratipadyate avikalpa ātma saṃvittau yā sphurat tā eva vastunaḥ sā siddhiḥ na vikalpāt tu vastu apekṣā vivarjitāt kevalam saṃvidaḥ saḥ  yam nairmalya itara viśramaḥ yad vikalpa anapekṣatva sāpekṣa tve nija ātmani niśīthe pi maṇi jñānī vidyut kāla pradarśitān tān  tān viśeṣān  cinute ratnānām bhūyasām api nairmalyam saṃvidaḥ ca idam pūrva abhyāsa vaśāt athaḥ aniyantreśvara icchāta iti etad carcayiṣyate pañcāśat vidha tā ca asya samāveśasya varṇitā tattva ṣaṭtriṃśakā etad stha sphuṭa bheda abhisandhitaḥ etad tattva antare yad puṃvidyā śakti ātmakam trayam ambhodhi kāṣṭhā jvalana saṃkhyaiḥ bhedaiḥ yatas  kramāt  puṃvidyā śakti saṃjñam yad tad sarva vyāpakam yatas  avyāpakebhyaḥ tena idam bhedena gaṇitam kila aśuddhi śuddhi amānatva śuddhitaḥ tu mithas  pi tad  bhūtāni adhyakṣa siddhāni kārya hetu anumeyataḥ tattva vargāt pṛthak bhūta samākhyānyata eva hi sarva pratīti sadbhāva gocaram bhūtam eva hi viduḥ catuṣṭaye ca atra sa avakāśe tad āsthitim rudra śakti samāveśaḥ pañcadhā nanu carcyate kaḥ  vakāśaḥ  bhavet tatra bhauta āveśa ādi varṇane prasaṃgāt etad iti ced samādhiḥ saṃbhavan  ayam na asmākam mānasa āvarjī lokaḥ  bhinna ruciḥ yatas  ucyate dvaita śāstreṣu parameśāt vibheditā bhūta ādīnām yathā sā atra na tathā dvaya varjite yāvān ṣaṭtriṃśakaḥ saḥ  yam yad anyat api kiṃcana etāvatī mahādevī rudra śaktiḥ anargalā tatas  eva dvitīye smin  adhikāre nyarūpyata dharā ādeḥ viśva rūpa tvam pāñcadaśya ādi bhedataḥ tasmāt yathā pura sthe rthe guṇa ādi aṃśa aṃśikā mukhāt niraṃśa bhāva saṃbodhaḥ tathā eva atra api budhyatām ata eva avikalpatva dhrauvya prābhava vaibhavaiḥ anyaiḥ vā śakti rūpa tvāt dharmaiḥ sva samavāyibhiḥ sarvaśas  pyatha vā aṃśena tam vibhum parameśvaram upāsate vikalpa ogha saṃskāra ādye śruta utthitāt  te tad tad sva vikalpa antar sphurat tad dharma pāṭavāt  dharmiṇam pūrṇa dharma ogham abhedena adhiśerate ūcivānata eva śrī vidyā adhipatiḥ ādarāt  tvad svarūpam avikalpamakṣajā kalpane na viṣayīkaroti ced  c antar ullikhita citra saṃvidaḥ  naḥ bhaveyuḥ anubhūtayaḥ sphuṭāḥ tad uktam śrī mataṅga ādau sva śakti kiraṇa ātmakam atha patyuḥ adhiṣṭhānam iti ādi uktam viśeṣaṇaiḥ tasyām divi su dīpta ātmā niṣkampaḥ  cala mūrtimān kāṣṭhā sā eva parā sūkṣmā sarva dikkā amṛta ātmikā pradhvasta āvaraṇā śāntā vastu mātra ati lālasā ādi anta uparatā sādhvī mūrti tvena upacaryate tathā upacārasya atra etad nimitam sa prayojanam tad mukhā sphuṭa tā dharmiṇī āśu tad maya tā sthitiḥ ta eva dharmāḥ śakti ākhyāḥ taiḥ taiḥ ucita rūpakaiḥ ākāraiḥ paryupāsyante tanmayībhāva siddhaye tatra kācid punar  śaktiḥ anantā vā mitāḥ ca vā ākṣipet havatā sattva nyāyāt dūra antika tvataḥ tena pūrṇa svabhāva tvam prakāśa tvam cit ātma tā bhairava tvam viśva śaktīḥ ākṣipet vyāpaka tvataḥ sadāśiva ādayaḥ tu ūrdhva vyāpti abhāvāt adhas juṣaḥ śaktīḥ samākṣipeyuḥ tad upāsā antika dūrataḥ itthaṃ bhāve ca śākta ākhyaḥ  vaikalpika patha kramaḥ iha tu uktaḥ  yatas tasmāt  pratiyogi avikalpakam avikalpa patha ārūḍhaḥ  yena yena pathā viśet  dharā sadāśiva antena tena tena śivībhavet  nirmale hṛdaye prāgrya sphurat bhūmi aṃśa bhāsini prakāśe tad mukhena eva saṃvid paraśiva ātma tā evam para icchā śakti aṃśa sat upāyam imam viduḥ śāmbhava ākhyam samāveśam sumatī antenivāsinaḥ śāktaḥ  tha bhaṇyate cetaḥ dhī  manohaṃkṛti sphuṭam sa vikalpa tayā māyā mayam icchā ādi vastutas  abhimānena saṃkalpa adhyavasāya krameṇa yaḥ śāktaḥ sa māyā upāyaḥ  pi tad ante nirvikalpakaḥ paśoḥ vai yā avikalpā bhūḥ daśā sā śāmbhavī param apūrṇā mātṛ daurātmyāt tad apāye vikasvarā evam vaikalpikī bhūmiḥ śākte kartṛtva vedane yasyām sphuṭe param tu asyām saṃkocaḥ pūrva nītitaḥ tathā saṃkoca saṃbhāra vilāyana parasya tu sā yathā iṣṭa antara ābhāsa kāriṇī śaktiḥ ujjvalā nanu vaikalpikī kim dhīrāṇave na asti tatra sā anya upāyātra tu uccāra rahita tvam nyarūpayat  uccāra śabdena atra uktā bahu antena tad ādayaḥ śakti upāye na santi ete bheda abhedau hi śakti tā aṇuḥ nāma sphuṭaḥ  bhedaḥ tad upāya iha aṇavaḥ vikalpa niścaya ātmā eva paryante nirvikalpakaḥ nanu dhī  mānasa ahaṃkṛt pumāṃsaḥ  vyāpnuyuḥ śivam na adhas varti tayā tena kathitam katham īdṛśam ucyate vastu tas  smākam śiva eva tathāvidhaḥ sva rūpa gopanam kṛtvā sva prakāśaḥ punar tathā dvaita śāstre mataṅga ādau ca api etad su nirūpitam adhas vyāptuḥ śivasya eva sa prakāśaḥ  vyavasthitaḥ yena buddhi manaḥ bhūmau  api bhāti param padam dvau  api etau samāveśau nirvikalpa arṇavam prati prayāta eva tad rūḍhim vinā na eva hi kiṃcana saṃvitti phala bhid ca atra na prakalpya iti atas  bravīt  kalpanāyāḥ ca mukhya tvam atra eva kila sūcitam vikalpa apekṣayā yaḥ  pi prāmāṇyam prāha tad mate tad vikalpa krama upātta nirvikalpa pramāṇa tā ratna tattvam avidvān prāc niścaya upāya carcanāt anupāya avikalpa āptau ratna jña iti bhaṇyate abheda upāyam atra uktam śāmbhavam śāktam ucyate bheda abheda ātmaka upāyam bheda upāyam tadā aṇavam ante jñāne tra sa upāye samastaḥ karma vistaraḥ prasphuṭena eva rūpeṇa bhāvī saḥ  ntarbhaviṣyati kriyā hi nāma vijñānāt na anyat vastu krama ātma tām upāya vaśataḥ prāptam tad kriyā iti purā uditam samyak jñānam ca mukti eka kāraṇam sva para sthitam yatas  hi kalpanā mātram sva para ādi vibhūtayaḥ tulye kālpanika tve ca yadā aikya sphuraṇa ātmakaḥ guruḥ sa tāvat eka ātmā siddhaḥ  muktaḥ ca bhaṇyate yāvān asya hi saṃtānaḥ  guruḥ tāvat sa kīrtitaḥ samyak jñāna mayaḥ ca iti sva ātmanā mucyate tatas  tatas  eva sva saṃtānam jñānī tārayati iti adaḥ yukti āgamābhyām saṃsiddham tāvān ekaḥ  yatas  muniḥ tena atra ye codayanti nanu jñānāt vimukta tā dīkṣā ādikā kriyā ca iyam sā katham muktaye bhavet  jñāna ātmā sā iti ced jñānam yatrastham tam vimocayet  anyasya mocane vā api bhavet kim na asamañjasam c iti te mūlataḥ kṣiptā yad tu atra anyaiḥ samarthitam malaḥ  nāma kila dravyam cakṣuḥ stha paṭala ādivat  tad vihantrī kriyā dīkṣā tu añjana ādika karmavat tad purastāt niṣetsyāmaḥ  yukti āgama vigarhitam mala māyā karmaṇām ca darśayiṣyāmahe sthitim evam śakti traya upāyam yad jñānam tatra paścimam mūlam tad uttaram madhyam uttarottaram ādimam tatas  pi paramam jñānam upāya ādi vivarjitam ānanda śakti viśrāntam anuttaram iha ucyate tad sva prakāśam vijñānam vidyā avidyeśvara ādibhiḥ api durlabha sadbhāvam śrī siddhātantra ucyate mālinyām sūcitam ca etad paṭale ṣṭādaśe sphuṭam na ca etad aprasannena śaṃkareṇa iti vākyataḥ iti anena eva pāṭhena mālinīvijayottare iti jñāna catuṣkam yad siddhi mukti mahā udayam c tad mayā tantryate tantra āloka nāmni atra śāsane tatra iha yad yad antar vā bahis vā parimṛśyate anudghāṭita rūpam tad pūrvam eva prakāśate tathā anudghāṭita ākārā nirvācyena ātmanā prathā saṃśayaḥ kutracid rūpe niścite sati na anyathā etad kim iti mukhye smin  etad aṃśaḥ su niścitaḥ saṃśayaḥ  stitvana asti ādi dharmān udghāṭita ātmakaḥ kim iti etasya śabdasya na adhikaḥ  rthaḥ prakāśate kim tu anunmudrita ākāram vastu eva abhidadhātyayam sthāṇuḥ vā puruṣaḥ  vā iti na mukhyaḥ  sti eṣa saṃśayaḥ bhūyas stha dharma jāteṣu niścaya utpāda eva hi āmarśanīyadvairūpyān udghāṭana vaśāt punar  saṃśayaḥ sa kim iti aṃśe vikalpaḥ tu anyathā sphuṭaḥ tena anudghāṭita ātmatva bhāva prathanam eva yad  prathamam sa iha uddeśaḥ praśnaḥ saṃśaya eva ca tathā anudghāṭita ākāra bhāva prasara vartmanā prasarantī sva saṃvittiḥ praṣṭrī śiṣya ātma tām gatā tathā antara parāmarśa niścaya ātma tirohiteḥ prasara anantara udbhūta saṃhāra udaya bhāj api yāvatī eva bhavet bāhya prasare prasphuṭa ātmani anunmīlita rūpā sā praṣṭrī tāvati bhaṇyate svayam evam vibodhaḥ ca tathā praśna uttara ātmakaḥ guru śiṣya pade pyeṣa dehabhedaḥ  hi atāt tvikaḥ bodhaḥ  hi bodha rūpa tvāt antar nāna ākṛtīḥ sthitāḥ bahis ābhāsayati eva drāc sāmānya viśeṣataḥ srakṣyamāṇa viśeṣa aṃśāka aṃkṣā yogyasya kasyacid  dharmasya sṛṣṭiḥ sāmānya sṛṣṭiḥ sā saṃśaya ātmikā srakṣyamāṇaḥ  viśeṣa aṃśaḥ  yadā tu uparamet tadā nirṇayaḥ  mātṛ rucitaḥ  na anyathā kalpa koṭibhiḥ tasya atha vastunaḥ sva ātma vīrya ākramaṇa pāṭavāt  unmudraṇam tayā ākṛtyā lakṣaṇa uttara nirṇayāḥ nirṇīta tāvat dharma aṃśa pṛṣṭha pāti tayā punar  bhūyaḥ bhūyas  samuddeśa lakṣaṇa ātma parīkṣaṇam dṛṣṭa anumāna aupamya āpta vacana ādiṣu sarvatas  uddeśa lakṣaṇa avekṣā tritayam prāṇinām sphuret  nirvikalpitam uddeśaḥ  vikalpaḥ  lakṣaṇam punar  parīkṣaṇam tathā adhyakṣe vikalpānām paramparā nagaḥ  yam iti ca uddeśaḥ  dhūmi tvāt agnimān iti lakṣyam vyāpti ādi vijñāna jālam tu atra parīkṣaṇam uddeśaḥ  yam iti prācyaḥ  gaḥ tulyaḥ  gavaya abhidhaḥ iti vā lakṣaṇam śeṣaḥ parīkṣā upamitau bhavet  svar kāma īdṛś uddeśaḥ  yajeta iti asya lakṣaṇam agniṣṭoma ādinā iti eṣā parīkṣā śeṣa vartinī vikalpa srakṣyamāṇa anya rucita aṃśa sahiṣṇunaḥ vastunaḥ  yā tathā tvena sṛṣṭiḥ sa uddeśa saṃjñitā tadā eva saṃvid cinute yāvataḥ srakṣyamāṇa tā yatas  hi akāla kalitā saṃdhatte sārvakālikam srakṣyamāṇasya yā sṛṣṭiḥ prāk sṛṣṭa aṃśasya saṃhṛtiḥ anūdyamāne dharme sā saṃvid lakṣaṇam ucyate tad pṛṣṭhapāti bhūyoṃśa sṛṣṭi saṃhāra viśramāḥ parīkṣā kathyate mātṛ rucitā kalpita avadhiḥ prāc paśyanti atha madhyā anyā vaikharī ca iti tā imāḥ parā parāparā devī caramā tu apara ātmikā icchā ādi śakti tritayam idam eva nigadyate etad prāṇita eva ayam vyavahāraḥ pratāyate etad praśna uttara ātma tve pārameśvara śāsane para saṃbandha rūpa tvam abhisaṃbandha pañcake yathā uktam ratnamālāyām sarvaḥ para kala ātmakaḥ mahān ava antaraḥ  divyaḥ  miśraḥ nyaḥ nyastu pañcamaḥ bhinnayoḥ praṣṭṛ tad vaktroḥ ca aikātmyam yad sa ucyate saṃbandhaḥ para tā ca asya pūrṇa aikātmya prathā mayī anena eva nayena syāt saṃbandha antaram api alam śāstra vācyam phala ādīnām paripūrṇatva yogataḥ ittham saṃvid iyam devī svabhāvāt eva sarvadā uddeśa ādi traya prāṇā sarva śāstra svarūpiṇī tatra ucyate pura uddeśaḥ pūrva jānuja bhedavān vijñāna bhid gata upāyaḥ para upāyaḥ tṛtīyakaḥ śākta upāyaḥ  nara upāyaḥ kāla upāyaḥ  tha saptamaḥ cakra udayaḥ  tha deśa adhvā tattva adhvā tattva bhedanam kalā ādi adhvā adhva upayogaḥ śaktipāta tirohitī dīkṣā upakramaṇam dīkṣā sāmayī pautrike vidhau prameya prakriyā sūkṣmā dīkṣā sadyas samutkramaḥ tulā dīkṣā atha pārokṣī liṅga uddhāraḥ  bhiṣecanam antyeṣṭiḥ śrāddhaklṛptiḥ ca śeṣa vṛtti nirūpaṇam liṅga arcā bahubhid parva pavitra ādi nimitta jam rahasya caryā mantra oghaḥ  maṇḍalam mudrikā vidhiḥ ekīkāraḥ sva svarūpe praveśaḥ śāstra melanam āyāti kathanam śāstra upādeyatva nirūpaṇam iti sapta adhikām ena am triṃśatam yaḥ sadā budhaḥ āhnikānām samabhyasyet  sa sākṣāt bhairavaḥ  bhavet  saptatriṃśatsu saṃpūrṇa bodhaḥ  yad bhairavaḥ  bhavet  kim citram aṇavaḥ  pyasya dṛśā bhairava tām iyuḥ iti eṣa pūrvaja uddeśaḥ kathyate tu anujaḥ  dhunā vijñāna bhid prakaraṇe bharvasya uddeśanam kramāt  dvitīyasmin prakaraṇe gata upāyatva bheditā viśva cit pratibinba tvam parāmarśa udaya kramaḥ mantra ādi abhinna rūpa tvam para upāye vivicyate vikalpa saṃskriyā tarka tattvam guru sa tattvakam yogāṅga anupayogi tvam kalpita arcā ādi anādaraḥ saṃvid cakra udayaḥ  mantra vīrya japya ādi vāstavam niṣedha vidhi tulya tvam śākta upāye tra carcyate buddhi dhyānam prāṇa tattva samuccāraḥ cit ātma tā uccāraḥ para tattva antar praveśa patha lakṣaṇam karaṇam varṇa tattvam ca iti āṇave tu nirūpyate cāra mānam ahorātra saṃkrānti ādi vikalpanam saṃhāra citra tā varṇa udayaḥ kāla adhva kalpane cakrabhid mantra vidyā abhid etad cakra udaye bhavet  parimāṇam purāṇām ca saṃgrahaḥ tattva yojanam etad deśa adhva nirdeśe dvayam tattva adhva nirṇaye kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ ca tattva krama nirūpaṇam vastu dharmaḥ tattva vidhiḥ jāgrat ādi nirūpaṇam pramātṛ bheda iti etad  tattva bhede vicāryate kalā svarūpam eka tri pañca ādyaiḥ tattva kalpanam varṇa bheda kramaḥ sarva ādhāra śakti nirūpaṇam kalā ādi adhva vicāra antaretāvat pravivicyate abheda bhāvanā kampa hāsau tu adhva upayojane saṃkhyā ādhikyam mala ādīnām tattvam śakti vicitra tā anapekṣitva siddhiḥ ca tirobhāva vicitra tā śaktipāta parīkṣāyām etāvān vācya saṃgrahaḥ tirobhāva vyapagamaḥ  jñānena paripūrṇa tā utkrānti anupayogi tvam dīkṣā upakramaṇe sthitam śiṣya aucitya parīkṣā ādau sthāna bhid sthāna kalpanam sāmānya nyāsa bhedaḥ  rgha pātram ca etad prayojanam dravya yogya tvam arcā ca bahis dvāra arcanam kramāt  praveśaḥ  diś svarūpam ca deha prāṇa ādi śodhanam viśeṣa nyāsa vaicitryam sa viśeṣa argha bhājanam deha pūjā prāṇa buddhi citsu adhva nyāsa pūjane anya śāstra gaṇa utkarṣaḥ pūjā cakrasya sarvatas  kṣetra grahaḥ pañcagavyam pūjanam bhū gaṇeśayoḥ astra arcā vahni kāryam ca api adhivāsanam agni gam tarpaṇam caru saṃsiddhiḥ dantakāṣṭha anta saṃskriyā śiva hasta vidhiḥ ca api śayyā klṛpti vicāraṇam svapnasya sāmayam karma samayāḥ ca iti saṃgrahaḥ samayitva vidhau  asmin syāt pañcadaśa āhnike maṇḍala ātma anusandhānam nivedya paśu vistaraḥ agni tṛptiḥ sva svabhāva dīpanam śiṣya deha gaḥ adhva nyāsa vidhiḥ śodhya śodhaka ādi vicitra tā dīkṣā bhedaḥ paraḥ  nyāsaḥ  mantra sattā prayojanam bhedaḥ  yojanikā ādeḥ ca ṣoḍaśe syāt iha āhnike sūtraklṛptiḥ tattva śuddhiḥ pāśa dāhaḥ  tha yojanam adhva bhedaḥ tathā iti evam kathitam pautrike vidhau janana ādi vihīna tvam mantra bhedaḥ  tha su sphuṭaḥ iti saṃkṣipta dīkṣā ākhye syāt aṣṭādaśa āhnike kalā avekṣā kṛpāṇi ādi nyāsaḥ cāraḥ śarīra gaḥ brahma vidyā vidhiḥ ca evam uktam sadyas samutkrame adhikāra parīkṣā antar saṃskāraḥ  tha tulā vidhiḥ iti etad vācya sarva svam syāt viṃśatitama āhnike mṛta jīvadvidhiḥ jālaḥ  padeśaḥ saṃskriyā gaṇaḥ bala abala vicāraḥ ca iti ekaviṃśa āhnike vidhiḥ śravaṇam ca abhyanujñānam śodhanam pātaka cyutiḥ śaṅkā ā  cheda iti spaṣṭam vācyam liṅga uddhṛti krame parīkṣā ācārya karaṇam tad vratam haraṇam mateḥ tad vibhāgaḥ sādhaka tvam abhiṣeka vidhau tu iyat  adhikārī atha saṃskāraḥ tad prayojanam iti adaḥ caturviṃśe ntyayāga ākhye vaktavyam paricarcyate prayojanam bhoga mokṣa dānena atra vidhiḥ sphuṭaḥ pañcaviṃśa āhnike śrāddha prakāśe vastu saṃgrahaḥ prayojanam śeṣa vṛtteḥ nitya arcā sthaṇḍile parā liṅga svarūpam bahudhā ca akṣa sūtra nirūpaṇam pūjā bheda iti vācyam liṅga arcā saṃprakāśane naimittika vibhāgaḥ tad prayojana vidhiḥ tatas  parva bhedāḥ tad viśeṣaḥ cakra carcā tad arcanam guru ādi anta dina ādi arcā prayojana nirūpaṇam mṛteḥ parīkṣā yogi īśī melaka ādi vidhiḥ tathā vyākhyā vidhiḥ śruta vidhiḥ guru pūjā vidhiḥ tu iyat  naimittika prakāśa ākhye pyaṣṭāviṃśa āhnike sthitam adhikāryātmanaḥ  bhedaḥ siddha patnī kula kramaḥ arcā vidhiḥ dauta vidhī rahasya upaniṣad kramaḥ dīkṣā abhiṣekau bodhaḥ ca iti ekonatriṃśa āhnike mantra svarūpam tad vīryam iti triṃśe nirūpitam śūla abja bhedaḥ  vyomaśasvastika ādi nirūpaṇam vistareṇa abhidhātavyam iti ekatriṃśa āhnike guṇa pradhāna tā bhedāḥ svarūpam vīrya carcanam kalā bheda iti proktam mudrāṇām saṃprakāśane dvātriṃśa tattvāt īśa ākhyāt prabhṛti prasphuṭaḥ  yatas  na bhedaḥ  sti tatas  na uktam uddeśa antaram atra tad  mukhya tvena ca vedya tvāt adhikāra antara kramaḥ iti uddeśa vidhiḥ proktaḥ sukha saṃgraha hetave atha asya lakṣaṇa avekṣe nirūpyete yathākramam ātmā saṃvid prakāśa sthitiḥ anavayavā saṃvid iti ātta śakti vrātam tasya svarūpam sa ca nija mahasaḥ chādanāt baddha rūpaḥ ātma jyotiḥ svabhāva prakaṭana vidhinā tasya mokṣaḥ sa ca ayam citra ākārasya citraḥ prakaṭita iha yad saṃgraheṇa artha  eṣaḥ mithyājñānam timiram asamān dṛṣṭi doṣān prasūte tad sadbhāvāt vimalam api tad bhāti mālinya dhāma yad tu prekṣyam dṛśi parigatam taimirīm doṣa mudrām dūram runddhet prabhavatu katham tatra mālinya śaṅkā bhāva vrātaḷ haṭhāt janasya hṛdayāni ākramya yad nartayan bhaṅgībhiḥ vividhābhiḥ ātma hṛdayam pracchādya saṃkrīḍase yaḥ tvām āha jaḍam jaḍaḥ sahṛdayaṃmanyatva duḥśikṣitaḥ  manye muṣya jaḍa ātma tā stuti padam tvad sāmya saṃbhāvanāt iha galita malāḥ parāvara jñāḥ śiva sadbhāva mayā adhikriyante guravaḥ pravicāraṇe yatas tad viphalā dveṣa kalaṃka hāni yācñā  ai tantrāloke bhinavara cite mutra vijñāna sattā bheda udgāra prakaṭana paṭa āvāhnike smin samāptiḥ  ch atha śrī tantra ālokasya dvitīyam āhnikam yad tatra ādyam padam avirata anuttara jñapti rūpam tad nirṇetum prakaraṇam idam ārabhe ham dvitīyam anupāyam hi yad rūpam kaḥ  rthaḥ  deśana yātra vai sakṛt syāt deśanā paścāt anupāya tvam ucyayate anupāyam idam tattvam iti upāyam vinā kutas  svayam tu teṣām tad tādṛś  kim brūmaḥ kila tān prati yad caturdhā uditam rūpam vijñānasya vibhoḥ asau svabhāva eva mantavyaḥ sa hi nitya uditaḥ  vibhuḥ etāvadbhiḥ asaṃkhyātaiḥ svabhāvaiḥ yad prakāśate ke pi aṃśa aṃśikayā tena viśanti anye niraṃśataḥ tatra api ca abhyupāya ādi sāpekṣa anyatva yogataḥ upāyasya api naḥ vāryā tad anya tvāt vicitra tā tatra ye nirmala ātmānaḥ  bhairavīyām sva saṃvidam nirupāyām upāsīnāḥ tad vidhiḥ praṇigadyate tatra tāvat kriyā yogaḥ  na abhyupāya tvam arhati sa hi tasmāt samudbhūtaḥ pratyuta pravibhāvyate jñaptau  upāya eva syāt iti ced jñaptiḥ ucyate prakāśa tvam sva prakāśe tad ca tatra anyatas  katham saṃvid tattvam sva prakāśam iti asmin kam nu yuktibhiḥ tad abhāve bhavet viśvam jaḍa tvāt aprakāśakam yāvān upāyaḥ  bāhyaḥ syāt āntaraḥ  vā api kaścana sa sarvaḥ tad mukha prekṣī tatra upāyatva bhāj katham tyaja avadhānāni nanu kva nāma dhatse vadhānam vicinu svayam tad  pūrṇe vadhānam na hi nāma yuktam na āpūrṇam abhyeti ca satyabhāvam tena avadhāna prāṇasya bhāvanā ādeḥ pare pathi bhairavīye kathaṃkāram bhavet sākṣāt upāya tā ye pi sākṣāt upāyena tad rūpam praviviñcate nūnam te sūrya saṃvittyai khadyota ādhitsavaḥ  jaḍāḥ kim ca yāvat idam bāhyam āntara upāya saṃmatam tad prakāśa ātma tā mātram śivasya eva nijam vapuḥ nīlam pītam sukham iti prakāśaḥ kevalaḥ śivaḥ amuṣmin parama advaite prakāśa ātmani kaḥ  paraḥ upāya upeya bhāvaḥ syāt prakāśaḥ kevalam hi saḥ idam dvaitama yam bheda idam advaitam iti api prakāśa vapuḥ eva ayam bhāsate parameśvaraḥ asyām bhūmau sukham duḥkham bandhaḥ mokṣaḥ citarjaḍaḥ ghaṭa kumbhavat eka arthāḥ śabdāḥ te pyekam eva ca praśāśe hi aprakāśa aṃśaḥ katham nāma prakāśatām prakāśamāne tasmin vā tad dvaitāḥ tasya lopitāḥ aprakāśe tha tasmin vā vastu tā katham ucyate na prakāśa viśeṣa tvam ata eva upapadyate ata eka prakāśaḥ  yam iti vāde tra susthite dūrāt āvāritāḥ satyam vibhinna jñāna vādinaḥ prakāśa mātram uditam aprakāśa niṣedhanāt eka śabdasya na tu arthaḥ saṃkhyā cit vyakti bheda bhāj  na eṣa śaktiḥ mahādevī na paratra āśritaḥ  yatas  na ca eṣa śaktimān devaḥ  na kasya api āśrayaḥ  yatas  na eṣa dhyeyaḥ  dhyātṛ abhāvāt na dhyātā dhyeya varjanāt  na pūjyaḥ pūjaka abhāvāt pūjya abhāvāt na pūjakaḥ na mantraḥ  na ca mantryaḥ  sau na ca mantrayitā prabhuḥ na dīkṣā dīkṣakaḥ  vā api na dīkṣāvān maheśvaraḥ sthāna āsana nirodha argha saṃghānāvāhana ādikam visarjana antam na asti atra kartṛ karma kriyā ujjhite na sanna ca asat sat asat na ca tad na ubhaya ujjhitam durvijñeyā hi sā avasthā kim api etad anuttaram ayam iti avabhāsaḥ  hi yaḥ  bhāvaḥ vacchidātmakaḥ sa eva ghaṭavat loke san  tathā na eṣa bhairavaḥ asattvam ca aprakāśa tvam na kutra api upayogi tā viśvasya jīvitam satyam prakāśa eka ātmakaḥ ca saḥ ābhyām eva tu hetubhyām na dvi ātmā na dvaya ujjhitaḥ sarva ātmanā hi bhāti eṣa kena rūpeṇa mantryatām śrīmat triśirasi proktam para jñāna svarūpakam śaktyā garbha antar vartinyā śakti garbha param padam na bhāvaḥ na api abhāvaḥ  na dvayam vācām agocarāt  akathya padavīrūḍham śakti stham śakti varjitam iti ye rūḍha saṃvitti parama artha pavitritāḥ anuttara pathe rūḍhāḥ te bhyupāyāniyantritāḥ teṣām idam samābhāti sarvatas  bhāva maṇḍalam puras stham eva saṃvitti bhairava agni vilāpitam eteṣām sukha duḥkha aṃśa śaṃkā taṃka vikalpanāḥ nirvikalpa para āveśa mātra śeṣa tvam āgatāḥ eṣām na mantraḥ  na dhyānam na pūjā na api kalpanā na samayi ādika ācārya paryantaḥ kaḥ  pi viśramaḥ samasta yantraṇā tantra troṭanā ṭaṃka dharmiṇaḥ na anugrahāt param kiṃcid śeṣa vṛttau prayojanam svam kartavyam kim api kalayan  loke  eṣa prayatnāt na u pārārthyam prati ghaṭayate kāṃcana sva pravṛttim yaḥ tu dhvasta akhila bhava malaḥ  bhairavībhāva pūrṇaḥ kṛtyam tasya sphuṭam idam iyat loka kartavya mātram tam ye paśyanti tādrūpya krameṇa amala saṃvidaḥ te pi tad rūpiṇaḥ tāvatī eva asya anugraha ātma tā etad tattva parijñānam mukhyam yāga ādi kathyate dīkṣā antam vibhunā śrīmat siddhayogīśvarīmate sthaṇḍilāt uttaram tūram tūrāt uttaratas  paṭaḥ paṭāt dhyānam tatas  dhyeyam tatas  syāt dhāraṇa uttarā tatas  pi yoga jam rūpam tatas  pi jñānam uttaram jñānena hi mahā siddhaḥ  bhavet yogi īśvaraḥ tu iti saḥ  pi svātantrya dhāmnā ced api anirmala saṃvidām anugraham cikīrṣuḥ tad bhāvinam vidhim āśrayet  anugrāhya anusāreṇa vicitraḥ sa ca kathyate parāpara ādi upāya ogha saṃkīrṇatva vibhedataḥ tad artham eva ca asya api parameśvara rūpiṇaḥ tad abhyupāya śāstra ādi śravaṇa adhyayana ādaraḥ na hi tasya svatantrasya kā api kutra api khaṇḍanā na anirmala citaḥ puṃsaḥ nugrahaḥ tu anupāyakaḥ śrīmat ūrmi mahāśāstre siddha saṃtāna rūpake idam uktam tathā śrīmat somānanda ādi daiśikaiḥ guroḥ vākyāt yukti pracaya racanā unmārjana vaśāt samāśvāsāt śāstram prati samuditāt vā api kathitāt  vilīne śaṃkā abhre tdṛdaya gagana udbhāsi mahasaḥ prabhoḥ sūryasya iva spṛśata caraṇān dhvānta jayinaḥ idam anuttara dhāma vivecakam vigalita aupayikam kṛtam āhnikam  ch śrī tantra ālokasya tṛtīyam āhnikam atha paraupayikam praṇigadyate padam anuttaram eva maheśituḥ b prakāśa mātram yad proktam bhairavīyam param mahaḥ tatra svatantra tā mātram adhikam pravivicyate yaḥ prakāśaḥ sa sarvasya prakāśa tvam prayacchati na ca tad vyatirekī asti viśvam sa dvāvabhāsate atas  sau parameśānaḥ sva ātma vyomani anargalaḥ iyataḥ sṛṣṭi saṃhāra āḍambarasya pradarśakaḥ nirmale makure yadvat bhānti bhūmi jala ādayaḥ amiśrāḥ tadvat ekasmin  cit nāthe viśva vṛttayaḥ sadṛśam bhāti nayana darpaṇa ambara vāriṣu tathā hi nirmale rūpe rūpam eva avabhāsate pracchanna rāgiṇī kānta pratibimbita sundaram darpaṇam kuca kumbhābhyām spṛśanti api na tṛpyati na hi sparśaḥ  sya vimalaḥ  rūpam eva tathā yatas  nairmalyam ca ati niviḍa sajātīya eka saṃgatiḥ svasmin  abhedāt bhinnasya darśana kṣamatā eva yā atyakta sva prakāśasya nairmalyam tad guru uditam nairmalyam mukhyam ekasya saṃvid nāthasya sarvatas  aṃśāṃśikātaḥ kvāpi anyat vimalam tad tad icchayā bhāvānām yad pratīghāti vapuḥ māyā ātmakam hi tad  teṣām eva asti sat vidyā mayam tu apratighātakam tad evam ubhaya ākāram avabhāsam prakāśayan vibhāti vara daḥ  bimba pratibimba dṛśā akhile yaḥ tu āha netra tejāṃsi su acchāt pratiphalanti alam viparyasya svakam vaktram gṛhṇanti iti sa pṛcchyate dehāt anyatra yad tejaḥ tad adhiṣṭhātuḥ ātmanaḥ tena eva tejasā jña tve kaḥ  rthaḥ syāt darpaṇena tu viparyastaiḥ tu tejobhiḥ grāhaka ātma tvam āgataiḥ rūpam dṛśyeta vadane nije na makura antare sva mukhe sparśavat ca etad rūpam bhāyāt mama iti alam na tu asya spṛśya bhinnasya vedya ekānta svarūpiṇaḥ rūpa saṃsthāna mātram tad sparśa gandha rasa ādibhiḥ nyagbhūtaiḥ eva tad yuktam vastu tad pratibimbitam nyagbhāvaḥ  grāhyatā bhāvāt tad abhāvaḥ  pramāṇataḥ sa ca artha saṃgama abhāvāt saḥ pyādarśe nava sthiteḥ ata eva gurutva ādiḥ dharmaḥ  na etasya lakṣyate na hi ādarśe saṃsthitaḥ  sau tad dṛṣṭau sa upāyakaḥ tasmāt tu na eṣa bhedena yad bhāti tatas  ucyate ādhāraḥ tatra tu upāyā dīpa dṛś saṃvidaḥ kramāt  dīpa cakṣuḥ vibodhānām kāṭhinya abhāvataḥ param sarvatas ca api nairmalyān na vibhādarśavat pṛthak etad ca devadevena darśitam bodha vṛddhaye mūḍhānām vastu bhavati tatas  pyanyatra na api alam pratīghāti svatantram naḥ na sthāyi asthāyi ca api na svacchasya eva eṣa kasya api mahimā iti kṛpālunā na deśom naḥ rūpam na ca samaya yogaḥ  na parimā na ca anyonya asaṃgaḥ  na ca tad apahāniḥ na ghana tā na ca avastu tvam syāt na ca kim api sāram nijam iti dhruvam mohaḥ śāmyet iti niradiśat darpaṇa vidhiḥ ittham pradarśite mutra pratibimbana vartmani śabdasya pratibimbam yad  pratiśrutkā iti bhaṇyate na ca asau śabda jaḥ śabda āgacchat tvena saṃśravāt  tena eva vaktrā dūra sthaiḥ śabdasya aśravaṇāt api piṭhira ādi pidhāna aṃśa viśiṣṭa chidra saṃgatau citra tvāt ca asya śabdasya pratibimbam mukha ādivat  idam anyasya vedyasya rūpam iti avabhāsate yathā ādarśe tathā kena api uktam ākarṇaye tu iti niyamāt bimba sāṃmukhyam pratibimbasya yad tatas  tad madhya gāḥ pramātāraḥ śṛṇvanti pratiśabdakam mukhya graham tu api vinā pratibimba grahaḥ  bhavet  sva paścāt stham priyam paśyet ṭaṅkitam mukure vapuḥ sāṃmukhyam ca ucyate tādṛś darpaṇa abheda saṃsthiteḥ atas  kūpa ādi piṭhira ākāśe tad pratibimbitam vaktra ākāśam sa śabdam sat bhāti tad para vaktavat yathā ca ādarśa pāścātya bhāga sthaḥ  vetti naḥ mukham tathā tathāvidha ākāśa paścāt sthaḥ  vetti na dhvanim śabdaḥ  na ca anabhivyaktaḥ pratibimbati tad dhruvam abhivyakti śrutī tasya sama kālam dvitīyake kṣaṇe tu pratibimba tvam śrutiḥ ca sama kālikā tulya kālam hi naḥ hasta tad chāyā rūpa niścayaḥ ittham pradarśite mutra pratibimba sa tattvake prakṛtam brūmahe tatra pratibimbanam arhati śabdaḥ  nabhasi sa ānande sparśa dhāmani sundaraḥ sparśaḥ  nyaḥ pi dṛḍha āghāta śūla śīta ādika udbhavaḥ c para sthaḥ pratibimba tvāt sva deha uddhūlana ākaraḥ na ca eṣa mukhyaḥ tad kārya pāramparya aprakāśanāt evam ghrāṇa antare gandhaḥ  rasaḥ  danta udake sphuṭaḥ yathā ca rūpam pratibimbitam dṛśoḥ na cakṣuṣā anyena vinā hi lakṣyate tathā rasa sparśana saurabha ādikam na lakṣyate kṣeṇa vinā sthitam tu api na ca antare sparśana dhāmani sthitam bahis spṛśaḥ nyākṣa dhiyaḥ sa gocaraḥ atas  ntika stha svaka tādṛś indriya prayojana antaḥkaraṇaiḥ yadā kṛtā tadā tadā attam pratibimbam indriye svakām kriyām sūyata eva tādṛśīm na tu smṛtāt mānasa gocara ādṛtā bhavet kriyā sā kila vartamānataḥ atas  sthitaḥ sparśa varaḥ tad indriye samāgataḥ san viditaḥ tathā akriyaḥ asaṃbhave bāhya gatasya tādṛśaḥ sva  eva tasmin pratibimbitaḥ tathā karoti tām sparśa varaḥ sukha ātmikām sa ca api kasyām api nāḍi saṃtatau tena saṃvittim akure viśvam ātmānam arpayat  nāthasya vadate muṣya vimalām viśva rūpa tām yathā ca gandha rūpa spṛś rasa ādyāḥ pratibimbitāḥ tad ādhāra uparāgeṇa bhānti khaṅge mukha ādivat  tathā viśvam idam bodhe pratibimbitam āśrayet  prakāśatva svatantratva prabhṛtim dharma vistaram yathā ca sarvatas  svacche sphaṭike sarvatas  bhavet  pratibimbam tathā bodhe sarvatas  svaccha tā juṣi atyanta svaccha tā sā yad svākṛtya navabhāsanam atas  svaccha tamaḥ  bodhaḥ  na ratnam tu ākṛti grahāt pratibimbam ca bimbena bāhya sthena samarpyate tasya eva pratibimba tve kim bimbam avaśiṣyatām yad vā api kāraṇam kiṃcid bimba tvena abhiṣicyate tad api pratibimba tvam eti bodhe nyathā tu asat ittham etad sva saṃvitti dṛḍha nyāya astra rakṣitam sāmrājyam eva viśvatra pratibimbasya jṛmbhate nanu bimbasya virahe pratibimbam katham bhavet  kim kurmaḥ  dṛśyate tad hi nanu tad bimbam ucyatām na evam tad lakṣaṇa abhāvāt bimbam kila kim ucyate anyāmiśram svatantram sat bhāsamānam mukham yathā svarūpa anapahānena para rūpa sadṛkṣa tām pratibimba ātma tām āhuḥ khaḍga ādarśa tala ādivat  uktam ca sati bāhye pi dhīḥ eka aneka vedanāt  aneka sadṛśa ākārā na tu aneka iti saugataiḥ nanu ittham pratibimbasya lakṣaṇam kim tad ucyate anya vyāmiśraṇā yogāt tad bheda aśakya bhāsanam c pratibimbam iti prāhuḥ darpaṇe vadanam yathā bodha miśram idam bodhāt bhedena aśakya bhāsanam para tattva ādi bodhe kim pratibimbam na bhaṇyate lakṣaṇasya vyavasthā eṣā akasmāt ced bimbam ucyatām prājñā vastuni yujyante na tu sāmayike dhvanau nanu na pratibimbasya vinā bimbam bhavet sthitiḥ kim tatas  pratibimbe hi bimbam tādātmya vṛtti na atas ca lakṣaṇasya asya proktasya tad asaṃbhave na hāniḥ hetu mātre tu praśnaḥ  yam paryavasyati tatra api ca nimitta ākhye na upādāne kathaṃcana nimitta kāraṇānām ca kadācid kvāpi saṃbhavaḥ ata eva puras vartini āloke smaraṇa ādinā nimittena ghanena astu saṃkrānta dayita ākṛtiḥ anyathā saṃvid ārūḍhā kāntā viccheda yoginī kasmāt bhāti na vai saṃvid  vicchedam puratas  gatā ata eva antaram kiṃcid dhī saṃjñam bhavatu sphuṭam yatra asya vicchidā bhānam saṃkalpa svapna darśane atas  nimittam devasya śaktayaḥ santu tādṛśe ittham viśvam idam nāthe bhairavīya cit ambare c pratibimba m alam svacche na khalu anya prasādataḥ ananya apekṣitā yāsya viśvātma tvam prati prabhoḥ tām parām pratibhām devīm saṃgirante hi anuttarām akulasya asya devasya kula prathana śālinī kaulikī sā parā śaktiḥ aviyuktaḥ  yayā prabhuḥ tayoḥ yadyām alam rūpam sa saṃghaṭṭa iti smṛtaḥ ānanda śaktiḥ sā eva uktā yatas  viśvam visṛjyate parāparāt param tattvam sā eṣā devī nigadyate tad sāram tad ca hṛdayam sa visargaḥ paraḥ prabhuḥ devīyāmala śāstre sā kathitā kālakarṣiṇī mahā ḍāmarake yāge śrī parā mastake tathā śrī pūrvaśāstre sā mātṛsadbhāva tvena varṇitā saṃghaṭṭe smiṃ  cit ātma tvāt yad tad pratyavamarśanam icchā śaktiḥ aghorāṇām śaktīnām sā parā prabhuḥ sā eva prakṣubdha rūpā ced īśitrī saṃprajāyate tadā ghorāḥ parā devyaḥ  jātāḥ śaiva adhva daiśikāḥ sva ātma pratyavam arśaḥ  yaḥ prāk abhūt eka vīrakaḥ jñātavya viśva unmeṣa ātmā jñāna śakti tayā sthitaḥ iyam parāparā devī ghorām yā mātṛ maṇḍalīm sṛjati aviratam śuddha aśuddha mārga eka dīpikām jñeya aṃśaḥ pronmiṣan kṣobham yadā eti balavat tvataḥ ūna tā bhāsanam saṃvid mātra tve jāyate tadā rūḍham tad jñeya vargasya sthiti prārambha ucyate rūḍhiḥ eṣā vibodha abdheḥ citra ākāra parigrahaḥ idam tad bīja saṃdarbha bījam cinvanti yoginaḥ icchā śaktiḥ dvi rūpa uktā kṣubhita akṣubhitā ca yā iṣyamāṇam hi sā vastu dvairūpyeṇa ātmani śrayet  acira dyuti bhāsinyā śaktyā jvalana rūpayā iṣyamāṇa samāpattiḥ sthairyeṇa atha dharā ātmanā unmeṣa śaktau  asti etad jñeyam yadi api bhūyasā tathā api vibhava sthānam sā na tu prācya janma bhūḥ icchā śakteḥ atas  prāhuḥ cātū rūpyam para amṛtam kṣobha antarasya asadbhāvāt na idam bījam ca kasyacid  prakṣobhaka tvam bīja tvam kṣobha ādhāraḥ ca yoni tā kṣobhakam saṃvidaḥ  rūpam kṣubhyati kṣobhayati api kṣobhaḥ syāt jñeya dharma tvam kṣobhaṇā tad bahiṣkṛtiḥ antar stha viśva abhinna eka bīja aṃśa visisṛkṣu tā kṣobhaḥ  tad icche tattva icchā bhāsanam kṣobhaṇām viduḥ yad aikya āpattim āsādya tad icchā kṛtinī bhavet  kṣobha ādhāram imam prāhuḥ śrī somānanda putrakāḥ saṃvidām īṣaṇā ādīnām anudbhinna viśeṣakam yad jñeya mātram tad bījam yad yogāt bīja tā svare tasya bījasya sā eva uktā visisṛkṣā ya udbhavaḥ c yatas  grāhyam idam bhāsyat bhinna kalpam cit ātmanaḥ eṣa kṣobhaḥ kṣobhaṇā tu tūṣṇīṃbhūta anya mātṛ gam haṭhāt yad audāsīnya aṃśa cyāvanam saṃvidaḥ  balāt  jātā api visisṛkṣā asau yad vimarśa antar aikyataḥ kṛtārthā jāyate kṣobha ādhāraḥ  traitat prakīrtitam tatas tadā antaram jñeyam bhinna kalpa tvam icchati viśva bījāt atas  sarva bāhyam bimbam vivartsyati kṣobhya kṣobhaka bhāvasya sa tattvam darśitam mayā śrīmat maheśvareṇa uktam guruṇā yad prasādataḥ prakṛtam brūmahe na idam bījam varṇa catuṣṭayam na api yoniḥ yatas  na etad kṣobha ādhāra tvam ṛcchati ātmani eva ca viśrāntyā tad proktam amṛta ātmakam ittham prāk uditam yad tad pañcakam tad parasparam ucchalat vividha ākāram anyonya vyatimiśraṇāt  yaḥ  nuttaraḥ paraḥ spandaḥ  yaḥ ca ānandaḥ samucchalan tau  icchā unmeṣa saṃghaṭṭāt gacchataḥ  tivicitra tām anuttara ānanda citī icchā śaktau niyojite trikoṇam iti tad prāhuḥ visarga āmoda sundaram anuttara ānanda śaktī tatra rūḍhim upāgate trikoṇa dvitva yogena vrajataḥ ṣaṣ ara sthitim ta eva unmeṣa yoge pi punar tad maya tām gate kriyāśakteḥ sphuṭam rūpam abhivyaṅktaḥ parasparam icchā unmeṣa gataḥ kṣobhaḥ  yaḥ proktaḥ tad gateḥ api te eva śaktī tādrūpya bhāginyau na anyathā sthite nanu anuttara tā ānandau sva ātmanā bheda varjitau katham etāvatīm enām vaicitrīm sva ātmani śritau śṛṇu tāvat ayam saṃvid nāthaḥ  parimita ātmakaḥ ananta śakti vaicitrya laya udaya kaleśvaraḥ asthāsyat eka rūpeṇa vapuṣā ced maheśvaraḥ maheśvara tvam saṃvid tvam tad atyakṣyat dhaṭa ādivat  paricchinna prakāśa tvam jaḍasya kila lakṣaṇam jaḍāt vilakṣaṇaḥ  bodhaḥ  yatas  na parimīyate tena bodha mahasindhorullāsinyaḥ sva śaktayaḥ āśrayanti ūrmaya iva sva ātma saṃghaṭṭa citra tām sva ātma saṃghaṭṭa vaicitryam śaktīnām yad parasparam etad eva param prāhuḥ kriyāśakteḥ sphuṭam vapuḥ asmin  caturdaśe dhāmni sphuṭībhūta tri śaktike triśūla tvam atas  prāha śāstā śrī pūrvaśāsane nirañjanam idam ca uktam gurubhiḥ tattva darśibhiḥ śaktimān añjyate yasmāt na śaktiḥ jātu kenacid  icchā jñānam kriyā ca iti yad pṛthak pṛthak añjyate tad eva śaktimat svaiḥ svaiḥ iṣyamāṇa ādikaiḥ sphuṭam etad tritayam aikyena yadā tu prasphuret tadā na kenacid upādheyam sva sva vipratiṣedhataḥ lolībhūtam atas  śakti tritayam tad triśūlakam c yasmin  āśu samāveśāt bhavet yogī nirañjanaḥ ittham para amṛta padāt ārabhya aṣṭakam īdṛśam brāhmī ādi rūpa saṃbhedāt yāti aṣṭa aṣṭaka tām sphuṭam atra anuttara śaktiḥ sā svam vapuḥ prakaṭa sthitam kurvanti api jñeya kalā kāluṣyāt vindu rūpiṇī uditāyām kriyāśaktau soma sūrya agni dhāmani avibhāgaḥ prakāśaḥ  yaḥ sa binduḥ paramaḥ  hi naḥ tattva rakṣā vidhāne ca tad uktam parameśinā hṛd padma maṇḍala antar sthaḥ  nara śakti śiva ātmakaḥ boddhavyaḥ  laya bhedena vinduḥ vimala tārakaḥ yaḥ  sau nāda ātmakaḥ śabdaḥ sarva prāṇiṣu avasthitaḥ adha u ūrdhva vibhāgena niṣkriyeṇa avatiṣṭhate hlāda taikṣṇya ādi vaicitryam sita rakta ādikam ca yad  svayam tad nirapekṣaḥ  sau prakāśaḥ  guruḥ āha ca yad na sūryaḥ  na vā somaḥ  na agniḥ bhāsayate pi ca na ca arka soma vahnīnām tad prakāśāt vinā mahaḥ kim api asti nijam kim tu saṃvid ittham prakāśate sva svātantrya prabhāva udyat vicitra upādhi saṃgataḥ prakāśaḥ  yāti taikṣṇya ādim avāntara vicitra tām durdarśanaḥ  pi gharmāṃśuḥ patitaḥ pāthasām pathi netra ānanda tvam abhyeti paśya upādheḥ prabhāvitām sūrya ādiṣu prakāśaḥ  sau  upādhi kaluṣīkṛtaḥ saṃvid prakāśam māheśam ata eva hi apekṣate prakāśa mātram su vyaktam sūrya iti ucyate sphuṭam prakāśya vastu sāra aṃśa varṣi tad soma ucyate sūrya pramāṇam iti āhuḥ somam meyam pracakṣate anyonyam aviyuktau tau svatantrau  api ubhau sthitau bhoktṛ bhogya ubhaya ātmā etad anyonya unmukha tām gatam tatas  jvalana cit rūpam citrabhānuḥ prakīrtitaḥ yaḥ  yam vahneḥ param tattvam pramātuḥ idam eva tad  saṃvid eva tu vijñeya tādātmyāt anapekṣiṇī svatantra tvāt pramātā uktā vicitraḥ  jñeya bhedataḥ soma aṃśa dāhyavaḥ tu uttha vaicitrya ābhāsa bṛṃhitaḥ tatas  eva agniḥ uditaḥ citrabhānuḥ maheśinā jñeya ādi upāya saṃghāta nirapekṣā eva saṃvidaḥ sthitiḥ mātā aham asmi iti jñātā śāstra jñavat yatas  ajña eva yatas  jñāta anubhava ātmā na rūpataḥ na tu sā jñātṛ tā yasyām śuddha jñeya ādi apekṣate tasyām daśāyām jñātṛ tvam ucyate yogyatā vaśāt mānatā eva tu sā prācya pramātṛ parikalpitā ucchalanti api saṃvittiḥ kāla krama vivarjanāt  uditā eva satī pūrṇā mātṛ meya ādi rūpiṇī pāka ādiḥ tu kriyā kāla paricchedāt krama ucitā mata antya kṣaṇa vandhyā api na pāka tvam prapadyate ittham prakāśa tattvasya soma sūrya agni tā sthitā api mukhyam tad prakāśa mātra tvam na vyapohyate eṣām yad prathamam rūpam hrasvam tad sūrya ucyate kṣobha ānanda vaśāt dīrgha viśrāntyā soma ucyate yad tad param plutam nāma soma ānandāt param sthitam prakāśa rūpam tad prāhuḥ āgneyam śāstra kovidāḥ atra prakāśa mātram yad sthite dhāma traye sati uktam vindutayā śāstre śivavinduḥ asau mataḥ makārāt anya eva ayam tad chāyā mātra dhṛt yathā rala hāḥ ṣaṇṭha vaisarga varṇa rūpatva saṃsthitāḥ ikāra eva repha aṃśa  chāyayā anyaḥ  yathā svaraḥ tathā eva maha leśa ādaḥ saḥ  nyaḥ dvedhā svaraḥ  pi san asya antar visisṛkṣā asau yā proktā kaulikī parā sā eva kṣobha vaśāt iti visarga ātmaka tām dhruvam uktam ca triśiraḥśāstre kalā vyāpti anta carcane kalā saptadaśī tasmāt amṛta ākāra rūpiṇī parāpara sva svarūpa bindu gatyā visarpitā prakāśyam sarva vastūnām visarga rahitā tu sā śaktikuṇḍalikā ca eva prāṇakuṇḍalikā tathā visarga prānta deśe tu parā kuṇḍalinī iti ca śiva vyoma iti paramam brahma ātma sthānam ucyate visarga mātram nāthasya sṛṣṭi saṃhāra vibhramāḥ sva ātmanaḥ sva ātmani sva ātma kṣepaḥ  vaisargikī sthitiḥ visarga evam utsṛṣṭa āśyāna tvam upāgataḥ haṃsaḥ prāṇaḥ  vyañjanam ca sparśaḥ ca paribhāṣyate anuttaram param dhāma tad eva ākulam ucyate visargaḥ tasya nāthasya kaulikī śaktiḥ ucyate visarga tā ca sā eva asyā yadānanda udaya kramāt  spaṣṭībhūta kriyā śakti paryantā procchalat sthitiḥ visarga eva tāvān yad ākṣipta etāvat ātmakaḥ iyat rūpam sāgarasya yad ananta ūrmi saṃtatiḥ ata eva visargaḥ  yama vyakta hakala ātmakaḥ kāma tattvam iti śrīmat kula guhvara ucyate yad tad akṣaram avyakta kāntā kaṇṭhe vyavasthitam dhvani rūpam aniccham tu dhyāna dhāraṇa varjitam tatra cittam samādhāya vaśayet yugapad jagat  ata eva visargasya haṃse yadvat sphuṭā sthitiḥ tadvat sa anuttara ādīnām kādi sānta tayā sthitiḥ anuttarāt kavargasya sūtiḥ pañca ātmanaḥ sphuṭam pañca śakti ātmatovaśa eka ekatra yathā sphuṭaḥ icchā śakteḥ sva svarūpa saṃsthāyā eka rūpataḥ cavargaḥ pañca śakti ātmā krama prasphuṭa tā ātmakaḥ yā tu uktā jñeya kāluṣya bhāj kṣi pracara yogataḥ dvi rūpāyāḥ tatas  jātam ṭa ta ādyam varga yugmakam unmeṣāt pādi vargaḥ tu yatas  viśvam samāpyate jñeya rūpam idam pañcaviṃśati antam yatas  sphuṭam jñeya tvāt sphuṭataḥ proktam etāvat sparśa rūpakam icchā śaktiḥ ca yā dvedhā kṣubhita akṣubhita tvataḥ sā vijātīya śakti aṃśa pronmukhī yāti yātma tām sā eva śīghratara upātta jñeya kāluṣya rūṣitā vijātīya unmukha tvena ratvam latvam ca gacchati tadvat unmeṣa śaktiḥ dvi rūpā vaijātya śakti gā vakāra tvam prapadyeta sṛṣṭi sāra pravarṣakam icchā eva anuttara ānanda yātā śīghratva yogataḥ vāyuḥ iti ucyate vahniḥ bhāsanāt sthairyataḥ dharā idam catuṣkam antaḥstham ata eva nigadyate icchā ādi antargata tvena sva samāptau ca saṃsthiteḥ sajātīyaka śaktīnām icchā ādyānām ca yojanam kṣobha ātmakam idam prāhuḥ kṣobha akṣobha ātmanām api anuttarasya sājātye bhavet tu dvitayī gatiḥ anuttaram yad tatra ekam tad ced ānanda sūtaye prabhaviṣyati tad yoge yogaḥ kṣobha ātmakaḥ sphuṭaḥ atra api anuttaram dhāma dvitīyam api sūtaye na paryāptam tadā kṣobham vinā eva anuttara ātma tā icchā yā karmaṇā hīnā yā ca eṣṭavyena rūṣitā śīghra sthairya prabhinnena tridhā bhāvam upāgatā anunmiṣitam unmīlat pronmīlitam iti sthitam iṣyamāṇam tridhā etasyām tādrūpyasya aparicyuteḥ tad eva sva ūṣmaṇā sva ātma svātantrya preraṇa ātmanā bahis bhāvya sphuṭam kṣiptam śa ṣa sa tritayam sthitam tatas  eva sakāre smin sphuṭam viśvam prakāśate amṛtam ca param dhāma yoginaḥ tad pracakṣate kṣobha ādi anta virāmeṣu tad eva ca para amṛtam sītkāra sukha sadbhāva samāveśa samādhiṣu tad eva brahma paramam avibhaktam pracakṣate uvāca bhagavān eva tad śrīmat kula guhkare śakti śaktimat aikātmya labdha anvartha abhidhānake kāka cañcu puṭa ākāram dhyāna dhāraṇa varjitam viṣa tattvam anacka ākhyam tava snehāt prakāśitam kāmasya pūrṇa tā tattvam saṃghaṭṭe pravibhāvyate viṣasya ca amṛtam tattvam chādya tve ṇoḥ cyute sati vyāptrī śaktiḥ viṣam yasmāt avyāptuḥ chādayet mahaḥ nirañjanam param dhāma tattvam tasya tu sa añjanam kriyāśakti ātmakam viśva mayam tasmāt sphuret yatas  icchā kāmaḥ  viṣam jñānam kriyā devī nirañjanam etad traya samāveśaḥ śivaḥ  bhairava ucyate atra rūḍhim sadā kuryāt iti naḥ guravaḥ  jaguḥ viṣa tattve saṃpraviśya na bhūtam na viṣam na ca grahaḥ kevala eva aham iti bhāvanayā sphuret  nanu atra ṣaṇṭha varṇebhyaḥ  janma uktam tena ṣaṇṭha tā katham syāt iti ced brūmaḥ  na atra ṣaṇṭhasya sotṛtā tathā hi tatragā yā asau  icchā śaktiḥ udīritā sā eva sūte sva kartavyam antar stham sva iṣṭa rūpakam yad tu atra rūṣaṇā hetuḥ eṣitavyam sthitam tatas  bhāgān na prasavaḥ tad jam kāluṣyam tad vapuḥ ca tad  jñeya ārūṣaṇayā yuktam samudāya ātmakam viduḥ ṣaṇṭham kṣobhaka tā kṣobha dhāmatva abhāva yogataḥ etad varṇa catuṣkasya sva ūṣmaṇa ābhāsanā vaśāt  ūṣmā iti kathitam nāma bhairaveṇa amala ātmanā kādi ha antam idam prahuḥ kṣobha ādhāra tayā budhāḥ yoni rūpeṇa tasya api yoge kṣobha antaram vrajet  tad nidarśana yogena pañcāśattama varṇa tā pañcaviṃśaka saṃjñeya prāgvat bhūmi su saṃsthitam catuṣkam ca catuṣkam ca bheda abheda gatam kramāt  ādyam catuṣkam saṃvitteḥ bheda saṃdhāna kovidam bhedasya abheda rūḍhi eka hetuḥ anyat catuṣṭayam ittham yad varṇa jātam tad sarva svara mayam purā vyakti yogāt vyañjanam tad svara prāṇam yatas  kila svarāṇām ṣaṭkam eva iha mūlam syāt varṇa saṃtatau ṣaṣ devatāḥ tu tā eva ye mukhyāḥ sūrya raśmayaḥ saurāṇām eva raśmīnām antar cāndrakalā yatas  atas  tra dīrgha tritayam sphuṭam cāndramasam vapuḥ candraḥ ca nāma na eva anyaḥ  bhogyam bhoktuḥ ca na aparam bhoktā eva bhogya bhāvena dvaividhyāt saṃvyavasthitaḥ ghaṭasya na hi bhogya tvam svam vapuḥ mātṛ gam hi tad  atas  mātari yā rūḍhiḥ sā asya bhogya tvam ucyate anuttaram parāmṛśya parāmarśaka bhāvataḥ saṃghaṭṭa rūpa tām prāptam bhogyam icchā ādikam tathā anuttara ānanda bhuvām icchā ādye bhogya tām gate saṃdhi akṣarāṇām udayaḥ  bhoktṛ rūpam ca kathyate anuttara ānandam ayaḥ  devaḥ  bhoktā eva kathyate icchā ādikam bhogyam eva tatas  eva asya śakti tā bhogyam bhoktari līnam ced  bhoktā tad vastutas  sphuṭaḥ atas  ṣaṇṇām trikam sāram cit iṣi unmeṣaṇa ātmakam tad eva tritayam prāhuḥ bhairavasya param mahaḥ tad trikam parameśasya pūrṇā śaktiḥ pragīyate tena ākṣiptam yatas  viśvamatas  smin samupāsite viśva śaktau  avaccheda vandhye jātam upāsanam iti eṣa mahimā etāvān iti tāvat na śakyate aparicchinna śakteḥ kaḥ kuryāt śakti paricchidām tasmāt anuttaraḥ  devaḥ svācchandya anuttara tvataḥ visarga śakti yukta tvāt saṃpannaḥ  viśvarūpakaḥ evam pañcāśat āmarśa pūrṇa śaktiḥ maheśvaraḥ vimarśa ātmā eka eva anyāḥ śaktayaḥ traiva niṣṭhitāḥ ekāśīti padā devī hi atra antar bhāvayiṣyate eka āmarśa svabhāva tve śabdarāśiḥ sa bhairavaḥ āmṛśya  chāyayā yogāt sa eva śaktiḥ ca mātṛkā sā śabda rāśi saṃghaṭṭāt bhinna yoniḥ tu mālinī prāgvat nava tayā āmarśāt pṛthak varga svarūpiṇī ekaika āmarśa rūḍhau tu sā eva pañcāśat ātmikā ittham nāda anuvedhena parāmarśa svabhāvakaḥ śivaḥ  mātā pitṛ tvena kartā viśvatra saṃsthitaḥ visarga eva śāktaḥ  yam śiva bindu tayā punar  garbhīkṛta ananta viśvaḥ śrayate nuttara ātma tām aparicchinna viśva antar sāre sva ātmani yaḥ prabhoḥ parāmarśaḥ sa eva uktaḥ  dvaya saṃpatti lakṣaṇaḥ anuttara visarga ātma śiva śakti advaya ātmani parāmarśaḥ  nirbhara tvāt aham iti ucyate vibhoḥ anuttara ādyā prasṛtiḥ ha antā śakti svarūpiṇī pratyāhṛta aśeṣa viśva anuttare sā nilīyate tad idam viśvam antaḥstham śaktau sā anuttare pare tad tasyām iti yad satyam vibhunā saṃpuṭīkṛtiḥ tena śrī trīśikā śāstre śakteḥ saṃpuṭita ākṛtiḥ saṃvittau bhāti yad viśvam tatra api khalu saṃvidā tad etad tritayam dvandva yogāt saṃghāta tām gatam ekam eva param rūpam bhairavasya aham ātmakam visarga śaktiḥ yā śaṃbhoḥ sa ittham sarvatra vartate tatas  eva samastaḥ  yama ānanda rasa vibhramaḥ tathā hi madhure gīte sparśe vā candana ādike mādhyasthya vigame yā asau hṛdaye spandamāna tā ānanda śaktiḥ sā eva uktā yatas  sahṛdayaḥ  janaḥ pūrva visṛjya sakalam kartavyam śūnyatā anale citta viśrānti saṃjñaḥ  yamāṇavaḥ tad anantaram dṛṣṭa śruta ādi tad vastu pronmukha tvam sva saṃvidi citta saṃbodha nāmā uktaḥ śākta ullāsa bhara ātmakaḥ tatra unmukhatva tad vastu saṃghaṭṭāt vastunaḥ  hṛdi rūḍheḥ pūrṇa tayā āveśāt mita citta layāt śive prāgvat bhaviṣyat aunmukhya saṃbhāvya mitatālayāt citta pralaya nāmā asau visargaḥ śāmbhavaḥ paraḥ tattva rakṣā vidhāne taḥ visarga traidham ucyate hṛd padma kośa madhya sthaḥ tayoḥ saṃghaṭṭa iṣyate visargaḥ  ntaḥ sa ca proktaḥ citta viśrānti lakṣaṇaḥ dvitīyaḥ sa visargaḥ tu citta saṃbodha lakṣaṇaḥ ekībhūtam vibhāti atra jagat etad carācaram grāhya grāhaka bhedaḥ  vai kiṃcid atra iṣyate yadā tadā asau sakalaḥ proktaḥ  niṣkalaḥ śiva yogataḥ grāhya grāhaka vicchitti saṃpūrṇa grahaṇa ātmakaḥ tṛtīyaḥ sa visargaḥ tu citta pralaya lakṣaṇaḥ ekībhāva ātmakaḥ sūkṣmaḥ  vijñāna ātmā ātma nirvṛtaḥ nirūpitaḥ  yam arthaḥ śrī siddhayogīśvarīmate sā atra kuṇḍalinī bījam jīva bhūtā cidātmikā tad jam dhruva icchā unmeṣa ākhyam trikam varṇāḥ tatas  punar  ā iti avarṇāt ityādi yāvat vaisargikī kalā kakāra ādi sakāra antā visargāt pañcadhā sa ca bahis ca antar ca hṛdaye nāde tha parame pade binduḥ ātmani mūrdha antam hṛdayāt vyāpakaḥ  hi saḥ ādimāntya vihīnāḥ tu mantrāḥ syuḥ śarad abhravat  guroḥ lakṣaṇam etāvat ādimāntyam ca vedayet  pūjyaḥ saḥ  ham iva jñānī bhairavaḥ  devatā ātmakaḥ śloka gātha ādi yad kiṃcid ādimāntya yutam tatas  tasmāt vidan  tathā sarvam mantra tvena eva paśyati visarga śaktiḥ viśvasya kāraṇam ca nirūpitā aitareya ākhya vedānte parameśena vistarāt  yad lohitam tad agniḥ yad vīryam sūrya indu vigraham iti brahma paramam tad saṃghaṭṭa udaya ātmakam tasya api ca param vīrya pañcabhūta kalā ātmakam bhogya tvena anna rūpam ca śabda sparśa rasa ātmakam śabdaḥ  pi madhuraḥ  yasmāt vīrya upacaya kārakaḥ tad hi vīryam param śuddham visisṛkṣā ātmakam matam tad balam ca tad ojaḥ ca te prāṇāḥ sā ca kānta tā tasmāt vīryāt prajāḥ tāḥ ca vīrya karmasu kathyate yajña ādikeṣu tad vṛṣṭau sauṣadhīṣu atha tāḥ punar  vīrye tad ca prajāsu evam visarge viśva rūpa tā śabdarāśiḥ sa eva uktaḥ  mātṛkā sā ca kīrtitā kṣobhya kṣobhaka tā āveśāt mālinīm tām pracakṣate bīja yoni samāpatti visarga udaya sundarā mālinī hi parā śaktiḥ nirṇītā viśva rūpiṇī eṣā vastuta ekā eva parā kālasya karṣiṇī śaktimat bheda yogena yāmala tvam prapadyate tasya pratyavam arśaḥ  yaḥ paripūrṇaḥ  hama ātmakaḥ sa sva ātmani svatantra tvāt vibhāgam avabhāsayet vibhāga ābhāsane ca asya tridhā vapuḥ udāhṛtam paśyantī madhyamā sthūlā vaikharī iti abhiśabditam tāsām api tridhā rūpam sthūla sūkṣma para tvataḥ tatra yā svara sandarbha subhagā nāda rūpiṇī sā sthūlā khalu paśyantī varṇa ādyapravibhāgataḥ avibhāga eka rūpa tvam mādhuryam śaktiḥ ucyate sthāna vāyu ādi gharṣa utthā sphuṭa tā eva ca pāruṣī tad asyām nāda rūpāyām saṃvid savidha vṛttitaḥ sājātya antar ma[ttama] yībhūtiḥ jhaj iti eva upalabhyate yeṣām na tanmayībhūtiḥ te deha ādi nimajjanam avidantaḥ  magna saṃvid mānāḥ tu ahṛdayā iti yad tu carma avanaddha ādi kiṃcid tatra eṣa yaḥ  dhvaniḥ sa sphuṭa asphuṭa rūpa tvāt madhyamā sthūla rūpiṇī madhyāyāḥ ca avibhāga aṃśa sadbhāva iti rakta tā avibhāga svara mayī yatra syāt tad surañjakam avibhāgaḥ  hi nirvṛtyai dṛśyatām tāla pāṭhataḥ kila avyakta dhvanau tasmin vādane parituṣyati yā tu sphuṭānām varṇānām utpattau kāraṇam bhavet  sā sthūlā vaikharī yasyāḥ kāryam vākya ādi bhūyasā asmin sthūla traye yad tad anusandhānam ādivat  pṛthak pṛthak tad tritayam sūkṣmam iti abhiśabdyate ṣaṣ jam karomi madhuram vādayāmi bruve vacaḥ pṛthak eva anusandhāna trayam saṃvedyate kila etasya api trayasya ādyam yadrupam anupādhimat tad param tritayam tatra śivaḥ para cit ātmakaḥ vibhāga ābhāsanāyām ca mukhyāḥ tisraḥ  tra śaktayaḥ anuttarā para icchā ca parāpara tayā sthitā unmeṣa śaktiḥ jñāna ākhyā tu aparā iti nigadyate kṣobha rūpāt punar tāsā muktāḥ ṣaḍ  saṃvidaḥ  malāḥ āsām eva samāveśāt kriyā śakti tayā uditāt  saṃvidaḥ  dvādaśa proktā yāsu sarvam samāpyate etāvat devadevasya mukhyam tad śakti cakrakam etāvatā devadevaḥ pūrṇa śaktiḥ sa bhairavaḥ parāmarśa ātmaka tvena visarga ākṣepa yogataḥ iyattā kalanāt jñānāt tāḥ proktāḥ kālikāḥ kvacid  śrī sāraśāstre ca api uktam madhya eka akṣarām parām pūjayet bhairava ātmā ākhyām yoginī dvādaśa āvṛtām tābhya eva catuḥṣaṣṭi paryantam śakti cakrakam ekārataḥ samārabhya sahasrāram pravartate tāsām ca kṛtya bhedena nāmāni bahudhā āgame upāsāḥ ca dvayāt vaitavya amiśra ākāra yogataḥ śrīmat traiśirame tad ca kathitam vistarāt bahu iha naḥ likhitam vyāsa bhayāt ca anupayogataḥ tā eva nirmalāḥ śuddhā aghorāḥ parikīrtitāḥ ghora ghoratarāṇām tu sotṛ tvāt ca tad ātmikāḥ sṛṣṭau sthitau ca saṃhāre tad upādhi traya atyaye tāsām eva sthitam rūpam bahudhā pravibhajyate upādhi atītam yad rūpam tad dvidhā guravaḥ  jaguḥ anullāsāt upādhīnām yad vā praśama yogataḥ praśamaḥ ca dvidhā śāntyā haṭha pāka krameṇa tu alam grāsa rasa ākhyena satatam jvalana ātmanā haṭha pāka praśamanam yad tṛtīyam tad eva ca c upadeśāya yujyeta bheda indhana vidāhakam nija bodha jaṭhara hutabhuji bhāvāḥ sarve samarpitā haṭhataḥ vijahati bheda vibhāgam nija śaktyā tam samindhānāḥ haṭha pākena bhāvānām rūpe bhinne vilāpite aśnanti amṛtasāt bhūtam viśvam saṃvitti devatāḥ tāḥ tṛptāḥ sva ātmanaḥ pūrṇa hṛdaya ekānta śāyinam cit vyoma bhairavam devam abhedena adhiśerate evam kṛtya kriyā āveśān nāma upāsāba hutvataḥ āsām bahuvidham rūpam abhede pyavabhāsate āsām eva ca devīnām āvāpa udvāpa yogataḥ eka dvi tri catuṣpañca ṣaṣ sapta aṣṭa nava uttaraiḥ rudrārkānya kalāsena aprabhṛtiḥ bheda vistaraḥ alam anyena bahunā prakṛte tha niyujyate saṃvid ātmani viśvaḥ yam bhāva vargaḥ prapañcavān pratibimba tayā bhāti yasya viśveśvaraḥ  hi saḥ evam ātmani yasya īdṛś avikalpaḥ sadā udayaḥ parāmarśaḥ sa eva asau śāṃbhava upāya mudritaḥ pūrṇāhanta aparām arśaḥ  yaḥ  syāyam pravivecitaḥ mantra mudrā kriyā upāsāḥ tad anyā na atra kāścana bhūyas bhūyas  samāveśam nirvikalpam imam śritaḥ abhyeti bhairavībhāvam jīvanmukti apara abhidham ita eva prabhṛti eṣā jīvanmuktiḥ vicāryate yatra sūtraṇayā api iyam upāya upeya kalpanā prāktane tu āhnike kācid bhedasya kalanā api naḥ tena anupāye tasmin kaḥ  mucyate vā katham kutas  nirvikalpe parāmarśe śāmbhavopāya nāmani pañcāśat bheda tām pūrva sūtritām yojayet budhaḥ dharām eva avikalpena sva ātmani pratibimbitām paśyan bhairava tām yāti jala ādiṣu api ayam vidhiḥ yāvat ante param tattvam samasta āvaraṇa ūrdhva gam vyāpi svatantram sarvajñam yad śivam parikalpitam tad api akalpita udāra saṃvid darpaṇa bimbitam paśyan vikalpa vikalaḥ  bhairavībhavati svayam yathā raktam puras  paśyat nirvikalpaka saṃvidā tad tad dvāra niraṃśa eka ghaṭa saṃvitti su sthitaḥ tadvat hara ādika ekaika saṃghāta samudāyataḥ parāmṛśan svam ātmānam pūrṇa eva avabhāsate matta eva uditam idam mayi eva pratibimbitam mada bhinnam idam ca iti tridhā upāyaḥ sa śāmbhavaḥ sṛṣṭeḥ sthiteḥ saṃhṛteḥ ca tad etad sūtraṇam kṛtam yatra sthitam yatas ca iti tad āha spandaśāsane etāvatā eva hi aiśvarya saṃvidaḥ khyāpitam param viśva ātmaka tvam ca iti anyat lakṣaṇam kim nu kathyatām sva ātmani eva cit ākāśe viśvam asmi avabhāsayan sraṣṭā viśvātmaka iti prathayā bhairava ātma tā ṣaḍadhva jātam nikhilam mayi eva pratibimbitam sthiti kartā aham asmi iti sphuṭeyam viśva rūpa tā sadā udita mahā bodha jvālā jaṭila tā ātmani viśvam dravati mayi etad iti paśyan praśāmyati ananta citra sat garbha saṃsāra svapna sadmanaḥ ploṣakaḥ śiva eva aham iti ullāsī hutāśanaḥ jagat sarvam mattaḥ prabhavati vibhedena bahudhā tathā api etad rūḍham mayi vigalite tu atra na paraḥ tad ittham yaḥ sṛṣṭi sthiti vilaya bhekīkṛti vaśāt anaṃśam paśyet sa sphurati hi turīyam pad bhitaḥ tad asmin parama upāye śāmbhavā dvaita śālini ke pyeva yānti viśvāsam pasma īśena bhāvitāḥ snānam vratam deha śuddhiḥ dhāraṇā mantra yojanā adhvaklṛptiḥ yāga vidhiḥ homa japya samādhayaḥ ityādi kalpanā kā api na atra bhedena yujyate para anugraha kāri tvam atra sthasya sphuṭam sthitam yadi tādṛś anugrāhyaḥ  daiśikasya upasarpati atha asau tādṛśaḥ  na syāt bhava bhaktyā ca bhāvitaḥ tam ca ārādhayate bhāvitādṛśa anugraha īritaḥ tadā vicitram dīkṣā ādi vidhim śikṣeta koviṃdaḥ bhāvinyaḥ  pi hi upāsāḥ tāḥ  straiva āyānti niṣṭhitim etad maya tvam paramam prāpyam nirvarṇyateśivam iti kathitam idam su vistaram paramam śāmbhavam ātma vedanam atha śrī tantrāloke caturtham āhnikam atha śāktam upāya maṇḍalam kathayāmaḥ paramātma saṃvide b anantara āhnika ukte smin svabhāve pārameśvare pravivikṣuḥ vikalpasya kuryāt saṃskāram añjasā vikalpaḥ saṃskṛtaḥ sūte vikalpam sva ātma saṃskṛtam sva tulyam saḥ  pi saḥ  pyanyam saḥ  pyanyam sadṛśa ātmakam caturṣu eva vikalpeṣu yaḥ saṃskāraḥ kramāt asau asphuṭaḥ sphuṭa tā bhāvī prasphuṭan sphuṭita ātmakaḥ tatas  sphuṭa taraḥ  yāvat ante sphuṭatamaḥ  bhavet  asphuṭa ādau vikalpe ca bhedaḥ  pyasti antarālikaḥ tatas  sphuṭatama udāra tādrūpya parivṛṃhitā saṃvid abhyeti vimalām avikalpa svarūpa tām atas ca bhairavīyam yad tejaḥ saṃvid svabhāvakam bhūyaḥ bhūyaḥ vimṛśatām jāyate tad sphuṭa ātma tā nanu saṃvid parāmraṣṭrī parāmarśa mayī svatas  parāmṛśyā katham tāthā rūpya sṛṣṭau tu sā jaḍā ucyate sva ātma saṃvittiḥ svabhāvāt eva nirbharā na asyām apāsyam na ādheyam kiṃcid iti uditam purā kim tu durghaṭa kāri tvāt svācchandyāt nirmalāt asau sva ātma pracchādana krīḍā paṇḍitaḥ parameśvaraḥ anāvṛtte svarūpe pi yad ātma ācchādanam vibhoḥ sā eva māyā yatas  bheda etāvān viśvavṛttikaḥ tathā ābhāsanam eva asya dvaitam uktam maheśituḥ tad dvaya apāsanena ayam parāmarśaḥ  bhidhīyate durbheda pādapasya asya mūlam kṛntanti kovidāḥ dhārā ārūḍhena sat tarka kuṭhāreṇa iti niścayaḥ tām enām bhāvanām āhuḥ sarva kāma dughām budhāḥ sphuṭayet vastu yā apetam manaḥ sthapadāt api śrī pūrvaśāstre tad proktam tarkaḥ  yogāṅgam uttamam heya ādi ālocanāt tasmāt tatra yatnaḥ praśasyate mārge cetaḥ sthirībhūtam heye pi viṣaya icchayā prerya tena nayet tāvat yāvat padam anāmayam mārgaḥ  tra mokṣa upāyaḥ sa heyaḥ śāstra antara uditaḥ viṣiṇoti nibadhnāti yā icchā niyati saṃgatam rāga tattvam tayā uktam yad  tena tatra anurajyate yathā sāmrājya saṃbhogam dṛṣṭvā adṛṣṭvā athabā adhame bhoge rajyeta durbuddhiḥ tadvat mokṣe pi rāgataḥ sa eva aṃśaka iti uktaḥ svabhāva ākhyaḥ sa tu sphuṭam siddhi aṅgam iti mokṣāya pratyūha iti kovidāḥ śiva śāsana māhātmyam vidannapyata eva hi vaiṣṇava adhyeṣu rajyeta mūḍhaḥ  rāgeṇa rañjitaḥ yatas tāvati sā tasya vāmā ākhyā śaktiḥ aiśvarī pāñcarātrika vairiñca saugata ādeḥ vijṛmbhate dṛṣṭāḥ sāmrājya saṃbhogam nindantaḥ ke pi vāliśāḥ na tu saṃtoṣataḥ sveṣu bhogeṣu āśīḥ pravartanāt evaṃcid bhairava āveśa nindā tatpara mānasāḥ bhavanti ati su ghorābhiḥ śaktibhiḥ pātitā yatas  tena śāṃbhava māhātmyam jānanyaḥ śāsana antare āśvastaḥ  na uttarītavyam tena bheda mahā arṇavāt  śrī kāmikāyām proktam ca pāśa prakaraṇe sphuṭam veda sāṃkhya purāṇa jñāḥ pāñcarātra parāyaṇāḥ ye kecid ṛṣayaḥ dhīrāḥ śāstra antara parāyaṇāḥ bauddha arhata ādyāḥ sarve te vidyā rāgeṇa rañjitāḥ māyā pāśena baddha tvāt śiva dīkṣām na vindate rāga śabdena ca proktam rāga tattvam niyāmakam māyīye tad ca tam tasmin śāstre niyamayet iti mokṣaḥ  pi vaiṣṇava ādeḥ yaḥ sva saṃkalpena bhāvitaḥ para prakṛti sāyujyam yad vā api ānanda rūpa tā viśuddha citta mātram vā dīpavat saṃtati kṣayaḥ sa sa vedya apavedya ātma pralaya ākala tāmayaḥ tam prāpya api ciram kālam tad gogābhoga bhuktatas  tad tattva pralaya ante tu tad ūrdhvām sṛṣṭim āgataḥ mantra tvam eti saṃbodhāt ananta īśena kalpitāt  etad ca agre taniṣyāma iti āstām tāvat atra tad  tena ajña jana tā āklṛpta pravādaiḥ yaḥ  viḍambitaḥ asat gurau rūḍha cit sa māyā pāśena rañjitaḥ saḥ  pi sat tarka yogena nīyate sat gurum prati sat tarkaḥ śuddha vidyā eva sā ca icchā parameśituḥ śrī pūrvaśāstre tena uktam sa yiyāsuḥ śiva icchayā bhukti mukti prasiddhi artham nīyate sat gurum prati śaktipātaḥ tu tatra eṣa kramikaḥ saṃpravartate sthitvā yaḥ  sat gurau śāstra antare vā sat patham śritaḥ guru śāstra gate sattve sattve ca atra vibhedakam śaktipātasya vaicitryam purastāt pravivicyate uktam svacchandaśāstre tad  vaiṣṇava ādyān pravādinaḥ sarvān bhramayate māyā sāmokṣe mokhṣa lipsayā yaḥ tu rūḍhaḥ  pi tatra udyat parāmarśa viśāradaḥ sa śuddha vidyā māhātmyāt śaktipāta pavitritaḥ ārohati eva sat mārgam pratyūha parivarjitaḥ sa tāvat kasyacid tarkaḥ svata eva pravartate sa ca sāṃsiddhikaḥ śāstre proktaḥ sva pratyaya ātmakaḥ kiraṇāyām yad api uktam gurutaḥ śāstrataḥ svatas  tatra uttarottaram mukhyam pūrva pūrva upāyakaḥ yasya svatas  yam sat tarkaḥ sarvatra eva adhikāravān abhiṣiktaḥ sva saṃvitti devībhiḥ dīkṣitaḥ ca saḥ sa eva sarva ācāryāṇām madhye mukhyaḥ prakīrtitaḥ tad saṃnidhāne na anyeṣu kalpiteṣu adhikāri tā sa samastam ca śāstra artham sat tarkāt eva manyate śuddhavidyā hi tad na asti satyam yadi anna bhāsayet  sarva śāstra artha vettṛ tvam akasmāt ca asya jāyate iti śrī pūva vākye tad  akasmāt iti  śabdataḥ loka aprasiddhaḥ  yaḥ  hetuḥ saḥ  kasmāt iti kathyate sa ca eṣa parameśāna śuddha vidyā vijṛmbhatam asya bhodāḥ ca bahavaḥ  nirbhittiḥ sahabhittikaḥ sarva gaḥ ṃśa gataḥ saḥ  pi mukhyā mukhya aṃśa niṣṭhitaḥ bhittiḥ para upajīvi tvam parā prajñā atha tad kṛtiḥ adṛṣṭa maṇḍalaḥ  pi evam yaḥ kaścid vetti tattvataḥ sa siddhi bhāj bhavet nityam sa yogī sa ca dīkṣitaḥ evam yaḥ  vetti tattvena tasya nirvāṇa gāminī dīkṣā bhavet iti proktam tad śrī triṃśakaśāsane akalpitaḥ  guruḥ jñayaḥ sāṃsiddhika iti smṛtaḥ yaḥ tu tad rūpa bhāga ātma bhāvanātaḥ param vinā śāstra vid sa guruḥ śāstre proktaḥ  kalpita kalpakaḥ tasya api bhedā utkṛṣṭa madhya manda ādi upāyataḥ bhāvanātaḥ  tha vā dhyānāt japāt svapnāt vratāt huteḥ prāpnoti akalpita udāram abhiṣekam mahāmatiḥ śrīmat vājasanīye śrī vīre śrī brahmayāmale śrī siddhāyām idam dhātrā proktam anyatra ca sphuṭam tasya sva icchā pravṛtta tvāt kāraṇa anantatā iṣyate kadācid bhakti yogena karmaṇā vidyayā api vā jñāna dharma upadeśena mantraiḥ vā dīkṣayā api vā evamādyaiḥ anekaiḥ ca prakāraiḥ parameśvaraḥ saṃsāriṇaḥ  nugṛhṇāti viśvasya jagataḥ patiḥ mātṛ maṇḍala saṃbodhāt saṃskārāt tapasaḥ priye dhyānāt yogāt japāt jñānāt mantra ārādhanātaḥ  vratāt  saṃprāpyam kula sāmānyam jñānam kaulika siddhi dam tattva jñāna ātmakam sādhyam yatra yatra eva dṛśyate sa eva hi guruḥ tatra hetu jālam prakalpyatām tattva jñānāt ṛte na anyat lakṣaṇam brahmayāmale tatra eva ca uktam sevāyām kṛtāyām avikalpataḥ sādhakasya na ced siddhiḥ kim kāryam iti codite ātmīyam asya saṃjñā na krameṇa sva ātma dīkṣaṇam sa sphuratva prasiddhi artham tatas  sādhyam prasiddhyati anena sva ātma vijñānam sa sphuratva prasādhakam uktam mukhya tayā ācāryaḥ  bhavet yadi na sa sphuraḥ tatra eva ca punar  śrīmat rakta ārādhana karmaṇi vidhim proktam sadā kurvan māsena ācārya ucyate pakṣeṇa sādhakaḥ  rdhārdhāt putrakaḥ samayī tathā dīkṣayet japa yogena raktādevī kramāt yatas  guroḥ alābhe proktasya vidhim etam samācaret  mate ca pustakāt vidyā adhyayane doṣa īdṛśaḥ uktaḥ  yaḥ tena tad doṣa abhāve sau na niṣiddha tā mantra dravya ādi gupta tve phalam kim iti codite pustaka adhīta vidyā ye dīkṣā samaya varjitāḥ tāmasāḥ para hiṃsā ādi vaśya ādi ca caranti alam na ca tattvam viduḥ tena doṣa bhāja iti sphuṭam pūrvam pada yugam vācyam anyonyam hetu hetumat  yaḥ tu śāstram vinā na eti śuddha vidyā ākhya saṃvidam guroḥ sa śāstram anvicchuḥ tad uktam kramam ācaret  yena kena api upāyena gurum ārādhya bhaktitaḥ tad dīkṣā krama yogena śāstra artham vetti asau tatas  abhiṣekam samāsādya yaḥ  bhavet sa tu kalpitaḥ san  api aśeṣa pāśa ogha vinivartana kovidaḥ yaḥ  yathā krama yogena kasmiṃścid śāstra vastuni ākasmikam brajet bodham kalpita akalpitaḥ  hi saḥ tasya yaḥ  kalpitaḥ  bhāgaḥ sa tu śreṣṭhamaḥ smṛtaḥ utkarṣaḥ śuddha vidyā aṃśa tāratamya kṛtaḥ  yatas  yathā bhedena ādi siddhāt śivāt mukta śivā hi adhas  tathā sāṃsiddhika jñānāt āhṛta jñāninaḥ dhamāḥ tad saṃnidhau na adhikāraḥ teṣām mukta śiva ātmavat  kim tu tūṣṇīṃ  sthitiḥ yad vā kṛtyam tad anuvartanam yaḥ tu akalpita rūpaḥ  pi saṃvāda dṛḍha tā kṛte anyatas  labdha saṃskāraḥ sa sākṣāt bhairavaḥ  guruḥ yatas  śāstra kramāt tad jña guru prajñā anuśīlanāt ātma pratyayitam jñānam pūrṇa tvāt bhairavāyate tena śrī kiraṇa uktam yad gurutaḥ śāstrataḥ svatas  tri pratyayam idam jñānam iti yad ca niśāṭane tad saṃghāta viparyāsa vigrahaiḥ bhāsate tathā karaṇasya vicitra tvāt vicitrām eva tām chidam kartum vāsīm ca ṭaṅkam ca krakacam ca api gṛhṇate tāvat ca chedanam hi ekam tathā eva adya abhisaṃdhitaḥ ittham eva mitau vācyam karaṇasya svakam vapuḥ na svatantram svatas  mānam kuryāt adhigamam haṭhāt  pramātṛ āśvāsa paryantaḥ  yatas  dhik ama ucyate āśvāsaḥ ca vicitraḥ  sau śaktipāta vaśāt tathā pramite pi pramāṇānām avakāśaḥ  styataḥ sphuṭaḥ dṛṣṭvā dṛṣṭvā samāśliṣya ciram saṃcarvya cetasā priyā yaiḥ parituṣyeta kim brūmaḥ kila tān prati ittham ca māna saṃplutyām api na adhigate gatiḥ na vyartha tā na anavasthā na anyonya āśraya tā api ca evam yogāṅgam iyati tarka eva na ca aparam antarantaḥ parāmarśa pāṭava atiśayāya saḥ ahiṃsā satyam asteya brahmacarya aparigrahāḥ iti pañca yamāḥ sākṣāt saṃvittau na upayoginaḥ tapaḥ prabhṛtayaḥ ye ca niyamā yad tathā āsanam prāṇāyāmāḥ ca ye sarvam etad bāhya vijṛmbhitam śrīmat vīrāvalau ca uktam bodha mātre śiva ātmake citta pralaya bandhena pralīne śaśi bhāskare prāpte ca dvādaśe bhāge jīva āditye sva bodhake mokṣaḥ sa eva kathitaḥ prāṇāyāmaḥ  nirarthakaḥ prāṇāyāmaḥ  na kartavyaḥ śarīram yena pīḍyate rahasyam vetti yaḥ  yatra sa muktaḥ sa ca mocakaḥ pratyāhāraḥ ca nāma ayam arthebhyaḥ  kṣadhiyām hi yaḥ anibaddhasya bandhasya tad antar  kila kīlanam cittasya viṣaye kvāpi bandhanam dhāraṇa ātmakam tad sadṛś jñāna saṃtānaḥ  dhyānam astamitā param yadā tu jñeya tādātmyam eva saṃvidi jāyate grāhya grahaṇa tā dvaita śūnyatā iyam samāhitiḥ tad eṣā dhāraṇā dhyāna samādhi tritayī parām saṃvidam prati naḥ kaṃcid upayogam samaśnute yoga aṅga tā yama ādeḥ tu samādhi antasya varṇyate sva pūrva pūrva upāya tvāt antya tarka upayogataḥ antar  saṃvidi rūḍham hi tad dvārā prāṇa dehayoḥ buddhau vārpyam tad abhyāsāt na eṣa nyāyaḥ tu saṃvidi atha vā asmad dṛśi prāṇa dhī deha ādeḥ api sphuṭam sarva ātmaka tvāt tatrasthaḥ  pyabhyāsaḥ  nyavyapohanam deha utpluti saṃpāta dharma ujjigamiṣā rasāt utplāvyate tad vipakṣa pātā śaṅkā vyapohanāt guru vākya parāmarśa sadṛśe sva vimarśane prabuddhe tad vipakṣāṇām vyudāsaḥ pāṭha cintane na hi asya guruṇā śakyam svam jñānam śabda eva vā dhiyi ropayitum tena sva prabodha kramaḥ  dhruvam ata eva svapna kāle śrute tatra api vastuni tādātmya bhāvanā yogaḥ  na phalāya na bhaṇyate saṃketānādare śabda niṣṭham āmarśanam paṭhiḥ tad ādare tad arthaḥ tu cintā iti paricarcyatām tad advayāyām saṃvittau  abhyāsaḥ  nupayogavān kevalam dvaitamālinya śaṅkā nirmūlanāya saḥ dvaita śaṅkāḥ ca tarkeṇa tarkyanta iti varṇitam tad tarka sādhanāyāḥ tu yama ādeḥ api upāya tā uktam śrī pūrva śastre ca na dvaitam na api ca advayam liṅga pūjā ādikam sarvam iti upakramya śaṃbhunā vihitam sarvam eva atra pratiṣiddham atha api vā prāṇāyāma ādikaiḥ aṅgaiḥ yogāḥ syuḥ kṛttrimā yatas  tad tena akṛtakasya asya kalām na arghanti ṣoḍaśīm kim tu etad atra deveśi niyamena vidhīyate tattve cetaḥ sthiram kāryam tad ca yasya yathā astu iti evam dvaita parāmarśa nāśāya parameśvaraḥ kvacid svabhāvam amalam āmṛśan  aniśam sthitaḥ yaḥ svabhāva parāmarśa indriya artha ādi upāyataḥ vinā eva tad mukhaḥ  nyaḥ vā svātantryāt tad vikalpanam tad ca svaccha svatantra ātma ratna nirbhāsini sphuṭam bhāva oghe bheda saṃdhātṛ sva ātmanaḥ  na aiśam ucyate tad eva tu samasta artha nirbhara ātma eka gocaram śuddha vidyā ātmakam sarvam eva idam aham iti alam idam vikalpanam śuddha vidyā rūpam sphuṭa ātmakam pratihanti iha māyīyam vikalpam bheda bhāvakam śuddha vidyā parām arśaḥ  yaḥ sa eva tu anekadhā snāna śuddhi arcana ahoma dhyāna japya ādi yogataḥ viśvam etad sva saṃvitti rasa nirbharitam rasāt  āviśya śuddhaḥ  nikhilam tarpayet adhva maṇlam ullāsi bodha hutabhuj dagdha viśva indhana udite sita
