bhasmani dehasya majjanam snānam ucyate ittham ca vihita snānaḥ tarpita ananta devataḥ tatas  pi deha ārambhīṇi tattvāni pariśodhayet  śiva ātmakeṣu api eteṣu buddhiḥ yā vyatirekiṇī sā eva aśuddhiḥ para ākhyātā śuddhiḥ tad dhī vimardanam evam sva deham bodha eka pātram galita bhedakam paśyan saṃvitti mātra tve svatantre tiṣṭhati prabhuḥ yad kiṃcid mānasa āhlādi yatra kvāpi indriya sthitau yojyate brahma sat dhāmni pūjā upakaraṇam hi tad  pūjā nāma vibhinnasya bhāva oghasya api saṃgatiḥ svatantra vimala ananta bhairavīya cit ātmanā tathā hi saṃvid eva iyam antar bāhya ubhaya ātmanā svātantryāt vartamānā eva parāmarśa svarūpiṇī sa ca dvādaśadhā tatra sarvam antar bhavet yatas  sūrya eva hi soma ātmā sa ca viśva mayaḥ sthitaḥ kalā dvādaśaka ātmā eva tad saṃvid parama arthataḥ sā ca mātari vijñāne māne karaṇa gocare meye caturvidham bhāti rūpam āśritya sarvadā śuddha saṃvid mayī prācye jñāne śabdana rūpiṇī karaṇe grahaṇa ākārā yatas  śrī yoga saṃcare ye cakṣuḥ maṇḍale śvete pratyakṣe parameśvari ṣoḍaśa aram dvādaśa aram tatrastham cakram uttamam prativāraṇavat rakte tad bahirye tad ucyate dvitīyam madhya ge ye te kṛṣṇa śvete ca maṇḍale tad antarye sthite śuddhe bhinnāñjana sama prabhe catur dale tu te jñeye agnīṣoma ātmake priye mithuna tve sthite ye ca cakre dve parameśvari saṃmīlana unmīlanam te anyonyam vidadhātake yathā yoniḥ ca liṅgam ca saṃyogāt sravataḥ  mṛtam tathā amṛta agni saṃyogāt dravataḥ te na saṃśayaḥ tad cakra pīḍanāt rātrau jyotiḥ bhāti arka soma gam tām dṛṣṭvā paramām jyotsnām kāla jñānam pravartate sahasrāram bhavet cakram tābhyām upari saṃsthitam tatas cakrāt samudbhūtam brahmāṇḍam tad udāhṛtam tatrasthām muñcate dhārām somaḥ  hi agni pradīpitaḥ sṛjati ittham jagat sarvam ātmani ātmani anantakam ṣoḍaśa dvādaśārābhyām aṣṭa āreṣu atha sarvaśas  evam krameṇa sarvatra cakreṣu amṛtam uttamam somaḥ sravati yāvat ca pañcānām cakra paddhatiḥ tad punar  pibati prītyā haṃsaḥ haṃsa iti sphuran sakṛt yasya tu saṃśrutyā puṇya pāpaiḥ na lipyate pañca are sa vikāraḥ  tha bhūtvā soma sruta amṛtāt dhāvati tris asārāṇi guhya cakrāṇi asau vibhuḥ yatas  jātam jagat līnam yatra ca svaka līlayā tatra ānandaḥ ca sarvasya brahmacārī ca tad paraḥ tatra siddhiḥ ca muktiḥ ca samam saṃprāpyate dvayam ata ūrdhvam punar yāti yāvat brahma ātmakam padam agnīṣomau samau tatra sṛjyete ca ātmanā ātmani tatrasthaḥ tāpitaḥ somaḥ  dvedhā jaṅghe vyavasthitaḥ adhas tam pātayet agniḥ amṛtam sravati kṣaṇāt  gulpha jānu ādiṣu vyaktam kuṭila arka pradīpitā sā śaktiḥ tāpitā bhūyas  pañcāra ādi kramam sṛjet  evam śrotre pi vijñeyam yāvat pāda anta gocaram pādāṅguṣṭhāt samārabhya yāvat brahmāṇḍa darśanam iti ajānanna eva yogī jānan viśva prabhuḥ bhavet  jvalan  iva asau brahma ādyaiḥ dṛśyate parameśvaraḥ atra tātparyataḥ proktam akṣe krama catuṣṭayam eka ekatra yatas tena dvādaśa ātmaka toditā na vyākhyātam tu nirbhajya yatas  tisarahasyakam meye pi devī tiṣṭhantī māsa rāśi ādi rūpiṇī ata eṣā sthitā saṃvid antar bāhya ubhaya ātmanā svayam nirbhāsya tatra anyat bhāsayantī iva bhāsate tatas ca prāk iyam śuddhā tathā ābhāsana sa utsukā sṛṣṭim kalayate devī tad nāmnā āgama ucyate tathā bhāsita vastu aṃśa rañjanām sā bahirmukhī sva vṛtti cakreṇa samam tatas  pi kalayanti alam sthitiḥ eṣā eva bhāvasya tām antar mukha tā rasāt saṃjihīrṣuḥ sthiteḥ nāśam kalayantī nirucyate tatas  pi saṃhāra rase pūrṇe vighna karīm svayam śaṅkām yama ātmikām bhāge sūte saṃharate pi ca saṃhṛtya śaṅkām śaṅkya artha varjam vā bhāva maṇḍale saṃhṛtim kalayati eva sva ātma vahnau vilāpanāt  vilāpana ātmikām tām ca bhāva saṃhṛtim ātmani āmṛśati eva yena eṣā mayā grastam iti sphuret  saṃhārya upādhiḥ etasyāḥ sva svabhāvaḥ  hi saṃvidaḥ nirupādhini saṃśuddhe saṃvid rūpeṣastamīyate vilāpite pi bhāva oghe kaṃcid bhāvam tadā eva sā āśyānayet ya eva āste śaṅkā saṃskāra rūpakaḥ śubha aśubha tayā saḥ  yam soṣyate phala saṃpadam pūrvam hi bhogāt paścāt vā śaṅkā iyam vyavatiṣṭhate anyadāśyānitam api tadā eva drāvayet iyam prāyaścitta ādi karmabhyaḥ  brahmahatyā ādi karmavat rodhanāt drāvaṇāt rūpam ittham kalayate citiḥ tad api drāvayet eva tad api āśyānayet atha ittham bhogye pi saṃbhukte sati tad karaṇāni api saṃharantī kalayate dvādaśa eva aham ātmani karma buddhi akṣa vargaḥ  hi buddhi antaḥ  dvādaśa ātmakaḥ prakāśaka tvāt sūrya ātmā bhinne vastuni jṛmbhate ahaṃkāraḥ tu karaṇam abhimāna eka sādhanam avicchinna parāmarśī līyate tena tatra saḥ yathā hi khaṅga pāśa ādeḥ karaṇasya vibhedinaḥ abhedini sva hasta ādau layaḥ tadvat ayam vidhiḥ tena indriya ogha mārtaṇḍa maṇḍalam kalayet svayam saṃvid devī svatantra tvāt kalpite haṃkṛtātmani sa eva parama ādityaḥ pūrṇa kalpaḥ trayodaśaḥ karaṇa tvāt prayāti eva kartari pralayam sphuṭam kartā ca dvividhaḥ proktaḥ kalpita ākalpita ātmakaḥ kalpitaḥ  deha buddhi ādi vyavacchedena carcitaḥ kālāgni rudra saṃjñā asya śāstreṣu paribhāṣitā kālaḥ  vyavacchittad yuktaḥ  vahniḥ bhoktā yatas  smṛtaḥ saṃsāra āklṛpti klṛptibhyām rodhanāt drāvaṇāt prabhuḥ anivṛtta paśūbhāvaḥ tatra ahaṃkṛt pralīyate saḥ  pi kalpita vṛtti tvāt viśva abheda eka śālini vikāsini mahākāle līyate hamidaṃmaye etasyām sva ātma saṃvittau  idam sarvam aham vibhuḥ iti pravikasat rūpā saṃvittiḥ avabhāsate tatas  ntar sthita sarva ātma bhāva bhoga uparāgiṇī paripūrṇā api saṃvittiḥ akule dhāmni līyate pramātṛ vargaḥ  māna oghaḥ pramāḥ ca bahudhā sthitāḥ meya ogha iti yad sarvam atra cit mātram eva tad  iyatīm rūpa vaicitrīm āśrayantyāḥ sva saṃvidaḥ svācchandyam anapekṣam yad sā parā parameśvarī imāḥ prāc ukta kalanāḥ tad vijṛmbhā ucyate yatas  kṣepaḥ  jñānam ca saṃkhyānam gatiḥ nāda iti kramāt  sva ātmanaḥ  bhedanam kṣepaḥ  bheditasya avikalpanam jñānam vikalpaḥ saṃkhyānam anyatas  vyatibhedanāt  gatiḥ svarūpa ārohi tvam pratibimbavat eva yad  nādaḥ sva ātma parāmarśa śeṣa tā tad vilopanāt  iti pañcavidhām ena am kalanām kurvatī parā devī kālī tathā kālakarṣiṇī ca iti kathyate mātṛsadbhāva saṃjñā asyāḥ tena uktā yad pramātṛṣu etāvat anta saṃvittau pramātṛ tvam sphuṭībhavet  vāmeśvarī iti  śabdena proktā śrī niśisaṃcare ittham dvādaśadhā saṃvid tiṣṭhantī viśva mātṛṣu ekā eva iti na kaḥ  pyasyāḥ kramasya niyamaḥ kvacid  krama abhāvāt na yugapad tad abhāvāt kramaḥ  pi na kramākrama kathā atītam saṃvid tattvam su nirmalam tad asyāḥ saṃvidaḥ  devyā yatra kvāpi pravartanam tatra tādātmya yogena pūjā pūrṇā eva vartate parāmarśa svabhāva tvāt etasyā yaḥ svayam dhvaniḥ sadā uditaḥ sa eva uktaḥ paramam hṛdayam mahat  hṛdaye sva vimarśaḥ  sau drāvita aśeṣa viśvakaḥ bhāva graha ādi paryanta bhāvī sāmānya saṃjñakaḥ spandaḥ sa kathyate śāstre sva ātmani ucchalana ātmakaḥ kiṃcid calanam etāvat ananya sphuraṇam hi yad  ūrmiḥ eṣā vibodha abdheḥ na saṃvid anayā vinā nistaraṅga taraṅga ādi vṛttiḥ eva hi sindhutā sāram etad samastasya yad cit sāram jaḍam jagat  tad adhīna pratiṣṭha tvāt tad sāram hṛdayam mahat  tathā hi sat idam brahma mūlam māyā aṇḍa saṃjñitam icchā jñāna kriyā āroham vinā na eva sat ucyate tad śakti tritaya ārohāt bhairavīye cit ātmani visṛjyate hi tad tasmāt bahis vā atha visṛjyate evam sat rūpa tā eva eṣām satām śakti traya ātma tām visargam para bodhena samākṣipya eva vartate tad sat eva bahīrūpam prāk bodha agni vilāpitam antar nadat parāmarśa śeṣībhūtam tatas  pyalam kha ātma tvam eva saṃprāptam śakti tritaya gocarāt  vedanā ātmaka tāmetya saṃhāra ātmani līyate idam saṃhāra hṛdayam prācyam sṛṣṭau ca hṛd matam etad rūpa parāmarśam akṛtrimam anābilam aham iti āhuḥ eṣa eva prakāśasya prakāśa tā etad vīryam hi sarveṣām mantrāṇām hṛdaya ātmakam vinā anena jaḍāḥ te syuḥ jīvā iva vinā hṛdā akṛtrimā etad hṛdaya ārūḍhaḥ  yad kiṃcid ācaret prāṇyāt vā mṛśate vā api sa sarvaḥ  sya japaḥ  mataḥ yad eva sva icchayā sṛṣṭi svābhāvyāt bahis antarā nirmīyate tad eva asya dhyānam syāt pāramārthikam nirākāre hi cit dhāmni viśva ākṛti maye sati phala arthinām kācid eva dhyeya tvena ākṛtiḥ sthitā yathā hi abhedāt pūrṇe pi bhāve jalam upāharan anya ākṛti apahānena ghaṭam arthayate rasāt  tathā eva parameśāna niyati pravijṛmbhaṇāt  kācid eva ākṛtiḥ kāṃcid  sūte phala vikalpanām yaḥ tu saṃpūrṇa hṛdayaḥ  na phalam nāma vāñchati tasya viśva ākṛtiḥ devī sā ca avaccheda varjanāt  kule yogina udrikta bhairavīya para āsavāt  ghūrṇitasya sthitiḥ dehe mudrā yā kācid eva sā antarindhana saṃbhāram anapekṣya eva nityaśas  jājvalī iti akhila akṣa ogha prasṛta ugra śikhaḥ śikhī bodha agnau tādṛśe bhāvā viśantaḥ tasya sat mahaḥ udrecayantaḥ  gacchanti homa karma nimitta tām yam kaṃcid parameśāna śaktipāta pavitritam purobhāvya svayam tiṣṭhet uktavat dīkṣitaḥ tu saḥ japya ādau homa paryante yadi api ekaika karmaṇi udeti rūḍhiḥ paramā tathā api ittham nirūpitam yathā hi tatra tatra aśvaḥ sama nimna unnata ādiṣu citre deśe vāhyamānaḥ  yāti icchā mātra kalpitām tathā saṃvid vicitrābhiḥ śānta ghoratara ādibhiḥ bhaṅgībhiḥ abhitaḥ dvaitam tyājitā bhairavāyate yathā puras sthe mukure nijam vaktram vibhāvayan bhūyaḥ bhūyas tad eka ātma vaktram vetti nija ātmanaḥ tathā vikalpa mukure dhyāna pūjā arcana ātmani ātmānam bhairavam paśyan  acirāt tanmayībhavet tanmayībhavanam nāma prāptiḥ sā anuttara ātmani pūrṇa tvasya parā kāṣṭhā sā iti atra na phala antaram phalam sarvam apūrṇa tve tatra tatra prakalpitam akalpite hi pūrṇa tve phalam anyat kim ucyatām eṣa yāga vidhiḥ kaḥ  pi kasya api hṛdi vartate yasya prasīdet cit cakram drāk apaścimajanmanaḥ atra yāge gataḥ  rūḍhim kaivalyam adhigacchati lokaiḥ ālokyamānaḥ  hi deha bandha vidhau sthitaḥ atra nāthaḥ samācāram paṭale ṣṭādaśe bhyadhāt  na atra śuddhiḥ na ca aśuddhiḥ na bhakṣya ādi vicāraṇam na dvaitam na api ca advaitam liṅga pūjā ādikam na ca na ca api tad parityāgaḥ  niṣparigraha tā api vā sa parigraha tā vā api jaṭā bhasma ādi saṃgrahaḥ tad tyāgaḥ  na vrata ādīnām caraṇa ācaraṇam ca yad  kṣetra ādi saṃpraveśaḥ ca samaya ādi prapālanam para svarūpa liṅga ādi nāma gotra ādikam ca yad  na asmin vidhīyate kiṃcid na ca api pratiṣidhyate vihitam sarvam eva atra pratiṣiddham atha api ca kim tu etad atra deveśi niyamena vidhīyate tattve cetaḥ sthirīkāryam su prasannena yoginā tad ca yasya yathā eva syāt sa tathā eva samācaret  tattve niścala cittaḥ tu bhuñjānaḥ  viṣayān api na saṃspṛśyeta doṣaiḥ sa padma patram iva ambhasā viṣa apahāri mantra ādi saṃnaddhaḥ  bhakṣayan  api viṣam na muhyate tena tadvat yogī mahāmatiḥ aśuddham hi katham nāma deha ādyam pāñcabhautikam prakāśa tā atirikte kim śuddhi aśuddhī hi vastunaḥ aśuddhasya ca bhāvasya śuddhiḥ syāt tādṛśā eva kim anyonya āśraya vaiyarthya anavasthā ittham atra hi pṛthivī jalataḥ śuddhyet jalam dharaṇitaḥ tathā anyonya āśraya tā sā iyam aśuddha tve pyayam kramaḥ aśuddhāt jalataḥ śuddhyet dharā iti vyartha tā bhavet  vā ayutaḥ  vāriṇaḥ vāyoḥ tejasaḥ tasya vā anyatas  bahurūpa ādikā mantrāḥ pāvanāt teṣu śuddha tā mantrāḥ svabhāvataḥ śuddhā yadi te pi na kim tathā śiva ātma tā teṣu śuddhiḥ yadi tatra api sā na kim śiva ātmatva aparijñānam na mantreṣu dharā ādivat  te tena śuddhā iti ced tad jñaptiḥ tarhi śuddha tā yoginam prati sā ca asti bhāveṣu iti viśuddha tā nanu codanayā śuddhi aśuddhi ādika viniścayaḥ ittham astu tathā api eṣā codanā eva śiva uditā kā syāt satī iti ced etad anyatra pravitānitam vaidikyā bādhitā iyam ced viparītam na kim bhavet  samyak ced manyase bādhaḥ  viśiṣṭa viṣaya tvataḥ apavādena kartavyaḥ sāmānya vihite vidhau śuddhi aśuddhī ca sāmānya vihite tattva bodhini puṃsi te bādhite eva tathā ca atra iti varṇitam na artha vāda ādi śaṅkā ca vākye māheśvare bhavet  abuddhi pūrvam hi tathā saṃsthite satatam bhavet  vyoma ādi rūpe nigame śaṅkā mithyārtha tām prati anavacchinna vijñāna vaiśvarūpya su nirbharaḥ śāstra ātmanā sthitaḥ  devaḥ  mithyātvam kvāpi na arhati icchāvān bhāva rūpeṇa yathā tiṣṭhāsurīśvaraḥ tad svarūpa abhidhānena tiṣṭhāsuḥ sa tathā sthitaḥ artha vādaḥ  pi yatra anya vidhi ādi mukham īkṣate tatra astu asatyaḥ svātantrye sa eva tu vidhāyakaḥ vidhi vākya antare gacchan  aṅga bhāvam atha api vā na nirarthakam eva ayam saṃnidheḥ ga jaḍa ādivat  sva artha pratyāyanam ca asya sva saṃvittyā eva bhāsate tad apahnavanam kartum śakyam vidhi niṣedhayoḥ yuktiḥ ca atra asti vākyeṣu sva saṃvid ca api abādhitā yā samagra artha māṇikya tattva niścaya kāriṇī mṛta dehe tha deha utthe yā ca aśuddhiḥ prakīrtitā anyatra na iti buddhi antām aśuddham saṃvidaḥ cyutam saṃvid tādātmyam āpannam sarvam śuddham atas  sthitam śrīmat vīrāvalau ca uktam śuddhi aśuddhi nirūpaṇe sarveṣām vāhakaḥ  jīvaḥ  na asti kiṃcid ajīvakam yad kiṃcid jīva rahitam aśuddham tad vijānata tasmāt yad saṃvidaḥ  na atidūre tad śudvimāvahet avikalpena bhāvena munayaḥ  pi tathā abhavan loka saṃrakṣaṇa artham tu tad tattvam taiḥ pragopitam bahis  satsu api bhāveṣu śuddhi aśuddhī na nīlavat  pramātṛ dharma eva ayam cit aikya anaikya vedanāt  yadi vā vastu dharmaḥ  pi mātṛ apekṣā nibandhanaḥ sautrāmaṇyām surā hotuḥ śuddhāni asya viparyayaḥ anena codanānām ca sva vākyaiḥ api bādhanam kvacid saṃdarśitam brahmahatyā vidhi niṣedhavat bhakṣya ādi vidhayaḥ  pyenam nyāyam āśritya carcitāḥ sarva jñāna uttara ādau ca bhāṣate sma maheśvaraḥ nara ṛṣi deva druhiṇa viṣṇu rudra ādi udīritam uttarottara vaiśiṣṭyāt  pūrva pūrva prabādhakam na śaivam vaiṣṇavaiḥ vākyaiḥ bādhanīyam kadācana vaiṣṇavam brahma saṃbhūtaiḥ na ityādi paricarcayet  bādhate yaḥ  vaiparītyāt sa mūḍhaḥ pāpa bhāj bhavet  tasmāt mukhya tayā skanda loka dharmān na ca ācaret na anya śāstra samuddiṣṭam srotasi uktam nije caret  yatas  yadi api devena veda ādi api nirūpitam tathā api kila saṃkoca bhāva abhāva vikalpataḥ saṃkoca tāratamyena pāśavam jñānam īritam vikāsa tāratamyena pati jñānam tu bādhakam idam dvaitam idam na iti paraspara niṣedhataḥ māyīya bheda klṛptam tad syāt akālpanike katham uktam bhargaśikhāyām ca mṛtyu kāla kalā ādikam dvaita advaita vikalpa uttham grasate kṛta dhīḥ iti siddhānte liṅga pūjā uktā viśva adhva maya tā vide kula ādiṣu niṣiddhā asau dehe viśva ātma tā vide iha sarva ātmake kasmāt tad vidhi pratiṣedhane niyama anupraveśena tādātmya pratipattaye jaṭā ādi kaule tyāgaḥ  sya sukha upāya upadeśataḥ vrata caryā ca mantra artha tādātmya pratipattaye tad niṣedhaḥ tu mantra artha sārvātmya pratipattaye kṣetra pīṭha upapīṭheṣu praveśaḥ  vighna śāntaye mantra ādi ārādhakasya atha tad lābhāya upadiśyate kṣetra ādi gamana abhāva vidhiḥ tu sva ātmanaḥ tathā vaiśvarūpyeṇa pūrṇa tvam jñātum iti api varṇitam samaya ācāra sadbhāvaḥ pālya tvena upadiśyate bheda prāṇa tayā tad tad tyāgāt tattva viśuddhaye samaya ādi niṣedhaḥ tu mata śāstreṣu kathyate nirmaryādam sva saṃbodham saṃpūrṇam buddhyatām iti parakīyam idam rūpam dhyeyam etad tu me nijam jvālā ādi liṅgam ca anyasya kapāla ādi tu me nijam ādi śabdāt tapaḥ caryā velā atithi ādi kathyate nāma śakti śiva ādi antam etasya mama na anyathā gotram ca guru saṃtānaḥ  maṭhikā kula śabditaḥ śrī saṃtatiḥ tryambakā ākhyā tad ardha āmarda saṃjñitā ittham ardha cata sraḥ  tra maṭhikāḥ śāṃkare krame yuga krameṇa kūrma ādyā mīna antā siddha saṃtatiḥ ādi śabdena ca gharam pallī pīṭha upapīṭhakam mudrā chummā iti teṣām ca vidhānam sva para sthitam tādātmya pratipattyai hi svam saṃtānam samāśrayet  bhuñjīta pūjayet cakram para saṃtāninā na hi etad ca mata śāstreṣu niṣiddham khaṇḍanā yatas  akhaṇḍe pi pare tattve bhedena anena jāyate evam kṣetra praveśa ādi saṃtāna niyama antatas na asmin vidhīyate tad hi sākṣāt na aupayikam śive na tasya ca niṣodhaḥ  ya nna tad tattvasya khaṇḍanam viśvātmanaḥ  hi nāthasya svasmin rūpe vikalpitau vidhiḥ niṣedhaḥ  vā śaktau na svarūpasya khaṇḍane para tattva praveśe tu yam eva nikaṭam yadā upāyam vetti sa grāhyaḥ tadā tyājyaḥ  tha vā kvacid  na yantraṇa atra kāryā iti proktam śrī trikaśāsane sama tā sarva devānāmovallī mantra varṇayoḥ āgamanām gatīnām ca sarvam śiva mayam yatas  sa hi akhaṇḍita sadbhāvam śiva tattvam prapaśyati yaḥ  hi akhaṇḍita sadbhāvam ātma tattvam prapadyate ketakī kusuma saurabhe bhṛśam bhṛṅga eva rasikaḥ  na makṣikā c bhairavīya parama advaya arcane kaḥ  pi rajyati maheśa coditaḥ asmin  ca yoge viśrāntim kurvatām bhava ḍambaraḥ himāni iva mahā grīṣme svayam eva vilīyate alam vā atiprasaṅgena bhūyasā ati prapañcite yogyaḥ  bhinavaguptaḥ  smin kaḥ pi yāga vidhau budhaḥ iti anuttara pada pravikāse śāktam aupayika madya viviktam atha śrī tantrāloke pañcamam āhnikam āṇavena vidhinā para dhāma prepsatām atha nirūpyata etad  b vikalpasya eva saṃskāre jāte niṣpratiyogini abhīṣṭe vastuni prāptiḥ niścitā bhoga mokṣayoḥ vikalpaḥ kasyacid sva ātma svātantryāt eva susthiraḥ upāya antara sāpekṣya viyogena eva jāyate kasyacid tu vikalpaḥ  sau sva ātma saṃskaraṇam prati upāya antara sāpekṣaḥ tatra uktaḥ pūrva kaḥ  vidhiḥ vikalpaḥ  nāma cit mātra svabhāvaḥ  yadi api sthitaḥ tathā api niścaya ātmā asau  aṇoḥ svātantrya yojakaḥ niścayaḥ  bahudhā ca eṣa tatra upāyāḥ ca bhedinaḥ aṇu śabdena te ca uktā dūra antika vibhedataḥ tatra buddhau tathā prāṇe dehe ca api pramātari apāramārthike pyasmin parama arthaḥ prakāśate yatas  prakāśāt cit mātrāt  prāṇa ādi avyatirekavat  tasya eva tu svatantra tvāt dviguṇam jaḍa cit vapuḥ uktam traiśirase ca etad devyai candra ardha maulinā jīvaḥ śaktiḥ śivasya eva sarvatra eva sthitā api sā svarūpa pratyaye rūḍhā jñānasya unmīlanāt parā tasya cit rūpa tām satyām svātantrya ullāsa kalpanāt  paśyan jaḍa ātma tā bhāgam tirodhāya advayaḥ  bhavet  tatra svātantrya dṛṣṭyā vā darpaṇe mukha bimbavat  viśuddham nija caitanyam niścinoti atad ātmakam buddhi prāṇāditaḥ  bhinnam caitanyam niścitam balāt  satyataḥ tad abhinnam syāt tasya anyonya vibhedataḥ viśva rūpa avibhedi tvam śuddha tvāt eva jāyate niṣṭhita eka sphurat mūrteḥ mūrti antara virodhataḥ antar  saṃvidi sat sarvam yadi api aparathā dhiyi prāṇe dehe thavā kasmāt saṃkrāmet kena vā katham tathā api nirvikalpe smin vikalpaḥ  na asti tam vinā dṛṣṭe pyadṛṣṭa kalpa tvam vikalpena tu niścayaḥ buddhi prāṇa śarīreṣu pārameśvaryam añjasā vikalpyam śūnya rūpe na pramātari vikalpanam buddhiḥ dhyāna mayī tatra prāṇa uccāraṇa ātmakaḥ uccāraṇam ca prāṇa ādyā vyāna antāḥ pañca vṛttayaḥ ādyā tu prāṇana abhikhyā para uccāra ātmikā bhavet  śarīrasya akṣa viṣaya etad piṇḍa tvena saṃsthitiḥ tatra dhyāna mayam tāvat anuttaram iha ucyate yaḥ prakāśaḥ svatantraḥ  yam cit svabhāvaḥ  hṛdi sthitaḥ sarva tattva mayaḥ proktam etad ca triśiromate kadalī saṃpuṭa ākāram sa bāhya abhyantara antaram īkṣate hṛdaya antar stham tad puṣpam iva tattva vid  soma sūrya agni saṃghaṭṭam tatra dhyāyet ananyadhīḥ tad dhyāna araṇi saṃkṣobhāt mahābhairava havya bhuj  hṛdaya ākhye mahā kuṇḍe jājvalan sphītatām vrajet  tasya śaktimataḥ sphīta śakteḥ bhairava tejasaḥ mātṛmān aprameya ākhyam dhāma abhedena bhāvayet  vahni arka soma śaktīnām tad eva tritayam bhavet  parā parāparā ca iyam aparā ca sadā uditā sṛṣṭi saṃsthiti saṃhāraiḥ tāsām pratyekataḥ tridhā caturtham ca anavacchinnam rūpam āsām akalpitam evam dvādaśa tā devyaḥ sūrya bimbavat āsthitāḥ ekaika m āsām vahni arka soma tad śānti bhāsanam etadā anuttaram cakram hṛdayāt cakṣuḥ ādibhiḥ vyomabhiḥ niḥsarati eva tad tad viṣaya gocare tad cakrabhābhiḥ tatra arthe sṛṣṭi sthiti laya kramāt  soma sūrya agni bhāsa ātma rūpam samavatiṣṭhate evam śabda ādi viṣaye śrotra ādi vyoma vartmanā cakreṇa anena patatā tādātmyam paribhāvayet  anena krama yogena yatra yatra patati adaḥ cakram sarva ātmakam tad tad sārvabhauma mahī īśavat ittham viśva adhva paṭalam ayatnena eva līyate bhairavīya mahā cakre saṃvitti parivārite tatas  saṃskāra mātreṇa viśvasya api parikṣaye sva ātma ucchalat tayā bhrāmyat cakram saṃcintayet mahat  tatas tad dāhya vilayāt tad saṃskāra parikṣayāt praśāmyat bhāvayet cakram tatas  śāntam tatas  śamam anena dhyāna yogena viśvam cakre vilīyate tad saṃvidi tatas  saṃvid vilīna arthā eva bhāsate cit svābhāvyāt tatas  bhūyas  sṛṣṭiḥ yad cit maheśvarī evam pratikṣaṇam viśvam sva saṃvidi vilāpayan visṛjan  ca tatas  bhūyas  śaśvat bhairava tām vrajet  evam triśūlāt  prabhṛti catuṣpañcāraka kramāt  pañcāśat ara paryantam cakram yogī vibhāvayet  catuṣṣaṣṭi śatāram vā sahasrāram atha api vā asaṃkhya āra sahasram vā cakram dhyāyet ananyadhīḥ saṃvid nāthasya mahataḥ  devasya ullāsi saṃvidaḥ na eva asti kācid kalanā viśva śakteḥ maheśituḥ śaktayaḥ sya jagat  kṛtsnam śaktimān  tu maheśvaraḥ iti māṅgala śāstre tu śrī śrīkaṇṭhaḥ  nyarūpayat  iti etad  prathama upāya rūpam dhyānam nyarūpayat  śrī śaṃbhunāthaḥ me tuṣṭaḥ tasmai śrī sumati prabhuḥ anayā eva diśā anyāni dhyānāni api samāśrayet  anuttara upāya dhurām yāni āyānti kramam vinā atha prāṇasya yā vṛttiḥ prāṇana ādyā nirūpitā tad upāya tayā brūmaḥ  nuttara pravikāsanam nija ānande pramātṛ aṃśa mātre hṛdi purā sthitaḥ śūnyatā mātra viśrānteḥ nirānandam vibhāvayet  prāṇa udaye prameye tu para ānandam vibhāvayet  tatra ananta prameya aṃśa pūraṇa apāna nirvṛtaḥ para ānanda gataḥ tiṣṭhet apāna śaśi śobhitaḥ tatas  nanta sphurat meya saṃghaṭṭa ekānta nirvṛtaḥ samāna bhūmim āgatya brahma ānanda m ayaḥ  bhavet  tatas  pi māna meya ogha kalanā grāsa tatparaḥ udāna vahnau viśrāntaḥ  mahānandam vibhāvayat  tatra viśrāntim abhyetya śāmyati asmin mahā arciṣi nirupādhiḥ mahāvyāptiḥ vyāna ākhya upādhi varjitā tadā khalu cit ānandaḥ  yaḥ  jaḍa anupabṛṃhitaḥ na hi atra saṃsthitiḥ kā api vibhaktā jaḍa rūpiṇaḥ yatra kaḥ  pi vyavacchedaḥ  na asti yad viśvatas  sphurat  yad anāhata saṃvitti parama amṛta bṛṃhitam yatra asti bhāvanā ādīnām na mukhyā kā api saṃgatiḥ tad eva jagat ānandam asmabhyam śaṃbhuḥ ūcivān tatra viśrāntiḥ ādheyā hṛdaya uccāra yogataḥ yā tatra samyak viśrāntiḥ sā anuttara mayī sthitiḥ iti etad hṛdaya ādi eka svabhāve pi sva dhāmani ṣaṣ prāṇa uccāra jam rūpam atha vyāptyā tad ucyate prāṇa daṇḍa prayogena pūrva apara samīkṛteḥ catuṣkika ambuja ālambi lambikā saudham āśrayet triśūla bhūmiṃ krāntvā atas  nāḍi tritaya saṅga tām icchā jñāna kriyā śakti sama tve praviśet  sudhīḥ ekām vikāsinīm bhūyastva saṃkocām vikasvarām śrayet bhrū bindunādānta śakti sopāna mālikām tatra ūrdhva kuṇḍalībhūmau spandana udara sundaraḥ visargaḥ tatra viśrāmyet matsya udara daśā juṣi rāsabhī vaḍavā yadvat svadhām ānanda mandiram vikāsa saṃkoca mayam praviśya hṛdi hṛṣyati tadvat muhur līna sṛṣṭa bhāva vrāta su nirbharām śrayet vikāsa saṃkoca rūḍha bhairava yāmalām ekīkṛta mahā mūla śūla vaisargike hṛdi parasmin  eti viśrāntim sarva āpūraṇa yogataḥ atra tad pūrṇa vṛttyā eva viśva āveśa mayam sthitam prakāśasya ātma viśrānta āvaham iti eva dṛśyatām anuttara vimarśe prāc vyāpāra ādi vivarjite cit vimarśa para ahaṃkṛt  prathama ullāsinī sphuret  tatas  udyoga saktena sa dvādaśa kalā ātmanā sūryeṇa ābhāsayet bhāvam pūrayet atha carcayet  atha induḥ ṣoḍaśa kalaḥ visarga grāsa mantharaḥ saṃjīvanī amṛtam bodha vahnau visṛjati sphuran icchā jñāna kriyā śakti sūkṣma randhra sruj agra gam tad evam a[tada]mṛtam divyam saṃvid devīṣu tarpakam visarga amṛtam etāvat  bodha ākhye huta bhojini visṛṣṭam ced bhavet sarvam hutam ṣoḍhā adhva maṇḍalam yatas  nuttara nāthasya visargaḥ kulanāyikā c tad kṣobhaḥ kāt iha antam tad prasaraḥ tattva paddhatiḥ aṃa iti kuleśvaryā sahitaḥ  hi kuleśitā paraḥ  visarga viśleṣaḥ tad mayam viśvam ucyate vid prāṇa guṇa deha antar bahis dravya mayīm imām arcayet juhuyāt dhyāyet ittham saṃjīvanīm kalām ānanda nāḍī yugala spandana avahitau sthitaḥ enām visarga niḥṣyanda saudha bhūmim prapadyate śākte kṣobhe kula āveśe sarva nāḍī agra gocare vyāptau sarva ātma saṃkoce hṛdayam praviśet sudhīḥ soma sūrya kalā jāla paraspara nigharṣataḥ agnīṣoma ātmake dhāmni visarga ānanda unmiṣet  alam rahasya kathayā guptam etad svabhāvataḥ yoginī hṛdayam tatra viśrāntaḥ syāt kṛtī budhaḥ hāna ādāna tiraskāra vṛttau rūḍhim upāgataḥ abheda vṛttitaḥ paśyet viśvam citi camatkṛteḥ artha kriyā arthitā dainyam tyaktvā bāhya antarātmani kha rūpe nirvṛtim prāpya phullām nāda daśām śrayet  vaktram antar tayā samyak  saṃvidaḥ pravikāsayet  saṃvid akṣa marut cakram jñeya abhinnam tatas  bhavet  tad jñeyam saṃvid ākhyena vahninā pravilīyate vilīnam tad  tri koṇe smin śakti vahnau vilīyate tatra saṃvedana udāra bindu sattā su nirvṛtaḥ saṃhāra bīja viśrāntaḥ  yogī parama yaḥ  bhavet  antar bāhye dvaye vā api sāmānya itarasundaraḥ saṃvid spandaḥ tri śakti ātmā saṃkoca pravikāsavān asaṃkoca vikāsaḥ  pi tad ābhāsanataḥ tathā antar lakṣyaḥ  bahis dṛṣṭiḥ paramam padam aśnute tatas  svātantrya nirmeye vicitra artha kriyā ākṛti vimarśanam viśeṣa ākhyaḥ spanda aunmukhya saṃjñitaḥ tatra viśrāntim āgacchet yad vīryam mantra maṇḍale śānti ādi siddhayaḥ tad tad rūpa tādātmyataḥ  yatas  divyaḥ  yaḥ ca akṣa saṃghaḥ  yam bodha svātantrya saṃjñakaḥ saḥ  nimīlita eva etad  kuryāt sva ātma mayam jagat  mahā sāhasa saṃyoga vilīna akhila vṛttikaḥ puñjībhūte sva raśmi oghe nirbharībhūya tiṣṭhati akicid cintakaḥ tatra spaṣṭa dṛś yāti saṃvidam yad visphuliṅgāḥ saṃsāra bhasma dāha eka hetavaḥ tad uktam parameśena triśiraḥ bhairava āgame śṛṇu devi pravakṣyāmi mantra bhūmyām praveśanam madhya nāḍya ūrdhva gamanam tad dharma prāpti lakṣaṇam visarga anta padā atītam prānta koṭi nirūpitam adhas pravāha saṃrodhāt ūrdhva kṣepa vivarjanāt  mahā prakāśam udaya jñāna vyakti pradāyakam anubhūya pare dhāmni mātrāvṛttyā puram viśet  nistaraṅga avatīrṇā sā vṛttiḥ ekā śiva ātmikā catuṣṣaṣ dvis dvi guṇita cakra ṣaṭka samujjvalā tad stham [tsthaḥ ] vicārayet  kham kham kha stham kha sthena saṃviśet  kham kham tyaktvā kham āruhya kha stham kham ca uccaret iti kham adhyāsya adhikāreṇa pada sthāḥ cit marīcayaḥ bhāvayet bhāvam antar stham bhāva sthaḥ  bhāva niḥspṛhaḥ bhāva abhāva gatī ruddhvā bhāva abhāva avarodha dṛś  ātma aṇu kula mūlāni śaktiḥ bhūtiḥ citī ratiḥ śakti trayam draṣṭṛ dṛśya uparaktam tad vivarjitam etad kham daśadhā proktam uccāra uccāra lakṣaṇam dhāma stham dhāma madhya stham dhāma udara puṭīkṛtam dhāmnā tu bodhayet dhāma dhāma dhāma anta gam kuru tad dhāma dhāma gatyā tu bhedyam dhāma antam āntaram bheda upabheda bhedena bhedaḥ kāryaḥ tu madhyatas  iti praveśa upāyaḥ yamāṇavaḥ parikīrtitaḥ śrī maheśvara nāthena yaḥ  hṛd sthena mama uditaḥ śrī brahmayāmale ca uktam śrīmān rāvaḥ  daśa ātmakaḥ sthūlaḥ sūkṣmaḥ paraḥ  hṛdyaḥ kaṇṭhyaḥ tālavya eva ca sarvatas ca vibhuḥ yaḥ sau vibhutva pada dāyakaḥ jita rāvaḥ  mahā yogī saṃkrāmet para deha gaḥ parām ca vindati vyāptim pratyaham hi abhyaseta tam tau  at yāvat arāve sā rāvān līyeta rāviṇī atra bhāvanayā deha gata upāyaiḥ pare pathi vivikṣoḥ pūrṇa tā sparśāt prāk ānandaḥ prajāyate tatas  pi vidyut āpāta sadṛśe deha varjite dhāmni kṣaṇam samāveśāt udbhavaḥ prasphuṭam plutiḥ jala pāṃsuvat abhyasta saṃvid deha aikya hānitaḥ sva bala ākramaṇāt deha śaithilyāt  kampam āpnuyāt  galite deha tādātmya niścaye ntarbhukha tvataḥ nidrāyate purā yāvat na rūḍhaḥ saṃvid ātmani tatas  satya pade rūḍhaḥ  viśva ātma tvena saṃvidam saṃvidan ghūrṇate ghūrṇiḥ mahāvyāptiḥ yatas  smṛtā ātmani anātma abhimatau satyām eva hi anātmani ātma abhimānaḥ  deha ādau bandhaḥ muktiḥ tu tad layaḥ ādau  ana ātmani ātma tve līne labdhe nija ātmani ātmani anātma tā nāśe mahāvyāptiḥ pravartate ānanda udbhavaḥ kampaḥ  nindrā ghūrṇiḥ ca pañcakam iti uktam ata eva śrī mālinīvijaya uttare pradarśite smin  ānanda prabhṛtau pañcake yadā yogī viśet tadā tad tad cakra īśa tvam haṭhāt vrajet  yathā sarva īśinā bodhena ākrāntā api tanuḥ kvacid  kiṃcid kartum prabhavati cakṣuṣā rūpa saṃvidam tathā eva cakre kutra api praveśāt kaḥ pi saṃbhavet  ānanda cakram vahni aśri kanda udbhava ucyate kampaḥ  hṛd tālu nidrā ca ghūrṇiḥ syāt ūrdhva kuṇḍalī etad ca sphuṭam eva uktam śrī mantra aiśirase mate evam pradarśita uccāra viśrānti hṛdayam param yad tad avyakta liṅgam nṛ śiva śakti avibhāgavat atra viśvam idam līnam atra antar stham ca gamyate idam tad lakṣaṇam pūrṇa śakti bhairava saṃvidaḥ deha ga adhva samunmeṣe samāveśaḥ tu yaḥ sphuṭaḥ ahanta ācchādita unmeṣi bhāva idaṃbhāva yuj  sa ca vyakta avyaktam idam liṅgam mantra vīryam parāparam nara śakti samunmeṣi śiva rūpāt vibheditam yad nyakkṛta śiva ahantā samāveśam vibhedavat  viśeṣa spanda rūpam tad  vyaktam liṅgam cit ātmakam vyaktāt siddhi prasavaḥ  vyakta avyaktāt dvayam vimokṣaḥ ca c avyaktāt balam ādyam parasya na anuttare tu iyam carcā ātma ākhyam yad vyaktam nara liṅgam tatra viśvam arpayataḥ vyakta avyaktam tasmāt galite tasmin  tad avyaktam tena ātma liṅgam etad  parame śiva śakti aṇu svabhāva maye avyakte viśrāmyati na anuttara dhāma gā tu iyam carcā ekasya spandanasya eṣā traidham bheda vyavasthitiḥ atra liṅge sadā tiṣṭhet  pūjā viśrānti tatparaḥ yoginī hṛdayam liṅgam idam ānanda sundaram bīja yoni samāpattyā sūte kām api saṃvidam atra prayāsa virahāt sarvaḥ  sau devatā gaṇaḥ ānanda pūrṇe dhāmni āste nitya udita cit ātmakaḥ atra bhairava nāthasya sa saṃkoca vikāsikā bhāsate durghaṭā śaktiḥ asaṃkoca vikāsinaḥ etad liṅga samāpatti visarga ānanda dhārayā siktam tad eva sat viśvam śaśvat   avanavāyate anuttare bhyupāyaḥ tra tādrūpyāt eva varṇitaḥ jvaliteṣu api dīpeṣu gharmāṃśuḥ kim na bhāsate artheṣu tad bhoga vidhau tad utthe duḥkhe sukhe vā galita abhiśaṅkam anāviśantaḥ  pi nimagna cittā jānanti vṛtti kṣaya saukhyam antar  sati eva ātmani cit svabhāva mahasi svānte tathā upaktiyām tasmai kurvati tad pracāra vivaśe sati akṣa varge pi ca satsu artheṣu sukha ādiṣu sphuṭataram yad bheda vandhya udayam yogī tiṣṭhati pūrṇa raśmi vibhavaḥ tad tattvam ācīyatām iti uccāra vidhiḥ proktaḥ karaṇam pravivicyate tad ca ittham triśiraḥśāstre parameśena bhāṣitam grāhya grāhaka cit vyāpti tyāga ākṣepa niveśanaiḥ karaṇam saptadhā prāhuḥ abhyāsam bodha pūrvakam tad vyāpti pūrvam ākṣepe karaṇam sva pratiṣṭhatā guru vaktrāt ca boddhavyam karaṇam yadi api sphuṭam tathā api āgama rakṣā artham tad agre varṇayiṣyate uktaḥ  ya eṣa uccāraḥ tatra yaḥ  sau sphuran sthitaḥ avyakta anukṛti prāyaḥ  dhvaniḥ varṇaḥ sa kathyate sṛṣṭi saṃhāra bījam ca tasya mukhyam vapuḥ viduḥ tad abhyāsa vaśāt yāti kramāt yogī cit ātma tām tathā hi anacke sācke vā ka ādau sa ante punar punar  smṛte proccārite vā api sā sā saṃvid prasūyāte bāhya artha samaya apekṣā ghaṭa ādyā dhvanayaḥ pi ye te pyartha bhāvanām kuryuḥ manaḥ rājyavat ātmani tad uktam parameśena bhairavaḥ  vyāpakaḥ  khile iti bhairava śabdasya saṃtata uccāraṇāt śivaḥ śrīmat traiśirase pyuktam mantra uddhārasya pūrvatas  smṛtiḥ ca smaraṇam pūrvam sarva bhāveṣu vastutas  mantra svarūpam tad bhāvya svarūpa āpatti yojakam smṛtiḥ svarūpa janikā sarva bhāveṣu rañjikā aneka ākāra rūpeṇa sarvatra avasthitena tu sva svabhāvasya saṃprāptiḥ saṃvittiḥ paramārthataḥ vyakti niṣṭhā tatas  viddhi sattā sā kīrtitā parā kim punar  samaya apekṣām vinā ye bīja piṇḍakāḥ saṃvidam spandapanti ete neyuḥ saṃvid upāya tām vācya abhāvāt udāsīna saṃvid spandāt sva dhāmataḥ prāṇa ullāsa nirodhābhyām bīja piṇḍeṣu pūrṇa tā sukha sītkāra sat samyak sāmya prathama saṃvidaḥ saṃvedanam hi prathamam sparśaḥ  nuttara saṃvidaḥ hṛd kaṇṭhyoṣṭhī atri dhāmā antar nitarām pravikāsini caturdaśaḥ praveśaḥ  ya ekīkṛta tad ātmakaḥ tatas  visarga uccāra aṃśe dvādaśānta pathau  ubhau hṛdayena saha aikadhyam nayate japa tatparaḥ kanda hṛd kaṇṭha tālu agra kauṇḍilī prakriyā antatas ānanda madhya nāḍī antar  spandanam bījam āvahet  saṃhāra bījam kham hṛd stham oṣṭhyam phullam sva mūrdhani tejaḥ tri aśram tālu kaṇṭhe binduḥ ūrdhva pade sthitaḥ iti enayā budhaḥ yuktyā varṇa japya parāyaṇaḥ anuttaram param dhāma praviśet acirāt  sudhīḥ varṇa śabdena nīla ādi yad vā dīkṣā uttare yathā saṃhāra nṛ agni marutaḥ  rudra bindu yutān smaret  hṛdaye tad mayaḥ  lakṣyam paśyet sapta dināt atha visphuliṅga agnivat nīla pīta rakta ādi citritam jājvalī iti hṛd ambhoje bīja dīpa prabodhitam dīpavat jvalitaḥ  binduḥ bhāsate vighana arkavat  svayaṃbhāsa ātmanā anena tādātmyam yāti ananyadhīḥ śivena hema tām yadvat tāmram sūtena vedhitam upalakṣaṇam etad ca sarva mantreṣu lakṣayet  yad yad saṃkalpa saṃbhūtam varṇa jālam hi bhautikam tad  saṃvid ādhikya vaśāt abhautikam iva sthitam atas tathāvidhe rūpe rūḍhaḥ  rohati saṃvidi anācchādita rūpāyām anupādhau prasanna dhīḥ nīle pīte sukhe duḥkhe saṃvid rūpam akhaṇḍitam gurubhiḥ bhāṣitam tasmāt upāyeṣu vicitra tā uccāra karaṇa dhyāna varṇaiḥ ebhiḥ pradarśitaḥ anuttara pada prāptau  abhyupāya vidhi kramaḥ akiṃcid cintanam vīryam bhāvanāyām ca sā punar  dhyāne tad api ca uccāre karaṇe saḥ  pi tad dhvanau sa sthāna kalpane bāhyam iti kramam upāśrayet  laṅghanena paraḥ  yogī manda buddhiḥ krameṇa tu vīryam vinā yathā ṣaṇṭhaḥ tasya api asti atha vā balam c mṛta deha iva iyam syāt bāhya antar parikalpanā iti āṇave nuttara tā abhyupāyaḥ proktaḥ  nayaḥ spaṣṭa pathena bāhyaḥ atha śrī tantrāloke sthāna prakalpa ākhya tayā sphuṭaḥ tu bāhyaḥ  bhyupāyaḥ pravivicyate tha b sthāna bhedaḥ tridhā proktaḥ prāṇe dehe bahis tathā prāṇaḥ ca pañcadhā dehe dvidhā bāhya antara tvataḥ maṇḍalam sthaṇḍilam pātram akṣa sūtram sa pustakam liṅgam tūram paṭaḥ pustam pratimā mūrtiḥ eva ca iti ekādaśadhā bāhyam punar tad bahudhā bhavet  tatra prāṇa āśrayam tāvat vidhānam upadiśyate adhvā samasta eva ayam ṣaḍvidhaḥ pyati vistṛtaḥ yaḥ  vakṣyate sa ekatra prāṇe tāvat pratiṣṭhitaḥ adhvanaḥ kalanam yad tad krama akrama tayā sthitam kramākramau hi citra eka kalanā bhāva gocare kramākrama ātmā kālaḥ ca paraḥ saṃvidi vartate kālī nāma parā śaktiḥ sā eva devasya gīyate sā eva saṃvid bahis  sva ātma garbhībhūtau kramākramau sphuṭayantī prarohaṇa prāṇa vṛttiḥ iti sthitā saṃvid mātram hi yad śuddham prakāśa parama arthakam tad meyam ātmanaḥ projjhya viviktam bhāsate nabhaḥ tad eva śūnya rūpa tvam saṃvidaḥ parigīyate na iti na iti vimarśena yoginām sā parā daśā sa eva kha ātmā meye smin bhedite svīkriyā unmukhaḥ patan samucchalattvena prāṇa spanda ūrmi saṃjñitaḥ tena āhuḥ kila saṃvid prāk prāṇe pariṇatā tathā antaḥkaraṇa tattvasya vāyuḥ āśrayatām gataḥ iyam sā prāṇanā śaktiḥ āntara udyoga doha dā spandaḥ sphurat tā viśrāntiḥ jīvaḥ  hṛd pratibhā matā sā prāṇa vṛttiḥ prāṇa ādyai rūpaiḥ pañcabhiḥ ātmasāt  deham yad kurute saṃvid pūrṇaḥ tena eṣa bhāsate prāṇanā vṛtti samastānām tattvānām ca param vapuḥ etad īśvara tattvam tad śivasya vapuḥ ucyate udrikta ābhoga kārya ātma viśva aikātmyam idam yatas  etad īśvara rūpa tvam parama ātmani yad kila tad pramātari māyīye dhiyaḥ na bhoktā jñaḥ  dhikāre tu vṛtta eva śivībhavet  sa eṣaḥ  vā antara layaḥ tad kṣaye sṛṣṭiḥ ucyate sāṃkhya veda ādi saṃsiddhān śrīkaṇṭhaḥ tad ahar mukhe sṛjati eva punar tena na samyak muktiḥ īdṛśī pradhāne yad ahorātram tad jam varṣa śatam vibhoḥ śrīkaṇṭhasya āyuḥ etad ca dinam kañcuka vāsinām tad kramāt niyatiḥ kālaḥ  rāgaḥ  vidyā kalā iti amī yānti anyonyam layam teṣām āyuḥ gāhanikam dinam tad dina prakṣaye viśvam māyāyām pravilīyate kṣīṇāyām niśi tāvatyām gahaneśaḥ sṛjet punar  evam avyakta kālam tu parārdhaiḥ daśabhiḥ jahi māyā hastāvatī rātriḥ bhavet pralaya eṣa saḥ māyā kālam parārdhānām guṇayitvā śatena tu aiśvaraḥ  divasaḥ  nādaḥ prāṇa ātmā atra sṛjet jagat  tāvatī ca aiśvarī rātriḥ yatra prāṇaḥ praśāmyati prāṇa garbha stham api atra viśvam sauṣumna vartmanā prāṇe brahma vile śānte saṃvid yā api avaśiṣyate aṃśa aṃśikātaḥ  pyetasyāḥ sūkṣma sūkṣma taraḥ  layaḥ guṇayitvā aiśvaram kālam parārdhānām śatena tu sādāśivam dinam rātriḥ mahāpralaya eva ca sadāśivaḥ sva kāla ante bindu ardhendu nirodhikāḥ ākramya nāde līyeta gṛhītvā sacarācaram nādaḥ  na ada anta vṛttyā tu bhittvā brahmabilam haṭhāt  śakti tattve layam yāti nija kāla parikṣaye etāvat śakti tattve tu vijñeyam khalu aharniśam śaktiḥ sva kāla vilaye vyāpinyām līyate punar  vyāpinyā tad divārātram līyate sā api anāśrite parārdha koṭyā hatvā api śakti kālam anāśrite dinam rātriḥ ca tad kāle parārdha guṇite pi ca saḥ  pi yāti layam sāmya saṃjñe sāmanase pade sa kālaḥ sāmya saṃjñaḥ syāt nityaḥ  kalyaḥ kalā ātmakaḥ yad tad sāmanasam rūpam tad sāmyam brahma viśva gam atas  sāmanasāt kālāt nimeṣa unmeṣa mātrataḥ tuṭi ādikam parārdha antam sūte sā eva atra niṣṭhitam daśa śata sahasram ayutam lakṣa niyuta koṭi sārbudam vṛndam kharva nikharve śaṃkha abja jaladhi madhya antam atha parārdham ca iti ekasmāt prabhṛti hi daśadhā daśadhā krameṇa kalayitvā eka ādi parārdha anteṣu aṣṭādaśasu sthitim brūyāt  catvāra ete pralayā mukhyāḥ sargāḥ ca tad kalāḥ bhū mūla naiśa śakti sthāḥ tad eva aṇḍa catuṣṭayam kālāgniḥ bhuvi saṃhartā māyā ante kāla tattva rāj  śrīkaṇṭhaḥ  mūla ekatra sṛṣṭi saṃhāra kārakaḥ tad layaḥ  vā antaraḥ tasmāt ekaḥ sṛṣṭi laya īśitā śrīmān aghoraḥ śakti ante saṃhartā sṛṣṭi kṛt ca saḥ tad sṛṣṭau sṛṣṭi saṃhārā niḥsaṃkhyā jagatām yatas  antarbhūtāḥ tatas  śāktī mahā sṛṣṭiḥ udāhṛtā laye brahmā harī rudra śatāni aṣṭaka pañcakam iti anyonyam kramāt yānti layam māyā antake dhvani māyā tattva laye tu ete prayānti paramam padam māyā ūrdhve ye sita adhva sthāḥ teṣām para śive layaḥ tatra api aupādhikāt bhedāt laye bhedam pare viduḥ evam tāttveśvare varge līne sṛṣṭau punar  pare tad sādhakāḥ śiveṣṭā vā tad sthānam adhiśerate brāhmī nāma parasya eva śaktiḥ tām yatra pātayet  sa brahmā viṣṇu rudra ādyā vaiṣṇavī ādeḥ atas  kramāt  śaktimantam vihāya anyam śaktiḥ kim yāti na īdṛśam chādita prathita aśeṣa śaktiḥ ekaḥ śivaḥ tathā evam visṛṣṭi pralayāḥ prāṇa ekatra niṣṭhitāḥ saḥ  pi saṃvidi saṃvid ca cit mātre jñeya varjite cit mātram eva devī ca sā parā parameśvarī aṣṭātriṃśam ca tad tattvam hṛdayam tad para aparam tena saṃvid tvam eva etad spandamānam svabhāvataḥ laya udayā iti prāṇe ṣaṣṭi abda udaya kīrtanam icchā mātra pratiṣṭheyam kriyā vaicitrya carcanā kāla śaktiḥ tatas  bāhye na etasyā niyatam vapuḥ svapna svapne tathā svapne supte saṃkalpa gocare samādhau viśva saṃhāra sṛṣṭi krama vivecane mitaḥ  pi kila kāla aṃśaḥ  vitata tvena bhāsate pramātṛ abhede bhede tha citraḥ  vitatimā api asau evam prāṇe yathā kālaḥ kriyā vaicitrya śakti jaḥ tathā pāne pi hṛdayāt mūla pīṭha visarpiṇi mūla abhidha mahā pīṭha saṅkoca pravikāsayoḥ brahma ādi anāśrita antānām cinute sṛṣṭi saṃhṛtī śaśvat yadi api apānaḥ  ya mittham vahati kiṃtu asau avedya yatnaḥ  yatnena yogibhiḥ samupāsyate hṛd kanda ānanda saṃkoca vikāsa dvādaśa anta gāḥ brahma ādayaḥ  na āśrita antāḥ sevyante tra su yogibhiḥ ete ca parameśāna śakti tvāt viśva vartinaḥ deham api aśnuvānāḥ tad kāraṇāni iti kāmike bālya yauvana vṛddhatva nidhaneṣu punarbhave muktau ca dehe brahma ādyāḥ ṣaṣ adhiṣṭhāna kāriṇaḥ tasya ante tu parā devī yatra yuktaḥ  na jāyate anena jñāta mātreṇa dīkṣā anugraha kṛt bhavet samasta kāraṇa ullāsa pade su vidite yatas  akāraṇam śivam vindet yad tad viśvasya kāraṇam adhas vaktram tu idam dvaita kalaṅka ekānta śātanam kṣīyate tad upāsāyām yena ūrdhva adhara ḍambaraḥ atra apāna udaye prāgvat ṣaṣṭi abda udaya yojanām yāvat kurvīta tuṭi ādeḥ yukta aṅgula vibhāgataḥ evam samāne pi vidhiḥ sa hi hārdīṣu nāḍiṣu saṃcaran sarvatodikkam daśadhā eva vibhāvyate daśa mukhyā mahānāḍīḥ pūrayan  eṣa tad gatāḥ nāḍī antara śritā nāḍīḥ krāman dehe sama sthitiḥ aṣṭāsu diś daleṣu eṣa krāman  tad dikpateḥ kramāt  ceṣṭitāni anukurvāṇaḥ  raudraḥ saumyaḥ ca bhāsate sa eva nāḍī tritaye vāma dakṣiṇa madhya ge indu arka agni maye mukhye caran  tiṣṭhati aharniśam sārdhanālī dvayam prāṇa śatāni nava yad sthitam tāvat vahan  ahorātram caturviṃśatidhā caret  viṣuvat vāsare prātar  sa aṃśām nālīm sa madhya gaḥ vāmetara udak savya anyaiḥ yāvat saṃkrānti pañcakam evam kṣīṇāsu pāda ūna caturdaśasu nāliṣu madhyāhne dakṣa viṣuvat nava prāṇa śatīm vahet  dakṣa udak anya udak dakṣaiḥ punar  saṃkrānti pañcakam navāsu śatam ekaikam tatas  viṣuvat uttaram pañcake pañcake tīte saṃkrānteḥ viṣuvat bahis  yadvat tathā antar  saṅkrāntiḥ nava prāṇa śatāni sā evam rātrau  api iti evam viṣuvat divasāt samāt ārabhya ahar niśā vṛddhi hrāsa saṅkrānti gaḥ pyasau rātrī anta dina pūrva aṃśau madhyāhnaḥ divasa kṣayaḥ sa śarvarī udayaḥ  madhyam udaktaḥ  viṣutedṛśī vyāptau viṣeḥ yatas  vṛttiḥ sāmyam ca vyāptiḥ ucyate tad arhati ca yaḥ kālaḥ  viṣuvat tad iha uditaḥ viṣuvat prabhṛti hrāsa vṛddhī ye dina rātri ge tad krameṇa eva saṃkrānti hrāsa vṛddhī divāniśoḥ ittham samāna marutaḥ  varṣa dvaya vikalpanam cāra ekatra na hi atra śvāsa praśvāsa carcanam samāne pi tuṭeḥ pūrvam yāvat ṣaṣṭi abda gocaram kāla saṃkhyā su sūkṣma eka cāra gā gaṇyate budhaiḥ saṃdhyā pūrvāhṇa madhyāhna madhyarātra ādi yad kila antar saṃkrānti gam grāhyam tad mukhyam tad phala uditeḥ uktaḥ samāna gaḥ kāla udāne tu nirūpyate prāṇa vyāptau yad uktam tad udāne pyatra kevalam nāsā śakti antayoḥ sthāne brahmarandhra ūrdhva dhāmanī tena udāne tra hṛdayāt mūrdhanya dvādaśānta gam tuṭi ādi ṣaṣṭi varṣa antam viśvam kālam vicārayet  vyāne tu viśvātma maye vyāpake krama varjite sūkṣma sūkṣma ucchalat rūpa mātraḥ kālaḥ  vyavasthitaḥ sṛṣṭiḥ pravilayaḥ sthemā saṃhāraḥ  nugrahaḥ  yatas  kramāt prāṇa ādike kāle tam tam tatra āśrayet tatas  prāṇa cāre tra yaḥ  varṇa pada mantra udayaḥ sthitaḥ yatna jaḥ  yatna jaḥ sūkṣmaḥ paraḥ sthūlaḥ sa kathyate ekaḥ  nāda ātmakaḥ  varṇaḥ sarva varṇa avibhāgavān saḥ  na stamita rūpa tvāt anāhata iha uditaḥ sa tu bhairava sadbhāvaḥ  mātṛsadbhāva eṣa saḥ parā sā ekākṣarā devī yatra līnam carācaram hrasva arṇa trayam ekaikam ravi aṅgulam atha itarat praveśa iti ṣaṣ varṇāḥ sūrya indu patha gāḥ kramāt  ikāra ukārayoḥ ādi sandhau saṃdhi akṣara dvayam e aḥ  iti praveśe tu ai au iti dvayam viduḥ ṣaṇṭha arṇāni praveśe tu dvādaśānta lalāṭayoḥ gale hṛdi ca bindu arṇa visargau paritas sthitau ka ādi pañcakam ādyasya varṇasya antar  sadā uditam evam sa sthāna varṇānām antar  sā sa arṇa santatiḥ hṛdi eṣa prāṇa rūpaḥ tu sa kāraḥ  jīvana ātmakaḥ binduḥ prakāśaḥ  ha arṇaḥ ca pūraṇa ātma tayā sthitaḥ uktaḥ paraḥ  yam udayaḥ  varṇānām sūkṣma ucyate praveśe ṣoḍaśa aunmukhye ravayaḥ ṣaṇṭha varjitāḥ tad eva indu arkam atra anye varṇāḥ sūkṣma udayaḥ tu ayam kālaḥ  rdhamātraḥ ka ādīnām trayastriṃśata ucyate mātrā hrasvāḥ pañca dīrgha aṣṭakam dvis tris  plutam tu lṝ ekāśītim imām ardha mātrāṇām āha naḥ guruḥ yad vaśāt bhagavān ekāśītikam mantram abhyadhāt  ekāśīti padā devī śaktiḥ proktā śiva ātmikā śrī mātaṅge tathā dharma saṃghāta ātmā śivaḥ  yatas  tathā tathā parāmarśa śakti cakra īśvaraḥ prabhuḥ sthūla ekāśīti pada ja parāmarśaiḥ vibhāvyate tatas  eva parāmarśaḥ  yāvatī ekaḥ samāpyate tāvat tad padam uktam naḥ suptij niyamayāntritam ekāśīti pada udāra vimarśaktam abṛṃhitaḥ sthūla upāyaḥ para upāyaḥ tu eṣa mātrā kṛtaḥ  layaḥ ardha mātrā nava nava syuḥ caturṣu caturṣu yad  aṅguleṣu iti ṣaṭtriṃśati ekāśīti pada udayaḥ aṅgule nava bhāgena vibhakte navamāśakāḥ vedā mātrā ardham anyat tu dvi catur ṣaṅguṇam trayam evam aṅgula randhra aṃśa catuṣka dvaya gam laghu dīrgham plutam kramāt dvi tri guṇam ardham tatas  pi hal kṣakāraḥ trī ardha mātrātmā mātrikaḥ sa tathā antarā viśrāntau  ardha mātrā asya tasmin  tu kalite sati aṅgula ardhe dri bhāgena tu ardha mātrā purā punar  kṣakāraḥ sarva saṃyoga grahaṇa ātmā tu sarvagaḥ sarva varṇa udaya ādi anta sandhiṣu udaya bhāj vibhuḥ ittham ṣaṭtriṃśake cāre varṇānām udayaḥ phale krūre saumye vilomena hādi yāvat apaścimam hṛdya kāraḥ  dvādaśānte hakāraḥ tad idam viduḥ aham ātmakam advaitam yaḥ prakāśa ātma viśramaḥ śiva śakti avibhāgena mātrā ekāśītikā tu iyam dvāsaptatau  aṅguleṣu dviguṇa tvena saṃsaret  uktaḥ sūkṣma udayaḥ traidham dvidhā uktaḥ tu para udayaḥ atha sthūla udayaḥ  rṇānām bhaṇyate guruṇā uditaḥ ekaikam ardha praharam dine varga aṣṭaka udayaḥ rātrau ca hrāsa vṛddhi atra kecid āhuḥ na ke pi tu eṣa varga udayaḥ  rātrau divā ca api ardha yāma gaḥ prāṇa trayodaśa śatī pañcāśat adhikā ca sā adhyardhā kila saṃkrāntiḥ varge varge divāniśoḥ tad aikye tu udayaḥ cāra śatānām saptaviṃśatiḥ nava vargān  tu ye prāhuḥ teṣām prāṇa śatī svīn[viḥ] sa tri bhāgā eva saṃkrāntiḥ varge pratyekam ucyate aharniśam tad aikye tu śatānām śruti cakṣuṣī sthūlaḥ  varga udayaḥ saḥ  yam atha arṇa udaya ucyate ekaika varṇe prāṇānām dvi śatam ṣoḍaśa adhikam bahis caṣaka ṣaṭtriṃśat dina ittham tathā niśi śatam aṣṭa uttaram tatra raudram śāktam atha uttaram yāmala sthiti yoge tu rudra śakti avibhāgi tā dina rātrī avibhāge tu dṛś vahni abdhi asu cāraṇāḥ sa pañcama aṃśā nāḍī ca bahis varṇa udayaḥ smṛtaḥ iti pañcāśikā sā iyam varṇānām paricarcitā ekonām ye tu tām āhuḥ tad matam saṃpracakṣmahe vedāḥ cārāḥ pañcama aṃśa nyūnam cāra ardham ekaśas  varṇe dhikam tad dviguṇam avibhāge divāniśoḥ sthūlaḥ  varṇa udayaḥ saḥ  yam purā sūkṣmaḥ  nigadyate iti kāla tattvam uditam śāstra mukha āgama nija anubhava siddham atha śrī tantrāloke atha parama rahasyaḥ  yam cakrāṇām bhaṇyate bhyudayaḥ b iti ayatna jam ākhyātam yatna jam tu nigadyate bīja piṇḍa ātmakam sarvam saṃvidaḥ spandana ātma tām vidadhat para saṃvittau  upāya iti varṇitam yathā raghaṭṭa cakra agra ghaṭī yantra ogha vāhanam eka anusaṃdhi yatnena citram yantra udayam bhajet  eka anusaṃdhāna balāt jāte mantra udaye niśam tad mantradevatā yatnāt tādātmyena prasīdati khe rasa eka akṣi nitya utthe tad ardham dvika piṇḍake trike sapta sahasrāṇi dviśatī iti udayaḥ  mataḥ catuṣke tu sahasrāṇi pañca ca eva catuḥśatī pañca arṇe bdhi sahasrāṇi triśatī viṃśatiḥ tathā ṣaṭke sahasra tritayam ṣaṭśatī codayaḥ  bhavet  saptake tri sahasram tu ṣaṣ aśīti adhikam smṛtam śataiḥ tu saptaviṃśatyā varṇa aṣṭaka vikalpite caturviṃśati śatyā tu nava arṇeṣu udayaḥ  bhavet  adhiṣaṣṭi ekaviṃśatyā śatānām daśa varṇake ekānna viṃśati śatam catuḥṣaṣṭiḥ śiva arṇake aṣṭādaśa śatāni syuḥ udayaḥ  dvādaśa arṇake trayodaśa arṇe dvāṣaṣṭyā śatāni kila ṣoḍaśa tricatvāriṃśatā pañcadaśa iti bhuvana arṇake caturdaśa śatī kha abdhiḥ syāt pañcadaśa varṇake trayodaśa śatī sārdhā ṣoḍaśa arṇe tu kathyate śatadvādaśikā saptadaśa arṇe sa ekasaptatiḥ aṣṭādaśa arṇe vijñeyā śatadvādaśikā budhaiḥ caturviṃśati saṃkhyāke cakre nava śatī bhavet  saptaviṃśati saṃkhyāte tu udayaḥ  ṣṭa śata ātmakaḥ dvātriṃśake mahā cakre ṣaṭśatī pañcasaptatiḥ dvi caturviṃśake cakre sārdhām śata catuṣṭayīm udayam piṇḍa yoga jñaḥ piṇḍa mantreṣu lakṣayet  catuṣpañcāśake cakre śatānām tu catuṣṭayam saptatriṃśat saha ardhena triśati aṣṭa aṣṭake bhavet  ardham ardha tri bhāgaḥ ca ṣaṭṣaṣṭiḥ dviśatī bhavet  ekāśīti pade cakre udayaḥ prāṇa cāra gaḥ cakre tu ṣaṇṇavati ākhye sa pādā dviśatī bhavet  aṣṭottaraśate cakre dviśataḥ tu udayaḥ  bhavet  krameṇa ittham idam cakram ṣaṣ kṛtvā u dviguṇam yadā tatas  pi dviguṇe ṣṭa aṃśasya ardham adhyardham ekakam tatas  pi sūkṣma kuśalaiḥ ardha ardha ādi prakalpane bhāga ṣoḍaśaka sthityā sūkṣmaḥ cāraḥ  bhilakṣyate evam prayatna saṃruddha prāṇa cārasya yoginaḥ krameṇa prāṇa cārasya grāsa eva upajāyate prāṇa grāsa krama avāpta kāla saṃkarṣaṇa sthitiḥ saṃvid ekā eva pūrṇā syāt jñāna bheda vyapohanāt tathā hi prāṇa cārasya navasya anudaye sati na kāla bheda janitaḥ  jñāna bhedaḥ prakalpate saṃvedya bhedāt na jñānam bhinnam śikhari vṛttavat  kālaḥ tu bhedakaḥ tasya sa tu sūkṣmaḥ kṣaṇaḥ  mataḥ saukṣmyasya ca avadhiḥ jñānam yāvat tiṣṭhati sa kṣaṇaḥ anyathā na sa nirvaktum nipuṇaiḥ api pāryate jñānam kiyat bhavet tāvat tad abhāvaḥ  na bhāsate tad abhāvaḥ ca naḥ tāvat yāvat tatra akṣa vartmani arthe vā ātma pradeśe vā na saṃyoga vibhāgi tā sā ced udayate spanda mayī tad prāṇa gā dhruvam bhavet eva tatas  prāṇa spanda abhāve na sā bhavet  tad abhāvāt na vijñāna abhāvaḥ sā evam tu sā eva dhīḥ na ca asau vastu tas  dīrghā kāla bheda vyapohanāt  vastu tas  hi ata eva iyam kālam saṃvid na saṃspṛśet  ata ekā eva saṃvittiḥ nānā rūpe tathā tathā vindānā nirvikalpā api vikalpaḥ  bhāva gocare spanda antaram na yāvat tad uditam tāvat eva saḥ tāvān ekaḥ  vikalpaḥ syāt vividham vastu kalpayan ye tu ittham na viduḥ teṣām vikalpaḥ  na upapadyate sa hi ekaḥ  na bhavet kaścid  trijagatyā api jātucit  śabdārūṣaṇayā jñānam vikalpaḥ kila kathyate sā ca syāt kramikā eva ittham kim katham kaḥ  vikalpayet  ghaṭa iti api na iyān syāt vikalpaḥ kā kathā sthitau na vikalpaḥ ca kaḥ  pyasti yaḥ  mātrā mātra niṣṭhitaḥ na ca jñāna samūhaḥ  sti teṣām ayugapad sthiteḥ tena astaṅgata eva eṣa vyavahāraḥ  vikalpa jaḥ tasmāt spanda antaram yāvat na udiyāt tāvat ekakam vijñānam tad vikalpa ātma dharma koṭīḥ api spṛśet  ekāśīti pada udāra śakti āmarśa ātmakaḥ tatas  vikalpaḥ śiva tā dāyī pūrvam eva nirūpitaḥ yathā karṇau nartayāmi iti evam yatnāt tathā bhavet  cakra cāra gatāt yatnāt tadvat tad cakra gā eva dhīḥ japa homa arcana ādīnām prāṇa sāmyam atas  vidhiḥ siddhāmate kuṇḍalinī śaktiḥ prāṇa sama unmanā uktam ca yoginī kaule tad etad parameśinā pada mantra akṣare cakre vibhāgam śakti tattva gam padeṣu kṛtvā mantra jñaḥ  japa ādau phala bhāj bhavet  dvi tri sapta aṣṭa saṃkhyātam lopayet śatika udayam iti śakti sthitā mantrā vidyā vā cakra nāyakāḥ pada piṇḍa svarūpeṇa jñātvā yojyāḥ sadā priye nitya udaye mahā tattve udaya sthe sadāśive ayuktāḥ śakti mārge tu na japtāḥ ca udayena ye te na siddhyanti yatnena japtāḥ koṭi śataiḥ api mālāmantreṣu sarveṣu mānasaḥ  japa ucyate upāṃśuḥ vā śakti udayam teṣām na parikalpayet  pada mantreṣu sarveṣu yāvat tad pada śakti gam śakyate satatam yuktaiḥ tāvat japyam tu sādhakaiḥ tāvatī teṣu vai saṃkhyā padeṣu pada saṃjñitā tāvantam udayam kṛtvā tri pada ukti āditaḥ kramāt  dvādaśa ākhye dvādaśite cakre sārdham śatam bhavet  udayaḥ tad hi sa catuścatvāriṃśat śatam bhavet  ṣoḍaśa ākhye dvādaśite dvānavati adhike śate cāra ardhena samam proktam śatam dvādaśaka adhikam ṣoḍaśa ākhye ṣoḍaśite bhavet caturaśīti gaḥ udayaḥ dvi śatam tad hi ṣaṭpañcāśat samuttaram cāra aṣṭa bhāgān  trīn atra kathayanti adhikān budhāḥ aṣṭa aṣṭake dvādaśite pāda ardham viṃśatim vasūn udayaḥ saptaśatikā sa aṣṭā ṣaṣṭiḥ yatas  hi saḥ eṣa cakra udayaḥ proktaḥ sādhakānām hita āvahaḥ niruddhya mānasīḥ vṛttīḥ cakre viśrāntim āgataḥ vyutthāya yāvat viśrāmyet tāvat cāra udayaḥ  hi ayam pūrṇe samudaye tu atra praveśa aikātmya nirgamāḥ traya iti ata eva uktaḥ siddhau madhya udayaḥ  varaḥ ādi anta udaya nirmuktā madhyama udaya saṃyutāḥ mantra vidyā cakra gaṇāḥ siddhi bhājaḥ  bhavanti hi mantra cakra udaya jñaḥ tu vidyā cakra udaya artha vid  kṣipram siddhyet iti proktam śrīmat dviṃśatike trike dvis tris catur vā mātrābhiḥ vidyām vā cakram eva vā tattva udaya yutam nityam pṛthak bhūtam japet sadā piṇḍa akṣara padaiḥ mantram ekaikam śakti tattva gam bahu akṣaraḥ tu yaḥ  mantraḥ  vidyā vā cakram eva vā śakti stham na eva tam tatra vibhāgaḥ tu oṃna monta gaḥ asmin  tattva udaye tasmāt ahorātraḥ triśas triśas  vibhajyate vibhāgaḥ ca punar eva triśas triśas  pūrva udaye tu viśramya dvitīyena ullaset yadā viśet ca ardhardhikā yogāt tadā ukta ardha udayaḥ  bhavet  yadā pūrṇa udaya ātmā tu samaḥ kālaḥ trike sphuret  praveśa viśrānti ullāse syāt sva tri aṃśa udayaḥ tadā eti eṣa kāla vibhavaḥ prāṇa eva pratiṣṭhitaḥ sa spade khe sa tad cityām tena asyām viśva niṣṭhiatiḥ atas  saṃvid pratiṣṭhānau yatas  viśva laya udayau śakti ante dhvani tad spandā saṃkhyātā vāstavī tatas  uktam śrī mālinītantre gātre yatra eva kutracid  vikāra upajāyeta tad tattvam tattvam uttamam prāṇe pratiṣṭhitaḥ kālaḥ tad ā āviṣṭā ca yad tanuḥ dehe pratiṣṭhitasya asya tatas  rūpam nirūpyate cit spanda prāṇa vṛttīnām antyā yā sthūla tā suṣiḥ sā nāḍī rūpa tām etya deham saṃtānayet imam śrī svacchande ta eva uktam yathā parṇam svatantubhiḥ vyāptam tadvat tanuḥ dvāra dvāri bhāvena nāḍibhiḥ pādāṅguṣṭha ādika ūrdhva stha brahma kuṇḍalikā anta gaḥ kālaḥ samastaḥ caturaśītau  eva aṅguleṣu itas  dvādaśānta avadhim kiṃcid sūkṣma kāla sthitim viduḥ ṣaṇṇavatyām adhas  ṣaṣ dvi kramāt ca aṣṭa uttaram śatam atra madhyama saṃcāri prāṇa udaya laya antare viśve sṛṣṭi layāḥ te tu citrā vāyu antara kramāt iti eṣa sūkṣma parimarśana śīlanīyaḥ cakra udayaḥ  nubhava śāstra dṛśā mayā uktaḥ  ch atha śītantrāloke aṣṭamam āhnikam deśa adhvanaḥ  pyatha samāsa vikāsa yogāt saṃgīyate vidhiḥ ayam śiva śāstra dṛṣṭaḥ b vicāritaḥ  yam kālādhvā kriyāśakti mayaḥ prabhoḥ mūrti vaicitrya jaḥ tad jaḥ  deśa adhvā atha nirūpyate adhvā samasta eva ayam cit mātre saṃpratiṣṭhitaḥ yad tatra na hi viśrāntam tad nabhaḥkusumāyate saṃvid dvāreṇa tad sṛṣṭe śūnye dhiyi marutsu ca nāḍī cakra anucakreṣu barhiḥ dehe dhva saṃsthitiḥ tatra adhvā evam nirūpya u yam yatas tad prakriyā kramam anusaṃdadhadeva drāg yogī bhairava tām vrajet  didṛkṣayā eva sarva arthān yadā vyāpya avatiṣṭhate tadā kim bahunā uktena iti uktam spandaśāsane jñātvā samastam adhvānam tad īśeṣu vilāpayet  tān deha prāṇa dhī cakre pūrvavat  gālayet kramāt  tad samastam sva saṃvittau sā saṃvid bharita ātmikā upāsyamānā saṃsāra sāgara pralaya analaḥ śrī mahīkṣa uttare ca etān adhva īśān guruḥ abravīt  brahma anantāt pradhāna antam viṣṇuḥ puṃsaḥ kalā anta gam rudraḥ  granthau ca māyāyām īśaḥ sādākhya gocare anāśritaḥ śivaḥ tasmāt vyāptā tad vyāpakaḥ paraḥ evam śiva tvam āpannam iti matvā nyarūpyata na prakriyā param jñānam iti svacchandaśāsane triśiraḥ śāsane bodhaḥ  mūla madhya agra kalpitaḥ ṣaṭtriṃśat tattva saṃrambhaḥ smṛtiḥ bheda vikalpanā avyāhata vibhāgaḥ  smibhāvaḥ  mūlam tu bodha gam samasta tattva bhāvaḥ  yam sva ātmani eva avibhāgakaḥ bodha madhyam bhavet kiṃcid ādhāra ādheya lakṣaṇam tattva bheda vibhāgena svabhāva sthiti lakṣaṇam bodha agram tad tu vid bodham nistaraṅgam bṛhat sukham saṃvid eka ātma tā ānīta bhūta bhāva pura ādikaḥ avyavacchinna saṃvittiḥ bhairavaḥ parameśvaraḥ śrī devyāyāmale ca uktam ṣaṭtriṃśat tattva sundaram adhvānam ṣaḍvidham dhyāyan sadyas  śivam ayaḥ  bhavet  yadi api amuṣya nāthasya saṃvitti anatirekiṇaḥ pūrṇasya ūrdhva ādi madhya anta vyavasthā na asti vāstavī tathā api pratipattṝṇām pratipādayituḥ tathā sva svarūpa anusāreṇa madhya āditva ādi kalpanāḥ tatas  pramātṛ saṃkalpa niyamāt  pārthivam viduḥ tattvam sarva antarāla stham yad sarva āvaraṇaiḥ vṛtam tad atra pārthive tattve kathyate bhuvana sthitiḥ netā kaṭāha rudrāṇām anantaḥ kāma sevinām pota ārūḍhaḥ  jalasya antar madya pāna vighūrṇitaḥ sa devam bhairavam dhyāyan nāgaiḥ ca parivāritaḥ kāla agreḥ bhuvanam ca ūrdhve koṭi yojanam ucchritam lokānām bhasmasāt bhāva bhayāt na ūrdhva sa vīkṣate sa ca vyāptā api viśvasya yasmāt pluṣyan  imām bhuvam narakebhyaḥ purā vyaktaḥ tena asau tad adhas  mataḥ daśa koṭyaḥ  vibhoḥ jvālā tad ardha śūnyam ūrdhvatas  tad ūrdhve naraka adhīśāḥ kramāt duḥkha eka vedanāḥ śdhaḥ madhye tad ūrdhve ca sthitā bheda antaraiḥ vṛtāḥ avīci kumbhī pāka ākhya rauravāḥ teṣu anukramāt  ekādaśa ekādaśa ca daśa iti antar  śara agni tad  pratyekam eṣām eka ūnā koṭiḥ ucchritiḥ antaram lakṣam atra kha vedāsya saṃkhyānām antarā sthitiḥ kūṣmāṇḍa ūrdhve lakṣa ūna koṭi sthānaḥ tad īśitā śāstra viruddha ācaraṇāt kṛṣṇam ye karma vidadhate tatra bhīmaiḥ loka puruṣaiḥ pīḍyante bhoga paryantam ye sakṛt api parameśam śivam ekāgreṇa cetasā śaraṇam yānti na te naraka yujaḥ kṛṣṇam teṣām sukha alpa tā dāyi sahasra navaka utsedham eka antaram atha kramāt  pātāla aṣṭakam ekaikam aṣṭame hāṭakaḥ prabhuḥ pratilokam niyukta ātmā śrīkaṇṭhaḥ  haṭhataḥ bahūḥ siddhīḥ dadāti asau  evam śrīmat raurava śāsane vratinaḥ  ye cikarma sthā niṣiddha ācāra kāriṇaḥ dīkṣitā api ye lupta samayā na ca kurvate prāyaścittān  tathā tad sthā vāma ācārasya dūṣakāḥ deva agni dravya vṛtti aṃśa jīvinaḥ ca uttama sthitāḥ adhas stha gāruḍa ādi anya mantra sevā parāyaṇāḥ te hāṭaka vibhoḥ agre kiṅkarā vividha ātmakāḥ te tu tatra api deveśam bhaktyā ced paryupāsate tad īśa tattve līyante kramāt ca parame śive anyathā ye tu vartante tad bhoga nirata ātmakāḥ te kāla vahni saṃtāpa dīna ākranda parāyaṇāḥ guṇa tattve nilīyante tatas  sṛṣṭi mukhe punar  pātyante mātṛbhiḥ ghora yātanā ogha purassaram adhama adhama deheṣu nija karma anurūpataḥ mānuṣa anteṣu tatra api kecid mantra vidaḥ kramāt  mucyante nye tu badhyante pūrva kṛtya anusārataḥ iti eṣa gaṇa vṛttāntaḥ  nāmnā hulahula ādinā proktam bhagavatā śrīmat ānanda adhika śāsane pātāla ūrdhve sahasrāṇi viṃśatiḥ bhū kaṭāhakaḥ siddhātantre tu pātāla pṛṣṭhe yakṣī samāvṛtam bhadrakālyāḥ puram yatra tābhiḥ krīḍanti sādhakāḥ tatas tamaḥ tapta bhūmiḥ tatas śūnyam tatas  hayaḥ etāni yātanā sthānam guru mantra ādi dūṣiṇām tatas  bhūmi ūrdhva [madhya] taḥ meruḥ sahasrāṇi sa ṣoḍaśa magnaḥ tad mūla vistāraḥ tad dvayena ūrdhva vistṛtiḥ sahasra abdhi vasu ucchrāyaḥ  haimaḥ sarva amara ālayaḥ madhya ūrdhva adhas  samudvṛtta śarāva caturaśrakaḥ bhairavīyam ca tad liṅgam dharaṇī ca asya pīṭhikā sarve devāḥ  nilīnā hi tatra tad pūjitam sadā madhye meru sabhā dhātuḥ tad īśa diśi ketanam jyotiṣka śikharam śaṃbhoḥ śrīkaṇṭha aṃśaḥ ca sa prabhuḥ avaruhya sahasrāṇi manovatyāḥ caturdaśa cakravāṭaḥ caturdikkaḥ  meruḥ atra tu lokapāḥ amarāvatikendrasya pūrvasyām dakṣiṇena tām atsaraḥ siddha sādhyāḥ tām uttareṇa vināyakāḥ tejovatī sva diśi agneḥ purī tām paścimena tu viśvedevā viśvakarmā kramāt tad anugāḥ ca ye yāmyām saṃyamanī tām tu paścimena kramāt  sthitāḥ mātṛnandā sva saṃkhyātā rudrāḥ tad sādhakāḥ tathā kṛṣṇa aṅgārā nirṛtiḥ ca tām pūrveṇa piśācakāḥ rakṣāṃsi siddha gandharvāḥ tu uttareṇa uttareṇa tām vāruṇī śuddhavatī ākhyā bhūta oghaḥ  dakṣiṇena tām uttareṇa uttareṇa enām vasu vidyādharāḥ kramāt  vāyoḥ gandhavatī tasyāḥ  dakṣiṇe kinnarāḥ punar  vīṇā sarasvatī devī nāradaḥ tumburuḥ tathā mahā udaya indoḥ guhyāḥ syuḥ paścime syāḥ punar  punar  kuberaḥ karma devāḥ ca tathā tad sādhakā api yaśasvinī maheśasya tasyāḥ paścimataḥ hariḥ dakṣiṇe dakṣiṇe brahma aśvinau dhanvantariḥ kramāt  mairave cakravāṭe smin  evam mukhyāḥ puraḥ ṣṭadhā antarāla gatāḥ tu anyāḥ punar  ṣaḍviṃśatiḥ smṛtāḥ iṣṭāpūrta ratāḥ puṇye varṣeye bhārate narāḥ te meru gāḥ sakṛt śambhum ye vā arcanti yathocitam meroḥ pradakṣiṇa āpya udak dikṣu viṣkambha parvatāḥ mandaraḥ  gandhamādaḥ ca vipulaḥ  tha supārśvakaḥ sita pīta nīla raktāḥ te kramāt pāda parvatāḥ etaiḥ bhuvam avaṣṭabhya meruḥ tiṣṭhati niścalaḥ caitraratha nandana ākhye vaiśrājam pitṛ vanam vanāni āhuḥ rakta uda māna sa sitam bhadram ca etad catuṣṭayam sarasām vṛkṣāḥ kadamba jambu aśvattha nyagrodhakāḥ kramaśas  eṣu ca caturṣu acaleṣu trayam trayam kramaśa etad āmnātam meru adhaḥ lavaṇa abdhi antam jambudvīpaḥ samantatas lakṣa mātraḥ sa navadhā jātaḥ  maryāda parvataiḥ niṣadhaḥ  hemakūṭaḥ ca himavān dakṣiṇe trayaḥ lakṣam sahasranavatiḥ tad aśītiḥ iti kramāt  nīlaḥ śvetaḥ triśṛṅgaḥ ca tāvantaḥ savyatas  punar  meroḥ ṣaṭ ete maryāda acalāḥ pūrva aparāyatāḥ pūrvatas  mālyavān paścāt gandhamādana saṃjñitaḥ savya uttara āyatau tau tu catustriṃśat sahasrakau aṣṭau  ete tatas  pyanyau dvau dvau pūrva ādiṣu kramāt  jāṭharaḥ kūṭa himavat yātra jārudhi śṛṅgiṇaḥ evam sthitaḥ  vibhāgaḥ  tra varṣa siddhyai nirūpyate samantāt cakravāṭa adhas  narka indu  caturaśrakam sahasra nava vistīrṇam ilā ākhyam tri mukha āyuṣam meroḥ paścimataḥ gandhamādaḥ  yaḥ tasya paścime ketumālam kula ādrīṇām saptakena vibhūṣitam meroḥ pūrva mālyavān yaḥ  bhadrāśvaḥ tasya pūrvatas  sahasra daśaka āyuḥ tad sa pañca kula parvatam pūrva paścimatas  savya uttaratas ca kramāt ime dvātriṃśat ca catustriṃśat sahasrāṇi nirūpite meroḥ udak  śṛṅgavān yaḥ tad bahis  kuru varṣakam cāpavat nava sāhasram āyuḥ tatra trayodaśa kuru varṣasya uttare tha vāyavye bdhau kramāt śarāḥ daśa ca iti sahasrāṇi dvīpau candraḥ  tha bhadrakaḥ yau śveta śṛṅgiṇau meroḥ vāme madhye hiraṇmayam tayoḥ navaka vistīrṇam āyuḥ ca ardha trayodaśa tatra vai vāmatas  śveta nīlayaḥ ramyakaḥ  ntare sahasra nava vistīrṇam āyuḥ dvādaśa tāni ca meroḥ dakṣiṇataḥ hema niṣadhau yau tad antare haryākhyam nava sāhasram tad sahasra adhika āyuṣam tatra eva dakṣiṇe hema himavat dvitaya antare kainnaram nava sāhasram tad sahasra adhika āyuṣam tatra eva dakṣiṇe meroḥ himavān yasya dakṣiṇe bhāratam nava sāhasram cāpavat karma bhoga bhūḥ ilāvṛtam ketubhadram kuruhairaṇya ramyakam hari kinnara varṣe ca bhoga bhūḥ na tu karma bhūḥ atra bāhulyataḥ karma bhū bhāvaḥ  trāpya karmaṇām paśūnām karma saṃskāraḥ syāt tādṛś dṛḍha saṃskṛteḥ saṃbhavanti api asaṃskārā bhārate nyatra ca api hi dṛḍha prāktana saṃskārāt īśa icchātaḥ śubha aśubham sthāna antare pi karma asti dṛṣṭam tad ca purātane tatra tretā sadā kālaḥ  bhārate tu caturyugam bhārate nava khaṇḍam ca sāmudreṇa ambha sā atra ca sthalam pañcaśatī tadvat jalam ca iti vibhajyate indraḥ kaśeruḥ tāmra ābhaḥ  nāgīyaḥ prāk gabhastimān saumya gāndharva vārāhāḥ kanyā ākhyam ca asamudrataḥ kanyā dvīpe ca navame dakṣiṇena abdhi madhya gāḥ upadvīpāḥ ṣaḍ  kula adri saptakena vibhūṣite aṅga yava malaya śaṅkuḥ kumuda varāhau ca malaya gaḥ gasti tatra eva ca trikūṭe laṅkā ṣaṭ amī hi upadvīpāḥ dvīpa upadvīpa gāḥ prāyaḥ mlecchā nānāvidhā janāḥ muktā kāñcana ratna āḍhyā iti śrī ruruśāsane bhārate yad kṛtam karma kṣapitam vā api avīcitaḥ śiva antam tena muktiḥ vā kanyā ākhye tu viśeṣataḥ mahākāla ādikā rudra koṭiḥ atra eva bhārate gaṅgā ādi pañcaśatikā janma tena atra durlabham anya varṣeṣu paśuvat  bhogāt karma ativāhanam prāpyam manoratha atītam api bhārata janmanām nānā varṇa āśrama ācāra sukha duḥkha vicitra tā kanyā dvīpe yatas tena karma bhūḥ sā iyam uttamā puṃsā sita asitāni atra kurvatām kila siddhi atas  para aparau svar nirayau  iti raurava vārtike evam meroḥ adhaḥ jambūḥ abhitas  yaḥ sa vistarāt  syāt  saptadaśadhā khaṇḍaiḥ navabhiḥ tu samāsatas  manoḥ svāyaṃbhuvasya āsan sutā daśa tatas trayaḥ prāvrajan  atha jambu ākhye rājā yaḥ  gnīdhra nāmakaḥ tasya abhavat nava sutāḥ tatas  yam navakhaṇḍakaḥ nābhiḥ yaḥ navamaḥ tasya naptā bharata ārṣabhiḥ tasya aṣṭau tanayāḥ sākam kanyayā navamom śakaḥ bhuktaiḥ taiḥ navadhā tasmāt lakṣa yojana mātrakāt lakṣa eka mātraḥ  lavaṇaḥ tad bāhye sya puraḥ drayaḥ ṛṣabhaḥ  dundubhiḥ dhūmraḥ kaṅka droṇa indavaḥ  hi udak  varāha nandana aśokāḥ paścāt  saha balāhakau dakṣiṇa cakra mainākau vāḍavaḥ  ntaḥ tayoḥ sthitaḥ abdheḥ dakṣiṇatas  kha akṣi sahasra atikramāt  giriḥ vidyutvān  tri sahasra ucchrit āyāmaḥ  tra phala āśinaḥ mala digdhā dīrgha keśa śmaśravaḥ  gaḥ sadharmakāḥ nagnāḥ saṃvatsara aśīti jīvinaḥ tṛṇa bhojinaḥ niryantrāṇi sadā tatra dvārāṇi bila siddhaye iti etad  gurubhiḥ gītam śrīmat raurava śāsane ittham ya eṣa lavaṇa samudraḥ pratipāditaḥ tad bahis  ṣaṭ amī dvīpāḥ pratyekam sva arṇavaiḥ vṛtāḥ krama dvi guṇitāḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ manu putraiḥ adhiṣṭhitāḥ śāka kuśa krauñcāḥ śalmali gomedha abjam iti ṣaṣ dvīpāḥ c kṣīra dadhi sarpiḥ aikṣava madirā madhura ambukāḥ ṣaṣ ambudhayaḥ medhātithiḥ vapuṣmān jyotiṣmān dyutimatā havī rājā saṃvara iti śāka ādiṣu jambudvīpe nyarūpi ca āgnīdhraḥ giri saptaka parikalpita tāvat khaṇḍāḥ tu pañca śāka ādyāḥ puṣkara saṃjñaḥ  dvi dalaḥ  hari yama varuṇa indavaḥ  tra pūrva ādau tripañcāśat ca lakṣāṇi dvi koṭi ayuta pañcakam svādu arṇava antam meru ardhāt yojana nām iyam pramā saptama jaladheḥ bāhye haimī bhūḥ koṭi daśakam atha lakṣam ucchrityā vistārāt ayutam loka itara acalaḥ kathitaḥ lokāloka diś aṣṭaka saṃstham rudra aṣṭakam sa lokeśam kevalam iti api kecid lokāloka antare raviḥ na bahis  pitṛ deva pathau  asya udak dakṣiṇa gau sva jāt pare vīthyau bhānoḥ uttara dakṣiṇam ayana dvayam etad eva kathayanti asarveṣām uttaraḥ  meruḥ lokālokaḥ ca dakṣiṇaḥ udaya astamayau  ittham sūryasya paribhāvayet  ardharātraḥ  marāvatyām yāmyāyāmaḥ tam eva ca madhyandinam tad vāruṇyām saumye sūrya udayaḥ smṛtaḥ udayaḥ yaḥ  marāvatyām saḥ  rdharātra u yama ālaye ke stam saumye ca madhyāhna ittham sūrya gata āgate pañcatriṃ śad koṭi saṃkhyā lakṣāṇi ekonaviṃśatiḥ catvāriṃśat sahasrāṇi dhvāntam loka acalāt bahis  sapta sāgara mānaḥ tu garbhoda ākhyaḥ samudrarāj  lokālokasya paratas  yad garbhe nikhilā eva bhūḥ siddhātantre tra garbha abdheḥ tīre kauśeya saṃjñitam maṇḍalam garuḍaḥ tatra siddha pakṣa samāvṛtaḥ krīḍantim parvata agre te nava ca atra kula adrayaḥ tatas  uṣṇa udakāḥ triṃśat nadyaḥ pātāla gāḥ tatas  catur diś naimira udyānam yoginī sevitam sadā tatas  meruḥ tatas  nāgā meghā hemāṇḍakam tatas  brahmaṇaḥ  ṇḍa kaṭāhena meroḥ ardhena koṭayaḥ pañcāśat evam daśasu dicu bhūrloka saṃjñitam paśu khaga mṛga taru mānuṣa sarīsṛpaiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ eṣa bhūrlokaḥ vyāptaḥ piśāca rakṣogandharvāṇām sa yakṣāṇām vidyā bhṛtām ca kim vā bahunā sarvasya bhūta sargasya abhimānataḥ  yatheṣṭam bhoga sthānam nivāsaḥ ca bhuvarlokaḥ tathā tu ā arkāt lakṣam ekam tad antare daśa vāyu pathāḥ te ca pratyekam ayuta antarāḥ ādyaḥ  vāyupathaḥ tatra vitatas paricarcyate pañcāśat yojana ūrdhve syāt ṛta ṛddhiḥ nāma mārutaḥ āpyāyakaḥ sa jantūnām tatas  prācetasaḥ  bhavet  pañcāśat yojanāt ūrdhva tasmāt ūrdhva śatena tu senānī vāyuḥ atra ete mūka meghāḥ taḍit mucaḥ ye mahyāḥ krośa mātreṇa tiṣṭhanti jala varṣiṇaḥ tebhya ūrdhva  śatāt meghā bheka ādi prāṇi varṣiṇaḥ pañcāśat ūrdhvam oghaḥ  tra viṣa vāri pravarṣiṇaḥ meghāḥ skanda udbhavāḥ ca anye piśācā ogha mārute tatas  pañcāśat ūrdhvam syuḥ meghā māraka saṃjñakāḥ tatra sthāne mahādeva janmānaḥ te vināyakāḥ ye haranti kṛtam karma narāṇām akṛtātmanām pañcāśat ūrdhvam vajrāṅkaḥ  vāyuḥ atra upala ambudāḥ vidyādhara adhamāḥ ca atra vajra aṅke saṃpratiṣṭhitāḥ ye vidyā pauruṣe ye ca śmaśāna ādi prasādhane mṛtāḥ tad siddhi siddhāḥ te vajrāṃke maruti sthitāḥ pañcāśat ūrdhvam vajra aṃkāt vaidyutaḥ  śani varṣiṇaḥ abdā apsarasaḥ ca atra ye ca puṇya kṛtaḥ  narāḥ bhṛgau vahnau jale ye ca saṃgrāme ca anivartinaḥ gograhe vadhya mokṣe vā mṛtāḥ te vaidyute sthitāḥ vaidyutāt raivataḥ tāvān  tatra puṣṭi vaha ambudāḥ ūrdhvam ca roga ambumucaḥ saṃvartāḥ tad anantare rocanā añjana bhasma ādi siddhāḥ tatra eva raivate krodha udaka mucām sthānam viṣāvartaḥ sa mārutaḥ pañcāśat ūrdhvam tatra eva durdina abdā hutāśa jāḥ vidyādhara viśeṣāḥ ca tathā ye parameśvaram gāndharveṇa sadā arcanti viṣa āvarte tha te sthitāḥ viṣāvartāt śatāt ūrdhva durjayaḥ śvāsa saṃbhavaḥ brahmaṇaḥ  tra sthitā meghāḥ pralaye vāta kāriṇaḥ puṣkara abdā vāyu gamā gandharvāḥ ca parāvahe jīmūta meghāḥ tad saṃjñāḥ tathā vidyādhara uttamāḥ ye ca rūpa vratā lokā āvahe te pratiṣṭhitāḥ mahāvahe tu īśakṛtāḥ prajā hita kara ambudāḥ mahā parivahe meghāḥ kapāla utthā maheśituḥ mahā parivaha antaḥ  yam ṛta ṛddheḥ prāc marut pathaḥ agni kanyā mātaraḥ ca rudra śaktyā tu adhiṣṭhitāḥ dvitīye tad pare siddhacāraṇā nija karma jāḥ turye deva āyudhāni aṣṭau diggajāḥ pañcame punar  ṣaṣṭhe garutmān anyasmiṅ gaṅgāni atra vṛṣaḥ  vibhuḥ dakṣaḥ tu navame brahma śaktyā samadhiti[ ni]ṣṭhitaḥ daśame vasavaḥ  rudrā ādityāḥ ca marut pathe nava yojana sāhasraḥ  vigrahaḥ  rkasya maṇḍalam triguṇam jñānaśaktiḥ sā tapati arka tayā prabhoḥ svarlokaḥ tu bhuvarlokāt dhruva antam paribhāṣyate sūryāt lakṣeṇa śītāṃśuḥ kriyāśaktiḥ śivasya sā candrān lakṣeṇa nākṣatram tatas  lakṣa dvayena tu pratyekam bhaumataḥ sūrya suta ante pañcakam viduḥ saurāt lakṣeṇa saptarṣi vargaḥ tasmāt dhruvaḥ tathā brahma eva apara rūpeṇa brahma sthāne dhruvaḥ  calaḥ medhī bhūtaḥ  vimānānām sarveṣām upari dhruvaḥ atra baddhāni sarvāṇi api ūhi ante nila maṇḍale svassapta māruta skandhā āmegha ādyāḥ pradhānataḥ itas ca kratu hotṛ ādi kṛtvā jñāna vivarjitāḥ svar yānti tad kṣaye lokam mānuṣyam puṇya śeṣatas  evam bhūmeḥ dhruva antam syāt lakṣāṇi daśa pañca ca dve koṭī pañca ca aśītiḥ lakṣāṇi svargataḥ  mahān mārkaṇḍa ādyā ṛṣi muni siddhāḥ tatra pratiṣṭhitāḥ nivartita adhikārāḥ ca devāḥ  mahati saṃsthitāḥ mahā antarāle tatra anye tu adhikāra bhujaḥ  janāḥ aṣṭau koṭyaḥ  mahat lokāt janaḥ  tra kapila ādayaḥ tiṣṭhanti sādhyāḥ tatra eva bahavaḥ sukha bhāginaḥ janāt tapa urka koṭyaḥ tra sanaka ādyā mahā dhiyaḥ prajāpatīnām tatra adhikāraḥ  brahma ātmajanmanām brahma ālayaḥ tu tapasaḥ satyaḥ ṣoḍaśa koṭayaḥ tatra sthitaḥ sa svayambhūḥ viśvam āviṣkaroti adaḥ satye vedāḥ tathā ca anye karma dhyānena bhāvitāḥ ānanda niṣṭhāḥ tatra ūrdhvekoṭiḥ vairiñcam āsanam brahmāsanāt koṭi yugmam puram viṣṇoḥ nirūpitam dhyāna pūjā japaiḥ viṣṇoḥ bhaktā gacchanti tad padam vaiṣṇavāt sapta koṭībhiḥ bhuvanam parameśituḥ rudrasya sṛṣṭi saṃhāra kartuḥ brahmāṇḍa vartmani dīkṣā jñāna vihīnā ye liṅga ārādhana tatparāḥ te yānti aṇḍa antare raudram puram na adhas  kadācana tad sthāḥ sarve śivam yānti rudrāḥ śrīkaṇṭha dīkṣitāḥ adhikāra kṣaye sākam rudra kanyā gaṇena te puram puram ca rudra ūrdhvam uttara uttara vṛddhitaḥ brahmāṇḍa adhas ca rudra ūrdhva daṇḍapāṇeḥ puram sa ca śiva icchayā dṛṇāti aṇḍam mokṣa mārga karoti ca śarva rudrau bhīma bhavau  ugraḥ  devaḥ  mahān atha īśāna iti bhūrlokāt  sapta loka īśvarāḥ śivāḥ sthūlaiḥ viśeṣaiḥ ārabdhāḥ sapta lokāḥ pare punar  sūkṣmaiḥ iti guruḥ ca eva rurau samyak nyarūpayat  ye brahmaṇā ādi sarge sva śarīrāt nirmitāḥ prabhūta ākhyāḥ sthūlāḥ pañca viśeṣāḥ saptāmī tad mayā lokāḥ paratas  liṅga ādhāraiḥ sūkṣmaiḥ tanmātra jaiḥ mahābhūtaiḥ lokānām āvaraṇaiḥ viṣṭabhya para speraṇa gandha ādyaiḥ kālāgneḥ daṇḍa pāṇi antam aṣṭānavati koṭayaḥ ata ūrdhvam kaṭāhaḥ  ṇḍe sa ghanaḥ koṭi yojanam pañcāśat koṭayaḥ ca ūrdhvam bhū pṛṣṭhāt adharam tathā evam koṭi śatam bhūḥ syāt  sauvarṇaḥ taṇḍulaḥ tatas  śata rudrau  adhiḥ hu phaj  bhedayet tad tu duḥśamam pratidikkam daśa daśa iti evam rudra śatam bahis  brahmāṇḍa ādhārakam tad ca sva prabhāveṇa sarvatas  aṇḍa svarūpam gurubhiḥ ca uktam śrī raurava ādiṣu vyakteḥ abhimukhībhūtaḥ pracyutaḥ śakti rūpataḥ āvāpavān anirbhaktaḥ  vastu piṇḍaḥ  ṇḍa ucyate tamaḥ leśa anuviddhasya kapālam sattvam uttaram rajaḥ  nuviddham nirmṛṣṭam sattvam asya adharam tamaḥ vastu piṇḍa iti proktam śiva śakti samūha bhāj  aṇḍaḥ syāt iti tad vyaktau saṃmukhībhāva ucyate tathā api śiva magnānām śaktīnāmaṇḍa tā bhavet  tad artha vākyam aparam tā hi na cyuta śaktitaḥ tanu akṣa ādau mā prasāṅkṣīt aṇḍa tā iti pada antaram tanu akṣa ādiṣu na eva āste kasya api āvāpanam yatas  tanu akṣa samudāya tve katham ekatvam iti atas  anirbhakta iti proktam sājātya paridarśakam vinā api vastu piṇḍa ākhya padena ekaikaśas  bhavet  tattveṣu aṇḍa svabhāva tvam nanu evam api kim na tad  guṇa tanmātra bhūta ogha maye tattve prasajyate ucyate vastu śabdena tanu akṣa bhuvana ātmakam rūpam uktam yatas tena tad samūhaḥ  ṇḍa ucyate bhavet ca tad samūha tvam patyuḥ viśva vapuḥ bhṛtaḥ tad artha bhedakāni anyāni upāttāni iti darśitam tāvat mātrāsu avasthāsu māyā adhīne dhva maṇḍale mā bhūt aṇḍa tvam iti āhuḥ anye bhedaka yojanam ittham ukta viriñca aṇḍamṛtaḥ  rudrāḥ śatam hi yad  teṣām sve patayaḥ  rudrā ekādaśa mahā arciṣaḥ anantaḥ  tha kapālyā agniḥ yama nairṛtakau balaḥ śīghraḥ  nidhi īśaḥ  vidyeśaḥ śambhuḥ sa vīrabhadrakaḥ madhu madhukṛtaḥ kadambam kesara jālāni yadvat āvṛṇate tadvat te śiva rudrā brahmāṇḍam asaṃkhya parivārāḥ śara aṣṭa niyutam koṭiḥ iti eṣām sanniveśanam śrīkaṇṭha adhiṣṭhitāḥ te ca sṛjanti saṃharanti ca īśvara tvam diviṣadām iti raurava vārtike siddhātantre tu hemāṇḍāt śatakoṭeḥ bahis  śatam aṇḍānām kramaśas  dvi dviguṇam rūpya ādi yojitam teṣu krameṇa brahmāṇaḥ saṃsyuḥ dviguṇa jīvitāḥ kṣīyante kramaśas te ca tad ante tad tvam ap mayam dharāta u tra jala ādi syāt uttarottarataḥ kramāt  daśadhā ahaṅkṛta antam dhīḥ tasyāḥ syāt śatadhā tatas  sahasradhā vyaktam atas  pauṃsnam daśa sahasradhā niyatiḥ lakṣadhā tasmāt tasyāḥ tu daśa lakṣadhā kalā antam koṭidhā tasmāt māyā viddaśa koṭidhā īśvaraḥ śata koṭiḥ syāt tasmāt koṭi sahasradhā sādākhyam vyaśnute tad ca śaktiḥ vṛndena saṃkhyayā vyāpinī sarvam adhvānam vyāpya devī vyavasthitā aprameyam tatas  śuddham śiva tattvam param viduḥ jala ādeḥ śiva tattva antam na dṛṣṭam kenacid śivāt  ṛte tatas  śiva jñānam paramam mokṣa kāraṇam tathā ca āha mahādevaḥ śrīmat svacchandaśāsane na anyathā mokṣam āyāti paśuḥ jñāna śataiḥ api śiva jñānam na bhavati dīkṣām aprāpya śāṅkarīm prāktanī pārameśī sā pauruṣeyī ca sā punar  śata rudrā ūrdhvatas  bhadrakālyā nīla prabham jayam na yajña dāna tapasā prāpyam kālyāḥ puram jayam tad bhaktāḥ tatra gacchanti tad maṇḍala su dīkṣitāḥ nirbīja dīkṣayā mokṣam dadāti parameśvarī vidyeśa āvaraṇe dīkṣām yāvatīm kurute nṛṇām tāvatīm gatim āyānti bhuvane tra niveśitāḥ tatas  koṭyā vīrabhadraḥ  yugānta agni sama prabhaḥ vijaya ākhyam puram ca asya ye smarantaḥ  maheśvaram jaleṣu maruṣu ca agnau śiraḥ chedena vā mṛtāḥ te yānti bodham aiśānam vīrabhadram mahā dyutim vairabhadra ūrdhvatas  koṭiḥ viṣkambhāt vistṛtam tridhā rudra aṇḍam sālilam tu aṇḍam śakra cāpa ākṛti sthitam ā vīrabhadra bhuvanāt bhadrakālī ālayāt tathā trayodaśabhiḥ anyaiḥ ca bhuvanaiḥ upaśobhitam tatas  bhuvaḥ saha adreḥ pūrgandha tanmātra dhāraṇāt  mṛtā gacchanti tām bhūmim dharitryāḥ paramām budhāḥ abdheḥ puram tatas tu āpi am rasa tanmātra dhāraṇāt  tatas  śriyaḥ puram rudra krīḍā avataraṇeṣu atha prayāga ādau śrīgirau ca viśeṣāt maraṇena tad  sārasvatam puram tasmāt śabda brahma vidām padam rudra ucitāḥ tā mukhya tvāt rudrebhyaḥ  nyāḥ tathā sthitāḥ pureṣu bahudhā gaṅgā deva ādau śrīḥ sarasvatī lakula ādi amara īśa antā aṣṭau  apsu surādhipāḥ tatas tu taijasam tattvam śiva agneḥ atra saṃsthitiḥ te ca enam vahnim āyānti vāhnīm ye dhāraṇām śritāḥ bhairava ādi hari indu antam taijase nāyaka aṣṭakam prāṇasya bhuvanam vāyoḥ daśadhā daśadhā tu tad  dhyātvā tyaktvā atha vā prāṇān kṛtvā tatra eva dhāraṇām tam viśanti mahātmānaḥ  vāyu bhūtāḥ kha mūrtayaḥ bhīma ādi gaya paryantam aṣṭakam vāyu tattva gam kha tattve bhuvanam vyomnaḥ prāpyam tad vyoma dhāraṇāt  vastra āpadāntam sthāṇu ādi vyoma tattve surāṣṭakam adīkṣitā ye bhūteṣu śiva tattva abhimāninaḥ jñāna hīnā api prauḍha dhāraṇāḥ te ṇḍataḥ bahis  dharā abdhi tejaḥ  nilakha pura gā dīkṣitāḥ ca vā tāvat saṃskāra yoga artham na param padam īhitum tathāvidha avatāreṣu mṛtāḥ ca āyataneṣu ye tad padam te samāsādya kramāt yānti śiva ātma tām punar  punar idam ca uktam śrīmat devī ākhya yāmale śrī kāmikāyām kaśmīra varṇane ca uktavān vibhuḥ sureśvarī mahā dhāmni ye mriyante ca tad pure brāhmaṇa ādyāḥ saṅkara antāḥ paśavaḥ sthāvara anta gāḥ rudra jātaya eva ete iti āha bhagavān śivaḥ ākāśa āvaraṇāt ūrdhvam ahaṅkārāt adhas  priye tanmātra ādi manaḥ  ntānām purāṇi śiva śāsane pañca varṇa yutam gandha tanmātra maṇḍalam mahat  ācchādya yojana aneka koṭibhiḥ sthitam antarā evam rasa ādi mātrāṇām maṇḍalāni svavarṇata śarvaḥ  bhavaḥ paśupatiḥ īśaḥ  bhīma iti kramāt  tanmātra īśā yad icchātaḥ śabda ādyāḥ kha ādi kāriṇaḥ tatas  sūrya indu vedānām maṇḍalāni vibhuḥ mahān ugraḥ cetyeṣu patayaḥ tebhyaḥ  rka indū sa yājakau iti aṣṭau tanavaḥ śaṃbhoḥ yāḥ parāḥ parikīrtitāḥ aparā brahmaṇaḥ  ṇḍe tā vyāpya sarvam vyavasthitāḥ kalpe kalpe prasūyante dharā ādyāḥ tābhya eva tu tatas  vāc ādi karma akṣa yuktam karaṇa maṇḍalam agni indra viṣṇu mitrāḥ sa brahmāṇaḥ teṣu nāyakāḥ prakāśa maṇḍalam tasmāt śrutam buddhi akṣa pañcakam diś vidyut arka varuṇa bhuvaḥ śrotra ādi devatāḥ prakāśa maṇḍalāt ūrdhvam sthitam pañca artha maṇḍalam manaḥ maṇḍalam etasmāt  somena adhiṣṭhitam yatas  bāhya deveṣu adhiṣṭhātā sāmya aiśvarya sukha ātmakaḥ manaḥ devaḥ tatas  divyaḥ somaḥ  vibhuḥ udīritaḥ tatas  pi sakala akṣāṇām yoneḥ buddhi akṣa janmanaḥ sthūla ādi  chagala anta aṣṭa yuktam ca ahaṅkṛteḥ puram buddhi tattvam tatas  devayoni aṣṭaka pura adhipam paiśāca prabhṛti brāhma paryantam tad ca kīrtitam etāni devayonīnām sthānāni eva purāṇi atas  avatīrya ātmajanmānam dhyāyantaḥ saṃbhavanti te parameśa niyogāt ca codyamānāḥ ca māyayā niyāmitā niyatyā ca brahmaṇaḥ  vyakta janmanaḥ vyajyante tena sarga ādau nāma rūpaiḥ anekadhā sva aṃśanā eva mahātmānaḥ  na tyajanti sva ketanam uktam ca śivatanau  idam adhikāra pada sthitena guruṇā naḥ aṣṭānām devānām śakti āvirbhāva yonayaḥ  hi etāḥ tanu bhogāḥ punar eṣām adhas  prabhūta ātmakāḥ proktāḥ catvāriṃśat tulya upabhoga deśa adhikāni bhuvanāni sādhana bhedāt kevalam aṣṭaka pañcaka tayā uktāni etāni bhakti yoga prāṇatyāga ādi gamyāni teṣu umāpatiḥ eva prabhuḥ svatantra indriyaḥ  vikaraṇa ātmā taratama yogena tatas  pi devayoni aṣṭakam lakṣyam tu lokānām akṣāṇi ca viṣaya paricchitti karaṇāni gandha ādeḥ mahat antāt eka ādhikyena jātam aiśvaryam aṇima ādi ātmakam asmin paiśāca ādye viriñca ante jñātvā evam śodhayet buddhim sārdham puryaṣṭaka indriyaiḥ krodha īśa aṣṭakam ānīlam saṃvarta ādyam tatas  viduḥ teja uṣṭakam balādhyakṣa prabhṛti krodha nāṣtakāt akṛta ādi tatas  buddhau yoga aṣṭakam udāhṛtam svacchandaśāsane tad tu mūle śrī pūrvaśāsane yoga aṣṭaka pade yad tu some śraikaṇṭham eva ca tatas  māyā puram bhūyas  śrīkaṇṭhasya ca kathyate tena dvitīyam bhuvanam tayoḥ pratyekam ucyate tatra māyā puram devyā yayā viśvam adhiṣṭhitam pratikalpam nāma bhedaiḥ bhaṇyate sā maheśvarī umāpateḥ puram paścāt mātṛbhiḥ parivāritam śrīkaṇṭha eva parayā mūrtyā umāpatiḥ ucyate brāhmyaiśī skanda jā hārī vārāhyā aindrī saviccikā [carcikā] pītā śuklā pīta nīle nīlā śukla aruṇā kramāt  agnīśa saumya yāmya apya pūrva nairṛta gāstu tāḥ aṃśena mānuṣe loke dhātrā tā hi avatāritāḥ svacchandāḥ tāḥ parāḥ ca anyāḥ pare vyomni vyavasthitāḥ svacchandam tā niṣevante saptadhā iyam umā yatas  umāpati purasya ūrdhva sthitam mūrti aṣṭakam param śarva ādikam yasya sṛṣṭiḥ dharā ādyā yājaka antatas tābhya īśāna mūrtiḥ yā sā merau saṃpratiṣṭhitā śrīkaṇṭhaḥ sphaṭika adrau sā vyāptā tanu aṣṭakaiḥ jagat  ye yogam sa guṇam śambhoḥ saṃyatāḥ paryupāsate tad maṇḍalam vā dṛṣṭvā eva mukta dvaitā hṛta trayāḥ guṇānām ādhara auttaryāt śuddha aśuddhatva saṃsthiteḥ tāratamyāt ca yogasya bhedāt phala vicitra tā tatas  bhoga phala avāpti bhedāt bhedaḥ  yam ucyate mūrti aṣṭaka upariṣṭāt tu suśivā dvādaśa uditāḥ vāma ādi eka śiva antāḥ te kuṅkuma ābhāḥ su tejasaḥ tad ūrdhva vīrabhadra ākhyaḥ  maṇḍala adhipatiḥ sthitaḥ yatta [sta] tsāyujyam āpannaḥ sa tena saha modate tatas  pyaṅguṣṭha mātra antam mahādeva aṣṭakam bhavet  buddhi tattvam idam proktam devayoni aṣṭaka āditaḥ mahādeva aṣṭaka ante tad  yoga aṣṭakam iha uditam tatra śraikaṇṭham uktam yad  tasya eva umāpatiḥ tathā mūrtayaḥ suśivā vīraḥ  mahādeva aṣṭakam vapuḥ upariṣṭāt hiyaḥ  dhas ca prakṛteḥ guṇa saṃjñitam tattvam tatra tu saṃkṣubdhā guṇāḥ prasuvate dhiyam na vaiṣamyam anāpannam kāraṇam kārya sūtaye guṇa sāmya tmikā tena prakṛtiḥ kāraṇam bhavet  nanu evam sā api saṃkṣobham vinā tān viṣamān guṇān katham suvīta tatra ādye kṣobhe syāt anavasthitiḥ sāṃkhyasya doṣa eva ayam yadi vā tena te guṇāḥ avyaktam iṣṭāḥ sāmyam tu saṅga mātram na ca itarat  asmākam tu svatantra īśa tathā icchā kṣobha saṃgatam avyaktam buddhi tattvasya kāraṇam kṣobhitā guṇāḥ nanu tattva īśvara icchātaḥ  yaḥ kṣobhaḥ prakṛteḥ purā tad eva buddhi tattvam syāt  kim anyaiḥ kalpitaiḥ guṇaiḥ na etad kāraṇa tārūpa parāmarśa avarodhi yad  kṣobha antaram tatas  kārya bīja ucchūna aṅkura ādivat  kramāt tamaḥ rajaḥ sattve gurūṇām paṅktayaḥ sthitāḥ tisraḥ  dvātriṃśat ekā atas triṃśat api ekaviṃśatiḥ sva jñana yoga balataḥ krīḍantaḥ  daiśika uttamāḥ trinetrāḥ pāśa nirmuktāḥ te tra anugraha kāriṇaḥ buddheḥ ca guṇa paryantam ubhe sapta adhike śate rudrāṇām bhuvanānām ca mukhyataḥ nye tad antare yoga aṣṭakam guṇa skandhe proktam śiva tanau punar  yonīḥ ati iti gauṇe skandhe syuḥ yoga dātāraḥ akṛta kṛta vibhu viriñcā hariḥ guhaḥ krama vaśāt tatas  devī karaṇāni aṇima ādi guṇāḥ kāryāṇi pratyaya prapañcaḥ ca avyaktāt utpannā guṇāḥ ca sattva āt ayaḥ  mīṣām dharma jñāna virāga anaiśvaryam tad phalāni vividhāni yacchanti guṇebhyaḥ  mī puruṣebhyaḥ  yoga dātāraḥ tebhyaḥ paratas  bhuvanam sattva ādi guṇa āsanasya devasya sakala jagat eka mātuḥ bhartuḥ śrīkaṇṭha nāthasya yena umāguha nīla brahmaṛbhukṣa kṛta akṛta ādi bhuvaneṣu graha rūpiṇyā śaktyā prābhvyā adhiṣṭhāni bhūtāni upasaṃjihīrṣuḥ iha yaḥ caturānana paṅkajam samāviśya dagdhvā caturaḥ  lokāñjana lokān nirmiṇoti punar  yasya icchātaḥ sattva ādi guṇa śarīrā visṛjati rudrāṇī anukalpaḥ  rudrāṇyā vedī tatra ijyate nukalpena paśupatiḥ indra upendra viriñcaiḥ atha tad upalambhataḥ  devaiḥ gandharva yakṣa rākṣasa pitṛ munibhiḥ citritāḥ tathā yāgāḥ guṇānām yad param sāmyam tad avyaktam guṇa ūrdhvatas  krodha īśa caṇḍa saṃvartā jyotiḥ piṅgala sūrakau pañcāntaka eka vīrau ca śikhodaḥ ca aṣṭa tatra te gahanam puruṣa nidhānam prakṛtiḥ mūlam pradhānam avyaktam guṇa kāraṇam iti ete māyā prabhavasya paryāyāḥ yāvantaḥ kṣetrajñāḥ sahaja āgantu kamala upadigdha citaḥ te sarve tra vinihitā rudrāḥ ca tad uttha bhoga bhujaḥ mūḍha vivṛtta vilīnaiḥ karaṇaiḥ kecid tu vikaraṇakāḥ akṛta adhiṣṭhāna tayā kṛtyā śaktāni mūḍhāni pratiniyata viṣaya bhāñji sphuṭāni śāstre vivṛttāni bhagnāni mahāpralaye sṛṣṭau na utpāditāni līnāni icchā adhīnāni punar vikaraṇa saṃjñāni kāryam api evam puṃstattve tuṣṭi navakam siddhayaḥ ṣṭau ca tad puras  tāvatya eva aṇima ādi bhuvana aṣṭakam eva ca atattve tattva buddhyā yaḥ santoṣaḥ tuṣṭiḥ atra sā heye pyādeya dhīḥ siddhiḥ tathā ca uktam hi kāpilaiḥ ādhyātmikāḥ catasraḥ prakṛti upādāna kāla bhāgya ākhyāḥ pañca viṣaya uparamataḥ rjana rakṣā saṅga saṃkṣaya vighātaiḥ ūhaḥ śabdaḥ  dhyayanam duḥkha vighātāḥ trayaḥ suhṛd prāptiḥ dānam ca siddhayaḥ ṣṭau siddheḥ pūrvaḥ ṅkuśaḥ trividhaḥ aṇima ādi ūrdhvatas tisraḥ paṅktayaḥ  guru śiṣya gāḥ tatra api triguṇa  chāyā yogāt tri tvam udāhṛtam nāḍī vidyā aṣṭakam ca ūrdhvam paṅktīnām syāt iḍā ādikam puṃsi nāda mayī śaktiḥ prasara ākhyā ca yad sthitā na hi akartā pumān kartuḥ kāraṇa tvam ca saṃsthitam akartari api vā puṃsi sahakāritayā sthite śeṣa kārya ātma tā eṣṭavyānyathā satkārya hānitaḥ tasmāt tathāvidhe kārye yā śaktiḥ puruṣasya sā tāvanti rūpāṇi ādāya pūrṇa tām adhigacchati nāḍī aṣṭaka ūrdhve kathitam vigraha aṣṭakam ucyate kāryam hetuḥ duḥkham sukham ca vijñāna sādhya karaṇāni sādhanam iti vigraha tā yuj aṣṭakam bhavati puṃstattve bhuvanam deha dharmāṇām daśānām vigraha aṣṭakāt  ahiṃsā satyam asteyam brahmā kalkā krudhaḥ  guroḥ śuśrūṣā śauca santoṣā ṛju tā iti daśa uditāḥ puṃstattva eva gandha antam sthitam ṣoḍaśakam punar  ārabhya dehapāśa ākhyam puram buddhi guṇāḥ tatas  tatra eva aṣṭau  ahaṃkāraḥ tridhā kāma ādikāḥ tathā pāśā āgantuka gāṇeśa vaidya īśvara bheditāḥ trividhāḥ te sthitāḥ puṃsi mokṣa mārga uparodhakāḥ yad kiṃcid parama advaita saṃvid svātantrya sundarāt parāt śivāt ukta rūpāt anyat tad pāśa ucyate tad evam puṃstvam āpanne pūrṇe pi parameśvare tad svarūpa aparijñānam citram hi puruṣāḥ tatas  ukta anuktāḥ tu ye pāśāḥ paratantra ukta lakṣaṇāḥ te puṃsi sarve tān  tatra śodhayan mucyate bhavāt  puṃsa ūrdhva  tu niyatiḥ tatrasthāḥ
