śaṃkarā daśa hema ābhāḥ susitāḥ kāla tattve tu daśa te śivāḥ koṭiḥ ṣoḍaśa sāhasram pratyekam parivāriṇaḥ rāge vīra īśa bhuvanam guru antevāsinām puram puram ca aśuddha vidyāyām syāt śakti navaka ujjvalam manonmanyanta gāḥ tāḥ ca vāma ādyāḥ parikīrtitāḥ kalāyām syāt mahādeva trayasya puram uttamam tatas  māyā tripuṭikā mukhyataḥ nanta koṭibhiḥ ākrāntā sā bhaga bilaiḥ proktam śaivyām tanau punar  aṅguṣṭha mātra paryantam mahādeva aṣṭakam niśi cakra aṣṭaka ādhipatyena tathā śrī mālinīmate vāma ādyāḥ puruṣa ādau ye proktāḥ śrī pūrvaśāsane te māyā tattva eva uktāstanau śaivyām anantatas kapāla vratinaḥ sva aṅga hotāraḥ kaṣṭa tāpasāḥ sarva abhayāḥ khaḍga dhārā vratāḥ tad tattva vedinaḥ kramāt tad tattvam āyānti yatra īśaḥ  nanta ucyate uktam ca tasya paratas  sthānam ananta adhipasya devasya sthiti vilaya sarga kartuḥ guhā bhaga dvārapālasya dharmān aṇima ādi guṇān jñānāni tapaḥ sukhāni yogān  ca māyā bilāt pradatte puṃsām niṣkṛṣya niṣkṛṣya tad śakti iddhasvabalā guhā adhikāra andhakāra guṇa dīpāḥ sarve nanta pramukhā dīpyante śata bhava pramukha antāḥ saḥ  vyaktam adhiṣṭhāya prakaroti jagat niyogataḥ śambhoḥ śuddha aśuddha srotaḥ  dhikāra hetuḥ śivaḥ  yasmāt  śiva guṇa yoge tasmin mahati pade ye pratiṣṭhitāḥ prathamam te nanta ādeḥ jagataḥ sarga sthiti vilaya kartāraḥ māyā bilam idam uktam paratas tu guhā jagadyoniḥ utpattyā teṣu asyāḥ pati śakti kṣobham anuvidhīyamāneṣu yoni vivareṣu nānā kāma samṛddheṣu bhaga saṃjñā kāmayate patiḥ enām icchā anuvidhāyinīm yadā devīm pratibhagam avyakta ādyāḥ prajāḥ tadā asyāḥ prajāyante teṣām ati sūkṣmāṇām etāvat tvam na varṇyate vidhiṣu avavarakāṇi ekasmin yad vatsāle bahūni baddhāni yoni bilāni ekasmin  tadvat māyā śiraḥ sāle māyā paṭalaiḥ sūkṣmaiḥ kuḍyaiḥ pihitāḥ parasparam adṛśyāḥ nivasanti tatra rudrāḥ sukhinaḥ pratibilam asaṃkhyātāḥ sthāne sāyujya gatāḥ sāmīpya gatāḥ pare sa loka sthāḥ pratibhuvanam evam ayam nivāsinām gurubhiḥ uddiṣṭaḥ api sarva siddha vācaḥ kṣīyeran dīrgha kālam udgīrṇāḥ na punar yoni ānantyāt ucyante srotasām saṃkhyāḥ tasmāt niraya ādi ekam yad proktam dvārapāla paryantam srotaḥ tena anyāni api tulya vidhānāni vedyāni avyakta kale guhayā prakṛti kalābhyām vikāra ātmīyaḥ otaḥ protaḥ  vyāptaḥ kalitaḥ pūrṇaḥ parikṣiptaḥ madhye puṭa trayam tasyāḥ  rudrāḥ ṣaṣ adhare ntare eka ūrdhve ca pañca iti dvādaśā ete nirūpitāḥ gahana asādhyau hari hara daśeśvarau trikala gopatī ṣaṭ ime madhye nantaḥ kṣemaḥ  dvija īśa vidyeśa viśvaśivāḥ iti pañca teṣu pañcasu ṣaṭsu ca puṭa geṣu tad parāvṛttyā parivarttate sthitiḥ kila devaḥ  nantaḥ tu sarvathā madhye ūrdhva adhara ga kapālaka puṭa ṣaṭka yugena tad parāvṛttyā madhyataḥ  ṣṭābhiḥ diś sthaiḥ vyāptaḥ  granthiḥ mataṅga śāstra uktaḥ śrī sāraśāsane punar eṣā ṣaṣ puṭa tayā vinirdiṣṭā granthi ākhyam idam tattvam māyā kāryam tatas  māyā māyā tattvam vibhu kila gahanam arūpam samasta vilaya padam tatra na bhuvana vibhāgaḥ  yuktaḥ  granthau  asau tasmāt  māyā tattva adhipatiḥ saḥ  nantaḥ samuditān vicārya aṇūn yugapad kṣobhayati niśām sā sūte saṃpuṭaiḥ anantaiḥ svaiḥ tena kalā ādi dhara antam yad uktam āvaraṇa jālam akhilam tad  niḥsaṃkhyam ca vicitram māyā eva ekā tu abhinnā iyam uktam śrī pūrvaśāstre ca dharā vyakta ātmakam dvayam asaṃkhyātam niśā śakti saṃjñam tu eka svarūpakam pāśāḥ purā uktāḥ praṇavāḥ pañcamāna aṣṭakam muneḥ kulam yoniḥ ca vāgīśī yasyām jātaḥ  na jāyate dīkṣā kāle dharādhva stha śuddhau yad ca adhara adhva gam anantasya samīpe tu tad sarvam pariniṣṭhitam sādhyaḥ  dātā damanaḥ  dhyānaḥ  bhasma iti bindavaḥ pañca pañcārtha guhya rudra aṅkuśa hṛdaya lakṣaṇam ca sa vyūham ākarṣa ādarśau ca iti aṣṭakam etad pramāṇānām alupta vibhavāḥ sarve māyā tattva adhikāriṇaḥ māyā maya śarīrāḥ te bhogam svam paribhuñjate pralaya ante hi anantena saṃhṛtāḥ te tu aharmukhe anya ananta prasādena vibudhā api tam param supta buddham manyamānāḥ svatantram manyatā jaḍāḥ sva ātmānam eva jānanti hetum māyā antarāla gāḥ atas  param sthitā māyā devī jantu vimohinī devadevasya sā śaktiḥ ati durghaṭa kāri tā nirvaira paripanthinyā tayā bhramita buddhayaḥ idam tattvam idam na iti vivadanti iha vādinaḥ guru deva agni śāstreṣu ye na bhaktā nara adhamāḥ sat patham tān parityājya sa utpatham nayati dhruvam asat yukti vicāra jñān śuṣka tarka avalambinaḥ bhramayati eva tān māyā hi amokṣe mokṣa lipsayā śiva dīkṣā asinā cchinnā śiva jñāna asinā tathā na prarohet punar na anyaḥ  hetuḥ tad chedanam prati mahāmāyā ūrdhvatas  śuddhā mahāvidyā atha mātṛkā vāgīśvarī ca tatrastham vāma ādi nava sat puram vāmā jyeṣṭhā raudrī kālī kala vikaraṇī bala vikārike tathā mathanī damanī manonmanī ca tridṛśaḥ pītāḥ samastāḥ tāḥ sapta koṭyaḥ  mukhya mantrā vidyā tattve tra saṃsthitāḥ ekaika arbuda lakṣa aṃśāḥ padma ākāra purā iha vidyā rājñyaḥ triguṇi ādyāḥ sapta sapta arbuda īśvarāḥ vidyā tattva ūrdhvam aiśam tu tattvam tatra krama ūrdhva gam śikhaṇḍi ādyam ananta antam pura aṣṭaka yutam puram śikhaṇḍī śrī galaḥ  mūrtiḥ eka netra eka rudrakau śiva uttamaḥ sūkṣma rudraḥ  nantaḥ  vidyeśvara aṣṭakam kramāt ūrdhva ūrdhva saṃsthānam saptānām nāyakaḥ  vibhuḥ ananta eva dhyeyaḥ ca pūjyaḥ ca api uttarottaraḥ mukhya mantreśvarāṇām yad  sārdham koṭi trayam sthitam tad nāyakā ime tena vidyeśāḥ cakravartinaḥ uktam ca gurubhiḥ ittham śiva tanu ādyeṣu śāsaneṣu etad  bhaga bila śata kalita guhā mūrdhāsana gaḥ ṣṭa śakti yuj devaḥ gahana ādyam niraya antam sṛjati ca rudrān  ca viniyuṅkte uddharati manonmanyā puṃsaḥ teṣu eva bhavati madhyasthaḥ te tena udasta citaḥ para tattva ālocane bhiniviśante sa punar adhas  patha vartiṣu adhikṛta eva aṇuṣu śivena avasita pati viniyogaḥ sārdham aneka ātma mantra koṭībhiḥ nirvāti ananta nāthaḥ tad hāma āviśati sūkṣma rudraḥ tu anugṛhya aṇum apūrvam sthāpayati patiḥ śikhaṇḍinaḥ sthāne iti aṣṭau paripāṭyā yāvat dhāmāni yāti guruḥ ekaḥ tāvat asaṃkhyātānām jantūnām nirvṛtim kurute te ṣṭau  api śakti aṣṭaka yoga amala jalaruha āsana āsīnāḥ ālokayanti devam hṛdaya stham kāraṇam paramam tam bhagavantam anantam dhyāyantaḥ sva hṛdi kāraṇam śāntam saptā anudhyāyanti api mantrāṇām koṭayaḥ śuddhāḥ māyā ādiḥ avīci antaḥ  bhavaḥ tu ananta ādiḥ ucyate pyabhavaḥ śiva śuddha guṇa adhīkāra antaḥ saḥ  pyeṣa heyaḥ ca atra api yatas  dṛṣṭa anugrāhyāṇām niyojyatā śaivī iṣṭā ca tad nivṛttiḥ hi abhavaḥ tu adhare na bhūyate yasmāt  patyuḥ apasarpati yatas  kāraṇa tā kārya tā ca siddhebhyaḥ kañcukavat śiva siddhau tau  ati bhava saṃjñayā ati madhya sthau dharma jñāna virāga aiśya catuṣṭaya puram tu yad  rūpa āvaraṇa saṃjñam tad tattve sminnaiśvare viduḥ vāmā jyeṣṭhā ca raudrī iti bhuvanatraya śobhitam sūkṣma āvaraṇam ākhyātam īśa tattve guru uttamaiḥ aiśāt sāda aśivam jñāna kriyā yugala maṇḍitam śuddha āvaraṇam iti āhuḥ uktā śuddha āvṛteḥ param vidyā āvṛtiḥ tatas  bhāva abhāva śakti dvaya ujjvalā śakti āvṛtiḥ pramāṇa ākhyā tatas  śāstre nirūpitā śakti āvṛteḥ tu tejasvi dhruva īśābhyām alaṅkṛtam tejasvī āvaraṇam veda purā māna āvṛtiḥ tatas  māna āvṛteḥ su śuddha āvṛt pura tritaya śobhitā su śuddha āvaraṇāt ūrdhva śaivam eka puram bhavet  śiva āvṛteḥ ūrdhvam āhuḥ mokṣa āvaraṇa saṃjñitam asyām mokṣa āvṛtau rudrā ekādaśa nirūpitāḥ mokṣa āvaraṇataḥ tu eka puram āvaraṇam dhruvam ūrdhve dhruva āvṛteḥ icchā āvaraṇam tatra te śivāḥ īśvara icchā gṛha antasthāḥ tad puram ca ekam ucyate icchā āvṛteḥ prabuddha ākhyam diś rudra aṣṭaka carcitam prabuddha āvaraṇāt ūrdhva samaya āvaraṇam mahat  bhuvanaiḥ pañcabhiḥ garbhīkṛta ananta samāvṛti sāmayāt sauśivam tatra sādākhyam bhuvanam mahat  tasmin sadāśivaḥ  devaḥ tasya savya apasavyayoḥ jñāna kriye para icchā tu śaktiḥ utsaṅga gāminī sṛṣṭi ādi pañca kṛtyāni kurute sa tayā icchayā pañca brahmāṇi aṅga ṣaṭkam sakala ādi aṣṭakam śivāḥ daśa aṣṭādaśa rudrāḥ ca taiḥ eva suśivaḥ  vṛtaḥ sadyas  vāma aghorau puruṣa īśau brahma pañcakam hṛdayam mūrdha śikhā varma dṛś astram aṅgāni ṣaḍ  prāhuḥ sakala akala śūnyaiḥ saha kalā āḍhya kham alaṅkṛte kṣapaṇam antyam kaṇṭhya oṣṭhyam aṣṭamam kila sakala aṣṭakam etad āmnātam om kāra śivau dīptaḥ  hetu īśa daśa īśakau su śiva kālau sūkṣma su tejaḥ śarvāḥ śivāḥ daśā ete tra pūrva ādeḥ vijayaḥ  niḥśvāsaḥ ca svāyambhuvaḥ  vahni vīra rauravakāḥ mukuṭa visara indu vindu prodgītā lalita siddha rudrau ca santāna śivau para kiraṇa pārameśā iti smṛtā rudrāḥ sarveṣām eteṣām jñānāni viduḥ sva tulya nāmāni mantra muni koṭi parivṛta matha vibhu vāma ādi rudra tad śakti yutam tāra ādi śakti juṣṭam suśiva āsanam atisitaka jama saṃkhya dalam yaḥ śakti rudra vargaḥ parivāre viṣṭare ca suśivasya pratyekam asya nija nija parivāre parārdha koṭayaḥ  saṃkhyāḥ māyā mala nirmuktāḥ kevalam adhikāra mātra saṃrūḍhāḥ suśiva āvaraṇe rudrāḥ sarva jñāḥ sarva śakti sampūrṇāḥ adhikāra bandha vilaye śāntāḥ śiva rūpiṇaḥ  punarbhavinaḥ ūrdhve bindu āvṛtiḥ dīptā tatra tatra padmam śaśi prabham śānti atītaḥ śivaḥ tatra tad śakti utsaṅga bhūṣitaḥ nivṛtti ādi kalā varga parivāra samāvṛtaḥ asaṃkhya rudra tad śakti pura koṭibhiḥ āvṛtaḥ śrīmat mataṅga śāstre ca laya ākhyam tattvam uttamam pāribhāṣikam iti etad nāmnā binduḥ iha ucyate catur mūrti mayam śubhram yad tad sakala niṣkalam tasmin bhogaḥ samuddiṣṭa iti atra idam ca varṇitam nivṛtti ādeḥ su sūkṣma tvāt hara ādi ārabdha deha tā mātuḥ sphūrjat mahā jñāna līna tvāt na vibhāvyate udrikta taijasa tvena hemnaḥ  bhū paramāṇavaḥ yathā pṛthak na bhānti evam ūrdhva adhas rudra deha gāḥ bindu ūrdhve rdhenduḥ etasya kalā jyotsnā ca tadvatī kāntiḥ prabhā ca vimalā pañca etā rodhikāḥ tatas  rundhanī rodhanī roddhrī jñāna bodhā tamopahā etāḥ pañca kalāḥ prāhuḥ nirodhinyām guru uttamāh ardha mātraḥ smṛtaḥ  binduḥ vyoma rūpī catuṣkalaḥ tad ardham ardhacandraḥ tad aṣṭa aṃśena nirodhikā hetūn brahma ādikān runddhe rodhikām tām tyajet tatas  nirodhikām imām bhittvā sādākhyam bhuvanam param para rūpeṇa yatra āste pañca mantra mahā tanuḥ iti ardhendu nirodhi anta bindu āvṛti u ūrdhvatas  mahān nādaḥ kiñjalka sadṛśaḥ  mahadbhiḥ puruṣaiḥ vṛtaḥ catvāri bhuvanāni atra dikṣu madhye ca pañcamam indhikā dīpikā ca eva rodhikā mocikā ūrdhva gā madhye tra padmam tatra ūrdhva gāmī tad śaktibhiḥ vṛtaḥ nāda ūrdhvataḥ tu sauṣumnam tatra tad śakti bhṛt prabhuḥ tad īśaḥ piṅgalelābhyām vṛtaḥ savya apasavyayoḥ yā prabhoḥ aṅka gā devī suṣumnā śaśi saprabhā grathitaḥ  dhvā tayā sarva ūrdhvaḥ ca adhastanaḥ tathā nādaḥ suṣumna ādhāraḥ tu bhittvā viśvam idam jagat  adhas śaktyā vinirgacchet ūrdhva śaktyā ca mūrdhataḥ nāḍyā brahmabile līnaḥ saḥ  vyakta dhvaniḥ akṣaraḥ nadan sarveṣu bhūteṣu śiva śaktyā hi adhiṣṭhitaḥ suṣumnā ūrdhve brahmabila saṃjñayā āvaraṇam tridṛś  tatra brahmā sitaḥ śūlī pañcāsyaḥ śaśiśekharaḥ tasya utsaṅge parā devī brahmāṇī mokṣa mārga gā roddhrī dātrī ca mokṣasya tām bhittvā ca ūrdhva kuṇḍalī śaktiḥ supta ahi sadṛśī sā viśva ādhāra ucyate tasyām sūkṣmā su sūkṣmā ca tathā anye amṛta amite madhyataḥ  vyāpinī tasyām vyāpi īśaḥ  vyāpinī dharaḥ śakti tattvam idam yasya prapañcaḥ  yam dharā antakaḥ śiva tattvam tatas tatra catur dikkam vyavasthitāḥ vyāpī vyoma ātmakaḥ  nantaḥ  nāthaḥ tad śakti bhāginaḥ madhye tu anāśritam tatra devadevaḥ  hi anāśritaḥ tad śakti utsaṅga bhṛt sūrya śata koṭi sama prabhaḥ śiva tattva ūrdhvataḥ śaktiḥ parā sā samanāhvayā sarveṣām kāraṇānām sā kartṛ bhūtā vyavasthitā bibharti aṇḍāni anekāni śivena samadhiṣṭhitā tad ārūḍhaḥ śivaḥ kṛtya pañcakam kurute prabhuḥ samanā karaṇam tasya hetu kartuḥ mahā ūśituḥ anāśritam tu vyāpāre nimittam hetuḥ ucyate tayā adhitiṣṭhati vibhuḥ kāraṇānām tu pañcakam anāśritaḥ  nātham ayam anantam kha vapuḥ sadā sa vyāpinam prerayati sva śaktyā karaṇena tu karma rūpā sthitā māyā yad adhas  śakti kuṇḍalī nādabindu ādikam kāryam ityādi jagat udbhavaḥ yad sadāśiva paryantam pārthiva ādyam ca śāsane tad sarva prākṛtam proktam vināśa utpatti saṃyutam atha sakala bhuvana mānam yad mahyam nigaditam nijaiḥ gurubhiḥ tad vakṣyate samāsāt buddhau yena āśu saṅkrāmet  aṇḍasya antaranantaḥ kālaḥ kūṣmāṇḍa hāṭakau brahma harī rudrāḥ śatam sa vīram bahis nivṛttiḥ tu sa aṣṭaśata bhuvanā syāt  jala tejaḥ samīra nabhaḥ  haṃkṛt dhī mūla saptake pratyekam aṣṭau ṣaṭpañcāśat bhuvanā tena pratiṣṭhā iti kalā kathitā atra prāhuḥ śodhyān aṣṭau kecid nija aṣṭaka adhipatīn anye tu samastānām śodhya tvam varṇayanti bhuvanānām śrī bhūtirāja miśrā guravaḥ prāhuḥ punar bahī rudra śatam aṣṭā  antaḥ sākam śarveṇa iti īdṛśī nivṛttiḥ iyam syāt  rudrāḥ kālī vīraḥ  dharā abdhi lakṣmyaḥ sarasvatī guhyam iti aṣṭakam jale nau vahni ati guhya dvayam maruti vāyoḥ sva puram gayā ādi khe ca vyoma pavitra aṣṭakam ca bhuvana yugam abhimāne haṅkāra  chagala ādi aṣṭakam atha antarā nabhaḥ  haṃkṛt  tanmātra arka indu śrati pura aṣṭakam buddhi karma devānām daśa tanmātra samūhe bhuvanam punar akṣa varga vinipatite manasaḥ ca iti abhimāne dvāviṃśatiḥ eva bhuvanānām dhiyi daivīnām aṣṭau kruttejaḥ yoga saṃjñakam trayam tad umā tad patiḥ atha mūrti aṣṭaka suśiva dvādaśaka vīrabhadrāḥ syuḥ tad atha mahādeva aṣṭakam iti buddhau saptadaśa saṃkhyā guṇa tattve paṅkti trayam iti ṣaṭpañcāśatam purāṇi viduḥ yadi api guṇa sāmya ātmani mūle krodha īśvara aṣṭakam tathā api dhiyi tad śodhitam iti gaṇanām na punar  prāptam pratiṣṭhāyām iti jala tattvāt mūlam tattva caturviṃśatiḥ pratiṣṭhāyām ambā ādi tuṣṭi vargaḥ tārā ādyāḥ siddhayaḥ ṇimādi gaṇaḥ guravaḥ  guru śiṣyā ṛṣi varga iḍā ādiḥ ca vigraha aṣṭaka yuj  gandha ādi vikāra puram buddhi guṇa aṣṭakam ahaṃkriyā viṣaya guṇāḥ kāma ādi saptaviṃśakam āgantu tathā gaṇeśa vidyeśa mayau iti pāśeṣu puratrayam ittham puruṣe tra bhuvana ṣoḍaśakam niyatau śaṅkara daśakam kāle śiva daśakam iti pura dvitayam rāge suhṛṣṭa bhuvanam guru śiṣya puram ca vid kalā yugale bhuvanam bhuvanam niśi puṭa pura trayam vāc puram pramāṇapuram iti saptaviṃśati purā vidyā puruṣa ādi tattva saptaka yuj  vāmeśa rūpa sūkṣmam śuddham vidyā atha śakti tejasvi mitiḥ su viśuddhi śivau mokṣa dhuveṣi saṃbuddha samaya sauśiva saṃjñāḥ saptadaśa purā śāntā vidyeśa sadāśiva pura tritaya yuktā bindu ardhendu nirodhyaḥ para sauśivam indhika ādi pura sauṣumne para nādaḥ  brahmabilam sūkṣma ādi yuta ūrdhva kuṇḍalī śaktiḥ vyāpi vyoma ananta an āthān āśrita purāṇi pañca tatas  ṣaṣṭham ca paramam anāśritam atha samanābhuvana ṣoḍaśī yadi vā bindu āvaraṇam para sauśivam ca pañca indhikā ādi bhuvanāni sauṣumnam brahmabilam kuṇḍalinī vyāpi pañcakam samanā iti ṣoḍaśa bhuvanā iyam tattva yugam śānti atītā syāt  śrīmat mataṅga śāstre ca kramaḥ  yam pura pūga gaḥ kālāgniḥ narakāḥ kha abdhi yutam mukhya tayā śatam kūṣmāṇḍaḥ sapta pātālī saptalokī maheśvaraḥ iti aṇḍa madhyam tad bāhye śatam rudrā iti sthitāḥ sthānānām dviśatī bhūmiḥ saptapañcāśatā yutā pañca aṣṭakasya madhyāt dvātriṃśat bhūta catuṣṭaye tanmātreṣu ca pañca syuḥ viśvedevāḥ tatas  ṣṭakam pañcamam sa indriye garve buddhau deva aṣṭakam guṇe yoga aṣṭakam krodha saṃjñam mūle kāle sanaiyate patat ruj ādyāḥ ca aṅguṣṭha mātra ādyā rāga tattva gāḥ dvādaśa eka śiva ādyāḥ syuḥ vidyāyām kalane daśa vāma ādyāḥ triśatī sā iyam tri parvaṇi abdhiḥ asya yuj  śaivāḥ kecid iha anantāḥ śraikaṇṭhā iti saṃgrahaḥ yatra yadā para bhogān bubhukṣate tatra yojanam kāryam śodhanam atha tad hānau śeṣam tu antargatam kāryam iti āgamam prathayitum darśitam etad vikalpitam tena anye pi bahu vikalpāḥ sva dhiyā ācāryaiḥ samabhyūhyāḥ śrī pūrvaśāsane punar aṣṭādaśa adhikam śatam kathitam tad iha pradhānam adhikam saṃkṣepeṇa ucyate śodhyam kālāgniḥ kūṣmāṇḍa u nara keśaḥ  hāṭakaḥ  tha bhūta lapaḥ brahmā muni loka īśaḥ  rudrāḥ pañca antarāla sthāḥ adhare nantaḥ prācyāḥ kapāli vahni anta nirṛti bala ākhyāḥ laghu nidhi pati vidyā adhipa śambhu ūrdhva antam sa vīra bhadrapati ekādaśabhiḥ bāhye brahmāṇḍam pañcabhiḥ tathā antarikaiḥ iti ṣoḍaśa puram etad nivṛtti kalayā iha kalanīyam lakulīśa bhāra bhūtī diṇḍya āṣāḍhī ca puṣkara nimeṣau prabhāsa sura īśau  iti salile pratyātmakam sa parivāre bhairava kedāra mahākālā madhyāmra jalpa ākhyāḥ śrīśaila hariścandrau  iti guhya aṣṭakam idam mahasi bhīma indra aṭṭahāsa vimalaka nakha lana akhala kuru sthiti gaya ākhyāḥ ati guhya aṣṭakam etad maruti ca sa tanmātrake ca sākṣe ca sthāṇu suvarṇa ākhyau kila bhadraḥ gokarṇa kaḥ  mahālayakaḥ avimukta rudra koṭī vastra āpada iti adaḥ pavitram khe sthūla sthūleśa śaṅkuśruti kālañjarāḥ ca maṇḍalabhṛt  mākoṭa aṇḍa dvitaya  chagala aṇḍā aṣṭakam hi ahaṅkāre anye haṅkāra antar tanmātrāṇi indriyāṇi ca api āhuḥ dhiyi yoni aṣṭakam uktam prakṛtau yoga aṣṭakam kila akṛta prabhṛti iti sapta aṣṭaka bhuvanā pratiṣṭhitiḥ salilataḥ  hi mūla antā nari vāmaḥ  bhīma ugrau bhaveśa vīrāḥ pracaṇḍa gaurīśau ajasā ananta eka śivau vidyāyām krodha caṇḍa yugmam syāt  saṃvartaḥ  jyotirathaḥ kalā niyatyām ca sūra pañca antau vīraśikhi īśa śrīkaṇṭha saṃjñam etad trayam ca kāle syāt  sa mahā tejāḥ  vāmaḥ  bhavodbhavaḥ ca eka piṅgala īśānau bhuvaneśa puraḥsarakau  aṅguṣṭha ime niśi sthitā hi aṣṭau aṣṭāviṃśati bhuvanā vidyā puruṣān niśā antam iyam hālāhala rudrakrudambikā ghorikāḥ sa vāmāḥ syuḥ vidyāyām vidyeśāḥ tu aṣṭau  īśe sadāśive pañca vāmā jyeṣṭhā raudrī śaktiḥ sakalā ca śontayam aṣṭādaśa bhuvanā syāt  śānti atītā tu abhuvanā eva iti deśa adhva vibhāgaḥ kathitaḥ śrī śambhunā samādiṣṭaḥ  ch śrī tantra ālokasya navamam āhnikam atha tattva pravibhāgaḥ  vistarataḥ kathyate krama prāptaḥ b yāni uktāni purāṇi amūni vividha ebhadaiḥ yadeṣu anvitam rūpam bhāti param prakāśa niviḍam devaḥ sa ekaḥ śivaḥ tad svātantrya rasāt punar  śiva padāt bhede vibhāte param yad rūpam bahudhā anugāmi tad idam tattvam vibhoḥ śāsane tathā hi kāla sadanāt vīrabhadra pura anta gam dhṛti kāṭhinya garima ādi avabhāsāt hara ātma tā evam jala ādi tattveṣu vācyam yāvat sadāśive svasmin kārye tha dharma oghe yad vā api sva sadṛgguṇe āste sāmānya kalpena tananāt vyāptṛ bhāvataḥ tad tattvam kramaśas  pṛthvī pradhānam puṃśivādayaḥ dehānām bhuvanānām ca na prasaṅgaḥ tatas  bhavet  śrīmat mataṅga śāstra ādau tad uktam parameśinā tatra eṣām darśyate dṛṣṭaḥ siddhayogīśvarīmate kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ  yaḥ śiva icchā parikalpitaḥ vastutas  sarva bhāvānām kartā īśānaḥ paraḥ śivaḥ asvatantrasya kartṛ tvam na hi jātu upapadyate svatantra tā ca cit mātra vapuṣaḥ parameśituḥ svatantram ca jaḍam ca iti tad anyonyam virudhyate jāḍyam pramātṛ tantra tvam sva ātma siddhim api prati na kartṛ tvāt ṛte ca anyat  kāraṇa tvam hi labhyate tasmin sati hi tad bhāva iti apekṣa eka jīvitam nirapekṣeṣu bhāveṣu sva ātma niṣṭha tayā katham sa pūrvam atha paścāt sa iti ced pūrva paścimau svabhāve nati riktau ced sama iti avaśiṣyate bījam aṅkura iti asmin sa tattve hetu tadvatoḥ ghaṭaḥ paṭaḥ ca iti bhavet  kārya kāraṇa tā na kim bījam aṅkura patra ādi tayā pariṇameta ced  atad svabhāva vapuṣaḥ sa svabhāvaḥ  na yujyate sa tad svabhāva iti ced  tarhi bīja aṅkurā nije tāvatī eva na viśrāntau tad anya atyanta saṃbhavāt tatas ca citra ākāraḥ  sau tāvān kaścid prasajyate astu ced  na jaḍe nyonya viruddha ākāra saṃbhavaḥ krameṇa citra ākāraḥ  stu jaḍaḥ kim nu viruddhyate kramaḥ  kramaḥ  vā bhāvasya na sva rūpa adhikaḥ  bhavet  tathā upalambha mātram tau upalambhaḥ ca kim tathā upalabdhā api vijñāna svabhāvaḥ  yaḥ  sya saḥ  pi hi krama upalambha rūpa tvāt krameṇa upalabheta ced  tasya tarhi kramaḥ kaḥ  sau tad anya anupalambhataḥ svabhāva iti ced na asau sva rūpāt adhikaḥ  bhavet  sva rūpa anadhikasya api kramasya sva svabhāvataḥ svātantryāt bhāsanam syāt ced  kim anyat brūmahe vayam ittham śrī śiva eva ekaḥ kartā iti paribhāṣyate kartṛ tvam ca etad etasya tathāmātra avabhāsanam tathā avabhāsanam ca asti kārya kāraṇa bhāva gam yathā hi ghaṭa sāhityam paṭasya api avabhāsate tathā ghaṭa anantara tā kim tu sā niyama ujjhitā atas  yad niyamena eva yasmāt ābhāti anantaram tad tasya kāraṇam brūmaḥ sati rūpa anvaye dhike niyamaḥ ca tathārūpa bhāsanā mātra sārakaḥ bījāt aṅkura iti evam bhāsanam na hi sarvadā yogi icchā anantara udbhūta tathā bhūta aṅkuraḥ  yatas  iṣṭe tathāvidha ākāre niyamaḥ  bhāsate yatas  svapne ghaṭa paṭa ādīnām hetu tadvat svabhāva tā bhāsate niyamena eva bādhā śūnyena tāvati tatas  yāvati yādrūpyāt niyamaḥ  bādha varjitaḥ bhāti tāvati tādrūpyāt dṛḍha hetu phala ātma tā tathābhūte ca niyame hetu tadvattva kāriṇi vastutaścid mayasya eva hetu tā tad hi sarvagam ata eva ghaṭa udbhūtau sāmagrī hetuḥ ucyate sāmagrī ca samagrāṇām yadi ekam na iṣyate vapuḥ hetu bhedāt na bhedaḥ syāt  phale tad ca asamañjasam yadi asya anuvidhatte tām anvaya vi atireki tām tad tasya hetu ced saḥ yam kuṇṭha tarkaḥ  na naḥ priyaḥ samagrāḥ ca yathā daṇḍasūtra cakra kara ādayaḥ dūrāḥ ca bhāvinaḥ ca ittham hetu tvena iti manmahe yadi tatra bhavet meruḥ bhaviṣyan vā api kaścana na jāyeta ghaṭaḥ  nūnam tad pratyūha vyapohitaḥ yathā ca cakram niyate deśe kāle ca hetu tām yāti karki sumeru ādyāḥ tadvat svastha avadhi sthitāḥ tathā ca teṣām hetunām saṃyojana viyojane niyate śiva eva ekaḥ svatantraḥ kartṛ tām iyāt kumbhakārasya yā saṃvid  cakra daṇḍa ādi yojane śiva eva hi sā yasmāt  saṃvidaḥ kā viśiṣṭa tā kaumbhakārī tu saṃvittiḥ avaccheda avabhāsanāt  bhinna kalpā yadi kṣepyā daṇḍa cakra ādi madhyatas  tasmāt ekaika nirmāṇe śivaḥ  viśva eka vigrahaḥ kartā iti puṃsaḥ kartṛtva abhimānaḥ  pi vibhoḥ kṛtiḥ ata eva tathā ābhāna parama artha tayā sthiteḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāvasya loke śāstre ca citra tā māyātaḥ  vyakta kalayoḥ iti raurava saṃgrahe śrī pūrve tu kalā tattvāt avyaktam iti kathyate tatas  eva niśā ākhyānāt kalībhūtāt aliṅgakam iti vyākhyā asmad ukte smin sati nyāye tiniṣphalā loke ca gomayāt kīṭāt  saṃkalpāt svapnataḥ smṛteḥ yogi icchātaḥ dravya mantra prabhāva ādeḥ ca vṛścikaḥ anya eva sa ced  kāmam kutaścid sva viśeṣataḥ sa tu sarvatra tulyaḥ tad parāmarśa aikyam asti tu tatas  eva svarūpe pi krame pyanyādṛśī sthitiḥ śāstreṣu yujyate citrāt  tathā abhāva svabhāvataḥ puṃrāga vid kalā kāla māyā jñāna uttare kramāt  niyatiḥ na asti vairiñce kalā ūrdhve niyatiḥ śratā puṃrāga vid trayāt ūrdhvam kalā niyati saṃpuṭam kālaḥ  māyā iti kathitaḥ kramaḥ kiraṇa śāstra gaḥ pumān niyatyā kālaḥ ca rāga vidyā kalā anvitaḥ iti eṣa krama uddiṣṭaḥ  mātaṅge pārameśvare kārya kāraṇa bhāvīye tattve ittham vyavasthite śrī pūrvaśāstre kathitām vacmaḥ kāraṇa kalpanām śivaḥ svatantra dṛś rūpaḥ pañca śakti sunirbharaḥ svātantrya bhāsita bhidā pañcadhā pravibhajyate cit ānanda īṣaṇa ajñāna kriyāṇām su sphuṭa tvataḥ śiva śakti sadeśānavidyā ākhyam tattva pañcakam ekaikatra api tattve smin sarva śakti su nirbhare tad tad prādhānya yogena sa sa bhedaḥ  nirūpyate tathā hi sva svatantratva paripūrṇa tayā vibhuḥ niḥsaṃkhyaiḥ bahubhī rūpaiḥ bhāti avaccheda varjanāt  śāṃbhavāḥ śakti jā mantra maheśā mantranāyaka ah mantrā iti viśuddhāḥ syuḥ amī pañca gaṇāḥ kramāt  svasmin svasmin gaṇe bhāti yad yad rūpam samanvayi tadeṣu tattvam iti uktam kālāgni ādeḥ dharā ādivat  tena yad prāhuḥ ākhyāna sādṛśyena viḍambitāḥ guru upāsām vinā eva ātta pustaka abhīṣṭa dṛṣṭayaḥ brahmā nivṛtti adhipatiḥ pṛthak tattvam na gaṇyate sadāśiva ādyāḥ tu pṛthak  gaṇyanta iti kaḥ  nayaḥ brahma viṣṇu hara īśānasu śivān āśrita ātmani ṣaṭke kāraṇa saṃjñe rdhajarati iyam iyam kutas  iti tad mūlataḥ dhvastam gaṇitam na hi kāraṇam yathā pṛthivī adhipatiḥ nṛpaḥ tattva antaram na hi tathā tad tad kaleśānaḥ pṛthak  tattva antaram katham tad evam pañcakam idam śuddhaḥ  dhvā paribhāṣyate tatra sākṣāt śiva icchā eva kartri ābhāsita bhedikā īśvara icchā vaśa kṣubdha bhoga lolika cid gaṇān saṃvibhaktum aghora īśaḥ sṛjati iha sitetaram aṇūnām lolikā nāma niṣkarmā yā abhilāṣitā apūrṇaṃmanyata ajñānam malam sa avacchida ujjhitā yogyatā mātram eva etad bhāvi avat cheda saṃgrahe malaḥ tena asya na pṛthak tattva bhāvaḥ  sti rāgavat  niravaccheda karma aṃśa mātra avacchedataḥ tu sā rāgaḥ puṃsi dhiyaḥ  dharmaḥ karma bheda vicitra tā apūrṇam anya tā ca iyam tathārūpa avabhāsanam svatantrasya śivasya icchā ghaṭa rūpaḥ  yathā ghaṭaḥ sva ātma pracchādana icchā eva vastu bhūtaḥ tathā malaḥ yathā eva avyatiriktasya dharā ādeḥ bhāvitātma tā tathā eva asya iti śāstreṣu vyatiriktaḥ sthitaḥ  malaḥ vyatiriktaḥ svatantraḥ tu na kaḥ  pi śakaṭa ādivat  tad sa dvitīyā sa aśuddhiḥ śiva muktā aṇu gā na kim malasya roddhrī kā api asti śaktiḥ sa ca api amukta gā iti nyāya ujjhitaḥ  vādaḥ śraddhā mātra eka kalpitaḥ roddhrī śaktiḥ jaḍasya asau svayam na eva pravartate svayam pravṛttau viśvam syāt tathā ca īśanikā pramā malasya roddhrīm tām śaktim īśaḥ ced saṃyunakti tad  kīdṛśam pratyaṇum iti praśne na asti uttaram vacaḥ malaḥ ca āvaraṇam tad ca na avāryasya viśeṣakam upalambham vihanti etad ghaṭasya iva paṭa āvṛtiḥ malena āvṛta rūpāṇām aṇūnām yad sa tattvakam śiva eva ca tad paśyet tasya eva asau malaḥ  bhavet  vibhoḥ jñāna kriyā mātra sārasya aṇu gaṇasya ca tad abhāvaḥ  malaḥ  rūpa dhvaṃsāya eva prakalpate dharmāt dharmiṇi yaḥ  bhedaḥ samavāyena ca ekatā na tad bhavadbhiḥ uditam kaṇa bhojana śiṣyavat na amūrtena na mūrtena prāvarītum ca śakyate jñānam cākṣuṣa raśmīnām tathā abhāve sarati api sa eva ca malaḥ  mūrtaḥ kim jñānena na vedyate sarvageṇa tatas  sarvaḥ sarvajña tvam na kim bhajet  yaḥ ca dhvāntāt prakāśasya āvṛtiḥ tad pratighātibhiḥ mūrtānām pratighaḥ tejaḥ  ṇūnām na amūrta īdṛśam na ca cetanam ātmānam asvatantraḥ  malaḥ kṣamaḥ āvarītum na cācyam ca madya āvṛti nidarśanam uktam bhavadbhiḥ eva ittham jaḍaḥ kartā na hi svayam svatantrasya īśvarasya etāḥ śaktayaḥ prerikāḥ kila atas  karma vipāka jña prabhu śakti bala īritam madyam sūte madam duḥkha sukha moha phala ātmakam na ca īśa preritaḥ puṃsaḥ mala āvṛṇuyāt yatas  nirmale puṃsi na īśasya preraka tvam tathā ucitam tulye nirmala bhāve ca prerayeyuḥ na te katham tam īśam prati yuktam yad  bhūyasām syāt sadharma tā tena svarūpa svātantrya mātram mala vijṛmbhitam nirṇītam vitatam ca etad mayā anyatra iti alam punar  malaḥ  bhilāṣaḥ ca ajñānam avidyā lolikā prathā bhava doṣaḥ  nuplavaḥ ca glāniḥ śoṣaḥ  vimūḍha tā ahaṃmam ātma tā taṅkaḥ  māyā śaktiratha āvṛtiḥ doṣa bījam paśu tvam ca saṃsāra aṅkura kāraṇam ityādi an vartha saṃjñābhiḥ tatra tatra eṣa bhaṇyate asmin sati bhavati bhavaḥ  duṣṭaḥ  bheda ātmanā iti bhava doṣaḥ mañcavat asmin duḥkha srotaḥ  ṇūn vahati yad plavaḥ tena śeṣāḥ tu sugama rūpāḥ śabdāḥ tatra artham ūhayet ucitam saṃsāra kāraṇam karma saṃsāra aṅkura ucyate caturdaśavidham bhūta vaiciatryam karma jam yatas  ata eva sāṃkhya yoga pāñcarātra ādi śāsane ahaṃmam eti saṃtyāgaḥ  naiṣkarmyāya upadiśyate niṣkarmā hi sthite mūla male pyajñāna nāmani vaicitrya kāraṇā bhāvāt na ūrdhva sarati na api adhas  kevalam pārimityena śiva abhedam asaṃspṛśan vijñāna kevalī proktaḥ śuddha cit mātra saṃsthitaḥ sa punar  śāṃbhavet śātaḥ śiva abhedam parāmṛśan kramāt mantreśa tannetṛ rūpaḥ  yāti śiva ātma tām nanu kāraṇam etasya karmaṇaḥ ced malaḥ katham sa vijñānākalasya api na sūte karma saṃtatim mā evam sa hi malaḥ  jñānākale didhvaṃsiṣuḥ katham hetuḥ syāt dhvaṃsamāna tvam svātantryāt eva ca udbhavet  didhvaṃsiṣu dhvaṃsamāna dhvasta ākhyāsu tisṛṣu atha daśāsu antaḥ kṛta avasthā antarāsu sva krama sthiteḥ vijñānākala mantra īśa tadīśa āditva kalpanā tatas ca supte turye ca vakṣyate bahu bheda tā atas  pradhvaṃsanā aunmukhya khilībhūta sva śaktikaḥ karmaṇaḥ  hetu tām etu malaḥ katham iva ucyatām kim ca karma api na malāt yatas  karma kriyā ātmakam kriyā ca kartṛ tā rūpāt  svātantryāt na punar malāt  yā tu asya karmaṇaḥ citra phala da tvena karma tā prasiddhā sā na saṃkocam vinā ātmani malaḥ ca saḥ vicitram hi phalam bhinnam bhogya tvena abhimanyate bhoktari ātmani tena iyam bheda rūpā vyavasthitiḥ iti sva kārya prasave sahakāri tvam āśrayan sāmarthya vyañjaka tvena karmaṇaḥ kāraṇam malaḥ nanu evam karma sadbhāvāt malasya api sthiteḥ katham vijñānākalatā tasya saṃkocaḥ  hi asti tādṛśaḥ maivam adhvasta saṃkocaḥ  pyasau bhāvanayā dṛḍham na aham kartā iti manvānaḥ karma saṃskāram ujjhati phaliṣyati idam karma iti yā dṛḍhā vṛttiḥ ātmani sa saṃskāraḥ phalāya iha na tu smaraṇa kāraṇam apradhvaste pi saṃkoce na aham kartā iti bhāvanāt  na phalam kṣīva mūḍha ādeḥ prāyaścitte tha vā kṛte yad mayā adya tapaḥ taptam tad asmai syāt iti sphuṭam abhisaṃdhimataḥ karma na phalet abhisandhitaḥ tathā abhisaṃdhāna ākhyām tu mānase karma saṃskriyām phala uparaktām vidadhat kalpate phala sampade yaḥ tu tatra api dārḍhyena phala saṃskāram ujjhati sa tad phala tyāga kṛtam viśiṣṭam phalam aśnute anayā paripāṭyā yaḥ samastām karma saṃtatim anahaṃyutayā projjhet  sa saṃkocaḥ  pi saḥ  kalaḥ nanu ittham duṣkṛtam kiṃcid ātmīyam abhisaṃdhitaḥ parasmai syāt na vijñātam bhavatā tāttvikam vacaḥ tasya bhoktuḥ tathā ced syāt abhisaṃdhiḥ yathā ātmani tad avaśyam parasya api sataḥ tad duṣkṛtam bhavet  para abhisaṃdhi saṃvittau sva abhisaṃdhiḥ dṛḍhībhavet  abhisaṃdhāna virahe tu asya naḥ phalayogi tā na me duṣkṛtam iti eṣā rūḍhiḥ tasya aphalāya sā para abhisandhi vicchede sva ātmanā anabhisaṃhitau dvayoḥ api phalam na syāt nāśa hetu vyavasthiteḥ sukha hetau sukhe ca asya sāmānyāt abhisaṃdhitaḥ nirviśeṣāt api nyāyyā dharma ādi phala bhoktṛ tā duḥkham me duḥkha hetuḥ vā stād iti eṣa punar na tu sāmānyaḥ  pyabhisaṃdhiḥ syāt tad adharmasya na āgamaḥ prakṛtam brūmahe jñānākalasya ukta carasya yad  anahaṃyutayā sarvā vilīnāḥ karma saṃskriyāḥ tasmāt asya na karma asti kasya api sahakāritām malaḥ karotu tena ayam dhvaṃsamāna tvam aśnute apadhvasta malaḥ tu antar śiva āveśa vaśīkṛtaḥ ahaṃbhāva paraḥ  pya iti na karma adhīna vṛtti tām uktam śrī pūrvaśāstre ca tad etad parameśinā malam ajñānam icchanti saṃsāra aṅkura kāraṇam dharma adharma ātmakam karma sukha duḥkha ādi lakṣaṇam lakṣayet sukha duḥkha ādi svam kārya hetu bhāvataḥ na hi hetuḥ kadāpi āste vinā kārya nijam kvacid  hetu tā yogya tā eva asau phala anantarya bhāvitā pūrvakasya tu hetu tvam pāramparyeṇa kim ca tad  lakṣyate sukha duḥkha ādyaiḥ samāne dṛṣṭa kāraṇe citraiḥ hetu antaram kiṃcid tad ca karma iha darśanāt  sva aṅge prasāda raukṣya ādi jāyamānam sva karmaṇā dṛṣṭam iti anya deha stham kāraṇam karma kalpyāte iha api anya anya deha sthe sphuṭam karma phale yatas  kṛṣi karma madhau bhogaḥ śaradi anyā ca sā tanuḥ anusaṃdhātuḥ ekasya saṃbhavaḥ tu yatas tatas  tasya eva tad phalam citram karma yasya purātanam kṣīvaḥ  pi rājā sūdam ced ādiśet prātar īdṛśam bhojaya iti anusaṃdhānāt vinā prāpnoti tad phalam ittham janma antara upātta karmā api adya anusaṃdhinā vinā bhuṅkte phalam hetuḥ tatra prācyā hi akampatā ata eva kṛtam karma karmaṇā tapasā api vā jñānena vā nirudhyeta phala pākeṣu anunmukham ārabdha kāryam dehe smin yad punar  karma tad katham ucchidyatām antya daśam niroddhum na hi śakyate tatra eva dehe yad tu nyadat yagam vā purātanam karma tad jñāna dīkṣā ādyaiḥ śaṇḍhīkartum prasahyate tathā saṃskāra dārḍhya hi phalāya dṛḍha tā punar  yadā yadā vinaśyeta karma dhvastam tadā tadā atas  moha para adhīnaḥ  yadi api akṛta kiṃcana tathā api jñāna kāle tad sarvam eva pradahyate uktam ca śrī pare hāna ādānaḥ sarvadṛś ulvaṇaḥ muhūrtāt nirdahet sarva deha stham akṛtam kṛtam deha stham iti dehena saha tādātmyam āśritā svācchandyāt saṃvid eva uktā tatrastham karma dahyate deha aikya vāsanā atyāgāt sa ca viśva ātma tā sthiteḥ akāla kalite vyāpini abhinne yā hi saṃskriyā saṃkoca eva sā anena saḥ  pi deha eka tāmayaḥ etad kārma m alam proktam yena sākam layākalāḥ syuḥ guhā gahana antar sthāḥ suptā iva sarīsṛpāḥ tatas  prabuddha saṃskārāḥ te yathocita bhāginaḥ brahma ādi sthāvara ante smin saṃsranti punar  punar  ye punar  karma saṃskāra hānyai prārabdha bhāvanāḥ bhāvanā pariniṣpattim aprāpya pralayam gatāḥ mahāntam te tathā antar stha bhāvanā pāka sauṣṭhavāt  mantra tvam pratipadyante citrāt citram ca karmataḥ asya kārmam alasya iyan māyā anta adhva visāriṇaḥ pradhānam kāraṇam proktam ajñāna ātmā aṇavaḥ  malaḥ kṣobhaḥ  sya lolikā ākhyasya sahakāritayā sphuṭam tiṣṭhāsā yogyatā aunmukhyam īśvara icchā vaśāt ca tad  na jaḍaḥ cit adhiṣṭhānam vinā kvāpi kṣamaḥ yatas  aṇavaḥ  nāma na eva anyat prakāśa ātmā maheśvaraḥ cit acit rūpa tā bhāsī pudgalaḥ kṣetra vid paśuḥ cit rūpa tvāt ca sa vyāpī nirguṇaḥ  niṣkriyaḥ tatas  yoga upāya īpsakaḥ  nityaḥ  mūrti vandhyaḥ prabhāṣyate acit tvāt ajña tā bhedaḥ  bhogyāt bhoktṛ antarāt atha teṣām aṇūnām sa mala īśvara icchā vaśāt bhṛśam prabudhyate tathā ca uktam śāstre śrī pūrva nāmani īśvara icchā vaśādasya bhoga icchā saṃprajāyate bhoga icchoḥ upakāra artham ādyaḥ  mantra maheśvaraḥ māyām vikṣobhya saṃsāram nirmimīte vicitrakam māyā ca nāma devasya śaktiḥ avyatirekiṇī bheda avabhāsa svātantryam tathā hi sa tayā kṛtaḥ ādyaḥ  bheda avabhāsaḥ  yaḥ  vibhāgam anupeyivān garbhīkṛta ananta bhāvi vibhāsā sā parā niśā sā jaḍā bheda rūpa tvāt  kāryam ca asyā jaḍam yatas  vyāpinī viśva hetu tvāt  sūkṣmā kārya eka kalpanāt  śiva śakti avinā abhāvāt nityā ekā mūla kāraṇam acetanam aneka ātma sarva kārya yathā ghaṭaḥ pradhānam ca tathā tasmāt  kārya na ātmā tu cetanaḥ ata eva adhvani proktā pūrvam māyā dvidhā sthitā yathā ca māyā devasya śaktiḥ abhyeti bhedinam tattva bhāvam tathā anyaḥ  pi kalā ādiḥ tattva vistaraḥ niruddha śakteḥ yā kiṃcitkartṛ tā udvalana ātmikā nāthasya śaktiḥ sādhastāt puṃsaḥ kṣeptrī kalā ucyate evam vidyāt ayaḥ  pyete dharā antāḥ paramārthataḥ śiva śakti mayā eva prokta nyāya anusārataḥ tathā api yad pṛthak bhānam kalā ādeḥ īśvara icchayā tatas  jaḍa tve kāryatve pṛthak tattva sthitau dhruvam upādānam smṛtā māyā kvacid tad kāryam eva ca tathā avabhāsa citram ca rūpam anyonya varjitam yad bhāti kila saṃkalpe tad asti ghaṭavat vahiḥ khapuṣpādyastitām brūmaḥ tatas  na vyabhicāritā khapuṣpam kāla diś mātṛ sāpekṣam nāstiśabdataḥ dharā ādivat  tathā atyanta abhāvaḥ  pi evam vivicyatām yad saṃkalpyam tathā tasya bahis dehaḥ  sti cetanaḥ caitravat sauśiva antam tad  sarva tādṛśa dehavat yasya dehaḥ  yathā tasya tad jātīyam puram bahis  atas  su śiva paryantā siddhā bhuvana paddhatiḥ ātmanām tad puram prāpyam deśa tvāt anya deśavat ātmanām adhu bhoktṛ tvam tatas  yatnena siddhyati sā māyā kṣobham āpannā viśvam sūte samantatas daṇḍa āhatā iva āmalakī phalāni kila yadi api tathā api tu tathā citra paurvāparya avabhāsanāt  māyā kārye pi tattva oghe kārya kāraṇa tā mithas  sā yadi api anya śāstreṣu bahudhā dṛśyate sphuṭam tathā api mālinīśāstra dṛśā tām saṃpracakṣmahe kalā ādi vasudhā antam yad māyā antaḥ saṃpracakṣate pratyātma bhinnam eva etad  sukha duḥkha ādi bhedataḥ ekasyām eva jagati bhoga sādhana saṃhatau sukha ādīnām samam vyakteḥ bhoga bhedaḥ kutaḥ bhavet  na ca asau karma bhedena tasya eva anupapattitaḥ tasmāt  kalā ādikaḥ  vargaḥ  bhinna eva kadācana aikyam eti īśvarecśātaḥ  nṛtta gīta ādi vādane eṣām kalā ādi tattvānām sarveṣām api bhāvinām śuddha tvam asti teṣām ye śaktipāta pavitritāḥ kalā hi śuddhā tad tādṛś  karma tvam saṃprasūyate mitam api āśu yena asmāt saṃsārāt eṣa mucyate rāga vidyā kālayati prakṛti akṣa artha saṃcayaḥ ittham śuddha iti procya guruḥ māna stutau vibhuḥ evam eṣā kalā ādīnām utpattiḥ pravivicyate māyā tattvāt kalā jātā kiṃcitkartṛtva lakṣaṇā māyā hi cit mayāt bhedam śivāt vidadhatī paśoḥ suṣupta tām iva ādhatte tatas  eva hi adṛkkriyaḥ kalā hi kiṃcitkartṛ tvam sūte su āliṅga nādaṇoḥ tasyāḥ ca api aṇunā anyonyam hi añjane sā prasūyate sadyonirvāṇa dīkṣā uttha puṃviśleṣe hi sā satī śliṣyanti api ca naḥ sūte tathā api sva phalam kvacid  ucchūna tā iva prathamā sūkṣma aṅkura kalā iva ca bījasya ambu agni mṛd kambu tuṣa yogāt prasūti kṛt  kalā māyā aṇu saṃyoga jā apyeṣā nirvikārakam na aṇum kuryāt upādānam kiṃtu māyām vikāriṇīm malaḥ ca āvārakaḥ  māyā bhāva upādāna kāraṇam karma syāt  sahakārī ā iva sukha duḥkha udbhavam prati atas  saṃcchanna caitanya samudbalana kārya kṛt kalā eva ananta nāthasya śaktyā saṃpreritā jaḍā na ca īśa śaktiḥ eva asya caitanyam balayiṣyati tad upodbalitam tad hi na kiṃcitkartṛ tām vrajet  sā iyam kalā na karaṇam mukhyam vidyā ādikam yathā puṃsi kartari sā kartrī prayojaka tayā yatas  alakṣya antarayoḥ ittham yadā puṃskalayoḥ bhavet  māyā garbheśa śakti ādeḥ antara jñānam āntaram tadā māyā puṃvivekaḥ sarva karma kṣayāt bhavet  vijñānākalatā māyā adhastāt na u yāti adhas  pumān dhī puṃviveke vijñāte pradhāna puruṣa antare api na kṣīṇa karmā syāt  kalāyām tad hi saṃbhavet  atas  sāṃkhya dṛśā siddhaḥ pradhāna adhas  na saṃsaret  kalā puṃsoḥ viveke tu māyā adhaḥ na eva gacchati malāt viviktam ātmānam paśyan  tu śiva tām vrajet  sarvatra ca aiśvaraḥ śaktipātaḥ  tra saha kāraṇam māyā garbha adhikārīyaḥ dvayoḥ antye tu nirmalaḥ sā iyam kalā kārya bhedāt anyā eva hi anumīyate anyathā ekam bhavet viśvam kāryāya iti anya nihnavaḥ iti mataṅga śāstra ādau yā proktā sā kalā svayam kiṃcid rūpa tayā ākṣipya kartṛ tvam iti bhaṅgitaḥ kiṃcid rūpa viśiṣṭam yad  kartṛ tvam tad katham bhavet  ajñasya iti tatas  sūte kiṃcijjñatva ātmikām vidam buddhim paśyati sā vidyā buddhi darpaṇa cāriṇaḥ sukha ādīn pratyayān moha prabhṛtīn kārya kāraṇe karma jālam ca tatrastham vivinakti nija ātmanā buddhiḥ tu guṇa saṃkīrṇā vivekena katham sukham duḥkham moha ātmakam vā api viṣayam darśayet api svacchāyām dhiyi saṃkrāman bhāvaḥ saṃvedyatām katham tayā vinā eti sā api anyat karaṇam puṃsi kartari nanu ca ubhayatas  śubhra ādarśa daśīya dhī gatāt puṃsprakāśāt bhāti bhāvaḥ mā evam tad pratibimbanam jaḍam eva hi mukhyaḥ  tha puṃsprakāśaḥ  sya bhāsanam bahis sthasya eva tasyāḥ tu buddheḥ kiṃkalpanā kṛtā abheda bhūmiḥ eṣā ca bhedaḥ ca iha vicāryate tasmāt buddhi gataḥ  bhāvaḥ vidyā karaṇa gocaraḥ bhāvānām pratibimbam ca vedyam dhī kalpanā tatas  kiṃcid tu kurute tasmāt nūnam asti aparam tu tad  rāga tattvam iti proktam yad tatra eva uparañjakam na ca avairāgya mātram tad tatra api āsakti vṛttitaḥ viraktau  api tṛptasya sūkṣma rāga vyavasthiteḥ kālaḥ tuṭi ādibhiḥ ca etad  kartṛ tvam kalayati atas  kārya avacchedi kartṛ tvam kālaḥ  vaśyam kaliṣyati niyatiḥ yojanām dhatte viśiṣṭe kārya maṇḍale vidyā rāgaḥ  tha niyatiḥ kālaḥ ca etad catuṣṭayam kalā kāryam bhoktṛ bhāve tiṣṭhat bhoktṛtva pūritam māyā kalā rāga vidye kālaḥ  niyatiḥ eva ca kañcukāni ṣaṣ uktāni saṃvidaḥ tad sthitau paśuḥ deha puryaṣṭaka ādyeṣu vedyeṣu kila vedanam etad ṣaṭkasa saṃkocam yad avedyam asau  aṇuḥ uktam śiva tanu śāstre tad idam bhaṅgi antareṇa punar  āvaraṇam sarva ātma gama śuddhiḥ anyā api ananya rūpā iva śiva dahana kiraṇa jālaiḥ dāhya tvāt  sā yatas  nyarūpā eva anidaṃpūrvatayā yad rañjayati nija ātmanā tatas  nanyā sahaja aśuddhimataḥ ṇoḥ īśa guhābhyām hi kañcukaḥ trividhaḥ tasya dvitīya citiḥ iva svacchasya niyujyate kalā ślakṣṇā anayā vidvasya paśoḥ upabhoga samartha tā bhavati vidyā ca asya kalātaḥ śaraṇa antar dīpaka prabhā ivā abhūt sukha duḥkha saṃvidam yā vivinakti paśoḥ vibhāgena rāgaḥ ca kalā tattvāt śuci vastra kaṣāyavat  samutpannaḥ tyaktum vāñchati na yatas  saṃsṛti sukha saṃvid ānandam evam avidyā malinaḥ samarthitaḥ triguṇa kañcuka balena gahana upabhoga garbhe paśuḥ avaśam adhomukhaḥ patati etena malaḥ kathitaḥ kambukavat aṇoḥ kalā ādikam tuṣavat  evam kalā ākhya tattvasya kiṃcitkartṛtva lakṣaṇe viśeṣa bhāge kartṛ tvam carcitam bhoktṛ pūrvakam viśeṣaṇa tayā yaḥ  tra kiñcid bhāgaḥ tadā utthitam vedya mātram sphuṭam bhinnam pradhānam sūyate kalā samam eva hi bhogyam ca bhoktāram ca prasūyate kalā bheda abhisaṃdhānāt aviyuktam parasparam bhoktṛ bhogya ātma tā na syāt viyogāt ca parasparam vilīnāyām ca tasyām syāt māyā asya api na kiṃcana nanu śrīmat raurava ādau rāga vidyā ātmakam dvayam sūte kalā hi yugapad tatas  vyaktam iti sthitiḥ uktam atra vibhāti eṣa kramaḥ satyam tathā hi alam rajyamānaḥ  veda sarva vidan  ca api atra rajyate tathā api vastu sattā iyam iha asmābhiḥ nirūpitā tasyām ca na kramaḥ kaḥ  pi syāt vā saḥ  pi viparyayāt  tasmāt vipratipattim naḥ kuryāt śāstra udite vidhau evam saṃvedya mātram yad  sukha duḥkha vimohataḥ bhotsyate yad tatas  proktam tad sāmya ātmakam āditas  sukham sattvam prakāśa tvāt  prakāśaḥ  hlāda ucyate duḥkham rajaḥ kriyā ātma tvāt  kriyā hi tad atad kramaḥ mohaḥ tamaḥ  varaṇakaḥ prakāśa abhāva yogataḥ ta ete kṣobham āpannā guṇāḥ kārya pratanvate akṣubdhasya vijātīyam na syāt  kāryamadaḥ purā uktam eva iti śāstre smin guṇān  tattva antaram viduḥ bhuvanam pṛthak eva atra darśitam guṇa bhedataḥ īśvara icchā vaśa kṣubdha lolikam puruṣam prati bhoktṛ tvāya svatantra īśaḥ prakṛtim kṣobhayet  bhṛśam tena yad ca udyate sāṃkhyam muktā aṇum prati kim na sā sūte puṃsaḥ vikāri tvāt iti tad na atra bādhakam guṇebhyaḥ  buddhi tattvam tad  sarvatas  nirmalam tatas  puṃsprakāśaḥ sa vedyaḥ  tra pratibimba tvam ārchati viṣaya pratibimbam ca tasyām akṣa kṛtam bahis  atad dvāram samutprekṣā pratibhā ādiṣu tādṛśī vṛttiḥ bodhaḥ bhavet buddheḥ sā ca api ālambanam dhruvam ātma saṃvid prakāśasya bodhaḥ  sau tad jaḍaḥ  pyalam buddheḥ ahaṃkṛt  tādṛkṣe pratibimbita puṃskṛteḥ prakāśe vedya kaluṣe yad ahaṃmanana ātma tā tayā pañcavidhaḥ ca eṣa vāyuḥ saṃrambha rūpayā preritaḥ  jīvanāya syāt anyathā maraṇam punar  ata eva viśuddha ātma svātantrya ahaṃsvabhāvataḥ akṛtrimāt idam tu anyat iti uktam kṛti śabdataḥ iti ayam karaṇa skandhaḥ  haṃkārasya nirūpitaḥ tridhā asya prakṛti skandhaḥ sāttva rājasa tāmasaḥ sattva pradhāna ahaṃkārāt bhoktṛ aṃśa sparśinaḥ sphuṭam manaḥ buddhi akṣa ṣaṭkam tu jātam bhedaḥ tu kathyate manaḥ  yad sarva viṣayam tena atra pravivakṣitam sarva tanmātra kartṛ tvam viśeṣaṇam ahaṃkṛteḥ buddhi ahaṃkṛt manaḥ prāhuḥ bodha saṃrabhaṇa eṣaṇe karaṇam bāhyadevaiḥ yad na eva api antarmukhaiḥ kṛtam prāṇaḥ ca na antaḥkaraṇam jaḍa tvāt  preraṇa ātmanaḥ prayatna icchā vibodha aṃśa hetu tvāt iti niścitam avasāyaḥ  bhimānaḥ ca kalpanā ca iti na kriyā eka rūpā tatas tri tvam yuktam antar kṛtau sphuṭam na ca buddhiḥ asaṃvedyā karaṇa tvāt manaḥ  yathā pradhānavat asaṃvedya buddhi vādaḥ tad ujjhitaḥ śabda tanmātra hetutva viśiṣṭā yā tu ahaṃkṛtiḥ sā śrotre karaṇam yāvat ghrāṇe gandhatva bhoditā bhautika tvam atas  pyaḥ tu niyamāt viṣayeṣu alam aham śṛṇomi paśyāmi jighrāmi ityādi saṃvidi ahaṃtā anugama āda ahaṃkārika tvam sphuṭam sthitam karaṇa tvam atas  yuktam kartṛ aśa spṛktva yogataḥ kartuḥ vibhinnam karaṇam prerya tvāt  karaṇam kutas  karaṇa antara vāñchāyām bhavet tatra anavasthitiḥ tasmāt  svātantrya yogena kartā svam bhedayan vapuḥ karma aśa sparśinam sva aṃśam karaṇīkurute svayam karaṇīkṛta tad sva aṃśa tanmayībhāvanā vaśāt karaṇīkurute tyanta vyatiriktam kuṭhāravat  tena aśuddhā eva vidyā asya sāmānyam karaṇam purā jñaptau kṛtau tu sāmānyam kalā karaṇam ucyate nanu śrīmat mataṅga ādau kalāyāḥ kartṛ tā uditā tasyām satyām hi vidyā ādyāḥ karaṇatva arhatā juṣaḥ ucyate kartṛ tā eva uktā karaṇa tve prayojikā tayā vinā tu na anyeṣām karaṇānām sthitiḥ yatas  atas  sāmānya karaṇa vargāt  tatra pṛthak  kṛtā vidyām vinā hi na anyeṣām karaṇānām nijā sthitiḥ kalām vinā na tasyāḥ ca kartṛ tve jñātṛ tā yatas  kalā vidye tatas  puṃsaḥ mukhyam tad karaṇam viduḥ ata eva vihīne pi buddhi karma indriyaiḥ kvacid  andhe paṅgau rūpa gati prakāśaḥ  na na bhāsate kiṃtu sāmānya karaṇa balāt vedye pi tādṛśi rūpa sāmānya eva andhaḥ pratipattim prapadyate tatas  eva tu ahaṃkārāt  tanmātra sparśinaḥ dhikam karmendriyāṇi vāc pāṇi pāyu upastha aṅghri jajñire vacmi ādade tyajāmi āśu visṛjāmi vrajāmi ca iti yā ahaṃkriyā kārya kṣamā karmendriyam tu tad  tena cchinna karasya asti hastaḥ karmendriya ātmakaḥ tasya pradhāna adhiṣṭhānam param pañcāṅguliḥ karaḥ mukhena api yad ādānam tatra yad  karaṇam sthitam sa pāṇiḥ eva karaṇam vinā kim saṃbhavet  kriyā tathā abhāve tu buddhi akṣaiḥ api kim syāt prayojanam darśanam karaṇa apekṣam kriyā tvāt iti ca ucyate paraiḥ gamau tu karaṇam na iṣyate ca iti vismayaḥ gamana utkṣepaṇa ādīni mukhyam karma upalambhanam punar guṇaḥ kriyā tu eṣā vaiyākaraṇa darśane kriyā karaṇa pūrva iti vyāptyā karaṇa pūrvakam jñānam na ādānam iti etad  sphuṭam āndhya vijṛmbhitam tasmāt  karmendriyāṇi āhuḥ tvagvat vyāptṝṇi mukhyatas  tad sthāne vṛttimanti iti mataṅge guravaḥ  mama nanu anyāni api karmāṇi santi bhūyāṃsi tad kṛte karaṇāni api vācyāni tathā ca akṣeṣu aniṣṭhitiḥ nanu etad  kheṭapāla ādyaiḥ nirākāri na karmaṇām yad sādhanam tad akṣam syāt  kiṃtu kasya api karmaṇaḥ etad na asmad kṛta praśna tṛṣṇā saṃtāpa śāntaye na hi asvat śamita prāyaiḥ jalaiḥ tṛpyanti barhiṇaḥ ucyate śrīmat ādiṣṭam śaṃbhu nā atra mama uttaram su accha saṃvedana udāra vikalā prabalīkṛtam iha karma anusaṃdhāna bhedāt ekam vibhidyate tatra anusaṃdhiḥ pañca ātmā pañca karmendriyāṇi atas  tyāgāya ādāna saṃpattyai dvayāya dvitayam vinā sva rūpa viśrānti kṛte caturdhā karma yad bahis  pāyu pāṇi aṅghri jananam karaṇam tad caturvidham antam prāṇa āśrayam yad tu karma atra karaṇam hi vāc  uktāḥ samāsatas ca eṣām citrāḥ kāryeṣu vṛttayaḥ tad etad vyatiriktam hi na karma kvāpi dṛśyate tad kasya arthe prakalpyā iyam indriyāṇām aniṣṭhitiḥ etad kartavya cakram tad asāṃkaryeṇa kurvate akṣāṇi saha vṛttyā tu buddhi ante saṃkaram jaḍāḥ ukta indriya vargaḥ  yam ahaṃkārāt  tu rājasāt  tamaḥ pradhāna ahaṃkārāt  bhoktṛ aṃśa  chādana ātmanaḥ bhūta ādi nāmnaḥ tanmātra pañcakam bhūtakāraṇam manaḥ buddhi akṣa karma akṣa vargaḥ tanmātravargakaḥ iti atra rājasa ahaṃkṛt yogaḥ saṃśleṣa kaḥ  dvaye anye tu āhuḥ manaḥ  jātam rājasa ahaṃkṛteḥ yatas samasta indriya saṃcāra caturam laghu vegavat  anye tu sāttvikāt  sva antam buddhi karma indriyāṇi tu rājasāt grāhaka grāhya bhāga sparśīni manvate kheṭapālāḥ tu manyante karmendriya gaṇaḥ sphuṭam rājasa ahaṃkṛteḥ jātaḥ  rajasaḥ karma tā yatas  śrī pūrvaśāstre tu manaḥ  rājasāt  sāttvikāt punar  indriyāṇi samastāni yuktam ca etad vibhāti naḥ tathā hi bāhya vṛttīnām akṣāṇām vṛtti bhāsane ālocane śaktiḥ antar yojane manasaḥ punar  uktam ca guruṇā kuryāt manaḥ  nu vyavasāyi sat  tad dvaya ālambanā mātṛ vyāpāra ātma kriyā iti tān mātraḥ tu gaṇaḥ  dhvānta pradhānāyāḥ  ahaṃkṛteḥ atra avivādaḥ sarvasya grāhya upakrama eva hi pṛthivyām saurabhāni ādi vicitre gandha maṇḍale yad sāmānyam hi gandha tvam gandha tanmātra nāma tad  vyāpakam tatas  eva uktam sa hetu tvāt tu na dhruvam sva kāraṇe tirobhūtiḥ dhvasaḥ yad tena na adhruvam evam rasa ādi śabda anta tanmātreṣu api yojanā viśeṣāṇām yatas  vaśyam daśā prāc aviśeṣiṇī kṣubhitam śabda tanmātram citra ākārāḥ śratīḥ dadhat  nabhaḥ śabdaḥ  vakāśa ātmā vācya adhyāsa sahaḥ yatas  tad etad sparśa tanmātra yogāt prakṣobham āgatam vāyu tām eti tena atra śabda sparśa ubhaya ātma tā anye tu āhuḥ dhvaniḥ kha eka guṇaḥ tad api yujyate yatas  vāyuḥ nijam rūpam labhate na vinā ambarāt  uttarottara bhūteṣu pūrva pūrva sthitiḥ yatas  tatas  eva marut vyomnoḥ viyogaḥ  mithas  smṛtaḥ śabda sparśau tu rūpeṇa samam prakṣobham āgatau tejaḥ tattvam tribhiḥ dharmaiḥ prāhuḥ pūrvavat eva tad  taiḥ tribhiḥ sarasairāpaḥ sa gandhaiḥ bhūḥ iti kramaḥ tatra pratyakṣataḥ siddhaḥ  dharā ādi guṇa saṃcayaḥ na hi gandha ādi dharma ogha vyatiriktā vibhāti bhūḥ yathā guṇa guṇi dvaita vādinām ekam api adaḥ citram rūpam paṭe bhāti kramāt dharmāḥ tathā bhuvi yathā ca vistṛte vastre yugapad bhāti citra tā tathā eva yoginām dharma sāmastyena avabhāti bhūḥ gandha ādi śabda paryanta citra rūpā dharā tatas  upāya bhedāt bhāti eṣā krama ākrama vibhāgataḥ tatas  eva krama vyakti kṛtaḥ  dhī bheda ucyate ṣaṣṭhī prayogaḥ  dhī bhedāt bhedi abhedaka tā tathā tena dharma atiriktaḥ  tra dharmī nāma na kaścana tatra aneka prakārāḥ syuḥ gandha rūpa rasāḥ kṣitau saṃsparśaḥ pākajaḥ  nuṣṇa aśītaḥ śabdaḥ  vicitrakaḥ śauklyam mādhurya śīta tve citrāḥ śabdāḥ ca vāriṇi śukla bhāsvarata uṣṇa tvam citrāḥ śabdāḥ ca pāvake apāka jaḥ ca aśīta uṣṇaḥ  dhvaniḥ citraḥ ca mārute varṇa ātmakaḥ  dhvaniḥ śabda pratibimbāni atha ambare yad tu na sparśavat dharmaḥ śabda ityādi bhaṇyate kāṇādaiḥ tad sva pratīti viruddham kena gṛhyatām paṭahe dhvaniḥ iti eva bhāti abādhitam eva yad  na ca hetutva mātreṇa tad ādānatva vedanāt śrotram ca asmad mate haṃkṛt kāraṇam tatra tatra tad  vṛtti bhāgī iti tad deśam śabdam gṛhṇāti alam tathā yaḥ tu āha śrotram ākāśam karṇa saṃyoga bheditam śabda jaḥ śabda āgatya śabda buddhim prasūyate tasya mande pi muraja dhvanau  ākarṇake sati amutra śrutiḥ eṣā iti dūre saṃvedanam katham na hi śabda ja śabdasya dūrādūra rava uditeḥ śrotra ākāśa gatasya asti dūrāt ūra svabhāva tā na ca asau prathamaḥ śabdaḥ tāvat vyāpi iti yujyate tatrasthaiḥ saha tīvra ātmā śrūyamāṇaḥ tu anena tu katham śrūyeta mandaḥ sanna hi dharma antara āśrayaḥ etad ca anyaiḥ apākāri bahudhā iti vṛthā punar  na āyaḥ tam patita āghāta dāne kaḥ  hi na paṇḍitaḥ amīṣām tu dharā ādīnām yāvān  tattva gaṇaḥ purā guṇa adhika tayā tiṣṭhan vyāptā tāvān prakāśate vyāpya vyāpaka tā yā eṣā tattvānām darśitā kila sā guṇa ādhikyataḥ siddhā na hetu tvāt na lāghavāt  ahetunā api rāgaḥ  hi vyāptaḥ  vidyā ādinā sphuṭam tad vinā na bhavet yad tad vyāptam iti ucyate yatas  na lāghavam ca nāma asti kiṃcid atra sva darśane guṇa ādhikya ādatas  jñeyā vyāpya vyāpaka tā sphuṭā yaḥ  hi yasmāt guṇa utkṛṣṭaḥ sa tasmāt ūrdhva ucyate ūrdhva tā vyāptṛ tā śrīmat mālinīvijaye sphuṭā atas  śiva tvāt prabhṛti prakāśatā svarūpam ādāya nija ātmani dhruvam samasta tattva āvali dharma saṃcayaiḥ vibhāti bhūḥ vyāptṛ tayā sthitaiḥ alam evam jala ādeḥ api śakti tattva paryanta dhāmnaḥ  vapuḥ asti tādṛś  kim tu uttaram śakti tayā eva tattvam pūrva tu tad dharmatayā iti bhedaḥ anuttara prakriyāyām vaitatyena pradarśitam etad  tasmāt  tatas  paśyet vistara arthī vivecakaḥ iti tattvasya rūpasya kṛtam samyak  prakāśanam  ch atha śrī tantrāloke daśamam āhnikam ucyate trikaśāstreka rahasyam tattva bhedanam b teṣām amīṣām tattvānām sva vargeṣu anugāminām bheda antaram api proktam śāstre tra śrītrikā abhidhe śaktimat śakti bhedena dharā ādyam mūla paścimam bhidyate pañcadaśadhā sva rūpeṇa sa hānarāt kalā antam bheda yuj hīnam rudravat pralayākalaḥ tadvat māyā ca navadhā jñākalāḥ saptadhā punar  mantrāḥ tad īśāḥ pāñcadhye mantreśa patayaḥ tridhā śivaḥ  na bhidyate sva eka prakāśa ghana cit mayaḥ śivaḥ  mantra maheśeśa mantrā akala yuj kalī śaktimantaḥ sapta tathā śaktayaḥ tad caturdaśa svam svarūpam pañcadaśam tad bhūḥ pañcadaśa ātmikā tathā hi tisraḥ  devasya śaktayaḥ varṇitāḥ purā tā eva mātṛm āmeya trairūpyeṇa vyavasthitāḥ parāṃśaḥ mātṛ rūpaḥ  tra pramāṇa aṃśaḥ parāparaḥ meyaḥ  paraḥ śaktimān  ca śaktiḥ svam rūpam iti adaḥ tatra svarūpam bhūmeḥ yad pṛthak jaḍam avasthitam mātṛ māna ādi upadhibhiḥ asaṃjāta uparāgakam sakala ādi śiva antaiḥ tu mātṛbhiḥ vedyatā asya yā śaktimadbhiḥ anudbhūta śaktibhiḥ sapta tad bhidaḥ sakala ādi śiva antānām śaktiṣu udrecita ātmasu vedya tā janitāḥ sapta bhedā iti caturdaśa sakalasya pramāṇa aṃśaḥ  yaḥ  sau vidyā kalā ātmakaḥ sāmānya ātmā sa śakti tve gaṇitaḥ  na tu tad bhidaḥ layākalasya māna aṃśaḥ sa eva parama sphuṭaḥ jñānākalasya mānam tu galat vidyā kalā vṛti aśuddha vidyā kalana adhvaṃsa saṃskāra saṃgatā prabubhutsuḥ śuddhavidyā santrāṇām karaṇam bhavet  prabuddhā śuddhavidyā tu tad saṃskāreṇa saṃgatā mānam mantreśvarāṇām syāt tad saṃskāra vivarjitā mānam mantra maheśānām karaṇam śaktiḥ ucyate svātantrya mātra sadbhāvā yā tu icchā śaktiḥ aiśvarī śivasya sā eva karaṇam tayā vetti karoti ca ā śivāt sakala antam ye mātāraḥ sapta te dvidhā nyagbhūta udrikta śakti tvāt tad bhedaḥ  vedya bhedakaḥ tathā hi vedya tā nāma bhāvasya eva nijam vapuḥ caitreṇa vedyam vedmi iti kiṃhi atra pratibhāsatām nanu caitrīya vijñāna mātram atra prakāśate vedya tā ākhyaḥ tu naḥ dharmaḥ  bhāti bhāvasya nīlavat  vedya tā ca svabhāvena dharmaḥ  bhāvasya ced tatas sarvān pratyeva vedyaḥ syāt haṭa nīla ādi dharmavat atha vedaka saṃvitti balāt vedyatva dharma bhāj  bhāvaḥ tathā api doṣaḥ  sau kuvinda kṛta vastravat  vedya tā ākhyaḥ tu yaḥ  dharmaḥ saḥ  vedyaḥ ced kha puṣpavat  vedyaḥ ced asti tatra api vedyetati anavasthitiḥ tatas  na kiṃcid vedyam syāt mūrchitam tu jagat bhavet  nanu vijñātru pādhyam śaḥ paskṛtam vapuḥ ucyatām bhāvasya artha prakāśa ātma yathā jñānam idam tu asat eka vijñātṛ vedya tve na jñātṛ antara vedya tā samasta jñātṛ vedya tve na eka vijñātṛ vedya tā tasmāt na vedya tā nāma bhāva dharmaḥ  sti kaścana bhāvasya vedya tā sā eva saṃvidaḥ  yaḥ samudbhavaḥ artha grahaṇa rūpam hi yatra vijñānam ātmani samavaiti prakāśyaḥ  rthaḥ tam pratyeṣa eva vedya tā atra brūmaḥ padārthānām na dharmaḥ  yadi vedya tā avedyā eva te saṃsyuḥ jñāne sati api varṇite yathā hi pṛthu budhna ādi rūpe kumbhasya sati api atadātmā paṭaḥ na eti pṛthu budhna ādi rūpa tām tathā sati api vijñāne vijñātṛ samavāyini avedya dharmakā bhāvāḥ katham vedya tvam āpnuyuḥ anarthaḥ su mahān  ca eṣa dṛśyatām vastu yad svayam prakāśa ātma na tad saṃvicca aprakāśā tad āśrayaḥ aprakāśaḥ  manaḥ dīpa cakṣuḥ ādi tathā eva tad  kim tad prakāśa tām nāma supte jagati sarvatas  jñānasya artha prakāśa tvam nanu rūpam pradīpavat  apūrvam atra viditam narīnṛtyāmahe tatas  artha prakāśaḥ  jñānasya yad rūpam tad nirūpya tām arthaḥ prakāśaḥ ced rūpam arthaḥ  vā jñānam eva vā atha arthasya prakāśaḥ  yaḥ tad rūpam iti bhaṇyate ṣaṣṭhī kartari ced uktaḥ  doṣa eva duruddharaḥ atha karmaṇi ṣaṣṭhī eṣā ṇi arthaḥ tatra hṛdi sthitaḥ tathā ca idam darśayāmaḥ kim prakāśaḥ prakāśate aprakāśaḥ  pi na eva asau tathā api ca na kiṃcana tarhi loke katham ṇi arthaḥ ucyate cetana sthitau mukhyaḥ  ṇi arthasya viṣayaḥ  jaḍeṣu tu aupacārikaḥ tathā hi gantum śaktaḥ  pi caitraḥ  nyāyat tatām gateḥ manvāna eva vakti asmi gamitaḥ svāminā iti hi svāmi api asya gatau śaktim buddhvā svādhīna tām sphuṭam paśyat nivṛttim āśaṃkya gamayāmi iti bhāṣate prerya prerakayoḥ evam maulikī ṇi artha saṃgatiḥ tad abhiprāyataḥ  nyaḥ pi loke vyavaharet tathā śaram gamayati iti atra punar vega ākhya saṃskriyām vidadhat prerakam manya upacāreṇa jāyate vāyuḥ adriṃ pātayati iti atra dvau  api tau jaḍau draṣṭṛbhiḥ preraka prerya vapuṣā parikalpitau ittham jaḍena saṃbandhe na mukhyā ṇi artha saṃgatiḥ āstām anyatra vitatam etad vistarataḥ  mayā arthe prakāśanā sā iyam upacāraḥ tatas  bhavet  astu ced bhāsate tarhi sa eva patat adrivat  upacāre nimittena kena api kila bhūyate vāyuḥ pātayati iti atra nimittam tad kṛtā kriyā girau yena eṣa saṃyoga nāśāt bhraṃśam prapadyate iha tu jñānam arthasya na kiṃcitkaram eva tad  upacāraḥ katham nāma bhavet saḥ pi hi avastu san aprakāśita eva arthaḥ prakāśatva upacārataḥ tādṛś eva śiśuḥ kim hi dahati agni upacārataḥ śiśau vahni upacāre yad bījam taikṣṇya ādi tad ca sat  prakāśatva upacāre tu kim bījam yatra satyatā siddhe hi cetane yukta upacāraḥ sa hi sphuṭam adhyāra upa ātmakaḥ saḥ  pi pratisaṃdhāna jīvitaḥ na ca adya api kim api asti cetanam jñānam api adaḥ aprakāśam tad anyena tad prakāśe pyayam vidhiḥ nanu pradīpaḥ  rūpasya prakāśaḥ katham īdṛśam atra api na vahanti etāḥ kim nu yukti vikalpanāḥ yādṛśā svena rūpeṇa dīpaḥ  rūpam prakāśayet  tādṛśā svayam api eṣa bhāti jñānam tu naḥ tathā pradīpaḥ ca eṣa bhāvānām prakāśa tvam dadā[dhā]ti alam anyathā na prakāśeḥ anna bhede ca īdṛśaḥ  vidhiḥ tasmāt prakāśa eva ayam pūrva uktaḥ paramaḥ śivaḥ yathā yathā prakāśeta tad tad bhāva vapuḥ sphuṭam evam ca nīla tā nāma yathā kācid prakāśate tadvat cakāsti vedya tvam tad ca bhāva aṃśa pṛṣṭha gam phalam prakaṭatā arthasya saṃvid vā iti dvayam tatas  vipakṣataḥ  rakṣitam ca saṃdhānam ca api tad mithaḥ tathā hi nibhṛtaḥ cauraḥ caitra vedyam iti sphuṭam buddhvā na adatta eva āśu parīpsā vivaśaḥ  pi san sā iyam paśyati mām netra tri bhāgena iti sādaram svam deham amṛtena iva siktam paśyati kāmukaḥ na ca etad jñāna saṃvitti mātram bhāva aṃśa pṛṣṭha gam artha kriyā karam tad ced na dharmaḥ konu asau bhavet  yad ca uktam vedya tā dharmā bhāvaḥ sarvān api prati syāt iti etad sva pakṣa ghnam duṣprayoga astravat tava asmākam tu sva prakāśa śiva tā mātra vādinām anyam prati cakāsti iti vaca eva na vidyate sarvān prati ca tad nīlam sa ghaṭaḥ ca iti yad vacaḥ tad api avidita prāyam gṛhītam mugdha buddhibhiḥ na hi kālāgniḥ udrīyakāya avagata nīlimā tava nīlaḥ kim nu pītaḥ  mā evam bhūt na tu nīlakaḥ na kaṃcid prati nīlaḥ  sau nīlaḥ  vā yam prati sthitaḥ tam pratyeva sa vedyaḥ syāt saṃkalpa dvārakaḥ  ntatas yathā ca artha prakāśa ātma jñānam saṃgīryate tvayā tathā tad jñātṛ vedya tvam bhāvīyam rūpam ucyatām na ca jñāta atra niyataḥ kaścid jñāne yathā tava arthe jñātā yadā yaḥ  yaḥ tad vedyam vapuḥ ucyatām tad tad vijñātṛ vedya tvam sarvān pratyeva bhāsatām iti evam codayat manye vrajet badhiradhuryatām na hi anyam prati vai kaṃcid bhāti sā vedya tā tathā bhāvasya rūpam iti ukte keyamasthāna vaidhurī anena nīti mārgeṇa nirmūlam apasāritā anavasthā tathā hi anyaiḥ nīla ādyaiḥ sadṛśī na sā vedya tā kiṃtu dharmaḥ  sau yad yogāt sarva dharmavān dharmī vedya tvam abhyeti sa sattā samavāyavat  brūṣe yathā hi kurute sattā satya sataḥ sataḥ samavāyaḥ  pi saṃśliṣṭaḥ śliṣṭān aśliṣṭa tā juṣaḥ antyaḥ  viśeṣaḥ  vyāvṛtti rūpaḥ  vyāvṛtti varjitān vyāvṛttān śvetimā śuklam aśuklam gamanam tathā tadvat nīla ādi dharma aṃśa yuktaḥ  dharmī svayam sthitaḥ avedyaḥ  vedya tā rūpāt dharmāt vedya tvam āgataḥ vedya tā bhāsamānā ca svayam nīla ādi dharmavat  aprakāśā sva prakāśāt dharmāda iti prakāśatām prakāśe khalu viśrāntim viśvam śrayati ced tatas na anyā kācid apekṣā asya kṛtakṛtyasya sarvatas  yathā ca śiva nāthena svātantryāt bhāsyate bhidā nīla ādivat tathā eva ayam vedya tā dharma ucyate evam siddham hi vedya tvam bhāva dharmaḥ  stu kā ghṛṇā idam tu cintyam sakala paryanta ukta pramātṛbhiḥ vedya tvam eka rūpam syāt cāturdaśyam atas  kutas  ucyate paripūrṇam ced bhāvīyam rūpam ucyate tad vibhuḥ bhairavaḥ  devaḥ  bhagavān eva bhaṇyate atha tad nija māhātmya kalpita um śāṃśikā kramaḥ sahyate kim kṛtam tarhi prokta kalpanayā anayā ata eva yadā yena vapuṣā bhāti yad yathā tadā tathā tad tad rūpam iti eṣa upaniṣad parā caitreṇa vedyam jānāmi dvābhyām bahubhiḥ api atha mantreṇa tad maheśena śivena udrikta śaktinā anyādṛśena vā iti evam bhāvaḥ bhāti yathā tathā artha kriyā ādi vaicitryam abhyetya parisaṃkhyayā tathā hi ekāgra sakala sāmājika janaḥ khalu nṛttam gītam sudhā sāra sāgara tvena manyate tatas  eva ucyate malla naṭa prekṣā upadeśane sarva pramātṛ tādātmyam pūrṇa rūpa anubhāvakam tāvat mātra artha saṃvitti tuṣṭāḥ pratyekaśaḥ  yadi kaḥ saṃbhūya guṇaḥ teṣām pramātra aikyam bhavet ca kim yadā tu tad tad vedyatva dharma saṃdarbha garbhitam tad vastu śuṣkāt prāgrūpāt anyat yuktam idam tadā śāstre pi tad tad vedya tvam viśiṣṭa artha kriyā karam bhūyasā eva tathā ca śrī mālinīvijaya uttare tathā ṣaḍvidham adhvānam anena adhiṣṭhitam smaret  adhiṣṭhānam hi devena yad viśvasya pravedanam tad īśa vedya tvena ittham jñātam prakṛta kārya kṛt  evam siddham vedya tā ākhyaḥ  dharmaḥ  bhāvasya bhāsate tad anābhāsa yoge tu svarūpam iti bhaṇyate upādhi yogita āśaṅkām apahastayataḥ  sphuṭam sva ātmanaḥ  yena vapuṣā bhāti arthaḥ tad svakam vapuḥ jānāmi ghaṭam iti atra vedya tā anuparāgavān ghaṭa eva sva rūpeṇa bhāta iti apadiśyate nanu tatra svayaṃvedya bhāvaḥ  mantra ādi apekṣayā api ca asti eva nanu astu na tu san pratibhāsate avedyam eva kālāgni vapuḥ meroḥ parā diśaḥ mama iti saṃvidi param śuddham vastu prakāśate bhāta tvāt vedyam api tad na vedya tvena bhāsanāt  avedyam eva bhānam hi tathā kam anuyuñjmahe evam pañcadaśa ātmā iyam dharā tadvat jala ādayaḥ avyakta antā yatas  sti eṣām sakalam prati vedya tā yad tu ucyate kalā ādyena dharā antena samanvitāḥ sakalā iti tad kośa ṣaṭka udreka upalakṣaṇam udbhūta aśuddha cit rāgakala ādi rasa kañcukāḥ sakala ālaya saṃjñāḥ tu nyagbhūta akhila kañcukāḥ jñānākalāḥ tu dhvasta etad kañcukā iti nirṇayaḥ tena pradhāne vedye pi pumān udbhūta kañcukaḥ pramātā asti eva sakalaḥ pāñcadaśyam atas  sthitam pāñcadaśyam dharādhantar niviṣṭe sakale pi ca sakala antaram asti eva prameye trāpi mātṛ hi sthūla āvṛta ādi saṃkoca tad anya vyāptṛ tā juṣaḥ pīta ādyāḥ sthira kampra tvāt caturdaśa dharā ādiṣu svarūpībhūta jaḍa tāḥ prāṇa deha pathe tatas  pramātṛ tā juṣaḥ proktā dhāraṇā vijaya uttare yadā tu meya tā puṃsaḥ kalā antasya prakalpyate tad udbhūtaḥ kañcuka aṃśaḥ meyaḥ  na asya pramātṛ tā atas  sakala saṃjñasya pramātṛ tvam na vidyate trayodaśa tvam tad śakti śaktimat dvaya varjanāt  nyagbhūta kañcukaḥ  mātā yukta [yata]ḥ tatra layākalaḥ māyā niviṣṭaḥ  vijñānākalā ādyāḥ prāgvat eva tu māyā tattve jñeya rūpe kañcuka nyagbhavaḥ  pi yaḥ saḥ  pi meyaḥ kañcuka aikyam yatas  māyā susūkṣmikā vijñānākala eva atra tatas  mātā apakañcukaḥ māyā niviṣṭe pyakale tathā iti ekādaśa ātma tā vijñāna kevale vedye kañcuka dhvaṃsa su sthite udbubhūṣu prabodhānām mantrāṇām eva mātṛ tā te pi mantrā yadā meyāḥ tadā mātā tad īśvaraḥ sa hi udbhavāt pūrṇa bodhaḥ tasmin prāpte tu meya tām udbhūta pūrṇa rūpaḥ  sau mātā mantra maheśvaraḥ tasmin vijñeya tām prāpte sva prakāśaḥ paraḥ śivaḥ pramātā svaka tādātmya bhāsita akhila vedyakaḥ śivaḥ pramātā naḥ meyaḥ  hi anya adhīna prakāśa tā meya tā sā na tatra asti sva prakāśaḥ  hi asau prabhuḥ sva prakāśe tra kasmiṃścid anabhyupagate sati aprakāśāt prakāśa tve hi anavasthā duruttarā tatas ca suptam viśvam syāt na ca evam bhāsate hi tad  anya adhīna prakāśam hi tad bhāti anyaḥ tu asau śivaḥ iti asya sva prakāśa tve kim anyaiḥ yukti ḍambaraiḥ mānānām hi paraḥ  jīvaḥ sa eva iti uktam āditas  nanu asti sva prakāśe pi śive vedya tvam īdṛśaḥ upadeśa u[śyaḥ ]padeṣṭṛtva vyavahāraḥ  nyathā katham satyam sa tu tathā sṛṣṭaḥ parameśena vedya tām nītaḥ  mantra maheśa ādi kakṣyām samadhiśāyyate tathābhūtaḥ ca vedyaḥ  sau na anavacchinna saṃvidaḥ pūrṇasya vedya tā yuktā paraspara virodhataḥ tathā vedya svabhāve pi vastu tas  na śiva ātma tām kaḥ  pi bhāvaḥ projjhati iti satyam tad bhāvanā phalet  śrī pūrvaśāstre tena uktam śivaḥ sākṣāt na bhidyate sākṣāt padena ayam arthaḥ samastaḥ prasphuṭīkṛtaḥ nanu eka rūpa tā yuktaḥ śivaḥ tad vaśataḥ bhavet  tri vedatāmantra mahā nāthe kātra vivāditā maheśvara īśa mantrāṇām tathā kevalinoḥ dvayoḥ ananta bhedatā ekaikam sthitā sakalavat kila tatas  layākale meye pramātā asti layākalaḥ atas trayodaśa tvam syāt ittham na ekādaśa ātma tā vijñānākala vedya tve pyanyaḥ  jñānākalaḥ bhavet  mātā tad ekādaśatā syāt na eva tu nava ātma tā evam mantra tad īśānām mantreśa antara saṃbhave vedya tvāt nava sapta syuḥ sapta pañca tu te katham ucyate satyam asti eṣā kalanā kiṃtu su sphuṭaḥ yathā atra sakale bhedaḥ  na tathā tu akalā ādike anantau  āntaredṛkṣa yoni bhedavataḥ sphuṭam caturdaśavidhasya asya sakalasya asti bheditā layākale tu saṃskāra mātrāt sati api asau bhidā akalena viśeṣāya sakalasya eva yujyate vijñāna kevala ādīnām tāvatī api na vai bhidā śiva svācchandya mātram tu bhedāya eṣām vijṛmbhate iti āśayena saṃpaśyan viśeṣam sakalāt iha layākalā ādau na uvāca trāyodaśi ādikam vibhuḥ nanu astu vedya tā bhāva dharmaḥ kiṃtu layākalau manvāte na iha vai kiṃcid tad apekṣā tu asau katham śrūyatām saṃvid aikātmya tattve smin saṃvyavasthite jaḍe pi citiḥ asti eva bhotsyamāne tu kā kathā sva bodha avasare tāvat bhotsyate layakevalī dvividhaḥ ca prabodhaḥ  sya mantra tvāya bhavāya ca bhāvanā ādi balāt anya vaiṣṇava ādinayā uditāt  yathā svam ādhara auttarya vicitrāt saṃskṛtaḥ tathā līnaḥ prabuddhaḥ  mantra tvam tad īśa tvam atha eti vā svātantrya varjitā ye tu balāt moha vaśīkṛtāḥ laya ākalāt sva saṃskārāt prabuddhi ante bhavāya te jñānākalaḥ pi mantreśa maheśa tvāya budhyate mantra ādi tvāya vā jātu jātu saṃsṛtaye pi vā avatāraḥ  hi vijñā niyogi bhāve sya bhidyate uktam ca bodhayāmāsa sa sisṛkṣuḥ jagatprabhuḥ vijñāna kevala anaṣṭau  iti śrī pūrvaśāsane atas  prabhotsyamāna tve yānayoḥ bodha yogya tā tad balāt vedya tā yogya bhāvena eva atra vedya tā tathā hi gāḍha nidre pi priye na āśaṅkita āgatām mām drakṣyati iti na aṅgeṣu sveṣu mātyabhisārikā evam śivaḥ  pi manute etasya etad pravedya tām yāsyati iti sṛjāmi iti tadānīm yogya tā eva sā vedya tā tasya bhāvasya bhoktṛtā tāvatī ca sā layākalasya citraḥ  hi bhogaḥ kena vikalpyate yathā yathā hi samvittiḥ sa hi bhogaḥ sphuṭaḥ  sphuṭaḥ smṛti yogyaḥ  pyanyathā vā bhogya bhāvam na tu ujjhati gāḍha nidrā vimūḍhaḥ  pi kāntā liṅgita vigrahaḥ bhoktā eva bhaṇyate saḥ  pi manute bhoktṛtām purā utprekṣā mātra hīnaḥ  pi kāṃcid kula vadhūm puras  saṃbhokṣyamāṇām dṛṣṭvā eva rabhasāt yāti saṃmadam tām eva dṛṣṭvā ca tadā samāna āśaya bhāj api anyaḥ tathā na saṃvitte kam atra upalabhāmahe loke rūḍham idam dṛṣṭiḥ asmin kāraṇam antarā prasīdati iva magnā iva nirvātī va iti vādini ittham vistarataḥ tattva bhedaḥ  yam samudāhṛtaḥ śakti śaktimatām bhedāt anyonyam tad kṛteṣu api bhedeṣu anyonyataḥ  bhedāt tathā tattva antaraiḥ saha bheda upabheda gaṇanām karvataḥ  na avadhiḥ kvacid  tatas  eva vicitraḥ  yam bhuvana ādi vidhiḥ sthitaḥ pārthiva tve pi naḥ sāmyam rudra vaiṣṇava lokayoḥ kā kathā anyatra tu bhavet bhoge vā api svarūpake sa ca naḥ vistaraḥ sākṣāt śakyaḥ  yadi api bhāṣitum tathā api mārga mātreṇa kathyamānaḥ  vivicyatām saptānām mātṛ śaktīnām anyonyam bhedane sati rūpam eka anna pañcāśat svarūpam ca adhikam tatas  sarvam sarva ātmakam yasmāt tasmāt sakala mātari layākalā ādi śaktīnām saṃbhavaḥ  sti eva tattvataḥ sa tu asphuṭaḥ  stu bheda aṃśam dātum tāvat prabhuḥ bhavet  teṣām api ca bhedānām anyonyam bahu bheda tā mukhyānām bheda bhedānām jala ādyaiḥ bhedane sati mukhya bheda prakāreṇa vidheḥ ānantyam ucyate sakalasya samudbhūtāḥ cakṣuḥ ādi sva śaktayaḥ nyagbhūtāḥ ca pratanvanti bheda antaram api sphuṭam evam layākalā ādīnām tad saṃskāra pada uditāt  pāṭavāt prakṣayāt vā api bheda antaram udīyate nyakkṛtām śaktim āsthāya api udāsīna tayā sthitim anāviśya iva yad vetti tatra anyā vedya tā khalu āviśi iva nimajjyā iva vikāsya iva vighūrṇya ca vidataḥ  vedya tā anyā eva bhedaḥ  tra artha kriyā ucitaḥ anya śakti tirobhāve kasyāścid su sphuṭa udaye bheda antaram api jñeyam vīṇā vādaka dṛṣṭivat  tirobhāva udbhavau śakteḥ sva śakti antarataḥ  nyatas  ca ityamānāt cetyāt vā tanvāte bahu bheda tām evam etad dharā ādīnām tattvānām yāvatī daśā kācid asti ghaṭa ākhyā api tatra saṃdarśitā bhidaḥ atra api vedya tā nāma tādātmyam vedakaiḥ saha tatas  sakala vedyaḥ  sau ghaṭaḥ sakala eva hi yāvat śiva eka vedyaḥ  sau śiva eva avabhāsate tāvat eka śarīraḥ  hi bodhaḥ  bhāti eva yāvatā adhunā atra samastasya dharā tattvasya darśyate sāmastya eva abhihitam pāñcadaśyam purā uditam dharā tattva avibhedena yaḥ prakāśaḥ prakāśate sa eva śivanāthaḥ  tra pṛthivī brahma tad matam dharā tattva gatāḥ siddhīḥ vitarītum samudyatān prerayanti śivecchātaḥ  ye te mantra maheśvarāḥ preryamāṇāḥ tu mantreśā mantrāḥ tad vācakāḥ sphuṭam dharā tattva gatam yogam abhyasya śiva vidyayā na tu pāśava sāṃkhyīya vaiṣṇava ādi dvitā dṛśā aprāpta dhruva dhāmānaḥ  vijñānākalatā juṣaḥ tāvat tattva upabhogena ye kalpa ante layam gatāḥ sauṣupta avasthayā upetāḥ te tra pralaya kevalāḥ sauṣupte tattva līna tvam sphuṭam eva hi lakṣyate anyathā niyata svapna saṃdṛṣṭiḥ jāyate kutas  sauṣuptam api citram ca svacchāsu accha ādi bhāsate asvāpsam sukham ityādi smṛti vaicitrya darśanāt yadā eva sa kṣaṇam sūkṣmam nidrāya eva prabuddhyate tadā eva smṛtiḥ eṣā iti na artha ja jñāna jā smṛtiḥ tena mūḍhaiḥ yad ucyeta prabuddhasya antarā antarā tūlikā ādi sukha sparśasmṛtiḥ eṣā iti tad kutas  māhā karma samullāsa saṃmiśrita m alābilāḥ dharā adhirohiṇaḥ  jñeyāḥ sakalā iha pudgalāḥ asya eva saptakasya sva sva vyāpāra prakalpane prakṣobhaḥ  yaḥ tad eva uktam śaktīnām saptakam sphuṭam śivaḥ  hi acyuta cit rūpaḥ tisraḥ tad śaktayaḥ tu yāḥ tāḥ svātantrya vaśa upātta grahītra ākāra tā vaśāt tridhā mantra avasānāḥ syuḥ udāsīnā iva sthitāḥ grāhya ākāra uparāgāt tu grahītra ākāra tā vaśāt sakala antāḥ tu tāḥ tisra icchā jñāna kriyā matāḥ saptadhā ittham pramātṛ tvam tad kṣobhaḥ  mānatā tathā yad tu grahītṛtā rūpa saṃvid saṃsparśa varjitam śuddham jaḍam tad svarūpam ittham viśvam trika ātmakam evam jala ādi api vadet bhedaiḥ bhinnam mahāmatiḥ anayā tu diśā prāyas  sarva bhedeṣu vidyate bhedaḥ  mantra maheśānteṣu eṣa pañcadaśa ātmakaḥ tathā api sphuṭa tā bhāvāt san  api eṣa na carcitaḥ etad ca sūtritam dhātrā śrī pūrve yad bravi iti hi sa vyāpāra adhipa tvena ityādinā jāgrat āditām abhinne pi śive ntaḥstha sūkṣma bodha anusārataḥ adhunā prāṇa śakti sthe tattva jāle vivicyate bhedaḥ  yam pāñcadaśī ādiḥ yathā śrī śaṃbhuḥ ādiśat  samaste rthe tra nirgrāhye tuṭayaḥ ṣoḍaśa kṣaṇāḥ ṣaṭtriṃśat aṅgule cāre sa aṃśa dvi aṅgula kalpitāḥ tatra ādyaḥ parama advaitaḥ  nirvibhāga rasa ātmakaḥ dvitīyaḥ  grāhaka ullāsa rūpaḥ prativibhāvyate antyaḥ tu grāhya tādātmyāt svarūpībhāvam āgataḥ pravibhāvyaḥ  na hi pṛthak upāntyaḥ  grāhakaḥ kṣaṇaḥ tṛtīyam kṣaṇam ārabhya kṣaṇa ṣaṭkam tu yad sthitam tad nirvikalpam prodgacchat vikalpa ācchādana ātmakam tad eva śiva rūpam hi para śakti ātmakam viduḥ dvitīyam madhyamam ṣaṭkam parāpara pada ātmakam vikalpa rūḍhiḥ api eṣā kramāt prasphuṭa tām gatā ṣaṭke tra prathame devyaḥ tisraḥ pronmeṣa vṛtti tām nimeṣa vṛtti tām ca āśu spṛśantyaḥ ṣaṭka tām gatāḥ evam dvitīya ṣaṭke pi kim tu atra grāhya vartmanā uparāga padam prāpya parāpara tayā sthitāḥ ādye tra ṣaṭke tā devyaḥ svātantrya ullāsa mātrataḥ jighṛkṣite pyupādhau syuḥ para rūpāt avicyutāḥ asti ca atiśayaḥ kaścid tāsām api uttarottaram yaḥ  viveka dhanaiḥ dhīraiḥ sphuṭīkṛtya api darśyate kecid tu ekām tuṭim grāhye ca ekām api grahītari tādātmyena vinikṣipya saptakam saptakam viduḥ tad asyām sūkṣma saṃvittau kalanāya samudyatāḥ saṃvedayante yad rūpam tatra kim vāc vikatthanaiḥ evam dharā ādi mūla antam prakriyā prāṇa gāminī guru parva kramāt proktā bhede pañcadaśa ātmake kramāt tu bheda nyūna tve nyūna tā syāt tuṭiṣu api tasyām hrāsaḥ  vikalpasya sphuṭa tā ca avikalpinaḥ yathā hi cira duḥkha ārtaḥ paścāt ātta sukha sthitiḥ vismarati eva tad duḥkham sukha viśrānti vartmanā tathā gata vikalpe pi rūḍhāḥ saṃvedane janāḥ vikalpa viśrānti balāt tām sattām na abhimanvate vikalpa nirhrāsa vaśena yāti vikalpa vandhyā parama artha satyā saṃvid svarūpa prakaṭa tvam ittham tatra avadhāne yatatām su buddhiḥ grāhya grāhaka saṃvittau saṃbandhe sāvadhāna tā iyam sā tatra tatra uktā sarva kāmadughā yatas  evam dvayam dvayam yāvat nyūnībhavati bheda gam tāvat tuṭi dvayam yāti nyūna tām kramaśas  sphuṭam ata eva śiva āveśe dvi tuṭiḥ parigīyate ekā tu sā tuṭiḥ tatra pūrṇā śuddhā eva kevalam dvitīyā śiva  śakti  rūpā eva sarva jñāna kriyā ātmikā tasyām avahitaḥ  yogī kim na vetti karoti vā tathā ca uktam kallaṭena śrīmatā tuṭi pāta gaḥ lābhaḥ sarvajña kartṛ tve tuṭeḥ pātaḥ  parā tuṭiḥ ādyāyām tu tuṭau sarvam sarvatas  pūrṇam eka tām gatam kim tatra vedyam vā kāryam vā vyapadeśa bhāj  atas  bheda samullāsa kalām prāthamikīm budhāḥ cinvanti pratibhām devīm sarvajñatva ādi siddhaye sā eva śaktiḥ śivasya uktā tṛtīya ādi tuṭiṣu atha mantra ādi  dhi nātha tad śakti mantra īśa ādyāḥ krama uditāḥ tāsu saṃdadhataḥ cittam avadhāna eka dharmakam tad tad siddhi samāveśaḥ svayam eva upajāyate ata eva yathā bheda bahu tvam dūra tā tathā saṃvittau tuṭi bāhulyādakṣa artha asaṃnikarṣavat  yathā yathā hi nyūna tvam tuṭīnām hrāsataḥ  bhidaḥ tathā tathā ati naikaṭyam saṃvidaḥ syāt śiva avadhi śiva tattvam atas  proktam antikam sarvatas  mutar  ata eva prayatnaḥ  yam tad praveśe na vidyate yathā yathā hi dūra tvam yatna yogaḥ tathā tathā bhāvanā karaṇa ādīnām śive niravakāśa tām ata eva hi manyante saṃpradāya dhanā janāḥ tathā hi dṛśyatām lokaḥ  ghaṭa ādeḥ vedane yathā prayatnavān iva ābhāti tathā kim sukha vedane āntara tvam idam prāhuḥ saṃvid naikaṭya śālitām tām ca cit rūpa tā unmeṣam bāhya tvam tad nimeṣa tām bhavinām tu antikaḥ  pi evam na bhāti iti ati dūra tā dūre pi hi antikībhūte bhānam syāt tu atra tad katham na ca bīja aṅkura latā dala puṣpa phala ādivat  kramikā iyam bhavet saṃvid sūtaḥ tatra kila aṅkuraḥ bījāt latā tu aṅkurān na u bījāt iha sarvatas  saṃvid tattvam bhāsamānam paripūrṇam hi sarvatas  sarvasya kāraṇam proktam sarvatra eva uditam yatas  tatas  eva ghaṭe pyeṣā prāṇa vṛttiḥ yadi sphuret  viśrāmyet ca āśu tatra eva śivabīje layam vrajet  na tu kramikatā kācid śiva ātma tve kadācana anyat mantra ādi  dhi nātha ādi kāraṇam tad tu saṃnidheḥ śiva abhedāt ca kim ca atha dvaite naikaṭya vedanāt  anayā ca diśā sarva sarvadā pravivecayan bhairavāyata eva drāk  cit cakra īśvara tām gataḥ sa ittham prāṇa gaḥ bhedaḥ khecarī cakra gopitaḥ mayā prakaṭitaḥ śrīmat śāmbhava ājñā anuvartinā atra eva adhvani vedya tvam prāpte yā saṃvid udbhavet  tasyāḥ svakam yad vaicitryam tad avasthā padā abhidham jāgrat svapnaḥ suṣuptam ca turyam ca tad atītakam iti pañca padāni āhuḥ ekasmin vedake sati tatra yā eṣā dharā tattvāt śiva antā tattva paddhatiḥ tasyām ekaḥ pramātā ced avaśyam jāgrat ādikam tad darśyate śaṃbhu nātha prasādāt viditam mayā yad adhiṣṭheyam eva iha na adhiṣṭhātṛ kadācana saṃvedana gatam vedyam tad jāgrat samudāhṛtam caitra maitra ādi bhūtāni tattvāni ca dharā āditaḥ abhidhākaraṇībhūtāḥ śabdāḥ kim ca abhidhā pramā pramātṛ meya tad māna pramā rūpam catuṣṭayam viśvam etad adhiṣṭheyam yadā jāgrat tadā smṛtam tathā hi bhāsate yad tad nīlam antar  pravedane saṃkalpa rūpe bāhyasya tad adhiṣṭhātṛ bodhakam yad tu bāhya tayā nīlam cakāsti asya na vidyate kathaṃcid api adhiṣṭhātṛ bhāvaḥ tad jāgrat ucyate tatra caitre bhāsamāne yaḥ  deha aṃśaḥ sa kathyate abuddhaḥ  yaḥ tu māna aṃśaḥ sa buddhaḥ  miti kārakaḥ prabuddhaḥ suprabuddhaḥ ca pramā mātrā iti ca kramaḥ cāturvidhyam hi piṇḍa stha nāmni jāgrati kīrtitam jāgrat ādi catuṣkam hi pratyekam iha vidyate jāgrat jāgrat abuddham tad jāgrat svapnaḥ tu buddha tā ityādi turyātītam tu sarvaga tvāt pṛthak kutas  uktam ca piṇḍa gam jāgrat abuddham buddham eva ca prabuddham suprabuddham ca caturvidham idam smṛtam meya bhūmiḥ iyam mukhyā jāgrat ākhyā an yad antarā bhūta tattva abhidhānānām yom śaḥ dhiṣṭheya ucyate piṇḍa stham iti tam prāhuḥ iti śrī mālinīmate laukikī jāgrat iti eṣā saṃjñā piṇḍa stham iti api yoginām yoga siddhi artham saṃjñā iyam paribhāṣyate adhiṣṭheya samāpattim adhyāsīnasya yoginaḥ tādātmyam kila piṇḍa stham mitam piṇḍam hi piṇḍitam prasaṃkhyāna eka rūḍhānām jñāninām tu tad ucyate sarvatobhadram āpūrṇam sarvatas  vedya sattayā sarva sattā samāpūrṇa viśvam paśyet yatas  yatas  jñānī tatas tatas  saṃvitta tvam asya prakāśate lokayoga prasaṃkhyāna traiḥ ūpya vaśataḥ kila nāmāni trīṇi bhaṇyante svapna ādiṣu api ayam vidhiḥ yad tu adhiṣṭhāna karaṇa bhāvam adhyāsya vartate vedyam sat pūrva kathitam bhūta tattva abhidha āmayam tad svapnaḥ  mukhyataḥ jñeyam tad ca vaikalpike pathi vaikalpika patha ārūḍha vedya sāmya avabhāsanāt  loka rūḍhaḥ  pyasau svapnaḥ sāmyam ca abāhya rūpa tā utprekṣā svapna saṃkalpa smṛti unmāda ādi dṛṣṭiṣu vispaṣṭam yad vedya jātam jāgrat mukhya tayā eva tad  yad tu tatra api avispaṣṭam spaṣṭa adhiṣṭhātṛ bhāsate vikalpa antara gam vedyam tad svapna padam ucyate tadā eva tasya vetti eva svayam eva hi abāhyatām pramātṛ antara sādhāra bhāva hānyasthira ātmate tatra api cāturvidhyam tad  prāc diśā eva prakalpayet  gatāgatam su vikṣiptam saṃgatam su samāhitam atra api pūrvavat nāma laukikam svapna iti adaḥ bāhya abhimata bhāvānām svāpaḥ  hi agrahaṇam matam sarva adhvanaḥ padam prāṇaḥ saṃkalpaḥ  vagam ātmakaḥ padam ca tad samāpatti pada stham yoginaḥ  viduḥ vedya sattām bahis bhūtām anapekṣya eva sarvatas  vedye svātantrya bhāj  jñānam svapnam vyāpti tayā bhajet  māna bhūmiḥ iyam mukhyā svapnaḥ  hi āmarśana ātmakaḥ vedya  chāyaḥ  vabhāsaḥ  hi meye dhiṣṭhānam ucyate yad tu adhiṣṭhātṛ bhūta ādeḥ pūrva uktasya vapuḥ dhruvam bījam viśvasya tad tūṣṇīṃbhūtam sauṣuptam ucyate anubhūtau vikalpe ca yaḥ  sau draṣṭā sa eva hi na bhāva grahaṇam tena suṣṭhu supta tvam ucyate tad sāmyāt laukikīm nidrām suṣuptam manvate budhāḥ bīja bhāvaḥ  thāgrahaṇam sāmyam tūṣṇīṃsvabhāva tā mukhyā mātṛ daśā sā iyam suṣupta ākhyā nigadyate rūpaka tvāt ca rūpam tad tādātmyam yoginaḥ punar  rūpa stham tad samāpatti audāsīnyam rūpiṇām viduḥ prasaṃkhyānavataḥ kā api vedya saṃkocana atra yad  na asti tena mahāvyāptiḥ iyam tad anusārataḥ udāsīnasya tasya api vedyam yena caturvidham bhūta ādi tad upādhi uttham atra bheda catuṣṭayam uditam vipulam śāntam su prasannam atha aparam yad tu pramā ātmakam rūpam pramātuḥ upari sthitam pūrṇa tā āgamana aunmukhyam audāsīnyāt paricyutiḥ tad turyam ucyate śakti samāveśaḥ  hi asau mataḥ sā saṃvid svaprakāśā tu kaiścid uktā prameyataḥ mānān mātuḥ ca bhinna eva tad artham tritayam yatas  meyam māne mātari tad  saḥ  pi tasyām mitau sphuṭam viśrāmyati iti sā eva eṣā devī viśva eka jīvitam rūpam dṛśā aham iti aṃśa trayam uttīrya vartate dvāra mātra āśrita upāyā paśyāmi iti anupāyikā pramātṛ tā svatantratva rūpā sā iyam prakāśate saṃvid turīya rūpā evam prakāśa ātmā svayam ca sā tad samāveśa tādātmye mātṛ tvam bhavati sphuṭam tad samāveśa uparāgāt māna tvam meya tā punar  tad samāveśa naikaṭyāt trayam tad tad anugrahāt vedya ādi bheda galanāt uktā sā iyam anāmayā mātṛ ā ādi anugraha ādā  dhā nāt sa vyāpāra iti bhaṇyate jāgrat ādi api devasya śakti tvena vyavasthitam aparam para aparam ca dvidhā tad sā parā tu iyam rūpaka tvāt udāsīnāt cyutā iyam pūrṇa tā unmukhī daśā tasyām samāpattī rūpātītam tu yoginaḥ pūrṇa tā aunmukhya yogi tvāt viśvam paśyati tad mayaḥ prasaṃkhyātā pracayataḥ tena iyam pracayaḥ matā na etasyām aparā turyadaśā saṃbhāvyate kila saṃvid na kila vedyā sā vittvena eva hi bhāsate jāgrat ādyāḥ tu saṃbhāvyāḥ tisraḥ  syāḥ prāc daśā yatas  tritaya anugrahāt sā iyam tena uktā trikaśāsane manonmanam anantam ca sarva artham iti bhedataḥ yad tu pūrṇa anavacchinna vapuḥ ānanda nirbharam turyātītam tu tad prāhuḥ tad eva paramam padam na atra yogasya sadbhāvaḥ  bhāvanā ādeḥ abhāvataḥ aprameye paricchinne svatantre bhāvyatā kutas  yoga ādi abhāvataḥ tena nāma asmin  ādiśat vibhuḥ prasaṃkhyāna balāt tu etad rūpam pūrṇatva yogataḥ anuttarāt iha proktam mahāpracaya saṃjñitam pūrṇa tvāt eva bhedānām asyām saṃbhāvanā na hi tad nirāsāya na etasyām bheda uktaḥ  viśeṣaṇam satata uditam iti etad sarva vyāpitva sūcakam na hi eka eva bhavati bhedaḥ kvacana kaścana turyātīte bheda ekaḥ satata udita iti ayam mūḍha vādaḥ tena siddham avibhedi tvam asya tu śrī pūrvaśāstre tena uktam pada stham aparam viduḥ mantrāḥ tad patayaḥ sa īśā rūpa stham iti kīrtyate rūpātītam parā śaktiḥ savyāpārā api anāmayā niṣprapañcaḥ  nirābhāsaḥ śuddhaḥ sva ātmani avasthitaḥ sarva atītaḥ śivaḥ  jñeyaḥ  yam viditvā vimucyate iti śrī sumati prajñā candrikā śānta tāmasaḥ śrī śaṃbhu nāthaḥ sadbhāvam jāgrat ādau nyarūpayat  anye tu kathayanti eṣām bhaṅgīm anyādṛśīm śritāḥ yad rūpam jāgrat ādīnām tad idānīm nirūpyate tatra akṣa vṛttim āśritya bāhya ākāra grahaḥ  hi yaḥ tad jāgrat sphuṭam āsīnam anubandhi punar  punar  ātma saṃkalpa nirmāṇam svapnaḥ  jāgrat viparyayaḥ layākalasya bhogaḥ  sau mala karma vaśāt na tu sthirībhavet niśā abhāvāt suptam saukhya ādya vedane jñānākalasya malataḥ kevalāt bhoga mātrataḥ bhedavantaḥ svatas  bhinnāḥ cikīrṣyante jaḍa ajaḍāḥ turye tatra sthitā mantra tad nātha adhīśvarāḥ trayaḥ yāvat bhairava bodha antar praveśana sahiṣṇavaḥ bhāvā vigalat ātmīya sārāḥ svayam abhedinaḥ turya atīta pade saṃsyuḥ iti pañcadaśa ātmake yasya yad yad sphuṭam rūpam tad jāgrat iti manyatām yad eva asthirama ābhāti sa pūrvam svapna īdṛśaḥ asphuṭam tu yadābhāti suptam tad tad puraḥ pi yad  trayasya asya anusaṃdhiḥ tu yad vaśāt upajāyate sraj sūtra kalpam tad turyam sarva bhedeṣu gṛhyatām yadtva dvaita bhara ullāsa drāvita aśeṣa bhedakam turyātītam tu tad prāhuḥ ittham sarvatra yojayet  layākale tu svam rūpam jāgrat tad pūrva vṛtti tu svapna ādi iti kramam sarvam sarvatra anusaret budhaḥ ekatra api prabhau pūrṇe cittuḥ yā atītam ucyate ānandaḥ turyam icchā eva bīja bhūmiḥ suṣupta tā jñānaśaktiḥ svapna uktaḥ kriyāśaktiḥ tu jāgṛtiḥ na ca evam upacāraḥ syāt sarvam tatra eva vastutas  na ced na kvāpi mukhya tvam na upacāraḥ  pi tad kvacid  etad śrī pūrva śāstre ca sphuṭa m uktam maheśinā tatra svarūpam śaktiḥ ca sakalaḥ ca iti tad trayam iti jāgrat avastheyam bhede pañcadaśa ātmake akalau svapna sauṣupte turyam mantra ādi varga bhāj  turyātītam śakti śaṃbhū trayodaśa abhidhe punar  svarūpam jāgrat anyat tu prāgvat pralaya kevale svam jāgrat svapna supte dve turyāt yatra ca pūrvavat  vijñānākala bhede pi svam mantrā mantra nāyakāḥ tad īśāḥ śakti śaṃbhvittham pañca syuḥ jāgrat ādayaḥ saptabhede tu mantra ākhye svam mantreśā maheśvarāḥ śaktiḥ śaṃbhuḥ ca pañca uktā avasthā jāgrat ādayaḥ svarūpam mantramāheśī śaktiḥ mantra maheśvaraḥ śaktiḥ śaṃbhuḥ imāḥ pañca mantreśe pañcabhedake svam kriyā jñānam icchā ca śaṃbhuḥ atra ca pañcamī maheśa bhede trividhe jāgrat ādi nirūpitam vyāpārāt ādhipatyāt ca tad dhānyā preraka tvataḥ icchā nivṛtteḥ svastha tvāt śiva ekaḥ  pi pañcadhā iti eṣa darśitaḥ  smābhiḥ tattva adhvā vistarāt atha  ch atha śrī tantrāloke ekādaśam āhnikam kalā adhvā vakṣyate śrīmat chāṃbhava ājñā anusārataḥ b yathā pūrva ukta bhuvana madhye nija nijam gaṇam anuyat paratas  bhinnam tattvam nāma iti bhaṇyate tathā teṣu api tattveṣu sva varge nugama ātmakam vyāvṛttam para vargāt ca kalā iti śiva śāsane kecid āhuḥ punar yāsau śaktiḥ antar  susūkṣmikā tattvānām sā kalā iti uktā dharaṇyām dhārikā yathā atra pakṣa dvaye vastu na bhinnam bhāsate yatas  anugāmi na sāmānyam iṣṭam naiyāyika ādivat  anye vadanti dīkṣā ādau sukha saṃgrahaṇa arthataḥ śivena kalpitaḥ  vargaḥ kalā iti samaya āśrayaḥ kṛtaḥ ca devadevena samayaḥ  parama artha tām na gacchati iti na asatyaḥ  na ca anya samaya udayaḥ nivṛttiḥ pṛthivī tattve pratiṣṭhā vyakta gocare vidyā niśā ante śāntā ca śakti ante ṇḍam idam catuḥ śānta atītā śive tattve kalā atītaḥ paraḥ śivaḥ na hi atra vargīkaraṇam samayaḥ kalanā api vā yujyate sarvatodikkam svātantrya ullāsa dhāmani svātantryāt tu nijam rūpam boddhṛ dharmāt avicyutam upadeśa tad āveśa parama arthatva siddhaye bodhyatām ānayan devaḥ sphuṭam eva vibhāvyate yatas  taḥ śiva tattve pi kalā saṃgatiḥ ucyate aṇḍam ca nāma bhuvana vibhāga sthiti kāraṇam prāhuḥ āvaraṇam tad ca śakti antam yāvat asti hi yadi api prāk  śiva ākhye pi tattve bhuvana paddhatiḥ uktā tathā api apratighe na asmin  āvṛti saṃbhavaḥ nanu evam dharaṇīm muktvā śaktau prakṛti māyayoḥ api ca apratigha tve pi katham aṇḍasya saṃbhavaḥ atra asmad
