guravaḥ prāhuḥ yad pṛthivī ādi pañcakam pratyakṣam idam ābhāti tatas  nyat na asti kiṃcana meya tve sthūla sūkṣma tvāt māna tve karaṇa tvataḥ kartṛ tā ullāsataḥ kartṛ bhāve sphuṭa tayā uditam triṃśat tattvam vibheda ātma tad abhedaḥ  niśā matā kāryatva karaṇatva ādi vibhāga galane sati vikāsa utka svatantra tve śiva antam pañcakam jaguḥ śrīmat kāla uttara ādau ca kathitam bhūyasā tathā pañca etāni tu tattvāni yaiḥ vyāptam akhilam jagat  pañca mantra tanau tena sadyojāta ādi bhaṇyate īśāna antam tatra tatra dharā ādi gagana antakam śiva tattvam atas  śūnya ati śūnyam syāt ana aśri[vṛ]tam yad tu sarva avibhāga ātma svatantram bodha sundaram saptatriṃśam tu tad prāhuḥ tattvam para śiva abhidham tasya api ukta nayāt vedya bhāve tra parikalpite yad ā āste hi anavacchinnam tad aṣṭātriṃśam ucyate na ca anavasthā hi evam syāt dṛśyatām hi mahātmabhiḥ yad vedyam kiṃcid ābhāti tad kṣaye yad prakāśate tad tattvam iti nirṇītam ṣaṭtriṃśam hṛdi bhāsate tad kim na kiṃcid vā kiṃcid iti ākāṅkṣā vaśe vapuḥ cit ānanda svatantra eka rūpam tad iti deśane saptatriṃśam samābhāti tatra ākāṅkṣā ca na aparā tad ca api klṛpta vedya tvam yatra bhāti sa cit mayaḥ aṣṭātriṃśattamaḥ saḥ  pi bhāvanāya upadiśyate yadi nāma tatas  saptatriṃśa eva punar bhavet avibhāga svatantratva cit mayatva ādi dharma tā samā eva vedyīkaraṇam kevalam tu adhikam yatas  dharāyām guṇa tattva ante māyā ante kramaśas  sthitāḥ gandhaḥ  rasaḥ  rūpam antar  sūkṣma bhāva krameṇa tu iti sthite naye śakti tattva ante pyasti saukṣmya bhāj  sparśaḥ kaḥ  pi sadā yasmai yoginaḥ spṛhayālavaḥ tad sparśa ante tu saṃvittiḥ śuddha cit vyoma rūpiṇī yasyām rūḍhaḥ samabhyeti sva prakāśa ātmikām parām atas  vinduḥ atas  nādaḥ  rūpam asmāt atas  rasaḥ iti uktam kṣobhaka tvena spande sparśaḥ tu naḥ tathā matam ca etad maheśasya śrī pūrve yad abhāṣata dhārikā āpyāyinī boddhrī pavitrī ca avakāśa dā ebhiḥ śabdaiḥ vyavaharan nivṛtti ādeḥ nijam vapuḥ pañcatattva vidhiḥ proktaḥ tri tattvam adhunā ucyate vijñānākala paryantam ātmā vidyeśvara antakam śeṣe śivaḥ tri tattve syāt eka tattve śivaḥ param imau bhedau  ubhau tattva bheda mātra kṛtau  iti tadtva adhvā eva ayam ittham ca na ṣaḍadhva sthiteḥ kṣatiḥ prakṛt  pumān yatiḥ kālaḥ  māyā vidyeśa sauśivau śivaḥ ca nava tattve pi vidhau tattva adhva rūpa tā evam aṣṭādaśa ākhye pi vidhau nyāyam vadet sudhīḥ yatra yatra hi bhoga icchā tad prādhānya upayogataḥ anya antar bhāvanātaḥ ca dīkṣā ananta vibheda bhāj  tena ṣaṭtriṃśataḥ  yāvat eka tattva vidhiḥ bhavet tattva adhvā eva sa devena proktaḥ  vyāsa samāsataḥ eka tattva vidhiḥ ca eṣa suprabuddham gurum prati śiṣyam ca gata bhoga āśa muditaḥ śaṃbhunā yatas  bhedam visphārya visphārya śaktyā svacchanda rūpayā sva ātmani abhinne bhagavān nityam viśramayan sthitaḥ ittham tri ātma adhvanaḥ  bhedaḥ sthūla sūkṣma para tvataḥ meya bhāga gataḥ proktaḥ pura tattva kalā ātmakaḥ adhunā mātṛ bhāga stham rūpam tredhā nirūpyate yad pramāṇa ātmakam rūpam adhvanaḥ  mātṛ bhāga gam padam hi avagama ātmatva samāveśāt tad ucyate tad eva ca padam mantraḥ prakṣobhāt pracyutam yadā gupta bhāṣī yatas  mātā tūṣṇīṃbhūtaḥ  vyavasthitaḥ tathā api na vimarśa ātma rūpam tyajati tena saḥ pramāṇa ātma vimarśa ātmā mānavat kṣobha bhāj natu mantrāṇām ca padānām ca tena uktam trikaśāsane abhinnam eva svam rūpam niḥspanda kṣobhite param audāsīnya parityāge prakṣobhān avarohaṇe varṇa adhvā mātṛ bhāge syāt  pūrvam yā kathitā pramā sā tu pūrṇa svarūpa tvāt avibhāga mayī yatas  tatas  ekaika varṇa tvam tattve tattve kṣamā āditaḥ kṛtvā śaive pare proktāḥ ṣoḍaśa arṇā visargataḥ tatra śakti parispandaḥ tāvān prāk  ca nirūpitaḥ saṃkalayya ucyate sarvam adhunā sukha saṃvide pada mantra varṇam ekam pura ṣoḍaśakam dharā iti ca nivṛttiḥ c tattva arṇam agni nayanam rasa śara puram astra mantra padam anyā muni tattva arṇam dvika pada mantram vasu akṣi bhuvanam apara kalā agni arṇa tattvam ekaka pada mantram sainya bhuvanam iti turyā ṣoḍaśa varṇāḥ pada mantra tattvam ekam ca śānti atītā iyam abhinavaguptena āryā trayam uktam saṃgrahāya śiṣyebhyaḥ saḥ  yam samasta eva adhvā bhairava abheda vṛttimān tad svātantryāt svatantra tvam aśnuvānaḥ  vabhāsate tathā hi mātṛ rūpa sthaḥ  mantrādhva iti nirūpitaḥ tathā hi cit vimarśena grastā vācya daśā yadā śiva jñāna kriyā āyatta manana trāṇa tatparā aśeṣa śakti paṭalī līlā lāmpaṭī apāṭavāt  cyutā māna mayāt rūpāt  saṃvid mantra adhvatām gatā pramāṇa rūpa tām etya prayāti adhvā pada ātma tām tathā hi mātuḥ viśrāntiḥ varṇān saṃghaṭya tān bahūn saṃghaṭṭanam ca kramikam saṃjalpa ātmakam eva tad  vikalpasya svakam rūpam bhoga āveśa mayam sphuṭam atas  pramāṇa tā rūpam padam asmad guruḥ jagau pramāṇa rūpa tā āveśam aparityajya meya tām gacchan kalanayā yogāt adhvā proktaḥ kalā ātmakaḥ śuddhe prameya tā yoge sūkṣma sthūlatva bhāgini tattva adhva bhuvana adhva tve krameṇa anusaret guruḥ prameya māna mātṝṇām yad rūpam upari sthitam pramātmā atra sthitaḥ  dhvāyam varṇa ātmā dṛśyatām kila ucchalat saṃvidā mātra viśrānti āsvāda yoginaḥ sarva abhidhāna sāmarthyāt aniyantrita śaktayaḥ sṛṣṭāḥ sva ātma saha utthe rthe dharā paryanta bhāgini āmṛśantaḥ sva cit bhūmau tāvataḥ  rthān abhedataḥ varṇa oghāḥ te pramā rūpām satyām bibhrati saṃvidam bālāḥ tiryak pramātāraḥ  ye pyasaṃketa bhāginaḥ te pyakṛtrima saṃskāra sārām ena am sva saṃvidam bhinna bhinnām upāśritya yānti citrām pramātṛ tām asyāḥ  ca akṛtrima ananta varṇa saṃvidi rūḍha tām saṃketā yānti ced te pi yānti asaṃketa vṛtti tām anayā tu vinā sarve saṃketā bahuśas  kṛtāḥ aviśrānta tayā kuryuḥ anavasthām duruttarām bālaḥ  vyutpādyate yena tatra saṃketa mārgaṇāt  aṅguli ādeśane pyasya na avikalpā tathā matiḥ vikalpaḥ śabda mūlaḥ ca śabdaḥ saṃketa jīvitaḥ tena anantaḥ  hi amāyīyaḥ yaḥ  varṇa grāma īdṛśaḥ saṃvid vimarśa sacivaḥ sadā eva sa hi jṛmbhate yata eva ca māyīyā varṇāḥ sūtim vitenire ye ca māyīya varṇeṣu vīrya tvena nirūpitāḥ saṃketa nirapekṣāḥ te pramā iti parigṛhyatām tathā hi para vākyeṣu śruteṣu āvriyate nijā pramā yasya jaḍaḥ  sau naḥ tatra arthe bhyeti mātṛ tām śukavat sa paṭhati eva param tad kramita eka bhāj  svātantrya lābhataḥ svākya pramālābhe tu boddhṛ tā yasya hi sva pramā bodhaḥ  vipakṣa udbheda nigrahāt vākya ādi varṇa puñje sve sa pramātā vaśībhavet  yathā yathā ca akṛtakam tad rūpam atiricyate tathā tathā camatkāra tāratamyam vibhāvyate ādyāmāyīya varṇa antar nimagne ca uttarottare sakete pūrva pūrva aṃśa majjane pratibhā bhidaḥ ādya udreka mahat tve pi pratibhā ātmani niṣṭhitāḥ dhruvam kavitva vaktṛtva śālitām yānti sarvatas  yāvat dhāmani saṃketa nikāra kalanā ujjhite viśrāntaḥ cit maye kim kim na vetti kurute na vā ata eva hi vāc siddhau varṇānām samupāsyatā sarvajñatva ādi siddhau vā kā siddhiḥ yā na tad mayī tad uktam vara dena śrī siddhayogīśvarīmate tena guptena guptāḥ te śeṣā varṇāḥ tu iti sphuṭam evam mā mātṛ mānatva meya tvaiḥ yaḥ  vabhāsate ṣaḍvidhaḥ sva vapuḥ śuddhau śuddhim saḥ  dhvā adhigacchati ekena vapuṣā śuddhau tatra eva anya prakāra tām antar bhāvya ācaret śuddhim anusaṃdhānavān guruḥ anantarbhāva śaktau tu sūkṣmam sūkṣmam tu śodhayet  tad viśuddham bīja bhāvāt  sūte na uttara saṃtatim śodhanam bahudhā tad tad bhoga prāpti ekatāna tā tad ādhipatyam tad tyāgaḥ tad śiva ātmatva vedanam tad līna tā tad nirāsaḥ sarvam ca etad kramākramāt  ata eva ca te mantrāḥ śodhakāḥ citra rūpiṇaḥ siddhānta vāma dakṣa ādau citrām śuddhim vitanvate anuttara trikānām akrama mantrāḥ tu ye kila te sarve sarva dāḥ kintu kasyācid  kvāpi mukhya tā atas  śodhaka bhāvena śāstre śrī pūrva saṃjñite parāpara ādi mantrāṇām adhvani uktā vyavasthitiḥ śodhaka tvam ca mālinyā devīnām tritayasya ca deva trayasya vaktrāṇām aṅgānām aṣṭakasya ca kim vā ati bahunā dvāra vāstu ādhāra guru krame lokapa astra vidhau mantrān muktvā sarvam viśodhakam yad ca etad adhvanaḥ proktam śodhya tvam śoddhṛ tā ca yā sā svātantryāt śiva abhede yuktā iti uktam ca śāsane sarvam etad vibhāti eva parameśitari dhruve pratibimba svarūpeṇa na tu bāhya tayā yatas  cit vyomni eva śive tad tad deha ādi matiḥ īdṛśī bhinnā saṃsāriṇām rajjau sarpa sraj vīci buddhivat  yatas  prāc deha maraṇa siddhāntaḥ svapna gocaraḥ deha antara ādiḥ maraṇe kīdṛś vā deha saṃbhavaḥ svapne pi pratibhā mātra sāmānya prathana abalāt viśeṣāḥ pratibhāsante na bhāvyante pi te yathā śālagrāma upalāḥ kecid citra ākṛti bhṛtaḥ  yathā tathā māyā ādi bhūmi anta lekhā citra hṛdaḥ citaḥ nagara arṇava śaila ādyāḥ tad icchā anuvidhāyinaḥ na svayam sat asantaḥ  naḥ kāraṇa akāraṇa ātmakāḥ niyateḥ cira rūḍhāyāḥ samucchedāt pravartanāt  arūḍhāyāḥ svatantraḥ  yam sthitaḥ cit vyoma bhairavaḥ ekacit mātra saṃpūrṇa bhairava abheda bhāgini evam asmi iti anām arśaḥ  bhedakaḥ  bhāva maṇḍale sarva pramāṇaiḥ naḥ siddham svapne kartṛ antaram yathā sva saṃvidaḥ sva siddhāyāḥ tathā sarvatra buddhyatām citta citra pura udyāne krīḍet evam hi vetti yaḥ aham eva sthitaḥ  bhūta bhāva tattva puraiḥ iti evam jātaḥ  mṛtaḥ  smi iti janma mṛtyu vicitra tāḥ ajanmani amṛtau bhānti citta bhittau sva nirmitāḥ pareha saṃvidā mātram para loka iha lokate vastutas  saṃvidaḥ  deśaḥ kālaḥ  vā na eva kiṃcana abhaviṣyat ayam sargaḥ  mūrtaḥ ced na tu cit mayaḥ tad avekṣyata tad madhyāt  kena ekaḥ  pi dharādharaḥ bhūta tanmātra varga ādeḥ ādhāra ādheya tā krame ante saṃvid mayī śaktiḥ śiva rūpā eva dhāriṇī tasmāt pratītiḥ eva ittham kartrī dhartrī ca sā śivaḥ tatas  bhāvāḥ tatra bhāvāḥ śaktiḥ ādhārikā tatas  sāṃkalpikam nirādhāram api na eva patati adhas  sva ādhāra śaktau viśrāntam viśvam ittham vimṛśyatām asyāḥ  ghana aham iti ādi rūḍhiḥ eva dharā āditā yāvat ante cit asmi iti nirvṛttā bhairava ātma tā maṇau  indrāyudhe bhāsa iva nīla ādayaḥ śive paramārtha ta eṣām tu na udayaḥ  na vyayaḥ kvacid  deśe kāle tra vā sṛṣṭiḥ iti etad asamañjasam cit ātmanā hi devena sṛṣṭiḥ dikkālayoḥ api jāgara abhimate sārdha hasta tritaya gocare prahare ca pṛthak  svapnāḥ citra diś kāla māninaḥ ata eva kṣaṇam nāma na kiṃcid api manmahe kriyā kṣaṇe vā api ekasmin bahvyaḥ saṃsyuḥ drutāḥ kriyāḥ tena ye bhāva saṃkocam kṣaṇa antam pratipedire te nūnam enayā nāḍyā śūnya dṛṣṭi avalambinaḥ tad ya eṣa sataḥ  bhāvān  śūnyīkartum tathā asataḥ sphuṭīkartum svatantra tvāt īśaḥ saḥ  smat prabhuḥ śivaḥ tad ittham parameśānaḥ  viśva rūpaḥ pragīyate na tu bhinnasya kasya api dharā ādeḥ upapanna tā uktam ca etad purā eva iti na bhūyas  pravivicyate bhūyobhiḥ ca api bāhya artha dūṣaṇaiḥ pravyaramyata tad ittham eṣa nirṇītaḥ kalā ādeḥ vistaraḥ  dhvanaḥ  ch atha śrī tantrāloke dvādaśam āhnikam atha adhvanaḥ  sya prakṛta upayogaḥ prakāśyate b ittham adhvā samastaḥ  yam yathā saṃvidi saṃsthitaḥ tad dvārā śūnya dhī prāṇa nāḍī cakra tanuṣu athaḥ bahis ca liṅga mūrti agni sthaṇḍila ādiṣu sarvatas  tathā sthitaḥ samastaḥ ca vyastaḥ ca eṣa kramākramāt  āsaṃvid tattvam ābāhyam yaḥ  yamadhvā vyavasthitaḥ tatra tatra ucitam rūpam svam svātantryeṇa bhāsayet  sarvam sarvatra rūpam ca tasya api na na bhāsate na hi avaccheditām kvāpi svapne pi viṣahāmahe evam viśva adhva saṃpūrṇam kāla vyāpāra citritam deśa kāla maya spanda sadma deham vilokayet  tathā vilokyamānaḥ  sau viśva antar devatā mayaḥ dhyeyaḥ pūjyaḥ ca tarpyaḥ ca tadā āviṣṭaḥ  vimucyate ittham ghaṭam paṭam liṅgam sthaṇḍilam pustakam jalam yad vā kiṃcid kvacid paśyet tatra tad maya tām vrajet  tatra arpaṇam hi vastūnām abhedena arcanam matam tathā saṃpūrṇa rūpatva anusaṃdhiḥ dhyānam ucyate saṃpūrṇatva anusaṃdhānam akampam dārḍhyam ānayan tathā antar jalpa yogena vimṛśan japa bhājanam tatra arpitānām bhāvānām svaka bheda vilāpanam kurvan  tad raśmi sadbhāvam dadyāt homa kriyā paraḥ tathā evaṃkurvataḥ sarvam sama bhāvena paśyataḥ niṣkampa tā vratam śuddham sāmyam nandiśikhā uditam tathā arcana japa dhyāna homa vrata vidhi kramāt paripūrṇām sthitim prāhuḥ samādhim guravaḥ purā atra pūjā japa ādyeṣu bahis antar dvaya sthitau dravya oghe na vidhiḥ kaḥ  pi na kā api pratiṣiddha tā kalpanā śuddhi saṃdhi ādeḥ na upayogaḥ  tra kaścana uktam śrī trika sūtre ca jāyate yajanam prati avidhi jñaḥ  vidhi jñaḥ ca iti evamādi su vistaram yadā yathā yena yatra svā samvittiḥ prasīdati tadā tathā tena tatra tad tad bhogyam vidhiḥ ca saḥ laukika alaukikam sarvam tena atra viniyojayet  niṣkampa tve sa kampaḥ tu kampam nirhrāsayet balāt  yathā yena abhyupāyena kramāt akramataḥ  pi vā vicikitsā galati antar tathā asau yatnavān bhavet  dhī karma akṣa gatā devīḥ niṣiddhaiḥ eva tarpayet  vīra vratam ca abhinandet iti bharga śikhā vacaḥ tathā hi śaṅkā mālinyam glāniḥ saṃkoca iti adaḥ saṃsāra kāra āgāra antaḥ sthūlasthūṇāghaṭāyate mantrā varṇa svabhāvā ye dravyam yad pāñcabhautikam yad cit ātma prāṇi jātam tatra kaḥ saṃkaraḥ katham saṃkara abhāvataḥ kā iyam śaṅkā tasyām api sphuṭam na śaṅketa tathā śaṅkā vilīyeta avahelayā śrī sarva ācāra vīra ālī niśācara krama ādiṣu śāstreṣu vitatam ca etad tatra tatra ucyate yatas  śaṅkayā jāyate glāniḥ śaṅkayā vighna bhājanam uvāca utpaladevaḥ ca śrīmān asmad guroḥ guruḥ sarva āśaṅkā aśanim mārgam numaḥ  māheśvaram tu iti anuttara pada āptaye tad idam āṇavam darśita abhyupāyam ati vistarāt nanu vidāṃkurudhvam budhāḥ  ch atha śrī tantrāloke trayodaśam āhnikam atha adhikṛti bhāhanam ka iha vā katham vā iti alam vivecayitum ucyate vividha śaktipāta kramaḥ b tatra kecid iha prāhuḥ śaktipāta imam vidhim tam pradarśya nirākṛtya sva matam darśayiṣyate tatra idam dṛśyamānam sat sukha duḥkha vimoha bhāj  viṣamam sat tathābhūtam samam hetum prakalpayet  saḥ  vyaktam tad ca sattva ādi nānā rūpam acetanam ghaṭa ādivat kāryam iti hetuḥ ekaḥ  sya sā niśā sā jaḍā kārya tādrūpyāt kāryam ca asyām sat eva hi kalā ādi dharaṇī prāntam jāḍyāt sā sūtaye kṣamā tena īśaḥ kṣobhayet enām kṣobhaḥ  syāḥ sūti yogya tā puṃsaḥ prati ca sā bhogyam sūte na ādīn pṛthagvidhān puṃsaḥ ca nirviśeṣa tve mukta aṇūn prati kim na tad  nimittam karma saṃskāraḥ sa ca teṣu na vidyate iti ced karma saṃskāra abhāvaḥ teṣām kutas  kila na bhogāt anya karma aṃśa prasaṅgaḥ  hi duratyayaḥ yugapad karmaṇām bhogaḥ  na ca yuktaḥ krameṇa hi phalet yad karma tad kasmāt svam rūpam saṃtyajet kvacid  jñānāt karma kṣayaḥ ced tad kuta īśvara coditāt  dharmāt yadi kutas  saḥ  pi karmataḥ ced tad ucyatām na hi karma asti tādṛkṣam yena jñānam pravartate karma ja tve ca tad jñānam phala rāśau patet dhruvam anya karma phalam prācyam karma rāśim ca kim dahet  īśasya dveṣa rāga ādi śūnyasya api katham kvacid  tathā abhisaṃdhiḥ na anyatra bheda hetoḥ abhāvataḥ nanu ittham pradahet jñānam karma jālāni karma hi ajñāna sahakārī idam sūte svarga ādikam phalam ajñānam jñānataḥ  naśyet anya karma phalāt api upavāsa ādikam ca anyat duṣṭa karma phalam bhavet  niṣphalīkurute duṣṭam karma iti aṅgīkṛtam kila ajñānam iti yad proktam jñāna abhāvaḥ sa ced sa kim prāgabhāvaḥ  thavā dhvaṃsa ādye kim sarva saṃvidām kasya api vā atha jñānasya prācyaḥ pakṣaḥ tu asaṃbhavī na kiṃcid yasya vijñānam udapādi tathāvidhaḥ na aṇuḥ asti bhave hi asmin  anādau kaḥ  nu ayam kramaḥ bhāvinaḥ prāc abhāvaḥ ca jñānasya iti sthite sati muktāṇoḥ api saḥ  sti eva janmataḥ prāk asau na ca jñānam bhāvi vimukte smin  iti ced carcyatām idam kasmāt jñānam na bhāvyatra nanu deha āt yajanmataḥ tad kasmāt karmaṇaḥ kṣaiṇyāt tad kutaḥ jñāna hānitaḥ ajñānasya katham hāniḥ prāc abhāve hi saṃvidaḥ ajñānam prāgabhāvaḥ  sau na bhāvi utpatti asaṃbhavāt kasmāt na bhāvi tad jñānam nanu deha āt yajanmataḥ iti eṣa sarva pakṣa ghnaḥ  niśitaḥ cakraka bhramaḥ atha pradhvaṃsa eva idam ajñānam tad sadā sthitam muktā aṇuṣu iti teṣu astu māyā kārya vijṛmbhitam atha ajñānam na hi abhāvaḥ  mithyājñānam tu tad matam tad eva karmaṇām svasmin kartavye saha kāraṇam vaktavyam tarhi kim karma yadā sūte svakam phalam tadā eva mithyājñānena satā hetu tvam āpyate atha yasmin kṣaṇe karma kṛtam tatra svarūpa sat  mithyājñānam yadi tatas tādṛśāt kamarṇaḥ phalam prāk pakṣe pralaye vṛtte prācya sṛṣṭi pravartane deha ādi abhāvāt naḥ mithyājñānasya kvāpi saṃbhavaḥ uttarasmin punar  pakṣe yadā yadyena yatra vā kriyate karma tad sarvam ajñāna sacivam tadā avaśyam iti kasya api na karma prakṣayaḥ  bhavet  yadi api jñānavān bhūtvā vidhatte karma kiṃcana viphalam syāt tu tad pūrva karma rāśau tu kā gatiḥ atha pralaya kāle pi cit svabhāvatva yogataḥ aṇūnā saṃbhavati eva jñānam mithyā iti tad kutas  svabhāvāt iti ced mukte śive vā kim tathā na hi yad ca adarśanam ākhyātam nimittam pariṇāmini pradhāne tad hi saṃkīrṇa vaivittayā ubhaya yogataḥ darśanāya pum artha eka yogyatā sacivam dhiyaḥ ārabhya sate dharaṇī paryantam tatra yad citaḥ buddhi vṛtti aviśiṣṭa tvam puṃsprayāśarprasādataḥ prakāśanāt hiyaḥ  rthena saha bhogaḥ sa bhaṇyate buddhiḥ eva asmi vikṛti dharmikāni aḥ tu kaḥ  pyasau mad vilakṣaṇa ekātmā iti evam vaivi ya saṃvidi pum arthasya kṛta tvena sahakāri viyogataḥ tam pumāṃsam prati na eva sūte kiṃtu anyam eva hi atra puṃsaḥ tha mūlasya dharmaḥ  darśana tā dvayoḥ athavā iti vikalpaḥ  yamāḥ tām etad tu bhaṇya tām bhogaḥ  viveka paryanta iti yad tatra kaḥ  vadhiḥ viveka lābhe nikhila sūti dṛś yadi sā api kim sāmānyena viśeṣaiḥ vā prācye syāt eka janmataḥ uttare na kadācid syāt bhāvi kālasya yogataḥ kaiścid eva viśeṣaiḥ ced sarveṣām yugapad bhavet vivekaḥ  na ādi saṃyogāt kā hi anyonyam vicitra tā tasmāt sāṃkhya dṛśā api idam jñānam na eva yujyate ajñānena vinā bandha mokṣau na eva vyavasthayā yujyete tad ca kathita yuktibhiḥ na upapadyate bhāyā karmāṇudeva icchā asadbhāve pi sthite tatas  na bandha mokṣayoḥ yogaḥ  bheda hetoḥ asaṃbhavāt tasmāt ajñāna śabdena jñatva kartṛtva dharmaṇām cit aṇūnām āvaraṇam kiṃcid vācyam vipaścitā āvāraṇa ātmanā siddham tad svarūpāt abhedavat  bhede pramāṇa abhāvāt ca tad ekam nikhila ātmasu tad ca kasmāt prasūtam syāt māyātaḥ ced katham nu sā kvacid eva suvīta etad na tu mukta ātmani iti ayam prācyaḥ paryanuyogaḥ syāt nimittam ced na labhyate utpatti abhāvataḥ tena nityam na ca vinaśyati tatas  eva eka tāyām ca anya ātma sādhāraṇa tvataḥ na vāvastu artha kāri tvāt na cittad saṃvṛti tvataḥ na ca etena ātmanām yogaḥ  hetumān  tad asaṃbhavāt tena ekam vastu sannityam nitya saṃbaddham ātmabhiḥ jaḍam malam tad ajñānam saṃsāra aṅkura kāraṇam tasya roddhrī yadā śaktiḥ udāste śiva raśmibhiḥ tadā aṇuḥ spṛśyate spṛṣṭaḥ svake jñāna kriye sphuṭe samāviśet ayam sūryakāntaḥ  rkeṇa iva coditaḥ roddhryāḥ ca śakteḥ mādhyasthya tāratamyavaśakramāat vicitra tvam atas  prāhuḥ abhivyaktau sva saṃvidaḥ sa eṣa śaktipāta ākhyaḥ śāstreṣu paribhāṣyate atra ucyate malaḥ tāvat ittham eṣa na yujyate iti pūrvāhṇike proktam punaruktau tu kim phalam malasya pākaḥ kaḥ  yam syāt nāśaḥ ceditara ātmanām sa ekaḥ  mala iti ukteḥ nairmalyam anuṣajyate atha pratyātma niyataḥ  na ādiḥ ca prāgabhāvavat  malaḥ  naśyet tathā api eṣa na āśaḥ yadi sa hetukaḥ hetuḥ karma īśvara icchā vā karma tāvat na tādṛśam īśvara icchā svatantrā ca kvacid eva tathā eva kim ahetukaḥ  sya nāśaḥ ced prāk eva eṣa vinaśyatu kṣaṇa antaram sadṛś  sūte iti ced sthira tā eva sā na ca nityasya bhāvasya hetu anāyatta janmanaḥ na āśaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ prāc abhāvaḥ tu avastu iti tathā astu saḥ atha asya pākaḥ  nāma eṣa sva śakti pratibaddha tā sarvān prati tathā eṣa syāt ruddha śaktiḥ viṣa agnivat  punar udbhūta śaktau ca sva kāryam syāt viṣa agnivat  muktā api na muktāḥ syuḥ śaktim ca asya na manmahe roddhrī iti ced kasya nṛṇām jñatva kartṛ tvayoḥ yadi sadbhāva mātrādra uddhṛ tve śiva muktā aṇu asaṃbhavaḥ saṃnidhāna atiriktam ca na kiṃcid kurute malaḥ ātmanā pariṇāmi tvāt anityatva prasaṅgataḥ jñatva kartṛtva mātram ca pudgalā na tad āśrayāḥ tad ced āvāritam hanta rūpa nāśaḥ prasajyate āvāraṇam ca adṛśya tvam na ca tad vastunaḥ  nyatām karoti ghaṭavat jñānam na avarītum ca śakyate jñānena āvaraṇīyena tad eva āvaraṇam katham na jñāyate tathā ca syāt āvṛtiḥ nāma mātrataḥ roddhryāḥ ca śakteḥ kaḥ tasya pratibandhaka īśvaraḥ yadi apekṣā virahitaḥ tatra prāc dattam uttaram karma sāmyam apekṣya atha tasya icchā saṃpravartate tasya api rūpam vaktavyam sama tā karmaṇām hi kā bhoga paryāya māhātmyāt kāle kvāpi phalam prati virodhāt karmaṇī ruddhe tiṣṭhataḥ sāmyam īdṛśam tam ca kāla aṃśakam devaḥ sarvajñaḥ  vīkṣya tam malam runddhe lakṣyaḥ sa kālaḥ ca sukha duḥkha ādi varjanaiḥ na etad kramika saṃśuddha vyāmiśra ākāra karmabhiḥ tathā eva deye sva phale kā iyam anya unya roddhṛtā rodhe tayoḥ ca jāti āyuḥ api na syāt atas  patet  dehaḥ  bhoga dayoḥ eva nirodha iti ced nanu jāti āyuṣprada karma aṃśa saṃnidhau yadi śaṃkaraḥ malam runddhe bhoga dātuḥ karmaṇaḥ kim bibheti saḥ śataśas  pi hlāda tāpa śūnyām saṃcinvate daśām na ca bhakti rasa āveśam iti bhūmnā vilokitam atha api kāla māhātmyam apekṣya parameśvaraḥ tathā karoti vaktavyam kālaḥ  sau kīdṛśaḥ tu iti kim ca anādiḥ ayam bhogaḥ karma anādi sa pudgalam tatas ca bhoga paryāya kālaḥ sarvasya niḥsamaḥ ādimattve hi kasya api vargāt asmāt bhavet iyam vaicitrī bhuktam etena kalpam etena tu dvayam iyataḥ  bhoga paryāyāt syāt sāmyam karmaṇām iti anena naya bījena manye vaicitrya kāraṇam jagataḥ karma yad klaptam tad tathā na avakalpate anādi mala saṃcchannā aṇavaḥ  dṛkkriyā ātmanā sarve tulyāḥ katham citrām śritāḥ karma paramparām bhoga lolikayā ced sā vicitra iti kutaḥ nanu anādi karma saṃskāra vaicitryāt iti ced punar  vācyam tad eva vaicitryam kutaḥ niyati rāgayoḥ mahimā ced ayam tau kim na asamañjasya bhāginau īśvara icchā anapekṣā tu bheda hetuḥ na kalpate atha anāditva mātreṇa yukti hīnena sādhyate vyavastheya m alam tarhi malena astu vṛthā amunā tathā hi karma tāvat na u yāvat māyā na pudgale vyāpriyeta na ca ahetuḥ tad vṛttiḥ tad mitaḥ  malaḥ ittham ca kalpite māyā kārye karmaṇi hetu tām anādi karma ced gacchet kim malasya upakalpanam nanu mābhūt malaḥ tarhi citra ākāreṣu karmasu santati āvartamāneṣu vyavasthā na prakalpate ādau madhye ca citra tvāt karmaṇām na yathā samaḥ ātma ākāraḥ  pi kaḥ  pyeṣa bhāvi kāle tathā bhavet  ittham ucchinna eva ayam bandha mokṣa ādikaḥ kramaḥ ajñānāt bandhanam mokṣaḥ  jñānāt iti parīkṣitam virodhe sva phale ca ete karmaṇī samaye kvacid  udāsāte yadi tatas  karma etad pratibudhyatām śiva śakti nipātasya kaḥ  vakāśaḥ tu tāvatā kvāpi kāle tayoḥ etad audāsīnyam yadā tatas  kāla antare tayoḥ tadvat virodhasya anivṛttitaḥ atas ca na phaleta ante tābhyām karma antaraṇi ca ruddhāni prāpta kāla tvāt gatābhyām upabhogya tām evam sadā eva vārtāyām dehapāte tathā eva ca jāte vimokṣa iti āstām śaktipāta ādi kalpanā atha udāsīna tad karma dvaya yoga kṣaṇa antare karma antaram phalam sūte tad kṣaṇe pi tathā na kim kṣaṇa antare tha te eva pratibandha vivarjite phalataḥ pratibandhasya varjanam kiṃkṛtam tayoḥ karma sāmyam sva rūpeṇa na ca tad tāratamya bhāj  na śiva icchā iti tad kārye śaktipāte na tad bhavet tirobhāvaḥ ca nāma ayam sa kasmāt udbhavet punar  karma sāmyena yatkṛtyam prāk eva etad kṛtam kila hetu tve ca īśvara icchāyā vācyam pūrvavat eva tu etena anye pi ye pekṣyā īśa icchāyām prakalpitāḥ dhvastāḥ te pi hi nitya ani ahetu ahetu ādi dūṣaṇāt vairāgyam bhoga vairasyam dharmaḥ kaḥ  pi viveki tā sat saṅgaḥ parameśāna pūjā ādi abhyāsa nitya tā āpad prāptiḥ tad nirīkṣā dehe kiṃcid ca lakṣaṇam śāstra sevā bhoga saṃgha pūrṇa tā jñānam aiśvaram iti apekṣyam yadi īśasya dūṣyam etad ca pūrvavat  vyabhicāraḥ ca sāmastya vyasta tvābhyām svarūpataḥ anyonya anupraveśaḥ ca anupapattiḥ ca bhūyasī tasmāt na manmahe kaḥ  yam śaktipāta vidheḥ kramaḥ ittham bhrānti viṣa āveśa mūrcchā nirmoka dāyinīm śrī śaṃbhu vadanodgīrṇām vacmi āgama mahauṣadhīm devaḥ svatantraḥ cit rūpaḥ prakāśa ātmā svabhāvataḥ rūpa pracchādana krīḍā yogāt aṇuḥ anekakaḥ sa svayam kalpita ākāra vikalpa ātmaka karmabhiḥ badhnāti ātmānam eva iha svātantryāt iti varṇitam svātantrya mahimā eva ayam devasya yad asau punar  svam rūpam pariśuddham sat spṛśati api aṇu tāmayaḥ na vācyam tu katham nāma kasmiṃścid puṃsi asau tathā na hi nāma pumān kaścit yasmin paryanuyujyate deva eva tathā asau ced  svarūpam ca asya tādṛśam tādṛś prathā svabhāvasya svabhāve kā anuyojyatā āha asmat parameṣṭhī ca śiva dṛṣṭau guru uttamaḥ pañca prakāra kṛtya ukti śiva tvāt nija karmaṇe pravṛttasya nimittānām apareṣām kva mārgaṇam channa sva rūpa tā ābhāse puṃsi yad yādṛśam phalam tatra aṇoḥ sata eva asti svātantryam karmataḥ hi tad  īśvarasya ca yā sva ātma tirodhitsā nimitta tām sā abhyeti karma malayoḥ atas  na ādi vyavasthitiḥ tirodhiḥ pūrṇa rūpasya āpūrṇa tvam tad ca pūraṇam prati bhinnena bhāvena spṛhātaḥ  lolikā malaḥ viśuddha sva prakāśa ātma śiva rūpa tayā vinā na kiṃcid yujyate tena hetuḥ atra maheśvaraḥ ittham sṛṣṭi sthiti dhvaṃsa traye māyām apekṣate kṛtyai malam tathā karma śiva icchā eva iti susthitam yad tu kasmiṃścana śivaḥ svena rūpeṇa bhāsate tatra asya na aṇuge tāvat apekṣye mala karmaṇī aṇu svarūpa tā hānau tad gatam hetu tām katham vrajet māyā anapekṣa tvam ata eva upapādayet tena śuddhaḥ sva prakāśaḥ śiva eva atra kāraṇam sa ca svācchandya mātreṇa tāratamya prakāśakaḥ kula jāti vapuṣkarma vayaḥ nuṣṭhāna saṃpadaḥ anapekṣya śive bhaktiḥ śaktipātaḥ  phala arthinām yā phala arthitayā bhaktiḥ sā karma ādyam apekṣate tatas  tra syāt phale bhedaḥ  na apavarge tu asau tathā bhoga apavarga dvitaya abhisaṃdhātuḥ api sphuṭam prāc bhāge pekṣate karma citra tvāt na uttare punar  anābhāsita rūpaḥ  pi tad ā abhāsitayā iva yad  sthitvā mantra ādi saṃgṛhya tyajet saḥ sya tirobhavaḥ śrī sāraśāstre bhagavān vastu etad samabhāṣata dharma adharma ātmakaiḥ bhāvaiḥ anekaiḥ veṣṭayet svayam asandeham svam ātmānam avīcya ādi śiva antake tadvat śakti samūhena sa eva tu viveṣṭayet  svayam badhnāti deveśaḥ svayam ca eva vimuñcati svayam bhoktā svayam jñātā svayam ca eva upalakṣayet svayam bhuktiḥ ca muktiḥ ca svayam devī svayam prabhuḥ svayam ekākṣarā ca eva yathā ūṣmā kṛṣṇavartmanaḥ vastu uktam atra svātantryāt sva ātma rūpa prakāśanam śrīmat niśā ākule pyuktam mithyā bhāvita cetasaḥ mala māyā vicāreṇa kliśyante su alpabuddhayaḥ sphaṭika upala gaḥ  reṇuḥ kim tasya kurutām priye vyomni iva nīlam hi malam malaśaṃkām tatas tyajet śrīmān vidyā aguruḥ ca āha pramāṇa stuti darśane dharma adharma vyāpti vināśa antara kāle śakteḥ pātaḥ  gāhani kairyaḥ pratipannaḥ tam sva icchātaḥ saṃgiramāṇāḥ stavaka ādyāḥ svātantryam tad tvayi anapekṣam kathayeyuḥ tāratamya prakāśaḥ  yaḥ tīvra madhyama manda tāḥ tā eva śaktipātasya pratyekam traidhamāsthitāḥ tīvra tīvraḥ śaktipātaḥ  dehapāta vaśāt svayam mokṣa pradaḥ tadā eva anya kāle vā tāratamyataḥ madhya tīvrāt punar  sarvam ajñānam vinivartate svayam eva yatas  vetti bandha mokṣa tayā ātma tām tad prātibham mahā jñānam śāstra ācārya anapekṣi yad  pratibhā candrikā śānta dhvāntaḥ ca ācārya candramāḥ tamaḥ tāpau hanti dṛśam visphārya ānanda nirbharām sa śiṣṭaḥ karma kartṛ tvāt śiṣyaḥ  nyaḥ karma bhāvataḥ śiṣṭaḥ sarvatra ca smārta pada kāla kula ādiṣu uktaḥ svayaṃbhūḥ śāstra artha pratibhā pariniṣṭhitaḥ yad mūlam śāsanam tena na riktaḥ kaḥ  pi jantukaḥ tatra api tāratamya uttham ānantyam dārḍhya kamprate yuktiḥ śāstram guruḥ vādaḥ  bhyāsa ityādi apekṣate kampamānam hi vijñānam svayam eva punar vrajet  kasya api dārḍhyam anyasya yukti ādyaiḥ kevala itaraiḥ yathā yathā para apekṣā tānavam prātibhe bhavet  tathā tathā guruḥ asau śreṣṭhaḥ  vijñāna pāragaḥ anyatas  śikṣita ananta jñānaḥ  pi pratibhā balāt  yad vetti tatra tatra asya śiva tā jyāyasī ca sā na ca asya samayi tvā ādi kramaḥ  na api abhiṣecanam na santāna ādi naḥ vidyā vratam prātibhavartmanaḥ ādi vidvān mahādevaḥ tena eṣaḥ  dhiṣṭhitaḥ  yatas  saṃskārāḥ tad adhiṣṭhāna siddhyai tad tasya tu svatas  devībhiḥ dīkṣitaḥ tena sa bhaktiḥ śiva śāsane dṛḍha tā kampratā bhedaiḥ saḥ  pi svayam atha vratāt  tapaḥ japa adeḥ gurutaḥ sva saṃskāram prakalpayet  yatas  vājasineya ākhya uktam siñcet svayam tanum ityādi upakramam yāvat ante tad pariniṣṭhitam abhiṣiktaḥ  bhavet evam na bāhya kalaśa ambubhiḥ śrī sarva vīra śrī brahma yāmala ādau ca tad tathā nirūpitam maheśena kiyat vā likhya tām idam ittham prātibhavi jñānam kim kim kasya na sādhayet  yad prātibhāt vā sarvam ca iti ūce śeṣa mahā muniḥ anye tu āhuḥ akāmasya prātibhaḥ guruḥ īdṛśaḥ sāmagrī janyatā kāmye tena ariman saṃskṛtaḥ  guruḥ niyateḥ mahimā na eva phale sādhye nivartate abhiṣiktaḥ cīrṇa vidyā vrataḥ tena phala pradaḥ asat etad iti prāhuḥ guravaḥ tattva darśinaḥ śrī somānanda kalyāṇa bhava bhūti purogamāḥ tathā hi trīśikā śāstra vivṛtau te bhyadhuḥ budhāḥ sāṃsiddhikam yad vijñānam tad cintā ratnam ucyate tad abhāve tad artham tadāhṛtam jñānam ādṛtam evam yaḥ  veda tattvena tasya nirvāṇa gāminī dīkṣā bhavati asandigdhā tila ājya āhuti varjitā adṛṣṭa maṇḍalaḥ  pi evam yaḥ kaścid vetti tattvataḥ sa siddhi bhāj bhavet nityam sa yogī sa ca dīkṣitaḥ avidhi jñaḥ  vidhāna jñaḥ  jāyate yajanam prati ityādi bhiḥ trīśikā uktaiḥ vākyaiḥ māheśvaraiḥ sphuṭam jñānam dīkṣā ādi saṃskāra sa tattvam iti varṇitam jñāna upāyaḥ tu dīkṣā ādi kriyā jñāna viyoginām iti etad adhunā eva āstā sva prastāve bhaviṣyati guru śāstra pramāṇa ādeḥ api upāya tvam aṃjasā pratibhā param iva eṣā sarva kāmadughā yatas  upāya yoga kramataḥ  nirupāyam atha ākramam yad rūpam tad param tattvam tatra tatra su niścitam yaḥ tu prātibha bāhya ātma saṃskāra dvaya sundaraḥ uktaḥ  nanya upakārya tvāt sa sākṣāt vara daḥ  guruḥ sva mukti mātre kasya api yāvat viśva vimocane pratibhoda iti khadyota ratna tāra indu sūryavat  tatas  prātibha saṃvittyai śāstram asmad kṛtam tu idam yaḥ  bhyasyet sa guruḥ na eva vastu arthā hi viḍambakāḥ para upajīvita abuddhyā sarva ittham na bhāsate tad uktyā na vinā vetti śaktipātasya māndyataḥ sphuṭam etad ca śāstreṣu teṣu teṣu nirūpyate kiraṇāyām tathā uktam ca gurutaḥ śāstrataḥ svatas  jñāna yogyāḥ tathā kecid caryā yogyāḥ tathā apare śrīmat nandiśikhātantre vitatya etad nirūpitam praśna uttara mukhena iti tad abhagnam nirūpyate anirdeśyaḥ śivaḥ tatra kaḥ  bhyupāyaḥ nirūpyatām iti praśne kṛte devyā śrīmān śaṃbhuḥ ni arūpayam upāyaḥ tra viveka ekaḥ sa hi heyam vihāpayan dadāti asya ca suśroṇi prātibham jñānam uttamam yadā pratibhayā yuktaḥ tadā muktaḥ ca mocayet  para śakti nipātena dhvasta māyā malaḥ pumān nanu prāk dīkṣayā mokṣaḥ  dhunā tu prātibhāt katham iti devyā kṛte praśne prāvartata vibhoḥ vacaḥ dīkṣayā mucyate jantuḥ prātibhena tathā priye guru āyattā tu sā dīkṣā badhya bandhana mokṣaṇe prātibhaḥ sya svabhāvaḥ tu kevalībhāva siddhi daḥ kevalasya dhruvam muktiḥ para tattvena sā nanu nṛ śakti śivam uktam hi tattva trayam idam tvayā nā badhyaḥ bandhane śaktiḥ karaṇam kartṛ tām spṛśat  śivaḥ kartā iti tad proktam sarvam guru āgamāt aṇoḥ punar vivekāt uktam tad uttarottaram ucyatām katham vivekaḥ kim vā asya devadeva vivicyate iti ukte parameśānyā jagāda ādi guruḥ śivaḥ śiva ādi tattva tritayam tad āgama vaśāt guroḥ adhra uttara gaiḥ vākyaiḥ siddham prātibhatām vrajet  dīkṣā asicchinna pāśa tvāt bhāvanā bhāvitasya hi vikāsam tattvam āyāti prātibham tad udāhṛtam bhasma  channa agnivat sphauṭyam prātibhe gaurava āgamāt  bījam kāla upta saṃsiktam yathā vardheta tad tathā yoga yāga ja paiḥ uktaiḥ guruṇā prātibham sphuṭet  vivekaḥ  tīndriyaḥ tu eṣa yadā āyāti vivecanam paśu pāśa pati jñānam svayam nirbhāsate tadā prātibhe tu samāyāte jñānam anyat tu sa indriyam vāc akṣi śruti gamyam ca api anya apekṣam varānane tad tyajet buddhim āsthāya pradīpam tu yathā divā prādurbhūta vivekasya syāt cit indriya gocare dūrāt śruti ādi vedha ādi vṛddhi krīḍā vicitritā sarva bhāva vivekāt tu sarva bhāva parāṅmukhaḥ krīḍāsu su virakta ātmā śiva bhāva eka bhāvitaḥ māhātmyam etad suśroṇi prātibhasya vidhīyate svacchāyādarśavat paśyet bahis antargatam śivam heya upādeya tattva jñaḥ tadā dhyāyet nijām citim siddhi jālam hi kathitam para pratyaya kāraṇam iha eva siddhāḥ kāya ante mucyeran  iti bhāvanāt  para bhāvana dārḍhyāt tu jīvanmuktaḥ  nigadyate etad te prātibhe bhede lakṣaṇam samudāhṛtam śāpa anugraha kāryeṣu tathā abhyāsena śaktayā teṣu udāsīnatāyām tu mucyate mocayet parān bhūta indriya ādi yogena baddhaḥ  ṇuḥ saṃsaret dhruvam sa eva pratibhā yuktaḥ śakti tattvam nigadyate tad pāta āveśataḥ  muktaḥ śiva eva bhava arṇavāt  nanu ācāryāt sa indriyam tad jñānam uktam atīndriyam viveka jam ca tad buddhyā tad katham syāt nirindriyam iti pṛṣṭaḥ  bhyadhāt svānta dhiyoḥ jāḍya eka vāsanāt  akṣa tvam pravivekena tad chittau bhāsakaḥ śivaḥ saṃskāraḥ sarva bhāvānām para tā parikīrtitā manaḥ buddhī na bhinne tu kasmiṃścid kāraṇa antare viveke kāraṇe hi ete prabhu śakti upavṛṃhite na manaḥ buddhi hīnaḥ tu jñānasya adhigamaḥ priye para bhāvāt tu tad sūkṣmam śakti tattvam nigadyate vivekaḥ sarva bhāvānām śuddha bhāvāt mahā āśayaḥ buddhi tattvam tu triguṇam uttama adhama madhyamam aṇima ādi gatam ca api bandhakam jaḍam indriyam nanu prātibhataḥ  muktau dīkṣayā kim śiva adhvare ūce jñānā hi dīkṣāyām bāla vāliśa yoṣitaḥ pāśa  chedāt vimucyante prabuddhi ante śiva adhvare tasmāt dīkṣā bhavati eṣu kāraṇa tvena sundari dīkṣayā pāśa mokṣe tu śuddha bhāvāt viveka jam iti eṣa paṭhitaḥ  granthaḥ svayam ye boddhum akṣamāḥ teṣām śiva ukti saṃvādāt bodhaḥ dārḍhyam vrajet iti śrīmat niśāṭane ca ātma guru śāstra vaśāt tridhā jñānam mukhyam sva upalabdhi vikalpa arṇava tāraṇam mantra ātma bhūta dravya āśa divya tattva ādi gocarā śaṃkā vikalpa mūlā hi śāmyet sva pratyayāt iti enam eva artham antar stham gṛhītvā mālinīmate evam asya ātmanaḥ kāle kasmiṃścid yogya tā vaśāt śaivī saṃbadhyate śaktiḥ śāntā mukti phala pradā tad saṃbandhāt tatas  kaścid tad kṣaṇāt apavṛjyate iti uktvā tīvra tīvra ākhya viṣayam bhāṣate punar  ajñānena saha ekatvam kasyacid vinivartate rudra śakti samāviṣṭaḥ sa yiyāsuḥ śiva icchayā bhukti mukti prasiddhi artham nīyate sat gurum prati tam ārādhya tatas tuṣṭāt dīkṣām āsādya śāṅkarīm tad kṣaṇāt vā upabhogāt vā dehapātāt śivam vrajet  asya arthā ātmanaḥ kācid kalana āmarśana ātmikā svam rūpam prati yā sā eva kaḥ  pi kāla iha uditaḥ yogya tā śiva tādātmya yoga arha tvam iha ucyate pūrvam kim na tathā kasmāt tadā eva iti na saṃgatam tathā ābhāsanam ujjhitvā na hi kālaḥ  sti kaścana svātantryāt tu tathā ābhāse kāla śaktiḥ vijṛmbhatām na tu paryanuyuktyai sā śive tad mahima uditā nanu śaivī mahāśaktiḥ saṃbaddhā eva ātmabhiḥ sthitā c satyam sa ācchādana ātmā tu śāntā tu eṣā svarūpa dṛś  kṣobhaḥ  hi bheda eva aikyam praśamaḥ tad mayī tatas  tayā śāntyā tu saṃbaddhaḥ sthitaḥ śakti svarūpa bhāj  tyakta aṇu bhāvaḥ  bhavati śivaḥ tad śakti dārḍhyataḥ tatra api tāratamya ādi vaśāt śīghracira āt itas  dehapātaḥ  bhavet asya yad vā kāṣṭha ādi tulya tā samasta vyavahāreṣu parācīnita cetanaḥ tīvra tīvra mahā śakti samāviṣṭaḥ sa sidhyati evam prāc viṣayaḥ  grantha iyān anyatra tu sphuṭam grantha antaram madhya tīvra śaktipāta aṃśa sūcakam ajñāna rūpa tā puṃsi bodhaḥ saṃkocite hṛdi saṃkoce vinivṛtte tu sva svabhāvaḥ prakāśate rudra śakti samāviṣṭa iti anena asya varṇyate cihna vargaḥ  ya uktaḥ  tra rudre bhaktiḥ su niścalā mantra siddhiḥ sarva tattva vaśi tvam kṛtya saṃpadaḥ kavi tvam sarva śāstra artha boddhṛtvam iti tad kramāt  sva tāratamya yogāt syāt eṣām vyasta samasta tā tatra api bhuktau muktau ca prādhānyam carcayet budhaḥ sa iti antaḥ  grantha eṣa dvitīya viṣayaḥ sphuṭaḥ anyaḥ tu manda tīvra ākhya śaktipāta vidhim prati manda tīvrāt śakti bala ādi iyāsā asya upajāyate śiva icchā vaśa yogena sat gurum prati saḥ  pi ca atra eva lakṣitaḥ śāstre yad uktam parameṣṭhinā yaḥ punar  sarva tattvāni vetti etāni yathārthataḥ sa guruḥ mad samaḥ proktaḥ  mantra vīrya prakāśakaḥ dṛṣṭāḥ saṃbhāvitāḥ tena spṛṣṭāḥ ca prīta cetasā narāḥ pāpaiḥ pramucyante sapta janma kṛtaiḥ api ye punar dīkṣitāḥ tena prāṇinaḥ śiva coditāḥ te yatheṣṭam phalam prāpya padam gacchanti anāmayam kim tattvam tattva vedī ka iti āmarśana yogataḥ pratibhānāt su ḥṛd saṅgāt gurau jigamiṣuḥ bhavet  evam jigamiṣā yogāt ācāryaḥ prāpyate sa ca tāratamya ādi yogena saṃsiddhaḥ saṃskṛtaḥ  pi ca prāc bheda bhāgī jhaṭiti kramāt sāmasti atoṃśataḥ ityādi bheda bhinnaḥ hi guroḥ lābha iha uditaḥ tasmāt dīkṣām sa labhate sadya eva śiva pradām jñāna rūpām yathā vetti sarvam eva yathārthataḥ jīvanmuktaḥ śivībhūtaḥ tadā eva asau nigadyate deha saṃbandhi tāpyasya śiva tāyai yatas  sphuṭā asyām bhedaḥ  hi kathanāt saṅgamāt avalokanāt śāstrāt saṃkramaṇāt sāmya caryā saṃdarśanāt caroḥ mantra mudrā ādi māhātmyāt samasta vyasta bhedataḥ kriyayā vā antara ākāra rūpa prāṇa praveśataḥ tadā ca deha saṃsthaḥ pi sa mukta iti bhaṇyate uktam ca śāstrayoḥ śrīmat ratna mālā gama ākhyayoḥ yasmin kāle tu guruṇā nirvikalpam prakāśitam tadā eva kila muktaḥ  sau yantram tiṣṭhati kevalam prārabdhṛ karma saṃbandhāt dehasya sukhi duḥkhite na viśaṅketa tad ca śrī gamaśāstre nirūpitam avidyā upāsitaḥ  dehaḥ  hi anya janma samudbhuvā karmaṇā tena bādhyante jñāninaḥ  pi kalevare jāti āyuḥ bhogadasya eka praghaṭṭaka tayā sthitiḥ ukta eka vacanāt hiḥ ca yatas tena iti saṃgatiḥ abhyāsa yukti saṃkrānti vedha ghaṭṭana rodhataḥ huteḥ vā mantra sāmarthyāt pāśa  cheda prayogataḥ sadyonirvāṇa dām kuryāt sadyas prāṇa viyojikām tatra tu eṣaḥ sti niyama āsanne maraṇa kṣaṇe tām kuryāt na anyathā ārabdhṛ karma yasmāt na śuddhi ati uktam ca pūrvam eva etad maṃtra sāmarthya yogataḥ prāṇaiḥ viyojitaḥ  pyeṣa bhuṅkte śeṣa phalam yatas  tad janma śeṣam vividham ativāhya tatas  sphuṭam karma antara nirodhena śīghram eva apavṛjyate tasmāt prāṇa harīm dīkṣām na ajñātvā maraṇa kṣaṇam vidadhyāt parameśa ājñā laṅghana ekaphalā hi sā ekaḥ trikaḥ  yam nirṇītaḥ śaktipāte pyathā paraḥ tīvra madhye tu dīkṣāyām kṛtāyām na tathā dṛḍhām sva ātmanaḥ  vetti śiva tām dehānte tu śivaḥ  bhavet  uktam ca niśi saṃcāra yoga saṃcāra śāstrayoḥ vikalpāt tu tanau sthitvā daha ante śiva tām vrajet  madhya madhye śaktipāte śiva lābha utsukaḥ  pi san bubhukṣuḥ yatra yuktaḥ tad bhuktvā deha kṣaye śivaḥ manda madhye tu tatra eva tattve kvāpi niyojitaḥ dehānte tattva gam bhogam bhuktvā paścāt śivam vrajet  tatra api tāratamyasya saṃbhavāt cira śīghra tā bahu alpa bhoga yogaḥ ca deha bhūma alpatā kramaḥ tīvra mande madhya mande manda mande bubhukṣu tā kramāt mukhyā atimātreṇa vidhinā eti antatas śivam anye yiyāsuḥ iti ādi grantham prāk grantha saṃgatam kurvanti madhya tīvra ākhya śakti saṃpāta gocaram yadā pratibhayā āviṣṭaḥ  pyeṣa saṃvāda yojanām icchanyiyāsuḥ bhavati tadā nīyeta sat gurum na sarvaḥ pratibhā āviṣṭaḥ śaktyā nīyeta sat gurum iti brūte yiyāsu tvam vaktavyam na anyathā dhruvam rudra śakti samāviṣṭaḥ  nīyate sat gurum prati tena prāpta viveka uttha jñāna saṃpūrṇa mānasaḥ dārḍhya saṃvāda rūḍhi ādeḥ yiyāsuḥ bhavati sphuṭam uktam nandiśikhātantre prācya ṣaṭke maheśinā abhilāṣaḥ śive deve paśūnām bhavate tadā yadā śaiva abhimānena yuktā vai paramāṇavaḥ tadā eva te vimuktāḥ tu dīkṣitā guruṇā yatas  prāpti mātrāt ca te siddha sādhyā iti hi gamyate tam ārādhya iti tu granthaḥ  manda tīvra eka gocaraḥ navadhā śaktipātaḥ  yam śaṃbhunāthena varṇitaḥ idam sāram iha jñeyam paripūrṇa cit ātmanaḥ prakāśaḥ paramaḥ śaktipātaḥ  vaccheda varjitaḥ tathāvidhaḥ pi bhoga aṃśa avacchedena upalakṣitaḥ aparaḥ śaktipātaḥ  sau paryante śiva tā pradaḥ ubhayatra api karma ādeḥ māyā antar vartinaḥ  yatas  na asti vyāpāra iti evam nirapekṣaḥ sa sarvatas  tena māyā antarāle ye rudrā ye ca tad ūrdhvatas  sva adhikāra kṣaye taiḥ taiḥ bhairavībhūyate haṭhāt  ye māyayā hi anākrāntāḥ te karma ādi anapekṣiṇaḥ śaktipāta vaśāt eva tām tām siddhim upāśritāḥ nanu pūjā japa dhyāna śaṃkarā sevana ādibhiḥ te mantra ādi tvam āpannāḥ katham karma anapekṣiṇaḥ mā evam tathāvidha uttīrṇa śiva dhyāna japa ādiṣu pravṛttiḥ eva prathamam eṣām kasmāt vivicyatām karma tad sāmya vairāgya mala pāka ādi dūṣitam īśvara icchā nimittam ced śakti pāta eka hetu tā japa ādikā kriyāśaktiḥ eva ittham na tu karma tad  karma tad loka rūḍham hi yad bhogam avaram dadat  tirodhatte bhoktṛ rūpam saṃjñāyā tu na naḥ bharaḥ teṣām bhoga utka tā kasmāt iti ced dattam uttaram citra ākāra prakāśaḥ  yam svatantraḥ parameśvaraḥ svātantryāt tu tirobhāva bandhaḥ  bhoge sya bhoktṛtām puṣṇan svam rūpam eva syāt mala karma ādi varjitam uktam sā iyam kriyāśaktiḥ śivasya paśu vartinī bandhayitrī iti tad karma kathyate rūpala upa kṛt  jñātā sā ca kriyāśaktiḥ sadyas  siddhi upapādikā avicchinna sva ātma saṃvid prathā siddhiḥ iha ucyate sā bhoga mokṣa svātantrya mahā lakṣmīḥ iha akṣayā viṣṇu ādi rūpa tā deve yā kācid sā nija ātmanā bheda yoga vaśāt māyā pada madhya vyavasthitā tena tad rūpa tā yogāt śaktipātaḥ sthitaḥ  pi san tāvantam bhogam ādhatte paryante śiva tām na tu yathā svātantryataḥ  rājā api anugṛhṇāti kaṃcana īśa śakti samāveśāt tathā viṣṇu ādayaḥ  pyalam māyā garbha adhikārīya śaktipāta vaśāt tatas  kaḥ  pi pradhāna puruṣa vivekī prakṛteḥ gataḥ utkṛṣṭāt tata eva āśu kaḥ  pi buddhā viveki tām kṣaṇāt puṃsaḥ kalāyāḥ ca puṃmāya antara vedakaḥ kalā āśrayasya api atyantam karmaṇaḥ  vinivartanāt  jñānākalaḥ prāktanaḥ tu karmī tasya āśraya sthiteḥ sa param prakṛteḥ budhne sṛṣṭim na āyāti jātucit  māyā dhare tu sṛjyeta ananta īśena pracodanāt  vijñānākalatām prāptaḥ kevalāt adhikārataḥ malāt mantra tad īśa ādi bhāvam eti sadā śivāt  patyuḥ parasmāt yaḥ tu eṣa śaktipātaḥ sa vai malāt  ajñāna ākhyāt viyoktā iti śiva bhāva prakāśakaḥ na anyena śiva bhāvaḥ  hi kenacid saṃprakāśate svacchandaśāstre tena uktam vādinām tu śata trayam triṣaṣṭi abhyadhikam bhrāntam vaiṣṇava ādyam niśā antare śiva jñānam kevalam ca śiva tā āpatti dāyakam śiva tā patti paryantaḥ śaktipātaḥ ca carcyate anyathā kim hi tad syāt yad śaivyā śaktyā anadhiṣṭhitam tena iha vaiṣṇava ādīnām na adhikāraḥ kathaṃcana te hi bheda eka vṛtti tvāt abhede dūra varjitāḥ svātantryāt tu maheśasya te pi ced śivatā unmukhāḥ dviguṇā saṃskriyāsti eṣām liṅga uddhṛtya atha dīkṣayā duṣṭa adhivāsa vigame puṣpaiḥ kumbhaḥ  dhivāsyate dviguṇā u sya sa saṃskāraḥ  na ittham śuddhe ghaṭe vidhiḥ ittham śrī śaktipātaḥ  yam nirapekṣa iha uditaḥ anayā eva diśā na iyam mataṅga kiraṇa ādikam grantha gaurava bhītyā tu tad likhitvā na yojitam purāṇe pi ca tasya eva prasādāt bhaktiḥ iṣyate yayā yānti parām siddhim tad bhāva gata mānasāḥ eva kāreṇa karma ādi sāpekṣa tvam niṣidhyate prasādaḥ  nirmalībhāvaḥ tena saṃpūrṇa rūpa tā ātmanā tena hi śivaḥ svayam pūrṇaḥ prakāśate śivībhāva mahā siddhi sparśavandhye tu kutracid  vaiṣṇava ādau hi yā bhaktiḥ na asau kevalataḥ śivāt  śivaḥ  bhavati tatra eṣa kāraṇam na tu kevalaḥ nirmalaḥ ca api tu prāpta avacchid karma ādi apekṣakaḥ yayā yānti parām siddhim iti asya idam tu jīvitam śrīmān utpaladevaḥ ca api asmākam paramaḥ  guruḥ śaktipāta samaye vicāraṇam prāptam īśa na karoṣi karhicit  adya mām prati kim āgatam yatas  sva prakāśana vidhau vilambase karhicit prāpta śabdābhyām anapekṣi tvam ūcivān durlabha tvam arāgi tvam śaktipāta vidhau vibhoḥ apara ardhena tasya eva śaktipātasya citra tām vyavadhāna cira kṣipra bheda ādyaiḥ upavarṇitaiḥ śrīmatā api aniruddhena śaktim unmīlinīm vibhoḥ vyācakṣāṇena mātaṅge varṇitā nirapekṣatā sthāvara ante pi devasya svarūpa unmīlana ātmikā śaktiḥ patantī sa apekṣā na kvāpi iti su vistarāt  evam vicitre pyetasmin śaktipāte sthite sati tāratamya ādibhiḥ bhedaiḥ samayi ādi vicitra tā kaścid rudrā śatā mātra āpādanāt tad prasādataḥ śiva tvam kramaśas  gacchet  samayī yaḥ  nirūpyate kaścid śuddha adhva bandhaḥ san putrakaḥ śīghram akramāt  bhoga vyavadhinā kaḥ  pi sādhakaḥ cira śīghrataḥ kaścid saṃpūrṇa kartavyaḥ kṛtya pañcaka bhāgini rūpe sthitaḥ  guruḥ saḥ  pi bhoga mokṣa ādi bheda bhāj  samayi ādi catuṣkasya samāsa vyāsa yogataḥ krama ākrama ādibhiḥ bhedaiḥ śaktipātasya citra tā kramikaḥ śaktipātaḥ ca siddhānte vāmake tatas  dakṣe mate kule kaule ṣaṣ ardhe hṛdaye tatas  ullaṅghana vaśāt vā api jhaṭitya kramam eva vā uktam śrī bhairava kule pañcadīkṣā susaṃskṛtaḥ guruḥ ullaṅghita adhas stha srotā vai trika śāstra gaḥ jñāna ācāra ādi bhedena hi uttara adhara tā vibhuḥ śāstreṣu ad īdṛśat śrīmat sarva ācāra hṛd ādiṣu vāma mārga abhiṣiktaḥ tu daiśikaḥ para tattva vid  tathā api bhairave tantre punar  saṃskāram arhati śaiva vaimala siddhāntā ārhatāḥ kārukāḥ ca ye sarve te paśavaḥ  jñeyā bhairave mātṛ maṇḍale kula kālī vidhau ca uktam vaiṣṇavānā viśeṣataḥ bhasma niṣṭhā prapannānām ityādau na eva yogya tā svacchandaśāstre saṃkṣepāt uktam ca śrīmaheśinā anya śāstra rataḥ  yaḥ tu na asau siddhi phala pradaḥ samayi ādi kramāt labdha abhiṣekaḥ  hi guruḥ mataḥ sa ca śakti vaśāt ittham vaiṣṇava ādiṣu kaḥ  nu ayaḥ chadma apaśravaṇa ādyaiḥ tu tad jñānam gṛhṇataḥ  bhavet  prāyaścittam atas tādṛś adhikārī atra kim bhavet  phala ākāṅkṣā yutaḥ śiṣyaḥ tad eka āyatta siddhikaḥ dhruvam pacyeta narake prāyaścitti upasevanāt  tirobhāva prakāraḥ  yam yattādṛśi niyojitaḥ gurau śivena tad bhaktiḥ śaktipātaḥ  sya na ucyate yadātu vaicitrya vaśāt jānīyāt tasya tādṛśam viparīta pravṛtta tvam jñānam tasmāt upāharet  tam ca tyajet pāpa vṛttim bhavet tu jñāna tatparaḥ yathā caurāt gṛhītvā artham tam nigṛhṇāti bhūpatiḥ vaiṣṇava ādeḥ tathā śaivam jñānam āhṛtya sanmatiḥ sa hi bheda eka vṛtti tvam śiva jñāne śrute pyalam na ujjhati iti dṛḍham vāma adhiṣṭhitaḥ tad paśu uttamaḥ śivena eva tirobhāvya sthāpitaḥ  niyateḥ balāt  kathaṅkāram pati padam prayātu para tantritaḥ svacchandaśāstre proktam ca vaiṣṇava ādiṣu ye ratāḥ bhramayati eva tān māyā hi amokṣe mokṣa lipsayā vaiṣṇava ādiḥ śaivaśāstram melayat nija śāsane dhruvam saṃśayam āpanna ubhaya bhraṣṭa tām vrajet  sva dṛṣṭau para dṛṣṭau ca samaya ullaṅghanāt asau pratyavāyam yatas  bhyeti caret tad na īdṛśam kramam uktam śrīmat gahvare ca parameśena tādṛśam na anya śāstra abhiyuktaṣu śiva jñānam prakāśate tad na saiddhāntikaḥ  vāme na asau dakṣe sa naḥ mate kula kaule trike na asau pūrvaḥ pūrvaḥ paratra tu avacchinnaḥ nava  chedam naḥ vetti ānantya saṃsthitaḥ sarvaṃsa hastataḥ dhaḥstha ūrdhva sthaḥ  dhikṛtaḥ  guruḥ sva ātmīya adhara saṃsparśāt prāṇayan  adharāḥ kriyāḥ saphalīkurute yad tad ūrdhva sthaḥ  guruḥ uttamaḥ adhas stha dṛś sthaḥ  pyeta adṛś guru sevī bhavet sa yaḥ tādṛś śakti nipāta iddhaḥ  yaḥ  drāk ūrdhvam imam nayet  tad tad giri nadī prāya avacchinne kṣetra pīṭhake uttarottara vijñāne na adhi kārya dharaḥ  dharaḥ uttarottaram ācāryam vidan  api adharaḥ  dharaḥ kurvan  adhikriyām śāstra laṅghī nigraha bhājanam śaktipāta balāt eva jñāna yogya vicitra tā śrautam cintā mayam dvi ātma bhāvanā mayam eva ca jñānam tad uttaram jyāyaḥ yatas  mokṣa eka kāraṇam tattvebhya uddhṛtim kvāpi yojanam sakale kale katham kuryāt vinā jñānam bhāvanā mayam uttamam yogī tu prāpta tad tattva siddhiḥ api uttame pade sadāśiva ādye su abhyasta jñāni tvāt eva yojakaḥ adhareṣu ca tattveṣu yā siddhiḥ yoga jāsya sā vimocanāyām na upāyaḥ sthitā api dhana dāravat yaḥ tu utpanna samasta adhva siddhiḥ sa hi sadāśivaḥ sākṣāt eṣa katham martyāt mocayet gurutām vrajan tena uktam mālinītantre vicārya jñānayogite yatas ca mokṣa daḥ proktaḥ su abhyasta jñānavān budhaiḥ tasmāt su abhyasta vijñāna tā eva ekam guru lakṣaṇam vibhāgaḥ tu eṣa me proktaḥ śaṃbhunāthena darśyate mokṣa jñāna paraḥ kuryāt gurum su abhyasta vedanam anyam tyajet prāptam api tathā ca uktam śivena tad  āmoda arthī yathā bhṛṅgaḥ puṣpāt puṣpa antaram vrajet  vijñāna arthī tathā śiṣyaḥ  guroḥ guḥ u antaram vrajet  śakti hīnam gurum prāpya mokṣa jñāne katham śrayet  naṣṭa mūle drume devi kutas  puṣpa phala ādikam uttarottaram utkarṣa lakṣmīm paśyan  api sthitaḥ adhame yaḥ pade tasmāt kaḥ nyaḥ syāt daiva dagdhakaḥ yaḥ tu bhogam ca mokṣam ca vāñchet vijñānam eva ca su abhyasta jñāninam yoga siddham sa gurum āśrayet  tad abhāve tu vijñāna mokṣayoḥ jñāninam śrayet  bhukti aṃśe yoginam yaḥ tad phalam dātum bhavet kṣamaḥ phala dāna akṣame yogini apāya eka upadeśini varam jñānī yaḥ  bhyupāyam diśet apica mocayet  jñānī na pūrṇa eva ekaḥ  yadi hi aṃśa aṃśikā kramāt jñānāni ādāya vijñānam kurvīta akhaṇḍa maṇḍalam tena asaṃkhyān gurūn kuryāt pūraṇāya sva saṃvidaḥ dhanyaḥ tu pūrṇa vijñānam jñāna arthī labhate gurum nānā guru āgama srotaḥ pratibhā mātra miśritam kṛtvā jñāna arṇavam svābhiḥ vipruṅgiḥ plāvayet na kim ā tapanāt moṭaka antam yasya me sti gurukramaḥ tasya me sarva śiṣyasya na upadeśa daridra tā śrīmatā kallaṭena ittham guruṇā tu nyarūpyata aham api ata eva adhas śāstra dṛṣṭi kutūhalāt tārkika śrauta bauddha arhat vaiṣṇavādīnna seviṣi loka adhyātma ati mārga ādi karma yoga vidhānataḥ saṃbodha utkarṣa bāhulyāt krama utkṛṣṭān vibhāvayet śrī pūrvaśāstre praṣṭāraḥ  munayaḥ  nārada ādayaḥ prāk vaiṣṇavāḥ saugatāḥ ca siddhānta ādi vidaḥ tatas  kramāt trika artha vijñāna candra utsukita dṛṣṭayaḥ tasmāt na guru bhūyaḥ tve viśaṅketa kadācana guru antara rate mūḍhe āgama antara sevake pratyavāyaḥ  ya āmnātaḥ sa ittham iti gṛhyatām yaḥ  yatra śāstre dhikṛtaḥ sa tatra guruḥ ucyate tatra anadhikṛtaḥ  yaḥ tu tad guru antaram ucyate yathā tad maṇḍala āsīnaḥ  maṇḍala antara bhūpatim sva maṇḍala jigīṣuḥ san sevamānaḥ  vinaśyati tathā uttara uttara jñāna siddhi prepsuḥ samāśrayan adharādharam ācāryam vināśam adhigacchati evam eva ūrdhva vartiṣṇoḥ āgamāt siddhi vāñchakaḥ māyīya śāstra nirataḥ  vināśam pratipadyate uktam ca śrīmat ānande karma saṃśritya bhāvataḥ jugupsate tad tasmin  ca viphale nyat samāśrayet  dināt dinam hrasan  tu evam pacyate raurava ādiṣu yaḥ tu ūrdhva ūrdhva patha prepsuḥ adharam gurum āgamam jihāset śaktipātena sa dhanyaḥ pronmukhīkṛtaḥ ata eva iha śāstreṣu śaiveṣu eva nirūpyate śāstra antara arthān āśvaḥ tān prati saṃskāra kaḥ vidhiḥ atas ca api uttamam śaivam yaḥ  nyatra patitaḥ sa hi iha anugrāhya ūrdhva ūrdhvam na itas tu patitaḥ kvacid  ata eva hi sarvajñaiḥ brahma viṣṇu ādibhiḥ nije na śāsane samāmnātam liṅga uddhāra ādi kiṃcana ittham viṣṇu ādayaḥ śaiva parama artha eka vedinaḥ kāṃścid prati tathā ādikṣuḥ te mohāt vimatim śritāḥ tathāvidhām eva matim satya saṃsparśana akṣamām dṛṣṭvā eṣām brahma viṣṇu ādyaiḥ buddhaiḥ api tathā uditam iti eṣa yukti āgamataḥ śaktipātaḥ  vivecitaḥ  ch atha śrī tantrāloke caturdaśam āhnikam tirobhāva svarūpam tu kathyamānam vivicyatām svabhāvāt  parameśānaḥ  niyati aniyatikramam spṛśan prakāśate yena tatas  svacchanda ucyate niyatim karma phalayoḥ āśritya eṣa maheśvaraḥ sṛṣṭi saṃsthiti saṃhārān vidhatte vā antara sthitīn mahā sarge punar  sṛṣṭi saṃhāra ānantya śālini ekaḥ sa devaḥ  viśvātmā niyati tyāgataḥ prabhuḥ avāntare yā ca sṛṣṭiḥ sthitiḥ ca atra api ayantritam na ujjhati eṣa vapuḥ tyakta niyatiḥ ca sthitaḥ  tra tad  niyatya eva yadā ca eṣa svarūpa ācchādana kramāt  bhuṅkte duḥkha vimoha ādi tadā karma phala kramaḥ tyaktvā tu niyamam kārmam duḥkha moha parīta tām bibhāsayiṣuḥ āste yam tirodhāne napekṣakaḥ yathā prakāśa svātantryāt  pratibuddhaḥ  pyabuddhavat  āste tadvat anuttīrṇaḥ  pyuttīrṇa iva ceṣṭate yathā ca buddhaḥ tām mūḍha ceṣṭām kurvan  api dviṣan hṛdi āḥ te mūḍha evam hi prabuddhānām viceṣṭitam śrī vidyā adhipatiḥ ca āha māna stotre tad īdṛśam ye yauṣmāke śāsana mārge kṛta dīkṣāḥ saṃgacchantaḥ  moha vaśāt vipratipattim nūnam teṣā na asti bhavat bhānu niyogaḥ saṅkocaḥ kim sūrya karaiḥ tāmarasānām jñāta jñeyā dhātṛ pada sthā api santaḥ  ye tvad mārgāt kāpatha gāste pi na samyaka prāyas teṣām laiṅgika buddhi ādi samutthaḥ  mithyā bodhaḥ sarpa vasā ādīpaja kalpaḥ yasmāt viddham sūtaka mukhyena nu tāmram tad yad bhūyas  svām prakṛtim naḥ samupeyāt  naḥ taiḥ pītam bhū tala saṃsthaiḥ amṛtam tad yeṣām tṛṣ kṣudh duḥkha vibādhāḥ punar asmin tatas  prabuddha ceṣṭā asau mantra caryā arcanā ādikā dveṣa iddhā antar dahati enam dāhaḥ śaṅkā eva sā yatas  na ca asya karma mahimā tādṛś yena ittham āsta saḥ kim hi tad karma kasmāt vā pūrveṇa atra samaḥ  vidhiḥ tasmāt sā parameśa icchā yayāyam mohitaḥ tathā ananta kāla saṃvedya duḥkha pātra tvam īhate tatra api ca icchā vaicitryāt iha amutra ubhaya ātmakaḥ duḥkhasya api vibhedaḥ  sti cira śaighrya kṛtaḥ tathā kāla kāma andhaka ādīnām paulastya pura vāsinām tathā anyeṣām tirobhāvaḥ tāvat duḥkhaḥ  hi amutra ca anyaḥ  pi ca tirobhāvaḥ samaya ullaṅghana ātmakaḥ yad uktam parameśena śrīmat ānanda gahvare samaya ullaṅghanāt devi kravyāda tvam śatam samāḥ tatra api manda tīvra ādi bhedāt bahuvidhaḥ kramaḥ svātantryāt ca maheśasya tirobhūtaḥ  pyasau svayam para dvāreṇa vā abhyeti bhūyaḥ nugraham api alam bhūyaḥ nugrahataḥ prāyaścitta ādi ācaraṇe sati anusāreṇa dīkṣā ādau kṛte syāt śiva tāmayaḥ tirobhūtaḥ pareta asuḥ api bandhu suhṛd gurūn ālambya śaktipātena dīkṣā ādyaiḥ anugṛhyate tatra api kāla śīghratva ciratva ādi vibheda tām tathā eti śaktipātaḥ  sau yena āyāti śiva ātma tām ittham sṛṣṭi sthiti dhvaṃsa tirobhāvam anugrahaḥ iti pañcasu kartṛ tvam śiva tvam saṃvid ātmanaḥ pañca kṛtya svatantratva saṃpūrṇa sva ātma māninaḥ yoginaḥ  rcā japa dhyāna yogāḥ saṃsyuḥ sadā uditāḥ aindrajālika vṛttānte na rajyeta kadācana sādāśivaḥ  pi yaḥ  bhogaḥ  bandhaḥ saḥ  pyucita ātmanām jñātṛ tvam eva śiva tā svātantryam tad iha ucyate kulālavat tu kartṛ tvam na mukhyam tad adhiṣṭhiteḥ iti jñātvā grahītavyā na eva jātu api khaṇḍanā śivaḥ  ham ced mad icchā anuvarti kim na jagattu iti mama icchām anuvartantām iti atra ahaṃvidi sphuret  śivaḥ  vā parameśānaḥ  deha ādiḥ atha nirmitaḥ śivasya tāvat asti etad dehaḥ tu eṣa tathā tvayā kṛtaḥ kā anyā deha tā asya tad kim syāt vācya tā padam uktam ca siddha santāna śrīmat ūrmi mahā kule pavana bhramaṇa prāṇa vikṣepa ādi kṛta śramāḥ kuhaka ādiṣu ye bhrāntāḥ te bhrāntāḥ parame pade sarvatra bahu mānena yā api utkrāntiḥ vimuktaye proktā sā sāra śāstreṣu bhoga upāya tayā uditā yadi sarva gatā devaḥ  vada utkramya kva yāsyati atha asarva gataḥ tarhi ghaṭa tulyaḥ tadā bhavet  utkrānti vidhi yogaḥ  yam eka deśena kathyate niraṃśe śiva tattve tu katham utkrānti saṃgatiḥ yathā dharā ādau vāyu ante bhṛgu ambu agni upavāsakaiḥ ātmanaḥ  yojanam vyomni tadvat utkrānti vartanā tasmāt na utkramayet jīvam para tattva samīhayā śrī pūrvaśāstre tu uktam yad utkrānteḥ lakṣaṇam na tad  mukti upāya tayā kiṃtu bhoga hānyai tathā eṣaṇāt  japa dhyāna ādi saṃsiddhaḥ svātantryāt śaktipātatas bhogam prati viraktaḥ ced ittham deham tyajet iti svacchanda mṛtyoḥ api yad  bhīṣma ādeḥ śrūyate kila bhoga vairasya saṃprāptau jīvita anta upasarpaṇam yoga mantra amṛta dravya vara ādyaiḥ siddhi bhāj tanuḥ hātum na hi anyathā śakyā vinā ukta krama yogataḥ uktam ca mālinītantre parameśena tādṛśam sarvam api athavā bhogam manyamānaḥ  virūpakam ityādi vadatā sarvaiḥ alakṣya antar sa tattvakam evam sṛṣṭi ādi kartavya sva svātantrya upadeśanam yad sā eva mukhya dīkṣā syāt śiṣyasya śiva dāyinī uktam śrī niśicāre ca bhairavīyeṇa tejasā vyāptam viśvam prapaśyanti vikalpa ujjhita cetasaḥ vikalpa yukta cittaḥ tu piṇḍa pātāt śivam vrajet  bāhya dīkṣā ādi yogena caryā samaya kalpanaiḥ avikalpaḥ tathā adya eva jīvanmuktaḥ  na saṃśayaḥ saṃsāra jīrṇa taru mūla kalāpa kalpa saṃkalpa sāntara tayā parama artha vahneḥ syuḥ visphuliṅga kaṇikā api ced tad ante dedīpyate vimala bodha hutāśa rāśiḥ ittham dīkṣā upakramaḥ  yam darśitaḥ śāstra saṃmataḥ  ch atha śrī tantrāloke pañcadaśam āhnikam atha etad upayogāya yāgaḥ tāvat nirūpyate tatra dīkṣā eva bhoge ca muktau ca āyāti upāya tām svayam saṃskāra yogāt vā tad aṅgam tad pradarśyate yaḥ  yatra abhilaṣet bhogān sa tatra eva niyojitaḥ siddhi bhāj mantra śaktyā iti śrīmat svāyaṃbhuve vibhuḥ yogyatauvaśataḥ  yatra vāsanā yasya tatra saḥ yojyaḥ  na cyavate tasmāt iti śrī mālinīmate vadan bhoga ādi upāya tvam dīkṣāyāḥ prāha naḥ guruḥ na ca adhikāritā dīkṣām vinā yoge sti śāṅkare na ca yoga adhikāri tvam ekam eva anayā bhavet  api mantra adhikāri tvam muktiḥ ca śiva dīkṣayā iti asmin mālinī vākye sākṣāt mokṣa abhyupāya tā dīkṣāyāḥ kathitā prācya granthena punar ucyate pāramparyeṇa saṃskṛtyā mokṣa bhoga abhyupāya tā yeṣā m adhyavasāyaḥ  sti na vidyām pratyaśaktitaḥ sukha upāyam idam teṣām vidhānam uditam guroḥ iti śrīmat mataṅga ākhye hi uktā mokṣa abhyupāya tā samyak jñāna svabhāvā hi vidyā sākṣāt vimocikā uktam tatra eva tattvānām kārya kāraṇa bhāvataḥ heya ādeyatva kathane vidyā pāda iti sphuṭam tatra aśaktāḥ tu ye teṣām dīkṣā caryā samādhayaḥ te vidyā pūrvakā yasmāt tasmāt jñāni uttama uttamaḥ jñānam ca śāstrāt tad ca api śrāvyaḥ  na adīkṣitaḥ  yatas  atas  sya saṃskriyā mātra upayogaḥ  dīkṣayā kṛtaḥ yatra tatra astu guruṇā yojitaḥ  sau phalam punar  sva vijñāna ucitam yāti jñāni iti uktam purā kila yasya tu īśa prasādena divyā kācana yogya tā guroḥ śiśoḥ ca tau na eva prati dīkṣā upayogi tā jñānam eva tadā dīkṣā śrī traiśika nirūpaṇāt  sarva śāstra artha vettṛ tvam akasmāt ca asya jāyate iti śrī mālinīni ityā yaḥ sāṃsiddhika saṃvidaḥ sa uttama adhikārī syāt jñānavān hi guruḥ mataḥ ātmane vā parebhyaḥ  vā hita arthī cetayet idam iti uktyā mālinīśāstre tad sarvam prakaṭīkṛtam jñāna yogyāḥ tathā kecid caryā yogyāḥ tathā apare dīkṣā yogyā yoga yogyā iti śrīkairaṇe vidhau tatra ukta lakṣaṇaḥ karma yoga jñāna viśāradaḥ uttara uttara tābhūmi utkṛṣṭaḥ  guruḥ udīritaḥ sa ca prāc ukta śakti anyatama pāta pa vitritam parīkṣya pṛṣṭvā vā śiṣyam dīkṣā karma samācaret  uktam svacchandaśāstre ca śiṣyam pṛcchet guruḥ svayam phalam prārthayase yādṛś ta adṛś sādhanam ārabhe vāsanā bhedataḥ sādhya prāptiḥ mantra pracoditā mantramudrā adhva dravyāṇām home sādhāraṇā sthitiḥ vāsanā bhedataḥ  bhinnam śiṣyāṇām ca guroḥ phalam sādhakaḥ  dvividhaḥ śaivadharmā loka ujjhita sthitiḥ loka dharmī phala akāṃkṣī śubha sthaḥ ca aśubha ujjhitaḥ dvidhā mumukṣuḥ nirbījaḥ samaya ādi vivarjitaḥ bāla bāliśa vṛddha strī bhoga bhuj vyādhita ādikaḥ anyaḥ sa bījaḥ  yasya ittham dīkṣā uktā śiva śāsane vidvat dvandvasahānām tu sa bījā samaya ātmikā dīkṣā anugrāhikā pālyā viśeṣa samayāḥ tu taiḥ abhāvam bhāvayet samyak karmaṇām prācya bhāvinām mumukṣoḥ nirapekṣasya prārabdhrekam na śādhayet  sādhakasya tu bhūti artham ittham eva viśodhayet  śiva dharmiṇī asau dīkṣā loka dharma apahāriṇī adharma rūpiṇām eva na śubhānām tu śodhanam loka dharmiṇī asau dīkṣā mantra ārādhana varjitā prārabdha deha bhede tu bhuṅkte sāvaṇim ādikam bhuktvā ūrdhvam yāti yatra eṣa yuktaḥ  tha sakale kale samaya ācāra pāśam tu nirbījāyām viśodhayet  dīkṣā mātreṇa muktiḥ syāt bhaktyā deve gurau sadā sadyonirvāṇa dā sā iyam nirbījā yā iti bhaṇyate atīta anāgata ārabdha pāśa traya viyojikā dīkṣā avasāne śuddhasya dehatyāge param padam dehatyāge sa bījāyām karma abhāvāt vipadyate samaya ācāra pāśam tu dīkṣitaḥ pālayet sadā evam pṛṣṭvā parijñāya vicārya ca guruḥ svayam ucitām saṃvidhitsuḥ tām vāsanām tādṛśīm śrayet  āyāta śaktipātasya dīkṣām prati na daiśikaḥ avajñām vidadhīta iti śaṃbhunā ājñā nirūpitā sva dhanena daridrasya kuryāt dīkṣām guruḥ svayam api dūrvā ambubhiḥ yad vā dīkṣāyai bhikṣate śiśuḥ bhikṣā upāttam nijam vā atha dhanam prāk gurave śiśuḥ dadyāt yena viśuddham tad yāga yogya tvam aśnute tatra ādau śiva tā patti svātantrya āveśa eva yaḥ sa eva hi guruḥ kāryaḥ tatas  sau dīkṣaṇe kṣamaḥ śiva tā āveśitā ca asya bahu upāyā pradarśitā kramikā bāhya rūpā tu snāna nyāsa arcana ādibhiḥ bahvīṣu tāsu tāsu eṣa kriyāsu śiva tām hṛdi saṃdadhat dṛḍham abhyeti śiva bhāvam prasanna dhīḥ śivībhūtaḥ  yad yad icchet tad tad kartum samīhate śiva abhimānita upāyaḥ  bāhyaḥ  hetuḥ na mokṣa daḥ śivaḥ  yam śiva eva asmi iti evam ācārya śiṣyayoḥ hetu tadvat tayā dārḍhya abhimānaḥ  mocakaḥ  hi aṇoḥ na adhyātmena vinā bāhyam na adhyātmam bāhya varjitam siddhyet jñāna kriyābhyām tad dvitīyam saṃprakāśate śrī brahmayāmale deva iti tena nyarūpayat  śrīmat ānandaśāstre ca na aśuddhiḥ syāt vipaścitaḥ kintu snānam su vastra tvam tuṣṭi saṃjananam bhavet  tatra prasiddha deha ādi mātṛ nirmala tā kramāt ayatnataḥ ntarantaḥ syāt nairmalya snāyatām tatas  snānam ca devadevasya yad mūrti aṣṭakam ucyate tatra evam mantra dīpte ntarmala dāhe nimajjanam tatra iṣṭa mantra hṛdayaḥ  gaḥ rajaḥ  ntaḥ pada trayam gatvā āgatya bhajet snānam pārthivam dhṛti dāyakam astra mantrita mṛddhūta malaḥ pañcāṅga mantritaiḥ jalaiḥ mūrdhā ādi pāda antam kramāt ākṣālayet tatas  nimajjet sa aṅga mūla ākhyam japannā tad maya tvataḥ utthāya aśeṣa sajjyotiḥ devatā garbham ambare sūryam jalena mālinyā tarpayet viśva tarpakam devān pitṝn munīn yakṣān rakṣāṃsi anyat ca bhautikam sarvam saṃtarpayet prāṇaḥ  vīrya ātmā sa ca bhāskaraḥ tatas  japet parām ekām prāc ukta uccāra yogataḥ ā tad mayatva saṃvitteḥ jala snānam idam matam agni uttham bhasma śastreṇa japtvā mala nivarhaṇam ka vaktra hṛd guhyapade pañcāṅgaiḥ bhasma mantritam bhasma muṣṭim sa aṅga mūla japtām mūrdhni kṣipet tatas  hasta pādau jalena eva prakṣālya ācamana ādikam tarpaṇam japa iti evam bhasma snānam hi taijasam goḥ ajovati anudrikte vāyau hlādini mantra vāc  gati āgati prayoge vā vāyavyam snānam ācaret  amale gagane vyāpinī ekāgrībhūta dṛṣṭikaḥ smaran mantram yadā āsīta kā anyā nirmala tā tatas  yadi vā nirmalāt vyomnaḥ patatā vāriṇā tanum sparśayet mantra japayuṅ nābhasam snānam īdṛśam evam soma arka tejaḥsu śiva bhāvena bhāvanāt  nimajjan dhauta mālinyaḥ kva vā yogyaḥ  na jāyate ātmā eva parameśānaḥ  nirācāra mahā hradaḥ viśvam nimajjya tatra eva tiṣṭhet śuddhaḥ ca śodhakaḥ iti snāna aṣṭakam śuddhau  uttarottaram uttamam sarvatra paścāt tam mantram ekībhūtam upāharet  ghṛtya āpyāya mala ploṣa vīrya vyāpti mṛji sthitīḥ abhedam ca kramāt iti snāna aṣṭaka paraḥ  muniḥ etā hi anugraha ātmānaḥ  mūrtayaḥ ṣṭau śiva ātmikāḥ sva rūpa śiva rūpābhyām dhyānāt tad tad phala pradāḥ anena vidhinā arcāyām kanda ādhāra ādi yojanām kurvan vyāsa samāsābhyām dharā ādeḥ tad phalam bhajet  tathā hi yoga saṃcāre mantrāḥ syuḥ bhuvi pārthivāḥ āpye āpyā yāvat amī śive śiva mayā iti śrī nirmaryāda śāstre pi tad ittham su nirūpitam dharā ādeḥ ca viśeṣaḥ  sti vīra sādhaka saṃmataḥ raṇa reṇuḥ vīra jalam vīra bhasma mahā marut  śmaśāna araṇya gaganam candra arkau tad upāhitau ātmā nirdhūta niḥśeṣa vikalpa ātaṅka su sthitaḥ snāna arcā ādau  iti upāsyam vīrāṇām vigraha aṣṭakam śrī mantri śirasi proktam madya śīdhu surā ādinā su svādunā prasannena tanunā su sugandhinā kandala ādi gatena antar bahis  saṃskāra pañcakam kṛtvā nirīkṣaṇam prokṣya tāḍana āpyāya guṇṭhanam mantra cakrasya tad madhye pūjām vipruṣ pratarpaṇam tena ātma sekaḥ kalaśa mudrayā ca abhiṣecanam devatā tarpaṇam deha prāṇa ubhaya patha āśritam sarva tīrtha tapaḥ yajña dāna ādi phalam aśnute madya snāne sādhaka indraḥ  mumukṣuḥ kevalī bhavet  yatas  śiva mayam madyam sarve mantrāḥ śiva udbhavāḥ śiva śaktyoḥ na bhedaḥ  sti śakti utthāstu marīcayaḥ tāsām ānanda janakam madyam śiva mayam tatas  prabuddhe saṃvidaḥ pūrṇe rūpe dhikṛti bhājanam mantra dhyāna samādhāna bhedāt snānam tu yad na tad  yuktam snānam yatas  nyāsa karma ādau yogyatā āvaham asya snāna aṣṭakasya asti bāhya antara tayā dvitā āntaram tad yathā ūrdhva indu dhārā amṛta pariplavaḥ yatas  randhra ūrdhva gāḥ sārdham aṅgulam vyāpya saṃsthitāḥ mūrtayaḥ ṣṭau  api proktāḥ pratyekam dvādaśāntatas eṣām ekatamam snānam kuryāt dvi tri ādiśaḥ pivā iti snāna vidhiḥ proktaḥ  bhairaveṇa amalīkṛtau snāna anantara kartavyam atha idam upadiśyate bhāvam prasannam ālocya vrajet yāga gṛham tatas  parvata agra nadī tīra eka liṅga ādi yad ucyate tad bāhyam iha tad siddhi viśeṣāya na muktaye ābhyantaram naga agra ādi dehāntaḥ prāṇa yojanam sādhakānām upāyaḥ syāt siddhaye na tu muktaye pīṭha sthānam sadā yāga yogyam śāstreṣu bhaṇyate tad ca bāhya antarāt rūpāt bahis dehe ca su sphuṭam yatas  śrī naiśasañcāre parameśaḥ  nyarūpayat  tasya icchā pīṭham ādhāraḥ  yatrastham sacarācaram agryam tad kāmarūpam syāt bindu nāda dvayam tatas  nāda pīṭham pūrṇa giriḥ dakṣiṇe vāmatas  punar  pīṭham uḍḍayanam binduḥ mukhyam pīṭha trayam tu idam jñeyam saṃkalpanā rūpam ardha pīṭham atas  param śāktam kuṇḍalinī veda kalam ca tri upapīṭhakam devī koṭṭa ujjayinyau dve tathā kulagiriḥ paraḥ lālanam baindavam vyāptiḥ iti saṃdohaka trayam puṇḍravardhana vāra indre tathā ekāmram idam bahis  navadhā kathitam pīṭham antar bāhya krameṇa tad  kṣetra aṣṭakam kṣetra vidaḥ  hṛd ambhoja dala aṣṭakam prayāgaḥ  varaṇā paścāt aṭṭahāsaḥ  jayantikā vārāṇasī ca kāliṅgam kulūtā lāhulā tathā upakṣetra aṣṭakam prāhuḥ hṛd padma agra dala aṣṭakam virajaiḥ uḍikā hālā elā pūḥ kṣīrikā purī māyā ākhyā maru deśaḥ ca bāhya abhyantara rūpataḥ hṛd padma dala sandhīnām upasaṃdohaka aṣṭa tā jālandharam ca naipālam kaśmīrā gargikā haraḥ mleccha diś dvāra vṛttiḥ ca kurukṣetram ca kheṭakam dvi patham dvaya saṃghaṭṭāt tri patham traya melakāt  catuṣpatham śaktimataḥ  layāt tatra eva manvate nāsā anta tālu randhra antam etad dehe vyavasthitam bhrū madhya kaṇṭha hṛt saṃjñam madhyamam tad udāhṛtam nābhi kanda mahā ānanda dhāma tad kaulikam trayam parvata agram nadī tīram eka liṅgam tad eva ca kim vā ati bahunā sarvam saṃvittau prāṇa gam tatas  tatas  deha sthitam tasmāt deha āyatana gaḥ bhavet  bāhye tu tādṛśa antar stha yoga mārga viśāradāḥ devyaḥ svabhāvāt jāyante pīṭham tad vāhyam ucyate yathā svabhāvataḥ  mlecchā adharma patha vartinaḥ tatra deśe niyatya ittham jñāna yogau sthitau kvacid  yathā cātat mayaḥ  pya iti pāpitām taiḥ samāgamāt  tathā pīṭha sthitaḥ  pya iti jñāna yoga ādi pātra tām mukhya tvena śarīre ntaḥ prāṇe saṃvidi paśyataḥ viśvam etad kim anyaiḥ syāt bahis bhramaṇa ḍambaraiḥ iti evam antar bāhye ca tad tad cakraphala arthinām sthāna bhedaḥ  vicitraḥ ca sa śāstre saṃkhyayā ujjhitaḥ śrī vīra āvali hṛdaye sapta sthānāni śakti kamala yugam sura patha catuṣpatha ākhya śmaśānam ekānta śūnya vṛkṣau ca iti nirvacana guṇa sthiti upacāra dṛśā vibodha eva uktaḥ tad adhiṣṭhite ca cakre śārīre bahis athaḥ bhavet yāgaḥ muktaye tad na yāgasya sthāna bhedaḥ prakalpyate deśa upāyā na sā yasmāt sā hi bhāva prasādataḥ uktam ca śrī niśācāre siddhi sādhana kāṅkṣiṇām sthānam mumukṣuṇā tyājyam sarpa kañcukavat tu idam muktiḥ na sthāna janitā yadā śrotra patham gatam guroḥ tattvam tadā muktiḥ tad dārḍhyāya tu pūjanam yatra yatra hṛd ambhojam vikāsam pratipadyate tatra eva dhāmni bāhye ntaryāga śrīḥ pratitiṣṭhati na anyatra gatyā mokṣaḥ  sti saḥ  jñāna granthi kartanāt tad ca saṃvid vikāsena śrīmat vīra āvalī pade guravaḥ tu vimuktau vā siddhau vā vimalā matiḥ hetuḥ iti ubhayatra api yāgaukaḥ  yad manoramam niyati prāṇa tā yogāt sāmagrītaḥ tu yadi api siddhayaḥ bhāva vaimalyam tathā api nikhila uttamam vimalībhūta hṛdayaḥ  yad tatra pratibimbayet  sādhyam tad asya dārḍhyena saphala tvāya kalpate uktam śrī sāraśāstre ca nirvikalpaḥ  hi sidhyati kliśyante sa vikalpāḥ tu kalpa ukte pi kṛte sati tad ā ākramya balam mantrā ayam eva udayaḥ sphuṭaḥ ityādibhiḥ spanda vākyaiḥ etad eva nirūpitam tasmāt siddhyai vimuktyai vā pūjā japa samādhiṣu tad sthānam yatra viśrānti sundaram hṛdayam bhavet  yāgaukaḥ prāpya śuddha ātmā bahis eva vyavasthitaḥ nyāsam sāmānyatas  kuryāt bahiryāga prasiddhaye mātṛkām mālinīm vā atha dvitayam vā kramākramāt  sṛṣṭi apyaya dvayaiḥ kuryāt ekaikam saṃghaśaḥ dviśas  lalāṭa vaktre dṛkkarṇa nāsā gaṇḍarada oṣṭha ge dvaye dvaye śikhā jihve visarga antāḥ tu ṣoḍaśa dakṣa anyayoḥ skandha bāhu kara aṅguli nakhe kacau vargau ṭatau kramāt kaṭyā mūrvā ādiṣu niyojayet  pavargam pārśvayoḥ pṛṣṭhe jaṭhare hṛd yathaḥ nava tvac rakta māṃsa sūtra asthi vasā śukra purogamān iti eṣa mātṛkā nyāsaḥ  mālinyāḥ tu nirūpyate na śikhā ṛ ṝ ḷ ḷḷ ca śiraḥ mālā tha mastakam netrāṇi ca ūrdhve dhaḥ nye ī ghrāṇam mudre ṇu ṇū śrutī baka varga  i ā vaktra danta jihvā giri kramāt  vabhayāḥ kaṇṭha dakṣa ādi skandhayoḥ bhujayoḥ ḍaḍhau ṭhaḥ  hastayoḥ jhañau śākhā jraṭau śūla kapālake pa hṛd chalau stanau kṣīramā sa jīvaḥ  visarga yuj  prāṇaḥ  havarṇaḥ kathitaḥ ṣakṣau  udara nābhi gau maśāntā kaṭi guhya uru yugma gā jānunī tathā eaikārau tad parau tu jaṅghe caraṇa gau daphau iti eṣā mālinī devī śaktimat kṣobhitā yatas  kṛtya āveśāt tatas  śāktī tanuḥ sā paramārthataḥ anyonyam bīja yonīnām kṣobhāt vaisargika udayāt kām kām siddhim na vitaret kim vā nyūnam na pūrayet  yoni bīja arṇa sāṃkaryam bahudhā yadi api sthitam tathā api na ādi phāntaḥ  yam kramaḥ  mukhyaḥ prakīrtitaḥ phakāra ādi samuccārān nakāra ante dhva maṇḍalam saṃhṛtya saṃvidyā pūrṇā sā śabdaiḥ varṇyate katham atas  śāstreṣu bahudhā kula puttalikā ādibhiḥ bhedaiḥ gītā hi mukhyeyam na ādi phānta iti mālinī śabdarāśeḥ bhairavasya yān ucchūna tayā antarī sā mātā iva bhaviṣyat tvāt tena asau mātṛkā uditā mālinī mālitā rudraiḥ dhārikā siddhi mokṣayoḥ phaleṣu puṣpitā pūjyā saṃhāra dhvani ṣaṭpadī saṃhāra dāna ādāna ādi śakti yuktā yatas  ralau eka tvena smaranti iti śaṃbhunāthaḥ nirūcivān śabdarāśiḥ mālinī ca śiva śakti ātmakam tu idam ekaikatra api pūrṇa tvāt śiva śakti svabhāva tā tena bhraṣṭe vidhau vīrye svarūpe vā anayā param mantrā nyastāḥ punar nyāsāt pūryante tad phala pradāḥ uktam śrī pūrvatantre ca viśeṣa vidhi hīnite nyasyet śā akta śarīra artham bhinna yoni tu mālinīm viśeṣaṇam idam hetau hetu arthaḥ ca nirūpitaḥ yatheṣṭa phala siddhyai ca iti atra eva idam abhāṣata sa añjanā api ye mantrā gāruḍa ādyā na te param mālinyā pūritāḥ sidhdyai balāt eva tu muktaye tasmāt phala īpsuḥ api anya mantram nyasya atra mālinīm nyasyet japtvā apica japet ayatnāt apavṛktaye iti evam mātṛkām nyasyet mālinīm vā kramāt dvayam siddhi mukti anusārāt vā varṇān vā yugapad dvayoḥ akṣa hrīm napha hrīm etau piṇḍau saṃghau  iha anayoḥ vācakau nyāsa etābhyām kṛte nyāse thavā ekakaḥ eṣa ca aṅga tanu brahma yuktaḥ  vā tad viparyayaḥ sāmudāyika vinyāse pṛthak  piṇḍau  imau kramāt  akramāt athavā nyasyet ekam eva atha yojayet  kriyayā siddhi kāmaḥ  yaḥ sa kriyām bhūyasīm caret  anīpsuḥ api yaḥ tasmai bhūyase sva phalāya sā yaḥ tu dhyāna japa abhyāsaiḥ siddhīpsuḥ sa kriyām param saṃskṛtyai sva icchayā kuryāt  prāk nayena atha bhūyasīm mumukṣuḥ atha tasmai vā yathā abhīṣṭam samācaret  śiva tā āpattiḥ eva arthaḥ  hi eṣām nyāsa ādi karmaṇām evam nyāsam vidhāya argha pātre vidhim upācaret  ukta nītyā eva tad paścāt  pūjayet nyasta vācakaiḥ yatas  samasta bhāvānām śivāt siddhi mayāt athaḥ pūrṇāda vyatireki tvam kārakāṇām iha arcayā samastam kāraka vrātam śiva abhinnam pradarśitam pūjā udāharaṇe sarvam vyaśnute gamana ādi api yathā hi vāha kaṭaka bhrama svātantryam āgataḥ aśvaḥ saṃgrāma rūḍhaḥ  pi tām śikṣām na ativartate tathā arcana kriyā abhyāsa śivī bhāvita kārakaḥ gacchan  tiṣṭhan  api dvaitam kārakāṇām vyapa ujjhati tathā aikya abhyāsa niṣṭhasyākramāt viśvam idam haṭhāt  saṃpūrṇa śiva tā kṣobha narīnartat iva sphuret  uvāca pūjana stotre hi asmākam paramaḥ  guruḥ ahaḥ svādu rasaḥ kaḥ  pi śiva pūjā āmaya utsavaḥ ṣaṭtriṃśataḥ  pi tattvānām kṣobhaḥ  yatra ullasati alam tad etādṛś pūrṇa śiva viśva āveśāya ye rcanam kurvanti te śivā eva tān pūrṇān prati kim phalam vinā api jñāna yogābhyām kriyā nyāsa arcanādikā ittham aikya samāpatti dānāt para phala pradā sādhakasya api tad sat vipra da mantra ekatām gatam viśvam vrajadavighna tvam svām siddhim śīghram āvahet  uktam ca parameśena na vidhiḥ na arcana kramaḥ kevalam smaraṇāt siddhiḥ vāñchita iti mata ādiṣu tad evam tanmayībhāva dāyinī arcā kriyā yatas  samasta kāraka aikātmyam tena asyāḥ paramam vapuḥ yaṣṭra ādhārasya tādātmyam sthāna śuddhi vidhi kramāt  yaṣṭṛ yājya tad ādhāra karaṇa ādāna saṃpradāḥ nyāsa krameṇa śiva tā tādātmyam adhiśerate arghapātram apādānam tasmāt ādīyate yatas  yad ca tad stham jala ādi etad karaṇam śodhane rcane arghapātra ambu vipruḍbhiḥ spṛṣṭam sarvam hi śudhyati śiva arka kara saṃsparśāt kānyā śuddhiḥ bhaviṣyati ūce śrī pūrvaśāstre tad argha pātra vidhau vibhuḥ na ca asaṃśodhitam vastu kiṃcid api upakalpayet  tena śuddham tu sarvam yad aśuddham api tad śuci aśuddha tā ca vijñeyā paśu tad śāsana āśayāt sva tādavasthyāt pūrvasmāt athavā api upakalpitāt  tena yad yad iha āsannam saṃvid aścit anugrahāt  kiyataḥ  pi tad atyantam yogyam yāge tra jīvavat  anena naya yogena yadā asatti vidūrate saṃvidā iti tadā tatra yogya ayogya tvam ādiśet vīrāṇām ata eva iha mithas  sva pratimā amṛtam tad tad yāgavidha āviṣṭam gurubhiḥ bhāvitātmabhiḥ unmajjayati nirmagnām saṃvidam yad tu suṣṭhu tad  arcāyai yogyam ānandaḥ  yasmāt unmagna tā citaḥ tena acit rūpa deha ādi prādhānya vinimajjakam ānanda jananam pūjā yogyam hṛdaya hāri yad  atas  kula krama uttīrṇa trika sāra mata ādiṣu madyakāt ambarī śīdhu dravya ādeḥ mahimā param loka sthitim racayitum madya ādeḥ paśu śāsane proktā hi aśuddhiḥ tatra eva tasya kvāpi viśuddha tā pañcagavye pavitra tvam soma carṇana pātrayoḥ vidhiḥ ca avabhṛtha snānam haste kṛṣṇa viṣāṇitā na patnyā ca vinā yāgaḥ sarva daivata tulya tā surā āhutiḥ brahma satre vapa antra hṛdaya āhutiḥ pāśaveṣu api śāstreṣu tad adarśi maheśinā ghora āndhya haimana niśā madhya gācira dīptivat  bhakṣyaḥ  haṃsaḥ na bhakṣyaḥ  sau  iti ripratipattiṣu smārtīṣu vijayati ekaḥ  yaḥ śivābheda śuddhikaḥ ajñatva veda ādarśitva rāga dveṣa ādayaḥ  hi amī munīnām vacasi svasmin prāmāṇya unmūlana kṣamāḥ vede pi yad abhakṣyam tad bhakṣyam iti upadiśyate na vidhi pratiṣedha ākhya dharmayoḥ ekam āspadam atha tatra na tad bhakṣyam tadā tena tathā tatas  evam viṣaya bhedāt naḥ śiva ukteḥ bādhikā śrutiḥ kvacid viṣaya tulya tvāt bādhya bādhaka tā yadi tad bādhyā śrutiḥ eva iti prāk eva etad nirūpitam prakṛtam brūmahe kṛtvā nyāsam deha argha pātrayoḥ sāmānyam argha pātra ambhaḥ vipruḍbhiḥ prokṣya ca akhilam yāga upakaraṇam paścāt bāhya yāgam samācaret  prabhā maṇḍalake khe vā su liptāyām ca vā bhuvi triśūla arka vṛṣāndika sthā mātaraḥ kṣetrapam yajet  yoginīḥ ca pṛthak mantraiḥ oṃnamaḥ nāma yojitaiḥ eka uccāreṇa vā bāhya parivāra iti śabditāḥ tāraḥ  nāma caturthī antam namaḥ ca iti arcane manuḥ evam bahis  pūjayitvā dvāram prokṣya prapūjayet  triśiraḥ śāsana ādau ca sa dṛṣṭaḥ  vidhiḥ ucyate gaṇeśa lakṣmyau dvāra ūrdhve dakṣe vāme tayoḥ punar  madhye vāgīśvarīm diṇḍi mahodara yugam tathā kramāt sva dakṣa vāma stham tathā etena krameṇa ca ekaikam pūjayet samyaṅ nandi kālau tri mārga gām kālindīm chāga meṣa āsyau sva dakṣāt dvāḥstha śākhayoḥ adhas dehalī ananta īśa ādhāra śaktīḥ ca pūjayet  dvāra madhye sarasvatyā mahā astram pūjayet amī padma ādhāra gatāḥ sarve pyuditā vighna nāśakāḥ pūjane pūrvavat mantraḥ  dīpaka dvaya kalpitaḥ argha puṣpa samālambha dhūpa naivedya vandanaiḥ pūjām kuryāt iha arghaḥ ca api uttama dravya yojitaḥ eka uccāreṇa vā kuryāt dvāḥstha daivata pūjanam rahasya pūjām ced kuryāt tad bāhya parivārakam dvāḥsthān  ca pūjayet antar deva agre kalpanā kramāt kṣiptvā astra japtam kusumam jvalat veśmani vghna nud  praviśya śivaraśmi iddhadṛśā veśma avalokayet  diśaḥ  streṇa ca badhnīya ācchādayet varmaṇā akhilāḥ tatra uttarāśā abhimukhaḥ  mumukṣuḥ tādṛśāya vā viśet tathā hi aghora agniḥ pāśān pluṣyati bandhakān yadi api asti na diś nāma kācid pūrvā para ādikā pratyayaḥ hi na tasyāḥ syāt ekasya anupāhiteḥ upādhiḥ pūrva tā ādiṣṭa iti ced tad kṛtam diśā upādhi mātram tu tathā vaicitryāya katham bhavet  tasmāt saṃvid prakāśaḥ  yam mūrti ābhāsana bhāgataḥ pūrva ādi diś vibhāga ākhya vaicitrya ullekha durmadaḥ tatra yad yad prakāśena sadā svīkaraṇe kṣamam tad eva ūrdhvam prakāśa ātma sparśa ayogyam adhas  punar  kiṃcid prakāśa tā madhyam tatas  vai diś samudbhavaḥ kiṃcid prakāśa yogyasya saṃmukham prasarat puras  parāṅmukham tu tad paścāt iti diś dvayam āgatam prakāśaḥ saṃmukham vastu gṛhītvā udrikta raśmikaḥ yatra tiṣṭha uddakṣiṇam tad prakāśasya ānukūlyataḥ dakṣiṇasya puras saṃstham vāmam iti upadiśyate tad prakāśita meya indu sparśa saumyam tad eva hi evam āśā ca tuṣke smin madhya viśrānti yogataḥ catuṣkam anyat tena aṣṭau diśaḥ tad tad adhiṣṭhitāḥ evam prakāśa mātre smin vara de parame śive diś vibhāgaḥ sthitaḥ  loke śāstre pica tathā ucyate kramāt sadāśiva adhīśaḥ pañca mantra tanuḥ yatas  īśan raghora vāma ākhya sadyaḥ dhobhedataḥ  diśaḥ īśa ūrdhvam prakāśa tvāt pūrvam vaktram prasāri yad  puruṣaḥ  dakṣiṇā caṇḍaḥ  vāmā vāmaḥ tu saumyakaḥ parāṅmukha tayā sadyas  paścimā paribhāṣyate pātāla vaktram adharama prakāśa tayā sthiteḥ kha marut vahni jala bhūkhāni vaktrāṇi amuṣya hi mukhya tvena kham eva ūrdhvam prakāśa m ayam ucyate tad eva mukhyataḥ dhastāt aprakāśam yatas  sphuṭam madhye tu yad prakāśam tad na prakāśyam na ca itarat  prakāśa tvāt diśyamānam atas  smin diś catuṣṭayam pañca mantra tanuḥ nātha ittham viśva digīśvaraḥ tatas  pīśaḥ tathā rudraḥ  viṣṇuḥ brahmā tathā sthitaḥ ūrdhva abhivyakti ayogya tvāt viṣṇoḥ dhātuḥ ca pañcamam na vaktram tau bheda mayau sṛṣṭi sthiti prabhū yatas  diś vibhāgaḥ tu tad jaḥ  sti vadanānām catuṣṭayāt  pañcamasya yuji tve tau parityakta nija ātmakau tatas  brahmāṇḍa madhye pi jñāna śaktiḥ vibhaḥ raviḥ diśām vibhāgam kurute prakāśa ghana vṛttimān tathā hi viṣuvat yoge yatas  pūrvam pradṛśyate tad pūrva yatra tad chāyā tad paścimam udāhṛtam tasmin jigamiṣa urasya yad savyam tad tu dakṣiṇam tatra eṣa caṇḍa tejobhiḥ bhāti jājvalyamānavat  tad puras varti vāmam tu tad bhāsā kha citam manāk  tatas  eva hi somyam tad na ca api hi aprakāśakam yatra asā  astam abhyeti tad paścimam iti sthitiḥ tatra eva paścime yeṣām prāc prakāśa avalokanam tad eva pūrvam eteṣām yathā adhvani nirūpitam sā sā diś ca tathā tasya phala dā api viparyaye vicitre phala saṃpattiḥ prakāśa adhīnikā yatas  ittham sūrya āśrayā diś syāt sā vicitrā api tādṛśī adhiṣṭhitā maheśena citra tad rūpa dhāriṇā kim vā ati bahunā yaḥ  sau yaṣṭā tad saṃmukha āditaḥ diśaḥ  pi pravibhajyante prāk savya uttara paścimāḥ sva anusāra kṛtam tam ca diś vibhāgam sadā śivaḥ adhitiṣṭhati arkam iva sa vicitra vapuḥ yatas sva utthā api diśaḥ sveśāḥ śakra ādyā hi adhiśerate te hi prakāśa śakti aṃśāḥ prakāśa anuvidhāyinaḥ prakāśasya yad aiśvaryam sa indraḥ  yad tu tad mahaḥ saḥ  gniḥ yantṛtva bhīma tve yamaḥ  rakṣaḥ tadūnimā prakāśyam varuṇaḥ tad ca cāñcalyāt vāyuḥ ucyate bhāva sañcaya yogena vitteśaḥ tad kṣaye vibhuḥ adṛṣṭa vigrahaḥ  nantaḥ  brahma ūrdhve vṛṃhakaḥ  vibhuḥ prakāśasya eva śakti aṃśā lokapāstena kīrtitāḥ ittham svādhīna rūpā api diś saurī tu upadiśyate tatra sarvaḥ  hi niṣkampam prakāśa tvam prapadyate sarva gaḥ pyanilaḥ yadvat vyajanena upavījitaḥ prabuddhaḥ svām kriyām kuryāt dharma nirṇodana ādikām tadvat sarva gatāḥ sarvā aindya ādyāḥ śaktayaḥ sphuṭam sādhaka āśvāsa saṃbuddhāḥ tad tad sva iṣṭa phala pradāḥ evam saurī diś īśāna brahma viṣṇu īśa sauśivaiḥ adhiṣṭhitā samāśvāsa dārḍhyāt tad tad phala pradā sādhakaḥ  yad ca vā kṣetram maṇḍalam veśma vā bhajet  sthitaḥ tad anusāreṇa madhyībhavati śaṃkaraḥ sa hi sarvam adhiṣṭhātā mādhyasthyena iti tasya yaḥ sauraḥ prakāśaḥ tad pūrvam ittham syāt diś vi avasthitiḥ tad madhya sthita nāthasya grahītum dakṣiṇam mahaḥ udaṅmukhaḥ syāt  pāścātyam grahītum pūrvatomukhaḥ upaviśya nija sthāne deha śuddhim samācaret  aṅguṣṭha agrāt kāla vahni jvālā bhāsvaram utthitam astram dhyātvā tad śikhābhiḥ bahis antar dahet tanum dāhaḥ ca dhvaṃsa eva uktaḥ  dhvaṃsakam mantra saṃjñitam tejaḥ tathā abhilāpa ākhya sva vikalpa rasombhitam tena mantra agninā dāha u dehe puryaṣṭake tathā deha puryaṣṭakā hantā vidhvaṃsāt eva jāyate na hi sadbhāva mātreṇa dehaḥ  sau  anya dehavat ahantāyām hi deha tvam sā dhvastā tad dahet dhruvam tad deha saṃskāra bharaḥ  bhasma tvena atha yaḥ sthitaḥ tam varma vāyunā ādhūya tiṣṭhet śuddha cit ātmani tasmin dhruve nistaraṅge samāpattim upāgataḥ saṃvidaḥ sṛṣṭi dharmi tvāt ādyāma iti taraṅgitām sā eva mūrtiḥ iti khyātā tāra sat binduha ātmikā tatas  nava ātma devena nyāsaḥ tattva udaya ātmakaḥ aṅga vaktrāṇi tasya eva sva sthāneṣu niyojayet  atha mātṛkayā prāgvat tad tattva sphuṭatā ātmakaḥ tri tattva nyāsa tā ca asya pṛṣṭhe kakṣyā traya āgate tatas  ghora aṣṭaka nyāsaḥ śiraḥ tad caraṇa ātmakam tatas  pi śiva sadbhāva nyāsaḥ svāṃgasya saṃyutaḥ ittha kṛte pañcake smin yad tad mukhya tayā bhavet  upāsyam arcyam tad sa aṅgam ṣaṣṭhe nyāse niyojayet  tena atra nyāsa yogyaḥ  sau bhagavān rati śekharaḥ ūrdhve nyāsyaḥ  nava ākhyasya mukhya tve nyonya dhāma tā evam bhairava sadbhāva nāthe mukhya tayā yadi upāsyatā tad tad sthāna prāṅnyāsyaḥ  rati śekharaḥ ittham śrī pūrvaśāstre me saṃpradāyam nyarūpayat  śaṃbhunāthaḥ nyāsa vidhau devaḥ  hi katham anyathā nyāsa vivarjyate muṣmin  aṅgāni api asya santi hi mūrtiḥ sṛṣṭiḥ tri tattvam ca iti aṣṭau mūrti aṅga saṃyutāḥ śivaḥ sa aṅgaḥ ca vijñeyaḥ  nyāsaḥ ṣoḍhā prakīrtitaḥ asya upari tatas  śāktam nyāsam kuryāt ca ṣaḍvidham para aparām sa vaktrām prāk tatas  prāk iti mālinīm paścāt para ādi tritayam śikhā hṛd pāda gam kramāt  tatas  ka vaktra kaṇṭheṣu hṛd nābhī guhya  ūrutaḥ jānu pāde pya ghorya ādyam tatas  vidyā aṅga pañcakam tatas tu āvāhayet śaktim mātṛsadbhāva rūpiṇīm yogeśvarīm parām pūrṇām kāla saṃkarṣiṇīm dhruvām aṅga vaktra parīvāra śakti dvādaśaka adhikām sādhya anuṣṭhāna bhedena nyāsa kāle smaret guruḥ para eva devī tritaya madhye yābhedinī sthitā sa anavaccheda cit mātra sadbhāveyam prakīrtitā sāraśāstre yāmale ca devyāḥ tena prakīrtitaḥ mūrtiḥ sa vaktrā śaktiḥ ca śakti trayam atha aṣṭakam pañcāṅgāni parā śaktiḥ nyāsaḥ śāktaḥ  pi ṣaḍvidhaḥ yāmalaḥ  yam mahānyāsaḥ siddhi mukti phala pradaḥ mukti eka arthī punar  pūrvam śāktam nyāsam samācaret  guravaḥ tu āhuḥ ittham yad nyāsa dvayam udāhṛtam mumukṣuṇā tu pāda ādi tad kāryam saṃhṛti kramāt  yāvantaḥ kīrtitā bhedāḥ śaṃbhu śakti aṇu vācakāḥ tāvat su apyeṣu mantreṣu nyāsaḥ ṣoḍhā eva kīrtitaḥ kiṃtu āvāhyaḥ tu yaḥ  mantraḥ sa tatra aṅga samanvitaḥ ṣaṣṭhaḥ syāt iti sarvatra ṣoḍhā eva ayam udāhṛtaḥ mudrā pradarśanam paścāt kāyena manasā girā pañca avasthā jāgrat ādyāḥ ṣaṣṭhī anuttaranāmikā ṣaṣ kāraṇa ṣaḍātma tvāt ṣaṭtriṃśat tattva yojanam evam ṣoḍhāmahānyāse kṛte viśvam idam haṭhāt  dehe tādātmyam āpannam śuddhām sṛṣṭim prakāśayet  mūrti nyāsāt samārabhya yā sṛṣṭiḥ prasṛta atra sā abhedam ānīya kṛtā śuddhā nyāsa bala kramāt  tena ye codayan mūḍhāḥ pāśa dāha vidhūnane kṛte śānte śive rūḍhaḥ punar  kim avarohati iti te dūratas  dhvastāḥ parama artham hi śāṃbhavam na viduḥ ta sva saṃvitti sphurat ta āsāra varjitāḥ na khalu eṣa śivaḥ śāntaḥ  nāma kaścid vibhedavān sarva itara adhva vyāvṛttaḥ  ghaṭa tulyaḥ  sti kutracid  mahā prakāśa rūpā hi yā iyam saṃvid vijṛmbhate sa śivaḥ śiva tā eva asya vaiśvarūpya avabhāsitā tathā ābhāsana yogaḥ  taḥ svarasena asya jṛmbhate bhāsyamānaḥ  tra ca abhedaḥ sva ātmanaḥ  bheda eva ca bhede vijṛmbhite māyā māyā mātuḥ vijṛmbhate abhede jṛmbhate sya eva māyā
