mātuḥ śiva ātma tā māyā pramātā tad rūpa vikalpa abhyāsa pāṭavāt  śiva eva tad abhyāsa phalam nyāsa ādi kīrtitam yathā hi duṣṭa karma asmi iti evam bhāvayataḥ tathā tathā śivaḥ  ham na anyaḥ  smi iti evam bhāvayataḥ tathā etad eva ucyate dārḍhyam vimarśa hṛdayaṅgamam śiva aikātmya vikalpa ogha dvārikā nirvikalpa tā anyathā tasya śuddhasya vimarśa prāṇa vartinaḥ katham nāma avimṛṣṭam syāt rūpam bhāsana dharmaṇaḥ tena ati durghaṭa ghaṭa asvatantra icchā vaśa ādayam bhān api prāṇa buddhi ādiḥ svam tathā na vikalpayet  pratyuta ati svatantra ātma viparīta svadharma tām vināśya nīśa āyattatva rūpām niścitya majjati tatas  saṃsāra bhāgīya tathā niścaya śātinīm nitya ādi niścaya dvārām avikalpām sthitim śrayet  ye tu tīvra tama udrikta śakti nirmala tā juṣaḥ na te dīkṣām anunyāsa kāriṇaḥ ca iti varṇitam evam viśva śarīraḥ san viśva ātma tvam gataḥ sphuṭam nyāsa mātrāt  tathābhūtam deham puṣpa ādinā arcayet pṛthak mantraiḥ vistareṇa saṃkṣepāt mūlamantrataḥ dhūpa naivedya tṛpti ādyaiḥ tathā vyāsa samāsataḥ saṃsāra vāma ācāra tvāt sarvam vāma kareṇa tu kuryāt tarpaṇa yogam ca daiśikaḥ tad anāmayā vāma śabdena guhyam śrī mataṅga ādau  api īritam vāma ācāra paraḥ  mantrī yāgam kuryāt iti sphuṭam śrīmat bharga śikhā śāstre tathā śrī gamaśāsane sarva tīrtheṣu yad puṇyam sarva yajñeṣu yad phalam tad phalam koṭi guṇita manāma atarpaṇāt priye śrīmat nandiśikhāyām ca śrīmat ānandaśāsane tad uktam sruc ca pūrṇāyām sruvaśva ājya āhutau bhavet  śeṣam vāma kareṇa eva pūjā homa japa ādikam evam ānanda saṃpūrṇam sarva aunmukhya vivarjitam yāgena deham miṣpa adya bhāvayeta śiva ātmakam galite viṣaya aunmukhye pārimitye vilāpite dehe kim avaśiṣyeta śiva ānanda rasāt ṛte śiva ānanda rasa apūrṇam ṣaṭtriṃśat tattva nirbharam deham divāniśam paśyan  arcayan syāt śiva ātmakaḥ viśva ātma deha viśrānti tṛptaḥ tad liṅga niṣṭhitaḥ bāhyam liṅga vrata kṣetra caryā ādi na hi vāñchati tāvat mātrāttva viśrānteḥ saṃvidaḥ kathitāḥ kriyāḥ uttarā bāhya yāga antāḥ sādhyā tu atra śiva ātma tā tatas  rgha pātram kartavyam śiva abheda mayam param ānanda rasa saṃpūrṇam viśva daivata tarpaṇam yathā eva dehe dāha ādi pūjā antam tadvat eva hi arghapātre pi kartavyam samāsa vyāsa yogataḥ kāni dravyāṇi yāgāya kaḥ  nu argha iti na uditam siddhi kāmasya tad siddhau sādhanā eva hi kāraṇam mukti kāmasya naḥ kiṃcid niṣiddham vihitam ca naḥ yad eva hṛdyam tad yogyam śiva saṃvid abhedane kṛtvā argha pātram pratibimbitaḥ vahniḥ prāṇaḥ sruc sruvau ca snehaḥ saṃkalpa cit rasaḥ ittham jñātvā āditaḥ kuṇḍasruc sruva ājya manūn bhṛśam dvādaśānta vibodha agnau ruddhvā pūrṇāhutim kṣipet  yathā yathā hi gaganam utpatet kalahaṃsakaḥ jale binbam bruḍati asya tathā iti atra api ayam vidhiḥ svābhāvikam sthiram ca eva dravam dīptam calam nabhaḥ māyā binduḥ tathā eva ātmā nādaḥ śaktiḥ śivaḥ tathā ittham vyāpya vyāpakataḥ vibhedya abhyantara antam tad adhas sthāni pṛthvī ādi mūla antāni tathā pumān avidyā rāga niyati kāla māyā kalāḥ tathā aṇuḥ vidyā tad īśa īśau sādākhyam śakti kuṇḍalī vyāpinī samanaunmanyam tatas  nāmani yojayet  recaka sthaḥ  madhya nāḍī sandhi vid guruḥ iti adaḥ proktam traiśirase tantre para yojana varṇane tatas  prāc sthāpitāni asta mantra saṃskṛta vahninā caruḥ sādhyaḥ  thavā śiṣyaiḥ homena sama kālakaḥ carau ca vīra dravyāṇi laukikāni athavā icchayā caru siddhau samastāḥ ca kriyā hṛd mantra yogataḥ tatas carum samādāya gururājyena pūritām srucam sruvam vā kṛtvā eva bhukti mukti anusārataḥ devānām atha śaktīnām yantrāṇām tu trayam trayam saptamam mātṛsadbhāvam kramāt ekaikaśas  paṭhan svā iti amṛta varṇena vahnau hutvā ājya śeṣakam carau hā iti agni rūpeṇa juhuyāt tad punar  punar  bhojya bhojaka carvagnyoḥ ittham eka anusandhitaḥ svāhā pratyavamarśāt syāt sa mantrāt advayam param eṣa saṃpāta saṃskāraḥ caroḥ bhoktā hi adhiṣṭhitaḥ bhogyasya paramam sāram bhogyam narnarti yatnatas  samam eka anusandhānāt pātatas  bhoktṛ bhogyayoḥ anyaḥ  nyatra ca saṃpātāt saṃgamāt cettham ucyate sthaṇḍile kubhbha karkaryoḥ bhāgam bhāgam nivedayet  bhāgena agnau mantra tṛptiḥ dvayam śiṣya ātmanoratha ittham vihita kartavyaḥ  vijñāpya īśam tad īritaḥ śaktipāta kramāt śiṣyān saṃskartum niḥsaret bahis  tatra eṣām pañcagavyam ca carum daśana mārjanam tasya pātaḥ śubhaḥ prācī saumya aiśāpya ūrdhva diggataḥ aśubhaḥ  nyatra tatra astra homa u pi aṣṭa śatam bhavet  netra mantrita sat vastra baddha netrān acañcalān ananya hṛdayībhūtān balāt ittham nirodhataḥ muktā ratna ādi kusuma saṃpūrṇa añjalikān guruḥ praveśya sthaṇḍila upāgra upaveśya eva jānubhiḥ prakṣepayet añjalim tam taiḥ śiṣyaiḥ bhāvitātmabhiḥ añjali punar āpūrya teṣām lāghavataḥ paṭam dṛśoḥ nivārayet saḥ pi śiṣyaḥ  jhaṭiti paśyati jhaṭiti ālokite māntra prabhāva ullāsite sthale tad āveśava śāt śiṣyaḥ tad maya tvam prapadyate yathā hi rakta hṛdayaḥ tān  tān kānta aguṇān svayam paśyati evam śaktipāta saṃskṛtaḥ  mantra sannidhim cakṣuḥ ādi indriyāṇām hi sahakāriṇi tādṛśe sati ati antam adṛṣṭe prāk api jāyeta yogya tā kṛta prajñā hi vinyasta mantram deham jalam sthalam pratima ādi ca paśyantaḥ  viduḥ saṃnidhi asaṃnidhī nyasta mantra aṃśu subhagāt kiṃcid bhūta ādi mudritāḥ trasyanti iva iti tad tad cit akṣaiḥ tad sahakāribhiḥ tatas  sa dakṣiṇe haste dīptam sarva adhva pūritam mantra cakram yajet vāma pāṇinā pāśa dāhakam tam śiṣyasya karam mūrdhni deha nyasta adhva saṃtateḥ nyasyet krameṇa sarva aṃṅgam tena eva asya ca saṃspṛśet  uktam dīkṣā uttare ca etad jvālā saṃpāta śobhinā dattena śiva hastena samayī sa vidhīyate sāyujyam īśvare tattve jīvataḥ  dhīti yogya tā śrī devī ā athāmale tu uktam aṣṭa ārāntaḥ triśūlake cakre bhairava sanna abhāva ghora ādi aṣṭa kārake bāhya apare parāna imau madhya śūla parāpare jvālā ākule ruṇe bhrāmyat mātṛ praṇava bhīṣaṇe cintite tu bahis haste saṃdṛṣṭe samayī bhavet  pāśa stobhā ādyaḥ tu sadya uccikramiṣuḥ asya tam prāṇaiḥ viyojakam mūrdhni kṣipet saṃpūjya tad bahis  anena śiva hastena samayī bhavati sphuṭam tasya eva bhāvividhivat tattva pāśa viyojane putraka tvam sa ca pare tattve yojyaḥ tu daiśikaiḥ sa eva mantra jāti jñaḥ  japa homa ādi tattva vid  nirvāṇa kalaśena ādau tatas  īśvara saṃjñinā abhiṣiktaḥ sādhakaḥ syāt bhoga ante sya pare layaḥ etaiḥ guṇaiḥ samāyuktaḥ  dīkṣitaḥ śiva śāsane catuṣpād saṃhitā abhijñaḥ tantra aṣṭādaśa tatparaḥ daśa tantra atimārga jña ācāryaḥ sa vidhīyate pṛthivīm āditaḥ kṛtvā nirvāṇa ante sya yojanām abhiṣeka vidhau kuryāt ācāryasya guru uttamaḥ etaiḥ vākyaiḥ idam ca uktam samayī rāja putravat  sarvatra eva adhikārī syāt putraka ādi pada traye putrakaḥ  daiśika tve tu tulya yojanikaḥ  bhavet  adhikārī sa na punar  sādhane bhinna yojane etad tantre samayi ādi kramāt āpta uttara kriyaḥ ācāryaḥ  na punar bauddha vaiṣṇava ādiḥ kadācana evam prasaṅgāt nirṇītam prakṛtam tu nirūpyate śiva hasta vidhim kṛtvā tena saṃpluṣṭa pāśakam śiṣyam vidhāya viśrānti paryantam dhyāna yogataḥ tatas  kumbhe stra kalaśe vahnau sva ātmani tam śiśum praṇāmam kārayet paścāt bhūta mātṛ balim kṣipet  tatas  śaṃkaram abhyarcya śayyām astra abhimantritām kṛtvā asyām śiṣyam āropya nyasta mantram vidhāya ca śiṣya hṛd cakra viśrāntim kṛtvā tad dvādaśānta gaḥ bhavet kṣīṇa kalā jālaḥ svara dvādaśa ka udayāt tatas  praveśa pracita kalā ṣoḍaśaka ujjvalaḥ saṃpūrṇasva ātma cid candraḥ  viśrāmyet hṛdaye śiśoḥ svayam vyutthāna paryantam dvādaśāntam tatas  vrajet  punar viśet ca hṛd cakram ittham nidrā vidhi kramaḥ āyāta nidraḥ śiṣyaḥ  sau nirmalau śaśi bhāskarau hṛd cakre pratisaṃdhatte balāt pūrṇa kṛśa ātmakau haṭha nirmala candra arka prakāśaḥ satyam īkṣate svapnam bhāvi śubha anyatva sphuṭī bhāvana kovidam uktam ca pūrṇām ca kṛśām dhyātvā dvādaśa gocare praviśya hṛdaye dhyāye tsuptaḥ svācchandyam āpnuyāt  āyāta nidre ca śiśau guruḥ abhyarcya śaṅkaram carum bhuñjīta sa sakhā tatas  dyāt danta dhāvanam svapyāt ca mantra raśmi iddha hṛt cakra arpita mānasaḥ prātar guruḥ kṛta aśeṣa nityaḥ  bhyarcita śaṃkaraḥ śiṣya ātmanoḥ svapna dṛṣṭau  arthau vitte balābalāt sva dṛṣṭam balavat na anyat saṃbodha udreka yogataḥ bodha sāmye punar  svapna sāmyam syāt guru śiṣyayoḥ deva agni guru tad pūjā kāraṇa upaskara ādikam hṛdyā strī madya pānam ca āpi āma māṃsasya bhakṣaṇam rakta pānam śiraḥ chedaḥ  rakta viṣ mūtra lepanam parvata aśva gaja prāya hṛdya yuj yādhirohaṇam yad prītyai syāt api prāyas tad tad śubham udāhṛtam tam khyāpayet tuṣṭi vṛddhyai hlādaḥ  hi paramam phalam atas  nyat aśubham tatra homaḥ  ṣṭa śatakaḥ  strataḥ aśubham na aśubham iti śiṣyebhyaḥ  kathayet guruḥ rūḍhām hi śaṅkām vicchettum yatnaḥ saṃghaṭate mahān yeṣām tu śaṅkā vilayaḥ teṣām svapna vaśa utthitam śubha aśubham na kiṃcid syāt  syuḥ ca ittham citra tā vaśāt sphuṭam paśyati sattva ātmā rājasaḥ  liṅga mātrataḥ na kiṃcid tāmasaḥ tasya sukha duḥkhāt śubha aśubham nanu atra tāmasaḥ  nāma katham yogyaḥ  vidhau bhavet  mā eva mā vigraham kaścid kvacid kasya api vai guṇaḥ sarva sāttvika ceṣṭaḥ  pi bhojane yadi tāmasaḥ kim tatas  saḥ  dhamaḥ kiva api utkṛṣṭaḥ tad viparyayaḥ āyāta śaktipātaḥ  pi dīkṣitaḥ  pi guṇa sthiteḥ vicitra ātmā bhavet eva mukhye tu arthe samāhitaḥ tatas  guruḥ śiśoḥ mantra pūrvakam devatā arcanam deśayet sa ca tad kuryāt saṃskuryāt tam tatas  guruḥ hṛd ādi cakra ṣaṭka sthān brahma ādīn ṣaḍ  samāhitaḥ spṛśet śiśoḥ prāṇa vṛttyā pratyekam ca aṣṭa saṃskriyāḥ hṛdaya ādi dvi ṣaṭka antam bodha sparśa pavitritaḥ āhāra bīja bhāva ādi doṣa dhvaṃsāt bhavet dvijaḥ vasu veda ākhya saṃskāra pūrṇa ittham dvijaḥ sthitaḥ garbhādhānam puṃsavanam sīmantaḥ  jātakarma ca nāma niṣkrāmaṇam ca anna praśaścūḍā tathā aṣṭamī vrata bandha aiṣṭike maujjībhautike saumikam kramāt  gaḥ dānam iti veda indu saṃskriyā brahmacaryataḥ pratyudvāhaḥ pañcadaśaḥ sapta pāka makhāḥ tu atas  aṣṭakāḥ pārvaṇī śrāddham śrāvaṇyāgrāyaṇī dvayam caitrī ca aśvayujī paścāt  sapta eva tu haviḥ makhāḥ ādheyam agni hotram ca paurṇamāsaḥ sa darśakaḥ cāturmāsyam paśu udbandhaḥ sautrāmaṇyā saha tu amī agniṣṭomaḥ  tipūrvaḥ tha sokyyaḥ ṣoḍaśivājapau āptoḥ yāma atirātrau ca sapta etāḥ soma saṃsthitāḥ hiraṇya pāda ādi makhaḥ sahasreṇa samāvṛtaḥ aṣṭatriṃśaḥ tu aśvamedhaḥ  gārhasthyam iyatā bhavet  vānasthi pārivrājye ca catvāriṃśat amī matāḥ dayā kṣamā anasūyā ca śuddhiḥ satkṛti maṅgale akārpaṇya aspṛhe ca ātma guṇa aṣṭakam idam smṛtam mekhalā daṇḍam ajina tri āyuṣe vahni upāsanam saṃdhyā bhikṣā iti saṃskārāḥ sapta sapta vratāni ca bhauteśa pāśupatye dve gāṇeśam gāṇapatyakam unmatta ka asi dhāra ākhya ghṛta īśāni caturdaśa ete tu vrata bandhasya saṃskārā aṅginaḥ smṛtāḥ pārivrājyasya garbhe syāt anti eṣṭiḥ iti saṃskṛtaḥ dvijaḥ  bhavet tatas  yogyaḥ  rudra aṃśa āpādanāya saḥ etān prāṇa krameṇa eva saṃskārān i ojayet guruḥ athavā āhuti yogena tila ādyaiḥ mantra pūrvakaiḥ praṇavaḥ  hṛdayam nāma śodhayāmi agnivallabhā evam krameṇa mūrdha ādyaiḥ aṅgaiḥ atat punar  punar  yatas cit dharma eva asau śānti ādi ātmā dvijanma tā tena rudra tayā saṃvid tad krameṇa eva jāyate yathā hema ādi dhātūnām pāke krama vaśāt bhavet  rajata ādi tathā saṃvid saṃskāre dvijatā antare yoniḥ na kāraṇam tatra śānta ātmā dvija ucyate muninā mokṣa dharma ādau  etad ca pravivecitam mukuṭa ādiṣu śāstreṣu devena api nirūpitam saṃvidaḥ  deha saṃbhedāt sadṛśāt sadṛśa udayāt bhūma abhiprāyataḥ smārte dvijanmā dvijayoḥ sutaḥ antyajātīya dhīva ādi jananī janma lābhataḥ utkṛṣṭa cittā ṛṣayaḥ kim brāhmaṇyena bhājanam ata eva artha sat tattva deśinī asmin  diśyate rahasya śāstre jāti ādi samācāraḥ  hi śāmbhave pāśavāni tu śāstrāṇi vāma śakti ātmakāni alam sṛṣṭyāṃci siddhaye śaṃbhoḥ śaṅkā tad phala kḷptaye āpādita dvija tvasya dvādaśānte nija aikyataḥ sparśa mātrāt na viśrāntyā jhaṭiti eva avarohataḥ rudra aṃśa āpādanam yena samayī saṃskṛtaḥ  bhavet  adhītau śravaṇe nityam pūjāyām guru sevane samayi adhikṛtaḥ  nyatra guruṇā vibhum arcayet  tam āpādita rudra aṃśam samayān śrāvayet guruḥ aṣṭa aṣṭaka ātmakān devyāya amala ādau nirūpitān avādaḥ  karaṇam gūḍhiḥ pūjā tarpaṇa bhāvane hananam mohanam ca iti samayā aṣṭakam aṣṭadhā svabhāvam mantra tantrāṇām samaya ācāra melakam asat pralāpam paruṣam anṛtam na aṣṭadhā vadet  aphalam ceṣṭitam hiṃsām para dāra abhimarśanam garvam dambham bhūta viṣa vyādhi tantram naca ācaret  svam mantram akṣa sūtram ca vidyām jñāna svarūpakam samācārān guṇān kleśān siddhi liṅgāni gūhayet  gurum śāstram deva vahnī jñāna vṛddhān  triyaḥ  vratam guru vargam yathāśaktyā pūjayet aṣṭakam tu idam dīnān kliṣṭān pitṝn kṣetrapālān prāṇi gaṇān khagān śmāśānikam bhūta gaṇam dehadevīḥ ca tarpayet  śivam śaktim tathā ātmānam mudrām mantra svarūpakam saṃsāra bhukti muktīḥ ca guru vaktrāt tu bhāvayet  rāgam dveṣam asūyām ca saṃkoca īrṣyā abhimānitāḥ samaya pratibhettṝn  tad anācārān  ca ghātayet  paśu mārga sthitān krūrān dveṣiṇaḥ piśunān jaḍān rājñaḥ ca anucarān pāpān vighna kartṝn  ca mohayet  śākinyaḥ pūjanīyāḥ ca tāḥ ca ittham śrī gama uditāḥ sāhasam dviguṇam yāsām kāmaḥ ca eva caturguṇaḥ lobhaḥ ca aṣṭaguṇaḥ tāsām śaṅkyam śākinya iti alam kula āmnāya sthitā vīra dravya bāhyāḥ tu ye na taiḥ paśubhiḥ saha vastavyam iti śrī mādhave kule devatā cakra guru agni śāstram sāmyāt sadā arcayet aniveditam etebhyaḥ  na kiṃcid api bhakṣayet  etad dravyam na apaharet guru vargam prapūjayet  sa ca tad bhrātṛ bhāryā tuj prāyaḥ  vidyā kṛtaḥ  bhavet  na yoni saṃbandha kṛtaḥ  laukikaḥ sa paśuḥ yatas  tasya abhiṣvaṅga bhūmiḥ tu guru ārādhana siddhaye arcyaḥ  na sva mahimnā tu tad vargaḥ  guruvat punar  guroḥ nindām na kurvīta tasyai hetum naca ācaret  na ca tām śṛṇuyāt na enam kopayet na agratas  sya ca vinā ājñayā prakurvīta kiṃcid tad sevanāt ṛte laukika alaukikam kṛtyam krodham krīḍām tapaḥ  japam guru upabhuktam yad kiṃcid śayyā vaḥ trāsana ādikam na upabhuñjīta tad padbhyām na spṛśet kiṃtu vandayet  śrīmat traiśirase pyuktam kṛcchra cāndrāyaṇa ādibhiḥ araṇye kāṣṭhavat tiṣṭhet asi dhārā vrataḥ  pi san niyama sthaḥ  yama sthaḥ  pi tad padam na aśnute param guru ārādhana saktaḥ tu manasā karmaṇā girā prāpnoti gurutaḥ tuṣṭāt  pūrṇam śreyaḥ  mahā adbhutam hima pātaiḥ yathā bhūmiḥ chāditā sā samantatas māruta śleṣa saṃyogāt aśmavat tiṣṭhate sadā yama ādau niścale tadvat bhāva ekaḥ tu gṛhyate guroḥ tu ārādhitāt pūrṇam prasarat jñānam āpyate sarvatas  vasthitam cit tvam jñeya stham yasya tad kathā sadya eva nayet ūrdhvam tasmāt ārādhayet gurum śrī sāre pyasya saṃbhāṣāt pātakam naśyati kṣaṇāt  tasmāt parīkṣya yatnena śāstra uktyā jñāna lakṣaṇaiḥ śāstra ācāreṇa varteta tena saṅgam tathā kuru snehāt jātu vadet jñānam lobhāt na hriyate hi saḥ tena tuṣṭena tṛpyanti devāḥ pitara eva ca uttīrya narakāt yānti sadyas  śiva puram mahat  bhuṅkte tiṣṭhet yatra gṛhe vrajet śiva puram tu saḥ iti jñātvā sadā pitrye śrāddhe svam gurum arcayet  bhuñjīta sa svayam ca anyān ādiśet tatkṛte guruḥ yaḥ  dīkṣitaḥ tu śrāddha ādau svatantram vidhim ācaret  tasya tad niṣphalam sarvam samayena ca laṅghyate saiddhāntika arpitam caṇḍī yogyam dravyam vivarjayet  śākinī vācakam śabdam na kadācid samuccaret  striyaḥ pūjyā virūpāḥ tu vṛddhāḥ śilpa upajīvikāḥ antyā vikārita aṅgyaḥ ca veśyāḥ svacchanda ceṣṭitāḥ tathā ca śrī game proktam pūjanīyāḥ prayatnataḥ nirācārāḥ sarva bhakṣyā dharma adharma vivarjitāḥ svacchanda gāḥ palāśinyaḥ  lampaṭā devatā iva veśyāḥ pūjyāḥ tad gṛham ca prayāgaḥ  tra yajet kramam strīṣu tad na ācaret kicid yena tābhyaḥ  jugupsate atas  na nagnāḥ tāḥ paśyet na cāpi prakaṭa stanīḥ vṛddhāyāḥ saṃsthitāyā vā na jugupseta mudrikām vaikṛtyam tatra saurūpyam melakam na prakāśayet  deva mūrtim śūnya tanum pūjayet tripatha ādiṣu sarva parvasu sāmānya viśeṣeṣu viśeṣataḥ pūjā guroḥ anadhyāya u melake lobha varjanam na jugupseta madya ādi vīra dravyam kadācana na nindet atha vandeta nityam tad joṣiṇaḥ tathā upadeśāya na doṣā hṛdayam ced na vidviṣet  vijātīya vikalpa aṃśa utpuṃsanāya yateta ca guroḥ śāstrasya devīnām nāma mantre yatas tatas  arcātaḥ  nyatra na uccāryam āhūtam tarpayet tatas  āgatasya ca mantrasya na kuryāt tarpaṇam yadi harati ardha śarīram tad iti ūce bhagavān yatas  śrīmat ūrmau ca devīnām vīrāṇām ceṣṭitam na vai prathayet na jugupseta vada it na adravya pāṇikaḥ śrī pūrvam nāma vaktavyam guroḥ dravya kareṇa ca guru ādīnām na laṅghyā ca chāyā na tairthikaiḥ saha jalpam kurvan sva śāstra artham vadet na apica sūcayet  nityāt viśeṣa pūjām ca kuryāt naimittike vidhau tatas  pi madhye varṣasya tatas  pi hi pavitrake anyasta mantraḥ  na āsīta sevyam śāstra antaram ca naḥ aprarūḍham hi vijñānam kampeta itara bhāvanāt gṛha upaskaraṇa astrāṇi davatā yāga yogataḥ arcyāni iti na padbhyām vai spṛśet na api vilaṅghyet  guru varge gṛha āyāte viśeṣam kaṃcid ācaret dīkṣitānām na nindā ādi kuryāt vidveṣa pūrvakam upadeśāya naḥ doṣaḥ sa hi avidveṣa pūrvakaḥ na vaṣṇava ādi ka adhas stha dṛṣṭibhiḥ saṃvaset alam saha bhojana śayyā ādi arnā eṣām prakaṭayet sthitim uktam śrīṃmādhava kule śāsana antara saṃsthitān veda uktim vaiṣṇava uktim ca taiḥ uktam varjayet sadā akulīneṣu saṃparkāt tad kulāt patanāt bhayam eka pātre kulāmnāye tasmāt tān parivarjayet  pramādāt ca kṛte sakhye goṣṭhyām cakram tu pūjayet  śrīmat ūrmau ca kathitam āgama antara sevake guru antara rate mūḍhe deva dravya upajīvake śakti hiṃsā kare duṣṭe saṃparkam na eva kārayet  na vikalpena dīkṣā ādau vrajet āyatana ādikam ukta āsthā śithila tve yad nimittam na eva tad caret śāsana sthān purā jātyā na paśyet na api udīrayet na ca vyavaharet sarvān śiva abhedena kevalam sat vidyaiḥ sākam āsīta jñāna dīptyai yateta ca na asaṃskṛtām vrajet tad jam viphala tvam na cānayet  melakā ardha niśācaryā jana varjam ca tad na hi māṃsa ādi dāha gandham ca jighret devī priyaḥ hi asau guru ājñām pālayan sarvam tyajet mantram ayaḥ  bhavet  śāstra pūjā japa dhyāna viveka tad upakriyāḥ akurvat niṣphalām na eva ceṣṭeta trividhām kriyām mantra tantraiḥ na vādam ca kuryāt na u bhakṣayet viṣam samayānām vilope ca gurum pṛcchet asannidhau tad vargam nija santānam anyam tasya api asaṃnidhau tena uktam anutiṣṭhet ca nirvikalpam prayatnataḥ yatas  śāstra ādi saṃbodha tanmayīkṛta mānasaḥ śiva eva guruḥ na asya vāc asatyā viniḥsaret  śivasya sva ātma saṃskṛtyai prahvībhāvaḥ  guroḥ punar  hlādāya iti ubhaya arthāya tad tuṣṭiḥ phala dā śiśoḥ guru āyatta eka siddhiḥ hisamayī api vibodha bhāj  tad bodha bahu mānena vidyāt gurutamam gurum atas  saṃprāpya vijñānam yaḥ  gurau bāhya mānavān na asau vijñāna viśvastaḥ  nāsatyam bhraṣṭa eva saḥ jñāna anāśvasta cittam tam vacaḥ mātreṇa śāstritam bhaktam ca na arcayet jātu hṛdā vijñāna dūṣakam tādṛś  ca na guruḥ kāryaḥ tam kṛtvā api parityajet  mukhya buddhyā na saṃpaśyet vaiṣṇava ādi gatān gurūn tathā ca śrīmat ūrmya ākhye guroḥ uktam viśeṣaṇam guru ājñā prāṇa saṃdehe na upekṣyā naḥ vikalpyate kaula dīkṣā kaula śāstram tattva jñānam prakāśitam yena asau guruḥ iti uktaḥ  hi anye vai nāma dhāriṇaḥ śrīmat ānandaśāstre ca tathā eva uktam viśeṣaṇam yasmāt dīkṣā mantra śāstram tattva jñānam sa vai guruḥ tiṣṭhet avyakta liṅgaḥ ca na liṅgam dhārayet  kvacid  na liṅgibhiḥ samam kaiścid kuryāt ācāra melanam kevalam liṅginaḥ pālyā na bībhatsyā virūpakāḥ śrīmat rātri kule ca uktam mokṣaḥ śaṅkā apahān itaḥ aśuddha vāsa snayā eṣā mokṣa vārtā api durlabhā na likhet mantra hṛdayam śrīmat mālā uditam kila tad aṅgāt uddharet mantram na tu lekhe vilekhayet  atattve bhiniveśam ca na kuryāt pakṣapātatas jāti vidyā ākula ācāra deha deśa guṇa artha jān grahān grahān iva aṣṭau drāk tyajet gahvararśitān tathā śrī niśicāra ādau haya tvena upadarśitān brāhmaṇaḥ  ham mayā veda śāstra uktāt aparam katham anuṣṭheya mayam jāti grahaḥ para nirodhakaḥ evam anye pyudāhāryāḥ kula gahvara vartmanā atad svabhāve tādrūpyam darśayan  avaśe pi yaḥ svarūpa ācchādakaḥ saḥ  tra grahaḥ  graha iva uditaḥ saṃvid svabhāve naḥ jāti prabhṛtiḥ kā api kalpanā rūpam sā tu asvarūpeṇa tad rūpam chādayati alam yā kācid kalpanā saṃvid tattvasya akhaṇḍita ātmanaḥ saṃkoca kāriṇī sarvaḥ sa grahaḥ tām parityajet  śrīmat ānandaśāstre ca kathitam parameṣṭhinā nirapekṣaḥ prabhuḥ vāmaḥ  na śuddhyā tatra kāraṇam devī tṛptiḥ makhe rakta māṃsaiḥ na u śauca yojanāt  dvijāntyajaiḥ samam kāryā carcā ante pi marīcayaḥ avikāra kṛtaḥ tena vikalpān nirayaḥ  bhavet  sarva deva mayaḥ kāyaḥ sarva prāṇiṣu iti sphuṭam śrīmadbhiḥ nakuleśa ādyaiḥ api etad su nirūpitam śarīram eva āyatanam na anyat āyatanam vrajet  tīrtham ekam smaret mantram anya tīrthāni varjayet  vidhim enam sukham jñātvā vidhi jālam parityajet  samādhiḥ niścayam muktvā na ca anyena upalabhyate iti matvā vidhāna jñaḥ saṃmoham parivarjayet  mantrasya hṛdayam muktvā na ca anyat paramam kvacid  iti matvā vidhāna jñaḥ  mantra jālam parityajet  naivedyam prāśayet nadyāḥ tad śeṣam ca jale kṣipet  taiḥ bhukte na bhavet doṣaḥ  jala jaiḥ pūrva dīkṣitaiḥ avayaśpāla nīya tvāt parattvena saṃgamāt  jñāna prāpti abhyupāya tvāt samayāḥ te prakīrtitāḥ evam saṃśrāvya samayān devam saṃpūjya daiśikaḥ visarjayet sva cit vyomni śānte mūrti vilāpanāt  yadi putraka dīkṣā asya na kāryā samanantaram tadā abhiṣiñcet sa astreṇa śiva kumbhena tam śiśum ātmānam ca tatas  yasmāt jala mūrtiḥ maheśvaraḥ mantra yuj nikhila āpyāyī kāryam tad abhiṣecanam iti samaya dīkṣaṇam idam prakāśitam vistarāt ca saṃkṣepāt   ch atha śrī tantrāloke ṣoḍaśam āhnikam atha putrakatva siddhyai nirūpyate śiva nirūpitaḥ  tra vidhiḥ yadā tu samaya sthasya putraka tve niyojanam c guru tve sādhaka tve vā kartum icchati daiśikaḥ tadā adhivāsam kṛtvā ahni dvitīye maṇḍalam likhet  sāmudāyika yāge tha tathā anyatra yathā uditam ṣaṣ aṣṭa tad dvi guṇita caturviṃśati saṃkhyayā cakrapañcakam ākhyātam śāstre śrī pūrva saṃjñite dvātriṃśat tad dvi guṇitam śrīmat traiśirase mate asaṃkhya cakra saṃbandhaḥ śrī siddha ādau nirūpitaḥ tasmāt yathā tathā yāgam yāvat cakreṇa saṃmitam pūjayet yena tena atra triśūla trayam ālikhet  triśūla tritaye devī trayam paryāya vṛttitaḥ madhya savyāni bhedena pūrṇam saṃpūjitam bhavet  vartanā maṇḍalasya agre saṃkṣepāt upadekṣyate ālikhya maṇḍalam gandha vastreṇa eva asya mārjanam kṛtvā snātaḥ  guruḥ prāgvat maṇḍala agre tra devatāḥ bāhya gāḥ pūjayet dvāra deśe ca dvāra devatāḥ maṇḍalasya purobhāge tadā aiśāna diśaḥ kramāt  āgneyī antam gaṇeśa ādīn kṣetrapāntān prapūjayet  gaṇapati guru parama ākhyāḥ parameṣṭhī pūrva siddha vāc kṣetra patiḥ iti saptakam ākhyātam guru paṅkti vidhau prapūjyam asmad gurubhiḥ tatas  ājñām gṛhītvā tu puṣpa dhūpa ādi pūjitam pūjyam ādhāra śakti ādi śūla mūlāt prabhṛti alam śiva antam sita padma ante triśūlānām traye kramāt  madhya śūle madhya gaḥ syāt sadbhāvaḥ parayā saha vāme ca aparayā sākam nava ātmā dakṣa gaṃ param triśūle dakṣiṇe madhya śṛṅga sthaḥ  rati śekharaḥ syāt parāparayā sākam dakṣe bhairava sat pare vāme triśūle madhyasthaḥ  nava ātmā aparayā saha syāt pare parayā sākam vāmāre san  ca bhairavaḥ ittham sarva gata tve śrī parādevyāḥ sthite sati yāgaḥ  bhavet su saṃpūrṇaḥ tad adhiṣṭhāna mātrataḥ eka śūle pyataḥ yāge cintayet tad adhiṣṭhitam avidhi jñaḥ  vidhāna jña iti evam trīśikā uditam tatas  madhye tathā dakṣe vāme śṛṅge ca sarvatas  lokapāla astra paryantam eka ātma tvena pūjayet  paratvena ca sarvāsām devatānām prapūjayet  śrīmantam mātṛ sadbhāva bhaṭṭārakam anāmayam tatas  pi bhoga yāgena vidyā aṅgam bhairava aṣṭakam yām alam cakra devīḥ ca sva sthāne pūjayet bahis  lokapālān astra yutān gandha puṣpa āsava ādibhiḥ pūjayet parayā bhaktyā vitta śāṭhya vivarjitaḥ tatas  kumbha astra kalaśī maṇḍala stha anala ātmanām pañcānām anusandhānam kuryāt advaya bhāvanāt ye tu tām advaya vyāptim na vindanti śiva ātmikām mantra nāḍī prayogeṇa te viśanti advaye pathi sva dakṣiṇena niḥsṛtya maṇḍala sthasya vāmatas  praviśya anyena niḥsṛtya kumbha sthe karkarī gate vahni sthe ca krameṇa ittham yāvat svasmin sva vāmataḥ mūla anusandhāna balāt prāṇa tantu umbhane sati ittham aikya sphurat tā ātmā vyāpti saṃvid prakāśate tatas  viśeṣa pūjām ca kuryāt advaya bhāvitām yad śiva advaya pīyūṣa saṃsiktam paramam hi tad  tena argha puṣpa gandha ādeḥ āsavasya paśoḥ atha yā śivā dvaya tā dṛṣṭiḥ sā śuddhiḥ paramīkṛtiḥ nivedayet vibhoḥ agre jīvān dhātūn  tad utthitān siddhān asiddhān vyāmiśrān yad vā kiṃcid carācaram dṛṣṭa prokṣita saṃdraṣṭṛ prālabdha upātta yojitaḥ nirvāpitaḥ  vīra paśuḥ saḥ  ṣṭadhā uttaratā uttamaḥ yathottaram na dātavyam ayogyebhyaḥ kadācana śiva upayuktam hi haviḥ na sarvaḥ  bhoktum arhati yaḥ tu dīkṣā vihīnaḥ  pi śiva icchā vidhi coditaḥ bhaktyā aśnāti sa saṃpūrṇaḥ samayī syāt su bhāvitaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ  valokitaḥ ca eva kiraṇa iddha dṛś arpaṇāt  prokṣitaḥ kevalam hi arghapātra vipruḍbhiḥ ukṣitaḥ saṃdraṣṭā darśita aśeṣa samyak pūjita maṇḍalaḥ prālabdha ukta tritaya saṃskṛtaḥ saḥ  pi dhūnayet  kampeta prasravet stabdhaḥ pralīnaḥ  vā yathottaram upāttaḥ yāga sānnidhye śamitaḥ śastra mārutaiḥ yojitaḥ kāraṇa tyāga krameṇa śiva yojanāt  nirvāpitaḥ kṛta abhyāsa guru prāṇa manorpaṇāt  dakṣiṇena agninā saumya kalā jāla vilāpanāt tathā hi ādau param rūpam ekībhāvena saṃśrayet  tasmāt āgneya cāreṇa jvālā mālā mucā āviśet paśoḥ vāmena candra aṃśu jālam tāpena gālayet  nābhi cakre tha viśrāmyet prāṇa raśmi gaṇaiḥ saha paraḥ  bhūtvā sva śaktyā atra jīvam jīvena veṣṭayet  sva cit sūryeṇa saṃtāpya drāvayet  kalām kalām tatas  drutam kalā jālam prāpayya eka tvam ātmani samasta tattva saṃpūrṇam āpyāyana vidhāyinam unmūlayeta saṃrambhāt karma baddham amum rasāt  tatas  unmūlana udveṣṭa yogāt vāmam paribhraman kuṇḍalī amṛta saṃpūrṇa svaka prāṇa prasevakaḥ vāma āvarta krama upātta hṛt padma amṛta kesaraḥ hṛd karṇikā rūḍhi lābhāt ojaḥ dhātum vilāpitam śuddha soma ātmakam sāram īṣat lohita pītalam ādāya kari hasta agra sadṛśe prāṇa vigrahe niḥsṛtya jhaṭiti sva ātma vāma mārgeṇa saṃviśet  āpyāyayan  apāna ākhya candra cakra hṛd ambuje sthitam tad devatā cakram tena sāreṇa tarpayet  anena vidhinā sarvān rasa rakta ādikān  tathā dhātūn samāharet saṃgha kramāt eka ekaśas  thavā kevalam tu athavā agni induravi saṃghaṭṭa madhya gam jyotīrūpam atha prāṇa śakti ākhyam jīvam āharet  jīvam samarasīkuryāt devī cakreṇa bhāvanāt  tad eva tarpaṇam mukhyam bhogya bhoktṛ ātma tā eva sā agni saṃpuṭa phulla arṇa tri aśra kāla ātmakaḥ  mahān piṇḍaḥ  rakta ādi sāra ogha cālana ākarṣaṇa ādiṣu ittham viśrānti yogena ghaṭikā ardha krame sati āvṛtti śata yogena paśoḥ nirvāpaṇam bhavet  kṛtvā katipayam kālam tatra abhyāsam ananyadhīḥ yathā cintāmaṇau proktam tena rūpeṇa yoga vid  niḥśaṅkaḥ siddhim āpnoti gopyam tad prāṇavat sphuṭam parokṣe pi paśau  evam vidhiḥ syāt yojanam prati praveśitaḥ  yāga bhuvi hataḥ tatra eva sādhitaḥ cakrajuṣṭaḥ ca tatra eva sa vīrapaśuḥ ucyate yaḥ tu anyatra api nihataḥ sāmastyena aṃśataḥ  pivā devāya vinivedyeta sa vai bāhya paśuḥ mataḥ rājyam lābhaḥ  tha tad sthairyam śive bhaktiḥ tad ātma tā śiva jñānam mantra loka prāptiḥ tad parivāra tā tad sāyujyam paśoḥ sāmyāt bāhya ādeḥ vīra dharmaṇaḥ puṣpādayaḥ  pi tad lābha bhāginaḥ śiva pūjayā eka upāyena deveśaḥ  viśva anugrahaṇa ātmakaḥ yāgena eva anugṛhṇāti kim kim yad na carācaram tena avīraḥ pi śaṅkā ādi yuktaḥ kāruṇikaḥ  pica na hiṃsā buddhim ādadhyāt paśu karmaṇi jātucit  paśoḥ mahā upakāraḥ  yam tadātve pyapriyam bhavet  vyādhi  cheda auṣadha tapaḥ yojana atra nidarśanam śrīmat mṛtyuñjaye proktam pāśa  chede kṛte paśoḥ mala traya viyogena śarīram na prarohati dharma adharma ogha vicchedāt śarīram cyacate kila tena etad māraṇam na uktam dīkṣā iyam citra rūpiṇī rūḍha pāśasya yaḥ prāṇaiḥ viyogaḥ  māraṇam hi tad  iyam tu yojanā eva syāt paśoḥ devāya tarpaṇe tasmāt deva uktim āśritya paśūn dadyāt bahūn iti niveditaḥ punar prāpta dehaḥ  bhūyoniveditaḥ ṣaṣ kṛtva ittham yaḥ saḥ  tra ṣaṣ janmā paśuḥ uttamaḥ yathā pāka kramāt śuddham hema tadvat sa kīrtitaḥ kām siddhim na eva vitaret svayam kiṃvā na mucyate uktam tu ānanda śāstre yaḥ  mantra saṃskāravān  tyajet  samayān kutsayet devīḥ dadyāt mantrān vinā nayāt  dīkṣā mantra ādikam prāpya tyajet putra ādi mohitaḥ tatas  manuṣya tām etya punar evam karoti api ittham eka ādi sapta anta janmā asau dvividhaḥ  dvipāt  catuṣpād vā paśuḥ devī carukā artham prajāyate dātṛ arpitaḥ  sau tad dvārā yāti sāyujyataḥ śivam iti saṃbhāvya citram tad paśūnām praviceṣṭitam bhogyī cikīrṣitam na eva kuryāt anyatra tam paśum na api na eṣa bhavet yogya iti buddhvā apasārayet tam paśum kiṃtu kāṅkṣā ced viśeṣe tam tu ḍhaukayet  tāvataḥ tān paśūn dadyāt tathā ca uktam maheśinā paśoḥ vapā medasī ca gālite vahni madhyatas  arpayet śakti cakrāya paramam tarpaṇam matam hṛd antra muṇḍa aṃsa yakṛt pradhānam vinivedayet  karṇikā kuṇḍalī majja parśu mukhyataram ca vā tatas  gnau tarpaṇam kuryāt mantra cakrasya daiśikaḥ tad nivedya ca devāya tatas  vijñāpayet prabhum guru tvena tvayā eva aham ājñātaḥ parameśvara sākṣāt svapna upadeśa ādyaiḥ japaiḥ guru mukhena vā anugrāhyāḥ tvayā śiṣyāḥ śiva śakti pracoditāḥ tad ete tadvidhāḥ prāptāḥ tvam ebhyaḥ kuru anugraham samāveśaya mām sva ātma raśmibhiḥ yad aham śivaḥ evam bhavatu iti tatas  śiva uktim abhinandayet  śiva abhinnam atha ātmānam pañca kṛtya karam smaret  sva ātmanaḥ karaṇam mantrān mūrtim ca anujighṛkṣayā tatas  baddhvā sita uṣṇīṣam hastayoḥ arcayet kramāt  anyonyam pāśa dāhāya śuddha tattva visṛṣṭaye tejaḥ rūpeṇa mantrān  ca śiva haste samarcayet  garbha āvaraṇa gān aṅga parivāra āsana ujjhitān ātmānam bhāvayet paścāt ekakam jala candravat  kṛtya upādhi vaśāt bhinnam ṣoḍhā bhinnam tu vastutas  maṇḍala sthaḥ  hameva ayam sākṣī ca akhila karmaṇām śuddhā hi draṣṭṛ tā śambhoḥ maṇḍale kalpitā mayā homa adhikaraṇa tvena vahnau  aham avasthitaḥ yad ātma tā iddhā mantrāḥ syuḥ pāśa ploṣa vidhau  alam sāmānya tejaḥ rūpa antara āhūtā bhuvaneśvarāḥ tarpitāḥ śrāvitāḥ ca aṇoḥ na adhikāram pratanvate ā yāga antam aham kumbhe saṃsthitaḥ  vighna śāntaye sāmānya rūpa tā yena viśeṣa āpyāya kāriṇī śiṣya dehe ca tad pāśa śithilatva prasiddhaye sa hi sva icchā vaśāt pāśān vidhunvan  iva vartate sākṣāt sva deha saṃsthaḥ  ham kartā anugraha karmaṇām jñāna kriyā svatantra tvāt dīkṣā karmaṇi peśalaḥ bhinna kārya ākṛti vrāta indriya cakra anusandhimān ekaḥ  yathā aham vahni ādi ṣaṣ rūpaḥ  smi tathā sphuṭam evam ālocya yena eṣaḥ  dhvanā dīkṣām cikīrṣati anusaṃhitaye śiṣya varjam pañcasu tam yajet  anusandhi bala ante ca samāsa vyāsa bhedataḥ kuryāt atyantam abhyastam anya antarbhāva pūritam tatas  pi cintayā bhūyaḥ nusandadhyāt śiva ātma tām aham eva param tattvam na ca pad dhaṭavat  kvacid  mahā prakāśaḥ tad tena mayi sarvam idam jagat  na ca tad kenacid bāhya pratibimbavat arpitam kartā aham asya tad na anya adhīnam ca mad adhiṣṭhitam itthaṃbhūta mahāvyāpti saṃvedana pavitritaḥ mad sama tvam gataḥ  jantuḥ mukta iti abhidhīyate tāpa nirgharṣa seka ādi pāramparyeṇa vahni tām yathāyogolakaḥ  yāti guruḥ evam śiva ātma tām tatas  puras sthitam yad vā puras bhāvita vigraham parokṣa dīkṣaṇe yad vā darbha ādyaiḥ kalpite mṛte śiṣye vīkṣya arcya puṣpa ādyaiḥ nyaset adhvānam asya tam yena adhvanā mukhya tayā dīkṣām icchati daiśikaḥ tam dehe nyasya tatra antar bhāvyam anyat iti sthitiḥ śodhya adhvani ca vinyaste tatra eva pariśodhakam nyaset yathā īpsitam mantram śodhya aucitya anusārataḥ kvacid śodhyam tu avinyasya śodhaka nyāsa mātrataḥ svayam śuddhi ati saṃśodhyam śodhakasya prabhāvataḥ aparam para aparam ca param ca vidhim icchayā tad yojana anusāreṇa śritvā nyāsaḥ ṣaḍadhvanaḥ lalāṭa antam veda vasau randhra antam rasa randhrake vasukha indau dvādaśāntam iti eṣa trividhaḥ  vidhiḥ krameṇa kathyate dṛṣṭaḥ śāstre śrī pūrva saṃjñite tatra tattveṣu vinyāsaḥ  gulpha ante catur aṅgule dharā jala ādi mūla antam pratyekam dvi aṅgulam kramāt  rasa śruti aṅgulam nābheḥ ūrdhvam ittham ṣaṣ aṅgule puṃsaḥ kalā antam ṣaṣ tattvīm pratyekam tri aṅgule kṣipet  aṣṭādaśa aṅgulam tu evam kaṇṭha kūpa avasānakam sadāśiva antam māyā ādi catuṣkam catur aṅgule pratyekam iti abdhi vasu saṃkhya mālika deśataḥ śiva tattvam tatas  paścāt tejaḥ rūpam anākulam sarveṣām vyāpaka tvena sa bāhya abhyantaram smaret  jalāt hi antam sārdha yugmam mūlam tri aṅgulam iti atas  dvādaśa aṅgula tā ādhikyāt vidhiḥ eṣa parāparaḥ jalāt hi antam tri aṅgule ced avyaktam tu catuṣṭaye tad caturviṃśati ādhikyāt paraḥ  pyaṣṭaśate vidhiḥ trividha unmānakam vyaktam vasu digbhyaḥ  ravi kṣayāt  mayatantre tathā ca uktam tad tad sva phala vāñchayā nava pañca catur tri eka tattva nyāse svayam dhiyā nyāsam prakalpayet tāvat tattva antarbhāva cintanāt kalā pañcaka veda aṇḍa nyāsaḥ  nena eva lakṣitaḥ uktam ca triśiraḥ tantre sva ādhāra stham yathāsthitam dvādaśa aṅgulam utthānam deha atītam samam tatas  dvāsaptatiḥ daśa dve ca deha stham śirasaḥ  ntatas pādāt ārabhya suśroṇi anāhata pada avadhi deha atīte pi viśrāntyā saṃvitteḥ kalpanā vaśāt  deha tvam iti tasmāt syāt utthānam dvādaśa aṅgulam iti nirṇetum atra etad uktam aṣṭa uttaram śatam pura nyāsaḥ  tha gulpha antam bhūḥ purāṇi atra ṣoḍaśa tasmāt eka aṅgula vyāptyā pratyekam lakula āditaḥ dvi s aṇḍa antam tri aṅgulam tu cchagala aṇḍam atha abdhiṣu deva yoga aṣṭake dve hi pratyeka aṅgula pādataḥ iti pradhāna paryantam ṣaṭcatvāriṃśat aṅgulam ṣaṭpañcāśat purāṇi ittham prāk dharāyām tu ṣoḍaśa tatas  pyardha aṅgula vyāptyā ṣaṣ purāṇi aṅgula traye catvāri yugma ekasmin  ekam ca puram aṅgule sa rāge puṃspurāṇi īśa saṃkhyāni ittham ṣaṣ aṅgule krodha īśa puram ekasmin dvaye ca aṇḍam iyam ca vid  saṃvarta jyotiṣoḥ evam kalā tattva gayoḥ kramāt  śūra pañca anta purayoḥ niyatau ca eka yugma tā śrī pūrvaśāstre tad ca uktam parameśena śaṃbhunā uttara ādi krama ādadvi eka bhedaḥ  vidyā ādike traye asāra tvāt kramasya ādau niyatiḥ paratas  kalā athavā anyonya saṃjñābhyām tattvayoḥ vyapadeśya tā eka vīra śikhā īśa śrīkaṇṭhāḥ kāle trayaḥ traye kālasya pūrvam vinyāsaḥ  niyateḥ abhidhīyate athavā anyonya saṃjñābhiḥ vyapadeśaḥ  hi dṛśyate evam pum ādiṣaṭ tattvī vinyasta aṣṭādaśa aṅgule tatas  pyaṅguṣṭha mātra antam māyā tattva stham aṣṭakam pratyekam ardha aṅgulataḥ syāt aṅgula catuṣṭaye ittham dvi akṣṇi purāṇi aṣṭāviṃśatiḥ puruṣān niśi puratrayam dvayoḥ tri aṃśa nyūna aṅgulam iti kramāt  dvayoḥ dvayam pañca purī vaidyīye catur aṅgule tatas  aiśa purāṇi aṣṭau catuṣke rdha aṅgula kramāt  tatas trīṇi dvaye dve ca dvayoḥ ittham catuṣṭaye sādāśivam pañcakam syāt ittham vasu ekakam ravau ṣoḍaśakam rasa viśikham vasu dvikam vasuśaśī iti pura vargāḥ vedā rasa abdhi yugma akṣi ca ravayaḥ tatra ca aṅgulāḥ kramaśas  aṣṭādaśa adhika śatam purāṇi dehe tra caturaśīti mite vinyastāni tad ittham śeṣe tu vyāpakam śivam tattvam iti vidhiḥ aparaḥ kathitaḥ parāpara ākhyaḥ  rasa śruti sthāne aṣṭa śaram saṃkhyānam kha muni kṛtam tad pare vidhau jñeyam lakula ādeḥ yoga aṣṭaka paryantasya atra bhuvana pūgasya adhikīkuryāt gaṇanā vaśena bhāgam vidhi dvaye kramaśas  apara ādi vidhi traitāt atha nyāsaḥ padādhvanaḥ pūrvam daśapadī ca uktā svatantrā nyasyate yadā tayā eva dīkṣā kāryā ced tadā iyam nyāsa kalpanā tattva ādi mukhya tā yogāt dīkṣāyām tu pada āvalī tad tattva ādi anusāreṇa tatra antar bhāvyate tathā sva pradhānatva yoge tu dīkṣāyām pada paddhatim nyasyet krameṇa tattva ādi vadanānavalokinīm caturṣu aṣṭāsu ca aṣṭāsu daśasu atha daśasu atha daśasu athaḥ pañcadaśasu atha veda śara induṣu dharā padān navapadīm mātṛkā mālinī gatām yojayet vyāptṛ daśamam padam tu śiva saṃjñitam dharā padam varjayitvā pañca yāni padāni tu vidhi dvayam syāt nikṣipya dvādaśa dvādaśa aṅgulān mantra adhvanaḥ  pyeṣa eva vidhiḥ vinyāsa yojane vyāpti mātram hi bhidyeta iti uktam prāk eva tad tathā varṇa adhvanaḥ  tha vinyāsaḥ kathyate tra vidhi traye ekam caturṣu pratyekam dvayoḥ aṅgulayoḥ kramāt  trayoviṃśati varṇī syāt  ṣaṣ varṇī ekaikaśas triṣu pratyekam atha catvāraḥ caturṣu iti vilomataḥ mālinī mātṛkā arṇāḥ syuḥ vyāptṛ śaivam rasendutaḥ varjayitvā adya varṇam tu tattvavat syāt ravīt navīn tām trayoviṃśatau varṇeṣu api anyat syāt vidhi dvayam śrī pūrvaśāstre tena ādau tad tveṣu uktam vidhi trayam atidiṣṭam tu tad bhinna abhinna varṇa dvaye samam dvividhaḥ  pi hi varṇānām ṣaḍvidhaḥ bheda ucyate tattva mārga vidhānena jñātavyaḥ paramārthataḥ upadeśa atideśābhyām yad uktam tad pada ādiṣu bhūyaḥ tidiṣṭam tatra eva śāstre smad hṛdaya īśvare pada mantra kalā ādīnām pūrva sūtra anusārataḥ tritaya tvam prakurvīta tattva varṇa ukta vartmanā uktam tad pada mantreṣu kalāsu atha nirūpyate caturṣu rasa vede dvāviṃśatau dvādaśasu atha nivṛtti ādyāḥ catasraḥ syuḥ vyāptrī syāt śānti atītikā dvitīyasyām kalāyām tu dvādaśa dvādaśa aṅgulān kramāt kṣiptvā vidhi dvaitam parāpara para ātmakam caturaṇḍa vidhiḥ tu ādi śabdena iha pragṛhyate kalā catuṣkavat tena tasmin vācyam vidhi trayam evam ṣaḍvidham adhvānam śodhya śiṣya tanau purā nyasya ekatama mukhya tvāt nyasyet śodhaka saṃmatam adhvani āsana mantra oghaḥ śodhakaḥ  hi eka āditas  śabdarāśiḥ mālinī ca samastavyastatas  dvidhā eka vīra tayā yad vā ṣaṭkam yāmala yogataḥ pañcavaktrī śakti tadvat bhedāt ṣoḍhā punar dvidhā ekāki yāmala tvena iti evam sā dvādaśa ātmikā ṣaḍaṅgī sakala anya tvāt dvividhā vaktravat punar  dvādaśa tvena guṇitā caturviṃśati bhedikā aghora ādi aṣṭake dve ca tṛtīyam yāmala udayāt mātṛsadbhāva mantraḥ ca kevalaḥ śruti cakra gaḥ eka dvi tri catur bhedāt trayodaśa bhidā ātmakaḥ eka vīra tayā saḥ  yam caturdaśa tayā sthitaḥ anāma saṃhṛti sthairya sṛṣṭi cakram caturvidham devatābhiḥ nijābhiḥ tad mātṛ sadbhāva vṛṃhitam ittham śodhaka vargaḥ  yam mantrāṇām saptatiḥ smṛtā ṣaṣ ardha śāstreṣu śrīmat sāra śāstre ca kathyate aghora ādi aṣṭakena iha śodhanīyam vipaścitā athavā eka akṣarā mantraiḥ athavā mātṛkā kramāt bhairavīya hṛdā vā api khecarī hṛdayena vā bhairaveṇa mahādevi tu atha vaktra aṅga pañcakaiḥ yena yena hi mantreṇa tantre smin  udbhavaḥ kṛtaḥ tena eva dīkṣayet mantrī iti ājñā pārameśvarī evam śodhaka bhedena saptatiḥ kīrtitā bhidaḥ śodhya nyāsam vinā mantraiḥ etaiḥ dīkṣā yadā bhavet  tadā saptatidhā jñeyā janana ādi vivarjitā śodhya bhedaḥ  tha vaktavyaḥ saṃkṣepāt saḥ  pi kathyate eka tri pañca ṣaṭtriṃśat bhedāt tāttvaḥ caturvidhaḥ pañca eka bhedāt ca adhvānaḥ tathā eva aṇḍa catuṣṭayam evam daśavidham śodhyam triṃśaddhā tad vidhi trayāt śodhya śodhaka bhedena śatāni tu ekaviṃśatiḥ atra api nyāsa yogena śodhye dhvani tathā ākṛteḥ śata ekaviṃśati bhidā janana ādi ujjhitā bhavet  janana ādi mayī tāvatī evam śata dṛśi śrutiḥ syāt saptati adhikā sā api dravya vijñāna bhedataḥ dvidhā iti pañca aśītiḥ syāt śatāni adhika khābdhikā bhoga mokṣa anusandhānāt dvividhā sā prakīrtitā aśubhasya eva saṃśuddhyā śubhasya api atha śodhanāt  dvidhā bhogaḥ śubhe śuddhiḥ kāla traya vibhedini eka dvi sāmastya vaśāt saptadhā iti aṣṭadhā bhujiḥ guru śiṣya kramāt saḥ pi dvidhā iti evam vibhidyate pratyakṣa dīkṣaṇe yasmāt dvayoḥ eka anusandhitaḥ tādṛś dīkṣā phalam pūrṇam visaṃvāde tu viplavaḥ parokṣa mṛta dīkṣā ādau guruḥ eva anusandhimān kriyā jñāna mahimnā tam śiṣyam dhāmni īpsite nayet  avibhinne kriyā jñāne karma śuddhau tathā eva te anusandhiḥ punar bhinnaḥ karma yasmāt tad ātmakam śrīmat svacchandaśāstre ca vāsanā bhedataḥ phalam śiṣyāṇām ca guroḥ ca uktam abhinne pi kriyā ādike bhogasya śodhakāt śodhyāt anusandheḥ ca tādṛśāt  vaicitryam asti bhedasya vaicitrya prāṇa tā yatas  tathā hi vaktraiḥ yasya adhvā śuddhaḥ taiḥ eva yojitaḥ bhoktum iṣṭe kvacid tattve sa bhoktā tad bala anvitaḥ śubhānām karmaṇām ca atra sadbhāve bhoga citra tā tādṛś eva bhavet karma śuddhau tu anyā eva citra tā bhogaḥ ca sadya  utkrāntyā dehena eva atha saṃgataḥ tadā eva abhyāsataḥ vā api dehānte vā iti asau catuḥ prāktana aṣṭa bhidā yogāt dvātriṃśat bheda ucyate mokṣa ekaḥ  pi bījasya samaya ākhyasya tādṛśam bāla ādikam jñāta śīghra maraṇam śakti varjitam vṛddham vā uddiśya śaktam vā śodhana aśodhanāt dvidhā sadya  utkrāntitaḥ traidham sā ca āsanna mṛtau guroḥ kāryā ityājñā maheśasya śrīmat gahvara bhāṣitā dṛṣṭvā śiṣyam jarā grastam vyādhinā paripīḍitam utkramayya tatas tu enam para tattve niyojayet  pañcatriṃśat amī bhedā guroḥ vā guru śiṣyayoḥ ukta dvaividhya kalanāt saptatiḥ parikīrtitāḥ etaiḥ bhedaiḥ purā uktān  tān bhedān dīkṣā gatān guruḥ hatvā vadet prasaṃkhyānam su abhyasta jñāna siddhaye pañcāśīti śatī yā catvāriṃśat samuttarā kathitā tām saptatyā bhittvā dīkṣā bhedān svayam kalayet  pañcakam iha lakṣāṇām ca saptanavatiḥ sahasra parisaṃkhyā aṣṭau śatāni dīkṣā bhedaḥ  yam mālinītantre saptatidhā śoddhṛ gaṇaḥ triṃśaddhā śodhya eka tattva ādiḥ sa aṇḍaḥ ṣaḍadhva rūpaḥ tathā iti kartavyatā catur bhedā dravya jñāna mayī sā janana ādi vivarjitā atha tad yuktā pañcatriṃśaddhā punar eṣā bhoga apavarga sandhānāt yasmāt dvātriṃśaddhā bhogaḥ śubha śuddhi aśuddhi kāla bhidā mokṣaḥ tredhā dviguṇā saptatiḥ iti kārya tā bhedāḥ śodhana śodhya vibheda āditi kartavyatva bhedataḥ ca eṣā dīkṣā bahudhā bhinnā śodhya vihīnā tu saptatidhā mantrāṇām sakala itara sa aṅga niraṅga ādi bheda saṃkalanāt  śyodhyasya ca tattva ādeḥ pañcadaśa ādi ukta bheda parigaṇanāt  bhedānām parigaṇanā na śakyate kartum iti asaṃkīrṇāḥ bhedāḥ saṃkīrṇāḥ punar anye bhūyastva kāriṇaḥ  bahudhā śodhaka śodhya ādīnām dvitra ādi vibheda sadbhāvāt bhoge sādhye yad yad bahu kartavyam tad āśrayet matimān kāraṇa bhūyaḥ tvam kila phala bhūyaḥ tvāya kim citram apavarge na tu bhedaḥ tena asmin vāsanā dṛḍhatva juṣā alpā api āśrayaṇīyā kriyā atha vijñāna mātre vā abhinavagupta guruḥ punar āha hi sati vitta deśa kāla ādau apavarge pi hi vistīrṇa karma vijñāna saṃgrahaḥ kāryaḥ cit vṛtteḥ vaicitryāt cāñcalye pi krameṇa sandhānāt  tasmin  tasmin vastuni rūḍhiḥ avaśyam śiva ātmikā bhavati tattvam idam etad ātmakam etasmāt proddhṛtaḥ  mayā śiṣyaḥ ittham krama saṃvittau mūḍhaḥ  pi śiva ātmakaḥ  bhavati kramika tathāvidha śiva tā anugraha subhagam ca daiśikam paśyan śiśuḥ api tad abheda dṛśā bhakti balāt ca abhyupaiti śiva bhāvam yadi api vikalpa vṛtteḥ api mokṣam dīkṣayā eva dehānte śāstre provāca vibhuḥ tathā api dṛḍha vāsanā yuktā mokṣe pyasti viśeṣaḥ kriyā alpa bhūyaḥtva jaḥ sa loka ādiḥ iti kecid tad ayuktam sa vicitraḥ  bhoga eva kathitaḥ syāt  saṃskāra śeṣa vartana jīvita madhye sya samaya lopa ādyam na āyāti vighna jālam kriyā bahu tvam mumukṣoḥ tad  yasmāt  sa bīja dīkṣā saṃskṛta puruṣasya samaya lopa ādye bhukte bhogān mokṣaḥ  na evam nirbīja dīkṣāyām iti kecid manyante yuktam tad ca api yad smṛtam śāstre samaya ullaṅghanāt devi kravyāda tvam śatam samāḥ tasmāt uruśiṣya matau śiva bhāva nirūḍhi vitaraṇa samartham kramikam tattva uddharaṇa ādi karma mokṣe pi yuktam ati vitatam yaḥ tu sadā bhāvanayā su abhyasta jñānavān guruḥ sa śiśoḥ apavargāya yathā iccham yam kaṃcid upāyam anutiṣṭhet evam śiṣya tanau śodhyam nyasya adhvānam yathā īpsitam śodhakam mantram upari nyasyet tattva anusārataḥ dvayoḥ mātṛkayoḥ tattva sthityā varṇa kramaḥ purā kathitaḥ tam tathā nyasyet tad tad tattva viśuddhaye varṇa adhvā yadi api proktaḥ śodhyaḥ pāśa ātmakaḥ tu saḥ māyīyaḥ śodhakaḥ tu anyaḥ śiva ātmā para vāc mayaḥ uvāca sadyojyotiḥ ca vṛttau svāyambhuvasya tad  bāḍham ekaḥ  hi pāśa ātmā śabdaḥ  nyaḥ ca śiva ātmakaḥ tasmāt tasya eva varṇasya yuktā śodhaka śodhya tā śrī pūrvaśāstre ca api uktam te taiḥ āliṅgitā iti sadyojāta ādi vaktrāṇi hṛd ādi aṅgāni pañca ca ṣaṣ kṛtvā u nyasya ṣaṭtriṃśat nyāsam kuryāt hara āditaḥ parāparāyā vailomyāt harāyām syāt pada trayam tatas  jalāt ahaṅkāre pañca aṣṭaka samāśrayāt padāni pañca dhī mūla puṃrāga ākhye traye trayam ekam tu aśuddha vid kāla dvaye ca ekam niyāmake kalā māyā dvaye ca ekam pada m uktam iha kramāt  vidyeśvara sadā śakti śiveṣu pada pañcakam ekonaviṃśatiḥ sā iyam padānām syāt parāparā sārdham ca ekam ca ekam sārdham dve dve śaśī dṛś atha yugmam trāṇi dṛś abdhiḥ candraḥ śrutiḥ śaśī pañca vidhu mahaḥ candrāḥ eka anna viṃśatau syāt akṣara saṃkhyā padeṣu iyam devyāḥ haldvayayutavasu citraguparisaṃkhyāta sva varṇāyāḥ mūla antam sārdha varṇam syāt māyā antam varṇam ekakam śakti antam ekam aparā nyāse vidhiḥ udīritaḥ māyā antam haltatas śakti paryante svara ucyate niṣkale śiva tattve vai paraḥ  nyāsaḥ para uditaḥ para aparā padāni eva hi aghoryādi aṣṭaka dvaye mantrāḥ tad anusāreṇa tattveṣu etad dvayam kṣipet  piṇḍa akṣarāṇām sarveṣām varṇa saṃkhyā vibhedataḥ avyakta antam svare nyasya śeṣam śeṣeṣu yojayet  bījāni sarva tattveṣu vyāptṛ tvena prakalpayet  piṇḍānām bījavat nyāsam anye tu pratipedire akṛte vā atha śodhyasya nyāse vastu balāt  sthiteḥ śodhaka nyāsa mātreṇa sarvam śodhyam viśudhyati śrīmat mṛtyuñjaya ādau ca kathitam parameṣṭhinā adhunā nyāsa mātreṇa bhūtaśuddhiḥ prajāyate deha śuddhi artham api etad tulyam etena vastutas  anya prakaraṇa uktam yadi uktam prakaraṇa antare jñāpaka tvena sākṣāt vā tad kim na anyatra gṛhyate mālinīmātṛkā aṅgasya nyāsaḥ  yaḥ  rcā vidhau purā proktaḥ kevala saṃśoddhṛ mantra nyāse sa eva tu tripadī dvayoḥ dvayoḥ syāt pratyekam atha aṣṭasu śruti padāni diś candra candra rasa ravi śara śara dṛś dṛś mṛgāṅka śaśi gaṇane aṅgula māne devyā aṣṭādaśa vaibhavena padam anyat  aparam mānam idam syāt  kevala śodhaka manunyāse turya padāt pada ṣaṭke māna dvitayam parāpara para ākhyam dvādaśakam dvādaśakam tattva upari pūrvavat tu anyat  kevala śodhaka mantra nyāsa abhiprāyataḥ  mahādevaḥ tattva krama uditam api nyāsam punar āha tad viruddham api niṣkale padam eka arṇam yāvat trīṇi tu pārthive ityādinā tattva gata krama nyāsa udīritaḥ punar ca mālinītantre varga vidyā vibhedataḥ dvidhā padāni iti uktvā ākhyat nyāsa manyādṛśam vibhuḥ ekaikam dvi aṅgulam jñeyam tatra pūrvam pada trayam aṣṭa aṅgulāni catvāri daśa aṅgulam atas  param dvi aṅgule dve pade ca anye ṣaṣ aṅgulam atas  param dvādaśa aṅgulam anyat ca dve nye pañcāṅgule pṛthak  pada dvayam catuṣparva tathā anye dve dvi parvaṇī evam parāparā devyāḥ svatantraḥ  nyāsa ucyate vidyā dvayam śiṣya tanau vyāptṛ tvena eva yojayet  iti darśayitum na asya pṛthak nyāsam nyarūpayat  evam śodhaka mantrasya nyāse tad raśmi yogataḥ pāśa jālam vilīyeta tad dhyāna balataḥ  guroḥ śodhya tattve samastānām yonīnām tulya kālataḥ jananāt bhogataḥ karma kṣaye syāt apavṛkta tā dehaiḥ tāvadbhiḥ asya aṇoḥ citram bhoktuḥ api sphuṭam manaḥ  nusandhiḥ na u viśva saṃyoga pravibhāgavat  niyatyā manasaḥ  deha mātre vṛttiḥ tatas  param na anusandhā yatas  sa eka svānta yukta akṣa kalpitā pradeśa vṛtti ca jñānam ātmanaḥ tatra tatra tad  bhogya jñānam na anya deheṣu anusandhānam arhati yadā tu manasaḥ tasya deha vṛtteḥ api dhruvam yoga mantra kriyā ādeḥ syāt vaimalyam tad vidā tadā yathāmalam manaḥ  dūra sthitam api āśu paśyati tathā pratyaya dīkṣāyām tad tad bhuvana darśanam janana ādi viyuktām tu yadā dīkṣām cikīrṣati tadā asmāt uddharāmi iti yuktam ūha prakalpanam yadā śodhyam vinā śoddhṛ nyāsaḥ tatra api mantrataḥ janana ādi kramam kuryāt tattva saṃśleṣa varjitam eka aki śoddhṛ nyāse ca janana ādi vivarjane tad śoddhṛ saṃpuṭam nāma kevalam parikalpayet  dravya yogena dīkṣāyām tila ājya akṣata taṇḍulam tad tad mantreṇa juhuyāt janma yoga viyogayoḥ yadā vijñāna dīkṣām tu kuryāt śiṣyam tadā bhṛśam tad mantra saṃjalpa balāt paśyedā ca avikalpakāt vikalpaḥ kila saṃjalpa m ayaḥ  yad sa vimarśakaḥ mantra ātmā asau vimarśaḥ ca śuddhaḥ  pāśavata ātmakaḥ nityaḥ ca anādi vara da śiva abheda upakalpitaḥ tad yogāt daiśikasya api vikalpaḥ śiva tām vrajet  śrī sāraśāstre tad idam parameśena bhāṣitam arthasya pratipattiḥ yā grāhya grāhaka rūpiṇī sā eva mantra śaktiḥ tu vitatā mantra santatau parāmarśa svabhāva ittham mantra śaktiḥ udāhṛtā parāmarśaḥ  dvidhā śuddha aśuddha tvāt mantra bhedakaḥ uktam śrī pauṣkare nye ca brahma viṣṇu ādayaḥ  ṇḍagāḥ prādhānikāḥ sa añjanāḥ te sāttva rājasa tāmasāḥ taiḥ aśuddha parāmarśāt tanmayībhāvitaḥ  guruḥ vaiṣṇava ādiḥ paśuḥ proktaḥ  na yogyaḥ pati śāsane ye mantrāḥ śuddha mārga sthāḥ śiva bhaṭṭāraka ādayaḥ śrīmat mataṅga ādi dṛśā tad mayaḥ  hi guruḥ śivaḥ nanu svatantra saṃjalpa yogāt astu vimarśitā prāk kutas  sa vimarśāt ced kutas  saḥ  pi nirūpaṇe ādyaḥ tathā avikalpatva pradaḥ syāt upadeṣṭṛtaḥ yaḥ saṃkrāntaḥ  bhijalpaḥ syāt tasya api anya upadeṣṭṛtaḥ pūrva pūrva kramāt ittham ya eva ādi guroḥ purā saṃjalpaḥ  hi abhisaṃkrāntaḥ saḥ  dyā apyasti iti gṛhyatām yaḥ tathāvidha saṃjalpa balāt kaḥ pi svatantrakaḥ vimarśaḥ kalpyate saḥ  pi tad ā ātmā eva su niścitaḥ ghaṭa kumbha iti ittham vā yadi bhedaḥ  nirūpyate saḥ  pyanyakalpanā dāyī hi anādṛtyaḥ prayatnataḥ paṇāyate karoti iti vikalpasya ucitau sphuṭam kara pāṇi abhijalpau tau saṃkīryetām katham kila śabdāt śabda antare tena vyutpattiḥ vyavadhānataḥ vyavahārāt tu sā sākṣāt citra upākhyā vimarśinī tad vimarśa udayaḥ prācya sva vimarśa mayaḥ sphuret  yāvat bālasya saṃvittiḥ akṛtrima vimarśane tena tad mantra śabda artha viśeṣa uttham vikalpanam śabda antara utthāt bhedena paśyatā mantra ādṛtaḥ yad ca api bīja piṇḍa ādeḥ uktam prāk bodha rūpakam tad tasya eva kutaḥ nyasya tad kasmāt anya kalpanā etad artham guroḥ yatnāt lakṣaṇe tatra tatra tad  lakṣaṇam kathitam hi eṣa mantra tantra viśāradaḥ tena mantra artha saṃbodhe mantra vārtikam ādarāt  ūhā apoha prayogam vā sarvathā guruḥ ācaret  mantra artha vid abhāve tu sarvathā mantra tad mayam gurum kuryāt  tad abhyāsāt tad saṃkalpam ayaḥ  hi asau tad samāna abhisaṃjalpaḥ  yadā mantra artha bhāvanāt guroḥ bhavet tadā sarva sāmye kaḥ  bheda ucyatām aṃśena api atha vaiṣamye na tatas  rtha kriyā hi sā gomayāt kīṭataḥ kīṭa iti evam nyāyataḥ  yadā saṃjalpa antarataḥ  pi artha kriyām tām eva paśyati tadā eṣa satya saṃjalpaḥ śiva eva iti kathyate sa yad vakti tad eva syāt mantraḥ  bhoga apavarga daḥ na eṣaḥ bhinavaguptasya pakṣaḥ  mantra arpita ātmanaḥ yaḥ  rtha kriyām āha bhinnām kīṭayoḥ api tādṛśoḥ mantra arpita manāḥ kiṃcidvat anyat tu viṣam haret  tad mantra eva śabdaḥ sa param tatra ghaṭa ādivat  kāntā saṃbhoga saṃjalpa sundaraḥ kāmukaḥ sadā tad saṃskṛtaḥ  pyanyat eṣa kurvan sva ātmani tṛpyati tathā tad mantra saṃjalpa bhāvitaḥ  nyat api bruvan anicchuḥ api tad rūpaḥ tathā kārya karaḥ  dhruvam vikalpayan  api ekārtham yatas  nyat api paśyati viṣa apahāri mantra ādi iti uktam śrī pūrvaśāsane yadi vā viṣa nāśe pi hetu bhedāt vicitra tā dhātu āpyāya ādika ananta kārya bhedāt bhaviṣyati tad evam mantra saṃjalpa vikalpa abhyāsa yogataḥ bhāvya vastu sphuṭībhāvaḥ saṃjalpa hrāsa yogataḥ vastu eva bhāvayati eṣa na saṃjalpam imam punar  gṛhṇāti bhāsana upāyam bhāte tatra tu tena kim evam saṃjalpa nirhrāse su parisphuṭatā ātmakam akṛt trima vimarśa ātma sphuret vastu avikalpakam nirvikalpā ca sā saṃvid yad yathā paśyati sphuṭam tad tathā eva tathā ātma tvāt vastunaḥ  pi bahis sthiteḥ viśeṣataḥ tu amāyīyaśivatā bheda śālinaḥ mokṣe bhyupāyaḥ saṃjalpaḥ  bandha mokṣau tatas  kila vikalpe pi guroḥ samyak abhinna śiva tā juṣaḥ avikalpaka paryanta pratīkṣā na upayujyate tad vimarśa svabhāvā hi sā vācyā mantradevatā mahā saṃvid samāsanna iti uktam śrī gamaśāsane nikaṭa sthā yathā rājñām anyeṣām sādhayanti alam siddhim rāja upagān śīghram evam mantra ādayaḥ parām ukta abhiprāya garbham tad uktam śrī mālinīmate mantrāṇām lakṣaṇam kasmāt iti ukte munibhiḥ kila yogam eka tvam icchanti vastunaḥ  nyena vastunā tad vastu jñeyam iti uktam heyatva ādi prasiddhaye tad prasiddhyai śivena uktam jñānam yad upavarṇitam sa bīja yoga saṃsiddhyai mantra lakṣaṇam api alam na ca adhikāritā dīkṣām vinā yoge sti śāṅkare kriyā jñāna vibhedena sā ca dvedhā nigadyate dvividhā sā prakartavyā tena ca etad udāhṛtam na ca yoga adhikāri tvam ekam eva anayā bhavet  api mantra adhikāri tvam muktiḥ ca śiva dīkṣayā anena etad api proktam yogī tadtva aikya siddhaye mantram eva āśrayet mūlam nirvikalpa antam ādṛtaḥ mantra abhyāsena bhogam vā mokṣam vā api prasādhayan tatra adhikāri tā labdhyai dīkṣām gṛhṇīta daiśikāt  tena mantra jñāna yoga balāt yad yad prasādhayet tad syāt asya anya tattve pi yuktasya guruṇā śiśoḥ dīkṣā hi asya upayujyeta saṃskriyāyām sa saṃskṛtaḥ sva balena eva bhogam vā mokṣam vā labhate budhaḥ tena vijñāna yoga ādi balī prāk  samayī bhavan putrakaḥ  vā na tāvān syāt apitu sva bala ucitaḥ yaḥ tu vijñāna yoga ādi vandhyaḥ saḥ  ndhaḥ yathā pathi daiśika āyatta eva syāt bhoge muktau ca sarvathā dīkṣā ca kevalā jñānam vinā api nijam āntaram mocikā eva iti kathitam yuktyā ca āgamataḥ purā yaḥ tu dīkṣā kṛtām eva apekṣya yojanikām śiśuḥ sphuṭībhūtyai tad ucitam jñānam yogam atha āśritaḥ saḥ  pi yatra eva yuktaḥ syāt tad maya tvam prapadyate guru dīkṣā mantra śāstra adhīna sarva sthitiḥ tatas  duṣṭānām eva sarveṣām bhūta bhavya bhaviṣyatām karmaṇām śodhanam kāryam bubhukṣoḥ na śubha ātmanām yaḥ punar laukikam bhogam rājya svarga ādikam śiśuḥ tyaktvā loka uttaram bhogam īpsuḥ tasya śubheṣu api tatra dravya mayīm dīkṣām kurvan  ājya tila ādikaiḥ karma asya śodhayāmi iti juhuyāt daiśika uttamaḥ jñāna mayyām tu dīkṣāyām tad viśuddhi ati sandhitaḥ guroḥ sva saṃvid rūḍhasya balāt tad prakṣayaḥ  bhavet  yadā asya aśubha karmāṇi śuddhāni syuḥ tadā śubham sva tāratamya āśrayaṇāt adhva madhye prasūti dam śubha pāka krama upātta phala bhoga samāptitaḥ yatra eṣa yojitaḥ tad sthaḥ bhāvi karma kṣaye kṛte bhāvinām ca ādya deha stha deha antara vibhedinām aśubha aṃśa viśuddhau syāt bhogasya eva anupakṣayaḥ bhuñjānasya asya satatam bhogān māyā ālaya antatas  na duḥkha phala dam deha ādi adhva madhye pi kiṃcana tatas  māyā ālaye bhukta samasta sukha bhogakaḥ niṣkale sakale vaiti layam yojanikā balāt iti prameyam kathitam dīkṣā kāle guroḥ yathā  ch atha śrī tantrāloke saptadaśam āhnikam atha bhairava tādātmya dāyinīm prakriyām bruve evam maṇḍala kumbha agni śiṣya sva ātmasu pañcasu gṛhītvā vyāptim aikyena nyasya adhvānam ca śiṣya gam karma māyā aṇu malina trayam bāhau gale tathā śikhāyām ca kṣipet sūtra granthi yogena daiśikaḥ tasya atad rūpa tā ābhānam malaḥ  granthiḥ sa kīrtyate iti pratīti dārḍhya artham bahis granthi upakalpanam bāhū karma āspadam viṣṇuḥ māyā ātmā gala saṃśritaḥ adhas vahā śikhā aṇu tvam tena ittham kalpanā kṛtā nara śakti śiva ākhyasya trayasya bahu bheda tām vaktum tris triguṇam sūtram granthaye parikalpayet  tejaḥ jala anna tritayam tredhā pratyekam api adaḥ śruti ante ke pyatas  śukla kṛṣṇa raktam prapedire tatas  gnau tarpita aśeṣa mantre cit vyoma mātrake sāmānya rūpe tattvānām kramāt śuddhim samācaret  tatra sva mantra yogena dharām āvāhayet purā iṣṭvā puṣpa ādibhiḥ sarpiḥ tila ādyaiḥ atha tarpayet  tad tattva vyāpikām paścāt māyā tattva adhidevatām māyā śaktim sva mantreṇa āvāhya abhyarcya pratarpayet  āvāhane mātṛkā arṇam mālinya ṛṇam ca pūjane kuryāt iti guruḥ prāha svarūpa āpyāyana dvayāt tāraḥ  varṇaḥ  tha saṃbuddhi padam tvām iti atas  param uttama eka yutam karma padam dīpakam api atas  tabhyam nāma caturthī antam tatas  pyucita dīpakam iti ūha mantra yogena tad tad karma pravartayet  āvāhana anantaram hi karma sarvam nigadyate āvāhanam ca saṃbodhaḥ sva svabhāva vyavasthiteḥ bhāvasya ahaṃmaya sva ātma tādātmya āveśyamāna tā śāktī bhūmiḥ ca sā eva uktā yasyām mukhyā asti pūjyatā abhāta tvāt abhedāt ca na hi asau nṛ śiva ātmanoḥ jaḍa ābhāseṣu tattveṣu saṃvid sthityai tatas  guruḥ āvāhana vibhaktim prāk  kṛtvā turya vibhaktitaḥ namaskāra anta tā yogāt pūrṇām sattām prakalpayet  tatas  pūrṇa svabhāva tvam tad rūpa udreka yogataḥ dhyeya udrekaḥ  bhavet dhyātṛ prahvībhāva vaśāt yatas  āvāhya iṣṭvā pratarpya iti śrī svacchande nirūpitam anena eva pathā āneyam iti asmad guravaḥ  jaguḥ paratvena tu yad pūjyam tad svatantra cit ātmakam anavacchid prakāśa tvāt na prakāśyam tu kutracid  tasya hi etad prapūjyatva dhyeyatva ādi yad ullaset  tasya eva tad svatantra tvam yāti durghaṭa kāri tā saṃbodha rūpe tad tasmin katham saṃbodhanā bhavet  prakāśanāyām na syāt prakāśasya prakāśa tā saṃbodhana vibhaktyā eva vinā karma ādi śakti tām svātantryāt tam darśayitum tatra ūham imam ācaret devam āvāhayāmi iti tatas  devāya dīpakam prāk yuktyā pūrṇa tā dāyi namaḥ svāhā ādikam bhavet  nutiḥ pūrṇa tvam agni indu saṃghaṭṭa āpyāya tā param āpyāyakam ca procchālam vauṣaṭ ādi pradīpayet  tatra bāhye pi tādātmya prasiddham karma codyate yadi karma padam tad naḥ guruḥ abhyūhayet kvacid  anābhāsita tad vastu bhāsanāya niyujyate mantraḥ kim tena tatra syāt sphuṭam yatra avabhāsi tad  tena prokṣaṇa saṃseka japa ādi vidhiṣu dhruvam tad karma abhyūhanam kuryāt pratyuta vyavadhātṛ tām bahis tathā ātma tā bhāve kāryam karma padohanam tṛptau  āhuti hutabhuj pāśa ploṣat chid ādiṣu yatra uddiṣṭe vidhau paścāt tad anantaiḥ kriyā ātmakaiḥ aṃśaiḥ sādhyam na tatra ūhaḥ dīkṣaṇa ādi vidhiṣu iva tatas  śiṣyasya tad tattva sthāne streṇa pratāḍanam kṛtvā atha śiva hastena hṛdayam parimarśayet  tatas  sva nāḍī mārgeṇa hṛdayam prāpya vai śiśoḥ śiṣya ātmanā saha ekatvam gatvā ādāya ca tam hṛdā puṭitam haṃsa rūpa ākhyam tatra saṃhāra mudrayā kuryāt ātmīya hṛdaya sthitam api avabhāsakam śiṣya dehasya tejobhī raśmi mātrā viyogataḥ sva bandha sthāna calanāt  svatantra sthāna lābhataḥ sva karma aparatantra tvāt sarvatra utpattim arhati tena ātma hṛdaya ānītam prāk kṛtvā pudgalam tatas  māyāyām tad dharā tattva śarīrāṇi asya saṃsṛjet  tatra asya garbhādhānam ca yuktam puṃsavana ādibhiḥ garbha niṣkrāma paryantaiḥ ekām kurvīta saṃskriyām jananam bhoga bhoktṛ tvam militvā ekātha saṃskriyā tatas  sya teṣu bhogeṣu kuryāt tad maya tām layam tatas tad tattva pāśānām vicchedam samupācaret  saṃskārāṇām catuṣke sminna parām ca parāparām mantrāṇām pañcadaśakam parām vā yojayet kramāt  pivani ādi aṣṭakam śastra ādikam ṣaṭkam parā tathā iti pañcadaśā ete syuḥ kramāt līnatva saṃskṛtau aparā mantramuktvā prāc amuka ātmana iti atha garbhādhānam karomi iti punar mantram tam eva ca svāhā antam uccaran dadyāt āhuti tritayam guruḥ param parāparā mantram amuka ātmana iti atha jātasya bhoga bhoktṛ tvam karomi atha parāparām ante svāhā iti proccārya vitaret tisra āhutīḥ uccārya pivanī mantram amuka ātmana iti atha bhoge layam karomi iti punar mantram tam eva ca svāhā antam āhutīḥ tisraḥ  dadyāt ājya tila ādibhiḥ eṣa eva vamani ādau vidhiḥ pañcadaśa antake pūrvam para ātmakam mantram amuka ātmana iti atha pāśa ācchedam karomi iti parā mantraḥ punar tatas  hum svāhā phaṭ  samuccārya dadyāt tisraḥ  pyathā āhutīḥ saṃskārāṇām catuṣke sminye mantrāḥ kathitā mayā teṣu karma padāt pūrvam dharā tattva padam vadet  tatas  dharā tattva patim āmantrya iṣṭvā pratarpya ca śiva abhimāna saṃrabdhaḥ  guruḥ evam samādiśet  tattva īśvara tvayā na asya putrakasya śiva ājñayā pratibandhaḥ prakartavyaḥ  yātuḥ padam anāmayam tatas  yadi samīheta dharā tattva antarāla gam pṛthak  śodhayitum mantrī bhuvana ādi adhva pañcakam aparā mantrataḥ prāgvat tisraḥ tisraḥ tad āhutīḥ dadyāt puram śodhayāmi iti ūha yuktam prasanna dhīḥ evam kalā mantra pada varṇeṣu api vicakṣaṇaḥ tisraḥ tisraḥ  hutīḥ dadyāt  pṛthak  sāmastyataḥ  pivā tatas  pūrṇāhutim dattvā parayā vauṣaṭ antayā aparā mantrataḥ śiṣyam uddhṛtya ātma hṛdam nayet  yadā tu ekena śuddhena tad antar bhāva cintanāt na pṛthak  śodhayet tattva nātha saṃśravaṇāt param tadā pūrṇām vitīrya aṇum utkṣipya ātmani yojayet  tātsthya ātma saṃsthya yogāya tayā eva aparayā āhutīḥ sa karma padayā dadyāt iti kecid tu manvate anye tu guravaḥ prāhuḥ bhāvanām ayam īdṛśam na atra bāhya āhutiḥ deyā daiśikasya pṛthak  punar  dadyāt vā yadi naḥ doṣaḥ syāt upāyaḥ sa bhāvane evam prāktana tātsthya ātma saṃstha tve yojayet guruḥ tatas  śiṣya hṛdam neyaḥ sa ātmā tāvataḥ  dhvanaḥ śuddhaḥ tad dārḍhya siddhyai ca pūrṇā syāt parayā punar  mahā pāśupatam pūrvam vilomasya viśuddhaye juhomi punar astreṇa vauṣaṭ anta iti kṣipet  punar  pūrṇām tatas  māyām abhyarcya atha visarjayet  dharā tattvam viśuddham sat jalena śuddha rūpiṇā bhāvayet miśritam vāri śuddhi yogyam tatas  bhavet  tathā tad tad purā tattva miśraṇāt uttarottaram sarvā śivībhavet tattva āvalī śuddhā anyathā pṛthak  pṛthaktvam ca malaḥ  māyā abhidhānaḥ tasya saṃbhave karma kṣaye pi naḥ muktiḥ bhavet vidyeśvara ādivat  tatas  pi jala tattvasya vahnau vyomni cit ātmake āhvāna ādi akhilam yāvat tejasi asya vimaśraṇam evam kramāt kalā tattve śuddhe pāśam bhuja āśritam chindyāt kalā hi sā kiṃcitkartṛtva unmīlana ātmikā karma ākhya mala jṛmbhā ātmā tam ca granthim sruc agra gam pūrṇāhutyā samam vahni mantra tejasi nirdahet  mantraḥ  hi viśva rūpaḥ san  upāśraya vaśāt tathā vyakta rūpaḥ tatas  vahnau pāśa ploṣa vidhāyakaḥ pluṣṭaḥ  līna svabhāvaḥ  sau pāśaḥ tam prati śambhuvat  parameśa mahā tejaḥ śeṣa mātra tvam aśnute karma pāśe tra hotavye pūrṇayā asya śubha aśubham aśubham vā bhavat bhūtam bhāvi vā atha samastakam dahāmi phaṭ trayam vauṣaṭ iti pūrṇām vinikṣipet  evam māyā anta saṃśuddhau kaṇṭha pāśam ca homayet  pūrṇasya tasya māyā ākhyam pāśa bheda prathā ātmakam dahāmi phaṭ trayam vauṣaṭ iti pūrṇām kṣipet guruḥ nirbījā yadi kāryā tu tadā atra eva aparām kṣipet  pūrṇām samaya pāśa ākhya bīja dāha pada anvitām gurau deve tathā śāstre bhaktiḥ kārya asya na hi asau samayaḥ śaktipātasya svabhāvaḥ  hi eṣa naḥ pṛthak  māyā ante śuddhim āyāte vāgīśī yā purā bhavat māyā śakti mayī sā eva vidyā śakti tvam aśnute tad śuddha vidyām āhūya vidyā śaktim niyojayet  evam krameṇa saṃśuddhe sadāśiva pade pyalam śikhām granthi yutām chittvā malam āṇavakam dahet  yatas  dhikāra bhoga ākhyau dvau pāśau tu sadāśive iti uktyā aṇava pāśaḥ  tra māyīyaḥ tu niśā avadhiḥ śiṣyaḥ  yathocitam snāyāt ācāmet daiśikaḥ svayam āṇava ākhye vinirdagdhe hi adhas vāhi śikhāmale tatas  prāc ukta sakala prameyam paricintayan śiṣya deha ādim ātmīya deha prāṇa ādi yojitam kṛtvā ātma deha prāṇa ādeḥ viśvam antar anusmaret ukta prakriyayā ca evam dṛḍha buddhiḥ ananyadhīḥ prāṇa stham deśa kāla adhva yugam prāṇam ca śakti gam tām ca saṃvid gatām śuddhām saṃvidam śiva rūpiṇīm śiṣya saṃvid abhinnām ca mantra vahni ādi abhedinīm dhyāyan prāgvat prayogeṇa śivam sakala niṣkalam dvi ātmakam vā kṣipet pūrṇām praśānta karaṇena tu uktam traiśirase tantre sarva saṃpūraṇa ātmakam mūlāt udaya gatyā tu śiva indu parisaṃplutam janma anta madhya kuhara mūla srotaḥ samutthitam śiva arka raśmibhiḥ tīvraiḥ kṣubdham jñāna amṛtam tu yad  tena saṃtarpayet samyak  praśānta karaṇena tu śūnya dhāma abja madhya stha prabhā kiraṇa bhāsvaraḥ ādheya ādhāra niḥspanda bodha śāstra parigrahaḥ janma ādheya prapañca eka sphoṭa saṃghaṭṭa ghaṭṭanaḥ mūla sthānāt samārabhya kṛtvā someśam anta gam kham iva ātiṣṭhate yāvat praśāntam tāvat ucyate uktam śrī pūrvaśāstre ca srucam āpūrya sarpiṣā kṛtvā śiṣyam tathā ātma stham mūlamantram anusmaran śivam śaktim tathā ātmānam śiṣyam sarpiḥ tathā analam ekīkurvan śanais gacchet dvādaśāntam ananyadhīḥ tatra kumbhakam āsthāya dhyāyan sakala niṣkalam tiṣṭhet tāvat anudvignaḥ  yāvat ājya kṣayaḥ  bhvet  evam yuktaḥ pare tattve guruṇā śiva mūrtinā na bhūyas  paśu tām eti dagdha māyā nibandhanaḥ dehapāte punar  prepset yadi tattveṣu kutracid  bhogān samasta vyastatva bhedaiḥ ante param padam tadā tad tattva bhūmau tu tad saṃkhyāyām ananyadhīḥ punar yojanikām kuryāt pūrṇāhuti antareṇa tu mukti pradā bhoga mokṣa pradā vā yā prakīrtitā dīkṣā sā syāt sa bījatva nirbīja ātma tayā dvidhā bāle nirjñāta maraṇe tu aśakte vā jarā ādibhiḥ kāryā nirbījikā dīkṣā śaktipāta bala udaye nirbījāyām sa āmayān  tu pāśān api viśodhayet  kṛta nirbīja dīkṣaḥ tu deva agni guru bhakti bhāj  iyatā eva śivam yāyāt  sadyas  bhogān vibhujya vā śrīmat dīkṣā uttare ca uktam cāre ṣaṭtriṃśat aṅgule tattvāni āpāda mūrdha antam bhuvanāni tyajet kramāt  tuṭi mātram niṣkalam tad adeham tad ahaṃparam śaktyā tatra kṣipāmi enam iti dhyāyan  tu dīkṣayet  sa bījāyām tu dīkṣāyām samayān na viśodhayet  viśeṣaḥ tu ayam etasyām yāvat jīvam śiśoḥ guruḥ śeṣa vṛttyai śuddha tattva sṛṣṭim kurvīta pūrṇayā abhinnāt śiva saṃbodha jaladheḥ yugapad sphurat pūrṇām kṣipan  tattva jālam dhyāyet bhārūpakam sṛtam viśuddha tattva sṛṣṭim vā kuryāt kumbha abhiṣecanāt  tathā dhyāna balāt eva yad vā pūrṇa abhiṣecanaiḥ pṛthivī sthira rūpā asya śiva rūpeṇa bhāvitā sthirīkaroti tām eva bhāvanām iti śuddhi ati jalam āpyāyayati enām tejaḥ  bhāsvaratām nayet  marut ānanda saṃsparśam vyoma vaitatyam āvahet  evam tanmātra vargaḥ  pi śiva tāmaya iṣyate para ānanda mahāvyāptiḥ aśeṣa mala vicyutiḥ śive gantṛ tvam ādānam upādeya śiva stutiḥ śiva āmoda bhara āsvāda darśana sparśanāni alam tad ākarṇanam iti evam indriyāṇām viśuddha tā saṃkalpa adhyavasāmānāḥ prakāśaḥ  rakti saṃsthitī śiva ātma tvena yad sā iyam śuddha tā mānasa ādike niyamaḥ  rañjanam kartṛ bhāvaḥ kalanayā saha vedanam heya vastu aṃśa viṣaye supta kalpa tā ittham śiva aikya rūḍhasya ṣaṣ kañcuka gaṇaḥ  pyayam śuddha eva pumān prāpta śiva bhāvaḥ  viśuddhi ati vidyeśa ādiṣu tattveṣu na eva kācid aśuddha tā iti evam śuddha tattvānām sṛṣṭyā śiṣyaḥ  pi tad mayaḥ bhavet hi etad sūcitam śrī mālinīvijaya uttare bandha mokṣau  ubhau  etau  indriyāṇi jaguḥ budhāḥ nigṛhītāni bandhāya vimuktāni vimuktaye etāni vyāpake bhāve yadā syuḥ manasā saha muktāni kvāpi viṣaye rodhāt bandhāya tāni tu iti evam dvividhaḥ  bhāvaḥ śuddha aśuddha prabhedataḥ indriyāṇām samākhyātaḥ siddhayogīśvare mate śrīmān vidyā aguruḥ tu āha pramāṇa stuti darśane samasta mantraiḥ dīkṣāyām niyamaḥ tu eṣa kathyate māyā anta śuddhau sarvāḥ syuḥ kriyā hi aparayā sadā dvi ātmayā sakala ante tu niṣkale parayā eva tu īśa ante ca pivani ādi sakala ante ṅga pañcakam iti evaṃvidhim ālocya karma kuryāt guru uttamaḥ purā adhvani hutīnām yā saṃkhyeyam tattva varṇayoḥ tām eva dviguṇīkuryāt pada adhvani caturguṇām kramāt mantra kalā mārge dviguṇā dviguṇā kramāt  yāvat tri tattva saṃśuddhau syāt viṃśati guṇā tatas  pratikarma bhavet ṣaṣṭiḥ āhutīnām tri tattvake eka tattve śatam prāhuḥ āhutīnām tu sa aṣṭakam viloma karmaṇā sākam yāḥ pūrṇāhutayaḥ smṛtāḥ tāsām sarva adhva saṃśuddhau saṃkhyā anya tvam na kiṃcana iti eṣā kathitā dīkṣā janana ādi samanvitā  ch atha śrī tantrāloke aṣṭādaśam āhnikam atha saṃkṣipta dīkṣā iyam śiva tā āpatti dā ucyate na rajaḥ  na adhivāsaḥ  tra na bhū kṣetra parigrahaḥ c yatra tatra pradeśe tu pūjayitvā guruḥ śivam adhvānam manasā dhyātvā dīkṣayet tattva pāragaḥ janana ādi vihīnām tu yena yena adhvanā guruḥ kuryāt sa eka tattva antān śiva bhāva eka bhāvitaḥ parā mantraḥ tatas  sya iti tattvam saṃśodhayāmi atha svāhā iti pratitattvam syāt śuddhe pūrṇāhutim kṣipet  evam mantra antaraiḥ kuryāt samastaiḥ athavā uktavat  parāsaṃpuṭitam nāma svāhā antam prathama antakam śatam sahasram sāṣṭam vā tena śaktyā eva homayet  tatas  pūrṇā iti saṃśodhya hīnam uttamam īdṛśam dīkṣā karma uditam tatra tatra śāstre maheśinā pratyekam mātṛkā yugma varṇaiḥ tattvāni śodhayet  yadi vā piṇḍa mantreṇa sarva mantreṣu ayam vidhiḥ yathā yathā ca su abhyasta jñānaḥ tad maya tā ātmakaḥ guruḥ tathā tathā kuryāt  saṃkṣiptam karma na anyathā śrī brahmayāmale ca uktam saṃkṣipte pi hi bhāvayet  vyāptim sarva adhva sāmānyām kiṃtu yāge na vistaraḥ atanmayībhūtam iti vikṣiptam karma sandadhat  kramāt tādātmyam eti iti vikṣiptam vidhim ācaret  saṃkṣiptaḥ  vidhiḥ uktaḥ  yam kṛpayā yaḥ śiva uditaḥ dīkṣā uttare kairaṇe ca tatra tatra api śāsane  ch atha śrī tantrāloke ekānna viṃśam āhnikam atha sadyas samutkrānti pradā dīkṣā nirūpyate tad kṣaṇāt ca upabhogāt vā dehapāte śivam vrajet  c iti uktyā mālinīśāstre sūcitā asau maheśinā dehapāte samīpa sthe śaktipāta sphuṭa tvataḥ āsādya śāṃkarīm dīkṣām tasmāt dīkṣā kṣaṇāt param śivam vrajet iti arthaḥ  tra pūrva apara vivecanāt vyākhyātaḥ śrīmatā asmākam guruṇā śambhu mūrtinā yadā hi āsanna maraṇe śaktipātaḥ prajāyate tatra mande tha guru ādi sevayā āyuḥ kṣayam vrajet  athavā bandhu mitra ādi dvārā sā asya vibhoḥ patet  pūrvam vā samayī na eva parām dīkṣām avāptavān āpta dīkṣaḥ  pi vā prāṇān jihāsuḥ kleśa varjitam antyān guruḥ tadā kuryāt sadya  utkrānti dīkṣaṇam na tu apakva male na api śeṣa kārmika vigrahe kuryāt utkramaṇam śrīmat gahvare ca nirūpitam dṛṣṭvā śiṣyam jarā grastam vyādhinā paripīḍitam utkramayya tatas tu enam para tattve niyojayet  viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya tve kāmacāra vidhānataḥ pūrva uktam artha jātam śrī śambhunā atra nirūpitam vidhim pūrva uditam sarvam kṛtvā samaya śuddhitaḥ kṣurikām asya vinyasyet jvalantīm marma kartarīm kṛtvā pūrva uditam nyāsam kāla anala sama prabham saṃhṛti kramataḥ sārdham sṛkchindi yugalena tu āgneyīm dhāraṇām kṛtvā sarva marma pratāpanīm pūrayet vāyunā deham aṅguṣṭhāt mastaka antakam tam utkṛṣya tatas  ṅguṣṭhāt ūrdhva antam vakṣyamāṇayā kṛntet marmāṇi randhra antāt kālarātryā visarjayet  anena krama yogena yojitaḥ  huti varjitaḥ samayī apyeti tām dīkṣām iti śrī mālinīmate ṣoḍaśa ādhāra ṣaṣ cakra lakṣya traya kha pañcakāt  kvacid anyataratra atha prāk ukta paśu karmavat  praviśya mūlam kanda ādeḥ chindan  aikya vibhāvanāt pūrṇāhuti prayogeṇa sva iṣṭe dhāmni niyojayet  jñāna triśūlam saṃdīptam dīpta cakra traya ujjvalam cintayitvā amunā tasya vedanam bodhanam bhramam dīpanam tāḍanam todam calanam ca punar  punar  kanda ādi cakra gam kuryāt viśeṣeṇa hṛd ambuje dvādaśānte tatas  kṛtvā bindu yugma gate kṣipet  nirlakṣye vā pare dhāmni saṃyuktaḥ parameśvaraḥ na tasya kuryāt saṃskāram kaṃcid iti āha gahvare devaḥ kim asya pūrṇasya śrāddha ādyaiḥ iti bhāvitaḥ śrīmat dīkṣā uttare tu eṣa vidhiḥ vahni puṭīkṛtaḥ haṃsaḥ pumān adhas tasya rudra bindu samanvitaḥ śiṣya dehe niyojya etad anudvagnaḥ śatam japet  utkramya ūrdhva nimeṣeṇa śiṣya ittham param vrajet  eṣa eva vidhiḥ śrīmat siddhayogīśvarīmate iyam utkrāmaṇī dīkṣā kartavyā yoginaḥ  guroḥ anabhyasta prāṇa cāraḥ katham enām kariṣyati vakṣyamāṇām brahma vidyām sakalām niṣka lombhi tām karṇe sya vā paṭhet bhūyas  bhūyaḥ vā api atha pāṭhayet  svayam ca karma kurvīta tattva śuddhi ādikam guruḥ mantra kriyā balāt pūrṇāhutyā ittham yojayet pare yoga abhyāsam akṛtvā api sadya  utkrānti dām guruḥ jñāna mantra kriyā dhyāna balāt kartum bhavet prabhuḥ anayā utkramyate śiṣyaḥ  balāt eva ekakam kṣaṇam kālasya ullaṅghya bhogaḥ  hi kṣaṇikaḥ  syāḥ tu kim tatas  sadya  utkrānti dā ca anyā yasyām pūrṇāhutim tadā dadyāt yadā asya prāṇāḥ syuḥ dhruvam niṣkramaṇa icchavaḥ vinā api kriyayā bhāvi brahma vidyā balāt guruḥ karṇa jāpa prayogeṇa tattva kañcuka jālataḥ niḥsārayan yathā abhīṣṭe sakale niṣkale dvaye tattve vā yatra kutra api yojayet pudgalam kramāt  samayī putrakaḥ  vā api paṭhet vidyām imām tathā tad pāṭhāt tu samayī uktām rudra aṃśa āpattim aśnute etau jape ca adhyayane yasmāt adhikṛtau  ubhau na adhyāpana upadeśe vā sa eṣaḥ  dhyayanāt ṛte paṭhatoḥ tu anayoḥ vastu svabhāvāt tasya sā gatiḥ yathā niṣiddha bhūta ādi karmā mantram smaran svayam āviṣṭe pi kvacid na eti lopam kartṛtva varjanāt  yathā ca vācayan śāstram samayī śūnya veśmani na lupyate tad antar stha prāṇi varga upakārataḥ tathā svayam paṭhan  eṣa vidyām vastu svabhāvataḥ tasmin mukte na lupyeta yatas  kiṃcid karaḥ tra saḥ nanu ca adīkṣita agre sa na uccaret śāstra paddhatim hanta kuḍya agratas  pyasya niṣedhaḥ tu atha kathyate paryudāsena yaḥ śrotum avadhārayitum kṣamaḥ sa eva atra niṣiddhaḥ  naḥ kuḍya kīṭa patatriṇaḥ tarhi pāṣāṇa tulyaḥ  sau vilīna indriya vṛttikaḥ tasya agre paṭhataḥ tasya niṣedha ullaṅghanā katham sa tu vastu svabhāvena galita akṣaḥ  pi budhyate akṣa an apekṣayā eva antar cid śaktyā sva prakāśayā prāk deham kila tityakṣuḥ na uttaram ca adhitaṣṭhivān madhye prabodhaka balāt  pratibudhyet  pudgalaḥ mantrāḥ śabda mayāḥ śuddha vimarśa ātma tayā svayam artha ātmanā ca avabhāntaḥ tad artha pratibodhakāḥ tena asya galita akṣasya prabodhaḥ  jāyate svayam sva cid samāna jātīya mantra āmarśana saṃnidheḥ yathā hi alpa javaḥ  vāyuḥ sajātīya vimiśritaḥ javī tathā ātmā saṃsuptām arśaḥ  pi evam prabudhyate prabuddhaḥ sa ca saṃjātaḥ  na ca adīkṣita ucyate dīkṣā hi nāma saṃskāraḥ  na tu anyat saḥ sti ca asya hi ata eva nijam śāstram paṭhati kvāpi sāmaye tad śrutvā kaḥ  pi dhanyaḥ ced mucyate na asya sā kṣatiḥ śāstra nindām mā eṣa kārṣīt dvayoḥ pātitya dāyinīm iti evaṃparam etad na adīkṣita agre paṭhet iti yathā ca samayī kāṣṭhe loṣṭe vā mantra yojanām kurvan  tasmin  calatyeti na lopam tadvat atra hi yatas  sya pratyaya prāpti prepsoḥ samayinaḥ tathā pravṛttasya svabhāvena tasmin mukte na vai kṣatiḥ sādhakaḥ tu sadā sādhye phale niyati yantraṇāt  makṣikā śruta mantraḥ  pi prāyaścitta aucitīm caret  ittham sadyas samutkrāntiḥ yā uktā tām ājñayā guroḥ samayi ādiḥ api prokta kāle prokta artha siddhaye svayam kuryāt samabhyasta prāṇa cāra gama āgamaḥ akṛta adhikṛtiḥ vā api guruḥ samaya śuddhaye adhastana pada avasthaḥ  na tu jñāna iddha cetanaḥ iti iyam sadya  utkrāntiḥ sūcitā mālinīmate svayam vā guruṇā vā atha kāryatvena maheśinā sarvam bhogam virūpam tu matvā deham tyajet yadi tadā tena krameṇa āśu yojitaḥ samayī śivaḥ uktā iyam sadya  utkrāntiḥ yā gopyā prāṇavat budhaiḥ  ch atha śrī tantrāloke viṃśatitamam āhnikam atha dīkṣām bruve mūḍha jana āśvāsa pradāyinīm tri koṇe vahni sadane vahni varṇa ujjvale bhitas  vāyavya pura nirdhūte kare savye sujājvale bījam kiṃcid gṛhītvā etad tathā eva hṛdaya antare kare ca dahyamānam sat cintayet tad japa eka yuj  vahni dīpita phaṭkāra dhoraṇī dāha pīḍitam bījam nirbīja tām eti sva sūti karaṇa akṣamam taptam na etad prarohāya tena eva pratyayena tu mala māyā ākhya karmāṇi mantra dhyāna kriyā balāt dagdhāni na sva kāryāya nirbīja pratyayam tu imam sa śrīmān su prasannaḥ  me śaṃbhunāthaḥ nyarūpayat  bījasya api atra kāryā ca yojanā kṛpayā guroḥ yatas  dīkṣā su dīpta tvāt sthāvarāṇi api mocayet  yaḥ  guruḥ japa homa arcā dhyāna siddha tvam ātmani jñātvā dīkṣām caret tasya dīkṣā sa pratyayā smṛtā avadhūte nirācāre tattva jñe na tu ayam vidhiḥ sa ācāraiḥ kriyate dīkṣā yā dṛṣṭa pratyaya anvitā nirācāreṇa dīkṣāyām pratyayaḥ tu na gadyate jñānam sva pratyayam yasmāt na phala antaram arhati dhyāna ādi tu phalāt sādhyam iti siddhāmata uditam tulā śuddhi parīkṣām vā kuryāt pratyaya yoginīm yathā śrī tantra sadbhāve kathitā parameśinā śrī pūrvaśāstre pyeṣā ca sūcitā parameśinā ānanda udbhavaḥ kampaḥ  nidrā ghūrṇiḥ ca pañcamī iti evaṃvadatā śakti tāratamya abhidhāyinā udbhavaḥ  laghu bhāvena deha graha tirohiteḥ dehaḥ  hi pārthivaḥ  mukhyaḥ tadā mukhya tvam ujjhati bhāvi lāghava mantreṇa śiṣyam dhyātvā samutplutam karmāṇi tatra aśeṣāṇi pūrva uktāni ācaret guruḥ uktā sā iyam tulā śuddhi dīkṣā pratyaya dāyinī  ch atha śrī tantrāloke ekaviṃśatitamam āhnikam parokṣa saṃsthitasya atha dīkṣā karma nigadyate bhukti mukti prasiddhi artham nīyate sat gurum prati iti asmin mālinī vākye pratiḥ sāṃmukhyā vācakaḥ sāṃmukhyam ca asya śiṣyasya tad kṛpā āspadatā ātmakam tam ārādhya iti vacanam kṛpā hetu upalakṣaṇam tad saṃbandhāt tatas  kaścid tad kṣaṇāt apavṛjyate iti asya ayam api hi arthaḥ  mālinī vākya sat maṇeḥ tad kṣaṇāt iti na asya asti yiyāsa ādi kṣaṇa antaram kiṃtu evam eva karuṇā nighnaḥ tam guruḥ uddharet  guru sevā kṣīṇa tanoḥ dīkṣām aprāpya pañcatām gatasya atha svayam mṛtyu kṣaṇa udita tathā aruceḥ athavā adhara tantra ādi dīkṣā saṃskāra bhāginaḥ prāpta sāmayikasya atha parām dīkṣām avindataḥ ḍimba āhatasya yogeśī bhakṣitasya abhicārataḥ mṛtasya guruṇā yantra tantra ādi nihatasya vā bhraṣṭa sva samayasya atha dīkṣām prāptavataḥ  pyalam bandhu bhāryā suhṛd putra gāḍha abhyarthana yogataḥ svayam tad viṣaya utpanna karuṇā balataḥ  pi vā vijñāta tad mukha āyāta śaktipāta aṃśa dharmaṇaḥ guruḥ dīkṣām mṛtoddhārīm kurvīta śiva dāyinīm śrī mṛtyuñjaya siddha ādau tad uktam parameśinā adīkṣite nṛpati ādau  alase patite mṛte bāla ātura strī vṛddhe ca mṛtoddhāram prakalpayet  vidhiḥ sarvaḥ pūrvam uktaḥ sa tu saṃkṣipta iṣyate guru ādi pūjā rahitaḥ  bāhye bhogāya sā yatas  adhivāsa caru kṣetram śayyā maṇḍala kalpane na upayogi atra tad śiṣya saṃskriyā svapna dṛṣṭaye mantra saṃnidhi saṃtṛpti yogāyātra tu maṇḍalam bhūyas dine ca deva arcā sākṣāt na asya upakāri tad  kriyā upakaraṇa sthāna maṇḍala ākṛti mantrataḥ dhyāna yoga eka tad bhakti jñāna tanmaya bhāvataḥ tad praviṣṭasya kasya api śiṣyāṇām ca guroḥ tathā ekādaśā ete kathitāḥ saṃnidhānāya hetavaḥ uttarottaram utkṛṣṭāḥ tathā vyāmiśraṇā vaśāt  kriyā atibhūyasī puṣpa ādi uttamam lakṣaṇa anvitam eka liṅga ādi ca sthānam yatra ātmā saṃprasīdati maṇḍalam tri triśūla abja cakram yad mantra maṇḍale anāhūte pi dṛṣṭam sat samayitva prasādhanam tad uktam mālinītantre siddham samaya maṇḍalam yena saṃdṛṣṭa mātrā iti siddha mātra pada dvayāt  ākṛtiḥ dīpta rūpā yā mantraḥ tadvat su dīptikaḥ śiṣṭam spaṣṭam atas  na iha kathitam vistarāt punar  kṛtvā maṇḍalam abhyarcya tatra devam kuśaiḥ atha gomayena ākṛtim kuryāt śiṣyavat tām nidhāpayet  tatas tasyām śodhyam ekam adhvānam vyāpti bhāvanāt  prakṛti antam vinikṣipya punar enam vidhim caret  mahā jāla prayogeṇa sarvasmāt adhva madhyataḥ cittam ākṛṣya tatrastham kuryāt tad vidhiḥ ucyate mūlādhārāt udetya prasṛta su vitata ananta nāḍī adhva daṇḍam vīryeṇa ākramya nāsā gagana parigatam vikṣipan vyāptum īṣṭe c yāvat dhūma abhirāma pracitatara śikhā jālakena adhva cakram saṃchādya abhīṣṭa jīva ānayanam iti mahājāla nāmā prayogaḥ etena ācchādanīyam vrajati para vaśam saṃmukhīna tvam ādau pañcāt ānīyate ced sakalam atha tatas  pyadhva madhyāt yatheṣṭam ākṛṣṭau  uddhṛtau vā mṛta jana viṣaye karṣaṇīye tha jīve yogaḥ śrī śaṃbhu nātha āgama parigamitaḥ  jāla nāmā mayā uktaḥ cira vighaṭite senā yugmeyathā milite punar haya gaja naram svām svām jātim rasāt abhidhāvati karaṇa pavanaiḥ nāḍī cakraiḥ tathā eva samāgataiḥ nija nija rasāt ekībhāvyam sva jāla vaśīkṛtaiḥ mahā jāla samākṛṣṭaḥ  jīvaḥ  vijñāna śālinā svar preta tiryak nirayān  tadā eva eṣa vimuñcati tad jñāna mantra yoga āptaḥ puruṣaḥ ca eṣa kṛtrimam yogī iva sādhya hṛdayāt tadā tādātmyam ujjhati sthāvara ādi daśāḥ citrāḥ tad sa loka samīpa tāḥ tyajet ca iti na citram sa evam yaḥ karmaṇā api vā adhikāri śarīra tvāt mānuṣye tu śarīra gaḥ na tadā mucyate dehāt deha ante tu śivam vrajet  tasmin dehe tu kāpyasya jāyate śāṅkarī parā bhaktiḥ ūhāt ca vijñānāt ācāryāt vāpi asevitāt tad deha saṃsthitaḥ  pyeṣa jīvaḥ  jāla bala ādimam dārbha ādi deham vyāpnoti sva adhiṣṭhitya api acetayan yoga mantra kriyā jñāna bhūyas bala vaśāt punar  manuṣya deham api eṣa tadā eva āśu vimuñcati supta kalpaḥ  pyadehaḥ  pi yaḥ  jīvaḥ saḥ  pi jālataḥ ākṛṣṭaḥ  dārbham āyāti deham phala mayam ca vā jātīphala ādi yad kiṃcid tena vā deha kalpanā antar bahis dvaya aucityāt tad atra utkṛṣṭam ucyate tatas  jāla krama ānītaḥ sa jīvaḥ suptavat sthitaḥ manaḥ viśiṣṭa deha ādi sāmagrī prāpti abhāvataḥ na spandate na jānāti na vakti na kila icchati tādṛśasya eva saṃskārān sarvān prāgvat prakalpayet  nirbīja dīkṣā yogena sarvam kṛtvā purā uditam vidhim yojanikām pūrṇāhutyā sākam kṣipet ca tam dārbha ādi dehe mantra agnau  arpite pūrṇayā saha mukta pāśaḥ śivam yāti punarāvṛtti varjitaḥ sa pratyayā tu iyam yatra spandate darbha jā tanuḥ tatra prāṇa manaḥ mantra arpaṇa yogāt tathā bhavet  sa abhyāsasya tad api uktam balāśvāsi na tad kṛte mṛtoddhāra uditaiḥ eva yathā saṃbhūti hetubhiḥ jīvat parokṣa dīkṣā api kāryā nirbījikā tu sā tasyām darbha ākṛti prāya kalpane jāla yogataḥ saṃkalpa mātreṇa ākarṣaḥ  jīvasya mṛti bhītitaḥ śiṣṭam prāgvat kuśa ādi uttha ākāra viploṣa varjitam pārimityāt anaiśvaryāt sādhye niyati yantraṇāt  jāla ākṛṣṭiḥ vinā abhyāsam rāga dveṣāt na jāyate parokṣa eva atulyābhiḥ dīkṣābhiḥ yadi dīkṣitaḥ tatra uttaram syāt balavat saṃskārāya tu adhastanam bhukti yojanikāyām tu bhūyobhiḥ gurubhiḥ tathā kṛtāyām bhoga vaicitryam hetu vaicitrya yogataḥ parokṣa dīkṣaṇe māyā uttīrṇe bhogāya yojayet  bhogānīpsā durlabhā hi satī vā bhoga hānaye uktam hi sva anya saṃvittyoḥ sva saṃvid balavattarā bādhaka tve bādhikā asau sāmya audāsīnyayoḥ tathā śrīmān dharma śivaḥ  pyāha pārokṣyām karma paddhatau parokṣa dīkṣaṇe samyak  pūrṇāhuti vidhau yadi agniḥ ciṭiciṭā śabdam sa dhūmam pratimuñcati dhatte nīla ambuda  chāyām muhur jvalati śāmyati vistaraḥ  ghora rūpaḥ ca mahīm dhāvati ca api adhas  dhvāṃkṣa ādya śravya śabdaḥ  vā tadā tam lakṣayet guruḥ brahmahatyā ādibhiḥ pāpaiḥ tad saṅgaiḥ ca upapātakaiḥ tadā tasya na kartavyā dīkṣā asmin  akṛte vidhau nava ātmā phaṣ puṭa antar sthaḥ punar  pañca phaṭ anvitaḥ amukasya iti pāpāni dahāmi anu phaṭ aṣṭakam iti sāhasrikaḥ  homaḥ kartavyaḥ tila taṇḍulaiḥ ante pūrṇā ca dātavyā tatas  smai dīkṣayā guruḥ para yojana paryantam kuryāt tattva viśodhanam pratyakṣe pi sthitasya aṇoḥ pāpinaḥ  bhagavat mayīm śaktim prāptavataḥ  jyeṣṭhām evam eva vidhim caret  yadi vā daiśikaḥ samyak  na dīptaḥ tasya tad purā prāyaścittaiḥ tathā dānaiḥ prāṇāyāmaiḥ ca śodhanam kṛtvā vidhim imām ca api dīkṣām kuryāt aśaṅkitaḥ sarvathā vartamānaḥ  pi tattva vid mocayet paśūn icchayā eva śivaḥ sākṣāt tasmāt tam pūjayet sadā śāṭhyam tatra na kāryam ca tad kṛtvā adhaḥ vrajet śiśuḥ na punar  kīrtayet tasya pāpam kīrtayitā vrajet  nirayam varjayet tasmāt iti dīkṣā uttare vidhiḥ eṣā parokṣa dīkṣā dvidhā uditā jīvaditara bhedena  ch atha śrī tantrāloke dvāviṃśatitamam āhnikam liṅga uddhārā ākhyām atha vacmaḥ śiva śāsana eka nirdiṣṭām uktam śrī mālinītantre kila pārthiva dhāraṇām uktvā yaḥ  yojitaḥ  yatra sa tasmāt na nivartate yogyatā vaśa saṃjātā yasya yatra eva śāsanā sa tatra eva niyoktavyaḥ  dīkṣā kāle tatas tu asau phalam sarvam samāsādya śive yuktaḥ  pavṛjyate ayuktaḥ  pyūrdhva saṃśuddhim saṃprāpya bhuvaneśataḥ śuddhaḥ śiva tvam āyāti dagdha saṃsāra bandhanaḥ uktvā puṃdhāraṇām ca uktam etad vaidāntikam mayā kapilāya purā proktam prathame paṭale tathā anena krama yogena saṃprāptaḥ paramam padam na bhūyas  paśu tām eti śuddhe sva ātmani tiṣṭhati atas  hi dhvanyate rthaḥ  yam śiva tattva adhareṣu api tattveṣu yojitasya asti punar uddharaṇīyatā samasta śāstra kathita vastu vaivikti adāyinaḥ śiva āgamasya sarvebhyaḥ  pyāgamebhyaḥ  viśiṣṭa tā śiva jñānena ca vinā bhūyaḥ pi paśu ta udbhavaḥ kramaḥ ca śakti saṃpātaḥ  mala hāniḥ yiyāsu tā dīkṣā bodhaḥ  heya hāniḥ upādeya laya ātma tā bhogyatva pāśava tyāgaḥ pati kartṛtva saṃkṣayaḥ sva ātma sthitiḥ ca iti evam hi darśana antara saṃsthiteḥ proktam uddharaṇīya tvam śiva śakti īritasya hi atha vaiṣṇava bauddha ādi tantra anta adhara vartinām yadā śiva arka raśmi oghaiḥ vikāsi hṛdaya ambujam liṅga uddhṛtiḥ tadā pūrvam dīkṣā karma tatas  param prāc liṅga antara saṃsthaḥ  pi dīkṣātaḥ śiva tām vrajet  tatra upavāsya tam ca anya dine
