sa ādhāra mantrataḥ sthaṇḍile pūjayitvā īśam śrāvayet tasya vartanīm eṣa prāc abhavat liṅgī coditaḥ tu adhunā tvayā prasannena tadetasmai kuru samyak anugraham sva liṅga tyāga śaṅkā uttham prāyaścittam ca māsya bhūt  acirāt tvad mayībhūya bhogam mokṣam prapadyatām evam astu iti atha ājñām ca gṛhīrvā vratam asya tad  apāsya ambhasi nikṣipya snapayet anurūpatas  snātam saṃprokṣayet argha pātra ambhobhiḥ anantaram pañcagavyam dantakāṣṭham tatas tasmai samarpayet  tatas tam baddha netram ca praveśya praṇipātayet  praṇavaḥ  mātṛkā māyā vyoma vyāpī ṣaṣ akṣaraḥ bahu rūpaḥ  tha netra ākhyaḥ sapta sādhāraṇā amī teṣām madhyāt ekatamam mantram asmai samarpayet  saḥ  pi ahorātram eva enam japet alpa bhuj api abhuj  mantram asmai samarpya atha sa ādhāra vidhi saṃskṛte vahnau tarpita tad mantre vrata śuddhim samācaret  pūjitena eva mantreṇa kṛtvā nāma asya saṃpuṭam prāyaścittam śodhayāmi phaṭsvāha iti ūha yogataḥ śatam sahasram vā hutvā punar  pūrṇāhutim tathā prayogāt vauṣaṭ antām ca kṣiptvā āhūya vrateśvaram tāraḥ  vrateśvarāya iti namaḥ ca iti enam arcayet śrāvayet ca tvayā na asya kāryam kiṃcid śiva ājñayā tatas  vrateśvaraḥ tarpyaḥ svāhā antena tatas ca saḥ kṣamayitvā visṛjyaḥ syāt tatas  gneḥ ca visarjanam tad śrāvaṇam ca devāya kṣamasva iti visarjanam tatas tṛtīya divase prāgvat sarvaḥ  vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ adhivāsa ādikaḥ sva iṣṭa dīkṣā karma avasānakaḥ prāc liṅginām mokṣa dīkṣā sādhikāra vivarjitā sādhaka ācārya tā mārge na yogyāḥ te punarbhuvaḥ punarbhuvaḥ  pi jñāna iddhā bhavanti gurutā āspadam mokṣāya eva na bhogāya bhogāya api abhyupāyataḥ iti uktavān svapaddhatyām īśāna śiva daiśikaḥ śrī devyā yāmalīyokti tattva samyak pravedakaḥ guru antasya api adhodṛṣṭi śāyinaḥ saṃskriyām imām kṛtvā rahasyam kathayet na anyathā kāmike kila anya tantra abhiṣikte pi rahasyam na prakāśayet  svatantra sthaḥ  pi guru antaḥ  guru m ajñam upāśritaḥ tatra paścāt anāśvastaḥ tatra api vidhim ācaret  ajñācārya mukha āyātam nirvīryam mantram eṣa yad  japtavān sa guruḥ ca atra na adhikāri ukta dūṣaṇāt tatas  sya śuddhim prāk kṛtvā tatas  dīkṣām samācaret  adhas darśana saṃsthena guruṇā dīkṣitaḥ purā tīvra śakti vaśāt paścāt yadā gacchet sa sat gurum tadā api asya śiśoḥ evam śuddhim kṛtvā sa sat guruḥ dīkṣā ādi karma nikhilam kuryāt ukta vidhānataḥ prāptaḥ  pi sat guruḥ yogya bhāvam asya na vetti ced  vijñāna dāne tad śiṣyaḥ  yogyatām darśayet nijām sarvathā tu abruvan  eṣa bruvāṇaḥ  vā viparyayam ajñaḥ vastuta eva iti tad tyaktvā ittham vidhim caret  na tirobhāva śaṅkā atra kartavyā buddhi śālinā adhas spṛś tvam tirobhūtiḥ na ūrdhva upāya vivecanam siddhānte dīkṣitāḥ tantre daśa aṣṭādaśa bhedini bhairavīye catuḥṣaṣṭau tān paśūn dīkṣayet trike siddha vīra āvalī sāre bhairavīye kule pi ca pañca dīkṣā krama upāttā dīkṣā anuttara saṃjñitā tena sarvaḥ  dhara sthaḥ  pi liṅga uddhṛtya anugṛhyate yaḥ  pi hṛd stha maheśāna codanātaḥ su vistṛtam śāstra jñānam samanvicchet saḥ  pi yāyāt bahūn gurūn tad dīkṣāḥ ca api gṛhṇīyāt abhiṣecana paścimāḥ jñāna upodbalikāḥ tā hi tad tad jñānavatā kṛtāḥ uktam ca śrīmate śāstre tatra tatra ca bhūyasā āmoda arthī yathā bhṛṅgaḥ puṣpāt puṣpa antaram vrajet  vijñāna arthī tathā śiṣyaḥ  guroḥ guḥ u antaram tu iti gurūṇām bhūyasām madhye yatas  vijñānam uttamam prāptam saḥ  sya guruḥ dīkṣā na atra mukhyā hi saṃvidi sarva jñāna nidhānam tu gurum saṃprāpya susthitaḥ tam eva ārādhayet dhīmān  tad tad jijñāsana unmukhaḥ iti dīkṣā vidhiḥ proktaḥ  liṅga uddharaṇa paścimaḥ  ch atha śrī tantrāloke trayoviṃśatitamam āhnikam atha abhiṣekasya vidhiḥ kathyate pārameśvaraḥ yā eṣā putraka dīkṣā uktā guru sādhakayoḥ api sā eva adhikāriṇī bhogya tattva yuktimatī kramāt  su abhyasta jñāninam santam bubhūṣum atha bhāvinam yogyam jñātvā sva adhikāram guruḥ tasmai samarpayet  yaḥ  na evam veda na eva asau  abhiṣiktaḥ  pi daiśikaḥ samayi ādi krameṇa iti śrīmat kāmika ucyate yaḥ  na veda adhva sandhānam ṣoḍhā bāhya antara sthitam sa guruḥ mocayet na iti siddhayogīśvarīmate sarva lakṣaṇa hīnaḥ  pi jñānavān guruḥ iṣyate jñāna prādhānyam eva uktam iti śrī kaca bhārgave pada vākya pramāṇa jñaḥ śiva bhakti eka tatparaḥ samasta śiva śāstra artha boddhā kāruṇikaḥ  guruḥ na svayaṃbhūḥ tasya ca uktam lakṣaṇam parameśinā abhaktaḥ  jīvita dhiyā kurvan  īśān adhiṣṭhitaḥ paśca ātmanā svayaṃbhu uṣṇuḥ na adhikārī sa kutracid  bhasma aṅkuraḥ  vratisutaḥ  duḥśīla atanayaḥ tathā kuṇḍaḥ golaḥ ca te duṣṭā uktam devī ākhya yāmale punarbhūḥ ca anyaliṅgaḥ  yaḥ punar  śaive pratiṣṭhitaḥ śrī pūrvaśāstre na tu eṣa niyamaḥ kaḥ  pi coditaḥ yathārtha tattva saṃgha jñaḥ tathā śiṣye prakāśakaḥ yaḥ punar  sarva tattvāni vetti ityādi ca lakṣaṇam yoga cāre ca yadi atra tantre coditam ācaret  tathā eva siddhaye sā iyam ājñā iti kila varṇitam yaḥ tu karmi tayā ācāryaḥ tatra kāṇa ādi varjanam yatas  kāraka sāmagryāt karmaṇaḥ  na adhikaḥ kvacid  devyā yāmala śāstre ca kāñcī ādi parivarjanam tad dṛṣṭa doṣāt krodha ādeḥ samyak jñātarī asau kutas  guravaḥ tu svayaṃbhvādi varjyam yadyāmala ādiṣu karmi abhiprāyataḥ sarvam tad iti vyācacakṣire atas  deśa kula ācāra deha lakṣaṇa kalpanām anādṛtya eva saṃpūrṇa jñānam kuryāt guruḥ gurum prāgvat saṃpūjya hutvā ca śrāvayitvā cikīrṣitam tatas  bhiṣiñcet tam śiṣyam catuḥṣaṣṭyā tatas  sakṛt  tad mantra rasa toyena pūrva ukta vidhinā guruḥ vibhavena su vistīrṇam tatas tasmai vadet svakam sarvam kartavya sāram yad śāstrāṇām paramam rahaḥ anugrāhyāḥ tvayā śiṣyāḥ śiva śakti pracoditāḥ uktam jñāna uttare ca etad brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā viśaḥ napuṃsakāḥ striyaḥ śūdrā ye ca anye pi tad arthinaḥ te dīkṣāyām na mīmāṃsyā jñāna kāle vicārayet  jñāna mūlaḥ  guruḥ proktaḥ sapta satrīm pravartayet  dīkṣā vyākhyā kṛpā maitrī śāstra cintā śivā eka tā anna ādi dānam iti etad pālayet sapta satrakam abhiṣeka vidhau ca asmai karaṇī khaṭikā ādikam sarva upakaraṇa vrātam arpaṇīyam vipaścite saḥ  bhiṣiktaḥ  gurum paścāt dakṣiṇābhiḥ prapūjayet  jñāna hīnaḥ  guruḥ karmī sva adhikāram samarpya naḥ dīkṣā ādi adhikṛtim kuryāt vinā tasya ājñayā punar  iti evam śrāvayet saḥ pi namaskṛtyā abhinandayet  tatas  prabhṛti asau pūrvaḥ guruḥ tyakta adhikārakaḥ yathā iccham vicaret vyākhyādīkṣa ādau yantraṇā ujjhitaḥ kurvan  bādhyate yasmāt dīpāt dīpavat īdṛśaḥ santānaḥ  na adhikārasya cyavaḥ  kurvan  bādhyate prāk  ca kurvan vihanyeta siddhātantre tad ucyate yathārtham upadeśam tu kurvan  ācārya ucyate na ca avajñā kriyā kāle saṃsāra uddharaṇam prati na dīkṣeta guruḥ śiṣyam tattva yuktaḥ tu garvataḥ yaḥ  sya syāt narake vāsa iha ca vyādhitaḥ  bhavet  prāpta abhiṣekaḥ sa guruḥ ṣaṣ māsāt mantra paddhatim sarvām tantra uditām dhyāyet japet ca ātanmaya tvataḥ yadā eva tanmayībhūtaḥ tadā vīryam upāgataḥ chindyāt pāśān  tatas  yatnam kuryāt tad maya tā sthitau hṛd cakrāt utthitā sūkṣmā śaśi sphaṭika saṃnibhā lekha ākārā nāda rūpā praśāntā cakra paṅkti gā dvādaśānte nirūḍhā sā sauṣumne tripathā antare tatra hṛd cakram āpūrya japet mantram jvalat prabham cakṣuḥ loma ādi randhra ogha vahat jvālā auru asaṃnibham yāvat śānta śikhā ākīrṇam viśva ājya pravilāpakam tad ājya dhārā saṃtṛpta māna abhikuhara antaram evam mantrā mokṣa dāḥ syuḥ dīptā buddhāḥ su nirmalāḥ mūla kandana bhona abhihṛd kaṇṭha ālika tālu gam ardha indu rodhi kā nādata danta vyāpi śakti gam samanonmana śuddha ātma para cakra samāśritam yatra yatra japet cakre samasta vyasta bhedanāt  tatra tatra mahāmantra iti devī ākhya yāmale vidyā vratam idam proktam mantra vīrya prasiddhaye tad ca tādātmyam eva iti yad uktam spandaśāsane tad ā ākramya balam mantrāḥ sarvajña bala śālinaḥ pravartante dhikārāya karaṇāni iva dehinām kṛtavidyā vrataḥ paścāt dīkṣā vyākhya ādi sarvatas  kuryāt yogyeṣu śiṣyeṣu na ayogyeṣu kadācana rahasye yojayet vipram parīkṣya viparītatas ācārāt śaktim api eva na anyathā iti ūrmi śāsane nitya ādi alpa alpakam kuryāt yad uktam brahmayāmale cīrṇa vidyā vrataḥ sarvam manasā vā smaret priye deha saṃbandha saṃchanna sārvajñyaḥ  dambha bhājanam avidandi īkṣamāṇaḥ  pi na duṣyet daiśikaḥ kvacid  jñātvā tu ayā ugya tām na enam dīkṣeta pratyavāyitām buddhvā jñāne śāstra siddhi gurutva ādau ca tam punar  bhūya eva parīkṣeta tad tad aucitya śālinam tatra tatra niyuñjīta na tu jātu viparyayāt  nanu tad vastu ayogyasya tatra icchā jāyate kutas  tad īśa adhiṣṭhita icchā eva yogya tām asya sūcayet  satyam kā api prabuddha asau  icchā rūḍhim na gacchati vidyutvat pāpa śīlasya yathā pāpa apavarjane rūḍhya rūḍhī tad icchāyāḥ  api śaṃbhu prasādataḥ aprarūḍha tathā icchākaḥ tatas  eva na bhājanam yaḥ samyak jñānam ādāya guru viśvāsa varjitaḥ lokam viplāvayet na asmin jñāte vijñānam arpayet  ajñāte pi punar jñāte vijñāna haraṇam caret  punar punar yadā jñātaḥ  viśvāsa parivarjitaḥ tadā tam agratas  dhyāyet sphurantam candra sūryavat  tatas  nija hṛd ambhoja bodha ambara tala uditām svarbhānu malinām dhyāyet vāmām śaktim vimohanīm vāma ācāra krameṇa enām niḥsṛtām sādhya gāminīm cintayitvā tayā grasta prakāśam tam vicintayet  anena krama yogena mūḍha buddheḥ durātmanaḥ vijñāna mantra vidyā ādyāḥ prakurvanti apakāritām nanu vijñānam ātma stham katham hartum kṣamam bhavet  atas  vijñāna haraṇam katham śrī pūrva ucyate ucyate na asya śiṣyasya vijñānam rūḍhim āgatam tathā tve haraṇam kasmāt pūrṇa yogyatva śālinaḥ kiṃtu eṣa vāmayā śaktyā mūḍhaḥ  gāḍham vibhoḥ kṛtaḥ svabhāvāt eva tena asya vidyā ādyam apakārakam guruḥ punar  śiva abhinnaḥ sanyaḥ pañcavidhām kṛtim kuryāt yadi tatas  pūrṇam adhikāri tvam asya tad  atas  yathā śuddha tattva sṛṣṭi sthityoḥ malātyaye yojana anugrahe kārya catuṣke dhikṛtaḥ  guruḥ śiva abhedena tad kuryāt tadvat pañcamam api ayam tirobhāva abhidham kṛtyam tathā asau śiva tā ātmakaḥ ata eva śive śāstre jñāne ca āśvāsa bhājanam guroḥ mūḍha tayā kopa dhāmā api na tirohitaḥ guruḥ hi kupitaḥ  yasya sa tirohita ucyate saṃsārī satu devaḥ  hi guruḥ na ca mṛṣāvidaḥ tatas  eva ca śāstra ādi dūṣa kaḥ yadi api krudhā na dahyate sau guruṇā tathā api eṣa tirohitaḥ asmad guru āgamaḥ tu eṣa tirobhūte svayam śiśau na kupyet na śapet dhīmān sa hi anugrāhakaḥ sadā īśa icchā coditaḥ pāśam yadi kaṇṭhe nipīḍayet  kim ācāryeṇa tatra asya kāryā syāt sahakāritā śiva abhinnaḥ pi hi guruḥ anugraha mayīm vibhoḥ mukhyām śaktim upāsīnaḥ  nugṛhṇīyāt sa sarvathā svātantrya mātra jñaptyai tu kathitam śāstra īdṛśam na kāryam patatām hasta ālambaḥ sahyaḥ  na pātanam ata eva svatantra tvāt icchāyāḥ punar unmukham prāyaścittaiḥ viśodhya enam dīkṣeta kṛpayā guruḥ ūrdhva dṛṣṭau prapannaḥ sannanāśvastaḥ tatas  param adhas śāstram prapadya api na śreyaḥ pātra tām iyāt  adhodṛṣṭau prapannaḥ tu tad anāśvasta mānasaḥ ūrdhva śāsana bhāj  pāpam tad ca ujjhet ca śivībhavet  rājñe druhi an  amātyā aṅga bhūtaḥ  pi hi vihanyate viparyayaḥ tu na iti evam ūrdhvām dṛṣṭim samāśrayet  śrī pūrvaśāstre tena uktam yāvat tena eva na uddhṛtaḥ atra hi arthaḥ  yam etāvat pūrva ukta jñāna vṛṃhitaḥ guruḥ tāvat sa eva atra tad śabdena avamṛśyate tādṛś su abhyasta vijñāna bhāja ūrdhva pada śālinā anuddhṛtasya na śreya etad anya guru uddhṛteḥ ata eva ambujanma arka dṛṣṭāntaḥ  tra nirūpitaḥ trijagat jyotiṣaḥ  hi anyat tejaḥ  nyat ca niśā kṛtaḥ jñānam anyat trika guroḥ anyattva dhara vartinām ata eva purā bhūta guru abhāvaḥ  yadā tadā tad anyam lakṣaṇa upetam āśrayet punar unmukhaḥ sati tasmin  tu unmukhaḥ san kasmāt jahyāt yadi sphuṭam syāt anyatara gaḥ doṣaḥ  yaḥ  dhikārāpa ghātakaḥ doṣaḥ ca iha na loka sthaḥ  doṣa tvena nirūpyate ajñāna khyāpanā yukta khyāpana ātmā tu asau mataḥ śiṣyasya api tathābhūta jñānānāśvasta rūpa tā mukhyaḥ  doṣaḥ tad anye hi doṣāḥ tad prabhavā yatas  na dhvasta vyādhikaḥ kaḥ  hi bhiṣajam bahu manyate asūyuḥ nūna m adhvasta vyādhiḥ svasthāyate balāt  evam jñāna samāśvastaḥ kim kim na gurave caret  naḥ ced nūnam aviśvastaḥ  viśvasta iva tiṣṭhati ajñāna ādaya eva ete doṣā na laukikā guroḥ iti khyāpayitum proktam mālinīvijayottare na tasya anveṣayet vṛttam śubham vā yadi vā aśubham sa eva tad vijānāti yuktam ca ayuktam eva vā akāryeṣu yadā saktaḥ prāṇa dravya apahāriṣu tadā nivāraṇīyaḥ  sau praṇatena vipaścitā viśeṣaṇam akāryāṇa am ukta abhiprāyam eva yad  tena ati vāryamāṇaḥ  pi yadi asau na nivartate tadā anyatra kvacid gatvā śivam eva anucintayet na hi asya sa guru tve syāt doṣaḥ  yena ūṣare kṛṣim kuryāt vrajet niśāyām vā sa tu artha prāṇa hārakaḥ tadīya apriya bhīruḥ tu param tādṛśam ācaret  yatas tad apriyam na eṣa śṛṇuyāt iti bhāṣitam śrī mātaṅge tad uktam ca na adhītam bhūma bhītitaḥ yad ca etad uktam etāvat kartavyam iti tad dhruvam tīvra śakti gṛhītānām svayam eva hṛdi sphuret  upadeśaḥ tu ayam manda madhya śakteḥ nijām kramāt  śaktim jvalayitum proktaḥ sā hi evam jājvalī iti alam dṛḍha anurāga subhaga saṃrambha ābhoga bhāginaḥ sva ullāsi smara sarvasyam dārḍhyāya anyatra dṛśyate nanu eṣa kasmāt dṛṣṭāntaḥ kim etena aśubham kṛtam cit spandaḥ sarva gaḥ bhinnāt upādheḥ sa tathā tathā bhavet kaḥ pi tirobhūtaḥ punar unmukhitaḥ  pi san vinā api daiśikāt prāgvat svayam eva vimucyate prakāraḥ tu eṣa na atra uktaḥ śaktipāta balāt gataḥ asaṃbhāvya tayā ca atra dṛḍha kopa prasādavat  iti eṣa yaḥ  guroḥ proktaḥ  vidhiḥ tam pālayet guruḥ anyathā na śivam yāyāt śrīmat sāre ca varṇitam anyāyam ye prakurvanti śāstra artham varjayanti alam te rdhanārīśa pura gā guravaḥ samaya cyutāḥ anyatra api adhikāram ca na iyāt vidyeśatām vrajet  anyatra samaya tyāgāt kravyāda tvam śatam samāḥ iyat tatratyatātparyam siddhānta guruḥ unnayaḥ bhavet piśāca vidyeśaḥ śuddha eva tu tāntrikaḥ ṣaṣ ardha daiśikaḥ ca ardhanārīśa bhuvana sthitiḥ eṣā karma pradhānānām gurūṇām gatiḥ ucyate jñāninām ca eṣa naḥ bandha iti sarvatra varṇitam sādhakasya abhiṣeke pi sarvaḥ  yam kathyate vidhiḥ adhikāra arpaṇam na atra na ca vidyā vratam kila sādhya mantra arpaṇam tu atra sva upayogi kriyā krame samaste pyupadeśaḥ syāt nija upakaraṇa arpaṇam abhiṣeka vidhiḥ nirūpitaḥ parameśena yathā nirūpitaḥ  ch atha śrī tantrāloke caturviṃśatitamam āhnikam atha śāmbhava śāsana uditām sa rahasyām śṛṇuta antya saṃskriyām b sarveṣām adhara sthānām guru antānām api sphuṭam śaktipātāt purā proktāt kuryāt antyeṣṭi dīkṣaṇam ūrdhva śāsana gānām ca samaya upahata ātmanām antyeṣṭi dīkṣā kartavyā guruṇā tattva vedinā samaya ācāra doṣeṣu pramādāt skhalitasya hi antyeṣṭi dīkṣā kāryā iti śrī dīkṣā uttara śāsane yad kiṃcid kathitam pūrvam mṛtoddhāra abhidhe vidhau pratimāyām tad eva atra sarvam śava tanau caret  śrī siddha atantra kathitaḥ  vidhiḥ eṣa nirūpyate antimam yad bhavet pūrvam tad kṛtvā antimama ādimam saṃhṛtya ekaikam iṣṭiḥ yā sāntya iṣṭiḥ dvitayī matā pūjā dhyāna japa āpluṣṭa samaye na tu sādhake piṇḍa pāta āt ayam muktaḥ khecaraḥ  vā bhavet priye ācārye tattva saṃpanne yatra tatra mṛte sati antyeṣṭiḥ na eva vidyeta śuddha cetasya mūrdhani mantra yoga ādibhiḥ ye ca māritā narake tu te kāryā teṣām iha antyeṣṭiḥ guruṇā ati kṛpālunā na maṇḍala ādikam tu atra bhavet śamāśānike vidhau kecid tad api kartavyam ūcire preta sadmani pūjayitvā vibhum sarvam nyāsam pūrvavat ācaret  saṃhāra krama yogena caraṇāt mūrdha paścimam tathā eva bodhayet enam kriyā jñāna samādhibhiḥ bindunā rodhayet tattvam śakti bījena vedhayet  ghaṭṭayet nāda deśe tu triśūlena tu tāḍayet  suṣumnā antargatena eva visargeṇa punar  punar  tāḍayeta kalāḥ sarvāḥ kampate sau tatas  paśuḥ utkṣipet vāma hastam vā tatas tam yojayet pare pratyayena vinā mokṣaḥ  hi aśraddheyaḥ  vimohitaiḥ tad artham etad uditam na tu mokṣa upayogi daḥ iti ūce parameśaḥ śrī kula gahvara śāsane sādhyaḥ  numeyaḥ  mokṣa ādiḥ pratyayaiḥ yad atīndriyaḥ dīkṣā uttare ca puryaṣṭa varga arpaṇam iha uditam tad vidhiḥ śruti patre bje madhye devam sadāśivam īśa rudra hari brahma catuṣkam prāc diś āditaḥ pūjayitvā śruti sparśau rasam gandham vapuḥ dvayam dhyahaṃkṛtī manaḥ ca iti brahma ādiṣu arpayet kramāt  eteṣām tarpaṇam kṛtvā śata homena daiśikaḥ eṣā sāṃnyāsikī dīkṣā puryaṣṭaka viśodhanī puryaṣṭakasya abhāve ca na svarga naraka ādayaḥ tathā kṛtvā na kartavyam laukikam kiṃcana api hi uktam śrī mādhava kule śāsana sthaḥ  mṛteṣu api piṇḍa pāta udaka asrvādi laukikam parivarjayet  śivam saṃpūjya cakra arcām yathāśakti samācaret  kramāt tridaśam atriṃśatriṃśa vatsara vāsare iti uktaḥ  ntyeṣṭi yāgaḥ  yam parameśvara bhāṣitaḥ  ch atha śrī tantrāloke pañcaviṃśatitamam āhnikam atha śrāddha vidhiḥ śrīmat ṣaṣ ardha uktaḥ  nigadyate b siddhātantre sūcitaḥ  sau mūrti yāga nirūpaṇe antyeṣṭyā su viśuddhānām aśuddhānām ca tad vidhiḥ tri ahe turye hni daśame māsi māsi ādi vatsare varṣe varṣe sarva kālam kāryaḥ tad svaiḥ sa pūrvavat  tatra prāgvat yajet devam homayet anale tathā tatas  naivedyam eva prāk gṛhītvā hasta gocare guruḥ anna mayīm śaktim vṛṃhikām vīrya rūpiṇīm dhyātvā tayā samāviṣṭam tam sādhyam cintayet sudhīḥ tatas  sya yaḥ pāśavom śaḥ bhogya rūpaḥ tam arpayet  bhoktari eka ātma bhāvena śiṣya ittham śivībhavet  bhogya tā anyā tanuḥ deha iti pāśa ātmakā matāḥ śrāddhe mṛtoddhṛtau  anta yāge teṣām śivīkṛtiḥ ekena eva vidhānena yadi api syāt kṛtārtha tā tathā api tanmayībhāva siddhyai sarvam vidhim caret  bubhukṣoḥ tu kriyā abhyāsa bhūmānau phala bhūmani hetu tatas  mṛtoddhāra śrāddha ādi asmai samācaret  tattva jñāna arka vidhvasta dhvāntasya tu na kaḥ  pyayam antya iṣṭi śrāddha vidhi ādiḥ upayogī kadācana teṣām tu guru tad varga vargya sabrahmacāriṇām tad santāna juṣām aikya dinam parva dinam bhavet  yadāhi bodhasya udrekaḥ tadā parva āha pūraṇāt  janma aikya divasau tena parvaṇī bodha siddhitaḥ putrakaḥ  pi yadā kasmaicana syāt upakārakaḥ tadā mātuḥ pituḥ śakteḥ vāma dakṣa antarāla gāḥ nāḍīḥ pravāhayet devāya arpayeta niveditam śrīmat bharuṇatantre ca tad śivena nirūpitam tad vāha kāla apekṣā ca kāryā tad rūpa siddhaye svācchandyena atha tad siddhim vidhinā bhāvinā caret  yasya kasya api vā śrāddhe guru deva agni tarpaṇam sa cakra iṣṭi bhavet śrautaḥ  na tu syāt pāśavaḥ  vidhiḥ śrī maukuṭe tathā ca uktam śiva śāstre sthitaḥ  pi yaḥ pratyeti vaidike bhagna ghaṇṭāvat na sa kiṃcana tathā ukta deva pūjā ādi cakra yāga anta karmaṇā rudra tvam eti asau jantuḥ bhogān divyān samaśnute atha vacmaḥ sphuṭam śrīmat siddhaye nāḍi cāraṇam yā vāhayitum iṣyeta nāḍī tām eva bhāvayet  bhāvanā tanmayībhāve sā nāḍī vahati sphuṭam yad vā vāhayitum yeṣṭā tad aṅgam tena pāṇinā āpīḍya kukṣim namayet sā vahet nāḍikā kṣaṇāt  evam śrāddha mukhena api bhoga mokṣa ubhaya sthitim kuryāt iti śivena uktam tatra tatra kṛpālunā śaktipāta udaye jantoḥ yena upāyena daiśikaḥ karoti uddharaṇam tad tad nirvāṇāya asya kalpate uddhartā devadevaḥ  hi sa ca acintya prabhāvakaḥ upāyam guru dīkṣa ādi dvāra mātreṇa saṃśrayet  uktam śrīmat mataṅga ākhye muni praśnāt anantaram muktiḥ vivekāt tattvānām dīkṣātaḥ  yogataḥ  yadi caryā mātrāt katham sā syāt iti atas  samam uttaram prahasya ūce vibhuḥ kasmāt bhrāntiḥ te parameśituḥ sarva anugrāhaka tvam hi saṃsiddham dṛśyatām kila prāpta mṛtyoḥ viṣa vyādhi śastra ādi kila kāraṇam alpam vā bahu vā tadvat anudhyā mukti kāraṇam mukti artham upacaryante bāhya liṅgāni amūni tu iti jñātvā na sandeha ittham kāryaḥ  vipaścitā iyatā eva katham muktiḥ iti bhaktim parām śrayet  uktaḥ śrāddha vidhiḥ bhrānti gara ātaṅka vimardanaḥ  ch atha śrī tantrāloke ṣaḍviṃśam āhnikam atha ucyate śeṣa vṛttiḥ jīvatām upayoginī b dīkṣā bahu prakārā iyam śrāddha antā yā prakīrtitā sā saṃskriyāyai mokṣāya bhogāya api dvayāya vā tatra saṃskāra siddhyai yā dīkṣā sākṣāt na mocanī anusaṃdhi vaśa ādyā ca sākṣāt moktrī sa bījikā tayā ubhayyā dīkṣitā ye teṣām ājīva vartanam vaktavyam putraka ādīnām tad mayatva prasiddhaye bubhukṣoḥ vā mumukṣoḥ vā sva saṃvid guru śāstrataḥ pramāṇa ādyā saṃskriyāyai dīkṣā hi guruṇā kṛtā tatas  sa saṃskṛtam yogyam jñātvā ātmānam sva śāsane tad ukta vastu anuṣṭhānam bhuktyai muktyai ca sevate ācārya pratyayāt eva yaḥ  pi syāt bhukti mukti bhāj  tad pratyūha udaya dhvastyai brūyāt tasya api vartanam sva saṃvid guru saṃvittyoḥ tulya pratyaya bhāj api śeṣa vṛttyā samādeśyaḥ tad vighna ādi praśāntaye yaḥ sarvathā para apekṣām ujjhitvā tu sthitaḥ  nijāt  pratyaya āt yaḥ  pi ca ācārya pratyayāt eva kevalāt  tau sāṃsiddhika nirbījau kaḥ  vadet śeṣa vṛttaye kramāt tad maya tā upāya guru arcana ratau tu tau tatra eṣām śeṣa vṛtti artham nitya naimittike dhruve kāmya varjam yatas  kāmāḥ citrāḥ citra abhyupāyakāḥ tatra nityaḥ  vidhiḥ sandhyā anuṣṭhānam devatā vraje guru agni śāstra sahite pūjā bhūta dayā iti ayam naimittikaḥ tu sarveṣām parvaṇām pūjanam japaḥ viśeṣa vaśataḥ kiṃca pavitraka vidhi kramaḥ ācāryasya ca dīkṣā iyam bahu bhedā vivecitā vyākhyā ādikam ca tad tasya adhikam naimittikam dhruvam tatra ādau śiśave vrūyāt guruḥ nitya vidhim sphuṭam tad yogya tām samālokya vitata avitata ātmanām mukhya itara ādi mantrāṇām vīrya vyāpti ādi yogya tām dṛṣṭvā śiṣye tam eva asmai mūlamantram samarpayet  tad śāstra dīkṣitaḥ  hi eṣa niryantra ācāra śaṅkitaḥ na mukhye yogya iti anya sevātaḥ syāt tu yogya tā sādhakasya bubhukṣoḥ tu sādhakī bhāvinaḥ  pivā puṣpa pāta vaśāt siddhaḥ  mantraḥ  rpyaḥ sādhya siddhaye vitate guṇa bhūte vā vidhau diṣṭe punar guruḥ jñātvā asmai yogyatām sāram saṃkṣiptam vidhim ācaret  tatra eṣa niyamaḥ  yad yad māntram rūpam na tad guruḥ likhitvā prathayet śiṣye viśeṣāt ūrdhva śāsane mantrā varṇa ātmakāḥ te ca parāmarśa ātmakāḥ sa ca guru saṃvid abhinna śvet saṃkrāmet sā tatas  śiśau lipi sthitaḥ tu yaḥ  mantraḥ  nirvīryaḥ saḥ  tra kalpitaḥ saṃketa balataḥ  na asya pustakāt prathate mahaḥ pustaka adhīta vidyāḥ ca iti uktam siddhāmate tatas  ye tu pustaka labdhe pi mantre vīryam prajānate te bhairavīya saṃskārāḥ proktāḥ sāṃsiddhikā iti iti jñātvā guruḥ samyak  parama ānanda ghūrṇitaḥ tādṛśe tādṛśe dhāmni pūjayitvā vidhim caret  yathā anya śiṣya anuṣṭhānam na anya śiṣyeṇa budhyate tathā kuryāt guruḥ gupti hāniḥ doṣavatī yatas  devīnām tritayam śuddham yad vā yāmala yogataḥ devīm ekām athaḥ śuddhām vadet vā yāmala ātmikām tatra mantram sphuṭam vaktrāt guruṇā upāṃśu coditam avadhāryā pravṛtteḥ tam abhyasyet manasā svayam tatas  su śikṣitām sthāna deha antar śodhana trayīm nyāsam dhyānam japam mudrām pūjām kuryāt prayatnataḥ tatra prabhāte saṃbudhya sveṣṭām prāk devatām smaret  kṛta āvaśyaka kartavyaḥ śuddhaḥ  bhūtvā tatas  gṛham āśritya uttara digvaktraḥ sthāna deha antara traye śuddhim vidhāya mantrāṇām yathāsthānam niveśanam mudrā pradarśanam dhyānam bheda abheda svarūpataḥ deha asu dhī vyoma bhūṣu manasā tatra ca arcanam japam ca atra yathāśakti devāya etad nivedanam tanmayībhāva siddhi artham pratisandhyam samācaret  anye tu prāc udak paścāt daśa dikṣu catuṣṭayīm sandhyānām āhuḥ etad ca tāntrikī iyam na naḥ matam yā asau kāla adhikāre prāk  sandhyā proktā catuṣṭayī tām eva antar  samādhāya sāndhyam vidhim upācaret  sandhyā catuṣṭayī kṛtyam ekasyām athavā śiśuḥ kuryāt svādhyāya vijñāna guru kṛtya ādi tatparaḥ sandhyā dhyāna udita ananta tanmayībhāva yuktitaḥ tad saṃskāra vaśāt sarvam kālam syāt tad mayaḥ  hi asau tatas  yathā iṣṭa kāle sau pūjām puṣpa āsava ādibhiḥ sthaṇḍila ādau śiśuḥ kuryāt vibhava ādi anurūpataḥ su śuddhaḥ san vidhim sarvam kṛtvā antara japa antakam arghapātram purā yadvat vidhāya sva iṣṭa mantrataḥ tena sthaṇḍila puṣpa ādi sarvam saṃprokṣayet budhaḥ tatas tatra eva saṃkalpya dvārāsana gurukramam pūjayet śiva tā āviṣṭaḥ sva deha arcā puraḥsaram tatas tad sthaṇḍilam vīdhra vyoma sphaṭika nirmalam bodha ātmakam samālokya tatra svam devatā gaṇam pratibimba tayā paśyet bimba tvena ca bodhataḥ etad āvāhanam mukhyam vyajanāt marutām iva sarva gaḥ pi marudya dvat vyajanena upajīvitaḥ artha kṛt sarva gam mantra cakram rūḍheḥ tathā bhavet  catuṣka pañcāśikayā tad etad tattvam ucyate śrī nirmaryāda śāstre ca tad etad vibhunā uditam devaḥ sarva gataḥ  deva nirmaryādaḥ katham śivaḥ āvāhyate kṣamyate vā iti evaṃpṛṣṭaḥ  bravīt vibhuḥ vāsanāvāhyate devi vāsanā ca visṛjyate parama arthena devasya na āvāhana visarjane āvāhitaḥ  mayā devaḥ sthaṇḍile ca pratiṣṭhitaḥ pūjitaḥ stuta iti evam hṛṣṭvā devam visarjayet  prāṇinām aprabuddhānām santoṣa jananāya vai āvāhana ādikam teṣām pravṛttiḥ katham anyathā kālena tu vijānanti pravṛttāḥ pati śāsane anukrameṇa devasya prāptim bhuvana pūrvikām jñāna dīpa dyuti dhvasta samasta ajñāna sañcayāḥ kutaḥ vā ānīyate devaḥ kutra vā nīyate pi saḥ sthūla sūkṣma ādi bhedena sa hi sarvatra saṃsthitaḥ āvāhite mantra gaṇe puṣpa āsava nivedanaiḥ dhūpaiḥ ca tarpaṇam kāryam śraddhā bhakti bala ucitaiḥ dīptānām śakti nāda ādi mantrāṇām āsavaiḥ palaiḥ raktaiḥ prāk  tarpaṇa paścāt  puṣpa dhūpa ādi vistaraiḥ āgatasya tu mantrasya na kuryāt tarpaṇam yadi harati ardha śarīram sa iti uktam kila śambhunā yad yad eva asya manasi vikāsi tvam prayacchati tena eva kuryāt pūjām sa iti śambhoḥ viniścayaḥ sādhakānām bubhukṣūṇām vidhiḥ niyati yantritaḥ mumukṣūṇām tattva vidām sa eva tu nirargalaḥ kārye viśeṣam ādhitsuḥ viśiṣṭam kāraṇam spṛśet  rakta karpāsa tūla icchuḥ tulya tad bīja puñjavat santi bhoge viśeṣāḥ ca vicitrāḥ kāraṇa īritāḥ deśa kāla anusandhāna guṇa dravya kriyā ādibhiḥ su alpā kriyā bhūyasī vā hṛdaya āhlāda dāyibhiḥ bāhyaiḥ saṃkalpa jaiḥ vā api kārakaiḥ parikalpitā mumukṣoḥ na viśeṣāya naiḥśreyasa vidhim prati na hi brahmaṇi śaṃsanti bāhulya alpatva durdaśāḥ citaḥ svātantrya sāra tvāt tasya ānanda ghana tvataḥ kriyā syāt tanmayībhūtyai hṛdaya āhlāda dāyibhiḥ śiva abheda bharāt bhāva vargaḥ ścyotati yam rasam tam eva parame dhāmni pūjanāya arpayet budhaḥ stotreṣu bahudhā ca etad mayā proktam nija āhnike adhiśayya pāramārthika bhāva prasara prakāśam ullasati yā parama amṛta dṛś  tvām tayā arcayante rahasya vidaḥ kṛtvā ādhāra dharām camatkṛti rasa prokṣa akṣaṇa kṣālitāmāttaiḥ mānasataḥ svabhāva kusumaiḥ sva āmoda sandohibhiḥ ānanda amṛta nirbhara sva hṛdayānargha argha pātra kramāt tvām devyā saha deha deva sadane deva arcaye harniśam nānā svāda rasām imām trijagatīm hṛd cakra yantra arpitām ūrdhva adhyasta viveka gaurava bharāt niṣpīḍya niḥṣyanditam yad saṃvid parama amṛtam mṛti jarā janma apaham jṛmbhate tena tvām haviṣā pareṇa parame saṃtarpaye harniśam iti śloka traya upāttam artham antar vibhāvayan yena kena api bhāvena tarpayet devatā gaṇam mudrām pradarśayet paścāt manasā vā api yogataḥ vacasā mantra yogena vapuṣā saṃniveśataḥ kṛtvā japam tatas  sarvam devatāyai samarpayet  tad ca uktam kartṛ tā tattva nirūpaṇa vidhau purā tatas  visarjanam kāryam bodha aikātmya prayogataḥ kṛtvā vā vahni gām mantra tṛptim prokta vidhānataḥ dvāra pīṭha guru vrāta samarpita nivedanāt ṛte nyatsvayam aśnīyāt agādhe mbhasi atha kṣipet  prāṇinaḥ  jala jāḥ pūrva dīkṣitāḥ śambhunā svayam vidhinā bhāvinā śrīmat mīna nātha avatāriṇā mārjāra mūṣika ādyaiḥ yad adīkṣaiḥ ca api bhakṣitam tad śaṅkā ātaṅka dānena vyādhaye narakāya ca atas tattva vidā dhvasta śaṅkā taṅkaḥ  pi paṇḍitaḥ prakaṭam na īdṛśam kuryāt loka anugraha vāñchayā śrīmat matamahāśāstre tad uktam vibhunā svayam svayam tu śaṅkā saṅkoca niṣkāsana parāyaṇaḥ bhavet tathā yathā anyeṣām śaṅkā naḥ manasi sphuret  mārjayitvā tatas  snānam puṣpeṇa atha prapūjayet  puṣpa ādi sarvam tad stham tad agādha ambhasi nikṣipet  uktaḥ sthaṇḍila yāgaḥ  yam nityakarmaṇi śambhunā  ch atha śrī tantrāloke saptaviṃśatitamam āhnikam atha ucyate liṅga pūjā sūcitā mālinīmate b eteṣām ūrdhva śāstra ukta mantrāṇām na pratiṣṭhitam bahiṣkuryāt tatas  hi ete rahasya tvena siddhi dāḥ sva vīrya ānanda māhātmya praveśa vaśa śālinīm ye siddhim dadate teṣām bāhya tvam rūpa vicyutiḥ kiṃca ca uktam samāveśa pūrṇaḥ  bhoktṛ ā ātmakaḥ śivaḥ bhoga lāmpaṭya bhāj bhoga vicchede nigraha ātmakaḥ śānta tu anyak kriyā udbhūta jighatsā   ṛṃhitam vapuḥ svayam pratiṣṭhitam yena saḥ  sya ābhoge vinaśyati uktam jñāna uttarāyām ca tad etad parameśinā śivaḥ  yāga priyaḥ  yasmāt viśeṣāt mātṛ madhya gaḥ tasmāt rahasya śāstreṣu ye mantrāḥ tān budhaḥ  bahis  na pratiṣṭhāpayet jātu viśeṣāt vyakta rūpiṇaḥ ata eva mṛtasya arthe pratiṣṭhā anyatra yoditā sā atra śāstreṣu naḥ kāryā kāryā sādhāraṇī punar  ā tad mayatva saṃsiddherā ca abhīṣṭa phala udayāt putrakaḥ sādhakaḥ  vyaktam avyaktam vā samāśrayet  putrakaiḥ guruḥ abhyarthyaḥ sādhakaḥ tu svayam vidan yadi tad sthāpayet na u ced tena api arthyaḥ  guruḥ bhavet  guruḥ ca atra nirodha ākhye kāla ittham vibhau vadet  jīvati asmin phala antam tvam tiṣṭheḥ jīva avadhi iti vā liṅgam ca bāṇa liṅgam vā ratna jam vā atha mauktikam pauṣpama annam athaḥ vā astram gandha dravya kṛtam ca vā na tu pāṣāṇa jam liṅgam śilpī uttham parikalpayet  dhātu uttham ca suvarṇa uttha varjam anyat vivarjayet na ca atra liṅgamāna ādi kvacid api upayujyate udāra vīryaiḥ mantraiḥ yad bhāsitam phala dam hi tad  tasya api sthaṇḍila ādi ukta vidhinā śuddhim ācaret  mantra arpaṇam tathā eva syāt nirodhaḥ tu ukta yuktitaḥ agnau ca tarpaṇam bhūri viśeṣāt dakṣiṇā guroḥ dīna ādi tṛptiḥ vibhavāt yāga iti adhikaḥ vidhiḥ sarveṣu avyakta liṅgeṣu pradhānam syāt akalpitam tathā ca tatra tatra uktam lakṣaṇe pārameśvare sūtre pātre dhvaje vastre svayambhū bāṇa pūjite nadī prasravaṇa utthe ca na āhvānam na api kalpanā pīṭha prasāda mantra aṃśa vela ādi niyamaḥ  na ca vyaktam vā citra pusta ādau devadāru suvarṇa jam atha dīkṣita sacśilpi kṛtam sthāpayate guruḥ athavā lakṣaṇa upeta mūrdha tad karpara āśritam paṅkti cakraka śūla abja vidhinā tūram āśrayet  tad lakṣaṇam bruve śrīmat picu śāstre nirūpitam tūre yogaḥ sadā śastaḥ siddhi daḥ  doṣa varjite jālakaiḥ jarjarai randhraiḥ dantaiḥ ūnā adhikai rujā yukte ca tūre hāniḥ syāt  tad hīne yāga uttamaḥ kāmya eva bhavet tūram iti kecid prapedire guravaḥ tu vidhau kāmye yatnāt doṣān  tyajet iti vyācakṣate picu proktam na nitye karmaṇi iti adaḥ śrī siddhātantra uktam ca tūra lakṣaṇam uttamam eka ādika catuṣkhaṇḍe gomukhe pūrṇa candrake padma gorocanā muktā nīra sphaṭika saṃnibhe eka ādi pañca sat randhra vidyā rekhā anvite śubhe na rūkṣa vakra śakala dīrgha nimnasa binduke ślakṣṇayā vajra sūcyā atra sphuṭam devī gaṇa anvitam sarvam samālikhet pūjyam sarva avayava sundaram etad eva anusartavyam argha pātre pi lakṣaṇam śrī brahmayāmale pyuktam pātram gomukham uttamam gaja kūrma talam kumbha vṛtta śaktika ja ākṛti akṣa sūtram athaḥ kuryāt tatra eva abhyarcayet kramam vīra dhātu jala udbhūta muktā ratna suvarṇa jam akṣa sūtram krama utkṛṣṭam raudrākṣam vā viśeṣataḥ śatam tithi uttaram yad vā sāṣṭam yad vā tad ardhakam tad ardham vā atha pañcāśat yuktam tad parikalpayet  vaktrāṇi pañca cit spanda jñāna icchā ākṛti saṃgateḥ pañcadhā ādi anta gam ca aikyam iti upāntyā akṣa gaḥ vidhiḥ śakti tadvat prabhedena tatra dvairūpyam ucyate tatas  dviguṇa māne tu dvi rūpam nyāsam ācaret  tatas  pi dviguṇe sṛṣṭi saṃhṛti dvitayena tam mātṛkām mālinīm vā atha nyasyet kha śara saṃmite uttame tu dvayīm nyasyet nyasya pūrvam pracoditān dīkṣāyām mukhyataḥ mantrān  tān pañcadaśa daiśikaḥ yadi vā tattva bhuvana kalā mantra pada arṇajaiḥ saṃkhyā bhedaiḥ kṛte sūtre tam tam nyāsam guruḥ caret  kṛtvā akṣa sūtram tasya api sarvam sthaṇḍilavat bhavet  pūjitena ca tena eva japam kuryāt atandritaḥ vidhiḥ uktaḥ tu ayam śrīmat mālinīvijaya uttare cakravat bhramayan  etad yad vakti sa japaḥ  bhavet  yadīkṣate juhoti etad bodha agnau saṃpraveśanāt  athavā argha mahāpātram kuryāt tad ca uttaram param nārikelam athaḥ bailvam sauvarṇam rājatam ca vā tasya api eṣa vidhiḥ sarvaḥ pratiṣṭhā ādau prakīrtitaḥ tad niṣkampa rasaiḥ pūrṇam kṛtvā asmin pūjayet kramam adhomukham sadā sthāpyam pūjitam pūjane punar  tad pātram unmukham tad ca riktam kuryāt na tādṛśam pūjā ante tad rasa āpūrṇam ātmānam pravidhāya tad  adhomukham ca saṃpūjya sthāpayet  vicakṣaṇaḥ khaṅgam kṛpāṇikām yad vā kartarīm makuram ca vā vimalam tad tathā kuryāt śrīmad kālī mukha uditam śrī bhairava kule pyuktam kula parva prapūjane sthaṇḍile gnau paṭe liṅge pātre padme tha maṇḍale mūrtau ghaṭe stra saṃghāte dhaṭe sūtre tha pūjayet  svena svena upacāreṇa saṅkaram varjayet iti yathā apsu śāntaye mantrāḥ tadvat astra ādiṣu dhruvam śatru  cheda ādi kartāraḥ kāmyaḥ  taḥ saṅkara ujjhitaḥ akāmasya tu te tad tad sthāna upādhi vaśāt dhruvam pāśa kartana saṃśuddha tattva āpyāya ādi kāriṇaḥ athavā pustakam tādṛśḥ ahaḥśāstra krama umbhitam su śuddham dīkṣita kṛtam tatra api eṣa vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ ittham svayaṃpratiṣṭheṣu yāvat yāvat sthitiḥ bhavet vibhavaiḥ tarpaṇam śuddhiḥ tāvat viccheda varjanam ata eva yadā bhūri dinam maṇḍala kalpanam tadā dine dine kuryāt vibhavaiḥ tarpaṇam bahu pratiṣṭhāyām ca sarvatra guruḥ pūrva uditam param sa tattvam anusandhāya saṃnidhim sphuṭam ācaret  siddhe tu tanmayībhāve phale putraka sādhakaiḥ anyasmai tad dvayāt anyatarasmai tad samarpyate tasya api eṣa vidhiḥ sarvaḥ tad alābhe tu sarvathā agādhe mbhasi tad kṣepyam kṣamayitvā visṛjya ca iti eṣa sva pratiṣṭhāna vidhiḥ śiva nirūpitaḥ para pratiṣṭhite liṅge bāṇīye tha svayaṃbhuvi sarvam āsana pakṣe prāc nyasya saṃpūjayet kramam śuddha aśuddha adhvajāḥ sarve mantrāḥ sarvaḥ śiva antakaḥ adhvā ca iha āsane proktaḥ tad sarvatra arcayet idam āvāhana visṛṣṭī tu tatra prākvat samācaret  uktam tantre pyaghora īśe svacchande vibhunā tathā athavā pratyaham proktamāna ardha ardha niyogataḥ kṛtvā iṣṭam maṇḍalam tatra samastam kramam arcayet  bahu prakāra bhinnasya liṅgasya arcā nirūpitā  ch atha śrī tantrāloke aṣṭāviṃśam āhnikam iti nitya vidhiḥ proktaḥ  naimittikam atha ucyate b niyatam bhāvi yad nityam tad iti asmin vidhau sthite mukhya tvam tad mayībhūtiḥ sarvam naimittikam tatas  dina ādi kalpanā utthe tu naiyatye sarva nitya tā dina māsa ṛkṣa varṣa ādinaiyatyāt ucyate tadā aśaṅkita vyāvaśyantā sattākam jātucit bhavam pramātra niyatam prāhuḥ naimittikam idam budhāḥ sandhyādi parva saṃpūjā pavitrakam idam sadā nityam niyata rūpa tvāt sarvasmin śāsana āśrite jñāna śāstra guru bhrātṛ tad varga prāptayaḥ tathā tad janma saṃskriyā bhedāḥ sva janma utsava saṃgatiḥ śrāddham vipad pratīkāraḥ pramodaḥ  dbhuta darśanam yoginī melakaḥ sva aṃśa santa ana ādyaiḥ ca melanam śāstra vyākhyā purā madhya avasānāni krama udayaḥ devatā darśanam svāpnam ājñā samaya niṣkṛtiḥ iti naimittikam śrīmat tantra sāre nirūpitam trayoviṃśati bhedena viśeṣa arcā nibandhanam tatra parva vidhim brūmaḥ  dvidhā parva kula ākulam kula aṣṭaka kṛtam pūrvam proktam śrī yoga saṃcare abdhi indu muniḥ iti etad māheśyā brahma santateḥ pratipad pañcadaśyau dve kaumāryā rasa vahni yuj  abdhirakṣi indu vaiṣṇavyā aindryāḥ tu astram trayodaśī vārāhyā randhra rudrau dve caṇḍyā vasu akṣi yugmakam dve dve tithī tu sarvāsām yogeśyā daśamī punar  tasyāḥ  api aṣṭamī yasmāt dvitithiḥ sā prakīrtitā anyāḥ ca ākula parvā api vaiparītyena lakṣitam kulaparva iti tad brūmaḥ yathā uktam bhairave kule haiḍare trika sadbhāve trika kālī kula ādike yaḥ  yam prāṇa āśritaḥ pūrvam kālaḥ proktaḥ su vistarāt  sa cakra bheda saṃcāre kāṃcid  sūte sva saṃvidam sva saṃvid pūrṇa tā lābha samayaḥ parva bhaṇyate parva pūraṇa iti eva yad vā pṝ pūraṇa arthakaḥ parva śabdaḥ  niruktaḥ ca parva tad pūraṇāt iti haiḍare tra ca śabdaḥ  yam dvidhā na antetaraḥ śrutaḥ tad cakracāra niṣṇātā ye kecid  pūrṇa saṃvidaḥ tad melaka samāyuktāḥ te tad pūjā parāḥ sadā yaḥ  pyatanmaya eṣaḥ  pi tad kāle sva krama arcanāt  tad yoginī siddha saṅgha melakāt  tad mayībhavet  yathā prekṣaṇake tad tad draṣṭṛ saṃvid bheditām krama uditām sadya eva labhate tad praveśanāt yoga abhyāsa krama upāttām tathā pūrṇām sva saṃvidam labhante sadya eva etad saṃvid aikya praveśanāt tad kālam ca api saṃvitteḥ pūrṇa tvāt  kāma dogdhṛtā tena tad tad phalam tatra kāle saṃpūjaya acirāt  yathā cira upātta dhanaḥ kurvan  utsavam ādarāt  atithim saḥ  nugṛhṇāti tad kāla abhijñam āgatam tathā su phala saṃsiddhyai yoginī siddha nāyakāḥ yatnavantaḥ  pi tad kāla abhijñam tam anugṛhṇate uktam ca tatra tena iha kule sāmānyatā iti alam yasya yad hṛdaye devi vartate daiśika ājñayā mantraḥ  yogaḥ kramaḥ ca eva pūjanāt  siddhi daḥ  bhavet  kula ācāreṇa deveśi pūjyam siddhi vimuktaye ye parvasveṣu deveśi tarpaṇam tu viśeṣataḥ gurūṇām devatānām ca na kurvanti pramādataḥ durācārā hi te duṣṭāḥ paśu tulyā varānane abhāvāt nitya pūjāyā avaśyam hi eṣu pūjayet  aṭanam jñāna śakti ādi lābha artham yad prakīrtitam śakti yāgaḥ ca yaḥ proktaḥ  vaśya ākarṣaṇa māraṇam tad sarvam parva divaseṣu ayatnena eva siddhyati tad sāmānya viśeṣābhyām ṣoḍhā parva nirūpitam māsasya ādyam pañcamam ca śrī dinam paribhāṣyate utkṛṣṭa tvāt  parva dinam śrī pūrva tvena bhāṣyate samayaḥ  hi eṣa yad guptam tad na anupapadam vadet  turya aṣṭamānya bhuvana caramāṇi dvayoḥ api pakṣayoḥ iha sāmānya sāmānyam parva kīrtitam yad eteṣu dineṣu eva bhaviṣyat graha bhā ātmakaḥ ubhaya ātmā viśeṣaḥ syāt tad sāmānya viśeṣa tā sā ca ekādaśadhā ekasmin  ekasmin vibhunā uditā sajātīyā tu sa utkṛṣṭā iti evam śambhuḥ nyarūpayat  kṛṣṇa yugam vahni sitam śruti kṛṣṇam vahni sitam iti pakṣāḥ arka indu jīva candrā budha yugma indu arkaka vi guru vidhu syāt  para phalguḥ caitramaghe tiṣyaḥ prāc phalgu karṇa śatabhiṣajaḥ mūlaprājāpatye viśākhikā śravaṇa saṃjñayā bhāni randhre tithi arka pare vasu randhre śaśi vṛṣa aṅka rasa randhra yugam prathama niśā madhya niśe madhyāhna śarā dina udayaḥ  madhya dinam prathama niśā iti ca samayaḥ  mārgaśiraḥ prabhṛti māseṣu kanyā antyajātha veśyā rāgavatī tattva vedinī dūtī vyāsa samāsāt  kramaśas  pūjyāḥ cakre nuyāga ākhye sarvatra ca parva dine kuryāt anuyāga cakram atiśayataḥ guptāk upta vidhāna ādi yāga caryā krameṇa sampūrṇam anuyāgaḥ kila mukhyaḥ sarvasmin  eva karma viniyoge anuyāga kāla lābhe tasmāt prayateta tad paramaḥ bhagraha samaya viśeṣaḥ  na aśvayuje kaḥ  pi tena tad varjam velā ābha graha kalanā kathita ekādaśasu māseṣu phālguna māse śuklam yad proktam dvādaśī dinam parva agratithi vedha yogaḥ  mukhya tamaḥ  sau viśeṣaḥ  tra divasa niśe kila kṛtvā tri bhāgaśas  prathama madhyama apara vibhāgaḥ pūjā kālaḥ tatra tri bhāgite mukhyatamaḥ kālaḥ yadi saṃghaṭeta velā mukhyatamā bhagrahau tathā cakram tad yāga ādi yāgaḥ tad kāmyam pūjayā eva parvasu siddhyet  dina vela ābha graha kalpanena tatra api saumya raudra tvam jñātvā sādhaka mukhyaḥ tad tad kāryam tadā tadā kuryāt  uktaḥ  yaḥ  rcākālaḥ tam ced ullaṅghya bhagra hatithiḥ syāt  tam anādṛtya viśeṣam pradhānayet sāmayam iti kecid  na iti tu asmad guravaḥ  viśeṣa rūpā hi tithiḥ iha na velā saṃvedya rūpa śaśadhara bhāgaḥ saṃvedaka arka kara nikaraiḥ yāvānyāvati pūrṇaḥ sā hi tithiḥ bhagrahaiḥ sphuṭībhavati tasmāt mukhyā atra tithiḥ sā ca viśeṣyā graha ṛkṣa yogena velā atra na pradhānam yuktam ca etad tathā hi parameśaḥ śrī trika bhairava kula śāstreṣūce na parva divaseṣu velā yogam kaṃcana tithibha graha yogataḥ  hi anyam tithiḥ tu pūjyā pradhāna rūpa tvāt  śveta abhāve kṛṣṇa  chāga ālambham hi kathayanti yad punar ūrmi prabhṛtini śāstre velā uditā api tad kāmyam mukhya tayā uddiśya vidhim tathā ca tatra pauṣa parva dine kṛtvā arcanam ardha niśi dhyātvā japtvā bahis gatasya yathā ādeśaḥ phalati tathā māghe cakrāt vacaḥ phalati acirāt abhīṣṭa siddhiḥ pañcasu maitrī dhanam ca melāpaḥ cakra sthāne krodhāt  pāṣāṇa sphoṭanena ripu nāśaḥ siddhādeśa prāptiḥ mārga antam kathyate vibhunā bhagraha yoga abhāve velām tu titheḥ avaśyam īkṣeta sā hi tathā sphuṭa rūpā titheḥ svabhāva udayam dadyāt  bhagrahatithi velā aṃśa anuyāyi sarva aṅga sundaram tu dinam yadi labhyeta tadā asmin viśeṣatama pūjanam racayet  na ca kāmyam eva kevalam etad parivarjane yatas  kathitaḥ samaya vilopaḥ śrīmat bhairava kula ūrmiśāstre ca duṣṭā hi durācārāḥ paśu tulyāḥ parva ye na viduḥ na ca kāmyasya akaraṇe syāt jātu pratyavāyi tvam tatra anuyāga siddhi artham cakrayāgaḥ  nirūpyate mūrti yāga iti proktaḥ  yaḥ śrī yogīśvarī mate nityam naimittikam karma yad atra uktam maheśinā sarvatra cakrayāgaḥ  tra mukhyaḥ kāmye viśeṣataḥ jñānī yogī ca puruṣaḥ strī vā asmin mūrti saṃjñake yoge prayatnataḥ  yojyaḥ tad hi pātram anuttaram tad saṃparkāt pūrṇa tā syāt iti traiśirasa ādiṣu tena sarvam hutam ceṣṭam trailokyam sacarācaram jñānine yogine vā api yaḥ  dadāti karoti vā dīkṣā uttare pi ca proktam annam brahmā rasaḥ  hariḥ bhoktā śiva iti jñānī śvapacān api atha uddhareat sarva tattvam ayaḥ  bhūtvā yadi bhuṅkte sa sādhakaḥ tena bhojita mātreṇa sakṛt koṭiḥ tu bhojitā atha tattva vid etasmin yadi bhuñjīta tad  priye parisaṃkhyā na vidyeta tad āha bhagavān śivaḥ bhojyam māyā ātmakam sarvam śivaḥ  bhoktā sa ca api aham evam yaḥ  vai vijānāti daiśikaḥ tattva pāragaḥ tam dṛṣṭvā devam āyāntam krīḍanti oṣadhayaḥ  gṛhe nivṛttam adya eva asmābhiḥ saṃsāra gahana arṇavāt  yad asya vaktram saṃprāptā yāsyāmaḥ paramam padam anye pāna bhujaḥ  hi ūrdhve prāṇaḥ  pānaḥ tu adhomukhaḥ tasmin bhoktari deveśi dātuḥ kula śatāni api āśu eva parimucyante naraka ādi ātanā arṇavāt  śrīmat niśāṭane pyuktam kathana anveṣaṇāt api śrotra abhyantara saṃprāpte guru vaktrāt vinirgate muktaḥ tadā eva kāle tu yantram tiṣṭhati kevalam surāpaḥ steya hārī ca brahma hā guru talpa gaḥ antyajaḥ  vā dvijaḥ  vā atha bālaḥ  vṛddhaḥ  yuvā api vā paryanta vāsī yaḥ  jñānī deśasya api pavitrakaḥ tatra saṃnihitaḥ  devaḥ sa devīkaḥ sa kiṅkaraḥ tasmāt prādhānyataḥ kṛtvā gurum jñāna viśāradam mūrti yāgam caret tasya vidhiḥ yogīśvarīmate pavitra ārohaṇe śrāddhe tathā parva dineṣu alam sūrya candra uparāga ādau laukikeṣu api parvasu utsave ca vivāha ādau viprāṇām yajña karmaṇi dīkṣāyām ca pratiṣṭhāyām samayānām viśodhane kāmanā artham ca kartavyaḥ  mūrti yāgaḥ sa pañcadhā kevalaḥ  yāmalaḥ  miśraḥ cakra yuj vīra saṅkaraḥ kevalaḥ kevalaiḥ eva gurubhiḥ miśritaḥ punar  sādhaka ādyaiḥ sa patnīkaiḥ yāmalaḥ sa dvidhā punar  patnī yogāt  kraya ānīta veśyā saṃyogataḥ  thavā cakriṇī ādyāḥ ca vakṣyante śakti yogāt yathocitāḥ tad saṃyogāt cakra yuktaḥ  yāgaḥ sarva phala pradaḥ sarvaiḥ tu sahitaḥ  yāgaḥ  vīra saṅkara ucyate madhye guruḥ bhavet teṣām guru vargaḥ tad āvṛtiḥ tisra āvṛtayaḥ bāhye samayī antā yathākramam paṅkti krameṇa vā sarve madhye teṣām guruḥ sadā tadā tad gandha dhūpa sraj samālambhana vāsasā pūjyam cakra anusāreṇa tad tad cakram idam tu iti ekārake yathā cakre eka vīra vidhim smaret  dvi are yāmalam anyatra trikam evam ṣaṣ asrake ṣaṣ yoginīḥ saptakam ca saptāre ṣṭa aṣṭake ca vā anyat vā tādṛśam tatra cakre tādṛś svarūpiṇi tatas  pātre lisaṃpūrṇe pūrvam cakram yajet sudhīḥ ādhāra yukte na ādhāra rahitam tarpaṇam kvacid  ādhāreṇa vinā bhraṃśaḥ  na ca tuṣyanti raśmayaḥ preta rūpam bhavet pātram śākta amṛtam atha asavaḥ bhoktrī tatra tu yā śaktiḥ sa śambhuḥ parameśvaraḥ aṇu śakti śiva ātma ittham dhyātvā saṃmilitam trayam tatas tu tarpaṇam kāryam āvṛteḥ āvṛteḥ kramāt  pratisaṃcara yogena punar antar  praveśayet  yāvat guru antikam tad hi pūrṇam bhramaṇam ucyate tatra ādau devatāḥ tarpyāḥ tatas  vīrā iti kramaḥ vīraḥ ca vīraśaktiḥ ca iti evam asmad guru kramaḥ tatas  vadaṃśān vividhān māṃsa matsya ādi saṃyutān agre tatra pravikiret  tṛpti antam sādhaka uttamaḥ pātra abhāve punar bhadram vellitā śuktim eva ca pātre kurvīta matimān iti siddhāmate kramaḥ dakṣa hastena bhadram syāt vellitā śuktiḥ ucyate dakṣa hastasya kurvīta vāma upari kanīyasīm tarjanī aṅguṣṭha yogena dakṣa adhaḥ vāmaka aṅgulīḥ niḥsandhi bandhau dvau  ittham vellitā śuktiḥ ucyate ye tatra pāna kāle tu bindavaḥ  yānti medinīm taiḥ tuṣyanti hi vetāla guhyaka ādyā gabhastayaḥ dhārayā bhairavaḥ tuṣyet  kara pānam param tatas  praveśaḥ  tra na dātavyaḥ pūrvam eva hi kasyacid  pramādāt tu praviṣṭasya vicāram na eva carcayet  evam kṛtvā krama ādyāgamante dakṣiṇayā yutam samālambhana tāmbūla vastra ādyam vitaret budhaḥ rūpaka ardhāt  param hīnām na dadyāt dakṣiṇām sudhīḥ samayibhyaḥ kramāt dvi dviguṇā guru antakam bhavet  eṣa syāt mūrtiyāgaḥ tu sarva yāga pradhānakaḥ kāmye tu saṃvidhau sapta kṛtvas  kāryaḥ tathāvidhaḥ jānanti prathamam geham tatas tasya samartha tām balābalam tatas  paścāt vismayante tra mātaraḥ tatas  pi saṃnidhīyante prīyante vara dāḥ tatas  devīnām atha nāthasya parivāra yujaḥ  pyalam vallabhaḥ  mūrti yāgaḥ  yamatas  kāryaḥ  vipaścitā rāktau gupte gṛhe vīrāḥ śaktayaḥ nyonyam api alam asaṃketa yujaḥ  yojyā devatā śabda kīrtanāt alābhe mūrti cakrasya kumārīḥ eva pūjayet  kāmya arthe tu na tām vyaṅgām stana puṣpavatīm tathā pratipad śruti saṃjñe ca caturthī ca uttarā traye haste ca pañcamī ṣaṣṭhī pūrvāsu atha punarvasau saptamī tad parā pitrye rohiṇyām navamī tathā mūle tu dvādaśī brāhme bhūta āśvinyām ca pūrṇimā dhaniṣṭhāyām amāvasyā saḥ  yam ekādaśa ātmakaḥ arka ādi traya śukra anyatama yuktaḥ  pyahargaṇaḥ yogaparva iti vikhyātaḥ  rātrau vā dina eva vā yogaparvaṇi kartavyaḥ  mūrti yāgaḥ tu sarvathā yaḥ sarvān yoga parva ākhyān vāsarān pūjayet sudhīḥ mūrti yāgena saḥ  pi syāt  samayī maṇḍalam vinā iti eṣa mūrti yāgaḥ śrī siddhayogīśvarīmate atha ucyate śivena uktaḥ pavitraka vidhiḥ sphuṭaḥ śrī ratna mālā triśiraḥ śāstrayoḥ sūcitaḥ punar  śrī siddhāṭana sadbhāva māli nī sāra śāsane tatra prādhānyataḥ śrīmat mālā uktaḥ  vidhiḥ ucyate kṣīrābdhi mathana udbhūta viṣa nidrā vimūrcchitaḥ nāga rājaḥ sva bhuvane megha kāle sma na avasat  kevalam tu pavitraḥ  yam vāyubhakṣaḥ samāḥ śatam divyam daśaguṇam nātham bhairavam paryapūjayat  vyajijñapat ca tam tuṣṭam nātham varṣāsu aham nije pātāle na asitum śaktaḥ saḥ  pyenam parameśvaraḥ nāgam nija jaṭa ajūṭa pīṭha gam paryakalpayat  tatas  samasta deva oghaiḥ dhāritaḥ  sau sva mūrdhani mahatām mahitānām hi na adbhuta viśva pūjyatā tasmāt maheśituḥ mūrdhni devatānām ca sarvaśas  ātmanaḥ ca pavitram tam kuryāt yāga puraḥsaram daśa koṭyaḥ  na pūjānām pavitra ārohaṇe samāḥ vṛthā dīkṣā vṛthā jñānam guru ārādhanam eva ca vinā pavitra ādyena etad haret nāgaḥ śiva ājñayā tasmāt sarva prayatnena sa kāryaḥ kula vedibhiḥ āṣāḍha śuklān mithuna karkaṭa sthe ravau vidhiḥ kartavyaḥ saḥ  nirodhena yāvat sā tula pūrṇimā tulā upalakṣitasya antyam kārtikasya dinam matam kula śabdam paṭhantaḥ  nye vyākhyā bhedam prakurvate nitya atantra vidaḥ kṛṣṇam kārtikāt caramam dinam kulasya nityācakrasya pūrṇa tvam yatra tad matam māgha śukla antya divasaḥ kulaparva iti tad matam pūrṇa tvam tatra candrasya sā tithiḥ kula pūrṇimā dakṣiṇa uttara gaḥ kālaḥ kula ākula tayā uditaḥ kulasya tasya carame dine pūrṇa tvam ucyate dakṣiṇāyana ṣaṣ māsa kartavya tvam atas  vidhau pavitrake prakāśatva siddhyai kṛṣṇasya vartmanaḥ tad etad bahu śāstra uktam rūpam devaḥ  nyarūpayat  ekena eva padena śrī ratna mālā ākula āgame tad atra samaye sarva vidhi saṃpūraṇa ātmakaḥ pavitraka vidhiḥ kāryaḥ śukla pakṣe tu sarvathā pūraṇam śakti yogena śakti ātma ca sitam dalam dakṣiṇāyana sājātyāt tena tad vidhiḥ ucyate eka dvi tri catur pañca ṣaṣ latā ekatamam mahat  hema ratna aṅkita granthi kuryāt muktā pavitrakam sauvarṇa sūtram triguṇam sa eka granthi śatam gurau pare gurau tu tri adhikam adhyabdhi parameṣṭhini prāc siddha ācārya yoga īśa viṣaye tu rasa adhikam aṣṭa adhikam śivasya uktam citra ratna prapūritam vidyā pīṭha akṣa sūtra ādau guruvat śivavat  punar  vaṭuke kanaka abhāve raupyam tu parikalpayet  pāṭṭasūtram atha kṣaumam kārpāsam tri tri tānitam tasmāt nava guṇāt  sūtrāt triguṇa ādi kramāt kuru caṇḍāṃśu guṇa paryantam tatas  pi triguṇam ca vā tena aṣṭādaśa tantu uttham adhamam madhyamam punar  aṣṭottaraśatam tasmāt  triguṇam tu uttamam matam granthayaḥ tattva saṃkhyātāḥ ṣaḍadhva kalanā vaśāt yad vā vyāsa samāsābhyām citrāḥ sat gandha pūritāḥ viśeṣa vidhinā pūrvam pūjayitvā arpayet tatas  pavitrakam samasta adhva paripūrṇatva bhāvanāt guru ātmanoḥ ja anunābhikaṇṭha mūrdha anta gam ca vā tatas  mahā utsavaḥ kāryaḥ  guru pūjā puraḥsaraḥ tarpyāḥ śāsana gāḥ sarve dakṣiṇau  astra bhojanaiḥ mahā utsavaḥ prakartavyaḥ  gīta nṛtta ātmakaḥ  mahān cāturmāsyam sapta dinam tri dinam vā api alābhataḥ tad ante kṣamayet devam maṇḍala ādi visarjayet  vahnim ca paścāt kartavyaḥ cakra yāgaḥ purā uditaḥ māse māse catur māse varṣe vā api pavitrakam sarvathā eva prakartavyam yathā vibhava vistaram vitta abhāve punar  kāryam kāśaiḥ api kuśombhitaiḥ sati vitte punar  śāṭhyam vyādhaye narakāya ca nitya pūjāsu pūrṇa tvam parva pūjā prapūraṇāt tatra api paripūrṇa tvam pavitraka samarcanāt  pavitraka vilope tu prāyaścittam japet sudhīḥ su śuddhaḥ san punar  kuryāt iti ājñā parameśituḥ atha triśirasi proktaḥ  likhyate tad vidhiḥ sphuṭaḥ tri prameyasya śaivasya pañca pañca ātmakasya vā daśa aṣṭādaśa bhedasya ṣaṭsrotasa iha ucyate ye narāḥ samaya bhraṣṭā guru śāstra ādi dūṣakāḥ nitya naimittika ādi anya parva sandhi vivarjitāḥ akāmāt  kāmataḥ  vā api sūkṣma pāpa pravartinaḥ teṣām praśamana arthāya pavitram kriyate śive śrāvaṇa ādau kārtika ante śukla pakṣe śubha prade na tu duḥkha prade kṛṣṇe kartṛ rāṣṭra nṛpa ādiṣu pāṭṭasūtram tu kauśeyam kārpāsam kṣaumam eva ca cāturāśramikāṇām tu subhruvā kartita ukṣitam tridhā tu triguṇīkṛtya māna saṃkhyām tu kārayet  aṣṭa uttaram tantu śatam tad ardham vā tad ardhakam hrāsaḥ tu pūrva saṃkhyāyāḥ  daśabhiḥ daśabhiḥ kramāt  navabhiḥ pañcabhiḥ saptaviṃśatyā vā śiva āditaḥ yādṛśaḥ tantu vinyāsaḥ  granthīn kuryāt tu tāvataḥ catur sama viliptān  tān athavā kuṅkumena tu vyakte jānu taṭa antam syāt liṅge pīṭha avasānakam arcāsu śobhanam mūrghni tri tattva parikalpanāt  dvādaśa granthi śaktīnām brahma vaktra arciṣām api vidyā pīṭhe cale liṅge sthaṇḍile ca guroḥ gaṇe ghaṇṭāyām sruc sruve śiṣya liṅgiṣu dvāra toraṇe sva dehe vahni pīṭhe ca yathā śobham tad iṣyate prāsāde yāga gehe ca kārayet navaraṅgikam vidyā pīṭhe tu kha śarāḥ pratimā āliṅga pīṭha gam vasu vedam ca ghaṇṭāyām śarākṣyaṣṭādaśa sruve veda akṣi sruci ṣaṭtriṃśat  prāsāde maṇḍape raviḥ rasendu  snāna gehe bdhi netre dhyāna gṛhe gurau sapta sādhaka gāḥ pañca putrake sapta sāmaye catvāraḥ  thānya śāstra sthe śiṣye pañcakam ucyate liṅginām kevalaḥ  granthiḥ toraṇe daśa kalpayet  dvāreṣu aṣṭau granthayaḥ syuḥ kṛtvā ittham tu pavitrakam pūjayitvā mantra jālam tad sthatva ātma sthate tatas  pavitrakāṇām saṃpādya kuryāt saṃpāta saṃskriyām tatas  saṃvatsaram dhyāyet bhairavam chidra sākṣiṇam dattvā pūrṇāhutim devi praṇamet mantrabhairavam om samasta kriyā doṣa pūraṇa īśa vratam prati yad kiṃcid akṛtam duṣṭam kṛtam vā mātṛ nandana tad sarvam mama deveśa tvad prasādāt praṇaśyatu sarvathā raśmi cakra īśa namaḥ tubhyam prasīda me anena dadyāt devāya nimantraṇa pavitrakam yoginī kṣetra mātṝṇām balim dadyāt tatas  guruḥ pañcagavyam carum dantakāṣṭham śiṣyaiḥ samantatas ācārya nidrām kurvīta prātar utthāya ca āhnikam tatas  vidhim pūjayitvā pavitrāṇi samāharet  dantakāṣṭham mṛd ca dhātrī samṛddhātrī saha ambunā catur samam ca taiḥ sārdham bhasma pañcasu yojayet  prāc dakṣa paścima ūrdhva stha vāma vaktreṣu vai kramāt  pañca etāni pavitrāṇi sthāpayet ca īśa gocare kuśa idhma pañcagavyam ca śarva agre viniyojayet  vāma amṛta ādi saṃyuktam naivedyam trividham tatas  dadyāt asṛk  tathā madyam pānāni vividhāni ca tatas  homaḥ  mahākṣmā aja māṃsaiḥ tila yutaiḥ athaḥ tilaiḥ ghṛta yutaiḥ yad vā taṇḍulaiḥ atha dhānyakaiḥ śarkarā khaṇḍa saṃyukta pañcāmṛta pariplutaiḥ mūlam sahasram sa aṣṭa uktam tri śaktau brahmavaktrakam arciṣām tu śatam sāṣṭam tatas  pūrṇāhutim kṣipet  tatas  ñjalau pavitram tu gṛhītvā prapaṭhet idam akāmāt athavā kāmāt yad mayā na kṛtam vibhaḥ tad acchidram mama astu īśa pavitreṇa tava ājñayā mūlamantraḥ pūrayā iti kriyā niyamam iti atha vauṣaṭ antam pavitram ca dadyāt bindu avasānakam nāda antam samanāntam ca api unmana antam kramāt trayam evam catuṣṭayam dadyāt anulomena bhautikaḥ naiṣṭhikaḥ tu vilomena pavitraka catuṣṭayam yad kiñcidvividham vastra  chatra alaṅkaraṇa ādikam tad nivedyam dīpa mālāḥ suvarṇa tila bhājanam vastra yugma yutam sarva sampūraṇa nimittatas bhojanīyāḥ pūjanīyāḥ śiva bhaktāḥ tu śaktitas  catur tri dvi eka māsa ādi dina ekāntam mahā utsavam kuryāt tatas  na vrajeyuḥ anya sthānam kadācana tatas tu daiśikaḥ pūjyaḥ  gām asmai kṣīriṇīm navām dadyāt suvarṇa ratna ādiḥ upya vastra vibhūṣitām vadet guruḥ ca saṃpūrṇaḥ  vidhiḥ tava bhavatu iti vaktavyam devadevasya punar āgamanāya ca tatas  visarjanam kāryam guptam ābharaṇa ādikam naivedyam guruḥ ādāya yāga arthe tad niyojayet  caturṇām api sāmānyam pavitrakam iti smṛtam na asmāt vratam param kiñcid  kā vā asya stutiḥ ucyate śeṣam tvac ādhe vāri oghe kṣipet na sthāpayet sthiram atha naimittika vidhiḥ yaḥ purā sūtritaḥ  mayā sa bhaṇyate tatra kāryā devasya arcā viśeṣataḥ cakrayāgaḥ ca kartavyaḥ pūrva ukta vidhinā budhaiḥ tatra yad yad nija abhīṣṭa bhoga mokṣa upakārakam pāramparyeṇa sākṣāt vā bhavet cit acit ātmakam tad pūjyam tad upāyāḥ ca pūjyāḥ tad maya tā āptaye tad upāyaḥ  pi saṃpūjyaḥ  mūrti kāla kriyā ādikaḥ upeya sūti sāmarthyam upāya tvam tad arcanāt  tad rūpa tanmayībhāvāt upeyam śīghram āpnuyāt  yathā yathā ca naikaṭyam upāyeṣu tathā tathā avaśyaṃbhāvi kāryatvam viśeṣāt ca arcana ādike jñānasya kasyacid prāptiḥ bhoga mokṣa upakāriṇaḥ yadā tad mukhyam eva uktam naimittika dinam budhaiḥ tad upāyaḥ śāstram atra vaktā api aupayikaḥ  guruḥ tad vidyaḥ  pi guru bhrātā saṃvādāt jñāna dāyakaḥ guroḥ patnī tathā bhrātā putra ityādikaḥ  gaṇaḥ na yoni saṃbandha vaśāt vidyā saṃbandha jaḥ tu saḥ vīrya aruṇa parīṇāma deha ahantā pratiṣṭhitāḥ deha upakāra santānā jñāteye pariniṣṭhitāḥ tathā ca smṛti śāstreṣu santateḥ dāya hāri tā yuktā eva tāvān sa hi uktaḥ  bhedāt dūra antika tvataḥ ye tu tyakta śarīra āsthā bodha ahambhāva bhāginaḥ bodha upakāra santāna dvayāt te bandhu tā juṣaḥ tatra ittham prāc yadā paśyet śakti unmīlita dṛkkriyaḥ dehaḥ tāvat ayam pūrva pūrva upādāna nirmitaḥ ātmā vikāra rahitaḥ śāśvata tvāt ahetukaḥ svātantryāt  punar ātmīya ādayam channa iva sthitaḥ punar ca prakaṭībhūya bhairavībhāva bhājanam tatra asya prakaṭībhāve bhukti mukti ātmake bhṛśam ya upāyaḥ samucitaḥ  jñāna santāna eṣa saḥ krama sphuṭībhavat tādṛś sadṛśa jñāna dhārayā gala dvijātīya tayā prāpyam śīghram hi labhyate evam ca anādi saṃsāra ucita vijñāna santateḥ dhvaṃse loka uttaram jñānam santāna antara tām śrayet  asaṃsāra ucita udāra tathā vijñāna santateḥ kāraṇam mukhyam ādyam tad guru vijñānam ātma gam atyantam sva viśeṣāṇām tatra arpaṇa vaśāt  sphuṭam upādānam hi tad yuktam dehabhede hi sati api deha santati gau bheda abhedau vijñāna santateḥ na tathā tvāya yogi icchā āviṣṭa śāva śarīravat yoginaḥ para deha ādi jīvatta āpādane nijam deham atyajataḥ  nānā jñāna upādāna tā na kim tena vijñāna santāna prādhānya ādyauna santateḥ anyonyam guru santānaḥ  yaḥ śiva jñāna niṣṭhitaḥ ittham sthite trayam mukhyam kāraṇam sahakāri ca eka kāraṇa kāryam ca vastu iti eṣa guroḥ gaṇaḥ guruḥ kāraṇam atra uktam tad patnī sahakāriṇī yatas  niḥśaktikasya asya na yāge dhikṛtiḥ bhavet  antar stha udāra saṃvitti śakteḥ bāhyām vinā api tām sāmarthyam yoginaḥ  yadvat vinā api sahakāriṇam ekajanyā bhrātaraḥ syuḥ tad sadṛś yaḥ tu kaḥ  pi saḥ punar  paramparā yogāt guru vargaḥ  pi bhaṇyate mukhya  eṣa tu santānaḥ pūjyaḥ  mānyaḥ ca sarvadā guru ādīnām ca sambhūtau dīkṣāyām prāyaṇe pi ca yad ahar tad hi vijñāna upāya deha ādi kāraṇam evam sva janma divasaḥ  vijñāna upāya ucyate tādṛś bhoga apavarga ādi hetoḥ dehasya kāraṇam dīkṣā ādikaḥ ca saṃskāraḥ sva ātmanaḥ  yatra ca ahni tad  bhavet janma dinam mukhyam jñāna santāna janmataḥ svakam mṛti dinam yad tu tad anyeṣām bhaviṣyati naimittikam mṛtaḥ  yasmāt śiva abhinnaḥ tadā bhavet  tatra prasaṅgāt maraṇa svarūpam brūmahe sphuṭam vyāpakaḥ  pi śivaḥ sva icchā kḷpta saṅkoca mudraṇāt  vicitra phala karma ogha vaśāt tad tad śarīra bhāj  śarīra bhāj tvam ca etāvat yad tad garbha stha deha gaḥ saṃvitteḥ śūnya rūḍhāyāḥ prathamaḥ prāṇana udayaḥ garbha stha deha nirmāṇe tasya eva īśvara tā punar  asaṅkocasya tanu ādi kartā tena īśa ucyate sa vāyu ātmā dṛḍhe tasmin deha yantre cit ātmanā preryamāṇaḥ  vicarati bhastrā yantra gavāyuvat atas  prāk gāḍha saṃsupta utthitavat sa prabuddhyate kramāt dehena sākam ca prāṇanā syāt balīyasī tatra api karma niyati balāt sā prāṇa nākṣatām gṛhṇāti śūnya suṣira saṃvid sparśa adhika tvataḥ evam krameṇa saṃpuṣṭa deha prāṇa balaḥ  bhṛśam bhogān karma kṛtān bhuṅkte yoni ayoni ja deha gaḥ uktam ca gahvara abhikhye śāstre śītāṃśu maulinā yathā gṛham viniṣpādya gṛhī samadhitiṣṭhati tathā dehī tanum kṛtvā kriyā ādi guṇa varjitaḥ kiñcid sphuraṇa mātraḥ prāgniṣkalaḥ saḥ  pi śabdyate sphuṭa indriya ādi tattvaḥ tu sakala ātmā iti bhaṇyate ityādi śrī gahvara uktam tatas  eva paṭhet bahu kṣaye tu karmaṇām teṣām dehayantre nyathāgate prāṇayantram vighaṭate dehaḥ syāt kuḍyavat tatas  nāḍī cakreṣu saṅkoca vikāsau viparītatas bhaṅgaḥ śoṣaḥ klidirvāta śleṣma agni apacaya uccayaiḥ iti evamādi yad kiñcit prāk saṃsthāna upamardakam dehayantre vighaṭanam tad eva uktam manīṣibhiḥ tasmin vighaṭite yantre sā saṃvid prāṇanā ātma tām gṛhṇāti yoni je nyatra vā dehe karma citrite sa dehaḥ pratibudhyeta prasupta utthitavat tadā tasya api bhoga tad hāni mṛtayaḥ prāgvat eva hi visṛṣṭi sthiti saṃhārā ete karma balāt yatas  atas  niyati kāla ādi vaicitrya anuvidhāyinaḥ anugrahaḥ tu yaḥ saḥ  yam sva svarūpe vikasvare jñapti ātmā iti katham karma niyatyādi pratīkṣate karma kāla niyati ādi yatas  saṅkoca jīvitam saṅkoca hāni rūpe smin katham hetuḥ anugrahe anugrahaḥ ca kramikaḥ tīvraḥ ca iti vibhidyate prāk  ca eṣa vistarāt prokta iti kim punaruktibhiḥ tena dīkṣā śiva jñāna dagdha saṅkoca bandhanaḥ dehānte śiva eva iti na asya deha antara sthitiḥ ye pi tattva avatīrṇānām śaṃkara ājñā anuvartinām svayambhū muni deva ṛṣi manuja ādi bhuvām gṛhe mṛtāḥ te tad puram prāpya pureśaiḥ dīkṣitāḥ kramāt  martye vatīrya vā naḥ vā śivam yānti apunarbhavāḥ tatra svayambhuvaḥ  dvedhā ke pi anugraha tatparāḥ ke pi sva kṛtyāyāta aṃśa sthāna mātra upasevinaḥ ye nugraha artham ājñaptāḥ teṣu yaḥ  mriyate naraḥ saḥ  nugraham sphuṭam yāti vinā martya avatārataḥ yaḥ tu sva kāryam kurvāṇaḥ tad sthānam na aṃśataḥ tyajet  yathā gaurī tapasyantī kaśmīreṣu guhā āgatā tatra eva vā yathā dhyāna uḍḍāre narahariḥ vibhuḥ vitastām nayataḥ  daityān  trāsayan dṛpta utthitaḥ sāligrāme yathā viṣṇuḥ śivaḥ  vā sva upabhoginaḥ tapasyantau badaryām ca nara nārāyaṇau tathā iti evamādayaḥ  devāḥ sva kṛtya aṃśa sthitāḥ tathā ārādhitāḥ sva ucitam tad śīghram vidadhate phalam sva kṛtya aṃśa sthitānām ca dhāmni ye ntam vrajanti te tatra bhogān  tathā bhuktvā martyeṣu avataranti api martya avatīrṇāḥ te tad tad aṃśakāḥ tad mayāḥ punar  tad dīkṣā jñāna caryā ādi kramāt yānti śiva ātma tām sthāvara ādyāḥ tiryak antāḥ paśavaḥ  smin dvaye mṛtāḥ sva karma saṃskriyā vedhāt tad loke citra tā juṣaḥ puṃsām ca paśu mātrāṇām sālokyam avivekataḥ avivekaḥ tad viśeṣān unmeṣān mauḍhyataḥ tathā sthāvara ādyāḥ tathā abhāvam uttarottara tām ca vā prapadyante na te sākṣāt rudratām tām kramāt punar  haṃsa kāraṇḍava ākīrṇe nānā taru kula ākule iti etad āgameṣu uktam tatas  eva pure pure kṣetra mānam bruve śrīmat sarva jñāna ādiṣu uditam liṅgāt hasta śatam kṣetram ācārya sthāpite sati svayambhūte sahasram tu tad ardham ṛṣi yojite tattva vid sthāpite liṅge svayambhū sadṛśam phalam atattva vidyat ācāryaḥ  liṅgam sthāpayate tadā punar vidhiḥ bhavet doṣaḥ  hi anyathā ubhaya dūṣakaḥ aham anyaḥ para ātmā anyaḥ śivaḥ  nya iti ced matiḥ na mocayet na muktaḥ ca sarvam ātma mayam yatas  tasmāt tattva vidā yad yad sthāpitam liṅgam uttamam tad eva āyatana tvena saṃśrayet bhukti muktaye uktam śrī ratna mālāyām jñātvā kālam upasthitam mokṣa arthī na bhayam gacchet tyajet deham aśaṅkitaḥ tīrtha āyatana puṇyeṣu kālam vā vañcayet priye ayogina āmayam panthā yogī yogena vañcayet  vañcane tu asamarthaḥ san kṣetram āyatanam vrajet  tīrthe samāśrayāt tasya vañcanam tu vijāyate anena ca dharā ādyeṣu tattveṣu abhyāsa yogataḥ tāvat siddhi juṣaḥ  pyuktā muktyai kṣetra upayogi tā samyak jñānini vṛttāntaḥ purastāt tu upadekṣyate paśūnām eṣa vṛttāntaḥ  ye tu tad tattva dīkṣitāḥ te tad īśa samīpa tvam yānti su aucitya yogataḥ yogyatā vaśa saṃjātā yasya yatra eva vāsanā sa tatra eva niyoktavyaḥ pureśāt ca ūrdhva śuddhi bhāj  iti śrī pūrva kathitam śrīmat svāyambhuve pica yaḥ  yatra abhilaṣet bhogān sa tatra eva niyojitaḥ siddhi bhāj mantra sāmarthyāt ityādi anyatra varṇitam ye tu tad tattva vijñāna mantra caryā ādi vartinaḥ mṛtāḥ te tatra tad rudrasa yuj tvam yānti kovidāḥ teṣām sa yuktvam yātānām api saṃskārataḥ  nijāt  tathā tathā vicitraḥ syāt avatāraḥ tad aṃśataḥ siddhānta ādau purāṇeṣu tathā ca śrūyate bahu tulye rudra avatāra tve citra tvam karma bhogayoḥ aneka śakti khacitam yatas  bhāvasya yad vapuḥ śaktibhyaḥ  rtha antaram na eṣa tad samūhāt ṛte bhavet  tena śakti samūha ākhyāt tasmāt rudrāt yad aṃśataḥ kṛtyam tad ucitam siddhyet  som śaḥ vatarati sphuṭam ye ca adhara prāpta dīkṣāḥ tad āsthān ujjhitāḥ pare tattve mṛtāḥ kāṣṭhavat te dhare pyutkarṣa bhāginaḥ ye tu ujjhita tad utkarṣāḥ te tad uttara bhāginaḥ ye pyūrdhva tattva dīkṣāḥ te vinā tāvat vivekataḥ prāpta adhara antā api tad dīkṣā phala subhāginaḥ atyakta āsthā hi te tatra dīkṣāyām api śāstritāt  vinā vivekāt āsthām te śritā loka prasiddhitaḥ paśu mātrasya sālokyam sāmīpyam dīkṣitasya tu tad parasya tu sāyujyam iti uktam parameśinā yaḥ tu ūrdhva śāstra gaḥ tatra tyakta āsthaḥ saṃśayena saḥ vrajan  āyatanam na eva phalam kiñcid samaśnute uktam tad viṣayam ca etad devadevena yad vṛthā dīkṣā jñānam tathā tīrtham tasya ityādi sa vistaram yaḥ tu tāvat ayogyaḥ  pi tathā āste sa śiva ālaye paścāt āsthānibandhena tāvat eva phalam bhajet  nadīnaga hrada prāyam yad ca puṇyam na tad mṛtau utkṛṣṭam tad mṛtānām tu svarga bhoga upabhogi tā ye punar  prāpta vijñāna vivekā maraṇa antike adhara āyataneṣu āsthām śritāḥ te tra tirohitāḥ tad jñāna dūṣaṇa uktam yad teṣām syāt kila pātakam tad tad pureśa dīkṣā ādi kramāt naśyet iti sthitiḥ dīkṣā āyatana vijñāna dūṣiṇaḥ  ye tu cetasā ācaranti ca tad te tra sarve niraya gāminaḥ jñāna āyatana dīkṣā dā  āsthābandha paricyutiḥ vyāpāra vyāhṛtaiḥ jñeyā tāni api dvividhāni ca yāni jātucit api eva svāsthye na udamiṣan punar  asvāsthye dhātu doṣa utthāni eva tad bhoga mātrakam dhātu doṣāt ca saṃsāra saṃskārāḥ te prabodhitāḥ chidra gā api bhūyiṣṭha jñāna dagdhā na rohiṇaḥ ye tu kaivalya bhāgīyāḥ svāsthye nunmiṣitāḥ sadā asvāsthye ca unmiṣanti ete saṃskārāḥ śaktipātatas yatas  sāṃsārikāḥ pūrva gāḍha abhyāsa upasaṃskṛtāḥ iti ūce bhujaga adhīśaḥ tad chidreṣu iti sūtrataḥ ye tu kaivalya bhāgīyāḥ pratyayāḥ te na jātucit  abhyastāḥ saṃsṛteḥ bhāvāt tena ete śaktipātatas vyāpāra vyāhṛtaiḥ tena dhātu doṣa prakopitaiḥ aprāpta niścaya āmarśaiḥ supta matta upamānakaiḥ viparītaiḥ api jñāna dīkṣā guru ādi dūṣakaiḥ tirobhāvaḥ  na vijñeyaḥ  hṛdaye rūḍhyabhāvataḥ ata eva prabuddhaḥ  pi karma utthān bhoga rūpiṇaḥ yama kiṅkara sarpa ādi pratyayān deha gaḥ bhajet  na etāvatā na muktaḥ  sau mṛtiḥ bhogaḥ  hi janmavat  sthitivat ca tatas  duḥkha sukhābhyām maraṇam dvidhā atas  yathā prabuddhasya sukha duḥkha vicitra tāḥ sthitau na ghnanti mukta tvam maraṇe pi tathā eva tāḥ ye punar yoginaḥ te pi yasmin  tattve su bhāvitāḥ cittam niveśayanti eva tad tattvam yānti aśaṅkitāḥ śrī svacchande tatas  proktam gandha dhāraṇayā mṛtāḥ ityādi mālinīśāstre dhāraṇānām tathā phalam eteṣām maraṇa abhikhyaḥ  bhogaḥ  na asti tu ye tanum dhāraṇābhiḥ tyajanti āśu para deha praveśavat etāvān mṛti bhogaḥ  hi marma  chid mūḍha tā akṣa gā dhvānta ābila tvam manasi tad ca eteṣu na vidyate tathā hi mānasam yatnam tāvat samadhitiṣṭhati ahaṃrūḍhyā pare dehe yāvat syāt buddhi saṃcaraḥ prāṇa cakram tadāyattam api saṃcarate pathā tena eva atas  prabuddhyeta para dehe kṣacakrakam makṣikā makṣikā rājam yathā utthitam anūtthitāḥ sthitam ca anuviśanti evam cittam sarva akṣa vṛttayaḥ atas  sya para deha ādi saṃcāre na asti melanam akṣāṇām madhya gam sūkṣmam syāt etad dehavat punar  evam para śarīra ādi cāriṇām iva yoginām tad tad tattva śarīra antar cāriṇām na asti mūḍha tā te ca api dvividhā jñeyā laukikā dīkṣitāḥ tathā pūrve śivāḥ syuḥ kramaśas  pare tad bhoga mātrataḥ dīkṣā api ūrdhva adhara aneka bheda yojanikā vaśāt bhidyamānā yoginām syāt vicitra phala dāyinī ye tu vijñāninaḥ te tra dvedhā kamprā itara tvataḥ tatra ye kampra vijñānāḥ te dehāntet  śivāḥ sphuṭam yatas  vijñānam eteṣām utpannam na ca su sphuṭam vikalpa antara yogena na ca api unmūlita ātmakam atas  dehe pramāda utthaḥ  vikalpaḥ  deha pātatas naśyet avaśyam tad ca api budhyate jñānam uttamam saṃskāra kalpanā tiṣṭhat adhvastīkṛtam antarā prāpta pākam saṃvarītuḥ apāye bhāsate hi tad  ye tu su abhyasta vijñāna mayāḥ śiva mayāḥ sadā jīvanmuktā hi te na eṣām mṛtau kā api vicāraṇā yathā hi jīvanmuktānām sthitau na asti vicāraṇā sukhi duḥkhi vimūḍha tve  mṛtau  api tathā na sā śrī ratna mālāśāstre tad uvāca parameśvaraḥ sva śāstre ca api ahi īśānaḥ  viśva ādhāra dhurandharaḥ rathyā antare mūtra purīṣa madhye caṇḍāla gehe niraye śmaśāne sa cintakaḥ  vā gata cintakaḥ  vā jñānī vimokṣam labhate pi ca ante apicā iti dhvaniḥ jīvanmukta tām asya bhāṣate sa cintā cintakatva uktiḥ etāvat saṃbhava sthitim tīrthe śvapaca gṛhe vā naṣṭa smṛtiḥ api parityajet deham jñāna sama kāla muktaḥ kaivalyam yāti hata śokaḥ ananta kārikā ca eṣā prāha idam bandhakam kila sukṛtam duṣkṛtam ca asya śaṅkyam tad ca asya naḥ bhavet  api śabdāt alupta smṛtyā vā saṃbhāvyate kila mṛtiḥ naṣṭa smṛteḥ eva mṛteḥ prāk  sā astu kim tayā liṅca saṃbhāvanāyām syāt iyat saṃbhāvyate kila sa ca kāla dhvaniḥ prāha mṛteḥ muktā avahetutām kaivalyam iti ca āśaṅkā padam yā api abhavat tanuḥ bheda pradatvena eṣā api dhvastā tena viśokatā para deha ādi saṃbandhaḥ  yathā na asya vibhedakaḥ tathā sva deha saṃbandhaḥ  jīvanmuktasya yadi api atas ca na viśeṣaḥ  sya viśva ākṛti nirākṛteḥ śiva abhinnasya dehe vā tad abhāve pi vā kila tathā api prācya tad bheda saṃskāra āśaṅkana sthiteḥ adhunā uktam kevala tvam yad vā mātṛ antara āśrayāt tāni enam na viduḥ bhinnam taiḥ sa muktaḥ  bhidhīyate śrīmat traiśirase pyuktam sūrya indu puṭa varjite jugupsā bhāva bhaṅga sthe sarvatas  stambhavat sthite sarva vyāpatti rahite pramāṇa pratyaya atige tasmin bodha antare līnaḥ karma kartā api anañjanaḥ pradhānam ghaṭa ākāśa ātmā maṣṭe ghaṭe pi kham na naśyet tadvat eva asau  ātmā śivam ayaḥ  bhavet  svatantraḥ  vasthitaḥ  jñānī prasaret sarva vastuṣu tasya bhāvaḥ naca abhāvaḥ saṃsthānam na ca kalpanā etad eva antarā gūrya guruḥ gītāsu abhāṣata yam yam vā api smaran bhāvam tyajati ante kalevaram tam tam eva eti kaunteya sadā tad bhāva bhāvitaḥ tasmāt sarveṣu kāleṣu mām anusmara yudhya ca yadā sattve vivṛddhe tu pralīnaḥ tu ūrdhva gaḥ tadā kramāt rajaḥ tamaḥ līnaḥ karma yoni vimūḍha gaḥ tatra indriyāṇām saṃmoha śvāsa āyāsa parīta tā ityādi mṛti bhogaḥ  yam dehe na tyajanam tanoḥ yaḥ tu asau kṣaṇa eva ekaḥ caramaḥ prāṇana ātmakaḥ yad anantaram eva eṣa dehaḥ syāt kāṣṭha kuḍyavat  sā dehatyāga kāla aṃśa kalā deha viyoginī tatas  eva hi tad deha sukha duḥkha ādika ujjhitā tasyām yad eva smarati prāc saṃskāra prabodhataḥ adṛṣṭa abhyāsa bhūyaḥtva śaktipāta ādi hetukāt  tad eva rūpam abhyeti sukhi duḥkhi vimūḍhakam yad vā niḥsukha duḥkha ādi yadi vā ānanda rūpakam kasmāt eti tad eva eṣa yatas  smarati saṃvidi prāk  prasphuret yad adhikam dehaḥ  sau cit adhiṣṭhiteḥ yad eva prāk adhiṣṭhānam citā tādātmya vṛttitaḥ sā eva atra līna tā proktā sattve rajasi tāmase nīla pīta ādike jñeye yatas  prāk kalpitām tanum adhiṣṭhāya eva saṃvittiḥ adhiṣṭhānam karoti alam atas  dhiṣṭheya mātrasya śarīra tve pi kuḍyataḥ dehasya asti viśeṣaḥ  yad sarva adhiṣṭheya pūrva tā tādātmya vṛttiḥ anyeṣām tad na sati api vedyate vedyānām kintu dehasya nitya avyabhicaritvataḥ sā ca tasya eva dehasya pūrva mṛtyanta janmanā smṛtyā prācya anubhavana kṛta saṃskāra citrayā yuktyā anaya asmat santāna guruṇā kallaṭena yad  deha aviśeṣe prāṇa ākhya dārḍhyam hetuḥ udīritam tad yuktam anyathā prāṇa dārḍhye kaḥ  hetuḥ ekatas  deha tvasya aviśeṣe pīti eṣa praśnaḥ  na śāmyati smaran  iti śatā hetau tad rūpam pratipadyate prāk  smaryate yatas  dehaḥ prāk cita adhiṣṭhitaḥ sphuran atas  smaraṇam antyam yad tad asarvajña mātṛṣu na jātu gocaraḥ  yasmāt deha antara viniścayaḥ yad tu bandhu priyā putra pāna ādi smaraṇam sphuṭam na tad deha antara asaṅgi na tad antyam yatas  bhavet  kasya api tu śarīra ante vāsanā yā prabhotsyate deha sattve tad aucityāt jāyeta anubhavaḥ sphuṭaḥ yathā purāṇe kathitam mṛga potaka tṛṣṇayā muniḥ kaḥ  pi mṛgībhāvam abhyuvāha adhivāsitaḥ tatra saḥ  nubhavaḥ  hetuḥ na janma antara sūtaye tasya etad vāsanā hetuḥ kākatālīyavat  sa tu nanu kasmāt tad eva eṣa smarati iti āha yad sadā tad bhāva bhāvitaḥ tena tad eva eṣa smarati alam evam asmi bhaviṣyāmi iti eṣa tad bhāva ucyate bhaviṣyataḥ  hi bhavanam bhāvyate na sataḥ kvacid  kramāt sphuṭatva karaṇam bhāvanam parikīrtyate sphuṭasya ca anubhavanam na bhāvanam idam sphuṭam tad ahar jāta bālasya paśoḥ kīṭasya vā taroḥ mūḍha tve pi tadānīm prāgbhāvanā hi abhavat sphuṭā sā tad mūḍha śarīra ante saṃskāra pratibodhanāt  smṛti dvāreṇa tad deha vaicitrya phala dāyinī deśa ādi vyavadhāne pi vāsanānām udīritāt  ānantarya eka rūpa tvāt smṛti saṃskārayoḥ atas  tathā anubhavana ārūḍhyā sphuṭasya api tu bhāvitā bhāvyamānā na kim sūte tad santāna sadṛk vapuḥ tad tādṛś ta adṛśaiḥ bandhu putra mitra ādibhiḥ saha bhāsate pi pare loke svapnavat vāsanā kramāt nanu mātṛ antaraiḥ bandhu putra ādyaiḥ tad tathā na kim vedyate ka idam prāha sa tāvat veda vedya tām vyāpāra vyāhṛti vrāta vedye mātrantara vraje svapne na asti sa iti eṣā vāc pramāṇa vivarjitā ya eva ete tu dṛśyante jāgrati ete mayā īkṣitāḥ svapna iti astu mithyā etad tad pramātṛ vacaḥ balāt yāna paśyam aham svapne pramātṝn  te na kecana na śocanti na ca īkṣante mām iti atra asti kā pramā yatas  sarva anumānānām sva saṃvedana niṣṭhitau pramātṛ antara sadbhāvaḥ saṃvid niṣṭhaḥ  na tad gataḥ ghaṭa ādeḥ astitā saṃvid niṣṭhitā na tu tad gatā tadvat mātṛ antare pyeṣā saṃvid niṣṭhā na tad gatā tena sthitam idam yad yad bhāvyate tad tad eva hi dehānte budhyate naḥ ced  syāt anyādṛś prabodhanam tathā hi antya kṣaṇe brahma vidyā karṇana saṃskṛtaḥ mucyate jantuḥ iti uktam prāc saṃskāra bala tvataḥ nipātābhyām anta śabdāt smaraṇāt śatuḥ antyatas  pādāt ca nikhilāt ardha ślokāt ca samanantarāt  līna śabdāt ca sarvam tad uktam artha sa tattvakam ajñātvā etad tu sarve pi kuśa kāśa avalambinaḥ yad tadoḥ vyatyayam kecid kecid anyādṛśam kramam bhinna kramau nipātau ca tyajati iti ca saptamīm vyācakṣate tad ca sarvam na upayogi ukta yojane na ca tad darśitam mithyā sva anta sammoha dāyakam tad itthaṃprāyaṇasya etad tattvam śrī śambhunāthataḥ adhigamya uditam tena mṛtyoḥ bhītiḥ vinaśyati vidita mṛti sa tattvāḥ saṃvid ambhaḥ nidhānāt acala hṛdaya vīrya ākarṣa niṣpīḍana uttham c amṛtam iti nigīrṇe kālakūṭe tra devāḥ  yadi pivatha tadānīm niścitam vaḥ śiva tvam utsavaḥ  pi hi yaḥ kaścid laukikaḥ saḥ  pi saṃmadam saṃvid abdhi taraṅga ābham sūte tad api parvavat  etena ca vipad dhvaṃsa pramoda ādiṣu parvatā vyākhyātā tena tatra api viśeṣāt devatā arcanam pura kṣobha ādi adbhutam yad tad svātantrye sva saṃvidaḥ dārḍhya dāyī iti tad lābha dine vaiśeṣika arcanam yoginī melakaḥ  dvedhā haṭhataḥ priyataḥ tathā prācye cchidrāṇi saṃrakṣet kāma cāri tvam uttare sa ca dvayaḥ pi mantra uddhṛt prasaṅge darśayiṣyate yoginī melakāt ca eṣaḥ  vaśyam jñānam prapadyate tena tad parva tadvat ca sva santānādi melanam saṃvid sarva ātmikā dehabheda ādyā saṅkucet tu sā melake nyonya saṅghaṭṭa pratibimbāt vikasvarā ucchalat nija raśmi oghaḥ saṃvid su pratibimbitaḥ bahu darpaṇavat dīptaḥ sarvāyeta api ayatnataḥ ata eva gīta gīta prabhṛtau bahu parṣadi yaḥ sarva tanmayībhāve hlādaḥ  na tu ekakasya saḥ ānanda nirbharā saṃvid pratyekam sā tathā ekatām nṛtta ādau viṣaye prāptā pūrṇa ānanda tvam aśnute īrṣyā asūya ādi saṅkoca kāraṇā bhāvataḥ tra sā vikasvarā niṣpratigham saṃvid ānanda yoginī atanmaye tu kasmiṃścid tatra sthe pratihanyate sthapuṭa sparśavat saṃvid vijātīya tayā sthite atas cakra arcanādyeṣu vijātīyam atanmayam na eva praveśayet saṃvid saṅkocana nibandhanam yāvanti eva śarīrāṇi sva aṅgavatsyuḥ su nirbharām ekām saṃvidam āviśya cakre tāvanti pūjayet  praviṣṭaḥ ced pramādena saṅkocam na vrajet tatas  prastutam sva samācāram tena sākam samācaret  sa tu anugraha śaktyā ced viddhaḥ tad tanmayībhavet vāma āvidhaḥ tu tad nindet paścāt tam ghātayet api śrīmat picumate ca uktam ādau yatnena rakṣayet  praveśam saṃpaviṣṭasya na vicāram tu kārayet  loka ācāra sthitaḥ  yaḥ tu praviṣṭe tādṛśe tu saḥ akṛtvā tam gurum abhyarthayeta pūjā puraḥ saram matimān saḥ  pi sva śāsanīye para śiṣye pivā api tādṛśam śāstram śrotum yogye kuryāt vyākhyānam vaiṣṇava ādi adhare karuṇā rasa paripūrṇaḥ  guruḥ punar marma dhāma matimān sūtrapada vākya paṭala grantha krama yojanena sambandhāt  avyāhata pūrvā param upavṛhya nayeta vākyāni maṇḍūka plavasiṃha avalokana ādyaiḥ yathāyatham nyāyaiḥ avihata pūrva aparakam śāstra artham yojayet asaṅkīrṇam tantra āvartana bādha prasaṅga tarka ādibhiḥ ca sannyāyaiḥ vastu vadet vākyajñaḥ  vastu antarataḥ  viviktatām vidadhat  yad yad vyāhṛti padavīm āyāti tad eva dṛḍhataraiḥ nyāyaiḥ balavat kuryāt dūṣyam yadi api agre bhaviṣyat syāt  dṛḍha racita pūrva pakṣa proddharaṇa pathena vastu yad vācyam śiṣya m atau  ārohati tadā āśu saṃśaya viparyayaiḥ vikalam bhāṣā nyāyaḥ  vādaḥ  layaḥ kramaḥ  yad yadā iti śiṣyasya sambodha upāya tvam tathā eva guruḥ āśrayet vyākhyām vācyam vastu samāpya pratarpaṇam pūjanam bhavet cakre punar aparam vastu vadet paṭalāt ūrdhvam tu naḥ jalpet sarvasmāt karmaṇaḥ  jālāt smṛti tattva kalā vidaḥ tathā api sthiti rakṣa artham kartavyaḥ coditaḥ  vidhiḥ atattva vedinaḥ  ye hi caryā mātra eka niṣṭhitāḥ teṣām dolāyite citte jñāna hāniḥ prajāyate prakartavyam iti śrī brahmayāmale brahma ghnaḥ  guru talpa sthaḥ  vīra dravya haraḥ tathā deva dravya hṛd ākāra prahartā liṅga bhedakaḥ nitya ādi lopa kṛt bhraṣṭa svaka mātra aparicchadaḥ śakti tatas  kuryāt iti uktam brahmayāmale dīkṣā abhiṣeka naimitta vidhyante guru pūjanam aparedyus  sadā kāryam siddhayogīśvarīmate pūrva ukta lakṣaṇa upetaḥ kaviḥ trika sa tattva vid  sa guruḥ sarvadā pūjyaḥ svaiḥ mantraiḥ puṣpa dhūpa argha vistaraiḥ samālambhana sat vastraiḥ naivedyaiḥ tarpaṇaiḥ kramāt  āśāntam pūjayitvā enam dakṣiṇābhiḥ yajet śiśuḥ sarva svam asmai saṃdadyāt ātmānam api bhāvitaḥ atoṣayitvā tu gurum dakṣiṇābhiḥ samantatas tattva jñaḥ  pyṛṇabandhena tena yāti adhikāri tām guru pūjām akurvāṇaḥ śatam janmāni jāyate adhikārī tatas  muktim yāti iti skandayāmale tasmāt avaśyam prabhṛti prabhedi naimittikam tu idam karma  ch atha śrī tantrāloke ekonatriṃśam āhnikam atha samucita adhikāriṇa uddiśya rahasya ucyate tra vidhiḥ atha sarvā api upāseyam kula prakriyayā ucyate tathā parameśasya śaktiḥ sāmarthyam ūrdhva tā svātantryam ojaḥ  vīryam ca piṇḍaḥ saṃvid śarīrakam tathā tvena samastāni bhāva jātāni paśyataḥ dhvasta śaṅkā samūhasya yāgaḥ tādṛśa eva saḥ tādṛś rūpa nirūḍhi artham manaḥ vāc kāya vartmanā yad yad samācaret vīraḥ kula yāgaḥ sa sa smṛtaḥ bahis  śaktau yāmale ca dehe prāṇa pathe matau iti ṣoḍhā kula ijyā syāt pratibhedam vibhedinī snāna maṇḍala kuṇḍa ādi ṣoḍhāni āsa ādi yad na tad  kiñcid atra upayujyeta kṛtam vā khaṇḍanāya naḥ ṣaṣ maṇḍala vinirmuktam sarva āvaraṇa varjitam jñāna jñeya mayam kaulam proktam traiśirase mate atra yāge ca yad dravyam niṣiddham śāstra santatau tad eva yojayet dhīmān vāma amṛta pariplutam śrī brahmayāmale pyuktam surā śiva rasaḥ  bahis  tām vinā bhukti muktī naḥ piṣṭa kṣaudra guḍaiḥ tu sā strī napuṃsaka puṃrūpā tu pūrva apara bhoga dā drākṣā uttham tu param tejaḥ  bhairavam kalpanā ujjhitam etad svayam rasaḥ śuddhaḥ prakāśa ānanda cit mayaḥ devatānām priyam nityam tasmāt etad pivet sadā śrīmat krama rahasye ca nyarūpi parameśinā arghapātram yāga dhāma dīpa iti ucyate trayam rahasyam kaulike yāge tatra arghaḥ śakti saṃgamāt  bhū vastra kāya pīṭha ākhyam dhāma ca utkarṣa bhāj  kramāt  dīpā ghṛta utthā gāvaḥ  hi bhūcaryaḥ  devatāḥ smṛtāḥ iti jñātvā traye muṣmi n yatnavān kaulikaḥ  bhavet  tena argha pātra prādhānyam jñātvā dravyāṇi śambhunā yāni uktāni aviśaṅkaḥ  tra bhavet śaṅkā hi dūṣikā yāgaukaḥ  gandha dhūpa āḍhyam praviśya prāc udak mukhaḥ parayā vā tha mālinyā vilomāt ca anulomataḥ dāha āpyāya mayīm śuddhim dīpta saumya vibhedataḥ krameṇa kuryāt athavā mātṛsadbhāva mantrataḥ dīkṣām ced pracikīrṣuḥ tad śodhya adhva nyāsa kalpanam tatas  saṃśodhya vastūni śaktyā eva amṛta tām nayet  parāsampuṭa gā yad vā mātṛ sampuṭa gāpi athaḥ kevalā mālinī yad vā tāḥ samasteṣu karmasu nanda hetu phalaiḥ dravyaiḥ argha pātram prapūrayet  tatra ukta mantra tādātmyāt bhairava ātma tvam ānayet  tena nirbharam ātmānam bahis cakra anucakra gam vipruḍbhiḥ ūrdhva adharayoḥ antar  pītyā ca tarpayet  tathā pūrṇa sva raśmi oghaḥ procchalat vṛtti tā vaśāt bahis tādṛśam ātmānam didṛkṣuḥ bahis arcayet  arka aṅgule tha tad dvi triguṇe rakta paṭe śubhe vyomni sindūra subhage rājavartta bhṛte thavā nārikela ātmake ka ādye madya pūrṇe tha bhājane yad vā samudite rūpe maṇḍala sthe ca tad ṛśi yāgam kurvīta matimān  tatra ayam krama ucyate diśi udīcyām rudra koṇā dvāya vyantam gaṇeśvaram vaṭukam trīn gurūn siddhān yoginīḥ pīṭham arcayet  prācyām diśi gaṇeśa adha ārabhya abhyarcayet tatas  siddha cakram diś catuṣke gaṇeśa adhastana antakam khaga indraḥ saha vid jāmba illā ī ambayā saha vaktaṣṭiḥ vimalaḥ  nanta mekhalā amba āyutaḥ purā śaktyā maṅgalayā kūrma illā ī ambayā saha jaitraḥ  yāmye hi avijitaḥ tathā sa ānanda mekhalaḥ kāma maṅgalayā meṣaḥ kullā ī ambayā saha vindhyaḥ  jitaḥ  pyajarayā saha mekhalayā pare mad chandaḥ kuṅkuṇa ambā ca ṣaṣ yugmam sādhikārakam saumye marutta īśa antam dvitīyā paṅktiḥ īdṛśī amara vara deva citrā ali vindhya guḍikā iti kramāt ṣaḍamī sillā ī eruṇayā tathā kumārī ca bodhā ī sa mahālacchī ca apara mekhalayā śaktayaḥ ṣaṭ imāḥ ete hi sa adhikārāḥ pūjyā yeṣām iyam bahu vibhedā santatiḥ anavacchinnā citrā śiṣya praśiṣya mayī ānanda āvali bodhi prabhu pāda anta atha yogi śabda antā etā ovallyaḥ syuḥ mudrā ṣaṭkam kramāt tu etad dakṣa aṅguṣṭha ādi kaniṣṭhikā antam atha sā kanīyasī vāmāt  dvidaśa anta ūrdhva ga kuṇḍali bainda vahṛt na abhikandam iti chu mmāḥ śava rāḍa billa paṭṭillāḥ kara billa ambi śara billāḥ aḍabīḍa umbī dakṣiṇa billāḥ kumbhārika akṣara ākhyāca devī koṭṭa kula adri tripurīkām ākhyam aṭṭahāsaḥ ca dakṣiṇa pīṭham ca etad ṣaṭkam ghara palli pīṭha gam kramaśas  iti saṅketa abhijñaḥ  bhramate pīṭheṣu yadi sa siddhīpsuḥ acirāt labhate tad tad prāpyam yad yoginī vadanāt bhaṭṭa indra valkalāhi indra gaja indrāḥ sa mahīdharāḥ ūrdhvaretasa ete ṣaṣ adhikāra pada ujjhitāḥ adhikāraḥ  hi vīryasya prasaraḥ kula vartmani tad aprasara yogena te proktā ūrdhvaretasaḥ anyāḥ ca guru tad patnyaḥ śrīmat kālī kula uditāḥ anātta dehāḥ krīḍanti taiḥ taiḥ dehaiḥ aśaṅkitāḥ prabodhita tathā icchākaiḥ tad je kaulam prakāśate tathārūpa tayā tatra guru tvam paribhāṣitam te viśeṣāt na saṃpūjyāḥ smartavyā eva kevalam tatas  bhyantarataḥ  vāyu vahnyoḥ mātṛkayā saha mālinī kramaśas  pūjyā tatas  ntar mantra cakrakam mantra siddha prāṇa saṃvid karaṇa ātmani yā kule cakra ātmake citiḥ prabhvī proktā sā iha kuleśvarī sā madhye śrī parā devī mātṛsadbhāva rūpiṇī pūjya atha tad samāropāt aparātha parāparā eka vīrā ca sā pūjyā yad ivā sa kula īśvarā prasaret śaktiḥ ucchūnā sa ullāsaḥ  bhairavaḥ punar  saṅghaṭṭa ānanda viśrāntyā yugmam ittham prapūjayet  mahā prakāśa rūpāyāḥ saṃvidaḥ  visphuliṅgavat  yaḥ  raśmi aḥ ghaḥ tam eva atra pūjayet devatā gaṇam antar dvādaśakam pūjyam tatas  ṣṭāṣṭākam eva ca catuṣkam vā yathā iccham vā kā saṅkhyā kila raśmiṣu māheśī vairiñcī kaumārī vaiṣṇavī catur dikkam aindrī yāmyā muṇḍā yogeśīrīśataḥ tu koṇeṣu pavana antam aghora ādikam aṣṭakam asmin  atha aṣṭake kramaśas  saṅghaṭṭa ānanda dṛśā sampūjyam yāmalībhūtam aṣṭa aṣṭake pi hi vidhau nānā nām aprapañcite bahudhā vidhiḥ eṣa eva vihitaḥ tad saṃkhyā dīpa mālā syāt  śrī ratna mālāśāstre tu varṇa saṃkhyāḥ pradīpakāḥ varṇān  ca mukhya pūjyāyā vidyāyā gaṇayet sudhīḥ pīṭha kṣetra ādibhiḥ sākam kuryāt vā kula pūjanam yathā śrī mādhava kule parameśena bhāṣitam sṛṣṭi saṃsthiti saṃhārānāmakrama catuṣṭayam pīṭha śmaśāna sahitam pūjayet bhoga mokṣayoḥ ātmanaḥ  vā athavā śakteḥ cakrasya atha smaret imam nyasyatvena vidhim dehe pīṭha ākhye pārameśvaram aṭṭahāsam śikhā sthāne caritram ca karandhrake śrutyoḥ kaulagirim nāsā randhrayoḥ ca jayantikām bhruvoḥ ujjayinīm vaktre prayāgam hṛdaye punar  vārāṇasīm skandha yuge śrī pīṭham virajam gale eḍābhīm udare hālām nābhau kande tu gaḥ śrutim upasthe marukośam ca nagaram pauṇḍravardhanam elā puram puras tīram sakthi ūrvoḥ dakṣiṇā āditaḥ kuḍyākeśīm ca sopānam māyā pūkṣīrake tathā jānu jaṅghe gulpha yugme tu āmrāta nṛpa sadmanī pāda ādhāre tu vairiñcīm kālāgni avadhi dārikām na aham asmi na ca anyaḥ  sti kevalāḥ śaktayaḥ tu aham iti evaṃvāsanām kuryāt sarvadā smṛti mātrataḥ na tithiḥ na ca nakṣatram na upavāsaḥ  vidhīyate grāmya dharma rataḥ siddhyet sarvadā smaraṇena hi mātaṅga kṛṣṇa saunika kārmuka cārmika vikoṣi dhātu vibhedāḥ mātsyika cākrika dayitāḥ teṣām patnyaḥ  nava atra nava yāge saṅgama varuṇa ākula giri aṭṭahāsa jayantī caritra ka āmraka koṭṭam haima puram navamam syāt madhye tāsām ca cakriṇī mukhyā bījam sā pīḍayate rasa śalka vibhāgataḥ  tra kuṇḍalinī adhyuṣṭa pīṭha netrī kanda sthā viśvatas  bhramati iṣṭvā cakra udayam tu ittham madhye pūjyā kuleśvarī saṅkarṣiṇī tad anta ante saṃhāra āpyāya kāriṇī eka vīrā cakra yuktā cakrayāmala gā api vā īśa indra agniyama kravyāt kavāyu udakṣu hāsataḥ trikam trikam yajet etad bhāvi svatrika saṃyutam hṛd kuṇḍalī bhruvoḥ madhyam etad eva kramāt trayam śmaśānāni kramāt kṣetra bhavam sat yoginī gaṇam vasu aṅgula unnatān ūrdhva vartulān kṣāma madhyakān raktavartīn śruti dṛśaḥ  dīpān kurvīta sarpiṣā yad kiñcid athavā madhye sva anuṣṭhānam prapūjayet  advaitam eva na dvaitam iti ājñā parameśituḥ siddhānta vaiṣṇava ādi uktā mantrā mala yutāḥ tatas  tāvat tejaḥ  sahiṣṇu tvāt nirjīvāḥ syuḥ iha advaye kalaśam netra bandha ādi maṇḍalam sruc sruva analam hitvā atra siddhiḥ sat madye pātre madhye kṛśām yajet  ahorātram imam yāgam kurvataḥ ca apare hani vīra bhojye kṛte vaśyam mantrāḥ siddhi antya yatnataḥ
