pīṭha stotram paṭhet atra yāge bhāgya avaha āhvaye mūrtīḥ eva athavā yugma rūpā vīra svarūpiṇīḥ avadhūtā nirācārāḥ pūjayet kramaśas  budhaḥ eka eva atha kauleśaḥ svayam bhūtvā api tāvatīḥ śaktīrya amala yogena tarpayet viśva rūpavat  kramaḥ  nāma na kaścid syāt prakāśa maya saṃvidi cit abhāvaḥ  hi na asti eva tena akālam tu tarpaṇam atra krame bheda taroḥ sa mūlam unmūla nāda āsana pakṣa carcā pṛthak na yuktā parameśvaraḥ  hi sva śakti dhāmni iva viśaṃśrami iti tatas  japaḥ prakartavyaḥ tri lakṣa ādi vibhedataḥ uktam śrī yoga sañcāre sa ca citra svarūpakaḥ udaye saṅgame śāntau tri lakṣaḥ  japa ucyate āsye gama āgame sūtre haṃsa ākhye śaiva yugmake pañcalakṣā ime proktā daśa aṃśam homam ācaret  netre gama āgame vaktre haṃse ca eva akṣa sūtrake śiva śakti samāyoge ṣaṣ lakṣaḥ  japa ucyate netre gama āgame karṇe haṃse vaktre ca bhāmini haste ca yugmake ca eva japaḥ saptavidhaḥ smṛtaḥ netre gama āgame karṇau  āsyam guhyam ca guhyakam śatāreṣu ca madhyastham sahasrāreṣu bhāmini japa eṣa rudra lakṣaḥ  homaḥ  pyatra daśa aṃśataḥ netre gama āgame karṇau mukham brahmabila antaram stanau hastau ca pādau ca guhya cakre dvis abhyaset  yatra yatra gatam cakṣuḥ yatra yatra gatam manaḥ haṃsaḥ tatra dvis abhyasya u vikāsa ākuñcana ātmakaḥ sa ātmā mātṛkā devī śivaḥ  deha vyavasthitaḥ anyaḥ saḥ  nyaḥ ham iti evam vikalpam na ācaret yatas  yaḥ  vilpayate tasya siddhi muktī su dūrataḥ atha ṣoḍaśa lakṣa ādi prāṇa cāre purā uktavat  śuddha aśuddha vikalpānām tyāga ekānta ucyate tatrasthaḥ svayam eva eṣa juhoti ca japati api japaḥ sañjalpa vṛttiḥ ca nādāmarśa svarūpiṇī tadā amṛṣṭasya cit vahnau layaḥ  homaḥ prakīrtitaḥ āmarśaḥ ca purā proktaḥ  devī dvādaśaka ātmakaḥ dve antye saṃvidau tatra laya rūpa āhuti kriyā daśa anyāḥ tad upāyāya iti evam home daśa aṃśa tām śrī śambhunātha ādikṣattrikā artha ambhodhi candramāḥ sākam bāhya sthayā śaktyā yadā tu eṣa samarcayet  tadā ayam parameśa uktaḥ  rahasyaḥ  bhaṇyate vidhiḥ uktam śrī yoga sañcāre brahmacarye sthitim bhajet  ānandaḥ  brahma paramam tad ca dehe tridhā sthitam upakāri dvayam tatra phalam anyat tad ātmakam oṣṭhyā antya tritaya āsevī brahmacārī sa ucyate tad varjitā ye paśava ānanda parivarjitāḥ ānanda kṛt trim āhārāḥ tad varjam cakra yājakāḥ dvaye pi niraye yānti raurave bhīṣaṇe tu iti śakteḥ lakṣaṇam etāvat tadvataḥ  hi avibheditā tādṛśīm tena tām kuryāt na tu varṇa ādi apekṣaṇam laukikālaukika dvyātma saṅgāt tādātmyataḥ  dhikāt  kārya hetu saha utthā sā tridhā uktā śāsane guroḥ sākṣāt paramparā yogāt tad tulyā iti tridhā punar  śrī sarva ācāra hṛdaye tad etad upasaṃhṛtam ṣaṭ etāḥ śaktayaḥ proktā bhukti mukti phala pradāḥ dvābhyām tu sṛṣṭi saṃhārau tasmāt melakam uttamam tām āhṛtya mithas  bhyarcya tarpayitvā parasparam antaraṅga krameṇa eva mukhya cakrasya pūjanam yad eva ānanda sandohi saṃvidaḥ  hi antaraṅgakam tad pradhānam bhavet cakram anucakramatas  param vikāsāt tṛptitaḥ pāśa utkartanāt kṛti śaktitaḥ cakram kaseścakeḥ kṛtyā karoteḥ ca kila uditam yāgaḥ ca tarpaṇam bāhye vikāsaḥ tad ca kīrtyate cakra anucakra antara gāt śaktimat parikalpitāt  prāṇa gāt api atha ānanda syandinaḥ  bhyavahārataḥ gandha dhūpa sraj ādeḥ ca bāhyāt ucchalanam citaḥ ittham sva ucita vastu aṃśaiḥ anucakreṣu tarpaṇam kurvīyātām iha anyonyam mukhya cakra ekatā kṛte uktam ca triśiraḥ tantre vimala āsana gocaraḥ akṣa ṣaṭkasya madhye tu rudra sthānam samāviśet  nija nija bhoga ābhoga pravikāsi nija svarūpa parimarśe kramaśas  nu cakra devyaḥ saṃvid cakram hi madhyamam yānti svastha tanoḥ aparasya tu tā deha adhiṣṭhitam vihāya yatas  āsata iti tad ahaṃyuḥ naḥ pūrṇaḥ  na api ca ucchalati anucakra devatā ātmaka marīci paripūraṇa adhigata vīryam tad śakti śaktimat yugam anyonya samunmukham bhavati tad yugalam ūrdhva dhāma praveśa saṃsparśa jāta saṅkṣobham kṣubhnāti anucakrāṇi api tāni tadā tad mayāni na pṛthak tu ittham yāmalam etad galita bhidā saṃkatham yad eva syāt  krama tāratamya yogāt sa eva hi saṃvid visarga saṅghaṭṭaḥ tad dhruva dhāmā anuttaram ubhaya ātmaka jagat udāra sa ānandam naḥ śāntam na api uditam śānta udita sūti kāraṇam param kaulam anavacchinna pada īpsuḥ tām saṃvidam ātmasāt sadā kuryāt  anavacchinnam paramārtha taḥ  hi rūpam citaḥ  devyāḥ īdṛś tā dṛś prāya praśama udaya bhāva vilaya parikathayā anavacchinnam dhāma praviśet vaisargikam subhagaḥ śānta udita ātmakam dvayam atha yugapad udeti śakti śaktimatoḥ rūpam uditam paraspara dhāma gatam śāntam ātma gatam eva ubhayam api vastutas  kila yāmalam iti tathā uditam śāntam śaktiḥ tadvat ucitām sṛṣṭim puṣṇāti naḥ tadvān śānta udita ātmaka ubhaya rūpa parāmarśa sāmya yoge pi pravikasvara madhya padā śaktiḥ śāstre tatas  kathitā tasyām eva kula artham samyak  saṃcārayet guruḥ tena tad dvāreṇa ca kathita krameṇa saṃcārayeta nṛṣu sva śarīra adhika sadbhāva bhāvi tām iti tatas  prāha śrīmat kallaṭa nāthaḥ prokta samasta artha labdhaye vākyam tad mukhya cakram uktam maheśinā yoginī vaktram tatra eṣa sampradāyaḥ tasmāt saṃprāpyate jñānam tad idam alekhyam bhaṇitam vaktrāt vaktra stha m ukta yuktyā ca vaktram pradhāna cakram svā saṃvid likhyatām ca katham atha sṛṣṭe dvitaye smin śānta udita dhāmni ye nusaṃdadhate prācyām visarga sattām anavacchidi te pade rūḍhāḥ ye siddhim āptu kāmāḥ te bhyuditam rūpam āhareyuḥ athaḥ  tena eva pūjayeyuḥ saṃvid naikaṭya śuddhatama vapuṣā tad apica mithas  hi vaktrāt pradhānataḥ vaktra gam yatas  bhaṇitam ajara amara pada dāna pravaṇam kula saṃjñitam paramam ye pyaprāpta vibodhāḥ te bhyudita utphulla yāga saṃrūḍhāḥ tad parikalpita cakra stha devatāḥ prāpnuvanti vijñānam te tatra śakti cakre tena eva ānanda rasa mayena bahis  dikṣu catasṛṣu prokta krameṇa gaṇanāthataḥ prabhṛti sarvam saṃpūjya madhyama pade kuleśa yugmam tvarā traye devīḥ bāhye pratyaram atha kila catuṣkam iti raśmi cakramarkāram aṣṭakam aṣṭa aṣṭakam atha vividham saṃpūjayet krameṇa muniḥ nija deha gate dhāmani tathā eva pūjyam samabhyasyet  yad tad śāntam rūpam tena abhyastena hṛdaya saṃvittyā śāntam śiva padam eti hi galita taraṅga arṇava prakhyam tad śānta pada adhyāsāt cakra sthaḥ  devatā gaṇaḥ sarvaḥ tiṣṭhati uparata vṛttiḥ śūnya ālambī nirānandaḥ yaḥ  pyanucakra dṛś ādi svarūpa bhāj  saḥ  pi yad tad āyattaḥ tena ānande magnaḥ tiṣṭhati ānanda sa ākāṅkṣaḥ para tad svarūpa saṅghaṭṭam antareṇa eṣa karaṇa raśmi gaṇaḥ āste hi niḥsvarūpaḥ svarūpa lābhāya ca unmukhitaḥ raṇa raṇaka rasān nija rasa bharita bahirbhāva carvaṇa vaśena viśrānti dhāma kiñcid labdhvā sva ātmani atha arpayate tad nija viṣaya arpaṇataḥ pūrṇa samucchalita saṃvid āsāraḥ anucakra devatā gaṇa paripūraṇa jāta vīrya vikṣobhaḥ cakreśvaraḥ  pi pūrva ukta yuktitaḥ procchalet rabhasāt  trividhaḥ  visarga ittham saṅghaṭṭaḥ proditaḥ tathā śāntaḥ visṛjati yatas  vicitraḥ sargaḥ  vigataḥ ca yatra sarga iti śrī tattva rakṣaṇe śrī nigame triśiromate ca tad proktam kuṇḍam śaktiḥ śivaḥ  liṅgam melakam paramam padam dvābhyām sṛṣṭiḥ saṃhṛtiḥ tad visargaḥ trividhaḥ game srotaḥ dvayasya niṣṭhā antam ūrdhva adhas cakra bodhanam viśrāmam ca samāveśam suṣīṇām marutām tathā gata bhedam ca yantrāṇām sandhīnām marmaṇām api dvāsaptati pade dehe sahasrāre ca nityaśas  gati āgati antarā vittī saṅghaṭṭayati yad śivaḥ tad prayatnāt sadā tiṣṭhet saṅghaṭṭe bhairave pade ubhayoḥ tad nirākāra bhāva saṃprāpti lakṣaṇam mātrā vibhāga rahitam su sphuṭa artha prakāśakam abhyasyet bhāva saṃvittim sarva bhāva nivartanāt sūrya somau tu saṃrudhya laya vikṣepa mārgataḥ evam trividha vimarśa āveśa samāpatti dhāmni ya udeti saṃvid parimarśa ātmā dhvaniḥ tad eva iha mantra vīryam syāt  tatra eva udita tādṛśa phala lābha samutsukaḥ svakam mantram anusandhāya sadā ced āste mantra udayam sa vai vetti atra eva japam kuryāt anucakra ekatva saṃvid āgamane yugapad lakṣa vibheda prapañcitam nāda vṛttyā eva śrī yoga sañcare pica mudrā iyam yoginīpriyā paramā koṇatraya antara āśrita nitya unmukha maṇḍala  chade kamale satatā viyutam na alam ṣoḍaśa dala kamala kalita sat mūlam madhyastha nāla gumphita saroja yuga ghaṭṭana kramāt agnau madhyastha pūrṇa sundara śaśadhara dinakara kalā ogha saṅghaṭṭāt  tridala aruṇa vīrya kalā saṅgāt madhye ṅkuraḥ sṛṣṭiḥ iti śaśadhara vāsara pati citra gu saṃghaṭṭa mudrayā jhaṭiti sṛṣṭi ādi kramam antar  kurvan  tuḥ ye sthitim labhate etad khecara mudrā āveśe nyonyasya śakti śaktimatoḥ pāna upabhoga līlā āhāsa ādiṣu yaḥ  bhavet vimarśa mayaḥ avyakta dhvani rāvasphoṭa śruti nādanā da antaiḥ avyucchinna anāhata rūpaiḥ tad mantra vīryam syāt  iti cakrāṣṭaka rūḍhaḥ sahajam japam ācaran pare dhāmni yad bhairava aṣṭaka padam tad labhate ṣṭaka kalā bhinnam gamana āgamane vasitau karṇe nayane dvi liṅga saṃparke tad saṃmelana yoge dehānta ākhye ca yāmale cakre kuca madhya hṛdaya deśāt oṣṭha antam kaṇṭha gam yad avyaktam tad cakra dvaya madhya gama ākarṇya kṣobha vigama samaye yad  nirvānti tatra ca evam yaḥ  ṣṭavidhaḥ  nādabhairavaḥ paramaḥ jyotiḥ dhvani samira kṛtaḥ sā māntrī vyāptiḥ ucyate paramā sakalākaleśa śūnyam kalā āḍhya kha male tathā kṣapaṇakam ca antar stham kaṇṭhya uṣṭhyam candrāt vyāptiḥ tathā unmana antā iyam evam karmaṇi karmaṇi yatra kvāpi smaran vyāptim satatam alepaḥ  jīvanmuktaḥ para bhairavībhavati tādṛś melaka kalikā kalita tanuḥ kaḥ  pi yaḥ  bhavet garbhe uktaḥ sa yoginībhūḥ svayam eva jñāna bhājanam rudraḥ śrī vīra āvaliśāstre bālaḥ  pi ca garbha gaḥ hi śiva rūpaḥ ādīyate yatas  sāram tasya mukhyasya ca eṣa yad  mukhyaḥ ca yāgaḥ tena ayam ādi yāga iti smṛtaḥ tatra tatra ca śāstre sya svarūpam stutavān vibhuḥ śrī vīra avalihārda īśa kha mata arṇava vartiṣu śrī siddha utphulla maryādā hīna caryā kula ādiṣu yugmasya asya prasādena vrata yoga vivarjitaḥ sarvadā smaraṇam kṛtvā ādi yāga eka tatparaḥ śakti dehe nije nyasyet vidyām kūṭam anukramāt  dhyātvā candra nibham padmam ātmānam bhāskara dyutim vidyā mantra ātmakam pīṭha dvayam atra eva melayet  na paṭhyate rahasya tvāt spaṣṭaiḥ śabdaiḥ mayā punar  kutūhalī tu ukta śāstra saṃpāṭhāt eva lakṣayet  yad bhajante sadā sarve yadvān devaḥ ca devatā tad cakram paramam devī yāga ādau saṃnidhāpakam deha eva param liṅgam sarva tattva ātmakam śivam devatā cakra saṃjuṣṭam pūjā dhāma tad uttamam tad eva maṇḍalam mukhyam tri triśūla abja cakra kham tatra eva devatā cakram bahis antar  sadā yajet  sva sva mantra parāmarśa pūrvam tad janmabhī rasaiḥ ānanda bahulaiḥ sṛṣṭi saṃhāra vidhinā spṛśet  tad sparśa rabhasa udbuddha saṃvid cakram tad īśvaraḥ labhate paramam dhāma tarpita aśeṣa daivataḥ anuyāga ukta vidhinā dravyaiḥ hṛdaya hāribhiḥ tathā eva sva sva kāmarśa yogāt antar  pratarpayet  kṛtvā ādhāra dharām camatkṛti rasa prokṣa akṣaṇa kṣālitāmāttaiḥ mānasataḥ svabhāva kusumaiḥ sva āmoda sandohibhiḥ ānanda amṛta nirbhara sva hṛdayānargha argha pātra kramāt tvām devyā saha deha deva sadane deva arcaye harniśam śrī vīra āvalya maryāda prabhṛtau śāstra sañcaye sa eṣa paramaḥ  yāgaḥ stutaḥ śītāṃśu maulinā athavā prāṇa vṛtti stham samastam devatā gaṇam paśyet pūrva ukta yuktyā eva tatra eva abhyarcayet guruḥ prāṇa āśritānām devīnām brahma nāsa ādi bhedibhiḥ karandhraiḥ viśata apāna cāndra cakreṇa tarpaṇam evam prāṇa krameṇa eva tarpayet devatā gaṇam acirāt tad prasādena jñāna siddhīratha aśnute saṃvid mātra sthitam devī cakram vā saṃvid arpaṇāt  viśvābhoga prayogeṇa tarpaṇīyam vipaścitā yatra sarve layam yānti dahyante tattva sañcayāḥ tām citim paśya kāyasthām kāla anala sama prabhām śūnya rūpe śmaśāne smin yoginī siddha sevite krīḍā sthāne mahā raudre sarva astamita vigrahe sva raśmi maṇḍala ākīrṇe dhvaṃsita dhvānta santatau sarvaiḥ vikalpaiḥ nirmukte ānanda pada kevale asaṃkhya citi saṃpūrṇe śmaśāne citi bhīṣaṇe samasta devatā ādhāre praviṣṭaḥ kaḥ  na siddhyati śrīmat vīra āvalī śāstre ittham provāca bhairavī ittham yāgam vidhāya ādau tādṛśa aucitya bhāginam lakṣaikīyam sva śiṣyam tam dīkṣayet tādṛśi krame rudra śaktyā tu tam prokṣya deva abhyāśe niveśayet  bhujau tasya samālokya rudra śaktyā pradīpayet  tayā eva asya arpayet puṣpam karayoḥ gandha digdhayoḥ nirālambau tu tau tasya sthāpayitvā vicintayet  rudra śakti ākṛṣyamāṇau dīptayā aṅkuśa rūpayā tatas  sa svayam ādāya vastram baddha dṛśiḥ bhavet  svayam ca pātayet puṣpam tad pātāt lakṣayet kulam tatas  sya mukham uddhāṭya pādayoḥ praṇipātayet  hastayoḥ mūrdhni ca api asya devī cakram samarcayet  ākarṣya ākarṣaka tvena prerya preraka bhāvataḥ uktam śrī ratna mālāyām nābhim daṇḍena saṃpuṭam vāma bhūṣaṇa jaṅghābhyām nitambena api alaṅkṛtam śiṣya haste puṣpa bhṛte codanā astram tu yojayet  yāvat sa stobham āyātaḥ svayam patati mūrdhani śiva hastaḥ svayam saḥ  yam sadyas pratyaya kārakaḥ anena eva prayogeṇa carukam grāhayet guruḥ śiṣyeṇa dantakāṣṭham ca tad pātaḥ prāgvat eva tu karaḥ tobhaḥ netra paṭa grahāt prabhṛti yaḥ kila dantakāṣṭha samādāna paryantaḥ tatra lakṣayet  tīvra manda ādi bhedena śaktipātam tathāvidham iti eṣa samayī proktaḥ śrī pūrve kara kampataḥ samayī tu kara stobhāt iti śrī bhoga hastake carveva vā guruḥ dadyāt vāma amṛta pariplutam niḥśaṅkam grahaṇāt śakti gotraḥ  māyā ujjhitaḥ  bhavet  sa kampaḥ tu ādadānaḥ syāt  samayī vācana ādiṣu kāla antare dhvasaṃśuddhyā pālanāt samaya sthiteḥ siddhipātram iti śrīmat ānandeśvara ucyate yadā tu putrakam kuryāt tadā dīkṣām samācaret  uktam śrī ratna mālāyām na ādi phāntām jvalat prabhām nyasyet śikha antam patati tena atra īdṛś  kramaḥ  bhavet  prokṣitasya śiśoḥ nyasta prokta śodhya adhva padhateḥ ṛju deha juṣaḥ śaktim pādāt mūrdha antam āgatām pāśān dahantīm saṃdīptām cintayet tad mayaḥ  guruḥ upaviśya tatas tasya mūla śodhyāt  prabhṛti alam anta śodhya avasāna antān dahantīm cintayet kramāt  evam sarvāṇi śodhyāni tattva ādīni purā uktavat  dagdhvā līnām śive dhyāyet niṣkale sakale thavā yoginā yojitā mārge sajātīyasya poṣaṇam kurute nirdahati antad bhinna jāti kadambakam anayā śodhyamānasya śiśoḥ tīvra ādi bhedataḥ śaktipāta at citi vyoma prāṇana antar bahis tanūḥ āviśantī rudra śaktiḥ kramāt sūte phalam tu idam ānandam udbhavam kampam nidrām ghūrṇim ca deha gām evam stobhita pāśasya yojitasya ātmanaḥ śive śeṣa bhogāya kurvīta sṛṣṭim saṃśuddha tattva gām athavā kasyacid na evam āveśaḥ tad dahet imam bahis antar ca ukta śaktyā patet ittham sa bhū tale yasya tu evam api syāt na tam atra upalavat tyajet atha sa pratyayām dīkṣām vakṣye tuṣṭena dhīmatā śaṃbhu nāthena upadiṣṭām dṛṣṭām sadbhāva śāsane sudhā agni marutaḥ  manda para kāla agni vāyavaḥ vahni saudhā su kūṭa agni vāyuḥ sarve sa ṣaṣṭhakāḥ etad piṇḍa trayam stobha kāri pratyekam ucyate śakti bījam smṛtam yad ca nyasyet sārvāṅgikam tu tad  hṛd cakre nyasyate mantraḥ  dvādaśa svara bhūṣitaḥ japā kusuma saṃkāśam caitanyam tasya madhyatas  vāyunā preritam cakram vahninā paridīpitam tad dhyāyet ca japet mantram nāma antarita yogataḥ nimeṣa ardhāt tu śiṣyasya bhavetḥ tobhaḥ na saṃśayaḥ ātmānam prekṣate devi tattve tattve niyojitaḥ yāvat prāptaḥ param tattvam tadā tu eṣa na paśyati anena krama yogena sarva adhvānam sa paśyati athavā sarva śāstrāṇi api udgrāhayati tad kṣaṇāt  pṛthak tattva vidhau dīkṣām yogyatā vaśavartinaḥ tattva abhyāsa vidhānena siddha yogī samācaret  iti saṃdīkṣitasya asya mumukṣoḥ śeṣa vartane kula krama iṣṭiḥ ādeśyā pañca avasthā samanvitā jāgrat ādiṣu saṃvittiḥ yathā syāt anapāyinī kula yāgaḥ tathā ādeśyaḥ  yoginī mukha saṃsthitaḥ sarvam jāgrati kartavyam svapne pratyeka mantra gam nivārya supte mūla ākhyaḥ sva śakti paribṛṃhitaḥ turye tu ekā eva dūtyā ākhyā tad atīte kuleśitā sva śakti paripūrṇānām ittham pūjā pravartate piṇḍa stha ādi ca pūrva uktam sarva atīta avasānakam avasthā pañcakam prokta bhedam tasmai nirūpayet  sādhakasya bubhukṣoḥ tu samyak yoga abhiṣecanam tatra iṣṭvā vibhavaiḥ devam hema ādi mayam avraṇam dīpa aṣṭakam raktavarti sarpiṣā pūrya bodhayet  kula aṣṭakena tad pūjyam śaṅkhe ca api kuleśvarau ānanda amṛta saṃpūrṇe śiva hasta ukta vartmanā tena abhiṣiñcet tam paścāt  sa kuryāt mantra sādhanam ācāryasya abhiṣekaḥ  yam adhikāra anvitaḥ sa tu kuryāt piṣṭa ādibhiḥ ca asya catuṣṣaṣṭim pradīpakān aṣṭa aṣṭakena pūjyāḥ te madhye prāgvat  kuleśvarau śiva hasta ukta yuktyā eva gurum api abhiṣecayet  abhiṣiktau  imau  evam sarva yogi gaṇena tu viditau bhavataḥ tatra guruḥ mokṣa pradaḥ  bhavet  tātparyam asya pādasya sa siddhīḥ saṃprayacchati guruḥ yaḥ sādhakaḥ prāk syāt anyaḥ  mokṣam dadāti alam anayoḥ kathayet jñānam trividham sarvam api alam svakīya ājñām ca vitaret  sva kriyā karaṇam prati ṣaṭkam kāraṇa saṃjñam yad tathā yaḥ paramaḥ śivaḥ sākam bhairava nāthena tad aṣṭakam udāhṛtam pratyekam tasya sārvātmyam paśyan  tām vṛttim ātma gām cakṣuḥ ādau saṃkramayet yatra yatra indriye guruḥ sa eva pūrṇaiḥ kalaśaiḥ abhiṣekaḥ paraḥ smṛtaḥ vinā bāhyaiḥ api iti uktam śrī vīra āvalibhairave sadya eva tu bhoga īpsoḥ yogāt siddha tamaḥ  guruḥ kuryāt sadyas tathā abhīṣṭa phala dam vedha dīkṣaṇam vedha dīkṣā ca bahudhā tatra tatra nirūpitā sā ca abhyāsavatā kāryā yena ūrdhva ūrdhva praveśataḥ śiṣyasya cakra saṃbheda pratyayaḥ jāyate dhruvaḥ yena aṇima ādikā siddhiḥ śrī mālāyām ca coditā ūrdhva cakra daśa alābhe piśāca āveśa eva sā mantra nāda bindu śakti bhujaṅgam apara ātmikā ṣoḍhā śrī gahvare vedha dīkṣā uktā parameśinā jvālā ākulam sva śāstra uktam cakram aṣṭa araka ādikam dhyātvā tena asya hṛd cakravedhanāt mantra vedhanam ākāram navadhā dehe nyasya saṃkramayet tatas  nyāsa yogena śiṣyāya dīpyamānam mahā arciṣam pāśa stobhāt tatas tasya para tattve tu yojanam iti dīkṣā uttare dṛṣṭaḥ  vidhiḥ me śaṃbhunā uditaḥ nāda uccāreṇa nāda ākhyaḥ sṛṣṭi krama niyogataḥ nādena vedhayet cittam nāda vedha udīritaḥ bindu sthāna gatam cittam bhrū madhya patha saṃsthitam hṛd lakṣye vā maheśāni bindum jvālā ākula prabham tena saṃbodhayet sādhyam bindu ākhyaḥ  yam prakīrtitaḥ śāktam śaktimat uccārāt gandha uccāreṇa sundari śṛṅgāṭaka āsana stham tu kuṭilam kuṇḍala ākṛtim anuccāreṇa ca uccārya vedhayet nikhilam jagat  evam bhramara vedhena śāktavedha udāhṛtaḥ sā ca eva paramā śaktiḥ ānanda pravikāsinī janma sthānāt param yāti phaṇa pañcaka bhūṣitā kalāḥ tattvāni nanda ādyā vyomāni ca kulāni ca brahma ādi kāraṇāni akṣāṇi eva sā pañcaka ātmikā evam pañca prakārā sā brahma sthāna vinirgatā brahma sthāne viśantī tu taḍit līnā virājate praviṣṭā vedhayet kāyam ātmānam pratibhedayet  evam bhujaṅga vedhaḥ tu kathitaḥ  bhairava āgame tāvat bhāvayate cittam yāvat cittam kṣayam gatam kṣīṇe citte sureśāni para ānanda udāhṛtaḥ na indriyāṇi na vai prāṇā na antaḥkaraṇa gocaraḥ na manaḥ  na api mantavyam na mantā na manikriyā sarva bhāva parikṣīṇaḥ para vedha udāhṛtaḥ manu śakti bhuvana rūpa jñā piṇḍa sthāna nāḍi para bhedāt navadhā kalayanti anye vedam guravaḥ  rahasya vidaḥ māyā garbha agni varṇa ogha yukte tri aśriṇi maṇḍale dhyātvā jvālā karālena tena granthīn vibhedayet  puṣpaiḥ hanyāt yojayet ca pare mantra abhidhaḥ vidhiḥ nāḍī ā viśya anyatarayā caitanyam kanda dhāmani piṇḍīkṛtya paribhramya pañca aṣṭa śikhayā haṭhāt  śakti śūla agra gamitam kvāpi cakre niyojayet  śaktyā iti śāktaḥ  vedhaḥ  yam sadyas pratyaya kārakaḥ ādhārāt nirgatayā śikhayā jyotsnā avadātayā rabhasāt  aṅguṣṭha mūla pīṭha krameṇa śiṣyasya līnayā vyomni deham svacchīkṛtya kṣādīna antān smaran pura ukta puryoghān nija maṇḍala nirdhyānāt pratibimbayate bhuvana vedhaḥ bhrū madhya udita baindavadhāma antaḥ kāṃcid ākṛtim rucirām tādātmyena dhyāyet śiṣyam paścāt ca tad mayīkuryāt  iti rūpa vedha uktaḥ sā ca iha ākṛtiḥ upaiti dṛśya tvam ante tad sāyujyam śiṣyaḥ ca āyāti tanmayībhūtaḥ vijñānam aṣṭadhā yad dhrāṇa ādika buddhi saṃjña karaṇa antaḥ tad  sva sva nāḍi sūtra krameṇa saṃcārayet śiṣye abhimāna dārḍhya bandha krameṇa vijñāna saṃjñakaḥ  vedhaḥ hṛdaya vyomani sadyas  divya jñāna arka samudayam dhatte piṇḍaḥ paraḥ kalā ātmā sūkṣmaḥ puryaṣṭakaḥ  bahis  sthūlaḥ chāyā ātmā sa parāṅmukha ādarśa ādau ca saṃmukhaḥ  jñeyaḥ iti yaḥ piṇḍa vibhedaḥ tam rabhasāt uttarottare śamayet  tad tad nalane kramaśas  parama padam piṇḍa vedhena yad yad dehe cakram tatra śiśoḥ etya viśramam kramaśas  ujjvalayet tad cakram sthāna ākhyaḥ tad phala pradaḥ  vedhaḥ nāḍyaḥ pradhāna bhūtāḥ tisraḥ  nyāḥ tad gatāḥ tu asaṃkhyeyāḥ ekīkāraḥ tābhiḥ nāḍī vedhaḥ  tra tad phala kṛt  abhilaṣita nāḍi vāhaḥ  mukhyābhiḥ cakṣuḥ ādi niṣṭhābhiḥ adbodha prāptiḥ syāt nāḍī vedhe vicitra bahu rūpā lāṅgūla ākṛti balavat  sva nāḍi saṃvoṣṭi tām apara nāḍīm āsphoṭya siddham api bhuvi pātayati haṭhāt mahā yogī para vedham samasteṣu cakreṣu adva etamāmṛśan param śivam prakurvīta śiva tā āpatti daḥ  guruḥ śrīmat vīra āvali kule tathā ca ittham nirūpitam abhedyam sarvathā jñeyam madhyam jñātvā na lipyate tad vibhāga krame siddhaḥ sa guruḥ mocayet  paśūn guroḥ agre viśet śiṣyaḥ  vaktram vaktre tu vedhayet  rūpam rūpe tu viṣayaiḥ yāvat samarasī bhavet citte samarasībhūte dvayoḥ aunmanasī sthitiḥ ubhayoḥ ca unmanaḥ gatyā tad kāle dīkṣitaḥ  bhavet  śaśi bhāskara saṃyoge jīvaḥ tad maya tām vrajet  atra brahma ādayaḥ  devāḥ  muktaye mokṣa kāṅkṣiṇaḥ nirudhya raśmi cakram svam bhoga mokṣau  ubhau  api grasate yadi tad dīkṣā śārvīyam parikīrtitā sa eṣa mokṣaḥ kathitaḥ  niḥspandaḥ sarva jantuṣu agnīṣoma kalā ghāta saṅghātāt spandanam haret  bāhyam prāṇam bāhya gatam timira ākāra yogataḥ niryātam romakūpaiḥ tu bhramantam sarva kāraṇaiḥ madhyam nirlakṣyam āsthāya bhramayet visṛjet tatas  saṃghaṭṭa utpāṭa yogena vedhayet granthi pañcakam saṃghaṭṭa vṛtti yugalam madhya dhāma vicintayet  na ātma vyoma bahis mantra deha saṃdhānam ācaret dīkṣā iyam sarva jantūnām śiva tā āpatti dāyikā dīkṣā ante dīpakān paktvā samastaiḥ sādhakaiḥ saha caruḥ prāśyaḥ kula ācāryaiḥ mahāpātaka nāśanaḥ iti śrī ratna mālāyāmūna adhika vidhiḥ tu yaḥ sa eva pātakam tasya praśamaḥ  yam prakīrtitaḥ pare hani guroḥ kāryaḥ  yāgaḥ tena vinā yatas  na vidhiḥ pūrṇa tām yāti kuryāt yatnena tam tatas  yena yena guruḥ tuṣyet tad tad asmai nivedayet  cakra caryā antarāle syā vidhiḥ saṃcāra ucyāte ali pātram su saṃpūrṇam vīra indra kara saṃsthitam avalokya param brahma tad piveda ājñayā guroḥ tarpayitvā tu bhūtāni gurave vinivedayet  kṛtvā bhuvi gurum na tu ādāya saṃtarpya khecarīḥ svam mantram tad ca vanditvā dūtīm gaṇaptim gurūn kṣetrapam vīra saṅghātam guru ādi kramaśas tatas  vīra spṛṣṭam svayam dravyam pivet na eva anyathā kvacid  para brahmaṇi avettāraḥ  gama āgama vivarjitāḥ lobha moha mada krodha rāga māyā juṣaḥ ca ye taiḥ sākam na ca kartavyam etad śreyorthinā ātmani yāga ādau yāga madhye ca yāga ante guru pūjane naimittikeṣu prokteṣu śiṣyaḥ kuryāt imam vidhim iti rahasya vidhiḥ paricarcitaḥ  guru mukha anubhavaiḥ su parisphuṭaḥ  ch atha śrī tantrāloke triṃśam āhnikam atha yathocita mantra kadambakam trika kula krama yogi nirūpyate tāvat vimarśānārūḍha dhiyām tātsiddhaye kramāt  pratibuddhā hi te mantrā vimarśa eka svabhāvakāḥ svatantrasya eva cit dhāmnaḥ svātantryāt  kartṛ tā āmayāḥ yam āviśanti ca ācāryam tam tādātmya nirūḍhitaḥ svatantrīkurvate yānti karaṇāni api kartṛ tām ādhāra śaktau hrīm pṛthvī prabhṛtau tu catuṣṭaye kṣlām kṣvīm vam kṣam iti prāhuḥ kramāt varṇa catuṣṭayam ham nāle yam tathā ram lam vam dharma ādi catuṣṭaye ṛṃ ṝm ḷm ḷḷm catuṣke ca viparīta kramāt bhavet  om aum hastrayam iti etad vidyā māyā kalā traye anusvāra visargau ca vidyeśa īśvara tattvayoḥ ka ādi bhāntāḥ kesareṣu prāṇaḥ  ṣṭa svara saṃyutaḥ sa bindu kaḥ  daleṣu aṣṭasu atha svam nāma dīpitam śaktīnām navakasya syāt śaṣasā maṇḍala traye sa bindukāḥ kṣmam prete jram śūla śṛṅgeṣu kalpayet  pṛthak āsana pūjāyām kramāt mantrā ime smṛtāḥ saṃkṣepa pūjane tu prāc ādya m antyam ca bījakam ādāya ādhāra śakti ādi śūla śṛṅga antam arcayet agni māruta pṛthvī ambu sa ṣaṣṭha svara bindukam rati śekhara mantraḥ  sya vaktra aṅgam hrasva dīrghakaiḥ agni prāṇa agni saṃhāra kāla indra ambu samīraṇāḥ sa ṣaṣṭha svara birndu adha candra ādyāḥ syuḥ nava ātmanaḥ bindu nāda ādikā vyāptiḥ śrīmat traiśirase mate kṣepa ākrānti cit udbodha dīpana sthāpanāni atha tad saṃvittiḥ tad āpattiḥ iti saṃjñā abhiśabditā etāvatī mahāvyāptiḥ mūrti tvena atra kīrtitā pariṇāmaḥ tallayaḥ ca namaskāraḥ sa ucyate eṣa tri arṇa ujjhitaḥ  dhastāt dīrghaiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ svaraiḥ yutaḥ ṣaḍaṅgāni hṛd ādīni vaktrāṇi asya ca kalpayet  kṣaya ravala bījaiḥ tu dīptaiḥ bindu vibhūṣitaiḥ jhakāra saṃhṛti prāṇāḥ sa ṣaṣṭha svara bindukāḥ eṣa bhairava sadmāvaḥ candra ardha ādi vibhūṣitaḥ mātṛkā mālinī mantrau prāk eva samudāhṛtau oṃkāraḥ  tha caturthī antā saṃjñā natiḥ iti kramāt  gaṇeśa ādiṣu mantraḥ syāt bījam yeṣu na coditam nāma ādi akṣaram ākāra bindu candra ādi dīpitam sarveṣām eva bījānām tad caturdaśa ṣaṣṭha yuj  āmantrita ani aghorya ādi tritayasya krama uditaiḥ bījaiḥ visargiṇī māyā hum hakāraḥ  visargavān punar devī trayasya api kramāt āmantraṇa trayam dvitīyasmin pade kāra ekārasya iha ca smṛtaḥ tatas  śakti dvaya amantraḥ  luptam tatra antyam akṣaram he gni varṇau  ubhau pañca svara yuktau parau pṛthak  akāra yuktau  astram hum ha visargī punar  śaraḥ tāreṇa saha vasu agni varṇa ardha arṇa dvaya adhikā eṣā parāparāt evyā vidyā śrī trikaśāsane pañca ṣaṭpañca veda akṣi vahni netra akṣaram padam aghorya ādau saptake syāt  pivanyāḥ pariśiṣṭakam pratyeka varṇa gaḥ pyuktaḥ siddhayogīśvarīmate devatā cakra vinyāsaḥ sa bahu tvāt na lipyate māyā visargiṇī hum phaṭ  ca iti mantraḥ  para ātmakaḥ parāyāḥ tu ukta sat vyāptiḥ jīvaḥ saha caturdaśaḥ sā aneka bhedā triśiraḥśāstre proktā maheśinā svarūpataḥ  vibhinnā api racanā aneka saṅkulā jīvaḥ prāṇa stha eva atra prāṇaḥ  vā jīva saṃsthitaḥ ādhāra ādheya bhāvena avinā abhāva yogataḥ haṃsam ca amṛta madhya stham kālarudra vibheditam bhuvaneśa śiraḥ yuktam anaṅga dvaya yojitam dīptāt dīptataram jñeyam ṣaṭcakra krama yojitam prāṇam daṇḍāsana stham tu guhya śakti icchayā yutam pareyam vācikā uddiṣṭā mahā jñāna svarūpataḥ sphuṭam bhairava hṛd jñānam idam tu eka akṣaram param amṛtam kevalam kha stham yad vā sāvitrikā yutam śūnya dvaya samopetam parāyā hṛdayam param yugma yāge prasiddham tu kartavyam tattva vedibhiḥ anye pyekākṣarā ye tu eka vīra vidhānataḥ guptā guptatarāḥ te tu aṃga abhijana varjitāḥ yaṣṭavyāḥ sādhaka indraiḥ tu kula sthāḥ siddhi dāyakāḥ kula krama vidhānena sūkṣma vijñāna yogataḥ anuṣṭheyāḥ sadā devi striyā vā puruṣeṇa vā sa kāraḥ  dīrgha ṣaṭkena yuktaḥ  ṅgāni ānanāni tu syāt  sa eva param hrasva pañca sva rakha saṃyutaḥ oṃkāraiḥ pañcabhiḥ mantraḥ  vidyā aṅga hṛdayam bhavet  praṇavaḥ ca amṛte tejaḥ mālini svāhayā saha ekādaśa akṣaram brahmaśiraḥ tad mālinīmate veda vedani hūm phaṭ ca praṇava ādi yutā śikhā vajriṇe vajradharāya svāhā iti oṃkāra pūrvakam ekādaśa akṣaram varma puruṣṭutam iti smṛtam tāraḥ  dvijihvaḥ kha śara svara yuj jī iva eva ca netram etad prakāśa ātma sarva sādhāraṇam smṛtam tāraḥ ślīm paśu  hum phat  ca tad astram rasa varṇakam laraṭakṣa vayaiḥ dīrghaiḥ sama yuktaiḥ sa bindukaiḥ indra ādayaḥ tad astrāṇi hrasvaiḥ viṣṇu prajāpatī smṛtau turya dvitīyābhyām hrasvābhyām padma cakrake namaḥ svāhā tathā vauṣaṭ  hum vaṣaṭ  phaṭ  ca jātayaḥ aṅgeṣu kramaśas  ṣaṭsu karmasu atha tad ātmikāḥ jape home tathā āpyāye samuccāṭe tha śāntike abhicāre ca mantrāṇām namaskāra ādi jātayaḥ akṣiṣaj mu nivargebhyaḥ  dvitīyāḥ saha bindunā yoni arṇena ca mātṝṇām sadmāvaḥ kālakarṣiṇī ādya ujjhitaḥ  vā api antena varjitaḥ  vā atha saṃmataḥ jīvaḥ prāṇa puṭa antar sthaḥ kāla anala sama dyutiḥ ati dīptaḥ tu vāma aṃghriḥ bhūṣitaḥ  mūrdhni bindunā dakṣa jānugataḥ ca ayam sarva mātṛ gaṇa arcitaḥ anena prāṇitāḥ sarve dadate vāñchitam phalam sadbhāvaḥ paramaḥ  hi eṣa mātṝṇām bhairavasya ca tasmāt enam japet mantrī ya icchet siddhim uttamām rudra śakti samāveśaḥ  nityam atra pratiṣṭhitaḥ yasmāt eṣā parā śaktiḥ bhedena anyena kīrtitā yāvatyaḥ siddhayaḥ tantre tāḥ sarvāḥ kurute tu iyam aṅga vaktrāṇi ca api asyāḥ prāgvat svara niyogataḥ daṇḍaḥ  jīvaḥ triśūlam ca dakṣa aṅguli apara stanau nābhi kaṇṭhau marut rudrau visargaḥ sa triśūlakaḥ sarva yogi nicakrāṇām adhipaḥ  yam udāhṛtaḥ asya api uccāraṇāt eva saṃvittiḥ syāt purā uditā mahā caṇḍa iti tu yogeśvaṛ iti aṣṭa varṇakam navārṇeyam guptatarā sadbhāvaḥ kālakarṣiṇī śrī ḍāmare mahā yāge parātparatara uditā sudhā ācchedaka ṣaṇṭha ādyaiḥ bījam chedakam asvaram adhyardha arṇā kālarātriḥ kṣurikā mālinīmate śatāvartanayā hi asyāḥ  jāyate mūrdhni vedanā evam pratyayam ālocya mṛtyu jit dhyānam āśrayet  na enām samuccaret devi ya icchet dīrgha jīvitam dvis daṇḍa agnī śūla nabhaḥ prāṇāḥ chettra nalau tathā kūṭa agnī sa visargāḥ ca pañca api ete tha pañcasu vyomasu iti śivena uktam tantra sadbhāva śāsane chedinī kṣurikā iyam syāt yayā yojayate pare bindu indu anala kūṭa agni marut ṣaṣṭha svaraiḥ yutam āpāda tala mūrdha antam smaret astram idam jvalat  kuñcanam ca aṅgulīnām tu kartavyam codanam tatas  jānu ādi para cakra antam cakrāt cakram tu kuñcayet  kathitam sa rahasyam tu sadyonirvāṇakam param atha ucyate brahma vidyā sadyas pratyaya dāyinī śivaḥ śrī bhūtirājaḥ  yām asmabhyam pratyapādayat  sarveṣām eva bhūtānām maraṇe samupasthite yayā paṭhitayā utkramya jīvaḥ  yāti nirañjanam yā jñāninaḥ  pi saṃpūrṇa kṛtyasya api śrutā satī prāṇa ādi  cheda jām mṛtyu vyathām sadyas  vyapohati yām ākarṇya mahā moha vivaśaḥ  pi kramāt gataḥ prabodham vaktṛ sāṃmukhyam abhyeti rabhasāt svayam parama padāt tvam iha āgāḥ sanātanaḥ tvam jahīhi dehāntam pādāṅguṣṭha ādi vibhaḥ nibandhanam bandhanam hi ugram āryā vākyam idam pūrvam bhuvana ākhyaiḥ padaiḥ bhavet  gulpha ante jānu gatam jatru stham bandhanam tathā meḍhre jahihi puram agrya madhyam hṛd padmāt tvam samuttiṣṭha etāvadbhiḥ padaiḥ etad āryā vākyam dvitīyakam haṃsa hayagrīva vibhaḥ sadāśivaḥ tvam paraḥ  si jīva ākhyaḥ ravi soma vahni saṅgha dṛbindu dehaḥ  hahaha samutkrāma tṛtīyam āryā vākyam prāc saṃkhyaiḥ eka adhikaiḥ padaiḥ haṃsa mahā mantra mayaḥ sanātanaḥ tvam śubha aśubha apekṣī maṇḍala madhya niviṣṭaḥ śakti mahā setu kāraṇa mahā arthaḥ kamala ubhaya viniviṣṭaḥ prabodham āyāhi devatā deha āryā vākyam idam sārdham rudra saṃkhya pada īritam niḥśvāse tu apa śabdasya sthāne sti upa iti dhvaniḥ ajñānāt tvam baddhaḥ prabodhita uttiṣṭha deva āde etad pañcamam ārya ardha vākyam syāt saptabhiḥ padaiḥ vraja tālusāhvaya antam hi auḍambara ghaṭṭitam mahā dvāram prāpya prayāhi haṃhaḥ haṃhaḥ vā vāmadeva padam āryyā vākyam idam ṣaṣṭham syāt caturdaśabhiḥ padaiḥ granthīśvara paramātman śānta mahātālu randhram āsādya utkrama he deha īśvara nirañjanam śiva padam prayāhi āśu āryā vākyam saptamam syāt tad caturdaśabhiḥ padaiḥ prabhañjanaḥ tvam iti evam pāṭhaḥ  niḥśvāsa śāsane ākramya madhya mārgam prāṇa apānau samāhṛtya dharma adharmau tyaktvā nārāyaṇa yāhi śānta antam āryā vākyam idam proktam aṣṭamam navabhiḥ padaiḥ he brahman he viṣṇaḥ he rudra śivaḥ  si vāsudevaḥ tvam agnīṣoma sanātana mṛd piṇḍam jahihi he mahā ākāśa etad bhuvana saṃkhyātaiḥ āryyā vākyam prakīrtitam sana ātma tri piṇḍam iti mahākośam iti sthitam pada trayam tu niḥśvāsa mukuṭa uttaraka ādiṣu aṅguṣṭha mātram amalam āvaraṇam jahihi he mahā sūkṣma āryyā vākyam idam ṣaḍbhiḥ padaiḥ daśamam ucyate alam dvis iti sūkṣmam ca iti evam śrī mukuṭa uttare puruṣaḥ tvam prakṛti mayaiḥ baddhaḥ  haṅkāra tantunā bandhaiḥ abhavā abhava nitya udita paramātman  tyaja sa rāgam adhvānam etad trayodaśa padam syāt āryā vākyam uttamam hrīṃhūṃmantra śarīram avilambam āśu tvam ehi dehāntam ārya ardha vākyam etad syāt  dvādaśam ṣaṣ padam param tad idam guṇa bhūta mayam tyaja sva  ṣoṭkośikam piṇḍam syāt  trayodaśam ārya ardham padaiḥ saptabhiḥ īdṛśam mā deham bhūta mayam pragṛhyatām śāśvatam mahā deham ārya ardha vākyam tāvadbhiḥ padaiḥ etad caturdaśam maṇḍalam amalam anantam tridhā sthitam gaccha bhittvā etad  ārya ardha vākyam aṣṭābhiḥ padaiḥ pañcadaśam tu idam sakaleyam brahma vidyā syāt pañcadaśabhiḥ sphuṭaiḥ vākyaiḥ pañcākṣaraiḥ tu asyā niṣkalā parikīrtyate prativākyam yayādi anta yojitā paripaṭhyate tāraḥ  māyā veda kalaḥ mātṛ tāraḥ  nava ātmakaḥ iti pañcākṣarāṇi syuḥ prokta vyāpti anusārataḥ bindu prāṇa amṛta jalam marut ṣaṣṭha svara anvitam etena śakti uccāra stha bījena ālabhyate paśuḥ kṛta dīkṣā vidhiḥ pūrvam brahma ghnaḥ  pi viśuddhi ati laghu tvena tulā śuddhiḥ sadyas pratyaya kāriṇī tāraḥ śama rayaiḥ piṇḍaḥ  natiḥ ca catur aṛṇakam śākinī stobhanam marma hṛdayam jīvitam tu idam ṣaṣṭha prāṇa trikūṭa ūrdhva bāhu śūla ākhya bindubhiḥ anackanā sā adhas vaktra candra khaṇḍaiḥ ca maṇḍitam hṛdayam bhairava ākhyam tu sarva saṃhāra kārakam agni maṇḍala madhya stha bhairava anala tāpitāḥ vaśam āyānti śākinyaḥ sthānam etena ced dahet visarjayet tāḥ prathamam anyathā cchidrayanti tāḥ hrīm klīm vlem kleṃ ebhiḥ varṇaiḥ dvādaśa svara bhūṣitaiḥ priyamelāpanam nāma hṛdayam sampuṭam japet  pratyekam athavā dvābhyām sarvaiḥ vā vidhiḥ uttamaḥ tulā melaka yogaḥ śrī tantra sadbhāva śāsane ya uktaḥ śambhunāthena sa mayā darśitaḥ kramāt  atha vitta vihīnānām prapannānām ca tattvataḥ deśa kāla ādi doṣeṇa na tathā adhyavasāyinām prakartavyā yathā dīkhṣā śrī santa tyāgama uditā kathyate hāṭakeśāna pātāla adhipa coditā śrī nātha ārya bhagavan  etad tritayam hi kanda ādhāre varuṇaḥ  mad chandaḥ  bhagavat ta iti trayam idam hṛdaye dharma ādi varga saṃjñāḥ catvāraḥ kaṇṭha deśa gāḥ pūjyāḥ hrīṃśrīṃpūrvāḥ sarve sambodha juṣaḥ ca pāda śabda antāḥ mūrdha tale vidyā trayam uktam bhāvi atha manaḥ  bhiyogena kusumaiḥ ānandaiḥ vā bhāvanayā vā api kevalayā guruṇā tattva vidā kila śiṣyaḥ  yadi mokṣa mātra kṛta hṛdayaḥ mokṣa eka dāna caturā dīkṣā sā iyam para upaniṣad uktā etad dīkṣā dīkṣita etad vidyā trayam smaran hṛdaye bāhya arcā ādi vinā eva hi vrajati param dhāma dehānte praṇavaḥ  māyā binduḥ varṇa trayam āditas  kuryāt  pada pañcakasya saṃbodhana yuktasya agni dayita ante siddha sādhani tad pūrvam śabdabrahma svarūpiṇi samasta bandha śabdena sahitam ca nikṛntani bodhani śiva sadbhāva jananyā mantritam ca tad  pañca aṣṭa randhra tri aṣṭa arṇa krameṇa pada pañcakam kha pañca arṇā para brahma vidyā iyam mokṣa dā śivā anuttara icche ghāntaḥ ca sa trayodaśa su svaraḥ asya varṇa trayasya ante tu antaḥsthānām catuṣṭayam varga ādi aśvau tri asra bindu yuj  pāntaḥ  rṇa trayāt atas  mahā hāṭaka śabda ādyam īśvarī iti arṇa saptakam āmantritam kṣamasva iti tri arṇam pāpa anta kāriṇi ṣaṣ arṇam pāpa śabda ādi vimoha nipadam tatas  pāpam hana dhuna dvis dvis daśa arṇam padam īdṛśam pañcamī antam ṣaṣ arṇam syāt rudra śakti vaśāt iti tatas  eka akṣaram yad tad visarga brahma kīrtitam tad anat katakāreṇa saha ekībhāvataḥ paṭhet  randhra abdhi varṇā vidyā iyam dīkṣā avidyā iti kīrtitā māyā arṇañca pare brahme catur vidye pada trayam aṣṭa arṇam atha pañca arṇam yoga dhāriṇi saṃjñitam ātma antarātma paramātma rūpam ca pada trayam ekāra antam bodhana stham daśārṇam parikīrtitam rudra śakti iti veda arṇam syāt rudra dayite tha me pāpam dahadahā iti eṣā dvādaśa arṇā catuṣpadī saumye sadāśive yugmam ṣaṭkam bindu iṣusāvahā sārdha varṇa catuṣkam tad iti eṣā samaya apahā vidyā sārdha arṇakha śara saṃkhyā sā pārameśvarī etad vidyā trayam śrīmat bhūti rājaḥ  nyarūpayat  yaḥ sākṣāt abhajat śrīmān śrīkaṇṭhaḥ  mānuṣīm tanum atra vīryam purā eva uktam sarvatra anusaret guruḥ artha bīja praveśa antar uccāra ādi anusārataḥ na hi tad kiṃcana api asti yad purā na nirūpitam niṣphalā punaruktiḥ tu na asmabhyam jātu rocate iti evam mantra vidyā ādi svarūpam upavarṇitam  ch atha śrī tantrāloke ekatriṃśam āhnikam atha maṇḍala sadbhāvaḥ saṃkṣepeṇa abhidhīyate sādhayitvā diśam pūrvām sūtram āsphālayet samam tad ardhayitvā madhya prāk pratīcīṣu aṅkayet punar  tatas  pyardha tad ardha ardha mānataḥ pūrva paścimau aṅkayet tāvatā dadyāt  sūtreṇa bhrama yugmakam matsya sandhi dvayam tu evam dakṣiṇa uttarayoḥ bhavet  tad madhye pātayet sūtram dakṣiṇa uttara siddhaye yadi vā prāc parāk tulya sūtreṇa uttara dakṣiṇe aṅkayet aparāt aṅkāt  pūrvāt api tathā eva te matsya madhye kṣipet sūtram āyatam dakṣiṇa uttare mata kṣetra ardha mānena madhyāt dikṣu aṅkayet tatas  sūtrābhyām diś dvaya utthābhyām matsyaḥ syāt pratikoṇa gaḥ matsyeṣu vedāḥ sūtrāṇi iti evam syāt caturasrakam ekasmāt prabhṛti proktam śata antam maṇḍalam yatas  siddhātantre maṇḍalānām śatam tad pīṭha ucyate yad tad madhya gatam mukhyam maṇḍalānām trayam smṛtam madhya śūlam tri triśūlam navaśūlam iti sphuṭam tatra śūla vidhānam yad uktam bhedaiḥ anantakaiḥ tad yoni maṇḍalam brūmaḥ sadbhāva krama darśitam veda āśrite catur haste tri bhāgam sarvatas tyajet bhāgaiḥ ṣoḍaśabhiḥ sarvam tad tad kṣetram vibhājayet  brahmasūtra dvayasya atha madhyam brahma padam sphuṭam kṛtvā avadhim tatas  lakṣyam caturtham sūtram āditas  tatas tiryak vrajet sūtram caturtham tad anantare koṣṭhe ca indu dvayam kuryāt bahirbhāga ardha bhāgataḥ tayoḥ lagnam brahmasūtrāt tṛtīye marmaṇi sthitam koṣṭhaka ardhe param ca iti yugmam antarmukham bhavet  brahmasūtrāt dvitīyasmin haste marmaṇi niścalam kṛtvā pūrṇa indu yugalam vartayeta vicakṣaṇaḥ brahmasūtra gatāt  ṣaṣṭhāt  tiryak bhāgāt tṛtīyake kṛtvā ardha koṣṭhake sūtram pūrṇa candra agra lambitam bhramayet unmukham khaṇḍa candra yuj vahni bhāga gam tiryak bhāga dvayam tyaktvā khaṇḍa indoḥ paścimāt tatas  koṇam yāvat tathā syāt ca kuryāt  khaṇḍam bhrama dvayam su tīkṣṇa kuṭila agram tad ekam śṛṅgam prajāyate dvitīyasmin  api proktaḥ śṛṅga eṣa vidhiḥ sphuṭaḥ madhya śṛṅge tha kartavye tṛtīye ūrdhva koṣṭhake caturtha ardhe ca candra ardha dvayam antarmukham bhavet  tad ca pūrṇa indum ekam prāc vartitam prāpnuyāt yathā anyonya granthi yogena baddhāra tvam prajāyate evam dvitīya pārśve sya khaṇḍa indu dvaya vartanāt madhyābhyām gaṇḍikā śliṣṭā parābhyām agratas  nayet  sūtram pārśva dvaye yena tīkṣṇam syāt madhya śṛṅga gam pārśva dvaya adhare paścāt brahmasūtram dvitīyakam avadhānena saṃgrāhyam ācāryeṇa ūha vedinā bhavet paścāt mukhaḥ  mantrī tasmin  ca brahmasūtrake madhya śṛṅgam varjayitvā sarvaḥ pūrva uditaḥ  vidhiḥ tatas  yad unmukham khaṇḍa candra yugmam purā uditam tatas  dvayena kartavyā gaṇḍikā antar su saṃgatā dvayena agra ga sūtrābhyām madhya śṛṅga dvayam bhavet  adhas  bhāga vivṛddhyā asya padmam vṛtta catuṣṭayam tatas cakram ṣoḍaśa aram dvādaśa aram dvidhā atha tad  madhye kuleśvarī sthānam vyoma vā tilakam ca vā padmam vā atha ṣaṣ aram vā viyat dvādaśakam ca vā tri triśūle tra saptāre śliṣṭa mātreṇa madhyatas  padmānām atha cakrāṇām vyomnām vā saptakam bhavet  miśritam vā atha saṃkīrṇam samāsa vyāsa bhedataḥ tatas  kṣetra ardha mānena kṣetram tatra adhikam kṣipet  tatra daṇḍaḥ smṛtaḥ  bhāgaḥ ṣaṣ ara amalasārakaḥ su tīkṣṇa agraḥ su rakta ābhaḥ kṣaṇāt āveśa kārakaḥ yā sā kuṇḍalinī devī taraṅga ākhyā mahā ūrmiṇī sā ṣaṣ aśreṇa kanda ākhye sthitā ṣaṣ devatā ātmikā aṣṭa bhāgaiḥ ca vistīrṇaḥ  dīrghaḥ ca api tad ardhataḥ tatas  dvārāṇi kāryāṇi citra vartanayā kramāt  veda aśrāyata rūpāṇi yad ivā vṛtta mātrataḥ spaṣṭa śṛṅgam athaḥ kuryāt yad ivā vaiparītyataḥ unmukham candra yugmam vā bhaṅktvā kuryāt catuṣṭayam kuṭilaḥ  madhyatas  spaṣṭaḥ  dhomukhaḥ pārśva gaḥ sthitaḥ uttānaḥ  rdhaḥ samaḥ pūrṇaḥ śliṣṭaḥ  granthi gataḥ tathā candrasya ittham dvādaśadhā vartanā bhrama bhedinī antar bahirmukha tvena sā punar dvividhā matā tad bhedāt maṇḍalānām syāt asaṅkhyaḥ  bheda vistaraḥ pīṭha vīthī bahiarbhūmi kaṇṭha karṇa kapolataḥ śobhā upaśobhā saṃbhedāt guṇa rekhā vikalpataḥ svastika dvitaya ādi aṣṭa tayā paryanta bhedataḥ bhāva abhāva vikalpena maṇḍalānām ananta tā tatas  rajāṃsi deyāni yathā śobhā anusārataḥ sindūram rājavartam ca khaṭikā ca sitottamā uttamāni rajāṃsi iha devatā traya yogataḥ parā candra sama prakhyā raktā devī parāparā aparā sā parā kālī bhīṣaṇā caṇḍa yoginī dṛṣṭvā etad maṇḍalam devyaḥ sarvā nṛtyanti sarvadā anarcite pyadīkṣeṇa dṛṣṭe dīkṣyeta mātṛbhiḥ kiṃvā ati bahunā uktena tri triśūla āra saptakāḥ śūla yāgāḥ ṣaḍ  sahasrāṇi evam sa ardha śata dvayam yā sā devī parā śaktiḥ prāṇa vāhā vyavasthitā viśvāntar  kuṇḍala ākārā sā sākṣāt atra vartitā tattvāni tattvadevyaḥ ca viśvam asmin pratiṣṭhitam atra ūrdhve tantu mātreṇa tisraḥ śūla āragāḥ sthitāḥ āsana tvena ca icchā ādyā bhoga mokṣa prasādhikāḥ tāḥ tu mokṣa eka kāmasya śūlārāviddha madhyakāḥ tasmāt enam mahā yāgam mahā vibhava vistaraiḥ pūjayet bhūti kāmaḥ  vā mokṣa kāmaḥ  pivā budhaḥ asya darśana mātreṇa bhūta vetāla guhyakāḥ palāyante daśa diśaḥ śivaḥ sākṣāt prasīdati manda śakti bala āviddhaḥ  pyetat maṇḍala pūjanāt  satatam māsa ṣaṭkena trika jñānam samaśnute yad prāpya heya upādeyam svayam eva vicārya saḥ dehānte syāt bhairava ātmā siddhi kāmaḥ  tha siddhyati maṇḍalasya asya yaḥ  vyāptim devatā nyāsam eva ca vartanām ca vijānāti sa guruḥ trikaśāsane tasya pāda rajaḥ  mūrdhni dhāryam śiva samīhinā atra sṛṣṭi sthiti dhvaṃsān kramāt  trīn api pūjayet  turyam tu madhyataḥ  yad vā sarveṣu paripūrakam catur triśūlam vā gupta daṇḍam yāgam samācaret  tatra tad  pūjayet samyak  sphuṭam krama catuṣṭayam iti etad kathitam gupte ṣaṣ ardha hṛdaye pare ṣaṭke proktam sūcitam śrī siddhayogīśvarīmate agratas  sūtrayitvā tu maṇḍalam sarva kāma dam mahā śūla samopetam padma cakra ādi bhūṣitam dvāre dvāre likhet śūlam varjayitvā tu paścimam koṇeṣu apica vā kāryam mahā śūlam druma anvitam amṛta ambhaḥ bha vārīṇām śūla agre tu trikam trikam śūla ittham prakartavyam aṣṭadhā tad  tridhā apivā evam saṃsūcitam divyam khecarīṇām puram tu iti sthāna antare pi kathitam śrī siddhātantra śāsane kajam madhye tad ardhena śūla śṛṅgāṇi tāni tu śūla aṅkam maṇḍalam kalpyam kamala aṅkam ca pūraṇe atha śūla abja vinyāsaḥ śrī pūrve triśiromate siddhātantre trika kule devyāya amala mālayoḥ yathā uktaḥ sāraśāstre ca tantra sadbhāva guhyayoḥ tathā pradarśyate spaṣṭam yadi api ukta kramāt gataḥ veda āśrite tri haste prāk  pūrvam ardha vibhājayet  hasta ardham sarvatas tyaktvā pūrva udagyāmi diggatam tri aṅgulaiḥ koṣṭhakaiḥ ūrdhvaiḥ tiryak  ca aṣṭa dvidhā ātmakaiḥ dvau dvau bhāgau parityajya punar dakṣiṇa saumya gau brahmaṇaḥ pārśvayoḥ jīvāt caturthāt  pūrvatas tathā bhāga ardha bhāga mānam tu khaṇḍa candra dvayam dvayam tayoḥ antar tṛtīye tu dakṣiṇa uttara pārśvayoḥ jīve khaṇḍa indu yugalam kuryāt antar bhramāt budhaḥ tayoḥ apara marma stham khaṇḍa indu dvaya koṭi gam bahirmukham bhramam kuryāt  khaṇḍa candra dvayam dvayam tadvat brahmaṇi kurvīta bhāga bhāga ardha saṃmitam tatas  dvitīya bhāga ante brahmaṇaḥ pārśvayoḥ dvayoḥ dve rekhe pūrva ge neye bhāga tri aṃśa śame budhaiḥ eka ardhendu ūrdhva koṭi stham brahmasūtra agra saṅgatam sūtra dvayam prakurvīta madhya śṛṅga prasiddhaye tad agra pārśvayoḥ jīvāt  sūtram ekāntare dhṛtam ādi dvitīya khaṇḍa indu koṇāt  koṇa antam ānayet  tayoḥ eva aparāt jīvāt  prathama ardha indu koṇataḥ tadvat eva nayet sūtram śṛṅga dvitaya siddhaye kṣetra ardhe ca apare daṇḍaḥ  dvi karaḥ channa pañcakaḥ ṣaṣ vistṛtam catur dīrgham tad adhas  malasārakam veda aṅgulam ca tad adhas  mūlam tīkṣṇa agram iṣyate ādi kṣetrasya kurvīta dikṣu dvāra catuṣṭayam hasta āyāmam tad ardham vā vistārāt api tad samam dviguṇam bāhyatas  kuryāt tatas  padmam yathā śṛṇu ekaika bhāga mānāni kuryāt vṛttāni vedavat  dikṣu aṣṭau punar api aṣṭau jīva sūtrāṇi ṣoḍaśa dvayoḥ dvayoḥ punar madhye tad saṃkhyātāni pātayet  eṣām tṛtīya vṛtta stham pārśva jīva samam bhramam etad antam prakurvīta tatas  jīvāgram ānayet  yatra eva kutracid saṅgaḥ tad saṃbandhe sthirīkṛte tatra kṛtvā nayet mantrī patra agrāṇām prasiddhaye ekaikasmin dale kuryāt kesarāṇām trayam trayam dviguṇa aṣṭa aṅgulam kāryam tadvat śṛṅgaka ja trayam karṇikā pīta varṇena mūla madhya agra bhedataḥ sitam raktam tathā pītam kāryam kesara jālakam dalāni śukla varṇāni prativāraṇayā saha pīṭham tadvat catuṣkoṇam karṇikā ardha samam bahis  sita rakta pīta kṛṣṇaiḥ tad pādān vahnitaḥ kramāt  caturbhiḥ api śṛṅgāṇi tribhiḥ maṇḍalam iṣyate daṇḍaḥ syāt nīla raktena pītam āmala sārakam raktam śūlam prakurvīta yad tad pūrvam prakalpitam paścāt dvārasya pūrveṇa tyaktvā aṅgula catuṣṭayam dvāram veda aśri vṛttam vā saṃkīrṇam vā vicitritam eka dvi tripuram tulyam sāmudgam athavā ubhayam kapola kaṇṭha śobha upaśobhā ādi bahu citritam vicitra ākāra saṃsthānam vallī sūkṣma gṛha anvitam śrī devyāyāmale tu uktam kṣetre veda āśrite sati ardham dvādaśadhā kṛtvā tiryak ūrdhvam ca tiryajam bhāgam ekam sva pārśva ūrdhvam guruḥ samavatārayet  madhyastham tam tri bhāgam ca tad ante bhramayet ubhau bhāgam ekam parityajya tad madhye bhramayet punar  tṛtīya aṃśa ūrdhvatas  bhrāmyam ūrdhva aṃśam yāvat antatas  caturtha aṃśāt tad ūrdhvam tu ūrdhva adhas  yojayet punar  tad mānāt ūrdhvam ābhrāmya caturthena niyojayet  ūrdhvāt yojayate sūtram brahmasūtra avadhi kramāt  kramāt vaipulyataḥ kṛtvā aṃśam vai hrāsayet  punar  ardha bhāga pramāṇaḥ tu daṇḍaḥ  dviguṇa  iṣyate bhāgam bhāgam gṛhītvā tu ubhayoḥ atha gocarāt  bhrāmyam pippalavat  patram vartanā eṣā tu adhas  bhavet  ṣoḍaśa aṃśe likhet padmam dvādaśa aṅgula lopanāt tad ūrdhvam madhya bhāge tu vāri janma samālikhet  madhya śṛṅga avasāne tu tṛtīyam vilikhet tatas  sa vyāsavye tathā eva iha kaṭi stha abje samālikhet  karṇikā pītalā rakta pīta śuklam ca kesaram dalāni padma bāhya sthā śuklā ca prativāraṇī śūlam kṛṣṇena rajasā brahmarekhā sitā punar  śūla agram jvālayā yuktam śūla daṇḍaḥ tu pītalaḥ śūla madhye ca yad padmam tatra īśam pūjayet sadā asya ūrdhve tu parām dakṣe nyām vāme ca aparām budhaḥ yā sā kāla antakā devī parātītā vyavasthitā grasate śūla cakram sā tu icchā mātreṇa sarvadā śānti rūpā kalā hi eṣā vidyā rūpā parā bhavet  aparā tu pratiṣṭhā syāt nivṛttiḥ tu parāparā bhairavam daṇḍa ūrdhva stham rūpam sādāśiva ātmakam catasraḥ śaktayaḥ tu asya sthūlāḥ sūkṣmāḥ tu anekadhā eṣa yāgaḥ samākhyātaḥ  ḍāmara ākhyaḥ tri śaktikaḥ atha traiśirase śūla abja vidhiḥ dṛṣṭaḥ  bhilikhyate vāma amṛta ādibhiḥ mukhyaiḥ pavitraiḥ su manoramaiḥ bhūmim rajāṃsi karaṇīm khaṭikām mūlataḥ  rcayet  caturaśre catur haste madhye śūlam karatrayam caṇḍaḥ dvi hasta ūrdhva adhas pīṭha yuj vipulaḥ tu asau vasu aṅgulaḥ prakartavyaḥ sūtra traya samanvitaḥ dvādaśa aṅgula mānena daṇḍa mūle tu pīṭhikā dairghyāt tu ucchrāyāt ca ūrdhve ca catur aṅgula mānataḥ ūrdhve pyucchrāyataḥ  vedāṅgulā dairghyāt daśa aṅgulā śūla mūla gatam pīṭhī madhyam kha abdhi sama aṅgulam kṛtvā daṇḍam triśūlam tu tribhiḥ bhāgaiḥ samantatas aṣṭa aṅgula pramāṇaiḥ syāt hasta mātram samantatas śūla agram śūla madhyam tad śūla mūlam tu tad bhavet vedī madhye prakartavyā ubhayoḥ ca ṣaṣ aṅgulam dvādaśa aṅgula dīrghā tu ubhayoḥ pārśvayoḥ tathā catur aṅgulam ucchrāyāt mūle vedīm prakalpayet  ubhayoḥ pārśvayoḥ ca evam ardha candra ākṛtim tathā bhrāmayet  khaṭikā sūtram kaṭim kuryāt dvis aṅgulām vaipulyāt dairghyataḥ  devi catur aṅgula mānataḥ yādṛśam dakṣiṇe bhāge vāme tadvat prakalpayet madhye śūla agra vaipulyāt aṅgulaḥ ca adhordhvataḥ catur aṅgula mānena vaipulyāt tu ṣaṣ aṅgulā ucchrāyāt tu tatas  kāryā gaṇḍikā tu svarūpataḥ pīṭha ūrdhve tu prakartavyam śūla mūlam tu suvrate śūla agram aṅgulam kāryam su tīkṣṇam tu ṣaṣ aṅgulam arā madhyam prakartavyam arādhaḥ tu ṣaṣ aṅgulam catur aṅgula nimnam tu madhyam tu parikalpayet  pūrva aparam tad eva iha madhye śūlam tu tad bahis  kārayeta tribhiḥ sūtraiḥ ekaikam vartayeta ca kaja trayam tu śūla agram veda aṃśaiḥ dvādaśa aṅgulam kramāt dakṣāni amadhyeṣu tri aṣṭa dvādaśa patrakam cakra trayam vāta puram padmam aṣṭa aṅgulārakam vidyā abhikhyam śūla mūle rajaḥ paścāt prapātayet  triśūlam daṇḍa paryantam rāja vartena pūrayet  sūtra trayasya pṛṣṭhe tu śuklam cārā trayam bhavet  śuklena rajasā śūla mūle vidyā ambujam bhavet  raktam rakta asitam śuklam kramāt ūrdhva ambuja trayam śuklena vyomarekhā syāt  sā sthaulyāt aṅgulam bahis  tām tyaktvā vedikā kāryā hasta mātram pramāṇātaḥ vaipulya triguṇam dairghyāt  prākāram caturaśrakam samantatas  tha dikṣu syuḥ dvārāṇi kara mātrataḥ tridhā vibhajya kramaśas  dvādaśa aṅgula mānataḥ kaṇṭham kapolam śobhām tu upaśobhām tad antatas  prākāram caturaśram tu sa bhūrekhā samanvitam sita rakta pīta kṛṣṇai rajobhiḥ kārayet tatas  raktai rajobhiḥ madhyam tu yathā śobham tu pūrayet  asyāḥ  vyāptau purā ca uktam tatra eva anusaret ca tad  arātraya vibhāgaḥ tu praveśaḥ  nirgamaḥ  bhramaḥ anāhata pada vyāptiḥ kuṇḍalyā udayaḥ paraḥ hṛdi sthāne gatā devyaḥ triśūlasya sumadhyame nābhi sthaḥ śūla daṇḍaḥ tu śūla mūlam hṛdi sthitam śakti sthāna gatam prāntam prānte cakra trayam smaret  utkṣipya utkṣipya kalayā deha madhya svarūpataḥ śūla daṇḍa anta madhya stha śūla madhya anta gocaram praviśet mūla madhya antam prānta ante śakti veśmani aspanda karaṇam kṛtvā ekadā spanda vartanam mūlam ānandam āpīḍya śakti traya padam viśet  tatra pūjyam prayatnena jāyante sarva siddhayaḥ samasta adhva samāyogāt ṣoḍhā adhva vyāpti bhāvataḥ samasta mantra cakra ādyaiḥ evam ādi prayatnataḥ ṣaṭtriṃśat tattva racitam triśūlam paribhāvayet  viṣuvat sthena vinyāsaḥ  mantrāṇām maṇḍala uttame kāryaḥ  smin pūjite yatra sarva īśvara padam bhajet  svastikena atha kartavyam yuktam tasya ucyate vidhiḥ nāḍikāḥ sthāpayet pūrvam muhūrtam parimāṇataḥ śakra vāruṇa diś sthāḥ ca yāmya saumya gatāḥ tathā ekonatriṃśat vaṃśāḥ syuḥ ṛjutiryak gatāḥ tathā aṣṭau marma śatāni ekacatvāriṃśat ca jāyate vaṃśaiḥ viṣaya saṃkhyaiḥ ca padmam yugma indu maṇḍalam rasa saṃkhyaiḥ bhavet pīṭham svastikam sarva kāma dam vasu saṃkhyaiḥ dvāra vīthau  evam bhāga parikramaḥ randhra vipra śara agnīn  ca lupyet bāhya antaram kramāt  marmāṇi ca catur dikṣu madhyāt dvāreṣu sundari vahni bhūta muni vyoma bāhya garbhe purīṣu ca lopayet ca eva marmāṇi antar nāḍi vivarjitān dvāra prākāra koṇeṣu netra anala śarān ṛtūn nāḍayaḥ  brahma vaṃśasya lopyā netrāt rasa sthitāḥ vahneḥ netra analau lopyau vedān netra yugam rasāt  netram saumya gatam lopyam pūrvā t veda analau rasāt  loka sthā nāḍikā hitvā netrādveda agnayaḥ kramāt  śaraiḥ vahni gatam ca eva yugam netra agnayaḥ  rasāt  netrāt  pūrva gatāt ca eva sumeruḥ dvāra saṃjñitaḥ svastikā ca purī ramyā catur dikṣu sthitau  ubhau marmaṇām ca śate dve ca ṛṣibhiḥ guṇitā diśaḥ netra ādikān  ca saṃmārjya mārga madhyāt  su śobhane ṛṣi traya kṛte madhye viṣayaiḥ karṇikā bhavet  netrīkṛtān vasūn patram netram sakṛt vibhājitam vahnim vasu gatam kṛtvā śaśāṅka sthān  ca lopayet  vahni iṣu ṛṣi madhyāt ca lopyam pīṭha induka avadhi brahmaṇaḥ  netra viṣayāt netrādveda analau haret  sāgare netrakam lopyam nāḍayaḥ pūrva diggatāḥ bhūta netra gatān mūrdhnā netrāt dvi vahni dṛś trikāt  saumya gāt  pīṭha koṇeṣu lopayeta caturṣu api dalāni kāryāṇi sitaiḥ kesaram rakta pītalaiḥ karṇikā kanaka prakhyā pallava antāḥ ca lohitāḥ vyomarekhā tu susitā vartula abja anta nīlabhāḥ pīṭham rekhā traya upetam sita lohita pītalam svastikāḥ ca catur varṇā agneḥ īśāna gocarāḥ vīthī vidruma saṃkāśā sva dikṣu astrāṇi bāhyatas  indranīla nibham vajram śaktim padma maṇi prabhām daṇḍam hāṭaka saṃkāśam vaktram tasya ati lohitam nīla dyuti samam khaḍgam pāśam vatsaka saprabham dhvajam puṣpa phala upetam pañca raṅgaiḥ ca śobhitam gadā hema nibha ati ugrā nānā ratna vibhūṣitā śūlam nīla ambuja samam jvalat vahni ugra śekharam tasya upari sitam padmam īṣat pīta aruṇa prabham cakram hema nibham dīptamarā vaiḍūrya saṃnibhāḥ arā madhyam su pītam ca bāhyam jvāla aruṇam bhavet  mandiram devadevasya sarva kāma phala pradam śrī siddhāyām śūla vidhiḥ prāk  kṣetre caturaśrite hasta mātram tridhā sūryāt nava khaṇḍam yathā bhavet  madhye śūlam ca tatra ittham madhya bhāgam tridhā bhajet  navabhiḥ koṣṭhakaiḥ yuktam tatas  yam vidhiḥ ucyate madhya bhāga trayam tyaktvā madhye bhāga dvayasya tu adhastāt bhrāmayet sūtram śaśāṅka śakala ākṛti ubhayatas  bhrāmayet tatra yathā agre ha ākṛtiḥ bhavet  koṭyām tatra kṛtam sūtram nayet rekhām tu pūrvikām apara dvāra pūrveṇa tyaktvā aṅgula catuṣṭayam rekhām vināśayet prājñaḥ  yathā śūla ākṛtiḥ bhavet  śūla agre tu ardha hastena tyaktvā padmāni kārayet  adhas  śṛṅga trayam hasta madhye padmam sa karṇikam mukha agre dhārayet sūtram tribhiḥ hastaiḥ tu pātayet  madhye ca ūrdhvam tatas  kuryāt adhastāt aṅgula dvayam rekhā dvayam pātayeta yathā śūlam bhavati api adhobhāga ādibhiḥ ca ūrdhvam tatra rekhā prapadyate samīkṛtya tatas  sūtre ūrdhve dve evam eva tu madhyam padmam pratiṣṭhāpyam śūla adhastāt yaśasvini iti eṣa maṇḍala vidhiḥ kathitaḥ saṃkṣepa yogataḥ  mahā gurubhiḥ  ch atha śrī tantrāloke dvātriṃśam āhnikam atha kathaye mudrāṇām guru āgama gītam atra vidhim b mudrā ca pratibimba ātmā śrīmat devī ākhya yāmale c uktā bimba udaya śrutyā vācya dvaya vivecanāt  bimbāt samudayaḥ yasyāḥ  iti uktā pratibimba tā vimbasya yasyāḥ  udaya iti uktā tad upāya tā mudam svarūpa lābha ākhyam deha dvāreṇa ca ātmanām rāti arpayati yad tena mudrā śāstreṣu varṇitā tatra pradhāna bhūtā śrīkhecarī devatā ātmikā niṣkala tvena vikhyātā sākalyena triśūlinī karaṅkiṇī krodhanā ca bhairavī lelihānikā mahā pretā yogamudrā jvālinī kṣobhiṇī dhruvā iti evaṃbahu bheda iyam śrīkhecarī eva gīyate anyāḥ tad aṅga bhūtāḥ tu padma ādyā mālinīmate tāsām bahutva amukhyatva yogābhyām na iha varṇanam śrī khecarī samāviṣṭaḥ  yad yad sthānam samāśrayet  devī saṃnidhaye tad syāt alam kim ḍambaraiḥ vṛthā kāmye karmaṇi tāḥ ca syuḥ mukhyāḥ kasya api jātucit  mudrā caturvidhā kāya kara vāc citta bhedataḥ tatra pūrṇena rūpeṇa khecarīm eva varṇaye baddhvā padmāsanam yogī nābhā   akṣa īśvaram kṣipet  daṇḍa ākāram tu tam tau  at nayet yāvat kakhatrayam nigṛhya tatra tad tūrṇam prerayet  kha trayeṇa tu etām baddhvā khe gatiḥ syāt iti śrī pūrvaśāsane dhvanijyotiḥ marut yuktam cittam viśramya ca upari anena abhyāsa yogena śivam bhittvā param vrajet  jatru adhastāt karau kṛtvā vāma pādam ca dakṣiṇe vidāryāsyam kaniṣṭhābhyām madhyamābhyām tu nāsikām anāme kuñcayet prājñaḥ  bhrū bhaṅgam tarjanī dvayam jihvām ca cālayet mantrī hāhākāram ca kārayet  triśūlena prayogeṇa brahmarandhram upasthitaḥ padam santyajya tanmātram sadyas tyajati medinīm śūnya aśūnyalaye kṛtvā eka daṇḍe nila analau śakti tritaya sambaddhe adhiṣṭhātṛ tri daivate triśūlam tad vijānīya āt yena vyoma utpatet budhaḥ ākāśa bhāvam santyajya sattā mātram upasthitaḥ śūlam samarasam kṛtvā rase rasa iva sthitaḥ eka daṇḍam sa vijñāya triśūlam kha caram priye baddhvā tu khecarīm mudrām dhyātvā ātmānam ca bhairavam khecarī cakra saṃjuṣṭam sadyas tyajati medinīm tyakta aṃśakaḥ  nirācāraḥ  niḥśaṅkaḥ  loka varjitaḥ avadhūtaḥ  nirācāraḥ  na aham asmi iti bhāvayam mantra eka niṣṭhaḥ saṃpaśyan deha sthāḥ sarva devatāḥ hlāda udvega asmitā kruṣṭa nidrā maithuna matsare rūpa ādau vā kartṛ karma karaṇeṣu ca sarvaśas  na aham asmi iti manvāna ekībhūtam vicintayan karṇa akṣi mukha nāsā ādi cakra stham devatā gaṇam grahītāram sadā paśyan khecaryā siddhyati sphuṭam vidyā śaṅkī mala āśaṅkī śāstra śaṅkī na siddhyati śivaḥ  raviḥ śivaḥ  vahniḥ paktṛ tvāt sa purohitaḥ tatrasthā devatāḥ sarvā dyotayantyaḥ  khilam jagat  kaniṣṭhayā vidāryāsyam tarjanībhyām bhruvau tathā anāme madhyame vaktre jihvayā tālukam spṛśet  eṣā karaṅkiṇī devī jvālinīm śṛṇu sāṃpratam hanuḥ lalāṭa gau hastau prasārya aṅgulitaḥ sphuṭau cālayet vāyu vegena kṛtvā antarbhrukuṭīm budhaḥ vidāryāsyam sa jihvam ca hāhākāram tu kārayet  eṣā jvālinī agni cakre tayā ca aṣṭa uttaram śatam japet yadi tatas  siddhyet trailokyam sacarācaram para deheṣu ca ātmānam param ca ātma śarīrataḥ paśyet carantam hānādāt gama āgama pada sthitam nava  chidra gatam ca ekam nadantam vyāpakam dhruvam anayā hi khacārī śrī yoga sañcāra ucyate kula kuṇḍalikām baddhvā aṇoḥ antara vedinīm vāmaḥ  yaḥ  yam jagati asmin  tasya saṃharaṇa udyatām sva sthāne nirvṛtim labdhvā jñāna amṛta rasa ātmakam vrajet kanda padam madhye rāvam kṛtvā hi arāvakam yāvat jīvam catuṣkoṇam piṇḍa ādhāram ca kāmikam tatra tām bodhayitvā tu gatim buddhvā krama āgatām cakra ubhaya nibaddhām tu śākhā prānta avalambinīm mūlasthānāt yathā devi tamaḥ granthim vidārayet  vajra ākhyām jñāna jena eva tathā śākhā ubhaya antatas koṇa madhya viniṣkrāntam liṅga mūlam vibhedayet  tatra saṅghaṭṭitam cakra yugmam aikyena bhāsate vaiparītyāt tu nikṣipya dvidhā bhāvam vrajati atas  ūru ādi aṅguṣṭha kālāgni paryante sā vinikṣipet  gamāgamana sañcāre caret sā liṅga liṅginī tatra tad pada saṃyogāt unmīlana vidhāyinī yaḥ  jānāti sa siddhyet tu rasa ādāna visargayoḥ sa saṅgamam idam sthānam ūrmiṇī unmīlanam param eṣa kramaḥ tatas  nyaḥ pi vyutkramaḥ khecarī parā yoni ādhāra iti vikhyātā śūla mūla iti śabdyate varṇāḥ tatra layam yānti hi avarṇe varṇa rūpiṇi na ādi phāntam samuccārya kauleśam deha saṃnibham ākramya prathamam cakram khe yantre pāda pīḍitam nādam vai śakti sat garbham sat garbhāt kaulinī padam bīja pañcaka cāreṇa śūlabheda krameṇa tu hṛd śūla granthi bhedaiḥ cit rudra śaktim prabodhayet  vāyu cakra anta nilayam bindu ākhyam nābhi maṇḍalam āgacchet lambikā sthānam sūtra dvādaśa nirgatam candra cakra vilomena praviśet bhūtapañjare bhūyas tu kurute līlām māyā pañjara vartinīm punar  sṛṣṭiḥ saṃhṛtiḥ ca khecaryā kriyate budhaiḥ śrīmat vīra āvalī yoga eṣa syāt khecarī vidhiḥ cumba ākāreṇa vaktreṇa yad tad tvam śrūyate param grasamānam idam viśvam candra arka puṭa saṃpuṭe tena eva syāt khagāmi iti śrīmat kāmika ucyate bhavān muktvā drāvayanti pāśān mudrā hi śaktayaḥ mukhya āsām khecarī sā ca tridhā uccāreṇa vācikī triśiromudgaraḥ  devi kāyikī paripaṭhyate nāsām netra dvayam ca api hṛd stana dvayam eva ca vṛṣaṇa dvaya liṅgam ca prāpya kāyam gatā tu iyam bhava sthāna abhava sthānam uccāreṇa avadhārayet  mānasīyam itastu anyāḥ padma ādyā aṣṭa mudrikāḥ mātṛ vyūha kule tāḥ syuḥ asyāḥ tu parivāra gāḥ śarīram tu samastam yad kūṭa akṣara samākṛti eṣā mudrā mahāmudrā bhairavasya iti gahvare su upaviṣṭaḥ padmake tu hasta agra aṅguli raśmibhiḥ parāṅmukhaiḥ jhaṭiti udyat raśmibhiḥ pṛṣṭha saṃsthitaiḥ antar sthitiḥ khecarī iyam saṃkoca ākhyā śaśāṅkinī tasmāt eva samuttambya bāhū ca eva avakuñcitau samyak vyomasu saṃsthānāt vyomā ākhyā khecarī matā muṣṭi dvitaya saṅghaṭṭāt hṛdi sā hṛdaya āhvāyāḥ  śānta ākhyā sā hasta yugmam ūrdhva adhas  sthitam udgatam sama dṛṣṭyā avalokyam ca bahis yojita pāṇikam eṣā eva śaktimudrā ced adhas dhāvita pāṇikā daśānām aṅgulīnām tu muṣṭi bandhāt anantaram drākkṣepāt khecarī devī pañcakuṇḍalinī matā saṃhāra mudrā ca eṣā eva yadi ūrdhvam kṣipyate kila utkrāmaṇī jhagiti eva paśūnām pāśa kartarī śvabhre sudūre jhaṭiti sva ātmānam pātayan  iva sāhasa anupraveśena kuñcitam hasta yugmakam adhas vīkṣaṇa śīlam ca samyak dṛṣṭi samanvitam vīrabhairava saṃjñā iyam khecarī bodha vardhinī aṣṭadhā ittham varṇitā śrī bhargā aṣṭaka śikhā ākule evam nānāvidhān bhedān āśritya ekā eva yā sthitā śrīkhecarī tayā āviṣṭaḥ param bījam prapadyate ekam sṛṣṭi mayam bījam yad vīryam sarva mantra gam ekā mudrā khecarī ca mudrā oghaḥ prāṇitaḥ  yayā tad evam khecarī cakra rūḍhau yad rūpam ullaset tad eva mudrā mantavyā śeṣaḥ syāt deha vikriyā yāga ādau tad madhye tad avasitau jñāna yoga parimarśe vighna praśame pāśa  chede mudrā vidheḥ samayaḥ bodha āveśaḥ sannidhiḥ aikyena visarjanam sva rūpa gatiḥ śaṅkā dalanam cakra udaya dīptiḥ iti kramāt kṛtyam iti mudrā vidhiḥ proktaḥ su gūḍhaḥ  yaḥ phala pradaḥ  ch atha śrī tantrāloke trayastriṃśam āhnikam atha avasara saṃprāpta ekīkāraḥ  nigadyate b yad uktam cakra bhedena sārdham pūjyam iti trikam c tatra eṣa cakra bhedānām ekīkāraḥ  diśā anayā viśvā tad īśā hāraudrī vīranetrī ambikā tathā gurvī iti ṣaṭ are devyaḥ śrī siddhāvīra darśitāḥ māheśī brāhmaṇī skāndī vaiṣṇavī aindrī yama ātmikā cāmuṇḍā ca eva yogi īśi iti aṣṭa aghoryādayaḥ  thavā agni nirṛti vāyu īśa mātṛbhiḥ dvādaśa anvitāḥ nandā bhadrā jayā kālī karālī vikṛta ānanā kroṣṭukī bhīma mudrā ca vāyu vegā haya ānanā gambhīrā ghoṣaṇī ca iti caturviṃśati are vidhiḥ siddhiḥ vṛddhiḥ dyutiḥ lakṣmīḥ medhā kāntiḥ sudhā dhṛtiḥ dīptiḥ puṣṭiḥ matiḥ kīrtiḥ susthitiḥ su gatiḥ smṛtiḥ suprabhā ṣoḍaśī ca iti śrīkaṇṭha ādika śaktayaḥ baliḥ ca balinandaḥ ca daśagrīvaḥ  haraḥ  hayaḥ mādhavaḥ ṣaṭ are cakre dvādaśa are tu amī smṛtāḥ dakṣaḥ caṇḍaḥ haraḥ śauṇḍī pramathaḥ  bhīma manmathau śakuniḥ sumatiḥ nandaḥ gopālaḥ ca pitāmahaḥ śrīkaṇṭhaḥ  nanta sūkṣmau ca trimūrtiḥ śaṃbareśvaraḥ arghīśaḥ  bhārabhūtiḥ ca sthitiḥ sthāṇuḥ haraḥ tathā jhaṇṭhi bhautika sadyoja anugraha krūra sainikāḥ dvi aṣṭau yad vā amṛtaḥ tena yuktāḥ pūrṇa ābha tad dravāḥ ogha ūrmi syandana aṅgāḥ ca vapuḥ udgāra vaktrakāḥ tanu secana mūrti īśāḥ sarva amṛta dharaḥ paraḥ śrī pāṭhāt śaktayaḥ ca etāḥ ṣoḍaśa eva prakīrtitāḥ saṃvartala kuli bhṛgusita baka khaṅgi pināki bhujaga bali kālāḥ dvis chaga lāṇḍau śikhi śoṇa meṣa mīna tridaṇḍi sa āṣāḍhi devī kānta tad ardhau dāruka hali soma nātha śarmāṇaḥ jaya vijaya jayanta ajita su jaya jaya rudra kīrtana āvahakāḥ tad mūrti utsāhadavardhanāḥ ca bala subalabhadradāvahakāḥ tad vāndātā ca īśaḥ nandana samabhadra tad mūrtiḥ śiva dasu manaḥ spṛhaṇakā durgaḥ  bhadra ākhya kālaḥ ca cetaḥ  nuga kauśika kāla viśvasu śivāḥ tathā aparaḥ kopaḥ śruti agni are syuḥ ete strī pāṭhāt śaktayaḥ tu etāḥ juṃkāraḥ  tha agnipatnī iti ṣaṭ are ṣaṇṭha varjitāḥ dvādaśa are tad sahitāḥ ṣoḍaśa are svarāḥ kramāt  halaḥ tad dviguṇe ṣṭāre yādyam hāntam tu tad trike dvātriṃśat arake sa antam binduḥ sarveṣu mūrdhani evam anyān bahūn  cakra bhedān asmāt prakalpayet eka eva cit ātmā eṣa viśva āmarśana sārakaḥ śaktiḥ tad vānataḥ  mātā śabdarāśiḥ prakīrtitau tayoḥ eva vibhāge tu śakti tadvat prakalpane śabdarāśiḥ mālinī ca kṣobha ātma vapuḥ īdṛśam tathā antar stha parāmarśa bhedane vastutas trikam anuttara icchā unmeṣa ākhyam yatas  viśvam vimarśanam ānandeśa ūrmi yoge tu tad ṣaṭkam samudāhṛtam antar stha ūṣma samāyogāt tad aṣṭakam udāhṛtam tadā amṛta catuṣka ūna bhāve dvādaśakam bhavet  tad yoge ṣoḍaśa ākhyam syāt evam yāvat asaṃkhya tā viśvam eka parāmarśa saha tvāt prabhṛti sphuṭam aṃśa aṃśikā parāmarśān paryante sahate yatas  atas  pañcāśat aikātmyam svara vyakti virūpa tā varga aṣṭakam varṇa bheda ekāśīti kalā udayaḥ iti pradarśitam pūrvam ardha mātrā sahatvataḥ svara ardham api asti yatas  svaritasya ardha mātrakam tasya āt ita udāttam tad kathitam pada vedinā ittham saṃvid iyam yājya svarūpa āmarśa rūpiṇī abhinnam saṃvidaḥ ca etad cakrāṇām cakravālakam svāmi āvaraṇa bhedena bahudhā tad prayojayet parāparā parā ca anyā sṛṣṭi sthiti tirodhayaḥ mātṛsadbhāva rūpā tu turyā viśrāntiḥ ucyate tad ca prakāśam vaktra stham sūcitam tu pade pade turye viśrāntiḥ ādheyā mātṛ sadbhāva sāriṇi tathā asya viśvam ābhāti sva ātma tad maya tām gatam iti eṣa śāstra arthasya ukta ekīkāraḥ  guru uditaḥ  ch atha śrī tantrāloke catustriṃśam āhnikam ucyate tha sva svarūpa praveśaḥ krama saṅgataḥ b yad etad bahudhā proktam āṇavam śiva tā āptaye c tatra antar antara āviśya viśrāmyet savidhe pade tatas  pyāṇava saṃtyāgāt śāktīm bhūmim upāśrayet  tatas  pi śāmbhavīm evam tāratamya kramāt sphuṭam ittham krama udita vibodha mahā marīci saṃpūrita prasara bhairava bhāva bhāgī ante bhyupāya nirapekṣa tayā eva nityam sva ātmānam āviśati garbhita viśva rūpam kathitaḥ  yam sva svarūpa praveśaḥ parameṣṭhinā  ch atha śrī tantrāloke pañcatriṃśam āhnikam atha ucyate samastānām śāstrāṇām iha melanam iha tāvat sama staḥ  yam vyavahāraḥ purātanaḥ prasiddhim anusandhāya sā eva ca āgama ucyate anvaya vyatirekau hi prasiddheḥ upajīvakau su āyatta tve tayoḥ vyakti pūge kim syāt tayoḥ gatiḥ pratyakṣam api netra ātma dīpa artha ādi viśeṣa jam apekṣate tatra mūle prasiddhim tām tathā ātmikām abhitas saṃvṛte jāta ekākī kṣudhitaḥ śiśuḥ kim karotu kim ādattām kena paśyatu kim vrajet  nanu vastu śata ākīrṇe sthāne pyasya yad eva hi paśyataḥ  jighrataḥ  vā api spṛśataḥ saṃprasīdati cetaḥ tad eva ādāya drāk  saḥ  nu aya vyatireka bhāj  hanta cetaḥ prasādaḥ  pi yaḥ  sāvartha viśeṣa gaḥ saḥ  pi prāk vāsanā rūpa vimarśa parikalpitaḥ na pratyakṣa anumāna ādi bāhyamāna prasāda jaḥ prāk vāsana upajīvyetat pratibhā mātram eva na na mṛd abhyavahāra icchā puṃsaḥ bālasya jāyate prāk vāsana upajīvī ced vimarśaḥ sā ca vāsanā prācyā ced āgatā sā iyam prasiddhiḥ paurvakālikī na ca cetaḥ prasattyā eva sarvaḥ  vyavahṛti kramaḥ mūlam prasiddhiḥ tad mānam sarvatra eva iti gṛhyatām pūrva pūrva upajīvitva mārgaṇe sā kvacid svayam sarvajña rūpe hi ekasmin niḥśaṅkam bhāsata purā vyavahāraḥ  hi na ekatra samastaḥ kaḥ  pi mātari tena asarvajña pūrvatva mātreṇa eṣā na siddhyati bahu sarvajña pūrva tve na mānam ca asti kiṃcana bhoga apavarga tad hetu prasiddhi śata śobhitaḥ tad vimarśa svabhāvaḥ  sau bhairavaḥ parameśvaraḥ tatas ca aṃśa aṃśikā yogāt sā prasiddhiḥ paramparām śāstram vā āśritya vitatā lokān saṃvyavahārayet  tayā eva āśaiśavāt sarve vyavahāra dharā juṣaḥ santaḥ samupajīvanti śaivam eva ādyam āgamam apūrṇā aḥ tu pare tena na mokṣa phala bhāginaḥ upajīvanti yāvat tu tāvat tad phala bhāginaḥ bālya apāye pi yad bhoktum annam eṣa pravartate tad prasiddhyā eva na adhyakṣāt na anumānāt asambhavāt na ca kā api atra doṣa āśā śaṅkāyāḥ ca nivṛttitaḥ prasiddhiḥ ca avigāna utthā pratītiḥ śabdana ātmikā mātuḥ svabhāvaḥ  yad tasyām śaṅkate na eṣa jātucit  sva kṛtatva vaśāt eva sarva vid sa hi śaṅkaraḥ yāvat tu śiva tā na asya tāvat sva ātma anusāriṇīm tāvatīm eva tām eṣa prasiddhim na abhiśaṅkate anyasyām abhiśaṅkī syāt bhūyas tām bahu manyate evam bhāvi śiva tvaḥ  mūm prasiddhim manyate dhruvam eka eva āgamaḥ ca ayam vibhunā sarva darśinā darśitaḥ  yaḥ pravṛtte ca nivṛtte ca pathi sthitaḥ dharma artha kāma mokṣeṣu pūrṇa āpūrṇa ādi bhedataḥ vicitreṣu phaleṣu eka upāyaḥ śāmbhava āgamaḥ tasmin viṣaya vaiviktyāt vicitra phala dāyini citra upāya upadeśaḥ  pi na virodhāvahaḥ bhavet  laukikam vaidikam sāṅkhyam yoga ādi pāñcarātrakam bauddha arhata nyāya śāstram padārtha krama tantraṇam siddhānta tantra śākta ādi sarvam brahma udbhavam yatas  śrī svacchanda ādiṣu proktam sadyojāta ādi bhedataḥ yathā ekatra api veda ādau tad tad āśrama gāminaḥ saṃskāra antaram atra api tathā liṅga uddhṛta ādikam yathā ca tatra pūrvasmin  āśrame na uttara āśramāt phalam eti tathā pāñcarātra ādau na śiva ātma tām eka eva āgamaḥ tasmāt tatra laukika śāstrataḥ prabhṛti āvaiṣṇavāt bauddhāt śaivāt sarvam hi niṣṭhitam tasya yad tad param prāpyam dhāma tad  trika śabditam sarva avibheda anucchedāt  tad eva kulam ucyate yathā ūrdhva adhara tā bhāj su deha aṅgeṣu vibhediṣu ekam prāṇitam evam syāt  trikam sarveṣu śāstrataḥ śrīmat kālī kule ca uktam pañca srotaḥ vivarjitam daśa aṣṭādaśa bhedasya sāram etad prakīrtitam puṣpe gandhaḥ tile tailam dehe jīvaḥ  jale mṛtam yathā tathā eva śāstrāṇām kulam antar  pratiṣṭhitam tad eka eva āgamaḥ  yam citraḥ citre dhikāriṇi tathā eva sā prasiddhiḥ hi sva yūthya para yūthya gā sāṃkhyam yogam pāñcarātram vedān  ca eva na nindayet  yatas  śiva udbhavāḥ sarva iti svacchandaśāsane ekasmāt āgamāt ca ete khaṇḍakhaṇḍā vyapa uddhṛtāḥ loke syuḥ āgamāḥ taiḥ ca janaḥ bhrāmyati mohitaḥ aneka āgama pakṣe pi vācyā viṣaya bheditā avaśyam ūrdhva adharatā sthityā prāmāṇya siddhaye anyathā na eva kasya api prāmāṇyam siddhyati dhruvam nitya tvam avisaṃvāda iti naḥ māna kāraṇam asmin  aṃśe pyamuṣya eva prāmāṇyam syāt tathā uditeḥ anyathā vyākṛtau kḷptau  asatya tve prarocane atiprasaṅga sarvasya api āgamasya apabādhakaḥ avaśya upetya iti asmin māna āgama nāmani avaśya upetyam eva etad śāstra niṣṭhāni rūpaṇam pradhāne ṅge kṛtaḥ  yatnaḥ phalavān vastutaḥ yatas  atas  smin yatnavān kaḥ  pi bhavet śaṃbhu pracoditaḥ tatra tatra ca śāstreṣu nyarūpyata maheśinā etāvatī adhikārī yaḥ sa durlabha iti sphuṭam ittham śrī śambhunāthena mama uktam śāstra melanam  ch atha śrī tantrāloke ṣaṭtriṃśam āhnikam āyātiḥ atha śāstrasya kathyate vasara āgatā b śrī siddha ādi vinirdiṣṭā gurubhiḥ ca nirūpitā c bhairavaḥ  bhairavī devī svacchandaḥ  lākulaḥ  ṇurāj  gahana īśaḥ  bjajaḥ śakraḥ  guruḥ koṭī apakarṣataḥ navabhiḥ kramaśas  dhītam nava koṭi pravistaram etaiḥ tatas  guruḥ koṭi mātrāt pādam vitīrṇavān dakṣa ādibhya ubhau pādau saṃvarta ādibhya eva ca pādam ca vāmana ādibhyaḥ pāda ardham bhārgavāya ca pāda pādam tu balaye pāda pāt aḥ tu yaḥ  paraḥ siṃhāya ardham tatas  śiṣṭāt dvau bhāgau vinatā abhuve pādam vāsuki nāgāya khaṇḍāḥ saptadaśa tu amī svargāt ardham rāvaṇaḥ  tha jahre rāmaḥ  rdham api atas  vibhīṣaṇa mukhāt āpa guru śiṣya vidhi kramāt  khaṇḍaiḥ ekāt na viṃśatyā vibhaktam tad abhūt tatas  khaṇḍam khaṇḍam ca aṣṭa khaṇḍam prokta pāda ādi bhedataḥ pādaḥ  mūla uddhārau  uttara vṛhat uttare tathā kalpaḥ sāṃhita kalpa skandau  anuttaram vyāpakam tridhā tisraḥ devyaḥ  tra nirūpyante kramaśas  vistāriṇā eva rūpeṇa navame pade tu gaṇanā na kācid uktā vyavacchidāhīne rāmāt ca lakṣmaṇaḥ tasmāt  siddhāḥ tebhyaḥ  pi dānavāḥ guhyakāḥ ca tatas tebhyaḥ  yoginaḥ  nṛvarāḥ tatas  teṣām krameṇa tad madhye bhraṣṭam kāla antarāt yadā tadā śrīkaṇṭhanātha ājñā vaśāt siddhā avātaram tryambakāmardaka abhikhya śrīnāthā advaye dvaye dvaya advaye ca nipuṇāḥ krameṇa śiva śāsane ādyasya ca anvayaḥ  jajñe dvitīyaḥ  duhitṛ kramāt  sa ca ardha tryambaka abhikhyaḥ saṃtānaḥ su pratiṣṭhitaḥ atas ca ardha cata sraḥ  tra maṭhikāḥ saṃtati kramāt  śiṣya praśiṣyaiḥ vistīrṇāḥ śata śākham vyavasthitaiḥ adhyuṣṭa saṃtati srotaḥ sāra bhūta rasa āhṛtim vidhāya tantrālokaḥ  yam syandate sakalān rasān uktāyātiḥ upādeya bhāvaḥ  nirṇīyate dhunā  ch atha śrī tantrāloke saptatriṃśam āhnikam ukta nītyā eva sarvatra vyavahāre pravartite prasiddhau  upajīvyāyām avaśya grāhya āgamaḥ yathā laukika dṛṣṭyā anya phala bhāj  tad prasiddhitaḥ samyak vyavaharan  tadvat śiva bhāj  tad prasiddhitaḥ tad avaśya grahītavye śāstre sva aṃśa upadeśini manāk phale bhyupādeyatamam tad viparītakam yathā khageśvarī bhāva niḥśaṅka tvāt viṣam vrajet  kṣayam karma sthitiḥ tadvat aśaṅkāt bhairava tvataḥ yadā ārṣe pāta hetu uktam tad asmin vāma śāsane āśu siddhyai yatas  sarvam ārṣam māyā udara sthitam tad ca yad sarva sarvajña dṛṣṭam tad ca api kim bhavet  yad aśeṣa upadeśena sūyate nuttaram phalam yathā adhara adhara prokta vastu tattva anuvādataḥ uttaram kathitam saṃvid siddham tad hi tathā bhavet  yad ukta adhika saṃvitti siddha vastu nirūpaṇāt apūrṇa sarva vid proktiḥ jñāyate dhara śāsane ūrdhva śāsana vastu aṃśe dṛṣṭvā apica samujjhite adhas  śāstreṣu māyā tvam lakṣyate sarga rakṣaṇāt  śrīmat ānanda śāstra ādau proktam ca parameśinā ṛṣi vākyam bahu kleśa madhruva alpa phalam mitam na eva pramāṇayet vidvān śaivam eva āgamam śrayet  tad ā ārṣe pāta hetu uktam tad asmin vāma śāsane āśu siddhyai yatas  sarvam ārṣam māyā udara sthitam yathā khageśvarī bhāva niḥśaṅka tvāt viṣam vrajet  kṣayam karma sthitiḥ tadvat aśaṅkāt bhairava tvataḥ ajña tvān upadeṣṭṛtva saṃdaṣṭe dhara śāsane etad viparyayāt grāhyam avaśyam śiva śāsanam dvauvāptau tatra ca śrīmat śrī kaṇṭhala kula īśvarau dvi pravāham idam śāstram mamyak niḥśreyasa pradam prācyasya tu yathā abhīṣṭa bhoga da tvam api sthitam tad ca pañcavidham proktam śakti vaicitrya citritam pañcasrota iti proktam śrīmat śrīkaṇṭha śāsanam daśa aṣṭādaśadhā srotaḥ pañcakam yad tatas  pyalam utkṛṣṭam bhairava abhikhyam catuḥṣaṣṭi vibheditam śrīmat ānanda śāstra ādau proktam bhagavatā kila samūhaḥ pīṭham etad ca dvidhā dakṣiṇa vāmataḥ mantraḥ  vidyā iti tasmāt ca mudrā maṇḍala gam dvayam manana trāṇa dam yad tu mantra ākhyam tatra vidyayā upodbalanam āpyāyaḥ sā hi vedya artha bhāsinī mantra pratikṛtiḥ mudrā tad āpyāyana kārakam maṇḍalam sāram uktam hi maṇḍa śrutyā śiva āhvayam evam anyonya saṃbheda vṛtti pīṭha catuṣṭayam yatas tasmāt bhavet sarvam pīṭhe pīṭhe pi vastutas  pradhāna tvāt tasya tasya vastunaḥ  bhinna tā punar  kathitā sādhaka indrāṇām tad tad vastu prasiddhaye pratyekam tad caturdhā evam maṇḍalam mudrikā tathā mantraḥ  vidyā iti ca pīṭham utkṛṣṭam ca uttara uttam vidyā pīṭha pradhānam ca siddhayogīśvarī matam tasya api paramam sāram mālinīvijaya uttaram uktam śrī ratnam ālāyām etad ca parameśinā aśeṣa tantra sāram tu vāma dakṣiṇam āśritam ekatra militam kaulam śrīṣaṣ ardhaka śāsane siddhānte karma bahulam mala māyā ādi rūṣitam dakṣiṇam raudra karma āḍhyam vāmam siddhi samākulam su alpa puṇyam bahu kleśam sva pratīti vivarjitam mokṣa vidyā vihīnam ca vinayam tyaja dūratas  yasmin kāle ca guruṇā nirvikalpam prakāśitam muktaḥ tena eva kālena yantram tiṣṭhati kevalam mayā etad srotasām rūpam anuttara padāt dhruvāt  ārabhya vistareṇa uktam mālinīśloka vārtike jijñāsuḥ tata eva idam avadhārayitum kṣamaḥ vayam tu ukta anuvacanam aphalam na ādriyāmahe ittham dadadana āyāsāt jīvanmukti mahā phalam yathā īpsita mahā bhoga dātṛ tvena vyavasthitam ṣaṣ ardha sāram sat śāstram upādeyam idam sphuṭam ṣaṭtriṃśatā tattva balena sūtā yadi api anantā bhuvanāvalīyam c brahmāṇḍam atyanta manoharam tu vaicitrya varjam na hi ramya bhāvaḥ bhūḥ ādi sapta pura pūrṇatame pi tasmin manye dvitīya bhuvanam bhavanam sukhasya kva anyatra citra gati sūrya śaśāṅka śobhi rātrindiva prasara bhoga vibhāga bhūṣā tatra apica tridiva bhoga mahārgha varṣa dvīpa antarāt adhikam eva kumārikā āhvam yatra adhara adhara padāt paramam śiva antam āroḍhum api adhikṛtiḥ kṛtinām anarghā prāk karma bhogi paśu ta ucita bhoga bhājā kim janmanā nanu sukha eka pade pi dhāmni sarvaḥ  hi bhāvini param paritoṣam eti saṃbhāvite na tu nimeṣiṇi vartamāne kanyā āhvaye pi bhuvane tra param mahīyān deśaḥ sa yatra kila śāstra varāṇi cakṣuḥ jāti andha sadmani na janma na kaḥ  bhinindet bhinnāñjanāyita ravi pramukha prakāśe niḥśeṣa śāstra sadanam kila madhyadeśaḥ tasmin  ajāyata guṇa abhyadhikaḥ  dvijanmā kaḥ  pyatrigupta iti nāma nirukta gotraḥ śāstra abdhi carvaṇa kalā udyat agastya gotraḥ tam atha lalita ādityaḥ  rājā nijam puram ānayat  praṇaya rabhasāt  kaśmīra ākhyam himālaya mūrdha gam adhivasati yad gaurīkāntaḥ karaiḥ vijaya ādibhiḥ yugapad akhilam bhoga asāram rasāt  paricarcitum sthāne sthāne munibhiḥ akhilaiḥ cakrire yad nivāsā yad ca adhyāste pratipadam idam sa svayam candracūḍaḥ tad manye ham samabhilaṣita aśeṣa siddheḥ na siddhyai kaśmīrebhyaḥ param atha puram pūrṇa vṛtteḥ na tuṣṭyai yatra svayam śārada candra śubhrā śrī śārada iti prathitā janeṣu śāṇḍilya sevā rasa su prasannā sarvam janam svaiḥ vibhavaiḥ yunakti nāraṅga aruṇa kānti pāṇḍu vikacat balla avadāta  chavi prodbhinna amala mātuluṅga kanaka  chāyā abhirāma prabham kerī kuntala kandalī pratikṛti śyāma prabhā bhāsvaram yasmin śakti catuṣṭaya ujjvala m alam madyam mahābhairavam trinayana mahā kopa jvālā vilīna iha sthitaḥ  madana viśikha vrātaḥ  madya  chalena vijṛmbhate katham itarathā rāgam moham madam madana jvaram vidadhat aniśam kāma ātaṅkaiḥ vaśīkurute jagat  yad kāntānām praṇaya vacasi prauḍhi mānam vidatte yad nirvighnam nidhuvana vidhau sādhu asam saṃdhunoti yasmin viśvāḥ kalita rucayaḥ  devatāḥ cakracaryaḥ tad mārdvīkam sapadi tanute yatra bhoga apabargau udyat gaura aṅkura vikasitaiḥ śyāma raktaiḥ palāśaiḥ antar gāḍha aruṇa ruci lasat kesara ālī vi citraiḥ ākīrṇā bhūḥ pratipadam asau yatra kāśmīra puṣpaiḥ samyak devī tritayaya jana udyānam āviṣkaroti sarvaḥ  lokaḥ kavi ratha budhaḥ yatra śūraḥ  pi vāgmī candra uddyotā masṛṇa gatayaḥ paura nāryaḥ ca yatra yatra aṅgāra ujjvala vikasita ananta sauṣumṇa mārga grasta arka induḥ gagana vimalaḥ  yoginīnām ca vargaḥ śrīmat param pravara nāma puram ca tatra yad nirmame pravarasena iti kṣitīśaḥ yaḥ sva pratiṣṭhita maheśvara pūjana ante vyoma utpatan  udasṛjat kila dhūpa ghaṇṭām āndola na udita manohara vīra nādaiḥ sā ca asya tad su caritam prathayāṃbabhūva sat vṛtta sāra guru taijasa mūrtayaḥ hi tyaktā api prabhu guṇa an adhikam dhvananti saṃpūrṇa candra vimala dyuti vīra kāntā gāḍha aṅga rāga ghana kuṅkuma piñjara śrīḥ proddhūta vetasa latā asita cāmara oghaiḥ ājya abhiṣekam aniśam dadatī smarasya rodhaḥ pratiṣṭhita maheśvara siddha liṅga sva ayaṃbhuva arcana vilepana gandha puṣpaiḥ āvarjyamāna tanu vīci nimajjana ogha vidhvasta pāpma muni siddha manuṣya vandyā bhoga apavarga paripūraṇa kalpavallī bhoga eka dāna rasikām sura siddha sindhum nyakkurvatī hara pinākakalā avatīrṇā yad bhūṣayati aviratam taṭinī vitastā tasmin kuvera pura cāri siṃta aṃśu mauli sāṃmukhya darśana virūḍha pavitra bhāve vaitasta rodhasi nivāsam amuṣya cakre rājā dvijasya parikalpita bhūri saṃpad  tasya anvaye mahati kaḥ  pi varāhagupta nāmā babhūva bhagavān svayam antakāle gīrvāṇa sindhu la harī kalita agra mūrdhā yasya akarot param anugraham āgraheṇa tasya ātmajaḥ cukhalaka iti jane prasiddhaḥ candra avadāta dhiṣaṇaḥ  narasiṃha guptaḥ yam sarva śāstra rasa majjana śubhra cittam māheśvarī param alaṃkurute sma bhaktiḥ tāruṇya sāgara taraṅga bharān apohya vairāgya potam adhiruhya dṛḍham haṭhena yaḥ  bhakti rohaṇam avāpya maheśa cintā ratnaiḥ alam dalayati sma bhava apadaḥ tāḥ tasya ātmajaḥ  bhinavagupta iti prasiddhaḥ śrī candra cūḍa caraṇa abja parāga pūtaḥ mātā vyayūyujadamum kila bālya eva daivam hi bhāvi parikarmaṇi saṃskaroti mātā param bandhuḥ iti pravādaḥ snohaḥ  tik āḍhīkurute hi pāśān tad mūla bandhe galite kila asya manye sthitā jīvata eva muktiḥ pitrā sa śabda gahane kṛta saṃpraveśaḥ tarka arṇava ūrmi pṛṣa ta amala pūta cittaḥ sāhitya sāndra rasa bhoga paraḥ  maheśa bhaktyā svayaṃgrahaṇa durmadayā gṛhītaḥ sa tad mayībhūya na loka vartanīm ajīgaṇat  kām api kevalam punar  tadīya saṃbhoga vivṛddhaye purā karoti dāsyam guru veśmasu svayam ānanda saṃtati mahā arṇava karṇa dhāraḥ sat daiśikairakavara ātmajavāmanāthaḥ śrī nātha saṃtati mahā ambara gharma kāntiḥ śrī bhūtirāja tanayaḥ sva pitṛ prasādaḥ traiyambaka prasara sāgara śāyi soma ānanda ātmaja utpala ja lakṣmaṇa gupta nāthaḥ turya ākhya saṃtati mahā udadhi pūrṇa candraḥ śrī somataḥ sakala vid kila śaṃbhu nāthaḥ śrī candra śarma bhava bhakti vilāsa yoga ānanda abhinanda śiva śakti vicitra nāthāḥ anye pi dharma śiva vāmanaka udbhaṭa śrī bhūta īśa bhāskara mukha pramukhā mahāntaḥ ete sevā rasa viracita anugrahāḥ śāstra sāra pauḍha ādeśa prakaṭa subhagam sva adhikāram kila asmai yad  saṃprāduḥ yad api ca janān na aikṣata akṣetra bhūtān sva ātma ārāmaḥ tad ayam aniśam tattva sevā rasaḥ  bhūt  saḥ  nugrahītum atha śāṃbhava bhakti bhājam svam bhrātaram akhila śāstra vimarśa pūrṇam yāvat manaḥ praṇidadhāti manoratha ākhyam tāvat janaḥ katipayaḥ tam upāsasāda śrī śauri saṃjña tanayaḥ kila karṇa nāmā yaḥ  yauvane vidita śāṃbhava tattva sāraḥ deham tyajan prathayati sma janasya satyam yoga cyutam prati mahā muni kṛṣṇa vākyam tad bāla mitram atha mantri sutaḥ prasiddhaḥ śrī mandra iti akhila sāra guṇa abhirāmaḥ lakṣmī sarasvati samam yama laṃcakāra sāpatnakam tirayate subhaga prabhāvaḥ anye pitṛvya tanayāḥ śiva śakti śubhrāḥ kṣemotpala abhinava cakraka padma guptāḥ ye saṃpadam tṛṇam amaṃsata śaṃbhu sevā saṃpūritam sva hṛdayam hṛdi bhāvayantaḥ ṣaṣ ardha śāstreṣu samastam eva yena adhijagme vidhi maṇḍala ādi sa rāmaguptaḥ  guru śaṃbhu śāstra sevā vidhi vyagra samagra mārgaḥ anyaḥ  pi kaścana janaḥ śiva śaktipāta saṃpreraṇa apara vaśa svaka śakti sārthaḥ abhyarthanā vimukha bhāvam aśikṣitena tena api anugraha padam kṛta eṣa vargaḥ ācāryam abhyarthayate sma gāḍham saṃpūrṇa tantra adhigamāya samyak  jāyeta daiva anugṛhīta buddheḥ saṃpad prabandha eka rasa eva saṃpad  saḥ  pyabhyupāgamat abhīpsitam asya yad vā svāta udyam eva hi ninartiṣataḥ  vatīrṇam saḥ  nugraha pravaṇa eva hi sat gurūṇām ājñā vaśena śubha sūti mahā aṅkureṇa vikṣipta bhāva parihāram athaḥ cikīrṣan mandraḥ svake pura vare sthitim asya vavre ābāla gopam api yatra maheśvarasya dāsyam janaḥ carati pīṭha nivāsa kalpe tasya abhavat kila pitṛvyavadhūḥ vidhātrā yā nirmame galita saṃsṛti citra cintā śītāṃśu mauli caraṇa abja pa rāga mātra bhūṣā vidhiḥ vihita vatsalikā ucita ākhyā mūrtā kṣamā iva karuṇā iva gṛhīta dehā dhārā iva vigrahavatī śubha śīla tāyāḥ vairāgya sāra paripāka daśā iva pūrṇā tattva artha ratna rucira sthiti rohaṇa urvī bhrātā api tasyāḥ śaśi śubhra mauleḥ bhaktyā param pāvita citta vṛttiḥ sa śauriḥ ātteśvara mantri bhāvaḥ tatyāja yaḥ  bhūpati mantri bhāvam tasya snuṣā karṇa vadhūḥ vidhūta saṃsāra vṛttiḥ sutam ekam eva yāsūta yogeśvari datta saṃjñam nāma anurūpa sphurat artha tattvam yām agra ge vayasi bhartṛ viyoga dīnām anvagrahīt  trinayanaḥ svayam eva bhaktyā bhāvi prabhāva rabhaseṣu janeṣu anarthaḥ satyam samākṛṣati saḥ  rtha paramparāṇām bhakti ullasat pulaka tām sphuṭam aṅga bhūṣām śrī śaṃbhunā athanatim eva lalāṭikām ca śaivaśrutim śravaṇa bhūṣaṇam api avāpya saubhāgyam abhyadhikam udvahati sma yāntaḥ ambā abhidhānā kila sā gurum tam svam bhrātaram śaṃbhu dṛśā abhyapaśyat bhāvi prabhāva ujjvala bhavya buddhiḥ sataḥ  vajānāti na bandhu buddhyā bhrātā tadīyaḥ  bhinavaḥ ca nāmnā na kevalam sat caritaiḥ api svaiḥ pītena vijñāna rasena yasya tatra eva tṛṣṇā vavṛdhe nikāmam saḥ  nyaḥ ca śāṃbhava marīci caya praṇaśyat saṃkoca hārda nalinī ghaṭita ujjvala śrīḥ tam lumpakaḥ paricacāra samudyameṣu sādhuḥ samāvahati hanta kara avalambam ittham gṛhe vatsalikā avitīrṇe sthitaḥ samādhāya matim bahūni pūrva śrutāni ākalayan sva buddhyā śāstrāṇi tebhyaḥ samavāpa sāram sa tad nibandham vidadhe mahārtham yukti āgama udīrita tantra tattvam ālokam āsādya yadi iyam eṣa lokaḥ sukham saṃcaritā kriyāsu santaḥ  nugṛhṇīta kṛtim tadīyām hṛhṇīta pūrvam vidhiḥ eṣa tāvat  tatas  pi gṛhṇātu bhavat matim sā sadyas  nugṛhṇātu ca tattva dṛṣṭyā idam abhinavagupta prombhitam śāstra sāram śiva niśamaya tāvat  sarvatas śrotra tantraḥ tava kila nutiḥ eṣā sā hi tvad rūpa carcā iti abhinava parituṣṭaḥ  lokam ātmīkuruṣva
